padmayoniriti hyevaṃ khyāto nāmnā bhaviṣyasi
putro me tvaṃ bhava brahman saptalokādhipaḥ prabho
tataḥ sa bhagavāndevo varaṃ dattvā kirīṭine
evaṃ bhavatu cetyuktvā prītātmā gatamatsaraḥ
pratyāsannam athāyāntaṃ bālārkābhaṃ mahānanam
bhavamatyadbhutaṃ dṛṣṭvā nārāyaṇamathābravīt
aprameyo mahāvaktro daṃṣṭrī dhvastaśiroruhaḥ
daśabāhustriśūlāṅko nayanairviśvataḥ sthitaḥ
lokaprabhuḥ svayaṃ sākṣādvikṛto muñjamekhalī
meṇḍhreṇordhvena mahatā nardamāno 'tibhairavam
kaḥ khalveṣa pumān viṣṇo tejorāśir mahādyutiḥ
vyāpya sarvā diśo dyāṃ ca ita evābhivartate
tenaivamukto bhagavān viṣṇurbrahmāṇamabravīt
padbhyāṃ talanipātena yasya vikramato'rṇave
vegena mahatākāśe'pyutthitāś ca jalaśayāḥ
sthūlādbhir viśvato 'tyarthaṃ sicyase padmasaṃbhava
ghrāṇajena ca vātena kampyamānaṃ tvayā saha
dodhūyate mahāpadmaṃ svacchandaṃ mama nābhijam
samāgato bhavānīśo hyanādiścāntakṛtprabhuḥ
bhavānahaṃ ca stotreṇa upatiṣṭhāva godhvajam
tataḥ kruddho 'mbujābhākṣaṃ brahmā provāca keśavam
bhavānna nūnamātmānaṃ vetti lokaprabhuṃ vibhum
brahmāṇaṃ lokakartāraṃ māṃ na vetsi sanātanam
ko hyasau śaṅkaro nāma āvayorvyatiricyate
tasya tatkrodhajaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā harirabhāṣata
mā maivaṃ vada kalyāṇa parivādaṃ mahātmanaḥ
mahāyogendhano dharmo durādharṣo varapradaḥ
heturasyātha jagataḥ purāṇapuruṣo 'vyayaḥ
bījī khalveṣa bījānāṃ jyotirekaḥ prakāśate
bālakrīḍanakairdevaḥ krīḍate śaṅkaraḥ svayam
pradhānamavyayo yoniravyaktaṃ prakṛtistamaḥ
mama caitāni nāmāni nityaṃ prasavadharmiṇaḥ
yaḥ kaḥ sa iti duḥkhārtairdṛśyate yatibhiḥ śivaḥ
eṣa bījī bhavānbījamahaṃ yoniḥ sanātanaḥ
sa evamukto viśvātmā brahmā viṣṇumapṛcchata
bhavān yonirahaṃ bījaṃ kathaṃ bījī maheśvaraḥ
etanme sūkṣmamavyaktaṃ saṃśayaṃ chettumarhasi
jñātvā ca vividhotpattiṃ brahmaṇo lokatantriṇaḥ
imaṃ paramasādṛśyaṃ praśnam abhyavadaddhariḥ
asmānmahattaraṃ bhūtaṃ guhyamanyanna vidyate
mahataḥ paramaṃ dhāma śivam adhyātmināṃ padam
dvividhaṃ caivamātmānaṃ pravibhajya vyavasthitaḥ
niṣkalastatra yo 'vyaktaḥ sakalaś ca maheśvaraḥ
yasya māyāvidhijñasya agamyagahanasya ca
purā liṅgodbhavaṃ bījaṃ prathamaṃ tvādisargikam
mama yonau samāyuktaṃ tadbījaṃ kālaparyayāt
hiraṇmayamakūpāre yonyāmaṇḍamajāyata
śatāni daśa varṣāṇām aṇḍam apsu pratiṣṭhitam
ante varṣasahasrasya vāyunā taddvidhā kṛtam
kapālamekaṃ dyaurjajñe kapālamaparaṃ kṣitiḥ
ulbaṃ tasya mahotsedho yo'sau kanakaparvataḥ
tataś ca pratisaṃdhyātmā devadevo varaḥ prabhuḥ
hiraṇyagarbho bhagavāṃstvabhijajñe caturmukhaḥ
ā tārārkendunakṣatraṃ śūnyaṃ lokamavekṣya ca
ko'hamityapi ca dhyāte kumārāste 'bhavaṃstadā
priyadarśanāstu yatayo yatīnāṃ pūrvajās tava
bhūyo varṣasahasrānte tata evātmajāstava
bhuvanānalasaṃkāśāḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇāḥ
śrīmānsanatkumāraś ca ṛbhuścaivordhvaretasau
sanakaḥ sanātanaścaiva tathaiva ca sanandanaḥ
utpannāḥ samakālaṃ te buddhyātīndriyadarśanāḥ
utpannāḥ pratibhātmāno jagatāṃ sthitihetavaḥ
nārapsyante ca karmāṇi tāpatrayavivarjitāḥ
alpasaukhyaṃ bahukleśaṃ jarāśokasamanvitam
jīvanaṃ maraṇaṃ caiva saṃbhavaś ca punaḥ punaḥ
alpabhūtaṃ sukhaṃ svarge duḥkhāni narake tathā
viditvā cāgamaṃ sarvamavaśyaṃ bhavitavyatām
ṛbhuṃ sanatkumāraṃ ca dṛṣṭvā tava vaśe sthitau
trayastu trīn guṇān hitvā cātmajāḥ sanakādayaḥ
vavartena tu jñānena pravṛttāste mahaujasaḥ
tatasteṣu pravṛtteṣu sanakādiṣu vai triṣu
bhaviṣyasi vimūḍhastvaṃ māyayā śaṅkarasya tu
evaṃ kalpe tu vaivṛtte saṃjñā naśyati te 'nagha
kalpe śeṣāṇi bhūtāni sūkṣmāṇi pārthivāni ca
sarveṣāṃ hyaiśvarī māyā jāgṛtiḥ samudāhṛtā
yathaiṣa parvato merurdevaloko hyudāhṛtaḥ
tasya cedaṃ hi māhātmyaṃ viddhi devavarasya ha
jñātvā ceśvarasadbhāvaṃ jñātvā māmaṃbujekṣaṇam
mahādevaṃ mahābhūtaṃ bhūtānāṃ varadaṃ prabhum
praṇavenātha sāmnā tu namaskṛtya jagadgurum
tvāṃ ca māṃ caiva saṃkruddho niḥśvāsānnirdahedayam
evaṃ jñātvā mahāyogamabhyuttiṣṭhanmahābalam
ahaṃ tvāmagrataḥ kṛtvā stoṣyāmyanalasaprabham
sūta uvāca
brahmāṇamagrataḥ kṛtvā tataḥ sa garuḍadhvajaḥ
atītaiś ca bhaviṣyaiś ca vartamānaistathaiva ca
nāmabhiśchāndasaiścaiva idaṃ stotramudīrayat
viṣṇuruvāca
namastubhyaṃ bhagavate suvratānantatejase
namaḥ kṣetrādhipataye bījine śūline namaḥ
sumeḍhrāyārcyameḍhrāya daṇḍine rūkṣaretase
namo jyeṣṭhāya śreṣṭhāya pūrvāya prathamāya ca
namo mānyāya pūjyāya sadyojātāya vai namaḥ
gahvarāya ghaṭeśāya vyomacīrāṃbarāya ca
namaste hyasmadādīnāṃ bhūtānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
vedānāṃ prabhave caiva smṛtīnāṃ prabhave namaḥ
prabhave karmadānānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
namo yogasya prabhave sāṃkhyasya prabhave namaḥ
namo dhruvanibaddhānāmṛṣīṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
ṛkṣāṇāṃ prabhave tubhyaṃ grahāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
vaidyutāśanimeghānāṃ garjitaprabhave namaḥ
mahodadhīnāṃ prabhave dvīpānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
adrīṇāṃ prabhave caiva varṣāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
namo nadīnāṃ prabhave nadānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
mahauṣadhīnāṃ prabhave vṛkṣāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
dharmavṛkṣāya dharmāya sthitīnāṃ prabhave namaḥ
prabhave ca parārdhasya parasya prabhave namaḥ
namo rasānāṃ prabhave ratnānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
kṣaṇānāṃ prabhave caiva lavānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
ahorātrārdhamāsānāṃ māsānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
ṛtūnāṃ prabhave tubhyaṃ saṃkhyāyāḥ prabhave namaḥ
prabhave cāparārdhasya parārdhaprabhave namaḥ
namaḥ purāṇaprabhave sargāṇāṃ prabhave namaḥ
manvantarāṇāṃ prabhave yogasya prabhave namaḥ
caturvidhasya sargasya prabhave 'nantacakṣuṣe
kalpodayanibandhānāṃ vātānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
namo viśvasya prabhave brahmādhipataye namaḥ
vidyānāṃ prabhave caiva vidyādhipataye namaḥ
namo vratādhipataye vratānāṃ prabhave namaḥ
mantrāṇāṃ prabhave tubhyaṃ mantrādhipataye namaḥ
pitṝṇāṃ pataye caiva paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ
vāgvṛṣāya namastubhyaṃ purāṇavṛṣabhāya ca
namaḥ paśūnāṃ pataye govṛṣendradhvajāya ca
prajāpatīnāṃ pataye siddhīnāṃ pataye namaḥ
daityadānavasaṃghānāṃ rakṣasāṃ pataye namaḥ
gandharvāṇāṃ ca pataye yakṣāṇāṃ pataye namaḥ
garuḍoragasarpāṇāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ pataye namaḥ
sarvaguhyapiśācānāṃ guhyādhipataye namaḥ
gokarṇāya ca goptre ca śaṅkukarṇāya vai namaḥ
varāhāyāprameyāya ṛkṣāya virajāya ca
namaḥ surāṇāṃ pataye gaṇānāṃ pataye namaḥ
aṃbhasāṃ pataye caiva ojasāṃ pataye namaḥ
namo'stu lakṣmīpataye śrīpāya kṣitipāya ca
balābalasamūhāya akṣobhyakṣobhaṇāya ca
dīptaśṛṅgaikaśṛṅgāya vṛṣabhāya kakudmine
namaḥ sthairyāya vapuṣe tejasānuvratāya ca
atītāya bhaviṣyāya vartamānāya vai namaḥ
suvarcase ca vīryāya śūrāya hyajitāya ca
varadāya vareṇyāya puruṣāya mahātmane
namo bhūtāya bhavyāya mahate prabhavāya ca
janāya ca namastubhyaṃ tapase varadāya ca
aṇave mahate caiva namaḥ sarvagatāya ca
namo bandhāya mokṣāya svargāya narakāya ca
namo bhavāya devāya ijyāya yājakāya ca
pratyudīrṇāya dīptāya tattvāyātiguṇāya ca
namaḥ pāśāya śastrāya namastvābharaṇāya ca
hutāya upahūtāya prahutaprāśitāya ca
namo'stviṣṭāya pūrtāya agniṣṭomadvijāya ca
sadasyāya namaścaiva dakṣiṇāvabhṛthāya ca
ahiṃsāyāpralobhāya paśumantrauṣadhāya ca
namaḥ puṣṭipradānāya suśīlāya suśīline
atītāya bhaviṣyāya vartamānāya te namaḥ
suvarcase ca vīryāya śūrāya hyajitāya ca
varadāya vareṇyāya puruṣāya mahātmane
namo bhūtāya bhavyāya mahate cābhayāya ca
jarāsiddha namastubhyamayase varadāya ca
adhare mahate caiva namaḥ sastupatāya ca
namaścendriyapatrāṇāṃ lelihānāya sragviṇe
viśvāya viśvarūpāya viśvataḥ śirase namaḥ
sarvataḥ pāṇipādāya rudrāyāpratimāya ca
namo havyāya kavyāya havyavāhāya vai namaḥ
namaḥ siddhāya medhyāya iṣṭāyejyāparāya ca
suvīrāya sughorāya akṣobhyakṣobhaṇāya ca
suprajāya sumedhāya dīptāya bhāskarāya ca
namo buddhāya śuddhāya vistṛtāya matāya ca
namaḥ sthūlāya sūkṣmāya dṛśyādṛśyāya sarvaśaḥ
varṣate jvalate caiva vāyave śiśirāya ca
namaste vakrakeśāya ūruvakṣaḥśikhāya ca
namo namaḥ suvarṇāya tapanīyanibhāya ca
virūpākṣāya liṅgāya piṅgalāya mahaujase
vṛṣṭighnāya namaścaiva namaḥ saumyekṣaṇāya ca
namo dhūmrāya śvetāya kṛṣṇāya lohitāya ca
piśitāya piśaṅgāya pītāya ca niṣaṅgiṇe
namaste saviśeṣāya nirviśeṣāya vai namaḥ
nama ījyāya pūjyāya upajīvyāya vai namaḥ
namaḥ kṣemyāya vṛddhāya vatsalāya namonamaḥ
namo bhūtāya satyāya satyāsatyāya vai namaḥ
namo vai padmavarṇāya mṛtyughnāya ca mṛtyave
namo gaurāya śyāmāya kadrave lohitāya ca
mahāsaṃdhyābhravarṇāya cārudīptāya dīkṣiṇe
namaḥ kamalahastāya digvāsāya kapardine
apramāṇāya sarvāya avyayāyāmarāya ca
namo rūpāya gandhāya śāśvatāyākṣatāya ca
purastādbṛṃhate caiva vibhrāntāya kṛtāya ca
durgamāya maheśāya krodhāya kapilāya ca
tarkyātarkyaśarīrāya baline raṃhasāya ca
sikatyāya pravāhyāya sthitāya prasṛtāya ca
sumedhase kulālāya namaste śaśikhaṇḍine
citrāya citraveṣāya citravarṇāya medhase
cekitānāya tuṣṭāya namaste nihitāya ca
namaḥ kṣāntāya dāntāya vajrasaṃhananāya ca
rakṣoghnāya viṣaghnāya śitikaṇṭhordhvamanyave
lelihāya kṛtāntāya tigmāyudhadharāya ca
pramodāya saṃmodāya yativedyāya te namaḥ
anāmayāya sarvāya mahākālāya vai namaḥ
praṇavapraṇaveśāya bhaganetrāntakāya ca
mṛgavyādhāya dakṣāya dakṣayajñāntakāya ca
sarvabhūtātmabhūtāya sarveśātiśayāya ca
puraghnāya suśastrāya dhanvine 'tha paraśvadhe
pūṣadantavināśāya bhaganetrāntakāya ca
kāmadāya variṣṭhāya kāmāṅgadahanāya ca
raṅge karālavaktrāya nāgendravadanāya ca
daityānāmantakeśāya daityākrandakarāya ca
himaghnāya ca tīkṣṇāya ārdracarmadharāya ca
śmaśānaratinityāya namo 'stūlmukadhāriṇe
namaste prāṇapālāya muṇḍamālādharāya ca
prahīṇaśokairvividhairbhūtaiḥ parivṛtāya ca
naranārīśarīrāya devyāḥ priyakarāya ca
jaṭine muṇḍine caiva vyālayajñopavītine
namo 'stu nṛtyaśīlāya upanṛtyapriyāya ca
manyave gītaśīlāya munibhir gāyate namaḥ
kaṭakaṭāya tigmāya apriyāya priyāya ca
vibhīṣaṇāya bhīṣmāya bhagapramathanāya ca
siddhasaṃghānugītāya mahābhāgāya vai namaḥ
namo muktāṭṭahāsāya kṣveḍitāsphoṭitāya ca
nardate kūrdate caiva namaḥ pramuditātmane
namo mṛḍāya śvasate dhāvate 'dhiṣṭhite namaḥ
dhyāyate jṛmbhate caiva rudate dravate namaḥ
valgate krīḍate caiva lambodaraśarīriṇe
namo 'kṛtyāya kṛtyāya muṇḍāya kīkaṭāya ca
nama unmattadehāya kiṅkiṇīkāya vai namaḥ
namo vikṛtaveṣāya krūrāyāmarṣaṇāya ca
aprameyāya goptre ca dīptāyānirguṇāya ca
vāmapriyāya vāmāya cūḍāmaṇidharāya ca
namastokāya tanave guṇairapramitāya ca
namo guṇyāya guhyāya agamyagamanāya ca
lokadhātrī tviyaṃ bhūmiḥ pādau sajjanasevitau
sarveṣāṃ siddhiyogānāmadhiṣṭhānaṃ tavodaram
madhye 'ntarikṣaṃ vistīrṇaṃ tārāgaṇavibhūṣitam
svāteḥ patha ivābhāti śrīmān hārastavorasi
diśo daśabhujāstubhyaṃ keyūrāṅgadabhūṣitāḥ
vistīrṇapariṇāhaś ca nīlāñjanacayopamaḥ
kaṇṭhaste śobhate śrīmān hemasūtravibhūṣitaḥ
daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ durdharṣamanaupamyaṃ mukhaṃ tathā
padmamālākṛtoṣṇīṣaṃ śiro dyauḥ śobhate 'dhikam
dīptiḥ sūrye vapuścandre sthairyaṃ śaile 'nile balam
auṣṇyamagnau tathā śaityam apsu śabdo 'mbare tathā
akṣarāntaraniṣpandādguṇānetānvidurbudhāḥ
japo japyo mahādevo mahāyogomaheśvaraḥ
pureśayo guhāvāsī khecaro rajanīcaraḥ
taponidhirguhagururnandano nandavardhanaḥ
hayaśīrṣā payodhātā vidhātā bhūtabhāvanaḥ
boddhavyo bodhitā netā durdharṣo duṣprakampanaḥ
bṛhadratho bhīmakarmā bṛhatkīrtir dhanañjayaḥ
ghaṇṭāpriyo dhvajī chattrī pinākī dhvajinīpatiḥ
kavacī paṭṭiśī khaḍgī dhanurhastaḥ paraśvadhī
aghasmaro 'naghaḥ śūro devarājo 'rimardanaḥ
tvāṃ prasādya purāsmābhir dviṣanto nihatā yudhi
agniḥ sadārṇavāṃbhastvaṃ pibannapi na tṛpyase
krodhākāraḥ prasannātmā kāmadaḥ kāmagaḥ priyaḥ
brahmacāri cāgādhaś ca brahmaṇyaḥ śiṣṭapūjitaḥ
devānām akṣayaḥ kośas tvayā yajñaḥ prakalpitaḥ
havyaṃ tavedaṃ vahati vedoktaṃ havyavāhanaḥ
prīte tvayi mahādeva vayaṃ prītā bhavāmahe
bhavānīśo 'nādimāṃstvaṃ ca sarvalokānāṃ tvaṃ brahmakartādisargaḥ
sāṃkhyāḥ prakṛteḥ paramaṃ tvāṃ viditvā kṣīṇadhyānāstvāmamṛtyuṃ viśanti
yogāś ca tvāṃ dhyāyino nityasiddhaṃ jñātvā yogān saṃtyajante punastān
ye cāpyanye tvāṃ prasannā viśuddhāḥ svakarmabhiste divyabhogā bhavanti
aprasaṃkhyeyatattvasya yathā vidmaḥ svaśaktitaḥ
kīrtitaṃ tava māhātmyam apārasya mahātmanaḥ
śivo no bhava sarvatra yo 'si so 'si namo 'stu te
sūta uvāca
ya idaṃ kīrtayedbhaktyā brahmanārāyaṇastavam
śrāvayedvā dvijān vidvān śṛṇuyādvā samāhitaḥ
aśvamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatphalaṃ tadavāpnuyāt
pāpācāro 'pi yo martyaḥ śṛṇuyācchivasannidhau
japedvāpi vinirmukto brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati
śrāddhe vā daivike kārye yajñe vāvabhṛthāntike
kīrtayedvā satāṃ madhye sa yāti brahmaṇo'ntikam
sūta uvāca
atyantāvanatau dṛṣṭvā madhupiṅgāyatekṣaṇaḥ
prahṛṣṭavadano 'tyartham abhavatsatyakīrtanāt
umāpatirvirūpākṣo dakṣayajñavināśanaḥ
pinākī khaṇḍaparaśuḥ suprītastu trilocanaḥ
tataḥ sa bhagavāndevaḥ śrutvā vāgamṛtaṃ tayoḥ
jānannapi mahādevaḥ krīḍāpūrvamathābravīt
kau bhavantau mahātmānau parasparahitaiṣiṇau
sametāvaṃbujābhakṣāv asmin ghore mahāplave
tāvūcaturmahātmānau saṃnirīkṣya parasparam
bhagavān kiṃ tu yatte 'dya na vijñānaṃ tvayā vibho
vibho rudra mahāmāya icchayā vāṃ kṛtau tvayā
tayostadvacanaṃ śrutvā abhinandyābhimānya ca
uvāca bhagavāndevo madhuraṃ ślakṣṇayā girā
bho bho hiraṇyagarbha tvāṃ tvāṃ ca kṛṣṇa bravīmyaham
prīto 'hamanayā bhaktyā śāśvatākṣarayuktayā
bhavantau hṛdayasyāsya mama hṛdyatarāvubhau
yuvābhyāṃ kiṃ dadāmyadya varāṇāṃ varamīpsitam
athovāca mahābhāgo viṣṇurbhavamidaṃ vacaḥ
sarvaṃ mama kṛtaṃ deva parituṣṭo 'si me yadi
tvayi me supratiṣṭhā tu bhaktirbhavatu śaṅkaraḥ
evamuktastu vijñāya saṃbhāvayata keśavam
pradadau ca mahādevo bhaktiṃ nijapadāṃbuje
bhavānsarvasya lokasya kartā tvamadhidaivatam
tadevaṃ svasti te vatsa gamiṣyāmyaṃbujekṣaṇa
evamuktvā tu bhagavān brahmāṇaṃ cāpi śaṅkaraḥ
anugṛhyāspṛśaddevo brahmāṇaṃ parameśvaraḥ
karābhyāṃ suśubhābhyāṃ ca prāha hṛṣṭataraḥ svayam
matsamastvaṃ na saṃdeho vatsa bhaktaś ca me bhavān
svastyastu te gamiṣyāmi saṃjñā bhavatu suvrata
evamuktvā tu bhagavāṃstato 'ntardhānamīśvaraḥ
gatavān gaṇapo devaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ
avāpya saṃjñāṃ govindāt padmayoniḥ pitāmahaḥ
prajāḥ sraṣṭumanāścakre tapa ugraṃ pitāmahaḥ
tasyaivaṃ tapyamānasya na kiṃcit samavartata
tato dīrgheṇa kālena duḥkhātkrodho hyajāyata
krodhāviṣṭasya netrābhyāṃ prāpatannaśrubindavaḥ
tatastebhyo 'śrubindubhyo vātapittakaphātmakāḥ
mahābhāgā mahāsattvāḥ svastikairapyalaṃkṛtāḥ
prakīrṇakeśāḥ sarpāste prādurbhūtā mahāviṣāḥ
sarpāṃstānagrajāndṛṣṭvā brahmātmānam anindayat
aho dhik tapaso mahyaṃ phalamīdṛśakaṃ yadi
lokavaināśikī jajñe ādāveva prajā mama
tasya tīvrābhavanmūrcchā krodhāmarṣasamudbhavā
mūrcchābhiparitāpena jahau prāṇānprajāpatiḥ
tasyāpratimavīryasya dehātkāruṇyapūrvakam
athaikādaśa te rudrā rudanto 'bhyakramaṃs tathā
rodanātkhalu rudratvaṃ teṣu vai samajāyata
ye rudrāste khalu prāṇā ye prāṇāste tadātmakāḥ
prāṇāḥ prāṇavatāṃ jñeyāḥ sarvabhūteṣvavasthitāḥ
atyugrasya mahattvasya sādhurācaritasya ca
prāṇāṃstasya dadau bhūyastriśūlī nīlalohitaḥ
labdhvāsūn bhagavānbrahma devadevamumāpatim
praṇamya saṃsthito 'paśyadgāyatryā viśvamīśvaram
sarvalokamayaṃ devaṃ dṛṣṭvā stutvā pitāmahaḥ
tato vismayamāpannaḥ praṇipatya muhurmuhuḥ
uvāca vacanaṃ śarvaṃ sadyāditvaṃ kathaṃ vibho
sūta uvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmaṇo bhagavān bhavaḥ
brahmarūpī prabodhārthaṃ brahmāṇaṃ prāha sasmitam
śvetakalpo yadā hyāsīd ahameva tadābhavam
śvetoṣṇīṣaḥ śvetamālyaḥ śvetāṃbaradharaḥ sitaḥ
śvetāsthiḥ śvetaromā ca śvetāsṛk śvetalohitaḥ
tena nāmnā ca vikhyātaḥ śvetakalpastadā hyasau
matprasūtā ca deveśī śvetāṅgā śvetalohitā
śvetavarṇā tadā hyāsīdgāyatrī brahmasaṃjñitā
tasmādahaṃ ca deveśa tvayā guhyena vai punaḥ
vijñātaḥ svena tapasā sadyojātatvamāgataḥ
sadyojāteti brahmaitadguhyaṃ caitatprakīrtitam
tasmādguhyatvamāpannaṃ ye vetsyanti dvijātayaḥ
matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
yadā caiva punastvāsīllohito nāma nāmataḥ
matkṛtena ca varṇena kalpo vai lohitaḥ smṛtaḥ
tadā lohitamāṃsāsthilohitakṣīrasaṃbhavā
lohitākṣī stanavatī gāyatrī gauḥ prakīrtitā
tato 'syā lohitatvena varṇasya ca viparyayāt
vāmatvāccaiva devasya vāmadevatvamāgataḥ
tatrāpi ca mahāsattva tvayāhaṃ niyatātmanā
vijñātaḥ svena yogena tasminvarṇāntare sthitaḥ
tataś ca vāmadeveti khyātiṃ yāto 'smi bhūtale
ye cāpi vāmadeva tvāṃ jñāsyantīha dvijātayaḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
yadāhaṃ punareveha pītavarṇo yugakramāt
matkṛtena ca nāmnā vai pītakalpo 'bhavattadā
matprasūtā ca deveśī pītāṅgī pītalohitā
pītavarṇā tadā hyāsīdgāyatrī brahmasaṃjñitā
tatrāpi ca mahāsattva yogayuktena cetasā
yasmādahaṃ tairvijñāto yogatatparamānasaiḥ
tatra tatpuruṣatvena vijñāto 'haṃ tvayā punaḥ
tasmāttatpuruṣatvaṃ vai mamaitatkanakāṇḍaja
ye māṃ rudraṃ ca rudrāṇīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram
vetsyanti tapasā yuktā vimalā brahmasaṃgatāḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
yadāhaṃ punarevāsaṃ kṛṣṇavarṇo bhayānakaḥ
matkṛtena ca varṇena saṃkalpaḥ kṛṣṇa ucyate
tatrāhaṃ kālasaṃkāśaḥ kālo lokaprakālakaḥ
vijñāto 'haṃ tvayā brahmanghoro ghoraparākramaḥ
matprasūtā ca gāyatrī kṛṣṇāṅgī kṛṣṇalohitā
kṛṣṇarūpā ca deveśa tadāsīdbrahmasaṃjñitā
tasmād ghoratvamāpannaṃ ye māṃ vetsyanti bhūtale
teṣāmaghoraḥ śāntaś ca bhaviṣyāmyahamavyayaḥ
punaś ca viśvarūpatvaṃ yadā brahmanmamābhavat
tadāpyahaṃ tvayā jñātaḥ parameṇa samādhinā
viśvarūpā ca saṃvṛttā gāyatrī lokadhāriṇī
tasmin viśvatvam āpannaṃ ye māṃ vetsyanti bhūtale
teṣāṃ śivaś ca saumyaś ca bhaviṣyāmi sadaiva hi
yasmācca viśvarūpo vai kalpo 'yaṃ samudāhṛtaḥ
viśvarūpā tathā ceyaṃ sāvitrī samudāhṛtā
sarvarūpā tathā ceme saṃvṛttā mama putrakāḥ
catvāraste mayā khyātāḥ putra vai lokasaṃmatāḥ
yasmācca sarvavarṇatvaṃ prajānāṃ ca bhaviṣyati
sarvabhakṣā ca medhyā ca varṇataś ca bhaviṣyati
mokṣo dharmastathārthaś ca kāmaśceti catuṣṭayam
yasmādvedāś ca vedyaṃ ca caturdhā vai bhaviṣyati
bhūtagrāmāś ca catvāra āśramāś ca tathaiva ca
dharmasya pādāścatvāraścatvāro mama putrakāḥ
tasmāccaturyugāvasthaṃ jagadvai sacarācaram
caturdhāvasthitaścaiva catuṣpādo bhaviṣyati
bhūrloko 'tha bhuvarlokaḥ svarlokaś ca mahas tathā
janastapaś ca satyaṃ ca viṣṇulokastataḥ param
aṣṭākṣarasthito lokaḥ sthāne sthāne tadakṣaram
bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahaścaiva pādāścatvāra eva ca
bhūrlokaḥ prathamaḥ pādo bhuvarlokastataḥ param
svarloko vai tṛtīyaś ca caturthastu mahas tathā
pañcamastu janastatra ṣaṣṭhaś ca tapa ucyate
satyaṃ tu saptamo loko hyapunarbhavagāminām
viṣṇulokaḥ smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ punarāvṛttidurlabham
skāndamaumaṃ tathā sthānaṃ sarvasiddhisamanvitam
rudralokaḥ smṛtastasmātpadaṃ tadyogināṃ śubham
nirmamā nirahaṅkārāḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitāḥ
drakṣyanti taddvijā yuktā dhyānatatparamānasāḥ
yasmāccatuṣpadā hyeṣā tvayā dṛṣṭā sarasvatī
pādāntaṃ viṣṇulokaṃ vai kaumāraṃ śāntamuttamam
aumaṃ māheśvaraṃ caiva tasmāddṛṣṭā catuṣpadā
tasmāttu paśavaḥ sarve bhaviṣyanti catuṣpadāḥ
tataścaiṣāṃ bhaviṣyanti catvāraste payodharāḥ
somaś ca mantrasaṃyukto yasmānmama mukhāccyutaḥ
jīvaḥ prāṇabhṛtāṃ brahman punaḥ pītastanāḥ smṛtāḥ
tasmātsomamayaṃ caiva amṛtaṃ jīvasaṃjñitam
catuṣpādā bhaviṣyanti śvetatvaṃ cāsya tena tat
yasmāccaiva kriyā bhūtvā dvipadā ca maheśvarī
dṛṣṭā punastathaivaiṣā sāvitrī lokabhāvinī
tasmācca dvipadāḥ sarve dvistanāś ca narāḥ śubhāḥ
tasmācceyamajā bhūtvā sarvavarṇā maheśvarī
yā vai dṛṣṭā mahāsattvā sarvabhūtadharā tvayā
tasmācca viśvarūpatvaṃ prajānāṃ vai bhaviṣyati
ajaścaiva mahātejā viśvarūpo bhaviṣyati
amogharetāḥ sarvatra mukhe cāsya hutāśanaḥ
tasmātsarvagato medhyaḥ paśurūpī hutāśanaḥ
tapasā bhāvitātmāno ye māṃ drakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ
īśitve ca vaśitve ca sarvagaṃ sarvataḥ sthitam
rajastamobhyāṃ nirmuktāstyaktvā mānuṣyakaṃ vapuḥ
matsamīpamupeṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
ityevamukto bhagavānbrahmā rudreṇa vai dvijāḥ
praṇamya prayato bhūtvā punarāha pitāmahaḥ
ya evaṃ bhagavān vidvān gāyatryā vai maheśvaram
viśvātmānaṃ hi sarvaṃ tvāṃ gāyatryāstava ceśvara
tasya dehi paraṃ sthānaṃ tathāstviti ca so'bravīt
tasmādvidvān hi viśvatvamasyāścāsya mahātmanaḥ
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ vacanād brahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ
sūta uvāca
śrutvaivamakhilaṃ brahmā rudreṇa paribhāṣitam
punaḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ rudramāha prajāpatiḥ
bhagavandevadeveśa viśvarūpaṃ maheśvara
umādhava mahādeva namo lokābhivandita
viśvarūpa mahābhāga kasminkāle maheśvara
yā imāste mahādeva tanavo lokavanditāḥ
kasyāṃ vā yugasaṃbhūtyāṃ drakṣyantīha dvijātayaḥ
kena vā tapasā deva dhyānayogena kena vā
namaste vai mahādeva śakyo draṣṭuṃ dvijātibhiḥ
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śarvaḥ samprekṣya taṃ puraḥ
smayanprāha mahādeva ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
tapasā naiva vṛttena dānadharmaphalena ca
na tīrthaphalayogena kratubhir vāptadakṣiṇaiḥ
na vedādhyayanairvāpi na vittena na vedanaiḥ
na śakyaṃ mānavairdraṣṭumṛte dhyānādahaṃ tviha
saptame caiva vārāhe tatastasminpitāmaha
kalpeśvaro 'tha bhagavān sarvalokaprakāśanaḥ
manurvaivasvataścaiva tava pautro bhaviṣyati
tadā caturyugāvasthe tasminkalpe yugāntike
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya ca
utpatsyāmi tadā brahman punar asmin yugāntike
yugapravṛttyā ca tadā tasmiṃś ca prathame yuge
dvāpare prathame brahmanyadā vyāsaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ
tadāhaṃ brāhmaṇārthāya kalau tasmin yugāntike
bhaviṣyāmi śikhāyuktaḥ śveto nāma mahāmuniḥ
himavacchikhare ramye chāgale parvatottame
tatra śiṣyāḥ śikhāyuktā bhaviṣyanti tadā mama
śvetaḥ śvetaśikhaścaiva śvetāsyaḥ śvetalohitaḥ
catvārastu mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
tataste brahmabhūyiṣṭhā dṛṣṭvā brahmagatiṃ parām
matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyanti dhyānayogaparāyaṇāḥ
tataḥ punaryadā brahman dvitīye dvāpare prabhuḥ
prajāpatiryadā vyāsaḥ sadyo nāma bhaviṣyati
tadā lokahitārthāya sutāro nāma nāmataḥ
bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin śiṣyānugrahakāmyayā
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā nāmataḥ parikīrtitāḥ
dundubhiḥ śatarūpaś ca ṛcīkaḥ ketumāṃstadā
prāpya yogaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ sthāpya brahma ca bhūtale
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti sahacāritvameva ca
tṛtīye dvāpare caiva yadā vyāsastu bhārgavaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi damanastu yugāntike
tatrāpi ca bhaviṣyanti catvāro mama putrakāḥ
vikośaś ca vikeśaś ca vipāśaḥ śāpanāśanaḥ
te 'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa yogoktena mahaujasaḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
caturthe dvāpare caiva yadā vyāso 'ṅgirāḥ smṛtaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi suhotro nāma nāmataḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrāścatvāro 'pi tapodhanāḥ
dvijaśreṣṭhā bhaviṣyanti yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
sumukho durmukhaścaiva durdaro duratikramaḥ
prāpya yogagatiṃ sūkṣmāṃ vimalā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
te'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa yogayuktā mahaujasaḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
pañcame dvāpare caiva vyāsastu savitā yadā
tadā cāpi bhaviṣyāmi kaṅko nāma mahātapāḥ
anugrahārthaṃ lokānāṃ yogātmaikakalāgatiḥ
catvārastu mahābhāgā vimalāḥ śuddhayonayaḥ
śiṣyā mama bhaviṣyanti yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
sanakaḥ sanandanaś caiva prabhuryaś ca sanātanaḥ
vibhuḥ sanatkumāraś ca nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ
matsamīpamupeṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
parīvarte punaḥ ṣaṣṭhe mṛtyurvyāso yadā vibhuḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi logākṣīr nāma nāmataḥ
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahābhāgāścatvāro lokasaṃmatāḥ
sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhapādraja eva ca
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve vai dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
te'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogasamanvitāḥ
matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
saptame parivarte tu yadā vyāsaḥ śatakratuḥ
vibhunāmā mahātejāḥ prathitaḥ pūrvajanmani
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin yugāntike
jaigīṣavyo vibhuḥ khyātaḥ sarveṣāṃ yogināṃ varaḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti yuge tathā
sārasvataś ca meghaś ca meghavāhaḥ suvāhanaḥ
te'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogaparāyaṇāḥ
gamiṣyanti mahātmāno rudralokaṃ nirāmayam
vasiṣṭhaścāṣṭame vyāsaḥ parīvarte bhaviṣyati
yadā tadā bhaviṣyāmi nāmnāhaṃ dadhivāhanaḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā yogātmāno dṛḍhavratāḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahāyogā yeṣāṃ nāsti samo bhuvi
kapilaścāsuriścaiva tathā pañcaśikho muniḥ
bāṣkalaś ca mahāyogī dharmātmāno mahaujasaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ jñānino dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
matsamīpaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
parivarte tu navame vyāsaḥ sārasvato yadā
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi ṛṣabho nāma nāmataḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ
parāśaraś ca gargaś ca bhārgavāṅgirasau tadā
bhaviṣyanti mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
dhyānamārgaṃ samāsādya gamiṣyanti tathaiva te
sarve tapobalotkṛṣṭāḥ śāpānugrahakovidāḥ
te'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa yogoktena tapasvinaḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
daśame dvāpare vyāsaḥ tripādvai nāma nāmataḥ
yadā bhaviṣyate viprastadāhaṃ bhavitā muniḥ
himavacchikhare ramye bhṛgutuṅge nagottame
nāmnā bhṛgostu śikharaṃ prathitaṃ devapūjitam
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti dṛḍhavratāḥ
balabandhurnirāmitraḥ ketuśṛṅgastapodhanaḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānastapoyogasamanvitāḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti tapasā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
ekādaśe dvāpare tu vyāsastu trivrato yadā
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi gaṅgādvāre kalau tathā
ugro nāma mahātejāḥ sarvalokeṣu viśrutaḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ
lambodaraś ca lambākṣo lambakeśaḥ pralambakaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te
dvādaśe parivarte tu śatatejā yadā muniḥ
bhaviṣyati mahātejā vyāsastu kavisattamaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi kalāviha yugāntike
haitukaṃ vanamāsādya atrirnāmnā pariśrutaḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhasmasnānānulepanāḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahāyogā rudralokaparāyaṇāḥ
sarvajñaḥ samabuddhiś ca sādhyaḥ sarvastathaiva ca
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te
trayodaśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte krameṇa tu
dharmo nārāyaṇo nāma vyāsastu bhavitā yadā
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi vālirnāma mahāmuniḥ
vālakhilyāśrame puṇye parvate gandhamādane
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vāsiṣṭho virajāstathā
mahāyogabalopetā vimalā ūrdhvaretasaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ gatā hi te
yadā vyāsastarakṣustu paryāye tu caturdaśe
tatrāpi punarevāhaṃ bhaviṣyāmi yugāntike
vaṃśe tvaṅgirasāṃ śreṣṭhe gautamo nāma nāmataḥ
bhaviṣyati mahāpuṇyaṃ gautamaṃ nāma tadvanam
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti kalau tadā
atrirdevasadaścaiva śravaṇo 'tha śraviṣṭhakaḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve yogasamanvitāḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
tataḥ pañcadaśe prāpte parivarte kramāgate
traiyyāruṇiryadā vyāso dvāpare samapadyata
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi nāmnā vedaśirā dvijaḥ
tatra vedaśiro nāma astraṃ tatpārameśvaram
bhaviṣyati mahāvīryaṃ vedaśīrṣaś ca parvataḥ
himavatpṛṣṭhamāsādya sarasvatyāṃ nagottame
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
kuṇiś ca kuṇibāhuś ca kuśarīraḥ kunetrakaḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
vyāso yuge ṣoḍaśe tu yadā devo bhaviṣyati
tatra yogapradānāya bhaktānāṃ ca yatātmanām
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi gokarṇo nāma nāmataḥ
bhaviṣyati supuṇyaṃ ca gokarṇaṃ nāma tadvanam
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti ca yoginaḥ
kāśyapo hyuśanāścaiva cyavano 'tha bṛhaspatiḥ
te'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa dhyānayogasamanvitāḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ gantāro rudrameva hi
tataḥ saptadaśe caiva parivarte kramāgate
yadā bhaviṣyati vyāso nāmnā devakṛtañjayaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi guhāvāsīti nāmataḥ
himavacchikhare ramye mahottuṅge mahālaye
siddhakṣetraṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ bhaviṣyati mahālayam
tatrāpi mama te putrā yogajñā brahmavādinaḥ
bhaviṣyanti mahātmāno nirmamā nirahaṃkṛtāḥ
utathyo vāmadevaś ca mahāyogo mahābalaḥ
teṣāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu śiṣyāṇāṃ dhyānayoginām
bhaviṣyanti tadā kāle sarve te dhyānayuñjakāḥ
yogābhyāsaratāścaiva hṛdi kṛtvā maheśvaram
mahālaye padaṃ nyastaṃ dṛṣṭvā yānti śivaṃ padam
ye cānye 'pi mahātmānaḥ kalau tasmin yugāntike
dhyāne manaḥ samādhāya vimalāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ
mama prasādādyāsyanti rudralokaṃ gatajvarāḥ
gatvā mahālayaṃ puṇyaṃ dṛṣṭvā māheśvaraṃ padam
tīrṇastārayate janturdaśa pūrvāndaśottarān
ātmānamekaviṃśaṃ tu tārayitvā mahālaye
mama prasādādyāsyanti rudralokaṃ gatajvarāḥ
tato 'ṣṭādaśame caiva parivarte yadā vibho
tadā ṛtañjayo nāma vyāsastu bhavitā muniḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi śikhaṇḍī nāma nāmataḥ
siddhakṣetre mahāpuṇye devadānavapūjite
himavacchikhare ramye śikhaṇḍī nāma parvataḥ
śikhaṇḍino vanaṃ cāpi yatra siddhaniṣevitam
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
vācaśravā ṛcīkaś ca śyāvāśvaś ca yatīśvaraḥ
yogātmāno mahātmānaḥ sarve te vedapāragāḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃvṛtāḥ
atha ekonaviṃśe tu parivarte kramāgate
vyāsastu bhavitā nāmnā bharadvājo mahāmuniḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi jaṭāmālī ca nāmataḥ
himavacchikhare ramye jaṭāyuryatra parvataḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ
hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo lokākṣī kuthumis tathā
īśvarā yogadharmāṇaḥ sarve te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ
tato viṃśatimaścaiva parivarto yadā tadā
gautamastu tadā vyāso bhaviṣyati mahāmuniḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi aṭṭahāsastu nāmataḥ
aṭṭahāsapriyāścaiva bhaviṣyanti tadā narāḥ
tatraiva himavatpṛṣṭhe aṭṭahāso mahāgiriḥ
devadānavayakṣendrasiddhacāraṇasevitaḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ
yogātmāno mahātmāno dhyāyino niyatavratāḥ
sumanturbarbarī vidvān kabandhaḥ kuśikaṃdharaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
ekaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate
vācaśravāḥ smṛto vyāso yadā sa ṛṣisattamaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi dāruko nāma nāmataḥ
tasmādbhaviṣyate puṇyaṃ devadāruvanaṃ śubham
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti mahaujasaḥ
plakṣo dārbhāyaṇiścaiva ketumān gautamas tathā
yogātmāno mahātmāno niyatā ūrdhvaretasaḥ
naiṣṭhikaṃ vratamāsthāya rudralokāya te gatāḥ
dvāviṃśe parivarte tu vyāsaḥ śuṣmāyaṇo yadā
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi vārāṇasyāṃ mahāmuniḥ
nāmnā vai lāṅgalī bhīmo yatra devāḥ savāsavāḥ
drakṣyanti māṃ kalau tasmin bhavaṃ caiva halāyudham
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti sudhārmikāḥ
bhallavī madhupiṅgaś ca śvetaketuḥ kuśas tathā
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ te'pi dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
vimalā brahmabhūyiṣṭhā rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ
parivarte trayoviṃśe tṛṇabinduryadā muniḥ
vyāso hi bhavitā brahmaṃstadāhaṃ bhavitā punaḥ
śveto nāma mahākāyo muniputrastu dhārmikaḥ
tatra kālaṃ jariṣyāmi tadā girivarottame
tena kālañjaro nāma bhaviṣyati sa parvataḥ
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā bhaviṣyanti tapasvinaḥ
uśiko bṛhadaśvaś ca devalaḥ kavireva ca
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gataḥ
parivarte caturviṃśe vyāsa ṛkṣo yadā vibho
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi kalau tasmin yugāntike
śūlī nāma mahāyogī naimiṣe devavandite
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
śālihotro 'gniveśaś ca yuvanāśvaḥ śaradvasuḥ
te 'pi tenaiva mārgeṇa rudralokāya saṃsthitāḥ
pañcaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate
vāsiṣṭhastu yadā vyāsaḥ śaktirnāmnā bhaviṣyati
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi daṇḍī muṇḍīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
chagalaḥ kuṇḍakarṇaś ca kubhāṇḍaś ca pravāhakaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogamamṛtatvāya te gatāḥ
ṣaḍviṃśe parivarte tu yadā vyāsaḥ parāśaraḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi sahiṣṇurnāma nāmataḥ
puraṃ bhadravaṭaṃ prāpya kalau tasmin yugāntike
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti sudhārmikāḥ
ulūko vidyutaścaiva śaṃbūko hyāśvalāyanaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokāya te gatāḥ
saptaviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate
jātūkarṇyo yadā vyāso bhaviṣyati tapodhanaḥ
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi somaśarmā dvijottamaḥ
prabhāsatīrthamāsādya yogātmā yogaviśrutaḥ
tatrāpi mama te śiṣyā bhaviṣyanti tapodhanāḥ
akṣapādaḥ kumāraś ca ulūko vatsa eva ca
yogātmāno mahātmāno vimalāḥ śuddhabuddhayaḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ rudralokaṃ tato gatāḥ
aṣṭāviṃśe punaḥ prāpte parivarte kramāgate
parāśarasutaḥ śrīmān viṣṇurlokapitāmahaḥ
yadā bhaviṣyati vyāso nāmnā dvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ
tadā ṣaṣṭhena cāṃśena kṛṣṇaḥ puruṣasattamaḥ
vasudevādyaduśreṣṭho vāsudevo bhaviṣyati
tadāpyahaṃ bhaviṣyāmi yogātmā yogamāyayā
lokavismayanārthāya brahmacāriśarīrakaḥ
śmaśāne mṛtam utsṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭvā kāyam anāthakam
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitārthāya praviṣṭo yogamāyayā
divyāṃ meruguhāṃ puṇyāṃ tvayā sārdhaṃ ca viṣṇunā
bhaviṣyāmi tadā brahmaṃllakulī nāma nāmataḥ
kāyāvatāra ityevaṃ siddhakṣetraṃ ca vai tadā
bhaviṣyati suvikhyātaṃ yāvad bhūmir dhariṣyati
tatrāpi mama te putrā bhaviṣyanti tapasvinaḥ
kuśikaś caiva gargaś ca mitraḥ kauruṣya eva ca
yogātmāno mahātmāno brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ
prāpya māheśvaraṃ yogaṃ vimalā hyūrdhvaretasaḥ
rudralokaṃ gamiṣyanti punarāvṛttidurlabham
ete pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ
liṅgārcanaratā nityaṃ bāhyābhyantarataḥ sthitāḥ
bhaktyā mayi ca yogena dhyānaniṣṭhā jitendriyāḥ
saṃsārabandhacchedārthaṃ jñānamārgaprakāśakam
svarūpajñānasiddhyarthaṃ yogaṃ pāśupataṃ mahat
yogamārgā anekāś ca jñānamārgās tv anekaśaḥ
na nivṛttimupāyānti vinā pañcākṣarīṃ kvacit
yadācarettapaścāyaṃ sarvadvandvavivarjitam
tadā sa mukto mantavyaḥ pakvaṃ phalamiva sthitaḥ
ekāhaṃ yaḥ pumānsamyak caretpāśupatavratam
na sāṃkhye pañcarātre vā na prāpnoti gatiṃ kadā
ityetadvai mayā proktamavatāreṣu lakṣaṇam
manvādikṛṣṇaparyantamaṣṭāviṃśad yugakramāt
tatra śrutisamūhānāṃ vibhāgo dharmalakṣaṇaḥ
bhaviṣyati tadā kalpe kṛṣṇadvaipāyano yadā
sūta uvāca
niśamyaivaṃ mahātejā mahādevena kīrtitam
rudrāvatāraṃ bhagavān praṇipatya maheśvaram
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ punaḥ prāha ca śaṅkaram
pitāmaha uvāca
sarve viṣṇumayā devāḥ sarve viṣṇumayā gaṇāḥ
na hi viṣṇusamā kācidgatiranyā vidhīyate
ityevaṃ satataṃ vedā gāyanti nātra saṃśayaḥ
sa devadevo bhagavāṃstava liṅgārcane rataḥ
tava praṇāmaparamaḥ kathaṃ devo hyabhūtprabhuḥ
sūta uvāca
niśamya vacanaṃ tasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
prapibanniva cakṣurbhyāṃ prītastatpraśnagauravāt
pūjāprakaraṇaṃ tasmai tamālokyāha śaṅkaraḥ
bhavānnārāyaṇaścaiva śakraḥ sākṣātsurottamaḥ
munayaś ca sadā liṅgaṃ sampūjya vidhipūrvakam
svaṃsvaṃ padaṃ vibho prāptās tasmāt sampūjayanti te
liṅgārcanaṃ vinā niṣṭhā nāsti tasmājjanārdanaḥ
ātmano yajate nityaṃ śraddhayā bhagavānprabhuḥ
ityevamuktvā brahmāṇamanugṛhya maheśvaraḥ
punaḥ samprekṣya deveśaṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata
tamuddiśya tadā brahmā namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ
sraṣṭuṃ tvaśeṣaṃ bhagavāṃllabdhasaṃjñastu śaṅkarāt
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ pūjyo mahādevo liṅgamūrtirmaheśvaraḥ
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa sāṃpratam
sūta uvāca
devyā pṛṣṭo mahādevaḥ kailāse tāṃ nagātmajām
aṅkasthāmāha deveśo liṅgārcanavidhiṃ kramāt
tadā pārśve sthito nandī śālaṅkāyanakātmajaḥ
śrutvākhilaṃ purā prāha brahmaputrāya suvratāḥ
sanatkumārāya śubhaṃ liṅgārcanavidhiṃ param
tasmādvyāso mahātejāḥ śrutavāñchrutisaṃmitam
snānayogopacāraṃ ca yathā śailādino mukhāt
śrutavān tatpravakṣyāmi snānādyaṃ cārcanāvidhim
śailādiruvāca
atha snānavidhiṃ vakṣye brāhmaṇānāṃ hitāya ca
sarvapāpaharaṃ sākṣācchivena kathitaṃ purā
anena vidhinā snātvā sakṛtpūjya ca śaṅkaram
brahmakūrcaṃ ca pītvā tu sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
trividhaṃ snānamākhyātaṃ devadevena śaṃbhunā
hitāya brāhmaṇādyānāṃ caturmukhasutottama
vāruṇaṃ purataḥ kṛtvā tataścāgneyamuttamam
mantrasnānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pūjayetparameśvaram
bhāvaduṣṭo 'mbhasi snātvā bhasmanā ca na śudhyati
bhāvaśuddhaścarecchaucamanyathā na samācaret
saritsarastaḍāgeṣu sarveṣv ā pralayaṃ naraḥ
snātvāpi bhāvaduṣṭaścenna śudhyati na saṃśayaḥ
nṛṇāṃ hi cittakamalaṃ prabuddhamabhavadyadā
prasuptaṃ tamasā jñānabhānorbhāsā tadā śuciḥ
mṛcchakṛttilapuṣpaṃ ca snānārthaṃ bhasitaṃ tathā
ādāya tīre niḥkṣipya snānatīrthe kuśāni ca
prakṣālyācamya pādau ca malaṃ dehādviśodhya ca
dravyaistu tīradeśasthaistataḥ snānaṃ samācaret
uddhṛtāsītimantreṇa punardehaṃ viśodhayet
mṛdādāya tataścānyadvastraṃ snātvā hyanulbaṇam
gandhadvārāṃ durādharṣāmiti mantreṇa mantravit
kapilāgomayenaiva khasthenaiva tu lepayet
punaḥ snātvā parityajya tadvastraṃ malinaṃ tataḥ
śuklavastraparīdhāno bhūtvā snānaṃ samācaret
sarvapāpaviśuddhyarthamāvāhya varuṇaṃ tathā
sampūjya manasā devaṃ dhyānayajñena vai bhavam
ācamya tristadā tīrthe hyavagāhya bhavaṃ smaran
punarācamya vidhivadabhimantrya mahājalam
avagāhya punastasmin japedvai cāghamarṣaṇam
tattoye bhānusomāgnimaṇḍalaṃ ca smaredvaśī
ācamya ca punastasmājjalāduttīrya mantravit
praviśya tīrthamadhye tu punaḥ puṇyavivṛddhaye
śṛṅgeṇa parṇapuṭakaiḥ pālāśaiḥ kṣālitais tathā
sakuśena sapuṣpeṇa jalenaivābhiṣecayet
rudreṇa pavamānena tvaritākhyena mantravit
taratsamandīvargādyais tathā śāntidvayena ca
śāntidharmeṇa caikena pañcabrahmapavitrakaiḥ
tattanmantrādhidevānāṃ svarūpaṃ ca ṛṣīn smaran
evaṃ hi cābhiṣicyātha svamūrdhni payasā dvijāḥ
dhyāyecca tryambakaṃ devaṃ hṛdi pañcāsyam īśvaram
ācamyācamanaṃ kuryātsvasūtroktaṃ samīkṣya ca
pavitrahastaḥ svāsīnaḥ śucau deśe yathāvidhi
abhyukṣya sakuśaṃ cāpi dakṣiṇena kareṇa tu
pibetprakṣipya tristoyaṃ cakrī bhūtvā hyatandritaḥ
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kuryāddhiṃsāpāpapraśāntaye
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ snānācamanamuttamam
sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ tu hitārthe dvijasattamāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge snānavidhirnāma pañcaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
nandyuvāca
āvāhayettato devīṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram
āyātu varadā devītyanenaiva maheśvarīm
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca tasyāścārghyaṃ pradāpayet
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā samāsīnaḥ sthito 'pi vā
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
gāyatrīṃ praṇavenaiva trividheṣvekamācaret
arghyaṃ dattvā samabhyarcya praṇamya śirasā svayam
uttame śikhare devītyuktvodvāsya ca mātaram
prācyālokyābhivandyeśāṃ gāyatrīṃ vedamātaram
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā prārthayedbhāskaraṃ tathā
udutyaṃ ca tathā citraṃ jātavedasameva ca
abhivandya punaḥ sūryaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca vidhānataḥ
tathā saurāṇi sūktāni ṛgyajuḥsāmajāni ca
japtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ paścāttriḥ kṛtvā ca vibhāvasoḥ
ātmānaṃ cāntarātmānaṃ paramātmānameva ca
abhivandya punaḥ sūryaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca vibhāvasum
munīn pitṝn yathānyāyaṃ svanāmnāvāhayettataḥ
sarvānāvāhayāmīti devānāvāhya sarvataḥ
tarpayedvidhinā paścāt prāṅmukho vā hyudaṅmukhaḥ
dhyātvā svarūpaṃ tattattvam abhivandya yathākramam
devānāṃ puṣpatoyena ṛṣīṇāṃ tu kuśāṃbhasā
pitṝṇāṃ tilatoyena gandhayuktena sarvataḥ
yajñopavītī devānāṃ nivītī ṛṣitarpaṇam
prācīnāvītī viprendra pitṝṇāṃ tarpayet kramāt
aṅgulyagreṇa vai dhīmāṃstarpayeddevatarpaṇam
ṛṣīn kaniṣṭhāṅgulinā śrotriyaḥ sarvasiddhaye
pitṝṃstu tarpayed vidvān dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhakena tu
tathaivaṃ muniśārdūla brahmayajñaṃ yajed dvijaḥ
devayajñaṃ ca mānuṣyaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ tathaiva ca
pitṛyajñaṃ ca pūtātmā yajñakarmaparāyaṇaḥ
svaśākhādhyayanaṃ vipra brahmayajña iti smṛtaḥ
agnau juhoti yaccānnaṃ devayajña iti smṛtaḥ
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ balidānaṃ vidhānataḥ
bhūtayajña iti prokto bhūtidaḥ sarvadehinām
sadārān sarvatattvajñān brāhmaṇān vedapāragān
praṇamya tebhyo yaddattamannaṃ mānuṣa ucyate
pitṝn uddiśya yaddattaṃ pitṛyajñaḥ sa ucyate
evaṃ pañca mahāyajñān kuryāt sarvārthasiddhaye
sarveṣāṃ śṛṇu yajñānāṃ brahmayajñaḥ paraḥ smṛtaḥ
brahmayajñarato martyo brahmaloke mahīyate
brahmayajñena tuṣyanti sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ
vedāś ca pitaraḥ sarve nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
grāmādbahirgato bhūtvā brāhmaṇo brahmayajñavit
yāvat tvadṛṣṭam abhavad uṭajānāṃ chadaṃ naraḥ
prācyāmudīcyāṃ ca tathā prāgudīcyām athāpi vā
puṇyamācamanaṃ kuryādbrahmayajñārthameva tat
prītyarthaṃ ca ṛcāṃ viprāḥ triḥ pītvā plāvya plāvya ca
yajuṣāṃ parimṛjyaivaṃ dviḥ prakṣālya ca vāriṇā
prītyarthaṃ sāmavedānāmupaspṛśya ca mūrdhani
spṛśedatharvavedānāṃ netre cāṅgirasāṃ tathā
nāsike brāhmaṇo 'ṅgānāṃ kṣālya kṣālya ca vāriṇā
aṣṭādaśapurāṇānāṃ brahmādyānāṃ tathaiva ca
tathā copapurāṇānāṃ saurādīnāṃ yathākramam
puṇyānāmitihāsānāṃ śaivādīnāṃ tathaiva ca
śrotre spṛśeddhi tuṣṭyarthaṃ hṛddeśaṃ tu tataḥ spṛśet
kalpādīnāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ kalpavitkalpavittamāḥ
evamācamya cāstīrya darbhapiñjūlam ātmanaḥ
kṛtvā pāṇitale dhīmānātmano dakṣiṇottaram
hemāṅgulīyasaṃyukto brahmabandhayuto 'pi vā
vidhivadbrahmayajñaṃ ca kuryātsūtrī samāhitaḥ
akṛtvā ca muniḥ pañca mahāyajñāndvijottamaḥ
bhuktvā ca sūkarāṇāṃ tu yonau vai jāyate naraḥ
tasmātsarvaprayatnena kartavyāḥ śubhamicchatā
brahmayajñādatha snānaṃ kṛtvādau sarvathātmanaḥ
tīrthaṃ saṃgṛhya vidhivatpraviśecchibiraṃ vaśī
bahireva gṛhātpādau hastau prakṣālya vāriṇā
bhasmasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād vidhivad dehaśuddhaye
śodhya bhasma yathānyāyaṃ praṇavenāgnihotrajam
jyotiḥ sūrya iti prātarjuhuyādudite yataḥ
jyotiragnis tathā sāyaṃ samyak cānudite mṛṣā
tasmāduditahomasthaṃ bhasitaṃ pāvanaṃ śubham
nāsti satyasamaṃ yasmādasatyaṃ pātakaṃ ca yat
īśānena śirodeśaṃ mukhaṃ tatpuruṣeṇa ca
urodeśamaghoreṇa guhyaṃ vāmena suvratāḥ
sadyena pādau sarvāṅgaṃ praṇavenābhiṣecayet
tataḥ prakṣālayetpādaṃ hastaṃ brahmavidāṃ varaḥ
vyapohya bhasma cādāya devadevamanusmaran
mantrasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryād āpohiṣṭhādibhiḥ kramāt
puṇyaiścaiva tathā mantrairṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaiḥ
dvijānāṃ tu hitāyaivaṃ kathitaṃ snānamadya te
saṃkṣipya yaḥ sakṛtkuryātsa yāti paramaṃ padam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pañcayajñavidhānaṃ nāma ṣaḍviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
vakṣyāmi śṛṇu saṃkṣepālliṅgārcanāvidhikramam
vaktuṃ varṣaśatenāpi na śakyaṃ vistareṇa yat
evaṃ snātvā yathānyāyaṃ pūjāsthānaṃ praviśya ca
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dhyāyeddevaṃ triyaṃbakam
pañcavaktraṃ daśabhujaṃ śuddhasphaṭikasannibham
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ citrāṃbaravibhūṣitam
tasya rūpaṃ samāśritya dāhanaplāvanādibhiḥ
śaivīṃ tanuṃ samāsthāya pūjayetparameśvaram
dehaśuddhiṃ ca kṛtvaiva mūlamantraṃ nyaset kramāt
sarvatra praṇavenaiva brahmāṇi ca yathākramam
sūtre namaḥ śivāyeti chandāṃsi parame śubhe
mantrāṇi sūkṣmarūpeṇa saṃsthitāni yatastataḥ
nyagrodhabīje nyagrodhas tathā sūtre tu śobhane
mahatyapi mahadbrahma saṃsthitaṃ sūkṣmavatsvayam
secayedarcanasthānaṃ gandhacandanavāriṇā
dravyāṇi śodhayetpaścātkṣālanaprokṣaṇādibhiḥ
kṣālanaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ caiva praṇavena vidhīyate
prokṣaṇī cārghyapātraṃ ca pādyapātram anukramāt
tathā hyācamanīyārthaṃ kalpitaṃ pātrameva ca
sthāpayed vidhinā dhīmān avaguṇṭhya yathāvidhi
darbhair ācchādayeccaiva prokṣayecchuddhavāriṇā
teṣu teṣvatha sarveṣu kṣipettoyaṃ suśītalam
praṇavena kṣipetteṣu dravyāṇyālokya buddhimān
uśīraṃ candanaṃ caiva pādye tu parikalpayet
jātikaṅkolakarpūrabahumūlatamālakam
cūrṇayitvā yathānyāyaṃ kṣipedācamanīyake
evaṃ sarveṣu pātreṣu dāpayeccandanaṃ tathā
karpūraṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ puṣpāṇi vividhāni ca
kuśāgramakṣatāṃścaiva yavavrīhitilāni ca
ājyasiddhārthapuṣpāṇi bhasitaṃ cārghyapātrake
kuśapuṣpayavavrīhibahumūlatamālakam
dāpayetprokṣaṇīpātre bhasitaṃ praṇavena ca
nyasetpañcākṣaraṃ caiva gāyatrīṃ rudradevatām
kevalaṃ praṇavaṃ vāpi vedasāramanuttamam
atha saṃprokṣayetpaścāddravyāṇi praṇavena tu
prokṣaṇīpātrasaṃsthena īśānādyaiś ca pañcabhiḥ
pārśvato devadevasya nandinaṃ māṃsamarcayet
dīptānalāyutaprakhyaṃ trinetraṃ tridaśeśvaram
bālendumukuṭaṃ caiva harivaktraṃ caturbhujam
puṣpamālādharaṃ saumyaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
uttare cātmanaḥ puṇyāṃ bhāryāṃ ca marutāṃ śubhām
suyaśāṃ suvratāṃ cāmbāṃ pādamaṇḍanatatparām
evaṃ pūjya praviśyāntarbhavanaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
dattvā puṣpāñjaliṃ bhaktyā pañcamūrdhasu pañcabhiḥ
gandhapuṣpais tathā dhūpairvividhaiḥ pūjya śaṅkaram
skandaṃ vināyakaṃ devīṃ liṅgaśuddhiṃ ca kārayet
japtvā sarvāṇi mantrāṇi praṇavādinamo'ntakam
kalpayedāsanaṃ paścātpadmākhyaṃ praṇavena tat
tasya pūrvadalaṃ sākṣād aṇimāmayam akṣaram
laghimā dakṣiṇaṃ caiva mahimā paścimaṃ tathā
prāptistathottaraṃ patraṃ prākāmyaṃ pāvakasya tu
īśitvaṃ nairṛtaṃ patraṃ vaśitvaṃ vāyugocare
sarvajñatvaṃ tathaiśānyaṃ karṇikā soma ucyate
somasyādhas tathā sūryastasyādhaḥ pāvakaḥ svayam
dharmādayo vidikṣvete tvanantaṃ kalpayetkramāt
avyaktādicaturdikṣu somasyānte guṇatrayam
ātmatrayaṃ tataścordhvaṃ tasyānte śivapīṭhikā
sadyojātaṃ prapadyāmītyāvāhya parameśvaram
vāmadevena mantreṇa sthāpayedāsanopari
sānnidhyaṃ rudragāyatryā aghoreṇa nirudhya ca
īśānaḥ sarvavidyānāmiti mantreṇa pūjayet
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca vibhoścārghyaṃ pradāpayet
snāpayedvidhinā rudraṃ gandhacandanavāriṇā
pañcagavyavidhānena gṛhya pātre 'bhimantrya ca
praṇavenaiva gavyaistu snāpayecca yathāvidhi
ājyena madhunā caiva tathā cekṣurasena ca
puṇyairdravyairmahādevaṃ praṇavenābhiṣecayet
jalabhāṇḍaiḥ pavitraistu mantraistoyaṃ kṣipettataḥ
śuddhiṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ sitavastreṇa sādhakaḥ
kuśāpāmārgakarpūrajātipuṣpakacampakaiḥ
karavīraiḥ sitaiścaiva mallikākamalotpalaiḥ
āpūrya puṣpaiḥ suśubhaiḥ candanādyaiś ca tajjalam
nyasenmantrāṇi tattoye sadyojātādikāni tu
suvarṇakalaśenātha tathā vai rājatena vā
tāmreṇa padmapatreṇa pālāśena dalena vā
śaṃkhena mṛnmayenātha śodhitena śubhena vā
sakūrcena sapuṣpeṇa snāpayenmantrapūrvakam
mantrāṇi te pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu sarvārthasiddhaye
yairliṅgaṃ sakṛdapyevaṃ snāpya mucyeta mānavaḥ
pavamānena mantrajñāḥ tathā vāmīyakena ca
rudreṇa nīlarudreṇa śrīsūktena śubhena ca
rajanīsūktakenaiva camakena śubhena ca
hotāreṇātha śirasārtharveṇa śubhena ca
śāntyā cātha punaḥ śāntyā bhāruṇḍenāruṇena ca
vāruṇena ca jyeṣṭhena tathā vedavratena ca
tathāntareṇa puṇyena sūktena puruṣeṇa ca
tvaritenaiva rudreṇa kapinā ca kapardinā
āvosajeti sāmnā tu bṛhaccandreṇa viṣṇunā
virūpākṣeṇa skandena śatargbhiḥ śivais tathā
pañcabrahmaiś ca sūtreṇa kevalapraṇavena ca
snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ sarvapāpapraśāntaye
vastraṃ śivopavītaṃ ca tathā hyācamanīyakam
gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ dīpamannaṃ krameṇa tu
toyaṃ sugandhitaṃ caiva punarācamanīyakam
mukuṭaṃ ca śubhaṃ channaṃ tathā vai bhūṣaṇāni ca
dāpayetpraṇavenaiva mukhavāsādikāni ca
tataḥ sphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ devaṃ niṣkalamakṣaram
kāraṇaṃ sarvadevānāṃ sarvalokamayaṃ param
brahmendraviṣṇurudrādyair ṛṣidevair agocaram
vedavidbhir hi vedāntaistvagocaramiti śrutiḥ
ādimadhyāntarahitaṃ bheṣajaṃ bhavarogiṇām
śivatattvamiti khyātaṃ śivaliṅge vyavasthitam
praṇavenaiva mantreṇa pūjayelliṅgamūrdhani
stotraṃ japecca vidhinā namaskāraṃ pradakṣiṇam
arghyaṃ dattvātha puṣpāṇi pādayostu vikīrya ca
praṇipatya ca deveśamātmanyāropayecchivam
evaṃ saṃkṣipya kathitaṃ liṅgārcanamanuttamam
ābhyantaraṃ pravakṣyāmi liṅgārcanamihādya te
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge liṅgārcanavidhirnāma saptaviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
āgneyaṃ sauramamṛtaṃ bimbaṃ bhāvyaṃ tata upari
guṇatrayaṃ ca hṛdaye tathā cātmatrayaṃ kramāt
tasyopari mahādevaṃ niṣkalaṃ sakalākṛtim
kāntārdharūḍhadehaṃ ca pūjayeddhyānavidyayā
tato bahuvidhaṃ proktaṃ cintyaṃ tatrāsti cedyataḥ
cintakasya tataścintā anyathā nopapadyate
tasmāddhyeyaṃ tathā dhyānaṃ yajamānaḥ prayojanam
smarettannānyathā jātu budhyate puruṣasya ha
pure śete puraṃ dehaṃ tasmātpuruṣa ucyate
yājyaṃ yajñena yajate yajamānastu sa smṛtaḥ
dhyeyo maheśvaro dhyānaṃ cintanaṃ nirvṛtiḥ phalam
pradhānapuruṣeśānaṃ yāthātathyaṃ prapadyate
iha ṣaḍviṃśako dhyeyo dhyātā vai pañcaviṃśakaḥ
caturviṃśakam avyaktaṃ mahadādyāstu sapta ca
mahāṃs tathā tvahaṅkāraṃ tanmātraṃ pañcakaṃ punaḥ
karmendriyāṇi pañcaiva tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca
manaś ca pañca bhūtāni śivaḥ ṣaḍviṃśakastataḥ
sa eva bhartā kartā ca vidherapi maheśvaraḥ
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ rudro 'sau janayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ
viśvādhikaś ca viśvātmā viśvarūpa iti smṛtaḥ
vinā yathā hi pitaraṃ mātaraṃ tanayāstviha
na jāyante tathā somaṃ vinā nāsti jagattrayam
sanatkumāra uvāca
kartā yadi mahādevaḥ paramātmā maheśvaraḥ
tathā kārayitā caiva kurvato 'lpātmanas tathā
nityo viśuddho buddhaś ca niṣkalaḥ parameśvaraḥ
tvayokto muktidaḥ kiṃ vā niṣkalaścetkaroti kim
śailādiruvāca
kālaḥ karoti sakalaṃ kālaṃ kalayate sadā
niṣkalaṃ ca manaḥ sarvaṃ manyate so'pi niṣkalaḥ
karmaṇā tasya caiveha jagatsarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
kimatra devadevasya mūrtyaṣṭakamidaṃ jagat
vinākāśaṃ jagannaiva vinā kṣmāṃ vāyunā vinā
tejasā vāriṇā caiva yajamānaṃ tathā vinā
bhānunā śaśinā lokastasyaitāstanavaḥ prabhoḥ
vicāratastu rudrasya sthūlametaccarācaram
sūkṣmaṃ vadanti ṛṣayo yanna vācyaṃ dvijottamāḥ
yato vāco nivartante aprāpya manasā saha
ānandaṃ brahmaṇo vidvānna bibheti kutaścana
na bhetavyaṃ tathā tasmājjñātvānandaṃ pinākinaḥ
vibhūtayaś ca rudrasya matvā sarvatra bhāvataḥ
sarvaṃ rudra iti prāhurmunayastattvadarśinaḥ
namaskāreṇa satataṃ gauravātparameṣṭhinaḥ
sarvaṃ tu khalvidaṃ brahma sarvo vai rudra īśvaraḥ
puruṣo vai mahādevo maheśānaḥ paraḥ śivaḥ
evaṃ vibhurvinirdiṣṭo dhyānaṃ tatraiva cintanam
caturvyūheṇa mārgeṇa vicāryālokya suvrata
saṃsārahetuḥ saṃsāro mokṣahetuś ca nirvṛtiḥ
caturvyūhaḥ samākhyātaścintakasyeha yoginaḥ
cintā bahuvidhā khyātā saikatra parameṣṭhinā
suniṣṭhetyatra kathitā rudraṃ raudrī na saṃśayaḥ
aindrī cendre tathā saumyā some nārāyaṇe tathā
sūrye vahnau ca sarveṣāṃ sarvatraivaṃ vicārataḥ
saivāhaṃ so'hamityevaṃ dvidhā saṃsthāpya bhāvataḥ
bhakto'sau nāsti yastasmāccintā brāhmī na saṃśayaḥ
evaṃ brahmamayaṃ dhyāyet pūrvaṃ vipra carācaram
carācaravibhāgaṃ ca tyajedabhimataṃ smaran
tyājyaṃ grāhyam alabhyaṃ ca kṛtyaṃ cākṛtyameva ca
yasya nāsti sutṛptasya tasya brāhmī na cānyathā
ābhyantaraṃ samākhyātamevamabhyarcanaṃ kramāt
ābhyantarārcakāḥ pūjyā namaskārādibhis tathā
virūpā vikṛtāścāpi na nindyā brahmavādinaḥ
ābhyantarārcakāḥ sarve na parīkṣyā vijānatā
nindakā eva duḥkhārtā bhaviṣyantyalpacetasaḥ
yathā dāruvane rudraṃ vinindya munayaḥ purā
tasmātsevyā namaskāryāḥ sadā brahmavidas tathā
varṇāśramavinirmuktā varṇāśramaparāyaṇaiḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivārcanatattvasaṃkhyādivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
idānīṃ śrotumicchāmi purā dāruvane vibho
pravṛttaṃ tadvanasthānāṃ tapasā bhāvitātmanām
kathaṃ dāruvanaṃ prāpto bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthāya cordhvaretā digambaraḥ
kiṃ pravṛttaṃ vane tasmin rudrasya paramātmanaḥ
vaktumarhasi tattvena devadevasya ceṣṭitam
sūta uvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā śrutisāravidāṃ varaḥ
śilādasūnurbhagavānprāha kiṃcidbhavaṃ hasan
śailādiruvāca
munayo dārugahane tapastepuḥ sudāruṇam
tuṣṭyarthaṃ devadevasya sadāratanayāgnayaḥ
tuṣṭo rudro jagannāthaścekitāno vṛṣadhvajaḥ
dhūrjaṭiḥ parameśāno bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
pravṛttilakṣaṇaṃ jñānaṃ jñātuṃ dāruvanaukasām
parīkṣārthaṃ jagannāthaḥ śraddhayā krīḍayā ca saḥ
nivṛttilakṣaṇajñānapratiṣṭhārthaṃ ca śaṅkaraḥ
devadāruvanasthānāṃ pravṛttijñānacetasām
vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthāya digvāsā viṣamekṣaṇaḥ
mugdho dvihastaḥ kṛṣṇāṅgo divyaṃ dāruvanaṃ yayau
mandasmitaṃ ca bhagavān strīṇāṃ manasijodbhavam
bhrūvilāsaṃ ca gānaṃ ca cakārātīva suṃdaraḥ
saṃprokṣya nārīvṛndaṃ vai muhurmuhuranaṅgahā
anaṅgavṛddhim akarodatīva madhurākṛtiḥ
vane taṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā vikṛtaṃ nīlalohitam
striyaḥ pativratāścāpi tamevānvayurādarāt
vanoṭajadvāragatāś ca nāryo visrastavastrābharaṇā viceṣṭāḥ
labdhvā smitaṃ tasya mukhāravindād drumālayasthās tam athānvayustāḥ
dṛṣṭvā kāścidbhavaṃ nāryo madaghūrṇitalocanāḥ
vilāsabāhyāstāścāpi bhrūvilāsaṃ pracakrire
atha dṛṣṭvāparā nāryaḥ kiṃcit prahasitānanāḥ
kiṃcid visrastavasanāḥ srastakāñcīguṇā jaguḥ
kāścittadā taṃ vipine tu dṛṣṭvā viprāṅganāḥ srastanavāṃśukaṃ vā
svānsvānvicitrān valayānpravidhya madānvitā bandhujanāṃś ca jagmuḥ
kācittadā taṃ na viveda dṛṣṭvā vivāsanā srastamahāṃśukā ca
śākhāvicitrān viṭapānprasiddhānmadānvitā bandhujanāṃstathānyāḥ
kāścijjagustaṃ nanṛturnipetuś ca dharātale
niṣedurgajavaccānyā provāca dvijapuṅgavāḥ
anyonyaṃ sasmitaṃ prekṣya cāliliṅguḥ samantataḥ
nirudhya mārgaṃ rudrasya naipuṇāni pracakrire
ko bhavāniti cāhustaṃ āsyatāmiti cāparāḥ
kutretyatha prasīdeti jajalpuḥ prītamānasāḥ
viparītā nipeturvai visrastāṃśukamūrdhajāḥ
pativratāḥ patīnāṃ tu saṃnidhau bhavamāyayā
dṛṣṭvā śrutvā bhavastāsāṃ ceṣṭāvākyāni cāvyayaḥ
śubhaṃ vāpyaśubhaṃ vāpi noktavānparameśvaraḥ
dṛṣṭvā nārīkulaṃ viprāstathābhūtaṃ ca śaṅkaram
atīva paruṣaṃ vākyaṃ jajalpuste munīśvarāḥ
tapāṃsi teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratyāhanyanta śaṅkare
yathādityaprakāśena tārakā nabhasi sthitāḥ
śrūyate ṛṣiśāpena brahmaṇastu mahātmanaḥ
samṛddhaśreyasāṃ yoniryajñā vai nāśamāptavān
bhṛgor api ca śāpena viṣṇuḥ paramavīryavān
prādurbhāvāndaśa prāpto duḥkhitaś ca sadā kṛtaḥ
indrasyāpi ca dharmajña chinnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ purā
ṛṣiṇā gautamenorvyāṃ kruddhena vinipātitam
garbhavāso vasūnāṃ ca śāpena vihitas tathā
ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva śāpena nahuṣaḥ sarpatāṃ gataḥ
kṣīrodaś ca samudro 'sau nivāsaḥ sarvadā hareḥ
dvitīyaścāmṛtādhāro hyapeyo brāhmaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ
avimukteśvaraṃ prāpya vārāṇasyāṃ janārdanaḥ
kṣīreṇa cābhiṣicyeśaṃ devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam
śraddhayā parayā yukto dehāśleṣāmṛtena vai
niṣiktena svayaṃ devaḥ kṣīreṇa madhusūdanaḥ
secayitvātha bhagavānbrahmaṇā munibhiḥ samam
kṣīrodaṃ pūrvavaccakre nivāsaṃ cātmanaḥ prabhuḥ
dharmaścaiva tathā śapto māṇḍavyena mahātmanā
vṛṣṇayaścaiva kṛṣṇena durvāsādyairmahātmabhiḥ
rāghavaḥ sānujaś cāpi durvāsena mahātmanā
śrīvatsaś ca muneḥ pādapatanāttasya dhīmataḥ
ete cānye ca bahavo viprāṇāṃ vaśamāgatāḥ
varjayitvā virūpākṣaṃ devadevamumāpatim
evaṃ hi mohitāstena nāvabudhyanta śaṅkaram
atyugravacanaṃ procuścogro 'pyantaradhīyata
te'pi dāruvanāttasmātprātaḥ saṃvignamānasāḥ
pitāmahaṃ mahātmānamāsīnaṃ paramāsane
gatvā vijñāpayāmāsuḥ pravṛttamakhilaṃ vibhoḥ
śubhe dāruvane tasmin munayaḥ kṣīṇacetasaḥ
so'pi saṃcintya manasā kṣaṇādeva pitāmahaḥ
teṣāṃ pravṛttamakhilaṃ puṇye dāruvane purā
utthāya prāñjalirbhūtvā praṇipatya bhavāya ca
uvāca satvaraṃ brahmā munīndāruvanālayān
dhig yuṣmān prāptanidhanān mahānidhim anuttamam
vṛthākṛtaṃ yato viprā yuṣmābhir bhāgyavarjitaiḥ
yastu dāruvane tasmiṃlliṅgī dṛṣṭo'pyaliṅgibhiḥ
yuṣmābhir vikṛtākāraḥ sa eva parameśvaraḥ
gṛhasthaiś ca na nindyāstu sadā hyatithayo dvijāḥ
virūpāś ca surūpāś ca malināścāpyapaṇḍitāḥ
sudarśanena muninā kālamṛtyurapi svayam
purā bhūmau dvijāgryeṇa jito hyatithipūjayā
anyathā nāsti saṃtartuṃ gṛhasthaiś ca dvijottamaiḥ
tyaktvā cātithipūjāṃ tāmātmano bhuvi śodhanam
gṛhastho 'pi purā jetuṃ sudarśana iti śrutaḥ
pratijñāmakarojjāyāṃ bhāryāmāha pativratām
suvrate subhru subhage śṛṇu sarvaṃ prayatnataḥ
tvayā vai nāvamantavyā gṛhe hyatithayaḥ sadā
sarva eva svayaṃ sākṣādatithiryatpinākadhṛk
tasmādatithaye dattvā ātmānamapi pūjaya
evamuktvātha saṃtaptā vivaśā sā pativratā
patimāha rudantī ca kimuktaṃ bhavatā prabho
tasyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā punaḥ prāha sudarśanaḥ
deyaṃ sarvaṃ śivāyārye śiva evātithiḥ svayam
tasmātsarve pūjanīyāḥ sarve'pyatithayaḥ sadā
evamuktā tadā bhartrā bhāryā tasya pativratā
śeṣāmivājñāmādāya mūrdhnā sā prācarattadā
parīkṣituṃ tathā śraddhāṃ tayoḥ sākṣād dvijottamāḥ
dharmo dvijottamo bhūtvā jagāmātha munergṛham
taṃ dṛṣṭvā cārcayāmāsa sārghyādyairanaghā dvijam
sampūjitastayā tāṃ tu prāha dharmo dvijaḥ svayam
bhadre kutaḥ patirdhīmāṃstava bhartā sudarśanaḥ
annādyairalamadyārye svaṃ dātumiha cārhasi
sā ca lajjāvṛtā nārī smarantī kathitaṃ purā
bhartrā nyamīlayannetre cacāla ca pativratā
kiṃcetyāha punastaṃ vai dharme cakre ca sā matim
nivedituṃ kilātmānaṃ tasmai patyurihājñayā
etasminnantare bhartā tasyā nāryāḥ sudarśanaḥ
gṛhadvāraṃ gato dhīmāṃstāmuvāca mahāmuniḥ
ehyehi kva gatā bhadre tamuvācātithiḥ svayam
bhāryayā tvanayā sārdhaṃ maithunastho 'hamadya vai
sudarśana mahābhāga kiṃ kartavyamihocyatām
suratāntastu viprendra saṃtuṣṭo 'haṃ dvijottama
sudarśanastataḥ prāha suprahṛṣṭo dvijottamaḥ
bhuṅkṣva caināṃ yathākāmaṃ gamiṣye 'haṃ dvijottama
hṛṣṭo 'tha darśayāmāsa svātmānaṃ dharmarāṭ svayam
pradadau cepsitaṃ sarvaṃ tamāha ca mahādyutiḥ
eṣā na bhuktā viprendra manasāpi suśobhanā
mayā caiṣā na saṃdehaḥ śraddhāṃ jñātumihāgataḥ
jito vai yastvayā mṛtyurdharmeṇaikena suvrata
aho'sya tapaso vīryamityuktvā prayayau ca saḥ
tasmāttathā pūjanīyāḥ sarve hyatithayaḥ sadā
bahunātra kimuktena bhāgyahīnā dvijottamāḥ
tameva śaraṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ gantumarhatha śaṅkaram
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmaṇo brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥ
brahmāṇamabhivandyārtāḥ procurākulitekṣaṇāḥ
brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ
nāpekṣitaṃ mahābhāga jīvitaṃ vikṛtāḥ striyaḥ
dṛṣṭo'smābhir mahādevo nindito yastvaninditaḥ
śaptaś ca sarvagaḥ śūlī pinākī nīlalohitaḥ
ajñānācchāpajā śaktiḥ kuṇṭhitāsyanirīkṣaṇāt
vaktumarhasi deveśa saṃnyāsaṃ vai krameṇa tu
draṣṭuṃ vai devadeveśamugraṃ bhīmaṃ kapardinam
pitāmaha uvāca
ādau vedānadhītyaiva śraddhayā ca guroḥ sadā
vicāryārthaṃ munerdharmān pratijñāya dvijottamāḥ
grahaṇāntaṃ hi vā vidvānatha dvādaśavārṣikam
snātvāhṛtya ca dārānvai putrānutpādya suvratān
vṛttibhiścānurūpābhistān vibhajya sutānmuniḥ
agniṣṭomādibhiśceṣṭvā yajñairyajñeśvaraṃ vibhum
pūjayet paramātmānaṃ prāpyāraṇyaṃ vibhāvasau
munirdvādaśavarṣaṃ vā varṣamātram athāpi vā
pakṣadvādaśakaṃ vāpi dinadvādaśakaṃ tu vā
kṣīrabhuk saṃyutaḥ śāntaḥ sarvān sampūjayetsurān
iṣṭvaivaṃ juhuyādagnau yajñapātrāṇi mantrataḥ
apsu vai pārthivaṃ nyasya gurave taijasāni tu
svadhanaṃ sakalaṃ caiva brāhmaṇebhyo viśaṅkayā
praṇipatya guruṃ bhūmau viraktaḥ saṃnyasedyatiḥ
nikṛtya keśān saśikhān upavītaṃ visṛjya ca
pañcabhir juhuyād apsu bhūḥ svāheti vicakṣaṇaḥ
tataścordhvaṃ caredevaṃ yatiḥ śivavimuktaye
vratenānaśanenāpi toyavṛttyāpi vā punaḥ
parṇavṛttyā payovṛttyā phalavṛttyāpi vā yatiḥ
evaṃ jīvanmṛto no cet ṣaṇmāsādvatsarāttu vā
prasthānādikamāyāsaṃ svadehasya caredyatiḥ
śivasāyujyamāpnoti karmaṇāpyevamācaran
sadyo 'pi labhate muktiṃ bhaktiyukto dṛḍhavratāḥ
tyāgena vā kiṃ vidhināpyanena bhaktasya rudrasya śubhairvrataiśca
yajñaiś ca dānairvividhaiś ca homairlabdhaiścaśāstrairvividhaiś ca vedaiḥ
śvetenaivaṃ jito mṛtyur bhavabhaktyā mahātmanā
vo'stu bhaktirmahādeve śaṅkare paramātmani
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
evamuktāstadā tena brahmaṇā brāhmaṇarṣabhāḥ
śvetasya ca kathāṃ puṇyām apṛcchan paramarṣayaḥ
pitāmaha uvāca
śveto nāma muniḥ śrīmān gatāyurgirigahvare
sakto hyabhyarcya yadbhaktyā tuṣṭāva ca maheśvaram
rudrādhyāyena puṇyena namasta ityādinā dvijāḥ
tataḥ kālo mahātejāḥ kālaprāptaṃ dvijottamam
netuṃ saṃcintya viprendrāḥ sānnidhyamakaronmuneḥ
śveto'pi dṛṣṭvā taṃ kālaṃ kālaprāpto'pi śaṅkaram
pūjayāmāsa puṇyātmā triyaṃbakamanusmaran
triyaṃbakaṃ yajedevaṃ sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam
kiṃ kariṣyati me mṛtyurmṛtyormṛtyurahaṃ yataḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sasmitaṃ prāha śvetaṃ lokabhayaṃkaraḥ
ehyehi śveta cānena vidhinā kiṃ phalaṃ tava
rudro vā bhagavān viṣṇurbrahmā vā jagadīśvaraḥ
kaḥ samarthaḥ paritrātuṃ mayā grastaṃ dvijottama
anena mama kiṃ vipra raudreṇa vidhinā prabhoḥ
netuṃ yasyotthitaścāhaṃ yamalokaṃ kṣaṇena vai
yasmādgatāyustvaṃ tasmānmune netumihodyataḥ
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhairavaṃ dharmamiśritam
hā rudra rudra rudreti lalāpa munipuṅgavaḥ
taṃ prāha ca mahādevaṃ kālaṃ samprekṣya vai dṛśā
netreṇa bāṣpamiśreṇa saṃbhrāntena samākulaḥ
śveta uvāca
tvayā kiṃ kāla no nāthaścāsti ceddhi vṛṣadhvajaḥ
liṅge 'smin śaṅkaro rudraḥ sarvadevabhavodbhavaḥ
atīva bhavabhaktānāṃ madvidhānāṃ mahātmanām
vidhinā kiṃ mahābāho gaccha gaccha yathāgatam
tato niśamya kupitastīkṣṇadaṃṣṭro bhayaṅkaraḥ
śrutvā śvetasya tadvākyaṃ pāśahasto bhayāvahaḥ
siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā cāsphāṭya ca muhurmuhuḥ
babandha ca muniṃ kālaḥ kālaprāptaṃ tamāha ca
mayā baddho'si viprarṣe śvetaṃ netuṃ yamālayam
adya vai devadevena tava rudreṇa kiṃ kṛtam
kva śarvastava bhaktiś ca kva pūjā pūjayā phalam
kva cāhaṃ kva ca me bhītiḥ śveta baddho'si vai mayā
liṅge'smin saṃsthitaḥ śveta tava rudro maheśvaraḥ
niśceṣṭo'sau mahādevaḥ kathaṃ pūjyo maheśvaraḥ
tataḥ sadāśivaḥ svayaṃ dvijaṃ nihantumāgatam
nihantumantakaṃ smayan smarāriyajñahā haraḥ
tvaran vinirgataḥ paraḥ śivaḥ svayaṃ trilocanaḥ
triyaṃbako 'mbayā samaṃ sanandinā gaṇeśvaraiḥ
sasarja jīvitaṃ kṣaṇād bhavaṃ nirīkṣya vai bhayāt
papāta cāśu vai balī munestu saṃnidhau dvijāḥ
nanāda cordhvamuccadhīrnirīkṣya cāntakāntakam
nirīkṣaṇena vai mṛtaṃ bhavasya viprapuṅgavāḥ
vineduruccamīśvarāḥ sureśvarā maheśvaram
praṇemuraṃbikāmumāṃ munīśvarāstu harṣitāḥ
sasarjur asya mūrdhni vai munerbhavasya khecarāḥ
suśobhanaṃ suśītalaṃ supuṣpavarṣamaṃbarāt
aho nirīkṣya cāntakaṃ mṛtaṃ tadā suvismitaḥ
śilāśanātmajo 'vyayaṃ śivaṃ praṇamya śaṅkaram
uvāca bāladhīrmṛtaḥ prasīda ceti vai muneḥ
maheśvaraṃ maheśvarasya cānugo gaṇeśvaraḥ
tato viveśa bhagavānanugṛhya dvijottamam
kṣaṇādgūḍhaśarīraṃ hi dhvastaṃ dṛṣṭvāntakaṃ kṣaṇāt
tasmānmṛtyuñjayaṃ caiva bhaktyā sampūjaye dvijāḥ
muktidaṃ bhuktidaṃ caiva sarveṣāmapi śaṅkaram
bahunā kiṃ pralāpena saṃnyasyābhyarcya vai bhavam
bhaktyā cāparayā tasmin viśokā vai bhaviṣyatha
śailādiruvāca
evamuktāstadā tena brahmaṇā brahmavādinaḥ
prasīda bhaktirdeveśe bhavedrudre pinākini
kena vā tapasā deva yajñenāpyatha kena vā
vratairvā bhagavadbhaktā bhaviṣyanti dvijātayaḥ
pitāmaha uvāca
na dānena muniśreṣṭhāstapasā ca na vidyayā
yajñair homair vratair vedair yogaśāstrair nirodhanaiḥ
prasāde naiva sā bhaktiḥ śive paramakāraṇe
atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā sarve te paramarṣayaḥ
sadāratanayāḥ śrāntāḥ praṇemuś ca pitāmaham
tasmātpāśupatī bhaktir dharmakāmārthasiddhidā
muner vijayadā caiva sarvamṛtyujayapradā
dadhīcastu purā bhaktyā hariṃ jitvāmarairvibhum
kṣayaṃ jaghāna pādena vajrāsthitvaṃ ca labdhavān
mayāpi nirjito mṛtyurmahādevasya kīrtanāt
śvetenāpi gatenāsyaṃ mṛtyormunivareṇa tu
mahādevaprasādena jito mṛtyuryathā mayā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
kathaṃ bhavaprasādena devadāruvanaukasaḥ
prapannāḥ śaraṇaṃ devaṃ vaktumarhasi me prabho
śailādiruvāca
tānuvāca mahābhāgān bhagavān ātmabhūḥ svayam
devadāruvanasthāṃstu tapasā pāvakaprabhān
pitāmaha uvāca
eṣa devo mahādevo vijñeyastu maheśvaraḥ
na tasmātparamaṃ kiṃcitpadaṃ samadhigamyate
devānāṃ ca ṛṣīnāṃ ca pitṝṇāṃ caiva sa prabhuḥ
sahasrayugaparyante pralaye sarvadehinaḥ
saṃharatyeṣa bhagavān kālo bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ
eṣa caiva prajāḥ sarvāḥ sṛjatyekaḥ svatejasā
eṣa cakrī ca vajrī ca śrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇaḥ
yogī kṛtayuge caiva tretāyāṃ kratur ucyate
dvāpare caiva kālāgnir dharmaketuḥ kalau smṛtaḥ
rudrasya mūrtayastvetā ye 'bhidhyāyanti paṇḍitāḥ
caturasraṃ bahiścāntaraṣṭāsraṃ piṇḍikāśraye
vṛttaṃ sudarśanaṃ yogyamevaṃ liṅgaṃ prapūjayet
tamo hyagnī rajo brahmā sattvaṃ viṣṇuḥ prakāśakam
mūrtirekā sthitā cāsya mūrtayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
yatra tiṣṭhati tadbrahma yogena tu samanvitam
tasmāddhi devadeveśamīśānaṃ prabhumavyayam
ārādhayanti viprendrā jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ
liṅgaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
aṅguṣṭhamātraṃ suśubhaṃ suvṛttaṃ sarvasaṃmatam
samanābhaṃ tathāṣṭāsraṃ ṣoḍaśāsram athāpi vā
suvṛttaṃ maṇḍalaṃ divyaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam
vedikā dviguṇā tasya samā vā sarvasaṃmatā
gomukhī ca tribhāgaikā vedyā lakṣaṇasaṃyutā
paṭṭikā ca samantādvai yavamātrā dvijottamāḥ
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ śailaṃ kṛtvā tāmramayaṃ tathā
vedikāyāś ca vistāraṃ triguṇaṃ vai samantataḥ
vartulaṃ caturasraṃ vā ṣaḍasraṃ vā trirasrakam
samantānnirvraṇaṃ śubhraṃ lakṣaṇaistat sulakṣitam
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ pūjālakṣaṇasaṃyutam
kalaśaṃ sthāpayettasya vedimadhye tathā dvijāḥ
sahiraṇyaṃ sabījaṃ ca brahmabhiś cābhimantritam
secayecca tato liṅgaṃ pavitraiḥ pañcabhiḥ śubhaiḥ
pūjayecca yathālābhaṃ tataḥ siddhimavāpsyatha
samāhitāḥ pūjayadhvaṃ saputrāḥ saha bandhubhiḥ
sarve prāñjalayo bhūtvā śūlapāṇiṃ prapadyata
tato drakṣyatha deveśaṃ durdarśamakṛtātmabhiḥ
yaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvamajñānamadharmaś ca praṇaśyati
tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā brahmāṇamamitaujasam
samprasthitā vanaukāste devadāruvanaṃ tataḥ
ārādhayitumārabdhā brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā
sthaṇḍileṣu vicitreṣu parvatānāṃ guhāsu ca
nadīnāṃ ca vivikteṣu pulineṣu śubheṣu ca
śaivālaśobhanāḥ kecitkecidantarjaleśayāḥ
keciddarbhāvakāśāstu pādāṅguṣṭhāgradhiṣṭhitāḥ
dantolūkhalinastvanye aśmakuṭṭās tathā pare
sthānavīrāsanāstvanye mṛgacaryāratāḥ pare
kālaṃ nayanti tapasā pūjayā ca mahādhiyaḥ
evaṃ saṃvatsare pūrṇe vasante samupasthite
tatasteṣāṃ prasādārthaṃ bhaktānām anukampayā
devaḥ kṛtayuge tasmingirau himavataḥ śubhe
devadāruvanaṃ prāptaḥ prasannaḥ parameśvaraḥ
bhasmapāṃsūpadigdhāṅgo nagno vikṛtalakṣaṇaḥ
ulmukavyagrahastaś ca raktapiṅgalalocanaḥ
kvacicca hasate raudraṃ kvacidgāyati vismitaḥ
kvacinnṛtyati śṛṅgāraṃ kvacidrauti muhurmuhuḥ
āśrame hyaṭate bhaikṣyaṃ yācate ca punaḥ punaḥ
māyāṃ kṛtvā tathārūpāṃ devastadvanam āgataḥ
tataste munayaḥ sarve tuṣṭuvuś ca samāhitāḥ
adbhir vividhamālyaiś ca dhūpairgandhaistathaiva ca
sapatnīkā mahābhāgāḥ saputrāḥ saparicchadāḥ
munayaste tathā vāgbhir īśvaraṃ cedam abruvan
ajñānāddevadeveśa yadasmābhir anuṣṭhitam
karmaṇā manasā vācā tatsarvaṃ kṣantumarhasi
caritāni vicitrāṇi guhyāni gahanāni ca
brahmādīnāṃ ca devānāṃ durvijñeyāni te hara
agatiṃ te na jānīmo gatiṃ naiva ca naiva ca
viśveśvara mahādeva yo'si so'si namo'stu te
stuvanti tvāṃ mahātmāno devadevaṃ maheśvaram
namo bhavāya bhavyāya bhāvanāyodbhavāya ca
anantabalavīryāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ
saṃhartre ca piśaṅgāya avyayāya vyayāya ca
gaṅgāsaliladhārāya ādhārāya guṇātmane
tryaṃbakāya trinetrāya triśūlavaradhāriṇe
kandarpāya hutāśāya namo'stu paramātmane
śaṅkarāya vṛṣāṅkāya gaṇānāṃ pataye namaḥ
daṇḍahastāya kālāya pāśahastāya vai namaḥ
vedamantrapradhānāya śatajihvāya vai namaḥ
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ ca yat
tava dehātsamutpannaṃ deva sarvamidaṃ jagat
pāsi haṃsi ca bhadraṃ te prasīda bhagavaṃstataḥ
ajñānādyadi vijñānād yat kiṃcit kurute naraḥ
tatsarvaṃ bhagavāneva kurute yogamāyayā
evaṃ stutvā tu munayaḥ prahṛṣṭairantarātmabhiḥ
yācanta tapasā yuktāḥ paśyāmastvāṃ yathāpurā
tato devaḥ prasannātmā svamevāsthāya śaṅkaraḥ
rūpaṃ tryakṣaṃ ca saṃdraṣṭuṃ divyaṃ cakṣuradātprabhuḥ
labdhadṛṣṭyā tayā dṛṣṭvā devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam
punastuṣṭuvurīśānaṃ devadāruvanaukasaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ekatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
namo digvāsase nityaṃ kṛtāntāya triśūline
vikaṭāya karālāya karālavadanāya ca
arūpāya surūpāya viśvarūpāya te namaḥ
kaṭaṅkaṭāya rudrāya svāhākārāya vai namaḥ
sarvapraṇatadehāya svayaṃ ca praṇatātmane
nityaṃ nīlaśikhaṇḍāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namonamaḥ
nīlakaṇṭhāya devāya citābhasmāṅgadhāriṇe
tvaṃ brahmā sarvadevānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ nīlalohitaḥ
ātmā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ sāṃkhyaiḥ puruṣa ucyate
parvatānāṃ mahāmerurnakṣatrāṇāṃ ca candramāḥ
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca vasiṣṭhas tvaṃ devānāṃ vāsavas tathā
oṅkāraḥ sarvavedānāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ sāma ca sāmasu
āraṇyānāṃ paśūnāṃ ca siṃhastvaṃ parameśvaraḥ
grāmyāṇāmṛṣabhaścāsi bhagavāṃllokapūjitaḥ
sarvathā vartamāno'pi yo yo bhāvo bhaviṣyati
tvāmeva tatra paśyāmo brahmaṇā kathitaṃ tathā
kāmaḥ krodhaś ca lobhaś ca viṣādo mada eva ca
etad icchāmahe boddhuṃ prasīda parameśvara
mahāsaṃharaṇe prāpte tvayā deva kṛtātmanā
karaṃ lalāṭe saṃvidhya vahnirutpāditastvayā
tenāgninā tadā lokā arcirbhiḥ sarvato vṛtāḥ
tasmādagnisamā hyete bahavo vikṛtāgnayaḥ
kāmaḥ krodhaś ca lobhaś ca moho dambha upadravaḥ
yāni cānyāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca
dahyante prāṇinaste tu tvatsamutthena vahninā
asmākaṃ dahyamānānāṃ trātā bhava sureśvara
tvaṃ ca lokahitārthāya bhūtāni pariṣiñcasi
maheśvara mahābhāga prabho śubhanirīkṣaka
ājñāpaya vayaṃ nātha kartāro vacanaṃ tava
bhūtakoṭisahasreṣu rūpakoṭiśateṣu ca
antaṃ gantuṃ na śaktāḥ sma devadeva namo 'stu te
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
nandyuvāca
tatastutoṣa bhagavān anugṛhya maheśvaraḥ
stutiṃ śrutvā stutasteṣāmidaṃ vacanamabravīt
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi yuṣmābhiḥ kīrtitaṃ stavam
śrāvayedvā dvijānvipro gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
vakṣyāmi vo hitaṃ puṇyaṃ bhaktānāṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
strīliṅgamakhilaṃ devī prakṛtirmama dehajā
puṃlliṅgaṃ puruṣo viprā mama dehasamudbhavaḥ
ubhābhyāmeva vai sṛṣṭirmama viprā na saṃśayaḥ
na nindedyatinaṃ tasmāddigvāsasamanuttamam
bālonmattaviceṣṭaṃ tu matparaṃ brahmavādinam
ye hi māṃ bhasmaniratā bhasmanā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
yathoktakāriṇo dāntā viprā dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
mahādevaparā nityaṃ caranto hyūrdhvaretasaḥ
arcayanti mahādevaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃyatāḥ
rudralokamanuprāpya na nivartanti te punaḥ
tasmādetadvrataṃ divyamavyaktaṃ vyaktaliṅginaḥ
bhasmavratāś ca muṇḍāś ca vratino viśvarūpiṇaḥ
na tānparivadedvidvānna caitānnābhilaṅghayet
na hasennāpriyaṃ brūyādamutreha hitārthavān
yastānnindati mūḍhātmā mahādevaṃ sa nindati
yas tvetān pūjayen nityaṃ sa pūjayati śaṅkaram
evameṣa mahādevo lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
yuge yuge mahāyogī krīḍate bhasmaguṇṭhitaḥ
evaṃ carata bhadraṃ vastataḥ siddhimavāpsyatha
atulamiha mahābhayapraṇāśahetuṃ śivakathitaṃ paramaṃ padaṃ viditvā
vyapagatabhavalobhamohacittāḥ praṇipatitāḥ sahasā śirobhir ugram
tataḥ pramuditā viprāḥ śrutvaivaṃ kathitaṃ tadā
gandhodakaiḥ suśuddhaiś ca kuśapuṣpavimiśritaiḥ
snāpayanti mahākumbhair adbhir eva maheśvaram
gāyanti vividhairguhyair huṃkāraiścāpi susvaraiḥ
namo devādhidevāya mahādevāya vai namaḥ
ardhanārīśarīrāya sāṃkhyayogapravartine
meghavāhanakṛṣṇāya gajacarmanivāsine
kṛṣṇājinottarīyāya vyālayajñopavītine
suracitasuvicitrakuṇḍalāya suracitamālyavibhūṣaṇāya tubhyam
mṛgapativaracarmavāsase ca prathitayaśase namo 'stu śaṅkarāya
tatas tān sa munīn prītaḥ pratyuvāca maheśvaraḥ
prīto 'smi tapasā yuṣmān varaṃ vṛṇuta suvratāḥ
tataste munayaḥ sarve praṇipatya maheśvaram
bhṛgvaṅgirā vasiṣṭhaś ca viśvāmitrastathaiva ca
gautamo 'triḥ sukeśaś ca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
marīciḥ kaśyapaḥ kaṇvaḥ saṃvartaś ca mahātapāḥ
te praṇamya mahādevamidaṃ vacanamabruvan
bhasmasnānaṃ ca nagnatvaṃ vāmatvaṃ pratilomatā
sevyāsevyatvamevaṃ ca hyetadicchāma veditum
tatasteṣāṃ vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavānparameśvaraḥ
sasmitaṃ prāha samprekṣya sarvānmunivarāṃstadā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ṛṣivākyaṃ nāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
etadvaḥ sampravakṣyāmi kathā sarvasvamadya vai
agnirhyahaṃ somakartā somaścāgnimupāśritaḥ
kṛtametadvahatyagnirbhūyo lokasamāśrayāt
asakṛttvagninā dagdhaṃ jagat sthāvarajaṅgamam
bhasmasādvihitaṃ sarvaṃ pavitramidamuttamam
bhasmanā vīryamāsthāya bhūtāni pariṣiñcati
agnikāryaṃ ca yaḥ kṛtvā kariṣyati triyāyuṣam
bhasmanā mama vīryeṇa mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
bhāsata ityeva yadbhasma śubhaṃ bhāvayate ca yat
bhakṣaṇāt sarvapāpānāṃ bhasmeti parikīrtitam
ūṣmapāḥ pitaro jñeyā devā vai somasaṃbhavāḥ
agnīṣomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam
ahamagnirmahātejāḥ somaścaiṣā mahāṃbikā
ahamagniś ca somaś ca prakṛtyā puruṣaḥ svayam
tasmādbhasma mahābhāgā madvīryamiti cocyate
svavīryaṃ vapuṣā caiva dhārayāmīti vai sthitiḥ
tadāprabhṛti lokeṣu rakṣārthamaśubheṣu ca
bhasmanā kriyate rakṣā sūtikānāṃ gṛheṣu ca
bhasmasnānaviśuddhātmā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ
matsamīpaṃ samāgamya na bhūyo vinivartate
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kāpilaṃ caiva nirmitam
pūrvaṃ pāśupataṃ hyetannirmitaṃ tadanuttamam
śeṣāścāśramiṇaḥ sarve paścātsṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā
sṛṣṭireṣā mayā sṛṣṭā lajjāmohabhayātmikā
nagnā eva hi jāyante devatā munayas tathā
ye cānye mānavā loke sarve jāyantyavāsasaḥ
indriyairajitairnagno dukūlenāpi saṃvṛtaḥ
taireva saṃvṛtairgupto na vastraṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtam
kṣamā dhṛtirahiṃsā ca vairāgyaṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ
tulyau mānāvamānau ca tadāvaraṇamuttamam
bhasmasnānena digdhāṅgo dhyāyate manasā bhavam
yadyakāryasahasrāṇi kṛtvā yaḥ snāti bhasmanā
tatsarvaṃ dahate bhasma yathāgnistejasā vanam
tasmād yatnaparo bhūtvā trikālamapi yaḥ sadā
bhasmanā kurute snānaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ sa gacchati
samāhṛtya kratūn sarvāngṛhītvā vratamuttamam
dhyāyanti ye mahādevaṃ līlāsadbhāvabhāvitāḥ
uttareṇāryapanthānaṃ te 'mṛtatvamavāpnuyuḥ
dakṣiṇena ca panthānaṃ ye śmaśānāni bhejire
aṇimā garimā caiva laghimā prāptireva ca
icchā kāmāvasāyitvaṃ tathā prākāmyameva ca
īkṣaṇena ca panthānaṃ ye śmaśānāni bhejire
aṇimā garimā caiva laghimā prāptireva ca
indrādayas tathā devāḥ kāmikavratamāsthitāḥ
aiśvaryaṃ paramaṃ prāpya sarve prathitatejasaḥ
vyapagatamadamohamuktarāgas tamorajodoṣavivarjitasvabhāvaḥ
paribhavamidamuttamaṃ viditvā paśupatiyogaparo bhavetsadaiva
imaṃ pāśupataṃ dhyāyan sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
yaḥ paṭhecca śucirbhūtvā śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati
te sarve munayaḥ śrutvā vasiṣṭhādyā dvijottamāḥ
bhasmapāṇḍuradigdhāṅgā babhūvurvigataspṛhāḥ
rudralokāya kalpānte saṃsthitāḥ śivatejasā
tasmānna nindyāḥ pūjyāśca vikṛtā malinā api
rūpānvitāś ca viprendrāḥ sadā yogīndraśaṅkayā
bahunā kiṃ pralāpena bhavabhaktā dvijottamāḥ
saṃpūjyāḥ sarvayatnena śivavannātra saṃśayaḥ
malināścaiva viprendrā bhavabhaktā dṛḍhavratāḥ
dadhīcastu yathā devadevaṃ jitvā vyavasthitaḥ
nārāyaṇaṃ tathā loke rudrabhaktyā na saṃśayaḥ
tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhasmadigdhatanūruhāḥ
jaṭino muṇḍinaścaiva nagnā nānāprakāriṇaḥ
saṃpūjyāḥ śivavannityaṃ manasā karmaṇā girā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge yogipraśaṃsā nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
kathaṃ jaghāna rājānaṃ kṣupaṃ pādena suvrata
dadhīcaḥ samare jitvā devadevaṃ janārdanam
vajrāsthitvaṃ kathaṃ lebhe mahādevānmahātapāḥ
vaktumarhasi śailāde jito mṛtyustvayā yathā
śailādiruvāca
brahmaputro mahātejā rājā kṣupa iti smṛtaḥ
abhūnmitro dadhīcasya munīndrasya janeśvaraḥ
cirāttayoḥ prasaṃgādvai vādaḥ kṣupadadhīcayoḥ
abhavat kṣatriyaśreṣṭho vipra eveti viśrutaḥ
aṣṭānāṃ lokapālānāṃ vapurdhārayate nṛpaḥ
tasmādindro hyayaṃ vahniryamaś ca nirṛtis tathā
varuṇaścaiva vāyuś ca somo dhanada eva ca
īśvaro 'haṃ na saṃdeho nāvamantavya eva ca
mahatī devatā yā sā mahataścāpi suvrata
tasmāttvayā mahābhāga cyāvaneya sadā hyaham
nāvamantavya eveha pūjanīyaś ca sarvathā
śrutvā tathā mataṃ tasya kṣupasya munisattamaḥ
dadhīcaś cyāvaniś cogro gauravādātmano dvijaḥ
atāḍayatkṣupaṃ mūrdhni dadhīco vāmamuṣṭinā
cicheda vajreṇa ca taṃ dadhīcaṃ balavān kṣupaḥ
brahmaloke purāsau hi brahmaṇaḥ kṣutasaṃbhavaḥ
labdhaṃ vajraṃ ca kāryārthaṃ vajriṇā coditaḥ prabhuḥ
svecchayaiva naro bhūtvā narapālo babhūva saḥ
tasmādrājā sa viprendramajayadvai mahābalaḥ
yathā vajradharaḥ śrīmānbalavāṃstamasānvitaḥ
papāta bhūmau nihato vajreṇa dvijapuṅgavaḥ
sasmāra ca tadā tatra duḥkhādvai bhārgavaṃ munim
śukro'pi saṃdhayāmāsa tāḍitaṃ kuliśena tam
yogādetya dadhīcasya dehaṃ dehabhṛtāṃvaraḥ
saṃdhāya pūrvavaddehaṃ dadhīcasyāha bhārgavaḥ
bho dadhīca mahābhāga devadevamumāpatim
sampūjya pūjyaṃ brahmādyairdevadevaṃ nirañjanam
avadhyo bhava viprarṣe prasādāttryambakasya tu
mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ tasmāllabdhametanmayā dvija
nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ śaṃbhorbhaktānāmiha sarvataḥ
mṛtasaṃjīvanaṃ cāpi śaivamadya vadāmi te
triyaṃbakaṃ yajāmahe trailokyapitaraṃ prabhum
trimaṇḍalasya pitaraṃ triguṇasya maheśvaram
tritattvasya trivahneś ca tridhābhūtasya sarvataḥ
trivedasya mahādevaṃ sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam
sarvabhūteṣu sarvatra triguṇe prakṛtau tathā
indriyeṣu tathānyeṣu deveṣu ca gaṇeṣu ca
puṣpeṣu gandhavatsūkṣmaḥ sugandhiḥ parameśvaraḥ
puṣṭiś ca prakṛtiryasmātpuruṣasya dvijottama
mahadādiviśeṣāntavikalpasyāpi suvrata
viṣṇoḥ pitāmahasyāpi munīnāṃ ca mahāmune
indrasyāpi ca devānāṃ tasmādvai puṣṭivardhanaḥ
taṃ devamamṛtaṃ rudraṃ karmaṇā tapasā tathā
svādhyāyena ca yogena dhyānena ca yajāmahe
satyenānena mukṣīyān mṛtyupāśād bhavaḥ svayam
bandhamokṣakaro yasmādurvārukamiva prabhuḥ
mṛtasaṃjīvano mantro mayā labdhastu śaṅkarāt
japtvā hutvābhimantryaivaṃ jalaṃ pītvā divāniśam
liṅgasya saṃnidhau dhyātvā nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ dvija
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tapasārādhya śaṅkaram
vajrāsthitvam avadhyatvam adīnatvaṃ ca labdhavān
evamārādhya deveśaṃ dadhīco munisattamaḥ
prāpyāvadhyatvamanyaiś ca vajrāsthitvaṃ prayatnataḥ
atāḍayacca rājendraṃ pādamūlena mūrdhani
kṣupo dadhīcaṃ vajreṇa jaghānorasi ca prabhuḥ
nābhūnnāśāya tadvajraṃ dadhīcasya mahātmanaḥ
prabhāvātparameśasya vajrabaddhaśarīriṇaḥ
dṛṣṭvāpyavadhyatvamadīnatāṃ ca kṣupo dadhīcasya tadā prabhāvam
ārādhayāmāsa hariṃ mukundamindrānujaṃ prekṣya tadāṃbujākṣam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge kṣupābidhanṛpaparābhavavarṇanaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
nandyuvāca
pūjayā tasya saṃtuṣṭo bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ
śrībhūmisahitaḥ śrīmāñśaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ
kirīṭī padmahastaś ca sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
pītāṃbaraś ca bhagavāndevairdaityaiś ca saṃvṛtaḥ
pradadau darśanaṃ tasmai divyaṃ vai garuḍadhvajaḥ
divyena darśanenaiva dṛṣṭvā devaṃ janārdanam
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhiḥ praṇamya garuḍadhvajam
tvamādistvamanādiś ca prakṛtistvaṃ janārdanaḥ
puruṣastvaṃ jagannātho viṣṇurviśveśvaro bhavān
yo'yaṃ brahmāsi puruṣo viśvamūrtiḥ pitāmahaḥ
tattvamādyaṃ bhavāneva paraṃ jyotirjanārdana
paramātmā paraṃ dhāma śrīpate bhūpate prabho
tvatkrodhasaṃbhavo rudrastamasā ca samāvṛtaḥ
tvatprasādājjagaddhātā rajasā ca pitāmahaḥ
tvatprasādātsvayaṃ viṣṇuḥ sattvena puruṣottamaḥ
kālamūrte hare viṣṇo nārāyaṇa jaganmaya
mahāṃs tathā ca bhūtādistanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca
tvayaivādhiṣṭhitānyeva viśvamūrte maheśvara
mahādeva jagannātha pitāmaha jagadguro
prasīda devadeveśa prasīda parameśvara
prasīda tvaṃ jagannātha śaraṇyaṃ śaraṇaṃ gataḥ
vaikuṇṭha śaure sarvajña vāsudeva mahābhuja
saṃkarṣaṇa mahābhāga pradyumna puruṣottama
aniruddha mahāviṣṇo sadā viṣṇo namo 'stu te
viṣṇo tavāsanaṃ divyamavyaktaṃ madhyato vibhuḥ
sahasraphaṇasaṃyuktastamomūrtirdharādharaḥ
adhaś ca dharmo deveśa jñānaṃ vairāgyameva ca
aiśvaryamāsanasyāsya pādarūpeṇa suvrata
saptapātālapādastvaṃ dharājaghanameva ca
vāsāṃsi sāgarāḥ sapta diśaścaiva mahābhujāḥ
dyaurmūrdhā te vibho nābhiḥ khaṃ vāyurnāsikāṃ gataḥ
netre somaś ca sūryaś ca keśā vai puṣkarādayaḥ
nakṣatratārakā dyauś ca graiveyakavibhūṣaṇam
kathaṃ stoṣyāmi deveśaṃ pūjyaś ca puruṣottamaḥ
śraddhayā ca kṛtaṃ divyaṃ yac chrutaṃ yacca kīrtitam
yadiṣṭaṃ tatkṣamasveśa nārāyaṇa namo 'stu te
śailādiruvāca
idaṃ tu vaiṣṇavaṃ stotraṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi kṣupeṇa parikīrtitam
śrāvayedvā dvijān bhaktyā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati
sampūjya caivaṃ tridaśeśvarādyaiḥ stutvā stutaṃ devamajeyamīśam
vijñāpayāmāsa nirīkṣya bhaktyā janārdanāya praṇipatya mūrdhnā
rājovāca
bhagavanbrāhmaṇaḥ kaściddadhīca iti viśrutaḥ
dharmavettā vinītātmā sakhā mama purābhavat
avadhyaḥ sarvadā sarvaiḥ śaṅkarārcanatatparaḥ
sāvajñaṃ vāmapādena sa māṃ mūrdhni sadasyatha
tāḍayāmāsa deveśa viṣṇo viśvajagatpate
uvāca ca madāviṣṭo na bibhemīti sarvataḥ
jetumicchāmi taṃ vipraṃ dadhīcaṃ jagadīśvara
yathā hitaṃ tathā kartuṃ tvamarhasi janārdana
śailādiruvāca
jñātvā so'pi dadhīcasya hyavadhyatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
sasmāra ca maheśasya prabhāvamatulaṃ hariḥ
evaṃ smṛtvā hariḥ prāha brahmaṇaḥ kṣutasaṃbhavam
viprāṇāṃ nāsti rājendra bhayametya maheśvaram
viśeṣādrudrabhaktānāmabhayaṃ sarvadā nṛpa
nīcānāmapi sarvatra dadhīcasyāsya kiṃ punaḥ
tasmāttava mahābhāga vijayo nāsti bhūpate
duḥkhaṃ karomi viprasya śāpārthaṃ sasurasya me
bhavitā tasya śāpena dakṣayajñe suraiḥ samam
vināśo mama rājendra punarutthānameva ca
tasmātsametya viprendraṃ sarvayatnena bhūpate
karomi yatnaṃ rājendra dadhīcavijayāya te
śailādiruvāca
śrutvā vākyaṃ kṣupaḥ prāha tathāstviti janārdanam
bhagavānapi viprasya dadhīcasyāśramaṃ yayau
āsthāya rūpaṃ viprasya bhagavān bhaktavatsalaḥ
dadhīcamāha brahmarṣimabhivandya jagadguruḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
bhobho dadhīca brahmarṣe bhavārcanaratāvyaya
varamekaṃ vṛṇe tvattastaṃ bhavāndātumarhati
yācito devadevena dadhīcaḥ prāha viṣṇunā
jñātaṃ tavepsitaṃ sarvaṃ na bibhemi tavāpyaham
bhavān viprasya rūpeṇa āgato 'si janārdana
bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ deveśa vartamānaṃ janārdana
jñātaṃ prasādādrudrasya dvijatvaṃ tyaja suvrata
ārādhito'si deveśa kṣupeṇa madhusūdana
jāne tavaināṃ bhagavanbhaktavatsalatāṃ hare
sthāne tavaiṣā bhagavanbhaktavātsalyatā hare
asti cedbhagavan bhītirbhavārcanaratasya me
vaktumarhasi yatnena varadāṃbujalocana
vadāmi na mṛṣā tasmānna bibhemi janārdana
na bibhemi jagatyasmin devadaityadvijādapi
nandyuvāca
śrutvā vākyaṃ dadhīcasya tadāsthāya janārdanaḥ
svarūpaṃ sasmitaṃ prāha saṃtyajya dvijatāṃ kṣaṇāt
śrībhagavānuvāca
bhayaṃ dadhīca sarvatra nāstyeva tava suvrata
bhavārcanarato yasmādbhavān sarvajña eva ca
bibhemīti sakṛdvaktuṃ tvamarhasi namastava
niyogānmama viprendra kṣupaṃ prati sadasyatha
evaṃ śrutvāpi tadvākyaṃ sāntvaṃ viṣṇormahāmuniḥ
na bibhemīti taṃ prāha dadhīco devasattamam
prabhāvāddevadevasya śaṃbhoḥ sākṣātpinākinaḥ
śarvasya śaṅkarasyāsya sarvajñasya mahāmuniḥ
tatastasya muneḥ śrutvā vacanaṃ kupito hariḥ
cakramudyamya bhagavāndidhakṣurmunisattamam
abhavatkuṇṭhitāgraṃ hi viṣṇoścakraṃ sudarśanam
prabhāvāddhi dadhīcasya kṣupasyaiva hi saṃnidhau
dṛṣṭvā tatkuṇṭhitāgraṃ hi cakraṃ cakriṇamāha saḥ
dadhīcaḥ sasmitaṃ sākṣāt sadasadvyaktikāraṇam
bhagavan bhavatā labdhaṃ purātīva sudāruṇam
sudarśanamiti khyātaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇo prayatnataḥ
bhavasyaitacchubhaṃ cakraṃ na jighāṃsati māmiha
brahmāstrādyaistathānyairhi prayatnaṃ kartumarhasi
śailādiruvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā nirvīryamāyudham
sasarja ca punastasmai sarvāstrāṇi samantataḥ
cakrurdevāstatastasya viṣṇoḥ sāhāyyamavyayāḥ
dvijenaikena yoddhuṃ hi pravṛttasya mahābalāḥ
kuśamuṣṭiṃ tadādāya dadhīcaḥ saṃsmaranbhavam
sasarja sarvadevebhyo vajrāsthiḥ sarvato vaśī
divyaṃ triśūlam abhavat kālāgnisadṛśaprabham
dagdhuṃ devānmatiṃ cakre yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ
indranārāyaṇādyaiś ca devaistyaktāni yāni tu
āyudhāni samastāni praṇemus triśikhaṃ mune
devāś ca dudruvuḥ sarve dhvastavīryā dvijottama
sasarja bhagavān viṣṇuḥ svadehātpuruṣottamaḥ
ātmanaḥ sadṛśān divyāṃllakṣalakṣāyutān gaṇān
tāni sarvāṇi sahasā dadāha munisattamaḥ
tato vismayanārthāya viśvamūrtirabhūddhariḥ
tasya dehe hareḥ sākṣādapaśyaddvijasattamaḥ
dadhīco bhagavānvipraḥ devatānāṃ gaṇān pṛthak
rudrāṇāṃ koṭayaścaiva gaṇānāṃ koṭayastadā
aṇḍānāṃ koṭayaścaiva viśvamūrtestanau tadā
dṛṣṭvaitadakhilaṃ tatra cyāvanir vismitaṃ tadā
viṣṇumāha jagannāthaṃ jaganmayamajaṃ vibhum
aṃbhasābhyukṣya taṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvarūpaṃ mahāmuniḥ
māyāṃ tyaja mahābāho pratibhāsā vicārataḥ
vijñānānāṃ sahasrāṇi durvijñeyāni mādhava
mayi paśya jagat sarvaṃ tvayā sārdham anindita
brahmāṇaṃ ca tathā rudraṃ divyāṃ dṛṣṭiṃ dadāmi te
ityuktvā darśayāmāsa svatanau nikhilaṃ muniḥ
taṃ prāha ca hariṃ devaṃ sarvadevabhavodbhavam
māyayā hyanayā kiṃ vā mantraśaktyātha vā prabho
vastuśaktyātha vā viṣṇo dhyānaśaktyātha vā punaḥ
tyaktvā māyāmimāṃ tasmādyoddhumarhasi yatnataḥ
evaṃ tasya vacaḥ śrutvā dṛṣṭvā māhātmyamadbhutam
devāś ca dudruvurbhūyo devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ ca tam
vārayāmāsa niśceṣṭaṃ padmayonirjagadguruḥ
niśamya vacanaṃ tasya brahmaṇastena nirjitaḥ
jagāma bhagavān viṣṇuḥ praṇipatya mahāmunim
kṣupo duḥkhāturo bhūtvā sampūjya ca munīśvaram
dadhīcamabhivandyāśu prārthayāmāsa viklavaḥ
dadhīca kṣamyatāṃ deva mayājñānātkṛtaṃ sakhe
viṣṇunā hi surairvāpi rudrabhaktasya kiṃ tava
prasīda parameśāna durlabhā durjanairdvija
bhaktirbhaktimatāṃ śreṣṭha madvidhaiḥ kṣatriyādhamaiḥ
śrutvānugṛhya taṃ vipro dadhīcastapatāṃ varaḥ
rājānaṃ muniśārdūlaḥ śaśāpa ca surottamān
rudrakopāgninā devāḥ sadevendrā munīśvaraiḥ
dhvastā bhavantu devena viṣṇunā ca samanvitāḥ
prajāpater makhe puṇye dakṣasya sumahātmanaḥ
evaṃ śaptvā kṣupaṃ prekṣya punarāha dvijottamaḥ
devaiś ca pūjyā rājendra nṛpaiś ca vividhairgaṇaiḥ
brāhmaṇā eva rājendra balinaḥ prabhaviṣṇavaḥ
ityuktvā svoṭajaṃ vipraḥ praviveśa mahādyutiḥ
dadhīcamabhivandyaiva jagāma svaṃ nṛpaḥ kṣayam
tadeva tīrthamabhavat sthāneśvaramiti smṛtam
sthāneśvaram anuprāpya śivasāyujyam āpnuyāt
kathitastava saṃkṣepādvivādaḥ kṣubdadhīcayoḥ
prabhāvaś ca dadhīcasya bhavasya ca mahāmune
ya idaṃ kīrtayeddivyaṃ vivādaṃ kṣubdadhīcayoḥ
jitvāpamṛtyuṃ dehānte brahmalokaṃ prayāti saḥ
ya idaṃ kīrtya saṃgrāmaṃ praviśettasya sarvadā
nāsti mṛtyubhayaṃ caiva vijayī ca bhaviṣyati
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge kṣupadadhīcisaṃvādo nāma ṣaṭtriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
bhavānkathamanuprāpto mahādevamumāpatim
śrotumicchāmi tatsarvaṃ vaktumarhasi me prabho
śailādiruvāca
prajākāmaḥ śilādo'bhūtpitā mama mahāmune
so'pyandhaḥ suciraṃ kalaṃ tapastepe suduścaram
tapatastasya tapasā saṃtuṣṭo vajradhṛk prabhuḥ
śilādamāha tuṣṭo'smi varayasva varāniti
tataḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ sahasrākṣaṃ sahāmaraiḥ
provāca muniśārdūla kṛtāñjalipuṭo harim
śilāda uvāca
bhagavandevatārighna sahasrākṣa varaprada
ayonijaṃ mṛtyuhīnaṃ putramicchāmi suvrata
śakra uvāca
putraṃ dāsyāmi viprarṣe yonijaṃ mṛtyusaṃyutam
anyathā te na dāsyāmi mṛtyuhīnā na santi vai
na dāsyati sutaṃ te 'tra mṛtyuhīnamayonijam
pitāmaho'pi bhagavānkimutānye mahāmune
so'pi devaḥ svayaṃ brahmā mṛtyuhīno na ceśvaraḥ
yonijaś ca mahātejāś cāṇḍajaḥ padmasaṃbhavaḥ
maheśvarāṅgajaścaiva bhavānyāstanayaḥ prabhuḥ
