dhyānayajñaratasyāsya tadā saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ
nāsti vijñānināṃ śaucaṃ prāyaścittādi codanā
viśuddhā vidyayā sarve brahmavidyāvido janāḥ
nāsti kriyā ca lokeṣu sukhaṃ duḥkhaṃ vicārataḥ
dharmādharmau japo homo dhyānināṃ saṃnidhiḥ sadā
parānandātmakaṃ liṅgaṃ viśuddhaṃ śivamakṣaram
niṣkalaṃ sarvagaṃ jñeyaṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitam
liṅgaṃ tu dvividhaṃ prāhurbāhyamābhyantaraṃ dvijāḥ
bāhyaṃ sthūlaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sūkṣmamābhyantaraṃ dvijāḥ
karmayajñaratāḥ sthūlāḥ sthūlaliṅgārcane ratāḥ
asatāṃ bhāvanārthāya nānyathā sthūlavigrahaḥ
ādhyātmikaṃ ca yalliṅgaṃ pratyakṣaṃ yasya no bhavet
asau mūḍho bahiḥ sarvaṃ kalpayitvaiva nānyathā
jñānināṃ sūkṣmamamalaṃ bhavetpratyakṣamavyayam
yathā sthūlamayuktānāṃ mṛtkāṣṭhādyaiḥ prakalpitam
artho vicārato nāstītyanye tattvārthavedinaḥ
niṣkalaḥ sakalaśceti sarvaṃ śivamayaṃ tataḥ
vyomaikamapi dṛṣṭaṃ hi śarāvaṃ prati suvratāḥ
pṛthaktvaṃ cāpṛthaktvaṃ ca śaṅkarasyeti cāpare
pratyayārthaṃ hi jagatām ekastho'pi divākaraḥ
eko'pi bahudhā dṛṣṭo jalādhāreṣu suvratāḥ
jantavo divi bhūmau ca sarve vai pāñcabhautikāḥ
tathāpi bahulā dṛṣṭā jātivyaktivibhedataḥ
dṛśyate śrūyate yadyattattadviddhi śivātmakam
bhedo janānāṃ loke'smin pratibhāso vicārataḥ
svapne ca vipulān bhogān bhuktvā martyaḥ sukhī bhavet
duḥkhī ca bhogaṃ duḥkhaṃ ca nānubhūtaṃ vicārataḥ
evamāhustathānye ca sarve vedārthatattvagāḥ
hṛdi saṃsāriṇāṃ sākṣātsakalaḥ parameśvaraḥ
yogināṃ niṣkalo devo jñānināṃ ca jaganmayaḥ
trividhaṃ parameśasya vapurloke praśasyate
niṣkalaṃ prathamaṃ caikaṃ tataḥ sakalaniṣkalam
tṛtīyaṃ sakalaṃ caiva nānyatheti dvijottamāḥ
arcayanti muhuḥ kecitsadā sakalaniṣkalam
sarvajñaṃ hṛdaye kecicchivaliṅge vibhāvasau
sakalaṃ munayaḥ kecitsadā saṃsāravartinaḥ
evamabhyarcayantyeva sadārāḥ sasutā narāḥ
yathā śivas tathā devī yathā devī tathā śivaḥ
tasmādabhedabuddhyaiva saptaviṃśatprabhedataḥ
yajanti dehe bāhye ca catuṣkoṇe ṣaḍasrake
daśāre dvādaśāre ca ṣoḍaśāre trirasrake
sa svecchayā śivaḥ sākṣāddevyā sārdhaṃ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ
saṃtāraṇārthaṃ ca śivaḥ sadasadvyaktivarjitaḥ
tamekamāhurdviguṇaṃ ca kecitkecittamāhustriguṇātmakaṃ ca
ūcus tathā taṃ ca śivaṃ tathānye saṃsāriṇaṃ vedavido vadanti
bhaktyā ca yogena śubhena yuktā viprāḥ sadā dharmaratā viśiṣṭāḥ
yajanti yogeśam aśeṣamūrtiṃ ṣaḍasramadhye bhagavantameva
ye tatra paśyanti śivaṃ trirasre tritattvamadhye triguṇaṃ triyakṣam
te yānti cainaṃ na ca yogino 'nye tayā ca devyā puruṣaṃ purāṇam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivādvaitakathanaṃ nāma pañcasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi svecchāvigrahasaṃbhavam
pratiṣṭhāyāḥ phalaṃ sarvaṃ sarvalokahitāya vai
skandomāsahitaṃ devamāsīnaṃ paramāsane
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt
skandomāsahitaṃ devaṃ sampūjya vidhinā sakṛt
yatphalaṃ labhate martyastadvadāmi yathāśrutam
sūryakoṭipratikāśairvimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ
rudrakanyāsamākīrṇair geyanāṭyasamanvitaiḥ
śivavatkrīḍate yogī yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ
aumaṃ kaumāramaiśānaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmameva ca
prājāpatyaṃ mahātejā janalokaṃ mahas tathā
aindram āsādya caindratvaṃ kṛtvā varṣāyutaṃ punaḥ
bhuktvā caiva bhuvarloke bhogān divyān suśobhanān
merumāsādya devānāṃ bhavaneṣu pramodate
ekapādaṃ caturbāhuṃ trinetraṃ śūlasaṃyutam
sṛṣṭvā sthitaṃ hariṃ vāme dakṣiṇe caturānanam
aṣṭāviṃśatirudrāṇāṃ koṭiḥ sarvāṅgasuprabham
pañcaviṃśatikaṃ sākṣātpuruṣaṃ hṛdayāttathā
prakṛtiṃ vāmataścaiva buddhiṃ vai buddhideśataḥ
ahaṅkāramahaṅkārāttanmātrāṇi tu tatra vai
indriyāṇīndriyādeva līlayā parameśvaram
pṛthivīṃ pādamūlāttu guhyadeśājjalaṃ tathā
nābhideśāt tathā vahniṃ hṛdayādbhāskaraṃ tathā
kaṇṭhātsomaṃ tathātmānaṃ bhrūmadhyānmastakāddivam
sṛṣṭaivaṃ saṃsthitaṃ sākṣājjagatsarvaṃ carācaram
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ devaṃ kṛtvā vidyāvidhānataḥ
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
tripādaṃ saptahastaṃ ca catuḥśṛṅgaṃ dviśīrṣakam
kṛtvā yajñeśamīśānaṃ viṣṇuloke mahīyate
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānkalpalakṣaṃ sukhī naraḥ
kramādāgatya loke 'sminsarvayajñāntago bhavet
vṛṣārūḍhaṃ tu yaḥ kuryātsomaṃ somārdhabhūṣaṇam
hayamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatpuṇyaṃ tad avāpya saḥ
kāñcanena vimānena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ tatraiva sa vimucyate
nandinā sahitaṃ devaṃ sāmbaṃ sarvagaṇairvṛtam
kṛtvā yatphalamāpnoti vakṣye tadvai yathāśrutam
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśair vimānair vṛṣasaṃyutaiḥ
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇair devadānavadurlabhaiḥ
nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghaiḥ sarvataḥ sarvaśobhitaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
nṛtyantaṃ devadeveśaṃ śailajāsahitaṃ prabhum
sahasrabāhuṃ sarvajñaṃ caturbāhum athāpi vā
bhṛgvādyairbhūtasaṃghaiś ca saṃvṛtaṃ parameśvaram
śailajāsahitaṃ sākṣādvṛṣabhadhvajamīśvaram
brahmendraviṣṇusomādyaiḥ sadā sarvairnamaskṛtam
mātṛbhir munibhiścaiva saṃvṛtaṃ parameśvaram
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yatphalaṃ tadvadāmyaham
sarvayajñatapodānatīrthadeveṣu yat phalam
tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ labdhvā yāti śivaṃ padam
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam
sṛṣṭyantare punaḥ prāpte mānavaṃ padamāpnuyāt
nagnaṃ caturbhujaṃ śvetaṃ trinetraṃ sarpamekhalam
kapālahastaṃ deveśaṃ kṛṣṇakuñcitamūrdhajam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
ibhendradārakaṃ devaṃ sāṃbaṃ siddhārthadaṃ prabhum
sudhūmravarṇaṃ raktākṣaṃ trinetraṃ candrabhūṣaṇam
kākapakṣadharaṃ mūrdhnā nāgaṭaṅkadharaṃ haram
siṃhājinottarīyaṃ ca mṛgacarmāṃbaraṃ prabhum
tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ gadāhastaṃ kapālodyatapāṇinam
huṃphaṭkāre mahāśabdaśabditākhiladiṅmukham
puṇḍarīkājinaṃ dorbhyāṃ bibhrantaṃ kambukaṃ tathā
hasantaṃ ca nadantaṃ ca pibantaṃ kṛṣṇasāgaram
nṛtyantaṃ bhūtasaṃghaiś ca gaṇasaṃghais tvalaṃkṛtam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvibhavavistaram
sarvavighnān atikramya śivaloke mahīyate
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam
jñānaṃ vicārato labdhvā rudrebhyastatra mucyate
ardhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ caturbhujamanuttamam
varadābhayahastaṃ ca śūlapadmadharaṃ prabhum
strīpuṃbhāvena saṃsthānaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivaloke mahīyate
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānaṇimādiguṇairyutaḥ
ācandratārakaṃ jñānaṃ tato labdhvā vimucyate
yaḥ kuryāddevadeveśaṃ sarvajñaṃ lakulīśvaram
vṛtaṃ śiṣyapraśiṣyaiś ca vyākhyānodyatapāṇinam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati
bhuktvā tu vipulāṃstatra bhogān yugaśataṃ naraḥ
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya tatraiva ca vimucyate
pūrvadevāmarāṇāṃ ca yatsthānaṃ sakalepsitam
kṛtamudrasya devasya citābhasmānulepinaḥ
tripuṇḍradhāriṇasteṣāṃ śiromālādharasya ca
brahmaṇaḥ keśakenaikamupavītaṃ ca bibhrataḥ
bibhrato vāmahastena kapālaṃ brahmaṇo varam
viṣṇoḥ kalevaraṃ caiva bibhrataḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya mucyate bhavasāgarāt
oṃnamo nīlakaṇṭhāya iti puṇyākṣarāṣṭakam
mantramāha sakṛdvā yaḥ pātakaiḥ sa vimucyate
mantreṇānena gandhādyairbhaktyā vittānusārataḥ
sampūjya devadeveśaṃ śivaloke mahīyate
jālandharāntakaṃ devaṃ sudarśanadharaṃ prabhum
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya dvidhābhūtaṃ jalaṃdharam
prayāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
sudarśanapradaṃ devaṃ sākṣātpūrvoktalakṣaṇam
arcamānena devena cārcitaṃ netrapūjayā
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivaloke mahīyate
tiṣṭhato'tha nikumbhasya pṛṣṭhataścaraṇāṃbujam
vāmetaraṃ suvinyasya vāme cāliṅgya cādrijām
śūlāgre kūrparaṃ sthāpya kiṅkiṇīkṛtapannagam
samprekṣya cāndhakaṃ pārśve kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam
rūpaṃ kṛtvā yathānyāyaṃ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
yaḥ kuryāddevadeveśaṃ tripurāntakamīśvaram
dhanurbāṇasamāyuktaṃ somaṃ somārdhabhūṣaṇam
rathe susaṃsthitaṃ devaṃ caturānanasārathim
tadākāratayā so'pi gatvā śivapuraṃ sukhī
krīḍate nātra saṃdeho dvitīya iva śaṅkaraḥ
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogān yāvad icchā dvijottamāḥ
jñānaṃ vicāritaṃ labdhvā tatraiva sa vimucyate
gaṅgādharaṃ sukhāsīnaṃ candraśekharameva ca
gaṅgayā sahitaṃ caiva vāmotsaṅge 'ṃbikānvitam
vināyakaṃ tathā skandaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ durgāṃ suśobhanām
bhāskaraṃ ca tathā somaṃ brahmāṇīṃ ca maheśvarīm
kaumārīṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ devīṃ vārāhīṃ varadāṃ tathā
indrāṇīṃ caiva cāmuṇḍāṃ vīrabhadrasamanvitām
vighneśena ca yo dhīmān śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
liṅgamūrtiṃ mahājvālāmālāsaṃvṛtam avyayam
liṅgasya madhye vai kṛtvā candraśekharamīśvaram
vyomni kuryāt tathā liṅgaṃ brahmāṇaṃ haṃsarūpiṇam
viṣṇuṃ varāharūpeṇa liṅgasyādhastvadhomukham
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam
madhye liṅgaṃ mahāghoraṃ mahāmbhasi ca saṃsthitam
kṛtvā bhaktyā pratiṣṭhāpya śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
kṣetrasaṃrakṣakaṃ devaṃ tathā pāśupataṃ prabhum
kṛtvā bhaktyā yathānyāyaṃ śivaloke mahīyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivamūrtipratiṣṭhāphalakathanaṃ nāma ṣaṭsaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
liṅgapratiṣṭhāpuṇyaṃ ca liṅgasthāpanameva ca
liṅgānāṃ caiva bhedāś ca śrutaṃ tava mukhādiha
mṛdādiratnaparyantairdravyaiḥ kṛtvā śivālayam
yatphalaṃ labhate martyastatphalaṃ vaktumarhasi
sūta uvāca
yasya bhakto'pi loke'smin putradāragṛhādibhiḥ
bādhyate jñānayuktaścenna ca tasya gṛhaistu kim
tathāpi bhaktāḥ parameśvarasya kṛtveṣṭaloṣṭairapi rudralokam
prayānti divyaṃ hi vimānavaryaṃ surendrapadmodbhavavanditasya
bālyāttu loṣṭena ca kṛtvā mṛdāpi vā pāṃsubhir ādidevam
gṛhaṃ ca tādṛgvidhamasya śaṃbhoḥ sampūjya rudratvamavāpnuvanti
tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhaktyā bhaktaiḥ śivālayam
kartavyaṃ sarvayatnena dharmakāmārthasiddhaye
kesaraṃ nāgaraṃ vāpi drāviḍaṃ vā tathāparam
kṛtvā rudrālayaṃ bhaktyā śivaloke mahīyate
kailāsākhyaṃ ca yaḥ kuryātprāsādaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
kailāsaśikharākārair vimānair modate sukhī
mandaraṃ vā prakurvīta śivāya vidhipūrvakam
bhaktyā vittānusāreṇa uttamādhamamadhyamam
mandarādripratīkāśairvimānairviśvatomukhaiḥ
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇairdevadānavadurlabhaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ ramyaṃ bhuktvā bhogān yathepsitān
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya gāṇapatyaṃ labhennaraḥ
yaḥ kuryānmerunāmānaṃ prāsādaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
sa yatphalamavāpnoti na tat sarvair mahāmakhaiḥ
sarvayajñatapodānatīrthavedeṣu yatphalam
tatphalaṃ sakalaṃ labdhvā śivavanmodate ciram
niṣadhaṃ nāma yaḥ kuryātprāsādaṃ bhaktitaḥ sudhīḥ
śivalokamanuprāpya śivavanmodate ciram
kuryādvā yaḥ śubhaṃ viprā himaśailamanuttamam
himaśailopamair yānair gatvā śivapuraṃ śubham
jñānayogaṃ samāsādya gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
nīlādriśikharākhyaṃ vā prāsādaṃ yaḥ suśobhanam
kṛtvā vittānusāreṇa bhaktyā rudrāya śaṃbhave
yatphalaṃ labhate martyastatphalaṃ pravadāmyaham
himaśaile kṛte bhaktyā yatphalaṃ prāk tavoditam
tatphalaṃ sakalaṃ labdhvā sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ
rudralokamanuprāpya rudraiḥ sārdhaṃ pramodate
mahendraśailanāmānaṃ prāsādaṃ rudrasaṃmatam
kṛtvā yatphalamāpnoti tatphalaṃ pravadāmyaham
mahendraparvatākārairvimānairvṛṣasaṃyutaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ bhuktvā bhogānyathepsitān
jñānaṃ vicāritaṃ rudraiḥ samprāpya munipuṅgavāḥ
viṣayān viṣavat tyaktvā śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
hemnā yastu prakurvīta prāsādaṃ ratnaśobhitam
drāviḍaṃ nāgaraṃ vāpi kesaraṃ vā vidhānataḥ
kūṭaṃ vā maṇḍapaṃ vāpi samaṃ vā dīrgham eva ca
na tasya śakyate vaktuṃ puṇyaṃ śatayugairapi
jīrṇaṃ vā patitaṃ vāpi khaṇḍitaṃ sphuṭitaṃ tathā
pūrvavatkārayedyastu dvārādyaiḥ suśubhaṃ dvijāḥ
prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ vāpi prākāraṃ gopuraṃ tu vā
karturapyadhikaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
vṛttyarthaṃ vā prakurvīta naraḥ karma śivālaye
yaḥ sa yāti na saṃdehaḥ svargalokaṃ sabāndhavaḥ
yaścātmabhogasiddhyarthamapi rudrālaye sakṛt
karma kuryādyadi sukhaṃ labdhvā cāpi pramodate
tasmād āyatanaṃ bhaktyā yaḥ kuryān munisattamāḥ
kāṣṭheṣṭakādibhir martyaḥ śivaloke mahīyate
prasādārthaṃ maheśasya prāsāde munipuṅgavāḥ
kartavyaḥ sarvayatnena dharmakāmārthamuktaye
aśaktaścenmuniśreṣṭhāḥ prāsādaṃ kartumuttamam
saṃmārjanādibhir vāpi sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt
saṃmārjanaṃ tu yaḥ kuryānmārjanyā mṛdusūkṣmayā
cāndrāyaṇasahasrasya phalaṃ māsena labhyate
yaḥ kuryādvastrapūtena gandhagomayavāriṇā
ālepanaṃ yathānyāyaṃ varṣacāndrāyaṇaṃ labhet
ardhakrośaṃ śivakṣetraṃ śivaliṅgātsamantataḥ
yas tyajed dustyajān prāṇāñ śivasāyujyam āpnuyāt
svāyaṃbhuvasya mānaṃ hi tathā bāṇasya suvratāḥ
svāyaṃbhuve tadardhaṃ syāt syād ārṣe ca tadardhakam
mānuṣe ca tadardhaṃ syātkṣetramānaṃ dvijottamāḥ
evaṃ yatīnāmāvāse kṣetramānaṃ dvijottamāḥ
rudrāvatāre cādyaṃ yacchiṣye caiva praśiṣyake
narāvatāre tacchiṣye tacchiṣye ca praśiṣyake
śrīparvate mahāpuṇye tasya prānte ca vā dvijāḥ
tasminvā yastyajetprāṇāñchivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
vārāṇasyāṃ tathāpyevamavimukte viśeṣataḥ
kedāre ca mahākṣetre prayāge ca viśeṣataḥ
kurukṣetre ca yaḥ prāṇānsaṃtyajedyāti nirvṛtim
prabhāse puṣkare 'vantyāṃ tathā caivāmareśvare
vaṇīśailākule caiva mṛto yāti śivātmatām
vārāṇasyāṃ mṛto janturna jātu jantutāṃ vrajet
triviṣṭape vimukte ca kedāre saṃgameśvare
śālaṅke vā tyajetprāṇāṃs tathā vai jambukeśvare
śukreśvare vā gokarṇe bhāskareśe guheśvare
hiraṇyagarbhe nandīśe sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
niyamaiḥ śoṣya yo dehaṃ tyajetkṣetre śivasya tu
sa yāti śivatāṃ yogī mānuṣe daivike'pi vā
ārṣe vāpi muniśreṣṭhās tathā svāyaṃbhuve'pi vā
svayaṃbhūte tathā deve nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
ādhāyāgniṃ śivakṣetre sampūjya parameśvaram
svadehapiṇḍaṃ juhuyādyaḥ sa yāti parāṃ gatim
yāvattāvannirāhāro bhūtvā prāṇān parityajet
śivakṣetre muniśreṣṭhāḥ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
chittvā pādadvayaṃ cāpi śivakṣetre vasettu yaḥ
sa yāti śivatāṃ caiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
kṣetrasya darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ praveśastacchatādhikaḥ
tasmācchataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ sparśanaṃ ca pradakṣiṇam
tasmācchataguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ jalasnānamataḥ param
kṣīrasnānaṃ tato viprāḥ śatādhikamanuttamam
dadhnā sahasramākhyātaṃ madhunā tacchatādhikam
ghṛtasnānena cānantaṃ śārkare tacchatādhikam
śivakṣetrasamīpasthāṃ nadīṃ prāpyāvagāhya ca
tyajeddehaṃ vihāyānnaṃ śivaloke mahīyate
śivakṣetrasamīpasthā nadyaḥ sarvāḥ suśobhanāḥ
vāpīkūpataḍāgāś ca śivatīrthā iti smṛtāḥ
snātvā teṣu naro bhaktyā tīrtheṣu dvijasattamāḥ
brahmahatyādibhiḥ pāpairmucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
prātaḥ snātvā muniśreṣṭhāḥ śivatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ
aśvamedhaphalaṃ prāpya rudralokaṃ sa gacchati
madhyāhne śivatīrtheṣu snātvā bhaktyā sakṛnnaraḥ
gaṅgāsnānasamaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
astaṃ gate tathā cārke snātvā gacchecchivaṃ padam
pāpakañcukamutsṛjya śivatīrtheṣu mānavaḥ
dvijās triṣavaṇaṃ snātvā śivatīrthe sakṛnnaraḥ
śivasāyujyamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
purātha sūkaraḥ kaścit śvānaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhayātpathi
prasaṃgādvāramekaṃ tu śivatīrthe 'vagāhya ca
mṛtaḥ svayaṃ dvijaśreṣṭhā gāṇapatyamavāptavān
yaḥ prātardevadeveśaṃ śivaṃ liṅgasvarūpiṇam
paśyetsa yāti sarvasmādadhikāṃ gatimeva ca
madhyāhne ca mahādevaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajñaphalaṃ labhet
sāyāhne sarvayajñānāṃ phalaṃ prāpya vimucyate
mānasairvācikaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikaiś ca mahattaraiḥ
tathopapātakaiścaiva pāpaiścaivānupātakaiḥ
saṃkrame devamīśānaṃ dṛṣṭvā liṅgākṛtiṃ prabhum
māsena yatkṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tyaktvā yāti śivaṃ padam
ayane cārdhamāsena dakṣiṇe cottarāyaṇe
viṣuve caiva sampūjya prayāti paramāṃ gatim
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kuryādyaḥ prāsādaṃ samantataḥ
savyāpasavyanyāyena mṛdugatyā śucirnaraḥ
pade pade 'śvamedhasya yajñasya phalamāpnuyāt
vācā yastu śivaṃ nityaṃ saṃrauti parameśvaram
so'pi yāti śivaṃ sthānaṃ prāpya kiṃ punareva ca
kṛtvā maṇḍalakaṃ kṣetraṃ gandhagomayavāriṇā
muktāphalamayaiścūrṇairindranīlamayais tathā
padmarāgamayaiścaiva sphāṭikaiś ca suśobhanaiḥ
tathā mārakataiścaiva sauvarṇai rājatais tathā
tadvarṇair laukikaiścaiva cūrṇairvittavivarjitaiḥ
ālikhya kamalaṃ bhadraṃ daśahastapramāṇataḥ
sakarṇikaṃ mahābhāgā mahādevasamīpataḥ
tatrāvāhya mahādevaṃ navaśaktisamanvitam
pañcabhiśca tathā ṣaḍbhir aṣṭābhiśceṣṭadaṃ param
punaraṣṭābhir īśānaṃ daśāre daśabhis tathā
punarbāhye ca daśabhiḥ sampūjya praṇipatya ca
nivedya devadevāya kṣitidānaphalaṃ labhet
śālipiṣṭādibhir vāpi padmamālikhya nirdhanaḥ
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ puṇyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
dvādaśāraṃ tathālikhya maṇḍalaṃ padam uttamam
ratnacūrṇādibhiścūrṇais tathā dvādaśamūrtibhiḥ
maṇḍalasya ca madhye tu bhāskaraṃ sthāpya pūjayet
grahaiś ca saṃvṛtaṃ vāpi sūryasāyujyamuttamam
evaṃ prākṛtam apyārthyāṃ ṣaḍasraṃ parikalpya ca
madhyadeśe ca deveśīṃ prakṛtiṃ brahmarūpiṇīm
dakṣiṇe sattvamūrtiṃ ca vāmataś ca rajoguṇam
agratastu tamomūrtiṃ madhye devīṃ tathāṃbikām
pañcabhūtāni tanmātrāpañcakaṃ caiva dakṣiṇe
karmendriyāṇi pañcaiva tathā buddhīndriyāṇi ca
uttare vidhivatpūjya ṣaḍasre caiva pūjayet
ātmānaṃ cāntarātmānaṃ yugalaṃ buddhimeva ca
ahaṅkāraṃ ca mahatā sarvayajñaphalaṃ labhet
evaṃ vaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ prākṛtaṃ maṇḍalaṃ param
ato vakṣyāmi viprendrāḥ sarvakāmārthasādhanam
gocarmamātramālikhya maṇḍalaṃ gomayena tu
caturaśraṃ vidhānena cādbhir abhyukṣya mantravit
alaṃkṛtya vitānādyaiś chatrair vāpi manoramaiḥ
budbudairardhacandraiś ca haimairaśvatthapatrakaiḥ
sitairvikasitaiḥ padmai raktair nīlotpalais tathā
muktādāmair vitānānte lambitastu sitairdhvajaiḥ
sitamṛtpātrakaiścaiva suślakṣṇaiḥ pūrṇakumbhakaiḥ
phalapallavamālābhir vaijayantībhir aṃśukaiḥ
pañcāśaddīpamālābhir dhūpaiḥ pañcavidhais tathā
pañcāśaddalasaṃyuktamālikhetpadmamuttamam
tattadvarṇais tathā cūrṇaiḥ śvetacūrṇairathāpi vā
ekahastapramāṇena kṛtvā padmaṃ vidhānataḥ
karṇikāyāṃ nyased devaṃ devyā deveśvaraṃ bhavam
varṇāni ca nyasetpatre rudraiḥ prāgādyanukramāt
praṇavādinamo'ntāni sarvavarṇāni suvratāḥ
sampūjyaivaṃ muniśreṣṭhā gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
brāhmaṇān bhojayettatra pañcāśadvidhipūrvakam
akṣamālopavītaṃ ca kuṇḍalaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum
āsanaṃ ca tathā daṇḍamuṣṇīṣaṃ vastrameva ca
dattvā teṣāṃ munīndrāṇāṃ devadevāya śaṃbhave
mahācaruṃ nivedyaivaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ gomithunaṃ tathā
ante ca devadevāya dāpayeccūrṇamaṇḍalam
yāgopayogadravyāṇi śivāya vinivedayet
oṅkārādyaṃ japeddhīmān prativarṇam anukramāt
evamālikhya yo bhaktyā sarvamaṇḍalamuttamam
yatphalaṃ labhate martyastadvadāmi samāsataḥ
sāṅgān vedān yathānyāyam adhītya vidhipūrvakam
iṣṭvā yajñairyathānyāyaṃ jyotiṣṭomādibhiḥ kramāt
tato viśvajidantaiś ca putrānutpādya tādṛśān
vānaprasthāśramaṃ gatvā sadāraḥ sāgnireva ca
cāndrāyaṇādikāḥ sarvāḥ kṛtvā nyasya kriyā dvijāḥ
brahmavidyāmadhītyaiva jñānamāsādya yatnataḥ
jñānena jñeyam ālokya yogī yatkāmamāpnuyāt
tatphalaṃ labhate sarvaṃ varṇamaṇḍaladarśanāt
yena kenāpi vā martyaḥ pralipyāyatanāgrataḥ
uttare dakṣiṇe vāpi pṛṣṭhato vā dvijottamāḥ
catuṣkoṇaṃ tu vā cūrṇair alaṃkṛtya samantataḥ
puṣpākṣatādibhiḥ pūjya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
yastu garbhagṛhaṃ bhaktyā sakṛdālipya sarvataḥ
candanādyaiḥ sakarpūrair gandhadravyaiḥ samantataḥ
vikīrya gandhakusumairdhūpairdhūpya caturvidhaiḥ
prārthayeddevamīśānaṃ śivalokaṃ sa gacchati
tatra bhuktvā mahābhogānkalpakoṭiśataṃ naraḥ
svadehagandhakusumaiḥ pūrayañchivamandiram
kramādgāndharvamāsādya gandharvaiś ca supūjitaḥ
kramādāgatya loke 'smin rājā bhavati vīryavān
ādidevo mahādevaḥ pralayasthitikārakaḥ
sargaś ca bhuvanādhīśaḥ śarvavyāpī sadāśivaḥ
śivabrahmāmṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ mokṣasādhanam uttamam
vyaktāvyaktaṃ sadā nityam acintyam arcayet prabhum
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge upalepanādikathanaṃ nāma saptasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
vastrapūtena toyena kāryaṃ caivopalepanam
śivakṣetre muniśreṣṭhā nānyathā siddhiriṣyate
āpaḥ pūtā bhavantyetā vastrapūtāḥ samuddhṛtāḥ
aphenā muniśārdūlā nādeyāś ca viśeṣataḥ
tasmādvai sarvakāryāṇi daivikāni dvijottamāḥ
adbhiḥ kāryāṇi pūtābhiḥ sarvakāryaprasiddhaye
jantubhir miśritā hyāpaḥ sūkṣmābhistānnihatya tu
yatpāpaṃ sakalaṃ cādbhir apūtābhiś ciraṃ labhet
saṃmārjane tathā nṝṇāṃ mārjane ca viśeṣataḥ
agnau kaṇḍanake caiva peṣaṇe toyasaṃgrahe
hiṃsā sadā gṛhasthānāṃ tasmāddhiṃsāṃ vivarjayet
ahiṃseyaṃ paro dharmaḥ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ dvijāḥ
tasmātsarvaprayatnena vastrapūtaṃ samācaret
taddānamabhayaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvadānottamottamam
tasmāttu parihartavyā hiṃsā sarvatra sarvadā
manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvadāhiṃsakaṃ naram
rakṣanti jantavaḥ sarve hiṃsakaṃ bādhayanti ca
trailokyamakhilaṃ dattvā yatphalaṃ vedapārage
tatphalaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ labhate 'hiṃsako naraḥ
manasā karmaṇā vācā sarvabhūtahite ratāḥ
dayādarśitapanthāno rudralokaṃ vrajanti ca
svāmivatparirakṣanti bahūni vividhāni ca
ye putrapautravatsnehādrudralokaṃ vrajanti te
tasmātsarvaprayatnena vastrapūtena vāriṇā
kāryamabhyukṣaṇaṃ nityaṃ snapanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
trailokyamakhilaṃ hatvā yatphalaṃ parikīrtyate
śivālaye nihatyaikamapi tatsakalaṃ labhet
śivārthaṃ sarvadā kāryā puṣpahiṃsā dvijottamāḥ
yajñārthaṃ paśuhiṃsā ca kṣatriyairduṣṭaśāsanam
vihitāvihitaṃ nāsti yogināṃ brahmavādinām
yatastasmānna hantavyā niṣiddhānāṃ niṣevaṇāt
sarvakarmāṇi vinyasya saṃnyastā brahmavādinaḥ
na hantavyāḥ sadā pūjyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api
pavitrāstu striyaḥ sarvā atreś ca kulasaṃbhavāḥ
brahmahatyāsamaṃ pāpamātreyīṃ vinihatya ca
striyaḥ sarvā na hantavyāḥ pāpakarmaratā api
na yajñārthaṃ striyo grāhyāḥ sarvaiḥ sarvatra sarvadā
sarvavarṇeṣu viprendrāḥ pāpakarmaratā api
malinā rūpavatyaś ca virūpā malināṃbarāḥ
na hantavyāḥ sadā martyaiḥ śivavacchaṅkayā tathā
vedabāhyavratācārāḥ śrautasmārtabahiṣkṛtāḥ
pāṣaṇḍina iti khyātā na saṃbhāṣyā dvijātibhiḥ
na spṛṣṭavyā na draṣṭavyā dṛṣṭvā bhānuṃ samīkṣate
tathāpi tena vadhyāś ca nṛpairanyaiś ca jantubhiḥ
prasaṃgādvāpi yo martyaḥ satāṃ sakṛdaho dvijāḥ
rudralokamavāpnoti samabhyarcya maheśvaram
bhavanti duḥkhitāḥ sarve nirdayā munisattamāḥ
bhaktihīnā narāḥ sarve bhave paramakāraṇe
ye bhaktā devadevasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
bhāgyavanto vimucyante bhuktvā bhogānihaiva te
putreṣu dāreṣu gṛheṣu nṝṇāṃ bhaktaṃ yathā cittamathādideve
sakṛtprasaṃgādyatitāpasānāṃ teṣāṃ na dūraḥ parameśalokaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge bhaktimahimavarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭasaptatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ pūjyo mahādevo martyairmandairmahāmate
kalpāyuṣair alpavīryair alpasattvaiḥ prajāpatiḥ
saṃvatsarasahasraiś ca tapasā pūjya śaṅkaram
na paśyanti surāścāpi kathaṃ devaṃ yajanti te
sūta uvāca
kathitaṃ tathyam evātra yuṣmābhir munipuṅgavāḥ
tathāpi śraddhayā dṛśyaḥ pūjyaḥ saṃbhāṣya eva ca
prasaṃgāccaiva sampūjya bhaktihīnairapi dvijāḥ
bhāvānurūpaphalado bhagavāniti kīrtitaḥ
ucchiṣṭaḥ pūjayanyāti paiśācaṃ tu dvijādhamaḥ
saṃkruddho rākṣasaṃ sthānaṃ prāpnuyān mūḍhadhīr dvijāḥ
abhakṣyabhakṣī sampūjya yākṣaṃ prāpnoti durjanaḥ
gānaśīlaś ca gāndharvaṃ nṛtyaśīlastathaiva ca
khyātiśīlas tathā cāndraṃ strīṣu sakto narādhamaḥ
madārtaḥ pūjayan rudraṃ somasthānamavāpnuyāt
gāyatryā devamabhyarcya prājāpatyamavāpnuyāt
brāhmaṃ hi praṇavenaiva vaiṣṇavaṃ cābhinandya ca
śraddhayā sakṛdevāpi samabhyarcya maheśvaram
rudralokamanuprāpya rudraiḥ sārdhaṃ pramodate
saṃśodhya ca śubhaṃ liṅgam amarāsurapūjitam
jalaiḥ pūtaistathā pīṭhe devamāvāhya bhaktitaḥ
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ yathānyāyaṃ praṇipatya ca śaṅkaram
kalpite cāsane sthāpya dharmajñānamaye śubhe
vairāgyaiśvaryasampanne sarvalokanamaskṛte
oṅkārapadmamadhye tu somasūryāgnisaṃbhave
pādyamācamanaṃ cārghyaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave
snāpayeddivyatoyaiś ca ghṛtena payasā tathā
dadhnā ca snāpayedrudraṃ śodhayecca yathāvidhi
tataḥ śuddhāṃbunā snāpya candanādyaiś ca pūjayet
rocanādyaiś ca sampūjya divyapuṣpaiś ca pūjayet
bilvapatrairakhaṇḍaiś ca padmairnānāvidhais tathā
nīlotpalaiś ca rājīvairnadyāvartaiś ca mallikaiḥ
campakair jātipuṣpaiśca bakulaiḥ karavīrakaiḥ
śamīpuṣpair bṛhatpuṣpair unmattāgastyajairapi
apāmārgakadambaiś ca bhūṣaṇairapi śobhanaiḥ
dattvā pañcavidhaṃ dhūpaṃ pāyasaṃ ca nivedayet
dadhibhaktaṃ ca madhvājyapariplutamataḥ param
śuddhānnaṃ caiva mudgānnaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ ca nivedayet
atha pañcavidhaṃ vāpi saghṛtaṃ vinivedayet
kevalaṃ cāpi śuddhānnam āḍhakaṃ taṇḍulaṃ pacet
kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ cānte namaskṛtya muhurmuhuḥ
stutvā ca devamīśānaṃ punaḥ sampūjya śaṅkaram
īśānaṃ puruṣaṃ caiva aghoraṃ vāmameva ca
sadyojātaṃ japaṃścāpi pañcabhiḥ pūjayecchivam
anena vidhinā devaḥ prasīdati maheśvaraḥ
vṛkṣāḥ puṣpādipatrādyair upayuktāḥ śivārcane
gāvaścaiva dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim
pūjayedyaḥ śivaṃ rudraṃ śarvaṃ bhavamajaṃ sakṛt
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ punarāvṛttivarjitam
arcitaṃ parameśānaṃ bhavaṃ śarvamumāpatim
sakṛtprasaṃgādvā dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
pūjitaṃ vā mahādevaṃ pūjyamānamathāpi vā
dṛṣṭvā prayāti vai martyo brahmalokaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
śrutvānumodayeccāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
yo dadyād ghṛtadīpaṃ ca sakṛlliṅgasya cāgrataḥ
sa tāṃ gatim avāpnoti svāśramair durlabhāṃ sthirām
dīpavṛkṣaṃ pārthivaṃ vā dāravaṃ vā śivālaye
dattvā kulaśataṃ sāgraṃ śivaloke mahīyate
āyasaṃ tāmrajaṃ vāpi raupyaṃ sauvarṇikaṃ tathā
śivāya dīpaṃ yo dadyādvidhinā vāpi bhaktitaḥ
sūryāyutasamaiḥ ślakṣṇairyānaiḥ śivapuraṃ vrajet
kārtike māsi yo dadyād ghṛtadīpaṃ śivāgrataḥ
sampūjyamānaṃ vā paśyedvidhinā parameśvaram
sa yāti brahmaṇo lokaṃ śraddhayā munisattamāḥ
āvāhanaṃ susānnidhyaṃ sthāpanaṃ pūjanaṃ tathā
samproktaṃ rudragāyatryā āsanaṃ praṇavena vai
pañcabhiḥ snapanaṃ proktaṃ rudrādyaiś ca viśeṣataḥ
evaṃ sampūjayennityaṃ devadevamumāpatim
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya praṇavena samarcayet
uttare devadeveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ gāyatriyā yajet
vahnau hutvā yathānyāyaṃ pañcabhiḥ praṇavena ca
sa yāti śivasāyujyamevaṃ sampūjya śaṅkaram
iti saṃkṣepataḥ prokto liṅgārcanavidhikramaḥ
vyāsena kathitaḥ pūrvaṃ śrutvā rudramukhātsvayam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivārcanavidhir nāmaikonāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ paśupatiṃ dṛṣṭvā paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
paśutvaṃ tatyajurdevāstanno vaktumihārhasi
sūta uvāca
purā kailāsaśikhare bhogyākhye svapure sthitam
sametya devāḥ sarvajñamājagmustatprasādataḥ
hitāya sarvadevānāṃ brahmaṇā ca janārdanaḥ
garuḍasya tathā skandhamāruhya puruṣottamaḥ
jagāma devatābhir vai devadevāntikaṃ hariḥ
sarve samprāpya devasya sārdhaṃ girivaraṃ śubham
sendrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sayamāḥ praṇemur girimuttamam
bhagavān vāsudevo 'sau garuḍād garuḍadhvajaḥ
avatīrya giriṃ merumāruroha surottamaiḥ
sakaladuritahīnaṃ sarvadaṃ bhogamukhyaṃ muditakuraravṛndaṃ nāditaṃ nāgavṛndaiḥ
madhuraraṇitagītaṃ sānukūlāndhakāraṃ padaracitavanāntaṃ kāntavātāntatoyam
bhavanaśatasahasrair juṣṭam ādityakalpair lalitagatividagdhair haṃsavṛndaiś ca bhinnam
dhavakhadirapalāśaiś candanādyaiś ca vṛkṣairdvijavaragaṇavṛndaiḥ kokilādyairdvirephaiḥ
kvacidaśeṣasuradrumasaṃkulaṃ kurabakaiḥ priyakaistilakais tathā
bahukadambatamālalatāvṛtaṃ girivaraṃ śikharairvividhais tathā
gireḥ pṛṣṭhe paraṃ śārvaṃ kalpitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
krīḍārthaṃ devadevasya bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
apaśyaṃstatpuraṃ devāḥ sendropendrāḥ samāhitāḥ
praṇemurdūrataścaiva prabhāvādeva śūlinaḥ
sahasrasūryapratimaṃ mahāntaṃ sahasraśaḥ sarvaguṇaiś ca bhinnam
jagāma kailāsagiriṃ mahātmā meruprabhāge puramādidevaḥ
tato'tha nārigajavājisaṃkulaṃ rathair anekair amarārisūdanaḥ
gaṇairgaṇeśaiś ca girīndrasannibhaṃ mahāpuradvāramajo hariś ca
atha jāṃbūnadamayairbhavanairmaṇibhūṣitaiḥ
vimānairvividhākāraiḥ prākāraiś ca samāvṛtam
dṛṣṭvā śaṃbhoḥ puraṃ bāhyaṃ devaiḥ sabrahmakairhariḥ
prahṛṣṭavadano bhūtvā praviveśa tataḥ puram
harmyaprāsādasambādhaṃ mahāṭṭālasamanvitam
dvitīyaṃ devadevasya caturdvāraṃ suśobhanam
vajravaiḍūryamāṇikyamaṇijālaiḥ samāvṛtam
dolāvikṣepasaṃyuktaṃ ghaṇṭācāmarabhūṣitam
mṛdaṅgamurajairjuṣṭaṃ vīṇāveṇunināditam
nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghair bhūtasaṃghaiś ca saṃvṛtam
devendrabhavanākārair bhavanair dṛṣṭimohanaiḥ
prāsādaśṛṅgeṣvatha pauranāryaḥ sahasraśaḥ puṣpaphalākṣatādyaiḥ
sthitāḥ karaistasya hareḥ samantātpracikṣipurmūrdhni yathā bhavasya
dṛṣṭvā nāryastadā viṣṇuṃ madāghūrṇitalocanāḥ
viśālajaghanāḥ sadyo nanṛturmumudurjaguḥ
kāściddṛṣṭvā hariṃ nāryaḥ kiṃcit prahasitānanāḥ
kiṃcid visrastavastrāś ca srastakāñcīguṇā jaguḥ
caturthaṃ pañcamaṃ caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ ca saptamaṃ tathā
aṣṭamaṃ navamaṃ caiva daśamaṃ ca purottamam
atītyāsādya devasya puraṃ śaṃbhoḥ suśobhanam
suvṛttaṃ sutarāṃ śubhraṃ kailāsaśikhare śubhe
sūryamaṇḍalasaṃkāśairvimānaiś ca vibhūṣitam
sphāṭikair maṇḍapaiḥ śubhrairjāṃbūnadamayais tathā
nānāratnamayaiścaiva digvidikṣu vibhūṣitam
gopurairgopateḥ śaṃbhornānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitaiḥ
anekaiḥ sarvatobhadraiḥ sarvaratnamayais tathā
prākārairvividhākārairaṣṭāviṃśatibhir vṛtam
upadvārairmahādvārair vidikṣu vividhairdṛḍhaiḥ
guhyālayairguhyagṛhairguhasya bhavanaiḥ śubhaiḥ
grāmyair anyair mahābhāgā mauktikair dṛṣṭimohanaiḥ
gaṇeśāyatanair divyaiḥ padmarāgamayais tathā
candanairvividhākāraiḥ puṣpodyānaiś ca śobhanaiḥ
taḍāgair dirghikābhiś ca hemasopānapaṅktibhiḥ
strīṇāṃ gatijitair haṃsaiḥ sevitābhiḥ samantataḥ
mayūraiścaiva kāraṇḍaiḥ kokilaiścakravākakaiḥ
śobhitābhiś ca vāpībhir divyāmṛtajalais tathā
saṃlāpālāpakuśalaiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ
stanabhārāvanamraiś ca madāghūrṇitalocanaiḥ
geyanādaratairdivyai rudrakanyāsahasrakaiḥ
nṛtyadbhir apsaraḥsaṃghair amarairapi durlabhaiḥ
praphullāṃbujavṛndādyais tathā dvijavarairapi
rudrastrīgaṇasaṃkīrṇair jalakrīḍāratais tathā
ratotsavarataiścaiva lalitaiś ca pade pade
grāmarāgānuraktaiś ca padmarāgasamaprabhaiḥ
strīsaṃghair devadevasya bhavasya paramātmanaḥ
dṛṣṭvā vismayamāpannāstasthurdevāḥ samantataḥ
tatraiva dadṛśurdevā vṛndaṃ rudragaṇasya ca
gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ vīrāṇāmapi vṛndaṃ sahasraśaḥ
suvarṇakṛtasopānān vajravaiḍūryabhūṣitān
sphāṭikān devadevasya dadṛśuste vimānakān
teṣāṃ śṛṅgeṣu hṛṣṭāś ca nāryaḥ kamalalocanāḥ
viśālajaghanā yakṣā gandharvāpsarasas tathā
kinnaryaḥ kiṃnarāścaiva bhujaṅgāḥ siddhakanyakāḥ
nānāveṣadharāścānyā nānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitāḥ
nānāprabhāvasaṃyuktā nānābhogaratipriyāḥ
nīlotpaladalaprakhyāḥ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇāḥ
padmakiñjalkasaṃkāśairaṃśukairatiśobhanāḥ
valayairnūpurairhāraiśchatraiścitraistathāṃśukaiḥ
bhūṣitā bhūṣitaiś cānyair maṇḍitā maṇḍanapriyāḥ
dṛṣṭvātha vṛndaṃ surasundarīṇāṃ gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ surasundarīṇām
jagmurgaṇeśasya puraṃ sureśāḥ puradviṣaḥ śakrapurogamāś ca
dṛṣṭvā ca tasthuḥ surasiddhasaṃghāḥ purasya madhye puruhūtapūrvāḥ
bhavasya bālārkasahasravarṇaṃ vimānamādyaṃ parameśvarasya
atha tasya vimānasya dvāri saṃsthaṃ gaṇeśvaram
nandinaṃ dadṛśuḥ sarve devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā nandinaṃ sarve praṇamyāhur gaṇeśvaram
jayeti devāstaṃ dṛṣṭvā so'pyāha ca gaṇeśvaraḥ
bho bho devā mahābhāgāḥ sarve nirdhūtakalmaṣāḥ
samprāptāḥ sarvalokeśā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ
tamāhurvaradaṃ devaṃ vāraṇendrasamaprabham
paśupāśavimokṣārthaṃ darśayāsmān maheśvaram
purā puratrayaṃ dagdhuṃ paśutvaṃ paribhāṣitam
śaṅkitāś ca vayaṃ tatra paśutvaṃ prati suvrata
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ proktaṃ bhavena parameṣṭhinā
vratenānena bhūteśa paśutvaṃ naiva vidyate
atha dvādaśavarṣaṃ vā māsadvādaśakaṃ tu vā
dinadvādaśakaṃ vāpi kṛtvā tad vratam uttamam
mucyante paśavaḥ sarve paśupāśairbhavasya tu
darśayāmāsa tāndevānnārāyaṇapurogamān
nandī śilādatanayaḥ sarvabhūtagaṇāgraṇīḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā devamīśānaṃ sāṃbaṃ sagaṇam avyayam
praṇemus tuṣṭuvuś caiva prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ
vijñāpya śitikaṇṭhāya paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
tasthustadāgrataḥ śaṃbhoḥ praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ
tataḥ samprekṣya tān sarvāndevadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
viśodhya teṣāṃ devānāṃ paśutvaṃ parameśvaraḥ
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caiva svayaṃ devo maheśvaraḥ
upadiśya munīnāṃ ca sahāste cāṃbayā bhavaḥ
tadāprabhṛti te devāḥ sarve pāśupatāḥ smṛtāḥ
paśūnāṃ ca patiryasmātteṣāṃ sākṣāddhi devatāḥ
tasmātpāśupatāḥ proktāstapastepuś ca te punaḥ
tato dvādaśavarṣānte muktapāśāḥ surottamāḥ
yayuryathāgataṃ sarve brahmaṇā saha viṣṇunā
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ pitāmahamukhācchrutam
purā sanatkumāreṇa tasmādvyāsena dhīmatā
yaḥ śrāvayecchucir viprāñchṛṇuyādvā śucirnaraḥ
sa dehabhedamāsādya paśupāśaiḥ pramucyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pāśupatavratamāhātmyaṃ nāmāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vratametattvayā proktaṃ paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
vrataṃ pāśupataṃ laiṅgaṃ purā devair anuṣṭhitam
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ yathāpūrvaṃ tvayā śrutam
sūta uvāca
purā sanatkumāreṇa pṛṣṭaḥ śailādirādarāt
nandī prāha vacastasmai pravadāmi samāsataḥ
devairdaityais tathā siddhairgandharvaiḥ siddhacāraṇaiḥ
munibhiś ca mahābhāgairanuṣṭhitamanuttamam
vrataṃ dvādaśaliṅgākhyaṃ paśupāśavimokṣaṇam
bhogadaṃ yogadaṃ caiva kāmadaṃ muktidaṃ śubham
aviyogakaraṃ puṇyaṃ bhaktānāṃ bhayanāśanam
ṣaḍaṅgasahitān vedānmathitvā tena nirmitam
sarvadānottamaṃ puṇyamaśvamedhāyutādhikam
sarvamaṅgaladaṃ puṇyaṃ sarvaśatruvināśanam
saṃsārārṇavamagnānāṃ jantūnāmapi mokṣadam
sarvavyādhiharaṃ caiva sarvajvaravināśanam
devairanuṣṭhitaṃ pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā
kṛtvā kanīyasaṃ liṅgaṃ snāpya candanavāriṇā
caitramāsādi viprendrāḥ śivaliṅgavrataṃ caret
kṛtvā haimaṃ śubhaṃ padmaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam
navaratnaiś ca khacitam aṣṭapatraṃ yathāvidhi
karṇikāyāṃ nyaselliṅgaṃ sphāṭikaṃ pīṭhasaṃyutam
tatra bhaktyā yathānyāyam arcayed bilvapatrakaiḥ
sitaiḥ sahasrakamalai raktairnīlotpalairapi
śvetārkakarṇikāraiś ca karavīrairbakairapi
etairanyair yathālābhaṃ gāyatryā tasya suvratāḥ
sampūjya caiva gandhādyairdhūpairdīpaiś ca maṅgalaiḥ
nīrājanādyaiścānyaiś ca liṅgamūrtimaheśvaram
agaruṃ dakṣiṇe dadyādaghoreṇa dvijottamāḥ
paścime sadyamantreṇa divyāṃ caiva manaḥśilām
uttare vāmadevena candanaṃ vāpi dāpayet
puruṣeṇa muniśreṣṭhā haritālaṃ ca pūrvataḥ
sitāgarūdbhavaṃ viprās tathā kṛṣṇāgarūdbhavam
tathā gugguludhūpaṃ ca saugandhikamanuttamam
sitāraṃ nāma dhūpaṃ ca dadyād īśāya bhaktitaḥ
mahācarurnivedyaḥ syādāḍhakānnamathāpi vā
etad vaḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ śivaliṅgamahāvratam
sarvamāseṣu sāmānyaṃ viśeṣo'pi ca kīrtyate
vaiśākhe vajraliṅgaṃ ca jyeṣṭhe mārakataṃ tathā
āṣāḍhe mauktikaṃ liṅgaṃ śrāvaṇe nīlanirmitam
māsi bhādrapade liṅgaṃ padmarāgamayaṃ śubham
āśvine caiva viprendrāḥ gomedakamayaṃ śubham
pravālenaiva kārtikyāṃ tathā vai mārgaśīrṣake
vaiḍūryanirmitaṃ liṅgaṃ puṣparāgeṇa puṣyake
māghe ca sūryakāntena phālgune sphāṭikena ca
sarvamāseṣu kamalaṃ haimamekaṃ vidhīyate
alābhe rājataṃ vāpi kevalaṃ kamalaṃ tu vā
ratnānām apyalābhe tu hemnā vā rājatena vā
rajatasyāpyalābhe tu tāmralohena kārayet
śailaṃ vā dārujaṃ vāpi mṛnmayaṃ vā savedikam
sarvagandhamayaṃ vāpi kṣaṇikaṃ parikalpayet
haimantike mahādevaṃ śrīpattreṇaiva pūjayet
sarvamāseṣu kamalaṃ haimamekamathāpi vā
rājataṃ vāpi kamalaṃ haimakarṇikamuttamam
rājatasyāpyabhāve tu bilvapatraiḥ samarcayet
sahasrakamalālābhe tadardhenāpi pūjayet
tadardhārdhena vā rudramaṣṭottaraśatena vā
bilvapatre sthitā lakṣmīrdevī lakṣaṇasaṃyutā
nīlotpale'ṃbikā sākṣādutpale ṣaṇmukhaḥ svayam
padmāśrito mahādevaḥ sarvadevapatiḥ śivaḥ
tasmātsarvaprayatnena śrīpattraṃ na tyajedbudhaḥ
nīlotpalaṃ cotpalaṃ ca kamalaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
sarvavaśyakaraṃ padmaṃ śilā sarvārthasiddhidā
kṛṣṇāgarusamudbhūtaṃ sarvapāpanikṛntanam
gugguluprabhṛtīnāṃ caiva dīpānāṃ ca nivedanam
sarvarogakṣayaṃ caiva candanaṃ sarvasiddhidam
saugandhikaṃ tathā dhūpaṃ sarvakāmārthasādhakam
śvetāgarūdbhavaṃ caiva tathā kṛṣṇāgarūdbhavam
saumyaṃ sītāridhūpaṃ ca sākṣānnirvāṇasiddhidam
śvetārkakusume sākṣāccaturvaktraḥ prajāpatiḥ
karṇikārasya kusume medhā sākṣādvyavasthitā
karavīre gaṇādhyakṣo bake nārāyaṇaḥ svayam
sugandhiṣu ca sarveṣu kusumeṣu nagātmajā
tasmādetairyathālābhaṃ puṣpadhūpādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ
pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ bhaktyā vittānusārataḥ
nivedayettato bhaktyā pāyasaṃ ca mahācarum
saghṛtaṃ sopadaṃśaṃ ca sarvadravyasamanvitam
śuddhānnaṃ vāpi mudgānnamāḍhakaṃ cārdhakaṃ tu vā
cāmaraṃ tālavṛntaṃ ca tasmai bhaktyā nivedayet
upahārāṇi puṇyāni nyāyenaivārjitānyapi
nānāvidhāni cārhāṇi prokṣitānyaṃbhasā punaḥ
nivedayecca rudrāya bhaktiyuktena cetasā
kṣīrādvai sarvadevānāṃ sthityarthamamṛtaṃ dhruvam
viṣṇunā jiṣṇunā sākṣādanne sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
bhūtānām annadānena prītir bhavati śaṅkare
tasmāt sampūjayed devam anne prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ
upahāre tathā tuṣṭirvyañjane pavanaḥ svayam
sarvātmako mahādevo gandhatoye hyapāmpatiḥ
pīṭhe vai prakṛtiḥ sākṣānmahadādyairvyavasthitā
tasmāddevaṃ yajedbhaktyā pratimāsaṃ yathāvidhi
paurṇamāsyāṃ vrataṃ kāryaṃ sarvakāmārthasiddhaye
satyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā śāntiḥ saṃtoṣo dānameva ca
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāmupavāsaṃ ca kārayet
saṃvatsarānte godānaṃ vṛṣotsargaṃ viśeṣataḥ
bhojayedbrāhmaṇānbhaktyā śrotriyān vedapāragān
tal liṅgaṃ pūjitaṃ tena sarvadravyasamanvitam
sthāpayed vā śivakṣetre dāpayed brāhmaṇāya vā
ya evaṃ sarvamāseṣu śivaliṅgamahāvratam
kuryādbhaktyā muniśreṣṭhāḥ sa eva tapatāṃ varaḥ
sūryakoṭipratīkāśairvimānai ratnabhūṣitaiḥ
gatvā śivapuraṃ divyaṃ nehāyāti kadācana
athavā hyekamāsaṃ vā caredevaṃ vratottamam
śivalokamavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
athavā saktacittaścedyānyān saṃcintayedvarān
varṣamekaṃ caredevaṃ tāṃstānprāpya śivaṃ vrajet
devatvaṃ vā pitṛtvaṃ vā devarājatvameva ca
gāṇapatyapadaṃ vāpi sakto'pi labhate naraḥ
vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ bhogārthī bhogamāpnuyāt
dravyārthī ca nidhiṃ paśyed āyuḥkāmaś cirāyuṣam
yānyāṃścintayate kāmāṃstāṃstānprāpyeha modate
ekamāsavratādeva so 'nte rudratvamāpnuyāt
idaṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ rahasyaṃ vratottamaṃ viśvasṛjāpi sṛṣṭam
hitāya devāsurasiddhamartyavidyādharāṇāṃ paramaṃ śivena
sampūjya pūjyaṃ vidhinaivamīśaṃ praṇamya mūrdhnā saha bhṛtyaputraiḥ
vyapohanaṃ nāma japetstavaṃ ca pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtya śivaṃ prayatnāt
purākṛtaṃ viśvasṛjā stavaṃ ca hitāya devena jagattrayasya
pitāmahenaiva suraiśca sārdhaṃ mahānubhāvena mahārghyam etat
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge paśupāśavimocanaliṅgapūjādikathanaṃ nāmaikāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
vyapohanastavaṃ vakṣye sarvasiddhipradaṃ śubham
nandinaś ca mukhācchrutvā kumāreṇa mahātmanā
vyāsāya kathitaṃ tasmādbahumānena vai mayā
namaḥ śivāya śuddhāya nirmalāya yaśasvine
duṣṭāntakāya sarvāya bhavāya paramātmane
pañcavaktro daśabhujo hyakṣapañcadaśairyutaḥ
śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
sarvajñaḥ sarvagaḥ śāntaḥ sarvopari susaṃsthitaḥ
padmāsanasthaḥ someśaḥ pāpamāśu vyapohatu
īśānaḥ puruṣaścaiva aghoraḥ sadya eva ca
vāmadevaś ca bhagavānpāpamāśu vyapohatu
anantaḥ sarvavidyeśaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvadaḥ prabhuḥ
śivadhyānaikasampannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
sūkṣmaḥ surāsureśāno viśveśo gaṇapūjitaḥ
śivadhyānaikasampannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
śivottamo mahāpūjyaḥ śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
sarvagaḥ sarvadaḥ śāntaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
ekākṣo bhagavānīśaḥ śivārcanaparāyaṇaḥ
śivadhyānaikasampannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
trimūrtir bhagavān īśaḥ śivabhaktiprabodhakaḥ
śivadhyānaikasampannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
śrīkaṇṭhaḥ śrīpatiḥ śrīmāñśivadhyānarataḥ sadā
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
trailokyanamitā devī solkākārā purātanī
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
trailokyanamitā devī solkākārā purātanī
dākṣāyaṇī mahādevī gaurī haimavatī śubhā
ekaparṇāgrajā saumyā tathā vai caikapāṭalā
aparṇā varadā devī varadānaikatatparā
umā suraharā sākṣātkauśikī vā kapardinī
khaṭvāṅgadhāriṇī divyā karāgratarupallavā
naigameyādibhir divyaiścaturbhiḥ putrakairvṛtā
menāyā nandinī devī vārijā vārijekṣaṇā
aṃbāyā vītaśokasya nandinaś ca mahātmanaḥ
śubhāvatyāḥ sakhī śāntā pañcacūḍā varapradā
sṛṣṭyarthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ prakṛtitvaṃ gatāvyayā
trayoviṃśatibhis tattvair mahadādyair vijṛmbhitā
lakṣmyādiśaktibhir nityaṃ namitā nandanandinī
manonmanī mahādevī māyāvī maṇḍanapriyā
māyayā yā jagatsarvaṃ brahmādyaṃ sacarācaram
kṣobhiṇī mohinī nityaṃ yogināṃ hṛdi saṃsthitā
ekānekasthitā loke indīvaranibhekṣaṇā
bhaktyā paramayā nityaṃ sarvadevairabhiṣṭutā
gaṇendrāmbhojagarbhendrayamavitteśapūrvakaiḥ
saṃstutā jananī teṣāṃ sarvopadravanāśinī
bhaktānāmārtihā bhavyā bhavabhāvavināśanī
bhuktimuktipradā divyā bhaktānāmaprayatnataḥ
sā me sākṣānmahādevī pāpam āśu vyapohatu
caṇḍaḥ sarvagaṇeśāno mukhācchaṃbhorvinirgataḥ
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmān sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
śālaṅkāyanaputrastu halamārgotthitaḥ prabhuḥ
jāmātā marutāṃ devaḥ sarvabhūtamaheśvaraḥ
sarvagaḥ sarvadṛk śarvaḥ sarveśasadṛśaḥ prabhuḥ
sanārāyaṇakair devaiḥ sendracandradivākaraiḥ
siddhaiś ca yakṣagandharvairbhūtairbhūtavidhāyakaiḥ
uragairṛṣibhiścaiva brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā
stutastrailokyanāthastu munirantaḥ puraṃ sthitaḥ
sarvadā pūjitaḥ sarvairnandī pāpaṃ vyapohatu
mahākāyo mahātejā mahādeva ivāparaḥ
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmānsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
merumandārakailāsataṭakūṭaprabhedanaḥ
airāvatādibhir divyairdiggajaiś ca supūjitaḥ
saptapātālapādaś ca saptadvīporujaṅghakaḥ
saptārṇavāṅkuśaścaiva sarvatīrthodaraḥ śivaḥ
ākāśadeho digbāhuḥ somasūryāgnilocanaḥ
hatāsuramahāvṛkṣo brahmavidyāmahotkaṭaḥ
brahmādyādhoraṇair divyair yogapāśasamanvitaiḥ
baddho hṛtpuṇḍarīkākhye staṃbhe vṛttiṃ nirudhya ca
nāgendravaktro yaḥ sākṣādgaṇakoṭiśatairvṛtaḥ
śivadhyānaikasampannaḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
bhṛṅgīśaḥ piṅgalākṣo 'sau bhasitāśastu dehayuk
śivārcanarataḥ śrīmānsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
caturbhistanubhir nityaṃ sarvāsuranibarhaṇaḥ
skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ śāntaḥ senānīḥ śikhivāhanaḥ
devasenāpatiḥ śrīmānsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
bhavaḥ śarvastatheśāno rudraḥ paśupatis tathā
ugro bhīmo mahādevaḥ śivārcanarataḥ sadā
etāḥ pāpaṃ vyapohantu mūrtayaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
mahādevaḥ śivo rudraḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ
īśāno vijayo bhīmo devadevo bhavodbhavaḥ
kapālīśaś ca vijñeyo rudrā rudrāṃśasaṃbhavāḥ
śivapraṇāmasampannā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
vikartano vivasvāṃś ca mārtaṇḍo bhāskaro raviḥ
lokaprakāśakaścaiva lokasākṣītrivikramaḥ
ādityaś ca tathā sūryaś cāṃśumāṃś ca divākaraḥ
ete vai dvādaśādityā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
gaganaṃ sparśanaṃ tejo rasaś ca pṛthivī tathā
candraḥ sūryastathātmā ca tanavaḥ śivabhāṣitāḥ
pāpaṃ vyapohantu mama bhayaṃ nirṇāśayantu me
vāsavaḥ pāvakaścaiva yamo nirṛtireva ca
varuṇo vāyusomau ca īśāno bhagavān hariḥ
pitāmahaś ca bhagavān śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
ete pāpaṃ vyapohantu manasā karmaṇā kṛtam
nabhasvānsparśano vāyuranilo mārutas tathā
prāṇaḥ prāṇeśajīveśau mārutaḥ śivabhāṣitāḥ
śivārcanaratāḥ sarve vyapohantu malaṃ mama
khecarī vasucārī ca brahmeśo brahmabrahmadhīḥ
suṣeṇaḥ śāśvataḥ pṛṣṭaḥ supuṣṭaś ca mahābalaḥ
ete vai cāraṇāḥ śaṃbhoḥ pūjayātīva bhāvitāḥ
vyapohantu malaṃ sarvaṃ pāpaṃ caiva mayā kṛtam
mantrajño mantravit prājño mantrarāṭ siddhapūjitaḥ
siddhavatparamaḥ siddhaḥ sarvasiddhipradāyinaḥ
vyapohantu malaṃ sarve siddhāḥ śivapadārcakāḥ
yakṣo yakṣeśadhanado jṛmbhako maṇibhadrakaḥ
pūrṇabhadreśvaro mālī śitikuṇḍalireva ca
narendraścaiva yakṣeśā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
anantaḥ kulikaścaiva vāsukistakṣakastathā
karkoṭako mahāpadmaḥ śaṅkhapālo mahābalaḥ
śivapraṇāmasampannāḥ śivadehaprabhūṣaṇāḥ
mama pāpaṃ vyapohantu viṣaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam
vīṇājñaḥ kinnaraścaiva surasenaḥ pramardanaḥ
atīśayaḥ sa prayogī gītajñaścaiva kinnarāḥ
śivapraṇāmasampannā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
vidyādharaś ca vibudho vidyārāśirvidāṃ varaḥ
vibuddho vibudhaḥ śrīmānkṛtajñaś ca mahāyaśāḥ
ete vidyādharāḥ sarve śivadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
vyapohantu malaṃ ghoraṃ mahādevaprasādataḥ
vāmadevī mahājambhaḥ kālanemirmahābalaḥ
sugrīvo mardakaścaiva piṅgalo devamardanaḥ
prahrādaścāpyanuhrādaḥ saṃhrādaḥ kila bāṣkalau
jambhaḥ kuṃbhaś ca māyāvī kārtavīryaḥ kṛtaṃjayaḥ
ete 'surā mahātmāno mahādevaparāyaṇāḥ
vyapohantu bhayaṃ ghoramāsuraṃ bhāvameva ca
garutmān khagatiścaiva pakṣirāṭ nāgamardanaḥ
nāgaśatrur hiraṇyāṅgo vainateyaḥ prabhañjanaḥ
nāgāśīrviṣanāśaś ca viṣṇuvāhana eva ca
ete hiraṇyavarṇābhā garuḍā viṣṇuvāhanāḥ
nānābharaṇasampannā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
agastyaś ca vasiṣṭhaś ca aṅgirā bhṛgureva ca
kāśyapo nāradaścaiva dadhīcaścyavanas tathā
upamanyustathānye ca ṛṣayaḥ śivabhāvitāḥ
śivārcanaratāḥ sarve vyapohantu malaṃ mama
pitaraḥ pitāmahāś ca tathaiva prapitāmahāḥ
agniṣvāttā barhiṣadas tathā mātāmahādayaḥ
vyapohantu bhayaṃ pāpaṃ śivadhyānaparāyaṇāḥ
lakṣmīś ca dharaṇī caiva gāyatrī ca sarasvatī
durgā uṣā śacī jyeṣṭhā mātaraḥ surapūjitāḥ
devānāṃ mātaraś caiva gaṇānāṃ mātaras tathā
bhūtānāṃ mātaraḥ sarvā yatra yā gaṇamātaraḥ
prasādāddevadevasya vyapohantu malaṃ mama
urvaśī menakā caiva raṃbhā ratitilottamāḥ
sumukhī durmukhī caiva kāmukī kāmavardhanī
tathānyāḥ sarvalokeṣu divyāścāpsarasas tathā
śivāya tāṇḍavaṃ nityaṃ kurvantyo 'tīva bhāvitāḥ
devyaḥ śivārcanaratā vyapohantu malaṃ mama
arkaḥ somo'ṅgārakaś ca budhaścaiva bṛhaspatiḥ
śukraḥ śanaiścaraścaiva rāhuḥ ketustathaiva ca
vyapohantu bhayaṃ ghoraṃ grahapīḍāṃ śivārcakāḥ
meṣo vṛṣo'tha mithunas tathā karkaṭakaḥ śubhaḥ
siṃhaś ca kanyā vipulā tulā vai vṛścikas tathā
dhanuś ca makaraścaiva kuṃbho mīnastathaiva ca
rāśayo dvādaśa hyete śivapūjāparāyaṇāḥ
vyapohantu bhayaṃ pāpaṃ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
aśvinī bharaṇī caiva kṛttikā rohiṇī tathā
śrīmanmṛgaśiraścārdrā punarvasupuṣyasārpakāḥ
maghā vai pūrvaphālgunya uttarāphālgunī tathā
hastacitrā tathā svātī viśākhā cānurādhikā
jyeṣṭhā mūlaṃ mahābhāgā pūrvāṣāḍhā tathaiva ca
uttarāṣāḍhikā caiva śravaṇaṃ ca śraviṣṭhikā
śatabhiṣak pūrvabhadrā tathā proṣṭhapadā tathā
pauṣṇaṃ ca devyaḥ satataṃ vyapohantu malaṃ mama
jvaraḥ kumbhodaraścaiva śaṅkukarṇo mahābalaḥ
mahākarṇaḥ prabhātaś ca mahābhūtapramardanaḥ
śyenajicchivadūtaś ca pramathāḥ prītivardhanāḥ
koṭikoṭiśataiścaiva bhūtānāṃ mātaraḥ sadā
vyapohantu bhayaṃ pāpaṃ mahādevaprasādataḥ
śivadhyānaikasampanno himarāḍ aṃbusannibhaḥ
kundendusadṛśākāraḥ kuṃbhakundendubhūṣaṇaḥ
vaḍavānalaśatruryo vaḍavāmukhabhedanaḥ
catuṣpādasamāyuktaḥ kṣīroda iva pāṇḍuraḥ
rudraloke sthito nityaṃ rudraiḥ sārdhaṃ gaṇeśvaraiḥ
vṛṣendro viśvadhṛg devo viśvasya jagataḥ pitā
vṛto nandādibhir nityaṃ mātṛbhir makhamardanaḥ
śivārcanarato nityaṃ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
gaṅgā mātā jaganmātā rudraloke vyavasthitā
śivabhaktā tu yā nandā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
bhadrā bhadrapadā devī śivaloke vyavasthitā
mātā gavāṃ mahābhāgā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
surabhiḥ sarvatobhadrā sarvapāpapraṇāśanī
rudrapūjāratā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
suśīlā śīlasampannā śrīpradā śivabhāvitā
śivaloke sthitā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
vedaśāstrārthatattvajñaḥ sarvakāryābhicintakaḥ
samastaguṇasampannaḥ sarvadeveśvarātmajaḥ
jyeṣṭhaḥ sarveśvaraḥ saumyo mahāviṣṇutanuḥ svayam
āryaḥ senāpatiḥ sākṣādgahano makhamardanaḥ
airāvatagajārūḍhaḥ kṛṣṇakuñcitamūrdhajaḥ
kṛṣṇāṅgo raktanayanaḥ śaśipannagabhūṣaṇaḥ
bhūtaiḥ pretaiḥ piśācaiś ca kūṣmāṇḍaiś ca samāvṛtaḥ
śivārcanarataḥ sākṣātsa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
brahmāṇī caiva māheśī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī tathā
vārāhī caiva māhendrī cāmuṇḍāgneyikā tathā
etā vai mātaraḥ sarvāḥ sarvalokaprapūjitāḥ
yoginībhir mahāpāpaṃ vyapohantu samāhitāḥ
vīrabhadro mahātejā himakundendusannibhaḥ
rudrasya tanayo raudraḥ śūlāsaktamahākaraḥ
sahasrabāhuḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvāyudhadharaḥ svayam
tretāgninayano devastrailokyābhayadaḥ prabhuḥ
mātṝṇāṃ rakṣako nityaṃ mahāvṛṣabhavāhanaḥ
trailokyanamitaḥ śrīmān śivapādārcane rataḥ
yajñasya ca śiraśchettā pūṣṇo dantavināśanaḥ
vahnerhastaharaḥ sākṣādbhaganetranipātanaḥ
pādāṅguṣṭhena somāṅgapeṣakaḥ prabhusaṃjñakaḥ
upendrendrayamādīnāṃ devānāmaṅgarakṣakaḥ
sarasvatyā mahādevyā nāsikoṣṭhāvakartanaḥ
gaṇeśvaro yaḥ senānīḥ sa me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā varadā varābharaṇabhūṣitā
mahālakṣmīrjaganmātā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
mahāmohā mahābhāgā mahābhūtagaṇairvṛtā
śivārcanaratā nityaṃ sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
lakṣmīḥ sarvaguṇopetā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutā
sarvadā sarvagā devī sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
siṃhārūḍhā mahādevī pārvatyāstanayāvyayā
viṣṇornidrā mahāmāyā vaiṣṇavī surapūjitā
trinetrā varadā devī mahiṣāsuramardinī
śivārcanaratā durgā sā me pāpaṃ vyapohatu
brahmāṇḍadhārakā rudrāḥ sarvalokaprapūjitāḥ
satyāś ca mānasāḥ sarve vyapohantu bhayaṃ mama
bhūtāḥ pretāḥ piśācāś ca kūṣmāṇḍagaṇanāyakāḥ
kūṣmāṇḍakāś ca te pāpaṃ vyapohantu samāhitāḥ
anena devaṃ stutvā tu cānte sarvaṃ samāpayet
praṇamya śirasā bhūmau pratimāse dvijottamāḥ
vyapohanastavaṃ divyaṃ yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādapi
vidhūya sarvapāpāni rudraloke mahīyate
kanyārthī labhate kanyāṃ jayakāmo jayaṃ labhet
arthakāmo labhedarthaṃ putrakāmo bahūn sutān
vidyārthī labhate vidyāṃ bhogārthī bhogamāpnuyāt
yānyānprārthayate kāmānmānavaḥ śravaṇādiha
tānsarvān śīghramāpnoti devānāṃ ca priyo bhavet
paṭhyamānamidaṃ puṇyaṃ yamuddiśya tu paṭhyate
tasya rogā na bādhante vātapittādisaṃbhavāḥ
nākāle maraṇaṃ tasya na sarpairapi daśyate
yatpuṇyaṃ caiva tīrthānāṃ yajñānāṃ caiva yatphalam
dānānāṃ caiva yatpuṇyaṃ vratānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
tatpuṇyaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ japtvā cāpnoti mānavaḥ
goghnaścaiva kṛtaghnaś ca vīrahā brahmahā bhavet
śaraṇāgataghātī ca mitraviśvāsaghātakaḥ
duṣṭaḥ pāpasamācāro mātṛhā pitṛhā tathā
vyapohya sarvapāpāni śivaloke mahīyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vyapohanastavanirūpaṇaṃ nāma dvyaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vyapohanastavaṃ puṇyaṃ śrutamasmābhir ādarāt
prasaṃgālliṅgadānasya vratānyapi vadasva naḥ
sūta uvāca
vratāni vaḥ pravakṣyāmi śubhāni munisattamāḥ
nandinā kathitānīha brahmaputrāya dhīmate
tāni vyāsādupaśrutya yuṣmākaṃ pravadāmyaham
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ pakṣayorubhayorapi
varṣamekaṃ tu bhuñjāno naktaṃ yaḥ pūjayecchivam
sarvayajñaphalaṃ prāpya sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
pṛthivīṃ bhājanaṃ kṛtvā bhuktvā parvasu mānavaḥ
ahorātreṇa caikena trirātraphalamaśnute
dvayor māsasya pañcamyordvayoḥ pratipadornaraḥ
kṣīradhārāvrataṃ kuryāt so'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ tu naktena yāvatkṛṣṇacaturdaśī
bhuñjanbhogānavāpnoti brahmalokaṃ ca gacchati
yo'bdamekaṃ prakurvīta naktaṃ parvasu parvasu
brahmacārī jitakrodhaḥ śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
saṃvatsarānte viprendrān bhojayedvidhipūrvakam
sa yāti śāṅkaraṃ lokaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
upavāsāt paraṃ bhaikṣyaṃ bhaikṣyāt param ayācitam
ayācitāt paraṃ naktaṃ tasmān naktena vartayet
devairbhuktaṃ tu pūrvāhṇe madhyāhne ṛṣibhis tathā
aparāhṇe ca pitṛbhiḥ saṃdhyāyāṃ guhyakādibhiḥ
sarvavelāmatikramya naktabhojanamuttamam
haviṣyabhojanaṃ snānaṃ satyamāhāralāghavam
agnikāryamadhaḥśayyāṃ naktabhojī samācaret
pratimāsaṃ pravakṣyāmi śivavratamanuttamam
dharmakāmārthamokṣārthaṃ sarvapāpaviśuddhaye
puṣyamāse ca sampūjya yaḥ kuryānnaktabhojanam
satyavādī jitakrodhaḥ śāligodhūmagorasaiḥ
pakṣayoraṣṭamīṃ yatnādupavāsena vartayet
bhūmiśayyāṃ ca māsānte paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ
snāpya rudraṃ mahādevaṃ sampūjya vidhipūrvakam
yāvakaṃ caudanaṃ dattvā sakṣīraṃ saghṛtaṃ dvijāḥ
bhojayed brāhmaṇāñśiṣṭāñjapecchāntiṃ viśeṣataḥ
tathā gomithunaṃ caiva kapilaṃ vinivedayet
bhavāya devadevāya śivāya parameṣṭhine
sa yāti muniśārdūla vāhneyaṃ lokamuttamam
bhuktvā sa vipulān lokān tatraiva sa vimucyate
māghamāse tu sampūjya yaḥ kuryān naktabhojanam
kṛśaraṃ ghṛtasaṃyuktaṃ bhuñjānaḥ saṃyatendriyaḥ
sopavāsaṃ caturdaśyāṃ bhavedubhayapakṣayoḥ
rudrāya paurṇamāsyāṃ tu dadyādvai ghṛtakambalam
kṛṣṇaṃ gomithunaṃ dadyātpūjayeccaiva śaṃkaram
bhojayedbrāhmaṇāṃścaiva yathāvibhavavistaram
yāmyamāsādya vai lokaṃ yamena saha modate
phālgune caiva samprāpte kuryādvai naktabhojanam
śyāmākānnaghṛtakṣīrairjitakrodho jitendriyaḥ
caturdaśyāmathāṣṭamyāmupavāsaṃ ca kārayet
paurṇamāsyāṃ mahādevaṃ snāpya sampūjya śaṅkaram
dadyādgomithunaṃ vāpi tāmrābhaṃ śūlapāṇaye
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tu prārthayetparameśvaram
sa yāti candrasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
caitre'pi rudramabhyarcya kuryādvai naktabhojanam
śālyannaṃ payasā yuktaṃ ghṛtena ca yathāsukham
goṣṭhaśāyī muniśreṣṭhāḥ kṣitau niśi bhavaṃ smaret
paurṇamāsyāṃ śivaṃ snāpya dadyādgomithunaṃ sitam
brāhmaṇān bhojayeccaiva nirṛteḥ sthānamāpnuyāt
vaiśākhe ca tathā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam
paurṇamāsyāṃ bhavaṃ snāpya pañcagavyaghṛtādibhiḥ
śvetaṃ gomithunaṃ dattvā so'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet
jyeṣṭhe māse ca deveśaṃ bhavaṃ śarvamumāpatim
sampūjya śraddhayā bhaktyā kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam
raktaśālyannamadhvā cādbhiḥ pūtaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ
vīrāsano niśārdhaṃ ca gavāṃ śuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu sampūjya devadevamumāpatim
snāpya śaktyā yathānyāyaṃ caruṃ dadyāc ca śūline
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca yathāvibhavavistaram
dhūmraṃ gomithunaṃ dattvā vāyuloke mahīyate
āṣāḍhe māsi cāpyevaṃ naktabhojanatatparaḥ
bhūrikhaṇḍājyasaṃmiśraṃ saktubhiścaiva gorasam
paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādyaistu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān
dadyādgomithunaṃ gauraṃ vāruṇaṃ lokamāpnuyāt
śrāvaṇe ca dvijā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam
kṣīraṣaṣṭikabhaktena sampūjya vṛṣabhadhvajam
paurṇamāsyāṃ ghṛtādyaistu snāpya pūjya yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śrotriyān vedapāragān
śvetāgrapādaṃ pauṇḍraṃ ca dadyādgomithunaṃ punaḥ
sa yāti vāyusāyujyaṃ vāyuvatsarvago bhavet
prāpte bhādrapade māse kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam
hutaśeṣaṃ ca viprendrān vṛkṣamūlāśrito divā
paurṇamāsyāṃ tu deveśaṃ snāpya sampūjya śaṅkaram
nīlaskandhaṃ vṛṣaṃ gāṃ ca dattvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca vedavedāṅgapāragān
yakṣalokamanuprāpya yakṣarājo bhavennaraḥ
tataścāśvayuje māsi kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam
saghṛtaṃ śaṅkaraṃ pūjya paurṇamāsyāṃ ca pūrvavat
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca śivabhaktān sadā śucīn
vṛṣabhaṃ nīlavarṇābhamurodeśasamunnatam
gāṃ ca dattvā yathānyāyam aiśānaṃ lokamāpnuyāt
kārtike ca tathā māse kṛtvā vai naktabhojanam
kṣīraudanena sājyena sampūjya ca bhavaṃ prabhum
paurṇamāsyāṃ ca vidhivatsnāpya dattvā caruṃ punaḥ
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca yathāvibhavavistaram
dattvā gomithunaṃ caiva kāpilaṃ pūrvavad dvijāḥ
sūryasāyujyamāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
mārgaśīrṣe ca māse'pi kṛtvaivaṃ naktabhojanam
yavānnena yathānyāyamājyakṣīrādibhiḥ samam
paurṇamāsyāṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ kṛtvā śarvāya śaṃbhave
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca daridrānvedapāragān
dattvā gomithunaṃ caiva pāṇḍuraṃ vidhipūrvakam
somalokamanuprāpya somena saha modate
ahiṃsā satyamasteyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ kṣamā dayā
triḥsnānaṃ cāgnihotraṃ ca bhūśayyā naktabhojanam
pakṣayorupavāsaṃ ca caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca
ityetadakhilaṃ proktaṃ pratimāsaṃ śivavratam
kuryādvarṣaṃ krameṇaiva vyutkrameṇāpi vā dvijāḥ
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ jñānayogamavāpnuyāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivavratakathanaṃ nāma tryaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
umāmaheśvaraṃ vakṣye vratamīśvarabhāṣitam
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca
naktamabdaṃ prakurvīta haviṣyaṃ pūjayedbhavam
umāmaheśapratimāṃ hemnā kṛtvā suśobhanām
rājatīṃ vātha varṣānte pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dattvā śaktyā ca dakṣiṇām
rathādyairvāpi deveśaṃ nītvā rudrālayaṃ prati
sarvātiśayasaṃyuktaiś chatracāmarabhūṣaṇaiḥ
nivedayedvrataṃ caiva śivāya parameṣṭhine
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nārī devyā yadi prabho
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ niyatā brahmacāriṇī
varṣamekaṃ na bhuñjati kanyā vā vidhavāpi vā
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā pūrvoktavidhinā tataḥ
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ dattvā rudrālaye punaḥ
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca bhavānyā saha modate
yā nāryevaṃ caredabdaṃ kṛṣṇāmekāṃ caturdaśīm
varṣānte pratimāṃ kṛtvā yena kenāpi vā dvijāḥ
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate
amāvāsyāṃ nirāhārā bhavedabdaṃ suyantritā
śūlaṃ ca vidhinā kṛtvā varṣānte vinivedayet
snāpyeśānaṃ yajedbhaktyā sahasraiḥ kamalaiḥ sitaiḥ
rājataṃ kamalaṃ caiva jāṃbūnadasukarṇikam
dattvā bhavāya viprebhyaḥ pradadyād dakṣiṇām api
kāmato'pi kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ bhrūṇahatyādikaṃ ca yat
tatsarvaṃ śūladānena bhindyānnārī na saṃśayaḥ
sāyujyaṃ caivamāpnoti bhavānyā dvijasattamāḥ
kuryādyadvā naraḥ so'pi rudrasāyujyamāpnuyāt
paurṇamāsyāmamāvāsyāṃ varṣamekamatandritā
upavāsaratā nārī naro'pi dvijasattamāḥ
niyogādeva tatkāryaṃ bhartṝṇāṃ dvijasattamāḥ
japaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ sarvamasvatantrā yataḥ striyaḥ
varṣānte sarvagandhāḍhyāṃ pratimāṃ saṃnivedayet
sā bhavānyāś ca sāyujyaṃ sārūpyaṃ cāpi suvratā
labhate nātra saṃdehaḥ satyaṃ satyaṃ vadāmyaham
kārtikyāṃ vā tu yā nārī ekabhaktena vartate
kṣamāhiṃsādiniyamaiḥ saṃyuktā brahmacāriṇī
dadyātkṛṣṇatilānāṃ ca bhāramekam atandritā
saghṛtaṃ saguḍaṃ caiva odanaṃ parameṣṭhine
dattvā ca brāhmaṇebhyaś ca yathā vibhavavistaram
aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyām upavāsaratā ca sā
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ sārūpyaṃ prāpya suvratā
kṣamā satyaṃ dayā dānaṃ śaucamindriyanigrahaḥ
sarvavrateṣvayaṃ dharmaḥ sāmānyo rudrapūjanam
samāsādvaḥ pravakṣyāmi pratimāsamanukramāt
mārgaśīrṣakamāsādikārttikāntaṃ yathākramam
vrataṃ suvipulaṃ puṇyaṃ nandinā paribhāṣitam
mārgaśīrṣakamāse 'tha vṛṣaṃ pūrṇāṅgamuttamam
alaṃkṛtya yathānyāyaṃ śivāya vinivedayet
sā ca sārdhaṃ bhavānyā vai modate nātra saṃśayaḥ
puṣyamāse tu vai śūlaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya nivedayet
pūrvoktamakhilaṃ kṛtvā bhavānyā saha modate
māghamāse rathaṃ kṛtvā sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam
dadyāt sampūjya deveśaṃ brāhmaṇāṃścaiva bhojayet
sā ca devyā mahābhāgā modate nātra saṃśayaḥ
phālgune pratimāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi
rājatenāpi tāmreṇa yathāvibhavavistaram
pratiṣṭhāpya samabhyarcya sthāpayecchaṅkarālaye
sā ca sārdhaṃ mahādevyā modate nātra saṃśayaḥ
caitre bhavaṃ kumāraṃ ca bhavānīṃ ca yathāvidhi
tāmrādyairvidhivatkṛtvā pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi
bhavānyā modate sārdhaṃ dattvā rudrāya śaṃbhave
kṛtvālayaṃ hi kauberaṃ rājataṃ rajatena vai
īśvaromāsamāyuktaṃ gaṇeśaiś ca samantataḥ
sarvaratnasamāyuktaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yathāvidhi
sthāpayetparameśasya bhavasyāyatane śubhe
vaiśākhe vai cared evaṃ kailāsākhyaṃ vratottamam
kailāsaparvataṃ prāpya bhavānyā saha modate
jyeṣṭhe māsi mahādevaṃ liṅgamūrtimumāpatim
kṛtāñjalipuṭenaiva brahmaṇā viṣṇunā tathā
madhye bhavena saṃyuktaṃ liṅgamūrti dvijottamāḥ
haṃsena ca varāheṇa kṛtvā tāmrādibhiḥ śubhām
pratiṣṭhāpya yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ
śivāya śivamāsādya śivasthāne yathāvidhi
brāhmaṇaiḥ sahitāṃ sthāpya devyāḥ sāyujyamāpnuyāt
āṣāḍhe ca śubhe māse gṛhaṃ kṛtvā suśobhanam
pakveṣṭakābhir vidhivadyathāvibhavavistaram
sarvabījarasaiścāpi sampūrṇaṃ sarvaśobhanaiḥ
gṛhopakaraṇaiścaiva musalolūkhalādibhiḥ
dāsīdāsādibhiścaiva śayanairaśanādibhiḥ
sampūrṇaiś ca gṛhaṃ vastrairācchādya ca samantataḥ
devaṃ ghṛtādibhiḥ snāpya mahādevamumāpatim
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayitvā yathāvidhi
vidyāvinayasampannaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam
prathamāśramiṇaṃ bhaktyā sampūjya ca yathāvidhi
kanyāṃ sumadhyamāṃ yāvat kālajīvanasaṃyutām
kṣetraṃ gomithunaṃ caiva tadgṛhe ca nivedayet
sāyanair vividhair divyair meruparvatasannibhaiḥ
golokaṃ samanuprāpya bhavānyā saha modate
bhavānyā sadṛśībhūtvā sarvakalpeṣu sāvyayā
bhavānyāścaiva sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
sarvadhātusamākīrṇaṃ vicitradhvajaśobhitam
nivedayīta śarvāya śrāvaṇe tilaparvatam
vitānadhvajavastrādyairdhātubhiś ca nivedayet
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūrvoktamakhilaṃ bhavet
kṛtvā bhādrapade māsi śobhanaṃ śāliparvatam
vitānadhvajavastrādyairdhātubhiś ca nivedayet
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dāpayecca yathāvidhi
sā ca sūryāṃśusaṃkāśā bhavānyā saha modate
kṛtvā cāśvayuje māsi vipulaṃ dhānyaparvatam
suvarṇavastrasaṃyuktaṃ dattvā sampūjya śaṅkaram
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca pūrvoktamakhilaṃ bhavet
sarvadhānyasamāyuktaṃ sarvabījarasādibhiḥ
sarvadhātusamāyuktaṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitam
śṛṅgaiścaturbhiḥ saṃyuktaṃ vitānacchatraśobhitam
gandhamālyais tathā dhūpaiścitraiścāpi suśobhitam
vicitrairnṛtyageyaiś ca śaṅkhavīṇādibhis tathā
brahmaghoṣairmahāpuṇyaṃ maṅgalaiś ca viśeṣataḥ
mahādhvajāṣṭasaṃyuktaṃ vicitrakusumojjvalam
nagendraṃ merunāmānaṃ trailokyādhāramuttamam
tasya mūrdhni śivaṃ kuryānmadhyato dhātunaiva tu
dakṣiṇe ca yathānyāyaṃ brahmāṇaṃ ca caturmukham
uttare devadeveśaṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam
indrādilokapālāṃś ca kṛtvā bhaktyā yathāvidhi
pratiṣṭhāpya tataḥ snāpya samabhyarcya maheśvaram
devasya dakṣiṇe haste śūlaṃ tridaśapūjitam
vāme pāśaṃ bhavānyāś ca kamalaṃ hemabhūṣitam
viṣṇoś ca śaṅkhaṃ cakraṃ ca gadāmabjaṃ prayatnataḥ
brahmaṇaścākṣasūtraṃ ca kamaṇḍalumanuttamam
indrasya vajram agneś ca śaktyākhyaṃ paramāyudham
yamasya daṇḍaṃ nirṛteḥ khaḍgaṃ niśicarasya tu
varuṇasya mahāpāśaṃ nāgākhyaṃ rudramadbhutam
vāyor yaṣṭiṃ kuberasya gadāṃ lokaprapūjitām
ṭaṅkaṃ ceśānadevasya nivedyaivaṃ krameṇa ca
śivasya mahatīṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā carusamanvitām
pūjayetsarvadevāṃś ca yathāvibhavavistaram
brāhmaṇānbhojayitvā ca pūjāṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ
mahāmeruvrataṃ kṛtvā mahādevāya dāpayet
mahāmerumanuprāpya mahādevyā pramodate
ciraṃ sāyujyam āpnoti mahādevyā na saṃśayaḥ
kārtikyāmapi yā nārī kṛtvā devīmumāṃ śubhām
sarvābharaṇasampūrṇāṃ sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitām
hematāmrādibhiścaiva pratiṣṭhāpya vidhānataḥ
devaṃ ca kṛtvā deveśaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
tayoragre hutāśaṃ ca sruvahastaṃ pitāmaham
nārāyaṇaṃ ca dātāraṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
lokapālais tathā siddhaiḥ saṃvṛtaṃ sthāpya yatnataḥ
rudrālaye vrataṃ tasmai dāpayedbhaktipūrvakam
sā bhavānyāstanuṃ gatvā bhavena saha modate
ekabhaktavrataṃ puṇyaṃ pratimāsamanukramāt
mārgaśīrṣakamāsādikārtikāntaṃ pravartitam
naranāryādijantūnāṃ hitāya munisattamāḥ
naraḥ kṛtvā vrataṃ caiva śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
nārī devyā na saṃdehaḥ śivena paribhāṣitam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāmaheśvaravrataṃ nāma caturaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
sarvavrateṣu sampūjya devadevamumāpatim
japetpañcākṣarīṃ vidyāṃ vidhinaiva dvijottamāḥ
japādeva na saṃdeho vratānāṃ vai viśeṣataḥ
samāptirnānyathā tasmājjapetpañcākṣarīṃ śubhām
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ pañcākṣarī vidyā prabhāvo vā kathaṃ vada
kramopāyaṃ mahābhāga śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
sūta uvāca
purā devena rudreṇa devadevena śaṃbhunā
pārvatyāḥ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ pravadāmi samāsataḥ
śrīdevyuvāca
bhagavandevadeveśa sarvalokamaheśvara
pañcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
pañcākṣarasya māhātmyaṃ varṣakoṭiśatairapi
na śakyaṃ kathituṃ devi tasmāt saṃkṣepataḥ śṛṇu
pralaye samanuprāpte naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame
naṣṭe devāsure caiva naṣṭe coragarākṣase
sarvaṃ prakṛtimāpannaṃ tvayā pralayameṣyati
eko'haṃ saṃsthito devi na dvitīyo'sti kutracit
tasminvedāś ca śāstrāṇi mantre pañcākṣare sthitāḥ
te nāśaṃ naiva samprāptā macchaktyā hyanupālitāḥ
ahameko dvidhāpyāsaṃ prakṛtyātmaprabhedataḥ
sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ śete devo māyāmayīṃ tanum
āsthāya yogaparyaṅkaśayane toyamadhyagaḥ
tannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ
sisṛkṣamāṇo lokānvai trīnaśakto 'sahāyavān
daśa brahmā sasarjādau mānasānamitaujasaḥ
teṣāṃ sṛṣṭiprasiddhyarthaṃ māṃ provāca pitāmahaḥ
matputrāṇāṃ mahādeva śaktiṃ dehi maheśvara
iti tena samādiṣṭaḥ pañcavaktradharo hyaham
pañcākṣarānpañcamukhaiḥ proktavān padmayonaye
tānpañcavadanairgṛhṇan brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
vācyavācakabhāvena jñātavānparameśvaram
vācyaḥ pañcākṣarairdevi śivastrailokyapūjitaḥ
vācakaḥ paramo mantrastasya pañcākṣaraḥ sthitaḥ
jñātvā prayogaṃ vidhinā ca siddhiṃ labdhvā tathā pañcamukho mahātmā
provāca putreṣu jagaddhitāya mantraṃ mahārthaṃ kila pañcavarṇam
te labdhvā mantraratnaṃ tu sākṣāllokapitāmahāt
tamārādhayituṃ devaṃ parātparataraṃ śivam
tatastutoṣa bhagavān trimūrtīnāṃ paraḥ śivaḥ
dattavānakhilaṃ jñānamaṇimādiguṇāṣṭakam
te'pi labdhvā varānviprāstadārādhanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ
merostu śikhare ramye muñjavānnāma parvataḥ
matpriyaḥ satataṃ śrīmānmadbhūtaiḥ parirakṣitaḥ
tasyābhyāśe tapastīvraṃ lokasṛṣṭisamutsukāḥ
divyavarṣasahasraṃ tu vāyubhakṣāḥ samācaran
tiṣṭhanto'nugrahārthāya devi te ṛṣayaḥ purā
teṣāṃ bhaktimahaṃ dṛṣṭvā sadyaḥ pratyakṣatāmiyām
pañcākṣaram ṛṣicchando daivataṃ śaktibījavat
nyāsaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ digbandhaṃ viniyogamaśeṣataḥ
proktavānahamāryāṇāṃ lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā
tacchrutvā mantramāhātmyamṛṣayaste tapodhanāḥ
mantrasya viniyogaṃ ca kṛtvā sarvamanuṣṭhitāḥ
tanmāhātmyāt tadā lokān sadevāsuramānuṣān
varṇānvarṇavibhāgāṃś ca sarvadharmāṃś ca śobhanān
pūrvakalpasamudbhūtāñchrutavanto yathā purā
pañcākṣaraprabhāvācca lokā vedā maharṣayaḥ
tiṣṭhanti śāśvatā dharmā devāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat
tad idānīṃ pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu cāvahitākhilam
alpākṣaraṃ mahārthaṃ ca vedasāraṃ vimuktidam
ājñāsiddhamasaṃdigdhaṃ vākyametacchivātmakam
nānāsiddhiyutaṃ divyaṃ lokacittānurañjakam
suniścitārthaṃ gaṃbhīraṃ vākyaṃ me pārameśvaram
mantraṃ mukhasukhoccāryam aśeṣārthaprasādhakam
tadbījaṃ sarvavidyānāṃ mantramādyaṃ suśobhanam
atisūkṣmaṃ mahārthaṃ ca jñeyaṃ tadvaṭabījavat
vedaḥ sa triguṇātītaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvakṛtprabhuḥ
omityekākṣaraṃ mantraṃ sthitaḥ sarvagataḥ śivaḥ
mantre ṣaḍakṣare sūkṣme pañcākṣaratanuḥ śivaḥ
vācyavācakabhāvena sthitaḥ sākṣātsvabhāvataḥ
vācyaḥ śivaḥ prameyatvān mantrastadvācakaḥ smṛtaḥ
vācyavācakabhāvo'yam anādiḥ saṃsthitastayoḥ
vede śivāgame vāpi yatra yatra ṣaḍakṣaraḥ
mantraḥ sthitaḥ sadā mukhyo loke pañcākṣaro mataḥ
kiṃ tasya bahubhir mantraiḥ śāstrairvā bahuvistṛtaiḥ
yasyaivaṃ hṛdi saṃstho'yaṃ mantraḥ syātpārameśvaraḥ
tenādhītaṃ śrutaṃ tena tena sarvamanuṣṭhitam
yo vidvānvai japetsamyagadhītyaiva vidhānataḥ
etāvaddhi śivajñānametāvatparamaṃ padam
etāvad brahmavidyā ca tasmānnityaṃ japedbudhaḥ
pañcākṣaraiḥ sapraṇavo mantro'yaṃ hṛdayaṃ mama
guhyādguhyataraṃ sākṣān mokṣajñānam anuttamam
asya mantrasya vakṣyāmi ṛṣicchando'dhidaivatam
bījaṃ śaktiṃ svaraṃ varṇaṃ sthānaṃ caivākṣaraṃ prati
vāmadevo nāma ṛṣiḥ paṅktiśchanda udāhṛtaḥ
devatā śiva evāhaṃ mantrasyāsya varānane
nakārādīni bījāni pañcabhūtātmakāni ca
ātmānaṃ praṇavaṃ viddhi sarvavyāpinamavyayam
śaktistvameva deveśi sarvadevanamaskṛte
tvadīyaṃ praṇavaṃ kiṃcin madīyaṃ praṇavaṃ tathā
tvadīyaṃ devi mantrāṇāṃ śaktibhūtaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
akārokāramakārā madīye praṇave sthitāḥ
ukāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca akāraṃ ca krameṇa vai
tvadīyaṃ praṇavaṃ viddhi trimātraṃ plutamuttamam
oṅkārasya svarodātta ṛṣirbrahma sitaṃ vapuḥ
chando devī ca gāyatrī paramātmādhidevatā
udāttaḥ prathamastadvaccaturthaś ca dvitīyakaḥ
pañcamaḥ svaritaścaiva madhyamo niṣadhaḥ smṛtāḥ
nakāraḥ pītavarṇaś ca sthānaṃ pūrvamukhaṃ smṛtam
indro'dhidaivataṃ chando gāyatrī gautama ṛṣiḥ
makāraḥ kṛṣṇavarṇo'sya sthānaṃ vai dakṣiṇāmukham
chando'nuṣṭup ṛṣiścātrī rudro daivatamucyate
śikāro dhūmravarṇo'sya sthānaṃ vai paścimaṃ mukham
viśvāmitra ṛṣistriṣṭup chando viṣṇustu daivatam
vākāro hemavarṇo'sya sthānaṃ caivottaraṃ mukham
brahmādhidaivataṃ chando bṛhatī cāṅgirā ṛṣiḥ
yakāro raktavarṇaś ca sthānam ūrdhvaṃ mukhaṃ virāṭ
chanda ṛṣirbharadvājaḥ skando daivatamucyate
nyāsamasya pravakṣyāmi sarvasiddhikaraṃ śubham
sarvapāpaharaṃ caiva trividho nyāsa ucyate
utpattisthitisaṃhārabhedatastrividhaḥ smṛtaḥ
brahmacārigṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ kramaśo bhavet
utpattirbrahmacāriṇāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ sthitiḥ sadā
yatīnāṃ saṃhṛtir nyāsaḥ siddhir bhavati nānyathā
aṅganyāsaḥ karanyāso dehanyāsa iti tridhā
utpattyāditribhedena vakṣyate te varānane
nyasetpūrvaṃ karanyāsaṃ dehanyāsam anantaram
aṅganyāsaṃ tataḥ paścādakṣarāṇāṃ vidhikramāt
mūrdhādipādaparyantamutpattinyāsa ucyate
pādādimūrdhaparyantaṃ saṃhāro bhavati priye
hṛdayāsyagalanyāsaḥ sthitinyāsa udāhṛtaḥ
brahmacārigṛhasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ caiva śobhane
saśiraskaṃ tato dehaṃ sarvamantreṇa saṃspṛśet
sa dehanyāsa ityuktaḥ sarveṣāṃ sama eva sa
dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhamārabhya vāmāṅguṣṭhānta eva hi
nyasyate yattadutpattirviparītaṃ tu saṃhṛtiḥ
aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ nyasyate hastayor dvayoḥ
atīva bhogado devi sthitinyāsaḥ kuṭuṃbinām
karanyāsaṃ purā kṛtvā dehanyāsam anantaram
aṅganyāsaṃ nyasetpaścādeṣa sādhāraṇo vidhiḥ
oṅkāraṃ saṃpuṭīkṛtya sarvāṅgeṣu ca vinyaset
karayorubhayoścaiva daśāgrāṃguliṣu kramāt
prakṣālya pādāvācamya śucirbhūtvā samāhitaḥ
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi nyāsakarma samācaret
smaret pūrvam ṛṣiṃ chando daivataṃ bījameva ca
śaktiṃ ca paramātmānaṃ guruṃ caiva varānane
mantreṇa pāṇī saṃmṛjya talayoḥ praṇavaṃ nyaset
aṅgulīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tathā cādyantaparvasu
sabindukāni bījāni pañca madhyamaparvasu
utpattyāditribhedena nyasedāśramataḥ kramāt
ubhābhyāmeva pāṇibhyāmāpādatalamastakam
mantreṇa saṃspṛśeddehaṃ praṇavenaiva saṃpuṭam
mūrdhni vaktre ca kaṇṭhe ca hṛdaye guhyake tathā
pādayor ubhayoścaiva guhye ca hṛdaye tathā
kaṇṭhe ca mukhamadhye ca mūrdhni ca praṇavādikam
hṛdaye guhyake caiva pādayormūrdhni vāci vā
kaṇṭhe caiva nyasedeva praṇavāditribhedataḥ
kṛtvāṅganyāsamevaṃ hi mukhāni parikalpayet
pūrvādi cordhvaparyantaṃ nakārādi yathākramam
ṣaḍaṅgāni nyasetpaścādyathāsthānaṃ ca śobhanam
namaḥ svāhā vaṣaḍḍhuṃ ca vauṣaṭphaṭkārakaiḥ saha
praṇavaṃ hṛdayaṃ vidyān nakāraḥ śira ucyate
śikhā makāra ākhyātaḥ śikāraḥ kavacaṃ tathā
ākāro netramastraṃ tu yakāraḥ parikīrtitaḥ
itthamaṅgāni vinyasya tato vai bandhayeddiśaḥ
vighneśo mātaro durgā kṣetrajño devatā diśaḥ
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu caturṣvapi yathākramam
aṅguṣṭhatarjanyagrābhyāṃ saṃsthāpya sumukhaṃ śubham
rakṣadhvamiti coktvā tu namaskuryātpṛthakpṛthak
gale madhye tathāṅguṣṭhe tarjanyādyāṅgulīṣu ca
aṅguṣṭhena karanyāsaṃ kuryādeva vicakṣaṇaḥ
evaṃ nyāsamimaṃ proktaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham
sarvasiddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ sarvarakṣākaraṃ śivam
nyaste mantre 'tha subhage śaṅkarapratimo bhavet
janmāntarakṛtaṃ pāpamapi naśyati tatkṣaṇāt
evaṃ vinyasya medhāvī śuddhakāyo dṛḍhavrataḥ
japetpañcākṣaraṃ mantraṃ labdhvācāryaprasādataḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi mantrasaṃgrahaṇaṃ śubhe
yaṃ vinā niṣphalaṃ nityaṃ yena vā saphalaṃ bhavet
ājñāhīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnam amānasam
ājñaptaṃ dakṣiṇāhīnaṃ sadā japtaṃ ca niṣphalam
ājñāsiddhaṃ kriyāsiddhaṃ śraddhāsiddhaṃ sumānasam
evaṃ ca dakṣiṇāsiddhaṃ mantraṃ siddhaṃ yatastataḥ
upāgamya guruṃ vipraṃ mantratattvārthavedinam
jñāninaṃ sadguṇopetaṃ dhyānayogaparāyaṇam
toṣayettaṃ prayatnena bhāvaśuddhisamanvitaḥ
vācā ca manasā caiva kāyena draviṇena ca
ācāryaṃ pūjayecchiṣyaḥ sarvadātiprayatnataḥ
hastyaśvaratharatnāni kṣetrāṇi ca gṛhāṇi ca
bhūṣaṇāni ca vāsāṃsi dhānyāni vividhāni ca
etāni gurave dadyād bhaktyā ca vibhave sati
vittaśāṭhyaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchetsiddhimātmanaḥ
paścānnivedayeddevi ātmānaṃ saparicchadam
evaṃ sampūjya vidhivadyathāśakti tvavañcayan
ādadīta gurormantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva krameṇa tu
evaṃ tuṣṭo guruḥ śiṣyaṃ pūjitaṃ vatsaroṣitam
śuśrūṣum anahaṅkāram upavāsakṛśaṃ śucim
snāpayitvā tu śiṣyāya brāhmaṇānapi pūjya ca
samudratīre nadyāṃ ca goṣṭhe devālaye'pi vā
śucau deśe gṛhe vāpi kāle siddhikare tithau
nakṣatre śubhayoge ca sarvadā doṣavarjite
anugṛhya tato dadyācchivajñānam anuttamam
svareṇoccārayet samyag ekānte'pi prasannadhīḥ
uccāryoccārayitvā tu ācāryaḥ siddhidaḥ svayam
śivaṃ cāstu śubhaṃ cāstu śobhano'stu priyo'stviti
evaṃ labdhvā paraṃ mantraṃ jñānaṃ caiva gurostataḥ
japennityaṃ sasaṃkalpaṃ puraścaraṇameva ca
yāvajjīvaṃ japennityam aṣṭottarasahasrakam
anaśnaṃstatparo bhūtvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
japedakṣaralakṣaṃ vai caturguṇitamādarāt
naktāśī saṃyamī yaś ca pauraścaraṇikaḥ smṛtaḥ
puraścaraṇajāpī vāpi vā nityajāpakaḥ
acirātsiddhikāṅkṣī tu tayoranyataro bhavet
yaḥ puraścaraṇaṃ kṛtvā nityajāpī bhavennaraḥ
tasya nāsti samo loke sa siddhaḥ siddhido vaśī
āsanaṃ ruciraṃ baddhvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ
prāṅmukhodaṅmukho vāpi japenmantramanuttamam
ādyāntayor japasyāpi kuryādvai prāṇasaṃyamān
tathā cānte japedbījaṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ śubham
catvāriṃśatsamāvṛtti prāṇānāyamya saṃsmaret
pañcākṣarasya mantrasya prāṇāyāma udāhṛtaḥ
prāṇāyāmādbhavetkṣipraṃ sarvapāpaparikṣayaḥ
indriyāṇāṃ vaśitvaṃ ca tasmātprāṇāṃś ca saṃyamet
gṛhe japaḥ samaṃ vidyādgoṣṭhe śataguṇaṃ bhavet
nadyāṃ śatasahasraṃ tu anantaḥ śivasannidhau
samudratīre devahrade girau devālayeṣu ca
puṇyāśrameṣu sarveṣu japaḥ koṭiguṇo bhavet
śivasya saṃnidhāne ca sūryasyāgre gurorapi
dīpasya gorjalasyāpi japakarma praśasyate
aṅgulījapasaṃkhyānamekamekaṃ śubhānane
rekhairaṣṭaguṇaṃ proktaṃ putrajīvaphalair daśa
śataṃ vai śaṅkhamaṇibhiḥ pravālaiś ca sahasrakam
sphāṭikair daśasāhasraṃ mauktikairlakṣamucyate
padmākṣairdaśalakṣaṃ tu sauvarṇaiḥ koṭirucyate
kuśagranthyā ca rudrākṣairanantaguṇamucyate
pañcaviṃśati mokṣārthaṃ saptaviṃśati pauṣṭikam
triṃśacca dhanasaṃpattyai pañcāśaccābhicārikam
tatpūrvābhimukhaṃ vaśyaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ cābhicārikam
paścimaṃ dhanadaṃ vidyāduttaraṃ śāntikaṃ bhavet
aṅguṣṭhaṃ mokṣadaṃ vidyāttarjanī śatrunāśanī
madhyamā dhanadā śāntiṃ karotyeṣā hy anāmikā
kaniṣṭhā rakṣaṇīyā sā japakarmaṇi śobhane
aṅguṣṭhena japejjapyamanyairaṅgulibhiḥ saha
aṅguṣṭhena vinā karma kṛtaṃ tadaphalaṃ yataḥ
śṛṇuṣva sarvayajñebhyo japayajño viśiṣyate
hiṃsayā te pravartante japayajño na hiṃsayā
yāvantaḥ karmayajñāḥ syuḥ pradānāni tapāṃsi ca
sarve te japayajñasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
māhātmyaṃ vācikasyaiva japayajñasya kīrtitam
tasmācchataguṇopāṃśuḥ sahasro mānasaḥ smṛtaḥ
yad uccanīcasvaritaiḥ śabdaiḥ spaṣṭapadākṣaraiḥ
mantramuccārayedvācā japayajñaḥ sa vācikaḥ
śanairuccārayenmantram īṣad oṣṭhau tu cālayet
kiṃcit karṇāntaraṃ vidyād upāṃśuḥ sa japaḥ smṛtaḥ
dhiyā yadakṣaraśreṇyā varṇādvarṇaṃ padātpadam
śabdārthaṃ cintayedbhūyaḥ sa tūkto mānaso japaḥ
trayāṇāṃ japayajñānāṃ śreyān syāduttarottaraḥ
bhavedyajñaviśeṣeṇa vaiśiṣṭyaṃ tatphalasya ca
japena devatā nityaṃ stūyamānā prasīdati
prasannā vipulān bhogāndadyānmuktiṃ ca śāśvatīm
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāś ca grahāḥ sarve ca bhīṣaṇāḥ
jāpinaṃ nopasarpanti bhayabhītāḥ samantataḥ
japena pāpaṃ śamayedaśeṣaṃ yattatkṛtaṃ janmaparaṃparāsu
japena bhogān jayate ca mṛtyuṃ japena siddhiṃ labhate ca muktim
evaṃ labdhvā śivaṃ jñānaṃ jñātvā japavidhikramam
sadācārī japannityaṃ dhyāyan bhadraṃ samaśnute
sadācāraṃ pravakṣyāmi samyagdharmasya sādhanam
yasmādācārahīnasya sādhanaṃ niṣphalaṃ bhavet
ācāraḥ paramo dharma ācāraḥ paramaṃ tapaḥ
ācāraḥ paramā vidyā ācāraḥ paramā gatiḥ
sadācāravatāṃ puṃsāṃ sarvatrāpyabhayaṃ bhavet
tadvadācārahīnānāṃ sarvatraiva bhayaṃ bhavet
sadācāreṇa devatvam ṛṣitvaṃ ca varānane
upayānti kuyonitvaṃ tadvad ācāralaṅghanāt
ācārahīnaḥ puruṣo loke bhavati ninditaḥ
tasmātsaṃsiddhimanvicchansamyagācāravān bhavet
durvṛttaḥ śuddhibhūyiṣṭhaḥ pāpīyān jñānadūṣakaḥ
varṇāśramavidhānoktaṃ dharmaṃ kurvīta yatnataḥ
yasya yadvihitaṃ karma tatkurvanmatpriyaḥ sadā
saṃdhyopāsanaśīlaḥ syātsāyaṃ prātaḥ prasannadhīḥ
udayāstamayātpūrvamāramya vidhinā śuciḥ
kāmānmohādbhayāllobhātsaṃdhyāṃ nātikrameddvijaḥ
saṃdhyātikramaṇādvipro brāhmaṇyātpatate yataḥ
asatyaṃ na vadet kiṃcinna satyaṃ ca parityajet
yatsatyaṃ brahma ityāhurasatyaṃ brahmadūṣaṇam
anṛtaṃ paruṣaṃ śāṭhyaṃ paiśunyaṃ pāpahetukam
paradārānparadravyaṃ parahiṃsāṃ ca sarvadā
kvaciccāpi na kurvīta vācā ca manasā tathā
śūdrānnaṃ yātayāmānnaṃ naivedyaṃ śrāddhameva ca
gaṇānnaṃ samudāyānnaṃ rājānnaṃ ca vivarjayet
annaśuddhau sattvaśuddhirna mṛdā na jalena vai
sattvaśuddhau bhavetsiddhis tato'nnaṃ pariśodhayet
rājapratigrahair dagdhān brāhmaṇān brahmavādinaḥ
svinnānāmapi bījānāṃ punarjanma na vidyate
rājapratigraho ghoro buddhvā cādau viṣopamaḥ
budhena parihartavyaḥ śvamāṃsaṃ cāpi varjayet
asnātvā na ca bhuñjīyād ajapo 'gnim apūjya ca
parṇapṛṣṭhe na bhuñjīyādrātrau dīpaṃ vinā tathā
bhinnabhāṇḍe ca rathyāyāṃ patitānāṃ ca saṃnidhau
śūdraśeṣaṃ na bhuñjīyātsahānnaṃ śiśukairapi
śuddhānnaṃ snigdham aśnīyāt saṃskṛtaṃ cābhimantritam
bhoktā śiva iti smṛtvā maunī caikāgramānasaḥ
āsyena na pibettoyaṃ tiṣṭhannañjalināpi vā
vāmahastena śayyāyāṃ tathaivānyaṃkareṇa vā
vibhītakārkakārañjasnuhicchāyāṃ na cāśrayet
staṃbhadīpamanuṣyāṇāmanyeṣāṃ prāṇināṃ tathā
eko na gacchedadhvānaṃ bāhubhyāṃ nottarennadīm
nāvaroheta kūpādiṃ nāroheduccapādapān
sūryāgnijaladevānāṃ gurūṇāṃ vimukhaḥ śubhe
na kuryādiha kāryāṇi japakarma śubhāni vā
agnau na tāpayetpādau hastaṃ padbhyāṃ na saṃspṛśet
agnernocchrayam āsīta nāgnau kiṃcin malaṃ tyajet
na jalaṃ tāḍayetpadbhyāṃ nāṃbhasyaṅgamalaṃ tyajet
malaṃ prakṣālayet tīre prakṣālya snānamācaret
nakhāgrakeśanirdhūtasnānavastraghaṭodakam
aśrīkaraṃ manuṣyāṇām aśuddhaṃ saṃspṛśedyadi
ajāśvānakhuroṣṭrāṇāṃ mārjanāt tuṣareṇukān
saṃspṛśed yadi mūḍhātmā śriyaṃ hanti harerapi
mārjāraś ca gṛhe yasya so'pyantyajasamo naraḥ
bhojayedyastu viprendrān mārjārasaṃnidhau yadi
taccāṇḍālasamaṃ jñeyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
sphigvātaṃ śūrpavātaṃ ca vātaṃ prāṇamukhānilam
sukṛtāni harantyete saṃspṛṣṭāḥ puruṣasya tu
uṣṇīṣī kañcukī nagno muktakeśo malāvṛtaḥ
apavitrakaro'śuddhaḥ pralapanna japet kvacit
krodho madaḥ kṣudhā tandrā niṣṭhīvanavijṛmbhaṇe
śvanīcadarśanaṃ nidrā pralāpāste japadviṣaḥ
eteṣāṃ saṃbhave vāpi kuryātsūryādidarśanam
ācamya vā japeccheṣaṃ kṛtvā vā prāṇasaṃyamam
sūryo'gniścandramāścaiva grahanakṣatratārakāḥ
ete jyotīṃṣi proktāni vidvadbhir brāhmaṇais tathā
prasārya pādau na japetkukkuṭāsana eva ca
anāsanaḥ śayāno vā rathyāyāṃ śūdrasannidhau
raktabhūmyāṃ ca khaṭvāyāṃ na japejjāpakas tathā
āsanastho japetsamyak mantrārthagatamānasaḥ
kauśeyaṃ vyāghracarmaṃ vā cailaṃ taulamathāpi vā
dāravaṃ tālaparṇaṃ vā āsanaṃ parikalpayet
trisaṃdhyaṃ tu guroḥ pūjā kartavyā hitamicchatā
yo guruḥ sa śivaḥ prokto yaḥ śivaḥ sa guruḥ smṛtaḥ
yathā śivas tathā vidyā yathā vidyā tathā guruḥ
śivavidyāgurostasmādbhaktyā ca sadṛśaṃ phalam
sarvadevamayo devi sarvaśaktimayo hi saḥ
saguṇo nirguṇo vāpi tasyājñāṃ śirasā vahet
śreyo'rthī yastu gurvājñāṃ manasāpi na laṅghayet
gurvājñāpālakaḥ samyak jñānasaṃpattimaśnute
gacchaṃstiṣṭhansvapan bhuñjanyadyatkarma samācaret
samakṣaṃ yadi tatsarvaṃ kartavyaṃ gurvanujñayā
gurordevasamakṣaṃ vā na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet
gururdevo yataḥ sākṣāttadgṛhaṃ devamandiram
pāpinā ca yathāsaṃgāt tatpāpaiḥ patanaṃ bhavet
tadvadācāryasaṃgena taddharmaphalabhāgbhavet
yathaiva vahnisaṃparkānmalaṃ tyajati kāñcanam
tathaiva gurusaṃparkātpāpaṃ tyajati mānavaḥ
yathā vahnisamīpastho ghṛtakuṃbho vilīyate
tathā pāpaṃ vilīyeta ācāryasya samīpataḥ
yathā prajvalito vahnir viṣṭhāṃ kāṣṭhaṃ ca nirdahet
gurustuṣṭo dahatyevaṃ pāpaṃ tanmantratejasā
brahmā haris tathā rudro devāś ca munayas tathā
kurvantyanugrahaṃ tuṣṭā gurau tuṣṭe na saṃśayaḥ
karmaṇā manasā vācā guroḥ krodhaṃ na kārayet
tasya krodhena dahyante āyuḥśrījñānasatkriyāḥ
tatkrodhaṃ ye kariṣyanti teṣāṃ yajñāś ca niṣphalāḥ
japānyaniyamāścaiva nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
gurorviruddhaṃ yadvākyaṃ na vadetsarvayatnataḥ
vaded yadi mahāmohād rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet
cittenaiva ca vittena tathā vācā ca suvratāḥ
mithyā na kārayeddevi kriyayā ca guroḥ sadā
durguṇe khyāpite tasya nairguṇyaśatabhāgbhavet
guṇe tu khyāpite tasya sārvaguṇyaphalaṃ bhavet
gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryādādiṣṭo vā na vā sadā
asamakṣaṃ samakṣaṃ vā guroḥ kāryaṃ samācaret
gurorhitaṃ priyaṃ kuryān manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ
kurvanpatatyadho gatvā tatraiva parivartate
tasmātsa sarvadopāsyo vandanīyaś ca sarvadā
samīpastho 'pyanujñāpya vadettadvimukho gurum
evamācāravān bhakto nityaṃ japaparāyaṇaḥ
gurupriyakaro mantraṃ viniyoktuṃ tato'rhati
viniyogaṃ pravakṣyāmi siddhamantraprayojanam
daurbalyaṃ yāti tanmantraṃ viniyogam ajānataḥ
yasya yena viyuñjīta kāryeṇa tu viśeṣataḥ
viniyogaḥ sa vijñeya aihikāmuṣmikaṃ phalam
viniyogajamāyuṣyamārogyaṃ tanunityatā
rājyaiśvaryaṃ ca vijñānaṃ svargo nirvāṇa eva ca
prokṣaṇaṃ cābhiṣekaṃ ca aghamarṣaṇameva ca
snāne ca saṃdhyayoścaiva kuryādekādaśena vai
śuciḥ parvatamāruhya japellakṣamatandritaḥ
mahānadyāṃ dvilakṣaṃ tu dīrghamāyuravāpnuyāt
dūrvāṅkurāstilā vāṇī guḍūcī ghuṭikā tathā
teṣāṃ tu daśasāhasraṃ homamāyuṣyavardhanam
aśvatthavṛkṣamāśritya japellakṣadvayaṃ sudhīḥ
śanaiścaradine spṛṣṭvā dīrghāyuṣyaṃ labhennaraḥ
śanaiścaradine 'śvatthaṃ pāṇibhyāṃ saṃspṛśetsudhīḥ
japedaṣṭottaraśataṃ somamṛtyuharo bhavet
ādityābhimukho bhūtvā japellakṣamananyadhīḥ
arkairaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā juhvanvyādhervimucyate
samastavyādhiśāntyarthaṃ palāśasamidhair naraḥ
hutvā daśasahasraṃ tu nirogī manujo bhavet
nityamaṣṭaśataṃ japtvā pibed ambho'rkasannidhau
audaryairvyādhibhiḥ sarvairmāsenaikena mucyate
ekādaśena bhuñjīyādannaṃ caivābhimantritam
bhakṣyaṃ cānyattathā peyaṃ viṣamapyamṛtaṃ bhavet
japel lakṣaṃ tu pūrvāhṇe hutvā cāṣṭaśatena vai
sūryaṃ nityamupasthāya samyagārogyamāpnuyāt
nadītoyena sampūrṇaṃ ghaṭaṃ saṃspṛśya śobhanam
japtvāyutaṃ ca tatsnānādrogāṇāṃ bheṣajaṃ bhavet
aṣṭāviṃśajjapitvānnam aśnīyād anvahaṃ śuciḥ
hutvā ca tāvatpālāśair evaṃ vārogyam aśnute
candrasūryagrahe pūrvam upoṣya vidhinā śuciḥ
yāvadgrahaṇamokṣaṃ tu tāvannadyāṃ samāhitaḥ
japetsamudragāminyāṃ vimokṣe grahaṇasya tu
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa pibedbrāhmīrasaṃ dvijāḥ
aihikāṃ labhate medhāṃ sarvaśāstradharāṃ śubhām
sārasvatī bhaveddevī tasya vāgatimānuṣī
grahanakṣatrapīḍāsu japedbhaktyāyutaṃ naraḥ
hutvā cāṣṭasahasraṃ tu grahapīḍāṃ vyapohati
duḥsvapnadarśane snātvā japedvai cāyutaṃ naraḥ
ghṛtenāṣṭaśataṃ hutvā sadyaḥ śāntirbhaviṣyati
candrasūryagrahe liṅgaṃ samabhyarcya yathāvidhi
yat kiṃcit prārthayed devi japedayutamādarāt
saṃnidhāvasya devasya śuciḥ saṃyatamānasaḥ
sarvānkāmānavāpnoti puruṣo nātra saṃśayaḥ
gajānāṃ turagāṇāṃ tu gojātīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ
vyādhyāgame śucirbhūtvā juhuyātsamidhāhutim
māsamabhyarcya vidhināyutaṃ bhaktisamanvitaḥ
teṣāmṛddhiś ca śāntiś ca bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
utpāte śatrubādhāyāṃ juhuyādayutaṃ śuciḥ
pālāśasamidhair devi tasya śāntirbhaviṣyati
ābhicārikabādhāyāmetaddevi samācaret
pratyag bhavati tacchaktiḥ śatroḥ pīḍā bhaviṣyati
vidveṣaṇārthaṃ juhuyādvaibhītasamidhāṣṭakam
akṣarapratilomyena ārdreṇa rudhireṇa vā
viṣeṇa rudhirābhyakto vidveṣaṇakaraṃ nṛṇām
prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpaviśuddhaye
pāpaśuddhiryathā samyak kartumabhyudyato naraḥ
pāpaśuddhir yataḥ samyag jñānasaṃpattihaitukī
pāpaśuddhirna cetpuṃsaḥ kriyāḥ sarvāścaniṣphalāḥ
jñānaṃ ca hīyate tasmātkartavyaṃ pāpaśodhanam
vidyālakṣmīviśuddhyarthaṃ māṃ dhyātvāñjalinā śubhe
śivenaikādaśenādbhir abhiṣiñcetsamantataḥ
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva snāyātpāpaviśuddhaye
sarvatīrthaphalaṃ tacca sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham
saṃdhyopāsanavicchede japedaṣṭaśataṃ naraḥ
viḍvarāhaiś ca cāṇḍālairdurjanaiḥ kukkuṭairapi
spṛṣṭamannaṃ na bhuñjīta bhuktvā cāṣṭaśataṃ japet
brahmahatyāviśuddhyarthaṃ japellakṣāyutaṃ naraḥ
pātakānāṃ tadardhaṃ syānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā
upapātakaduṣṭānāṃ tadardhaṃ parikīrtitam
śeṣāṇāmapi pāpānāṃ japetpañcasahasrakam
ātmabodhaparaṃ guhyaṃ śivabodhaprakāśakam
śivaḥ syātsa japenmantraṃ pañcalakṣam anākulaḥ
pañcavāyujayaṃ bhadre prāpnoti manujaḥ sukham
japecca pañcalakṣaṃ tu vigṛhītendriyaḥ śuciḥ
pañcendriyāṇāṃ vijayo bhaviṣyati varānane
dhyānayukto japedyastu pañcalakṣam anākulaḥ
viṣayāṇāṃ ca pañcānāṃ jayaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
caturthaṃ pañcalakṣaṃ tu yo japedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ
bhūtānāmiha pañcānāṃ vijayaṃ manujo labhet
caturlakṣaṃ japedyastu manaḥ saṃyamya yatnataḥ
samyagvijayamāpnoti karaṇānāṃ varānane
pañcaviṃśatilakṣāṇāṃ japena kamalānane
pañcaviṃśatitattvānāṃ vijayaṃ manujo labhet
madhyarātre 'tinirvāte japedayutamādarāt
brahmasiddhimavāpnoti vratenānena suṃdari
japellakṣamanālasyo nirvāte dhvanivarjite
madhyarātre ca śivayoḥ paśyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
andhakāravināśaś ca dīpasyeva prakāśanam
hṛdayāntarbahirvāpi bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhyarthaṃ japedayutamātmavān
sabījasaṃpuṭaṃ mantraṃ śatalakṣaṃ japecchuciḥ
matsāyujyamavāpnoti bhaktimān kimataḥ param
iti te sarvamākhyātaṃ pañcākṣaravidhikramam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
śrāvayecca dvijāñchuddhānpañcākṣaravidhikramam
daive karmaṇi pitrye vā śivaloke mahīyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pañcākṣaramāhātmyaṃ nāma pañcāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
japācchreṣṭhatamaṃ prāhurbrāhmaṇā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ
viraktānāṃ prabuddhānāṃ dhyānayajñaṃ suśobhanam
tasmādvadasva sūtādya dhyānayajñam aśeṣataḥ
vistārātsarvayatnena viraktānāṃ mahātmanām
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā munīnāṃ dīrghasattriṇām
rudreṇa kathitaṃ prāha guhāṃ prāpya mahātmanām
saṃhṛtya kālakūṭākhyaṃ viṣaṃ vai viśvakarmaṇā
sūta uvāca
guhāṃ prāpya sukhāsīnaṃ bhavānyā saha śaṅkaram
munayaḥ saṃśitātmānaḥ praṇemustaṃ guhāśrayam
astuvaṃś ca tataḥ sarve nīlakaṇṭhamumāpatim
atyugraṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ saṃhṛtaṃ bhagavaṃstvayā
ataḥ pratiṣṭhitaṃ sarvaṃ tvayā deva vṛṣadhvaja
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
prahasanprāha viśvātmā sanandanapurogamān
kimanena dvijaśreṣṭhā viṣaṃ vakṣye sudāruṇam
saṃharettadviṣaṃ yastu sa samartho hyanena kim
na viṣaṃ kālakūṭākhyaṃ saṃsāro viṣamucyate
tasmātsarvaprayatnena saṃhareta sudāruṇam
saṃsāro dvividhaḥ proktaḥ svādhikārānurūpataḥ
puṃsāṃ saṃmūḍhacittānām asaṃkṣīṇaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
īṣaṇārāgadoṣeṇa sargo jñānena suvratāḥ
tadvaśādeva sarveṣāṃ dharmādharmau na saṃśayaḥ
asannikṛṣṭe tvarthe'pi śāstraṃ tacchravaṇātsatām
buddhimutpādayatyeva saṃsāre viduṣāṃ dvijāḥ
tasmāddṛṣṭānuśravikaṃ duṣṭamityubhayātmakam
saṃtyajetsarvayatnena viraktaḥ so'bhidhīyate
śāstramityucyate bhāgaṃ śruteḥ karmasu taddvijāḥ
mūrdhānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sāramṛṣīṇāṃ karmaṇaḥ phalam
nanu svabhāvaḥ sarveṣāṃ kāmo dṛṣṭo na cānyathā
śrutiḥ pravartikā teṣāmiti karmaṇyatadvidaḥ
nivṛttilakṣaṇo dharmaḥ samarthānām ihocyate
