tasmādajñānamūlo hi saṃsāraḥ sarvadehinām
kalā saṃśoṣamāyāti karmaṇānyasvabhāvataḥ
sakalastrividho jīvo jñānahīnastvavidyayā
nārakī pāpakṛtsvargī puṇyakṛt puṇyagauravāt
vyatimiśreṇa vai jīvaścaturdhā saṃvyavasthitaḥ
udbhijjaḥ svedajaścaiva aṇḍajo vai jarāyujaḥ
evaṃ vyavasthito dehī karmaṇājño hyanirvṛtaḥ
prajayā karmaṇā muktirdhanena ca satāṃ na hi
tyāgenaikena muktiḥ syāttadabhāvādbhramatyasau
evamajñānadoṣeṇa nānākarmavaśena ca
ṣaṭkauśikaṃ samudbhūtaṃ bhajatyeṣa kalevaram
garbhe duḥkhānyanekāni yonimārge ca bhūtale
kaumāre yauvane caiva vārddhake maraṇe'pi vā
vicārataḥ satāṃ duḥkhaṃ strīsaṃsargādibhir dvijāḥ
duḥkhenaikena vai duḥkhaṃ praśāmyatīha duḥkhinaḥ
na jātu kāmaḥ kāmānām upabhogena śāmyati
haviṣā kṛṣṇavartmeva bhūya evābhivardhate
tasmādvicārato nāsti saṃyogādapi vai nṛṇām
arthānām arjane'pyevaṃ pālane ca vyaye tathā
paiśāce rākṣase duḥkhaṃ yākṣe caiva vicārataḥ
gāndharve ca tathā cāndre saumyaloke dvijottamāḥ
prājāpatye tathā brāhme prākṛte pauruṣe tathā
kṣayasātiśayādyaistu duḥkhairduḥkhāni suvratāḥ
tāni bhāgyānyaśuddhāni saṃtyajecca dhanāni ca
tasmādaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhogaṃ tathā ṣoḍaśadhā sthitam
caturviṃśatprakāreṇa saṃsthitaṃ cāpi suvratāḥ
dvātriṃśadbhedamanaghāścatvāriṃśadguṇaṃ punaḥ
tathāṣṭacatvāriṃśacca ṣaṭpañcāśatprakārataḥ
catuḥṣaṣṭividhaṃ caiva duḥkhameva vivekinaḥ
pārthivaṃ ca tathāpyaṃ ca taijasaṃ ca vicārataḥ
vāyavyaṃ ca tathā vyaumamānasaṃ ca yathākramam
ābhimānikamapyevaṃ bauddhaṃ prākṛtameva ca
duḥkhameva na saṃdeho yogināṃ brahmavādinām
gauṇaṃ gaṇeśvarāṇāṃ ca duḥkhameva vicārataḥ
ādau madhye tathā cānte sarvalokeṣu sarvadā
vartamānāni duḥkhāni bhaviṣyāṇi yathātatham
doṣaduṣṭeṣu deśeṣu duḥkhāni vividhāni ca
na bhāvayantyatītāni hyajñāne jñānamāninaḥ
kṣudvyādheḥ parihārārthaṃ na sukhāyānnamucyate
yathetareṣāṃ rogāṇāmauṣadhaṃ na sukhāya tat
śītoṣṇavātavarṣādyais tattatkāleṣu dehinām
duḥkhameva na saṃdeho na jānanti hyapaṇḍitāḥ
svarge'pyevaṃ muniśreṣṭhā hyaviśuddhakṣayādibhiḥ
rogair nānāvidhair grastā rāgadveṣabhayādibhiḥ
chinnamūlataruryadvadavaśaḥ patati kṣitau
puṇyavṛkṣakṣayāttadvadgāṃ patanti divaukasaḥ
duḥkhābhilāṣaniṣṭhānāṃ duḥkhabhogādisaṃpadām
asmāttu patatāṃ duḥkhaṃ kaṣṭaṃ svargāddivaukasām
narake duḥkhamevātra narakāṇāṃ niṣevaṇāt
vihitākaraṇāccaiva varṇināṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
yathā mṛgo mṛtyubhayasya bhīta ucchinnavāso na labheta nidrām
evaṃ yatirdhyānaparo mahātmā saṃsārabhīto na labheta nidrām
kīṭapakṣimṛgāṇāṃ ca paśūnāṃ gajavājinām
dṛṣṭam evāsukhaṃ tasmāt tyajataḥ sukhamuttamam
vaimānikānāmapyevaṃ duḥkhaṃ kalpādhikāriṇām
sthānābhimānināṃ caiva manvādīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ
devānāṃ caiva daityānāmanyonyavijigīṣayā
duḥkhameva nṛpāṇāṃ ca rākṣasānāṃ jagattraye
śramārthamāśramaścāpi varṇānāṃ paramārthataḥ
āśramairna ca devaiś ca yajñaiḥ sāṃkhyairvratais tathā
ugraistapobhir vividhairdānairnānāvidhairapi
na labhante tathātmānaṃ labhante jñāninaḥ svayam
tasmātsarvaprayatnena caretpāśupatavratam
bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ vrate pāśupate budhaḥ
pañcārthajñānasampannaḥ śivatattve samāhitaḥ
kaivalyakaraṇaṃ yogaṃ vividhakarmacchidaṃ budhaḥ
pañcārthayogasampanno duḥkhāntaṃ vrajate sudhīḥ
parayā vidyayā vedyaṃ vidantyaparayā na hi
dve vidye veditavye hi parā caivāparā tathā
aparā tatra ṛgvedo yajurvedo dvijottamāḥ
sāmavedastathātharvo vedaḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ chanda eva ca
jyotiṣaṃ cāparā vidyā parākṣaramiti sthitam
tadadṛśyaṃ tadagrāhyamagotraṃ tadavarṇakam
tad acakṣus tad aśrotraṃ tad apāṇi apādakam
tad ajātam abhūtaṃ ca tad aśabdaṃ dvijottamāḥ
asparśaṃ tadarūpaṃ ca rasagandhavivarjitam
avyayaṃ cāpratiṣṭhaṃ ca tannityaṃ sarvagaṃ vibhum
mahāntaṃ tad bṛhantaṃ ca tadajaṃ cinmayaṃ dvijāḥ
aprāṇamamanaskaṃ ca tadasnigdhamalohitam
aprameyaṃ tadasthūlamadīrghaṃ tadanulbaṇam
ahrasvaṃ tadapāraṃ ca tadānandaṃ tadacyutam
anapāvṛtamadvaitaṃ tadanantamagocaram
asaṃvṛtaṃ tadātmaikaṃ parā vidyā na cānyathā
parāpareti kathite naiveha paramārthataḥ
ahameva jagatsarvaṃ mayyeva sakalaṃ jagat
matta utpadyate tiṣṭhanmayi mayyeva līyate
matto nānyaditīkṣeta manovākpāṇibhis tathā
sarvamātmani saṃpaśyetsaccāsacca samāhitaḥ
sarvaṃ hyātmani saṃpaśyan na bāhye kurute manaḥ
adhodṛṣṭyā vitastyāṃ tu nābhyāmuparitiṣṭhati
hṛdayaṃ tadvijānīyād viśvasyāyatanaṃ mahat
hṛdayasyāsya madhye tu puṇḍarīkamavasthitam
dharmakandasamudbhūtaṃ jñānanālaṃ suśobhanam
aiśvaryāṣṭadalaṃ śvetaṃ paraṃ vairāgyakarṇikam
chidrāṇi ca diśo yasya prāṇādyāś ca pratiṣṭhitāḥ
prāṇādyaiścaiva saṃyuktaḥ paśyate bahudhā kramāt
daśaprāṇavahā nāḍyaḥ pratyekaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
dvisaptatisahasrāṇi nāḍyaḥ samparikīrtitāḥ
netrasthaṃ jāgrataṃ vidyātkaṇṭhe svapnaṃ samādiśet
suṣuptaṃ hṛdayasthaṃ tu turīyaṃ mūrdhani sthitam
jāgre brahmā ca viṣṇuś ca svapne caiva yathākramāt
īśvarastu suṣupte tu turīye ca maheśvaraḥ
vadanty evam athānye 'pi samastakaraṇaiḥ pumān
vartamānastadā tasya jāgradityabhidhīyate
manobuddhir ahaṅkāraṃ cittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam
yadā vyavasthitastvetaiḥ svapna ityabhidhīyate
karaṇāni vilīnāni yadā svātmani suvratāḥ
suṣuptaḥ karaṇairbhinnasturīyaḥ parikīrtyate
parasturīyātīto'sau śivaḥ paramakāraṇam
jāgratsvapnasuṣuptiś ca turīyaṃ cādhibhautikam
ādhyātmikaṃ ca viprendrāścādhidaivikamucyate
tatsarvamaham eveti veditavyaṃ vijānatā
buddhīndriyāṇi viprendrās tathā karmendriyāṇi ca
manobuddhir ahaṅkāraś cittaṃ ceti catuṣṭayam
adhyātmaṃ pṛthagevedaṃ caturdaśavidhaṃ smṛtam
draṣṭavyaṃ caiva śrotavyaṃ ghrātavyaṃ ca yathākramam
rasitavyaṃ muniśreṣṭhāḥ sparśitavyaṃ tathaiva ca
mantavyaṃ caiva boddhavyam ahaṃkartavyameva ca
tathā cetayitavyaṃ ca vaktavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
ādātavyaṃ ca gantavyaṃ visargāyitameva ca
ānanditavyamityete hyadhibhūtamanukramāt
ādityo'pi diśaścaiva pṛthivī varuṇas tathā
vāyuścandras tathā brahmā rudraḥ kṣetrajña eva ca
agnirindras tathā viṣṇurmitro devaḥ prajāpatiḥ
ādhidaivikamevaṃ hi caturdaśavidhaṃ kramāt
rājñī sudarśanā caiva jitā saumyā yathākramam
moghā rudrāmṛtā satyā madhyamā ca dvijottamāḥ
nāḍī rāśiśukā caiva asurā caiva kṛttikā
bhāsvatī nāḍayaścaitāścaturdaśanibandhanāḥ
vāyavo nāḍimadhyasthā vāhakāś ca caturdaśa
prāṇo vyānastvapānaś ca udānaś ca samānakaḥ
vairambhaś ca tathā mukhyo hyantaryāmaḥ prabhañjanaḥ
kūrmakaś ca tathā śyenaḥ śvetaḥ kṛṣṇas tathānilaḥ
nāga ityeva kathitā vāyavaś ca caturdaśa
yaścakṣuḥṣvatha draṣṭavye tathāditye ca suvratāḥ
nāḍyāṃ prāṇe ca vijñāne tvānande ca yathākramam
hṛdyākāśe ya etasminsarvasminnantare paraḥ
ātmā ekaś ca carati tamupāsīta māṃ prabhum
ajaraṃ tamanantaṃ ca aśokamamṛtaṃ dhruvam
caturdaśavidheṣveva saṃcaratyeka eva saḥ
līyante tāni tatraiva yadanyaṃ nāsti vai dvijāḥ
eka eva hi sarvajñaḥ sarveśastveka eva saḥ
eṣa sarvādhipo devastvantaryāmī mahādyutiḥ
upāsyamānaḥ sarvasya sarvasaukhyaḥ sanātanaḥ
upāsyati na caiveha sarvasaukhyaṃ dvijottamāḥ
upāsyamāno vedaiś ca śāstrairnānāvidhairapi
na vaiṣa vedaśāstrāṇi sarvajño yāsyati prabhuḥ
asyaivānnamidaṃ sarvaṃ na so'nnaṃ bhavati svayam
svātmanā rakṣitaṃ cādyādannabhūtaṃ na kutracit
sarvatra prāṇināmannaṃ prāṇināṃ granthirasmyaham
praśāstā nayanaścaiva pañcātmā sa vibhāgaśaḥ
annamayo'sau bhūtātmā cādyate hyannamucyate
prāṇamayaścendriyātmā saṃkalpātmā manomayaḥ
kālātmā soma eveha vijñānamaya ucyate
sadānandamayo bhūtvā maheśaḥ parameśvaraḥ
so'ham evaṃ jagatsarvaṃ mayyeva sakalaṃ sthitam
paratantraṃ svatantre'pi tadabhāvādvicārataḥ
ekatvamapi nāstyeva dvaitaṃ tatra kutastvaho
evaṃ nāstyatha martyaṃ ca kuto 'mṛtamajodbhavaḥ
nāntaḥprajño bahiḥprajño na cobhayagatas tathā
na prajñānaghanastvevaṃ na prājño jñānapūrvakaḥ
viditaṃ nāsti vedyaṃ ca nirvāṇaṃ paramārthataḥ
nirvāṇaṃ caiva kaivalyaṃ niḥśreyasamanāmayam
amṛtaṃ cākṣaraṃ brahma paramātmā parāparam
nirvikalpaṃ nirābhāsaṃ jñānaṃ paryāyavācakam
prasannaṃ ca yadekāgraṃ tadā jñānamiti smṛtam
ajñānamitaratsarvaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
itthaṃ prasannaṃ vijñānaṃ gurusaṃparkajaṃ dhruvam
rāgadveṣānṛtakrodhaṃ kāmatṛṣṇādibhiḥ sadā
aparāmṛṣṭamadyaiva vijñeyaṃ muktidaṃ tvidam
ajñānamalapūrvatvātpuruṣo malinaḥ smṛtaḥ
tatkṣayāddhi bhavenmuktirnānyathā janmakoṭibhiḥ
jñānamekaṃ vinā nāsti puṇyapāpaparikṣayaḥ
jñānam evābhyaset tasmān muktyarthaṃ brahmavittamāḥ
jñānābhyāsāddhi vai puṃsāṃ buddhirbhavati nirmalā
tasmātsadābhyasejjñānaṃ tanniṣṭhastatparāyaṇaḥ
jñānenaikena tṛptasya tyaktasaṃgasya yoginaḥ
kartavyaṃ nāsti viprendrā asti cettattvavinna ca
iha loke pare cāpi kartavyaṃ nāsti tasya vai
jīvanmukto yatas tasmād brahmavit paramārthataḥ
jñānābhyāsarato nityaṃ jñānatattvārthavit svayam
kartavyābhyāsamutsṛjya jñānamevādhigacchati
varṇāśramābhimānī yastyaktakrodho dvijottamāḥ
anyatra ramate mūḍhaḥ so 'jñānī nātra saṃśayaḥ
saṃsāraheturajñānaṃ saṃsārastanusaṃgrahaḥ
mokṣahetus tathā jñānaṃ muktaḥ svātmanyavasthitaḥ
ajñāne sati viprendrāḥ krodhādyā nātra saṃśayaḥ
krodho harṣas tathā lobho moho dambho dvijottamāḥ
dharmādharmau hi teṣāṃ ca tadvaśāttanusaṃgrahaḥ
śarīre sati vai kleśaḥ so'vidyāṃ saṃtyajedbudhaḥ
avidyāṃ vidyayā hitvā sthitasyaiva ca yoginaḥ
krodhādyā nāśamāyānti dharmādharmau ca vai dvijāḥ
tatkṣayācca śarīreṇa na punaḥ samprayujyate
sa eva muktaḥ saṃsārādduḥkhatrayavivarjitaḥ
evaṃ jñānaṃ vinā nāsti dhyānaṃ dhyātur dvijarṣabhāḥ
jñānaṃ gurorhi saṃparkānna vācā paramārthataḥ
caturvyūhamiti jñātvā dhyātā dhyānaṃ samabhyaset
sahajāgantukaṃ pāpamasthivāgudbhavaṃ tathā
jñānāgnirdahate kṣipraṃ śuṣkendhanam ivānalaḥ
jñānātparataraṃ nāsti sarvapāpavināśanam
abhyasecca sadā jñānaṃ sarvasaṃgavivarjitaḥ
jñāninaḥ sarvapāpāni jīryante nātra saṃśayaḥ
krīḍannapi na lipyeta pāpairnānāvidhairapi
jñānaṃ yathā tathā dhyānaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samabhyaset
dhyānaṃ nirviṣayaṃ proktam ādau saviṣayaṃ tathā
ṣaṭprakāraṃ samabhyasya catuḥṣaḍdaśabhis tathā
tathā dvādaśadhā caiva punaḥ ṣoḍaśadhā kramāt
dvidhābhyasya ca yogīndro mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
śuddhajāṃbūnadākāraṃ vidhūmāṅgārasannibham
pītaṃ raktaṃ sitaṃ vidyutkoṭikoṭisamaprabham
athavā brahmarandhrasthaṃ cittaṃ kṛtvā prayatnataḥ
na sitaṃ vāsitaṃ pītaṃ na smared brahmavid bhavet
ahiṃsakaḥ satyavādī asteyī sarvayatnataḥ
parigrahavinirmukto brahmacārī dṛḍhavrataḥ
saṃtuṣṭaḥ śaucasampannaḥ svādhyāyanirataḥ sadā
madraktaścābhyaseddhyānaṃ gurusaṃparkajaṃ dhruvam
na budhyati tathā dhyātā sthāpya cittaṃ dvijottamāḥ
na cābhimanyate yogī na paśyati samantataḥ
na ghrāti na śṛṇotyeva līnaḥ svātmani yaḥ svayam
na ca sparśaṃ vijānāti sa vai samarasaḥ smṛtaḥ
pārthive paṭale brahmā vāritattve hariḥ svayam
vāhneye kālarudrākhyo vāyutattve maheśvaraḥ
suṣire sa śivaḥ sākṣātkramādevaṃ vicintayet
kṣitau śarvaḥ smṛto devo hy apāṃ bhava iti smṛtaḥ
rudra eva tathā vahnau ugro vāyau vyavasthitaḥ
bhīmaḥ suṣiranāke 'sau bhāskare maṇḍale sthitaḥ
īśānaḥ somabimbe ca mahādeva iti smṛtaḥ
puṃsāṃ paśupatirdevaścāṣṭadhāhaṃ vyavasthitaḥ
kāṭhinyaṃ yattanau sarvaṃ pārthivaṃ parigīyate
āpyaṃ dravamiti proktaṃ varṇākhyo vahnirucyate
yatsaṃcarati tadvāyuḥ suṣiraṃ yaddvijottamāḥ
tadākāśaṃ ca vijñānaṃ śabdajaṃ vyomasaṃbhavam
tathaiva viprā vijñānaṃ sparśākhyaṃ vāyusaṃbhavam
rūpaṃ vāhneyamityuktamāpyaṃ rasamayaṃ dvijāḥ
gandhākhyaṃ pārthivaṃ bhūyaścintayedbhāskaraṃ kramāt
netre ca dakṣiṇe vāme somaṃ hṛdi vibhuṃ dvijāḥ
ājānu pṛthivītattvam ānābher vārimaṇḍalam
ākaṇṭhaṃ vahnitattvaṃ syāllalāṭāntaṃ dvijottamāḥ
vāyavyaṃ vai lalāṭādyaṃ vyomākhyaṃ vā śikhāgrakam
haṃsākhyaṃ ca tato brahma vyomnaścordhvaṃ tataḥ param
vyomākhyo vyomamadhyastho hyayaṃ prāthamikaḥ smaret
na jīvaḥ prakṛtiḥ sattvaṃ rajaścātha tamaḥ punaḥ
mahāṃstathābhimānaś ca tanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca
vyomādīni ca bhūtāni naiveha paramārthataḥ
vyāpya tiṣṭhadyato viśvaṃ sthāṇurityabhidhīyate
udeti sūryo bhītaś ca pavate vāta eva ca
dyotate candramā vahnirjvalatyāpo vahanti ca
dadhāti bhūmirākāśamavakāśaṃ dadāti ca
tadājñayā tataṃ sarvaṃ tasmādvai cintayeddvijāḥ
tenaivādhiṣṭhitaṃ tasmādetatsarvaṃ dvijottamāḥ
sarvarūpamayaḥ śarva iti matvā smaredbhavam
saṃsāraviṣataptānāṃ jñānadhyānāmṛtena vai
pratīkāraḥ samākhyāto nānyathā dvijasattamāḥ
jñānaṃ dharmodbhavaṃ sākṣājjñānād vairāgyasaṃbhavaḥ
vairāgyātparamaṃ jñānaṃ paramārthaprakāśakam
jñānavairāgyayuktasya yogasiddhirdvijottamāḥ
yogasiddhyā vimuktiḥ syātsattvaniṣṭhasya nānyathā
tamovidyāpadacchannaṃ citraṃ yatpadamavyayam
sattvaśaktiṃ samāsthāya śivamabhyarcayeddvijāḥ
yaḥ sattvaniṣṭho madbhakto madarcanaparāyaṇaḥ
sarvato dharmaniṣṭhaś ca sadotsāhī samāhitaḥ
sarvadvandvasaho dhīraḥ sarvabhūtahite rataḥ
ṛjusvabhāvaḥ satataṃ svasthacitto mṛduḥ sadā
amānī buddhimāñchāntastyaktaspardho dvijottamāḥ
sadā mumukṣurdharmajñaḥ svātmalakṣaṇalakṣaṇaḥ
ṛṇatrayavinirmuktaḥ pūrvajanmani puṇyabhāk
jarāyukto dvijo bhūtvā śraddhayā ca guroḥ kramāt
anyathā vāpi śuśrūṣāṃ kṛtvā kṛtrimavarjitaḥ
svargalokamanuprāpya bhuktvā bhogānanukramāt
āsādya bhārataṃ varṣaṃ brahmavijjāyate dvijāḥ
saṃparkājjñānamāsādya jñānino yogavidbhavet
kramo'yaṃ malapūrṇasya jñānaprāpterdvijottamāḥ
tasmādanena mārgeṇa tyaktasaṃgo dṛḍhavrataḥ
saṃsārakālakūṭākhyānmucyate munipuṅgavāḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mayā yuṣmākamacyutam
jñānasyaiveha māhātmyaṃ prasaṃgādiha śobhanam
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kathitaṃ tvīśvareṇa tu
na deyaṃ yasya kasyāpi śivoktaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
dātavyaṃ yogine nityaṃ bhasmaniṣṭhāya supriyam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi saṃsāraśamanaṃ naraḥ
sa yāti brahmasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge saṃsāraviṣakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍaśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
niśamya te mahāprājñāḥ kumārādyāḥ pinākinam
procuḥ praṇamya vai bhītāḥ prasannaṃ parameśvaram
evaṃ cedanayā devyā haimavatyā maheśvara
krīḍase vividhairbhogaiḥ kathaṃ vaktumihārhasi
sūta uvāca
evamuktaḥ prahasyeśaḥ pinākī nīlalohitaḥ
prāha tām aṃbikāṃ prekṣya praṇipatya sthitān dvijān
bandhamokṣau na caiveha mama svecchā śarīriṇaḥ
akartajñaḥ paśurjīvo vibhurbhoktā hyaṇuḥ pumān
māyī ca māyayā baddhaḥ karmabhir yujyate tu saḥ
jñānaṃ dhyānaṃ ca bandhaś ca mokṣo nāstyātmano dvijāḥ
yadaivaṃ mayi vidvān yastasyāpi na ca sarvataḥ
eṣā vidyā hyahaṃ vedyaḥ prajñaiṣā ca śrutiḥ smṛtiḥ
dhṛtireṣā mayā niṣṭhā jñānaśaktiḥ kriyā tathā
icchākhyā ca tathā hyājñā dve vidye na ca saṃśayaḥ
na hyeṣā prakṛtirjaivī vikṛtiś ca vicārataḥ
vikāro naiva māyaiṣā sadasadvyaktivarjitā
purā mamājñā madvaktrātsamutpannā sanātanī
pañcavaktrā mahābhāgā jagatāmabhayapradā
tāmājñāṃ sampraviśyāhaṃ cintayan jagatāṃ hitam
saptaviṃśatprakāreṇa sarvaṃ vyāpyānayā śivaḥ
tadāprabhṛti vai mokṣapravṛttirdvijasattamāḥ
sūta uvāca
evamuktvā tadāpaśyadbhavānīṃ parameśvaraḥ
bhavānī ca tamālokya māyāmaharadavyayā
te māyāmalanirmuktā munayaḥ prekṣya pārvatīm
prītā babhūvurmuktāś ca tasmādeṣā parā gatiḥ
umāśaṅkarayorbhedo nāstyeva paramārthataḥ
dvidhāsau rūpamāsthāya sthita eva na saṃśayaḥ
yadā vidvānasaṃgaḥ syādājñayā parameṣṭhinaḥ
tadā muktiḥ kṣaṇādeva nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ
kramo 'vivakṣito bhūtavivṛddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
prasādena kṣaṇānmuktiḥ pratijñaiṣā na saṃśayaḥ
garbhastho jāyamāno vā bālo vā taruṇo'pi vā
vṛddho vā mucyate jantuḥ prasādātparameṣṭhinaḥ
aṇḍajaś codbhijjo vāpi svedajo vāpi mucyate
prasādāddevadevasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
eṣa eva jagannātho bandhamokṣakaraḥ śivaḥ
bhūrbhūvaḥsvarmahaś caiva janaḥ sākṣāttapaḥ svayam
satyalokas tathāṇḍānāṃ koṭikoṭiśatāni ca
vigrahaṃ devadevasya tathāṇḍāvaraṇāṣṭakam
saptadvīpeṣu sarveṣu parvateṣu vaneṣu ca
samudreṣu ca sarveṣu vāyuskandheṣu sarvataḥ
tathānyeṣu ca lokeṣu vasanti ca carācarāḥ
sarve bhavāṃśajā nūnaṃ gatistveṣāṃ sa eva vai
sarvo rudro namastasmai puruṣāya mahātmane
viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ tathā jātaṃ bahudhā rudra eva saḥ
rudrājñaiṣā sthitā devī hyanayā muktiraṃbikā
ityevaṃ khecarāḥ siddhā jajalpuḥ prītamānasāḥ
yadāvalokya tān sarvānprasādādanayāṃbikā
tadā tiṣṭhanti sāyujyaṃ prāptāste khecarāḥ prabhoḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge munimohaśamanaṃ nāma saptāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kena yogena vai sūta guṇaprāptiḥ satāmiha
aṇimādiguṇopetā bhavantyeveha yoginaḥ
tatsarvaṃ vistarātsūta vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaṃ paramadurlabham
pañcadhā saṃsmaredādau sthāpya citte sanātanam
kalpayeccāsanaṃ padmaṃ somasūryāgnisaṃyutam
ṣaḍviṃśacchaktisaṃyuktamaṣṭadhā ca dvijottamāḥ
tataḥ ṣoḍaśadhā caiva punardvādaśadhā dvijāḥ
smarec ca tat tathā madhye devyā devam umāpatim
aṣṭaśaktisamāyuktamaṣṭamūrtimajaṃ prabhum
tābhiścāṣṭavidhā rudrāścatuḥṣaṣṭividhāḥ punaḥ
śaktayaś ca tathā sarvā guṇāṣṭakasamanvitāḥ
evaṃ smaretkrameṇaiva labdhvā jñānamanuttamam
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ mokṣasiddhipradāyakam
tasyāṇimādayo viprā nānyathā karmakoṭibhiḥ
tatrāṣṭaguṇamaiśvaryaṃ yogināṃ samudāhṛtam
tatsarvaṃ kramayogena hyucyamānaṃ nibodhata
aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptireva ca
prākāmyaṃ caiva sarvatra īśitvaṃ caiva sarvataḥ
vaśitvamatha sarvatra yatra kāmāvasāyitā
taccāpi trividhaṃ jñeyamaiśvaryaṃ sārvakāmikam
sāvadyaṃ niravadyaṃ ca sūkṣmaṃ caiva pravartate
sāvadyaṃ nāma yattatra pañcabhūtātmakaṃ smṛtam
indriyāṇi manaścaiva ahaṅkāraś ca yaḥ smṛtaḥ
tatra sūkṣmapravṛttistu pañcabhūtātmikā punaḥ
indriyāṇi manaścittabuddhyahaṅkārasaṃjñitam
tathā sarvamayaṃ caiva ātmasthā khyātireva ca
saṃyoga eva trividhaḥ sūkṣmeṣveva pravartate
punaraṣṭaguṇaścāpi sūkṣmeṣveva vidhīyate
tasya rūpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāha bhagavānprabhuḥ
trailokye sarvabhūteṣu yathāsya niyamaḥ smṛtaḥ
aṇimādyaṃ tathāvyaktaṃ sarvatraiva pratiṣṭhitam
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ duṣprāpyaṃ samudāhṛtam
tat tasya bhavati prāpyaṃ prathamaṃ yogināṃ balam
laṅghanaṃ plavanaṃ loke rūpamasya sadā bhavet
śīghratvaṃ sarvabhūteṣu dvitīyaṃ tu padaṃ smṛtam
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ mahimnā caiva vanditam
mahitvaṃ cāpi loke'smiṃs tṛtīyo yoga ucyate
trailokye sarvabhūteṣu yatheṣṭagamanaṃ smṛtam
prākāmān viṣayān bhuṅkte tathāpratihataḥ kvacit
trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ sukhaduḥkhaṃ pravartate
īśo bhavati sarvatra pravibhāgena yogavit
vaśyāni cāsya bhūtāni trailokye sacarācare
icchayā tasya rūpāṇi bhavanti na bhavanti ca
yatra kāmāvasāyitvaṃ trailokye sacarācare
śabdaḥ sparśo raso gandho rūpaṃ caiva manas tathā
pravartante 'sya cecchāto na bhavanti yathecchayā
na jāyate na mriyate chidyate na ca bhidyate
na dahyate na muhyeta līyate na ca lipyate
na kṣīyate na kṣarati khidyate na kadācana
kriyate vā na sarvatra tathā vikriyate na ca
agandharasarūpastu asparśaḥ śabdavarjitaḥ
avarṇo hyasvaraś caiva asavarṇastu karhicit
sa bhuṅkte viṣayāṃścaiva viṣayairna ca yujyate
aṇutvāttu paraḥ sūkṣmaḥ sūkṣmatvād apavargikaḥ
vyāpakastvapavargācca vyāpakātpuruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ
puruṣaḥ sūkṣmabhāvāttu aiśvarye parame sthitaḥ
guṇottaramathaiśvarye sarvataḥ sūkṣmamucyate
aiśvaryaṃ cāpratīghātaṃ prāpya yogamanuttamam
apavargaṃ tato gacchetsūkṣmaṃ tatparamaṃ padam
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ jñātavyaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
svargāpavargaphaladaṃ śivasāyujyakāraṇam
athavā gatavijñāno rāgātkarma samācaret
rājasaṃ tāmasaṃ vāpi bhuktvā tatraiva mucyate
tathā sukṛtakarmā tu phalaṃ svarge samaśnute
tasmātsthānātpunaḥ śreṣṭho mānuṣyamupapadyate
tasmādbrahma paraṃ saukhyaṃ brahma śāśvatam uttamam
brahma eva hi seveta brahmaiva hi paraṃ sukham
pariśramo hi yajñānāṃ mahatārthena vartate
bhūyo mṛtyuvaśaṃ yāti tasmānmokṣaḥ paraṃ sukham
athavā dhyānasaṃyukto brahmatattvaparāyaṇaḥ
na tu cyāvayituṃ śakyo manvantaraśatairapi
dṛṣṭvā tu puruṣaṃ divyaṃ viśvākhyaṃ viśvatomukham
viśvapādaśirogrīvaṃ viśveśaṃ viśvarūpiṇam
viśvagandhaṃ viśvamālyaṃ viśvāṃbaradharaṃ prabhum
gobhir mahīṃ saṃpatate patatriṇo naivaṃ bhūyo janayatyevameva
kaviṃ purāṇam anuśāsitāraṃ sūkṣmācca sūkṣmaṃ mahato mahāntam
yogena paśyenna ca cakṣuṣā punarnirindriyaṃ puruṣaṃ rukmavarṇam
aliṅginaṃ nirguṇaṃ cetanaṃ ca nityaṃ sadā sarvagaṃ sarvasāram
paśyanti yuktyā hyacalaprakāśaṃ tadbhāvitāstejasā dīpyamānam
apāṇipādodarapārśvajihvo hyatīndriyo vāpi susūkṣma ekaḥ
paśyatyacakṣuḥ sa śṛṇotyakarṇo na cāstyabuddhaṃ na ca buddhir asti
sa veda sarvaṃ na ca sarvavedyaṃ tamāhuragryaṃ puruṣaṃ mahāntam
acetanāṃ sarvagatāṃ sūkṣmāṃ prasavadharmiṇīm
prakṛtiṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ yuktāḥ paśyanti yoginaḥ
sarvataḥ pāṇipādaṃ tatsarvato'kṣiśiromukham
sarvataḥ śrutimal loke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati
yukto yogena ceśānaṃ sarvataś ca sanātanam
puruṣaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ taṃ vidvānna vimuhyati
bhūtātmānaṃ mahātmānaṃ paramātmānamavyayam
sarvātmānaṃ paraṃ brahma tadvai dhyātā na muhyati
pavano hi yathā grāhyo vicaransarvamūrtiṣu
puri śete sudurgrāhyastasmātpuruṣa ucyate
atha celluptadharmā tu sāvaśeṣaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ
tatastu brahmagarbhe vai śukraśoṇitasaṃyute
strīpuṃsoḥ saṃprayoge hi jāyate hi tataḥ prabhuḥ
tatastu garbhakālena kalalaṃ nāma jāyate
kālena kalalaṃ cāpi budbudaṃ samprajāyate
mṛtpiṇḍastu yathā cakre cakrāvartena pīḍitaḥ
hastābhyāṃ kriyamāṇastu biṃbatvamanugacchati
evamādhyātmikairyuktā vāyunā saṃprapūritaḥ
yadi yoniṃ vimuñcāmi tatprapadye maheśvaram
yāvaddhi vaiṣṇavo vāyurjātamātraṃ na saṃspṛśet
tāvatkālaṃ mahādevamarcayāmīti cintayet
jāyate mānuṣastatra yathārūpaṃ yathāvayaḥ
vāyuḥ saṃbhavate khāttu vātādbhavati vai jalam
jalāt sambhavati prāṇaḥ prāṇācchukraṃ vivardhate
raktabhāgās trayastriṃśad retobhāgāś caturdaśa
bhāgato'rdhaphalaṃ kṛtvā tato garbho niṣicyate
tatastu garbhasaṃyuktaḥ pañcabhir vāyubhir vṛtaḥ
pituḥ śarīrātpratyaṅgaṃ rūpamasyopajāyate
tato 'sya māturāhārāt pītalīḍhapraveśanāt
nābhideśena vai prāṇāste hyādhārā hi dehinām
navamāsāt parikliṣṭaḥ saṃveṣṭitaśirodharaḥ
veṣṭitaḥ sarvagātraiś ca aparyāptapraveśanaḥ
navamāsoṣitaścāpi yonicchidrādavāṅmukhaḥ
tataḥ svakarmabhiḥ pāpairnirayaṃ samprapadyate
asipatravanaṃ caiva śālmalicchedanaṃ tathā
tāḍanaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ caiva pūyaśoṇitabhakṣaṇam
yathā hyāpastu saṃchinnāḥ saṃśleṣmam upayānti vai
tathā chinnāś ca bhinnāśca yātanāsthānam āgatāḥ
evaṃ jīvāstu taiḥ pāpaistapyamānāḥ svayaṃkṛtaiḥ
prāpnuyuḥ karmabhiḥ śeṣairduḥkhaṃ vā yadi vetarat
ekenaiva tu gantavyaṃ sarvamutsṛjya vai janam
ekenaiva tu bhoktavyaṃ tasmātsukṛtamācaret
na hyenaṃ prasthitaṃ kaścid gacchantam anugacchati
yadanena kṛtaṃ karma tadenamanugacchati
te nityaṃ yamaviṣayeṣu sampravṛttāḥ krośantaḥ satatamaniṣṭasaṃprayogaiḥ
śuṣyante parigatavedanāḥ śarīrā bahvībhiḥ subhṛśamanantayātanābhiḥ
karmaṇā manasā vācā yadabhīkṣṇaṃ niṣevate
tadabhyāso haratyenaṃ tasmātkalyāṇamācaret
anādimānprabandhaḥ syātpūrvakarmaṇi dehinaḥ
saṃsāraṃ tāmasaṃ ghoraṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ pratipadyate
mānuṣyātpaśubhāvaś ca paśubhāvān mṛgo bhavet
mṛgatvātpakṣibhāvaś ca tasmāccaiva sarīsṛpaḥ
sarīsṛpatvādgacchedvai sthāvaratvaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
sthāvaratve punaḥ prāpte yāvad unmilate janaḥ
kulālacakravadbhrāntastatraiva parivartate
ityevaṃ hi manuṣyādiḥ saṃsāraḥ sthāvarāntikaḥ
vijñeyastāmaso nāma tatraiva parivartate
sāttvikaścāpi saṃsāro brahmādiḥ parikīrtitaḥ
piśācāntaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ svargasthāneṣu dehinām
brāhme tu kevalaṃ sattvaṃ sthāvare kevalaṃ tamaḥ
caturdaśānāṃ sthānānāṃ madhye viṣṭambhakaṃ rajaḥ
marmasu chidyamāneṣu vedanārtasya dehinaḥ
tatastatparamaṃ brahma kathaṃ vipraḥ smariṣyati
saṃsāraḥ pūrvadharmasya bhāvanābhiḥ praṇoditaḥ
mānuṣaṃ bhajate nityaṃ tasmāddhyānaṃ samācaret
caturdaśavidhaṃ hyetad buddhvā saṃsāramaṇḍalam
nityaṃ samārabheddharmaṃ saṃsārabhayapīḍitaḥ
tatastarati saṃsāraṃ krameṇa parivartitaḥ
tasmācca satataṃ yukto dhyānatatparayuñjakaḥ
tathā samārabhedyogaṃ yathātmānaṃ sa paśyati
eṣa āpaḥ paraṃ jyotireṣa seturanuttamaḥ
vivṛtyā hyeṣa saṃbhedād bhūtānāṃ caiva śāśvataḥ
tadenaṃ setumātmānamagniṃ vai viśvatomukham
hṛdisthaṃ sarvabhūtānāmupāsīta maheśvaram
tathāntaḥ saṃsthitaṃ devaṃ svaśaktyā parimaṇḍitam
aṣṭadhā cāṣṭadhā caiva tathā cāṣṭavidhena ca
sṛṣṭyarthaṃ saṃsthitaṃ vahniṃ saṃkṣipya ca hṛdi sthitam
dhyātvā yathāvaddeveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam
hutvā pañcāhutīḥ samyak taccintāgatamānasaḥ
vaiśvānaraṃ hṛdisthaṃ tu yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
āpaḥ pūtāḥ sakṛtprāśya tūṣṇīṃ hutvā hyupāviśan
prāṇāyeti tatastasya prathamā hyāhutiḥ smṛtā
apānāya dvitīyā ca vyānāyeti tathā parā
udānāya caturthī syāt samānāyeti pañcamī
svāhākāraiḥ pṛthagghutvā śeṣaṃ bhuñjīta kāmataḥ
apaḥ punaḥ sakṛtprāśya ācamya hṛdayaṃ spṛśet
prāṇānāṃ granthirasyātmā rudro hyātmā viśāntakaḥ
rudro vai hyātmanaḥ prāṇa evamāpyāyayetsvayam
prāṇe niviṣṭo vai rudrastasmātprāṇamayaḥ svayam
prāṇāya caiva rudrāya juhotyamṛtamuttamam
śivāviśeha māmīśa svāhā brahmātmane svayam
evaṃ pañcāhutīścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ
puruṣo'si pure śeṣe tvaṃ aṅguṣṭhapramāṇataḥ
āśritaścaiva cāṅguṣṭham īśaḥ paramakāraṇam
sarvasya jagataścaiva prabhuḥ prīṇātu śāśvataḥ
tvaṃ devānāmasi jyeṣṭho rudrastvaṃ ca puro vṛṣā
mṛdustvamannamasmabhyametadastu hutaṃ tava
ityevaṃ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ guṇaprāptiviśeṣataḥ
yogācāraḥ svayaṃ tena brahmaṇā kathitaḥ purā
evaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ jñātavyaṃ ca prayatnataḥ
bhasmasnāyī bhaven nityaṃ bhasmaliptaḥ sadā bhavet
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
daive karmaṇi pitrye vā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ṇimādyaṣṭasiddhitriguṇasaṃsāraprāgnau homādivarṇanaṃ nāmāṣṭāśītitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi śaucācārasya lakṣaṇam
yadanuṣṭhāya śuddhātmā paretya gatimāpnuyāt
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvabhūtahitāya vai
saṃkṣepātsarvavedārthaṃ saṃcayaṃ brahmavādinām
udayārthaṃ tu śaucānāṃ munīnāmuttamaṃ padam
yastatrāthāpramattaḥ syātsa munirnāvasīdati
mānāvamānau dvāvetau tāvevāhur viṣāmṛte
avamāno 'mṛtaṃ tatra sanmāno viṣamucyate
gurorapi hite yuktaḥ sa tu saṃvatsaraṃ vaset
niyameṣvapramattastu yameṣu ca sadā bhavet
prāpyānujñāṃ tataścaiva jñānayogamanuttamam
avirodhena dharmasya careta pṛthivīmimām
cakṣuḥpūtaṃ carenmārgaṃ vastrapūtaṃ jalaṃ pibet
satyapūtaṃ vadedvākyaṃ manaḥpūtaṃ samācaret
matsyagṛhyasya yatpāpaṃ ṣaṇmāsābhyantare bhavet
ekāhaṃ tatsamaṃ jñeyam apūtaṃ yajjalaṃ bhavet
apūtodakapāne tu japecca śatapañcakam
aghoralakṣaṇaṃ mantraṃ tataḥ śuddhimavāpnuyāt
athavā pūjayecchaṃbhuṃ ghṛtasnānādivistaraiḥ
tridhā pradakṣiṇīkṛtya śudhyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
ātithyaśrāddhayajñeṣu na gacchedyogavitkvacit
evaṃ hyahiṃsako yogī bhavediti vicāritam
vahnau vidhūme 'tyaṅgāre sarvasminbhuktavajjane
carettu matimān bhaikṣyaṃ na tu teṣveva nityaśaḥ
athainam avamanyante pare paribhavanti ca
tathā yuktaṃ caredbhaikṣyaṃ satāṃ dharmam adūṣayan
bhaikṣyaṃ caredvanastheṣu yāyāvaragṛheṣu ca
śreṣṭhā tu prathamā hīyaṃ vṛttirasyopajāyate
ata ūrdhvaṃ gṛhastheṣu śīlīneṣu careddvijāḥ
śraddadhāneṣu dānteṣu śrotriyeṣu mahātmasu
ata ūrdhvaṃ punaścāpi aduṣṭāpatiteṣu ca
bhaikṣyacaryā hi varṇeṣu jaghanyā vṛttirucyate
bhaikṣyaṃ yavāgūstakraṃ vā payo yāvakameva ca
phalamūlādi pakvaṃ vā kaṇapiṇyākasaktavaḥ
ityeva te mayā proktā yogināṃ siddhivarddhanāḥ
āhārāsteṣu siddheṣu śreṣṭhaṃ bhaikṣyamiti smṛtam
abbinduṃ yaḥ kuśāgreṇa māsi māsi samaśnute
nyāyato yaścaredbhaikṣyaṃ pūrvoktātsa viśiṣyate
jarāmaraṇagarbhebhyo bhītasya narakādiṣu
evaṃ dāyayate tasmāttadbhaikṣyamiti saṃsmṛtam
dadhibhakṣāḥ payobhakṣā ye cānye jīvakṣīṇakāḥ
sarve te bhaikṣyabhakṣasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm
bhasmaśāyī bhavennityaṃ bhikṣācārī jitendriyaḥ
ya icchet paramaṃ sthānaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret
yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ cāndrāyaṇaṃ bhavet
ekaṃ dve trīṇi catvāri śaktito vā samācaret
asteyaṃ brahmacaryaṃ ca alobhastyāga eva ca
vratāni pañca bhikṣūṇāmahiṃsā paramā tviha
akrodho guruśuśrūṣā śaucamāhāralāghavam
nityaṃ svādhyāya ityete niyamāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
bījayoniguṇā vastubandhaḥ karmabhir eva ca
yathā dvipa ivāraṇye manuṣyāṇāṃ vidhīyate
devaistulyāḥ sarvayajñakriyāstu yajñājjāpyaṃ jñānamāhuś ca jāpyāt
jñānād dhyānaṃ saṃgarāgādapetaṃ tasminprāpte śāśvatasyopalambhaḥ
damaḥ śamaḥ satyamakalmaṣatvaṃ maunaṃ ca bhūteṣvakhileṣu cārjavam
atīndriyaṃ jñānamidaṃ tathā śivaṃ prāhus tathā jñānaviśuddhabuddhayaḥ
samāhito brahmaparo 'pramādī śucis tathaikāntaratir jitendriyaḥ
samāpnuyādyogamimaṃ mahātmā maharṣayaścaivam aninditāmalāḥ
prāpyate 'bhimatān deśānaṅkuśena nivāritaḥ
etanmārgeṇa śuddhena dagdhabījo hyakalmaṣaḥ
sadācāraratāḥ śāntāḥ svadharmaparipālakāḥ
sarvāṃllokān vinirjitya brahmalokaṃ vrajanti te
pitāmahenopadiṣṭo dharmaḥ sākṣātsanātanaḥ
sarvalokopakārārthaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ pravadāmi vaḥ
gurūpadeśayuktānāṃ vṛddhānāṃ kramavarttinām
abhyutthānādikaṃ sarvaṃ praṇāmaṃ caiva kārayet
aṣṭāṅgapraṇipātenatridhā nyastena suvratāḥ
triḥpradakṣiṇayogena vandyo vai brahmaṇo guruḥ
jyeṣṭhānye 'pi ca te sarve vandanīyā vijānatā
ājñābhaṅgaṃ na kurvīta yadīcchet siddhim uttamām
dhātuśūnyabilakṣetrakṣudramantropajīvanam
viṣagrahaviḍambādīn varjayet sarvayatnataḥ
kaitavaṃ vittaśāṭhyaṃ ca paiśunyaṃ varjayetsadā
atihāsam avaṣṭambhaṃ līlāsvecchāpravartanam
varjayetsarvayatnena gurūṇāmapi saṃnidhau
tadvākyapratikūlaṃ ca ayuktaṃ vai gurorvacaḥ
na vadetsarvayatnena aniṣṭaṃ na smaretsadā
yatīnāmāsanaṃ vastraṃ daṇḍādyaṃ pāduke tathā
mālyaṃ ca śayanasthānaṃ pātraṃ chāyāṃ ca yatnataḥ
yajñopakaraṇāṅgaṃ ca na spṛśed vai padena ca
devadrohaṃ gurudrohaṃ na kuryātsarvayatnataḥ
kṛtvā pramādato viprāḥ praṇavasyāyutaṃ japet
devadrohagurudrohātkoṭimātreṇa śudhyati
mahāpātakaśuddhyarthaṃ tathaiva ca yathāvidhi
pātakī ca tadardhena śudhyate vṛttavānyadi
upapātakinaḥ sarve tadardhenaiva suvratāḥ
saṃdhyālope kṛte vipraḥ trirāvṛttyaiva śudhyati
āhnikacchedane jāte śatamekamudāhṛtam
laṅghane samayānāṃ tu abhakṣyasya ca bhakṣaṇe
avācyavācane caiva sahasrācchuddhirucyate
kākolūkakapotānāṃ pakṣiṇāmapi ghātane
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ japtvā mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
yaḥ punastattvavettā ca brahmavid brāhmaṇottamaḥ
smaraṇācchuddhimāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
naivamātmavidāmasti prāyaścittāni codanā
viśvasyaiva hi te śuddhā brahmavidyāvido janāḥ
yogadhyānaikaniṣṭhāś ca nirlepāḥ kāñcanaṃ yathā
śuddhānāṃ śodhanaṃ nāsti viśuddhā brahmavidyayā
uddhṛtānuṣṇaphenābhiḥ pūtābhir vastracakṣuṣā
adbhiḥ samācaretsarvaṃ varjayetkaluṣodakam
gandhavarṇarasairduṣṭamaśucisthānasaṃsthitam
paṅkāśmadūṣitaṃ caiva sāmudraṃ palvalodakam
saśaivālaṃ tathānyairvā doṣairduṣṭaṃ vivarjayet
vastraśaucānvitaḥ kuryātsarvakāryāṇi vai dvijāḥ
namaskārādikaṃ sarvaṃ guruśuśrūṣaṇādikam
vastraśaucavihīnātmā hyaśucirnātra saṃśayaḥ
devakāryopayuktānāṃ pratyahaṃ śaucamiṣyate
itareṣāṃ hi vastrāṇāṃ śaucaṃ kāryaṃ malāgame
varjayetsarvayatnena vāso 'nyair vidhṛtaṃ dvijāḥ
kauśeyāvikayo rūkṣaiḥ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ
śrīphalairaṃśupaṭṭānāṃ kutapānāmariṣṭakaiḥ
carmaṇāṃ vidalānāṃ ca vetrāṇāṃ vastravanmatam
valkalānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ chatracāmarayorapi
cailavacchaucamākhyātaṃ brahmavidbhir munīśvaraiḥ
bhasmanā śudhyate kāṃsyaṃ kṣāreṇāyasam ucyate
tāmramamlena vai viprāstrapusīsakayorapi
haimam adbhiḥ śubhaṃ pātraṃ raupyapātraṃ dvijottamāḥ
maṇyaśmaśaṅkhamuktānāṃ śaucaṃ taijasavatsmṛtam
agner apāṃ ca saṃyogādatyantopahatasya ca
rasānāmiha sarveṣāṃ śuddhirutplavanaṃ smṛtam
tṛṇakāṣṭhādivastūnāṃ śubhenābhyukṣaṇaṃ smṛtam
uṣṇena vāriṇā śuddhis tathā sruksruvayorapi
tathaiva yajñapātrāṇāṃ muśalolūkhalasya ca
śṛṅgāsthidārudantānāṃ takṣaṇenaiva śodhanam
saṃhatānāṃ mahābhāgā dravyāṇāṃ prokṣaṇaṃ smṛtam
asaṃhatānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ pratyekaṃ śaucamucyate
abhuktarāśidhānyānām ekadeśasya dūṣaṇe
tāvanmātraṃ samuddhṛtya prokṣayedvai kuśāṃbhasā
śākamūlaphalādīnāṃ dhānyavacchuddhiriṣyate
mārjanonmārjanair veśma punaḥpākena mṛnmayam
ullekhanenāñjanena tathā saṃmārjanena ca
gonivāsena vai śuddhā secanena dharā smṛtā
bhūmistham udakaṃ śuddhaṃ vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yatra gaurvrajet
avyāptaṃ yadamedhyena gandhavarṇarasānvitam
vatsaḥ śuciḥ prasravaṇe śakuniḥ phalapātane
svadārāsyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ ratau bhāryābhikāṅkṣayā
hastābhyāṃ kṣālitaṃ vastraṃ kāruṇā ca yathāvidhi
kuśāṃbunā susaṃprokṣya gṛhṇīyāddharmavittamaḥ
paṇyaṃ prasāritaṃ caiva varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ
śucirākarajaṃ teṣāṃ śvā mṛgagrahaṇe śuciḥ
chāyā ca vipluṣo viprā makṣikādyā dvijottamāḥ
rajo bhūr vāyur agniś ca medhyāni sparśane sadā
suptvā bhuktvā ca vai viprāḥ kṣuttvā pītvā ca vai tathā
ṣṭhīvitvādhyayanādau ca śucirapyācametpunaḥ
pādau spṛśanti ye cāpi parācamanabindavaḥ
te pārthivaiḥ samā jñeyā na tairaprayato bhavet
kṛtvā ca maithunaṃ spṛṣṭvā patitaṃ kukkuṭādikam
sūkaraṃ caiva kākādi śvānamuṣṭraṃ kharaṃ tathā
yūpaṃ cāṇḍālakādyāṃś ca spṛṣṭvā snānena śudhyati
rajasvalāṃ sūtikāṃ ca na spṛśedantyajāmapi
sūtikāśaucasaṃyuktaḥ śāvāśaucasamanvitaḥ
saṃspṛśenna rajastāsāṃ spṛṣṭvā snātvaiva śudhyati
naivāśaucaṃ yatīnāṃ ca vanasthabrahmacāriṇām
naiṣṭhikānāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ ca maṇḍalīnāṃ ca suvratāḥ
tataḥ kāryavirodhāddhi nṛpāṇāṃ nānyathā bhavet
vaikhānasānāṃ viprāṇāṃ patitānāmasaṃbhavāt
asaṃcayād dvijānāṃ ca snānamātreṇa nānyathā
tathā saṃnihitānāṃ ca yajñārthaṃ dīkṣitasya ca
ekāhād yajñayājināṃ śuddhiruktā svayaṃbhuvā
tatastvadhītaśākhānāṃ caturbhiḥ sarvadehinām
sūtakaṃ pretakaṃ nāsti tryahād ūrdhvam amutra vai
arvāg ekādaśāhāntaṃ bāndhavānāṃ dvijottamāḥ
snānamātreṇa vai śuddhirmaraṇe samupasthite
tata ṛtutrayādarvāg ekāhaḥ parigīyate
saptavarṣāt tataścārvāk trirātraṃ hi tataḥ param
daśāhaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ vai prathame 'hani vā pituḥ
daśāhaṃ sūtikāśaucaṃ māturapyevamavyayāḥ
arvāk trivarṣātsnānena bāndhavānāṃ pituḥ sadā
aṣṭābdād ekarātreṇa śuddhiḥ syād bāndhavasya tu
dvādaśābdāttataścārvāk trirātraṃ strīṣu suvratāḥ
sapiṇḍatā ca puruṣe saptame vinivartate
atikrānte daśāhe tu trirātramaśucirbhavet
tataḥ saṃnihito vipraścārvāk pūrvaṃ tadeva vai
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu snānamātreṇa śudhyati
spṛṣṭvā pretaṃ trirātreṇa dharmārthaṃ snānamucyate
dāhakānāṃ ca netṝṇāṃ snānamātramabāndhave
anugamya ca vai snātvā ghṛtaṃ prāśya viśudhyati
ācāryamaraṇe caiva trirātraṃ śrotriye mṛte
pakṣiṇī mātulānāṃ ca sodarāṇāṃ ca vā dvijāḥ
bhūpānāṃ maṇḍalīnāṃ ca sadyo nīrāṣṭravāsinām
kevalaṃ dvādaśāhena kṣattriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ
nābhiṣiktasya cāśaucaṃ saṃpramādeṣu vai raṇe
vaiśyaḥ pañcadaśāhena śūdro māsena śudhyati
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktā dravyaśuddhiranuttamā
aśaucaṃ cānupūrvyeṇa yatīnāṃ naiva vidyate
tretāprabhṛti nārīṇāṃ māsi māsyārtavaṃ dvijāḥ
kṛte sakṛd yugavaśājjāyante vai sahaiva tu
prayānti ca mahābhāgā bhāryābhiḥ kuravo yathā
varṇāśramavyavasthā ca tretāprabhṛti suvratāḥ
bhārate dakṣiṇe varṣe vyavasthā netareṣvatha
mahāvīte suvīte ca jaṃbūdvīpe tathāṣṭasu
śākadvīpādiṣu prokto dharmo vai bhārate yathā
rasollāsā kṛte vṛttistretāyāṃ gṛhavṛkṣajā
saivārtavakṛtād doṣād rāgadveṣādibhir nṛṇām
maithunātkāmato viprāstathaiva paruṣādibhiḥ
yavādyāḥ samprajāyante grāmyāraṇyāścaturdaśa
oṣadhyaś ca rajodoṣāḥ strīṇāṃ rāgādibhir nṛṇām
akālakṛṣṭā vidhvastāḥ punarutpāditās tathā
tasmātsarvaprayatnena na saṃbhāṣyā rajasvalā
prathame 'hani cāṇḍālī yathā varjyā tathāṅganā
dvitīye 'hani viprā hi yathā vai brahmaghātinī
tṛtīye 'hni tadardhena caturthe 'hani suvratāḥ
snātvārdhamāsāt saṃśuddhā tataḥ śuddhirbhaviṣyati
ā ṣoḍaśāt tataḥ strīṇāṃ mūtravacchaucamiṣyate
pañcarātraṃ tathāspṛśyā rajasā vartate yadi
sā viṃśaddivasādūrdhvaṃ rajasā pūrvavattathā
snānaṃ śaucaṃ tathā gānaṃ rodanaṃ hasanaṃ tathā
yānamabhyañjanaṃ nārī dyūtaṃ caivānulepanam
divāsvapnaṃ viśeṣeṇa tathā vai dantadhāvanam
maithunaṃ mānasaṃ vāpi vācikaṃ devatārcanam
varjayetsarvayatnena namaskāraṃ rajasvalā
rajasvalāṅganāsparśasaṃbhāṣe ca rajasvalā
saṃtyāgaṃ caiva vastrāṇāṃ varjayetsarvayatnataḥ
snātvānyapuruṣaṃ nārī na spṛśettu rajasvalā
īkṣayedbhāskaraṃ devaṃ brahmakūrcaṃ tataḥ pibet
kevalaṃ pañcagavyaṃ vā kṣīraṃ vā cātmaśuddhaye
caturthyāṃ strī na gamyā tu gato'lpāyuḥ prasūyate
vidyāhīnaṃ vratabhraṣṭaṃ patitaṃ pāradārikam
dāridryārṇavamagnaṃ ca tanayaṃ sā prasūyate
kanyārthinaiva gantavyā pañcamyāṃ vidhivatpunaḥ
raktādhikyādbhavennārī śukrādhikye bhavetpumān
same napuṃsakaṃ caiva pañcamyāṃ kanyakā bhavet
ṣaṣṭhyāṃ gamyā mahābhāgā satputrajananī bhavet
putratvaṃ vyañjayettasya jātaputro mahādyutiḥ
pumiti narakasyākhyā duḥkhaṃ ca narakaṃ viduḥ
puṃsastrāṇānvitaṃ putraṃ tathābhūtaṃ prasūyate
saptamyāṃ caiva kanyārthī gacchetsaiva prasūyate
aṣṭamyāṃ sarvasampannaṃ tanayaṃ samprasūyate
navamyāṃ dārikāyārthī daśamyāṃ paṇḍito bhavet
ekādaśyāṃ tathā nārīṃ janayetsaiva pūrvavat
dvādaśyāṃ dharmatattvajñaṃ śrautasmārtapravartakam
trayodaśyāṃ jaḍāṃ nārīṃ sarvasaṃkarakāriṇīm
janayatyaṅganā yasmānna gacchetsarvayatnataḥ
caturdaśyāṃ yadā gacchet sā putrajananī bhavet
pañcadaśyāṃ ca dharmiṣṭhāṃ ṣoḍaśyāṃ jñānapāragam
strīṇāṃ vai maithune kāle vāmapārśve prabhañjanaḥ
caredyadi bhavennārī pumāṃsaṃ dakṣiṇe labhet
strīṇāṃ maithunakāle tu pāpagrahavivarjite
uktakāle śucirbhūtvā śuddhāṃ gacchecchucismitām
ityevaṃ saṃprasaṃgena yatīnāṃ dharmasaṃgrahe
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ sadācāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyād vāpi sadācāraṃ śucirnaraḥ
śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ brāhmaṇān dagdhakilbiṣān
brahmalokamanuprāpya brahmaṇā saha modate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sadācārakathanaṃ nāmaikonanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi yatīnāmiha niścitam
prāyaścittaṃ śivaproktaṃ yatīnāṃ pāpaśodhanam
pāpaṃ hi trividhaṃ jñeyaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃbhavam
satataṃ hi divā rātrau yenedaṃ veṣṭyate jagat
tatkarmaṇā vināpyeṣa tiṣṭhatīti parā śrutiḥ
kṣaṇamevaṃ prayojyaṃ tu āyuṣyaṃ tu vidhāraṇam
bhavedyogo 'pramattasya yogo hi paramaṃ balam
na hi yogātparaṃ kiṃcin narāṇāṃ dṛśyate śubham
tasmād yogaṃ praśaṃsanti dharmayuktā manīṣiṇaḥ
avidyāṃ vidyayā jitvā prāpyaiśvaryamanuttamam
dṛṣṭvā parāvaraṃ dhīrāḥ paraṃ gacchanti tatpadam
vratāni yāni bhikṣūṇāṃ tathaivopavratāni ca
ekaikātikrame teṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate
upetya tu striyaṃ kāmātprāyaścittaṃ vinirdiśet
prāṇāyāmasamāyuktaṃ caretsāṃtapanaṃ vratam
tataścarati nirdeśātkṛcchraṃ cānte samāhitaḥ
punar āśramam āgatya caredbhikṣuratandritaḥ
na dharmayuktamanṛtaṃ hinastīti manīṣiṇaḥ
tathāpi na ca kartavyaṃ prasaṃgo hyeṣa dāruṇaḥ
ahorātropavāsaś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā
asadvādo na kartavyo yatinā dharmalipsunā
paramāpadgatenāpi na kāryaṃ steyamapyuta
steyādabhyadhikaḥ kaścinnāstyadharma iti śrutiḥ
hiṃsā hyeṣā parā sṛṣṭā stainyaṃ vai kathitaṃ tathā
yadetaddraviṇaṃ nāma prāṇā hyete bahiścarāḥ
sa tasya harate prāṇānyo yasya harate dhanam
evaṃ kṛtvā suduṣṭātmā bhinnavṛtto vratāccyutaḥ
bhūyo nirvedamāpannaścareccāndrāyaṇaṃ vratam
vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena saṃvatsaramiti śrutiḥ
tataḥ saṃvatsarasyānte bhūyaḥ prakṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ
punarnirvedamāpannaścaredbhikṣuratandritaḥ
ahiṃsā sarvabhūtānāṃ karmaṇā manasā girā
akāmādapi hiṃseta yadi bhikṣuḥ paśūn kṛmīn
kṛcchrātikṛcchraṃ kurvīta cāndrāyaṇamathāpi vā
skandedindriyadaurbalyāt striyaṃ dṛṣṭvā yatiryadi
tena dhārayitavyā vai prāṇāyāmāstu ṣoḍaśa
divā skannasya viprasya prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate
trirātramupavāsāś ca prāṇāyāmaśataṃ tathā
rātrau skannaḥ śuciḥ snātvā dvādaśaiva tu dhāraṇā
prāṇāyāmena śuddhātmā virajā jāyate dvijāḥ
ekānnaṃ madhumāṃsaṃ vā aśṛtānnaṃ tathaiva ca
abhojyāni yatīnāṃ tu pratyakṣalavaṇāni ca
ekaikātikramātteṣāṃ prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate
prājāpatyena kṛcchreṇa tataḥ pāpātpramucyate
vyatikramāś ca ye kecid vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃbhavāḥ
sadbhiḥ saha viniścitya yadbrūyustatsamācaret
careddhi śuddhaḥ samaloṣṭakāñcanaḥ samastabhūteṣu ca satsamāhitaḥ
sthānaṃ dhruvaṃ śāśvatamavyayaṃ tu paraṃ hi gatvā na punarhi jāyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge yatiprāyaścittaṃ nāma navatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi ariṣṭāni nibodhata
yena jñānaviśeṣeṇa mṛtyuṃ paśyanti yoginaḥ
arundhatīṃ dhruvaṃ caiva somachāyāṃ mahāpatham
yo na paśyenna jīvetsa naraḥ saṃvatsarātparam
ariśmavantam ādityaṃ raśmivantaṃ ca pāvakam
yaḥ paśyati na jīvedvai māsādekādaśātparam
vamenmūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tathā
pratyakṣamathavā svapne daśamāsānna jīvati
rukmavarṇaṃ drumaṃ paśyedgandharvanagarāṇi ca
paśyet pretapiśācāṃś ca navamāsān sa jīvati
akasmācca bhavetsthūlo hyakasmācca kṛśo bhavet
prakṛteś ca nivarteta cāṣṭau māsāṃś ca jīvati
agrataḥ pṛṣṭhato vāpi khaṇḍaṃ yasya padaṃ bhavet
pāṃsuke kardame vāpi saptamāsānsa jīvati
kākaḥ kapoto gṛdhro vā nilīyedyasya mūrdhani
kravyādo vā khago yasya ṣaṇmāsān nātivartate
gacched vāyasapaṅktībhiḥ pāṃsuvarṣeṇa vā punaḥ
svacchāyāṃ vikṛtāṃ paśyeccatuḥpañca sa jīvati
anabhre vidyutaṃ paśyeddakṣiṇāṃ diśamāsthitām
udake dhanur aindraṃ vā trīṇi dvau vā sa jīvati
apsu vā yadi vādarśe yo hyātmānaṃ na paśyati
aśiraskaṃ tathā paśyen māsād ūrdhvaṃ na jīvati
śavagandhi bhavedgātraṃ vasāgandhamathāpi vā
mṛtyurhyupāgatastasya ardhamāsānna jīvati
yasya vai snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pariśuṣyati
dhūmaṃ vā mastakātpaśyeddaśāhānna sa jīvati
saṃbhinno māruto yasya marmasthānāni kṛntati
adbhiḥ spṛṣṭo na hṛṣyeta tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
ṛkṣavānarayuktena rathenāśāṃ ca dakṣiṇām
gāyannṛtyan vrajet svapne vidyānmṛtyurupasthitaḥ
kṛṣṇāṃbaradharā śyāmā gāyantī vāpyathāṅganā
yaṃ nayeddakṣiṇāmāśāṃ svapne so'pi na jīvati
chidraṃ vā svasya kaṇṭhasya svapne yo vīkṣate naraḥ
nagnaṃ vā śramaṇaṃ dṛṣṭvā vidyānmṛtyumupasthitam
ā mastakatalādyas tu nimajjetpaṅkasāgare
dṛṣṭvā tu tādṛśaṃ svapnaṃ sadya eva na jīvati
bhasmāṅgārāṃś ca keśāṃś ca nadīṃ śuṣkāṃ bhujaṅgamān
paśyedyo daśarātraṃ tu na sa jīvati tādṛśaḥ
kṛṣṇaiś ca vikaṭaiścaiva puruṣairudyatāyudhaiḥ
pāṣāṇaistāḍyate svapne yaḥ sadyo na sa jīvati
sūryodaye pratyuṣasi pratyakṣaṃ yasya vai śivāḥ
krośantyabhimukhaṃ pretya sa gatāyurbhavennaraḥ
yasya vā snātamātrasya hṛdayaṃ pīḍyate bhṛśam
jāyate dantaharṣaś ca taṃ gatāyuṣamādiśet
bhūyobhūyastrasedyastu rātrau vā yadi vā divā
dīpagandhaṃ ca nāghrāti vidyānmṛtyum upasthitam
rātrau cendradhanuḥ paśyeddivā nakṣatramaṇḍalam
paranetreṣu cātmānaṃ na paśyenna sa jīvati
netramekaṃ sravedyasya karṇau sthānācca bhraśyataḥ
vakrā ca nāsā bhavati vijñeyo gatajīvitaḥ
yasya kṛṣṇā kharā jihvā padmābhāsaṃ ca vai mukham
gaṇḍe vā piṇḍikārakte tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
muktakeśo hasaṃścaiva gāyannṛtyaṃś ca yo naraḥ
yāmyāmabhimukhaṃ gacchettadantaṃ tasya jīvitam
yasya śvetaghanābhāsā śvetasarṣapasaṃnibhā
śvetā ca mūrtirhyasakṛttasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
uṣṭrā vā rāsabhā vābhiyuktāḥ svapne rathe śubhāḥ
yasya so'pi na jīvettu dakṣiṇābhimukho gataḥ
dve vātha parame 'riṣṭe ekībhūtaḥ paraṃ bhavet
ghoṣaṃ na śṛṇuyātkarṇe jyotir netre na paśyati
śvabhre yo nipatetsvapne dvāraṃ cāpi pidhīyate
na cottiṣṭhati yaḥ śvabhrāttadantaṃ tasya jīvitam
ūrdhvā ca dṛṣṭirna ca sampratiṣṭhā raktā punaḥ samparivartamānā
mukhasya śoṣaḥ suṣirā ca nābhiratyuṣṇamūtro viṣamastha eva
divā vā yadi vā rātrau pratyakṣaṃ yo nihanyate
hantāraṃ na ca paśyecca sa gatāyurna jīvati
agnipraveśaṃ kurute svapnānte yastu mānavaḥ
smṛtiṃ nopalabheccāpi tadantaṃ tasya jīvitam
yastu prāvaraṇaṃ śuklaṃ svakaṃ paśyati mānavaḥ
kṛṣṇaṃ raktamapi svapne tasya mṛtyurupasthitaḥ
ariṣṭe sūcite dehe tasminkāla upasthite
tyaktvā khedaṃ viṣādaṃ ca upekṣed buddhimān naraḥ
prācīṃ vā yadi vodīcīṃ diśaṃ niṣkramya vai śuciḥ
same 'tisthāvare deśe vivikte jantuvarjite
udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā svasthaś cācānta eva ca
svastikenopaviṣṭastu namaskṛtvā maheśvaram
samakāyaśirogrīvo dhārayan nāvalokayet
yathā dīpo nivātastho neṅgate sopamā smṛtā
prāgudakpravaṇe deśe tathā yuñjīta śāstravit
kāmaṃ vitarkaṃ prītiṃ ca sukhaduḥkhe ubhe tathā
nigṛhya manasā sarvaṃ śuklaṃ dhyānam anusmaret
ghrāṇe ca rasane nityaṃ cakṣuṣī sparśane tathā
śrotre manasi buddhau ca tatra vakṣasi dhārayet
kālakarmāṇi vijñāya samūheṣveva nityaśaḥ
dvādaśādhyātmamityevaṃ yogadhāraṇamucyate
śatamardhaśataṃ vāpi dhāraṇāṃ mūrdhni dhārayet
khinnasya dhāraṇāyogādvāyurūrdhvaṃ pravartate
tataścāpūrayed deham oṅkāreṇa samanvitaḥ
tathauṃkāramayo yogī akṣare tvakṣarī bhavet
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi oṅkāraprāptilakṣaṇam
eṣa trimātro vijñeyo vyañjanaṃ cātra ceśvaraḥ
prathamā vidyutī mātrā dvitīyā tāmasī smṛtā
tṛtīyāṃ nirguṇāṃ caiva mātrāmakṣaragāminīm
gāndhārī caiva vijñeyā gāndhārasvarasaṃbhavā
pipīlikāgatisparśā prayuktā mūrdhni lakṣyate
yathā prayukta oṅkāraḥ pratiniryāti mūrdhani
tathauṃkāramayo yogī tvakṣarī tvakṣarī bhavet
praṇavo dhanuḥ śaro hyātmā brahmalakṣaṇamucyate
apramattena veddhavyaṃ śaravat tanmayo bhavet
omityekākṣaraṃ hyetadguhāyāṃ nihitaṃ padam
omityetattrayo lokāstrayo vedāstrayo 'gnayaḥ
viṣṇukramāstrayastvete ṛksāmāni yajūṃṣi ca
mātrā cārdhaṃ ca tisrastu vijñeyāḥ paramārthataḥ
tatprayuktastu yo yogī tasya sālokyamāpnuyāt
akāro hyakṣaro jñeya ukāraḥ sahitaḥ smṛtaḥ
makārasahitauṃkāras trimātra iti saṃjñitaḥ
akāras tveṣa bhūrloka ukāro bhuva ucyate
savyañjano makārastu svarloka iti gīyate
oṅkārastu trayo lokāḥ śirastasya triviṣṭapam
bhuvanāṅgaṃ ca tatsarvaṃ brāhmaṃ tatpadamucyate
mātrāpādo rudraloko hyamātraṃ tu śivaṃ padam
evaṃ jñānaviśeṣeṇa tatpadaṃ samupāsyate
tasmāddhyānaratirnityamamātraṃ hi tadakṣaram
upāsyaṃ hi prayatnena śāśvataṃ sukhamicchatā
hrasvā tu prathamā mātrā tato dīrghā tvanantaram
tataḥ plutavatī caiva tṛtīyā copadiśyate
etāstu mātrā vijñeyā yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
yāvadeva tu śakyante dhāryante tāvadeva hi
indriyāṇi mano buddhiṃ dhyāyannātmani yaḥ sadā
ardhaṃ tanmātram api cec chṛṇu yat phalamāpnuyāt
māse māse 'śvamedhena yo yajeta śataṃ samāḥ
tena yatprāpyate puṇyaṃ mātrayā tadavāpnuyāt
na tathā tapasogreṇa na yajñairbhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
yatphalaṃ prāpyate samyaṅmātrayā tadavāpnuyāt
tatra caiṣā tu yā mātrā plutā nāmopadiśyate
eṣā eva bhavetkāryā gṛhasthānāṃ tu yoginām
eṣāṃ caiva viśeṣeṇa aiśvarye hyaṣṭalakṣaṇe
aṇimādye tu vijñeyā tasmādyuñjīta tāṃ dvijāḥ
evaṃ hi yogasaṃyuktaḥ śucir dānto jitendriyaḥ
ātmānaṃ vidyate yastu sa sarvaṃ vindate dvijāḥ
tasmātpāśupatairyogairātmānaṃ cintayedbudhaḥ
ātmānaṃ jānate ye tu śucayaste na saṃśayaḥ
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni vedopaniṣadas tathā
yogajñānādavāpnoti brāhmaṇo 'dhyātmacintakaḥ
sarvadevamayo bhūtvā abhūtaḥ sa tu jāyate
yonisaṃkramaṇaṃ tyaktvā yāti vai śāśvataṃ padam
yathā vṛkṣāt phalaṃ pakvaṃ pavanena samīritam
namaskāreṇa rudrasya tathā pāpaṃ praṇaśyati
yatra rudranamaskāraḥ sarvakarmaphalo dhruvaḥ
anyadevanamaskārānna tatphalamavāpnuyāt
tasmāttriḥpravaṇaṃ yogī upāsīta maheśvaram
daśavistārakaṃ brahma tathā ca brahmavistaraiḥ
evaṃ dhyānasamāyuktaḥ svadehaṃ yaḥ parityajet
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ samuddhṛtya kulatrayam
athavāriṣṭamālokya maraṇe samupasthite
avimukteśvaraṃ gatvā vārāṇasyāṃ tu śodhanam
yena kenāpi vā dehaṃ saṃtyajen mucyate naraḥ
śrīparvate vā viprendrāḥ saṃtyajetsvatanuṃ naraḥ
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
avimuktaṃ paraṃ kṣetraṃ jantūnāṃ muktidaṃ sadā
seveta satataṃ dhīmān viśeṣānmaraṇāntike
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge ariṣṭakathanaṃ nāma ekanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
evaṃ vārāṇasī puṇyā yadi sūta mahāmate
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ tatprabhāvaṃ hi sāṃpratam
kṣetrasyāsya ca māhātmyam avimuktasya śobhanam
vistareṇa yathānyāyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
sūta uvāca
vakṣye saṃkṣepataḥ samyak vārāṇasyāḥ suśobhanam
avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ yathāha bhagavān bhavaḥ
vistareṇa mayā vaktuṃ brahmaṇā ca mahātmanā
śakyate naiva viprendrā varṣakoṭiśatairapi
devaḥ purā kṛtodvāhaḥ śaṅkaro nīlalohitaḥ
himavacchikharāddevyā haimavatyā gaṇeśvaraiḥ
vārāṇasīmanuprāpya darśayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ vāsaṃ tatra cakāra saḥ
vārāṇasīkurukṣetraśrīparvatamahālaye
tuṅgeśvare ca kedāre tatsthāne yo yatirbhavet
yoge pāśupate samyak dinamekaṃ yatirbhavet
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya caret pāśupataṃ vratam
devodyāne vasettatra śarvodyānamanuttamam
manasā nirmame rudro vimānaṃ ca suśobhanam
darśayāmāsa ca tadā devodyānamanuttamam
haimavatyāḥ svayaṃ devaḥ sanandī parameśvaraḥ
kṣetrasyāsya ca māhātmyam avimuktasya śaṅkaraḥ
uktavānparameśānaḥ pārvatyāḥ prītaye bhavaḥ
praphullanānāvidhagulmaśobhitaṃ latāpratānādimanoharaṃ bahiḥ
virūḍhapuṣpaiḥ paritaḥ priyaṅgubhiḥ supuṣpitaiḥ kaṇṭakitaiś ca ketakaiḥ
tamālagulmairnicitaṃ sugandhibhir nikāmapuṣpairvakulaiś ca sarvataḥ
aśokapunnāgaśataiḥ supuṣpitair dvirephamālākulapuṣpasaṃcayaiḥ
kvacit praphullāmbujareṇubhūṣitair vihaṅgamaiś cānukalapraṇādibhiḥ
vināditaṃ sārasacakravākaiḥ pramattadātyūhavaraiś ca sarvataḥ
kvacicca kekārutanāditaṃ śubhaṃ kvacicca kāraṇḍavanādanāditam
kvacicca mattālikulākulīkṛtaṃ madākulābhir bhramarāṅganādibhiḥ
niṣevitaṃ cārusugandhipuṣpakaiḥ kvacit supuṣpaiḥ sahakāravṛkṣaiḥ
latopagūḍhaistilakaiś ca gūḍhaṃ pragītavidyādharasiddhacāraṇam
pravṛttanṛttānugatāpsarogaṇaṃ prahṛṣṭanānāvidhapakṣisevitam
pranṛttahārītakulopanāditaṃ mṛgendranādākulamattamānasaiḥ
kvacit kvacid gandhakadambakair mṛgair vilūnadarbhāṅkurapuṣpasaṃcayam
praphullanānāvidhacārupaṅkajaiḥ sarastaḍāgairupaśobhitaṃ kvacit
viṭapanicayalīnaṃ nīlakaṇṭhābhirāmaṃ madamuditavihaṅgaṃ prāptanādābhirāmam
kusumitataruśākhālīnamattadvirephaṃ navakisalayaśobhāśobhitaṃ prāṃśuśākham
kvacicca dantakṣatacāruvīrudhaṃ kvacillatāliṅgitacāruvṛkṣakam
kvacidvilāsālasagāminībhir niṣevitaṃ kiṃpuruṣāṅganābhiḥ
pārāvatadhvanivikūjitacāruśṛṅgairabhraṅkaṣaiḥ sitamanoharacārurūpaiḥ
ākīrṇapuṣpanikarapravibhaktahaṃsairvibhrājitaṃ tridaśadivyakulairanekaiḥ
phullotpalāṃbujavitānasahasrayuktaṃ toyāśayaiḥ samanuśobhitadevamārgam
mārgāntarākalitapuṣpavicitrapaṅktisambaddhagulmaviṭapair vividhairupetam
tuṅgāgrair nīlapuṣpastabakabharanataprāṃśuśākhair aśokair dolāprāntāntanīlaśrutisukhajanakair bhāsitāntaṃ manojñaiḥ
rātrau candrasya bhāsā kusumitatilakairekatāṃ samprayātaṃ chāyāsuptaprabuddhasthitahariṇakulāluptadūrvāṅkurāgram
haṃsānāṃ pakṣavātapracalitakamalasvacchavistīrṇatoyaṃ toyānāṃ tīrajātapracakitakadalīcāṭunṛtyanmayūram
māyūraiḥ pakṣacandraiḥ kvacidavanigatai rañjitakṣmāpradeśaṃ deśe deśe vilīnapramuditavilasanmattahārītavṛndam
sāraṅgaiḥ kvacidupaśobhitapradeśaṃ pracchannaṃ kusumacayaiḥ kvacidvicitraiḥ
hṛṣṭābhiḥ kvacidapi kinnarāṅganābhir vīṇābhiḥ sumadhuragītanṛttakaṇṭham
saṃsṛṣṭaiḥ kvacidupaliptakīrṇapuṣpairāvāsaiḥ parivṛtapādapaṃ munīnām
ā mūlāt phalanicitaiḥ kvacidviśālairuttuṅgaiḥ panasamahīruhairupetam
phullātimuktakalatāgṛhanītasiddhasiddhāṅganākanakanūpurarāvaramyam
ramyaṃ priyaṅgutarumañjarisaktabhṛṅgaṃ bhṛṅgāvalīkavalitāmrakadambapuṣpam
puṣpotkarānilavighūrṇitavāriramyaṃ ramyadvirephavinipātitamañjugulmam
gulmāntaraprasabhabhītamṛgīsamūhaṃ vāteritaṃ tanubhṛtāmapavargadātṛ
candrāṃśujālaśabalais tilakair manojñaiḥ sindūrakuṅkumakusumbhanibhair aśokaiḥ
cāmīkaradyutisamairatha karṇikāraiḥ puṣpotkarairupacitaṃ suviśālaśākhaiḥ
kvacidañjanacūrṇābhaiḥ kvacid vidrumasannibhaiḥ
kvacitkāñcanasaṃkāśaiḥ puṣpair ācitabhūtalam
punnāgeṣu dvijaśatavirutaṃ raktāśokastabakabharanatam
ramyopāntaklamahārabhavanaṃ phullābjeṣu bhramaravilasitam
sakalabhuvanabhartā lokanāthastadānīṃ tuhinaśikharaputryā sārdhamiṣṭairgaṇeśaiḥ
vividhataruviśālaṃ mattahṛṣṭānnapuṣṭair upavanam atiramyaṃ darśayāmāsa devyāḥ
puṣpairvanyaiḥ śubhaśubhatamaiḥ kalpitairdivyabhūṣairdevīṃ divyāmupavanagatāṃ bhūṣayāmāsa śarvaḥ
sā cāpyenaṃ tuhinagirisutā śaṅkaraṃ devadevaṃ puṣpairdivyaiḥ śubhataratamair bhūṣayāmāsa bhaktyā
sampūjya pūjyaṃ tridaśeśvarāṇāṃ samprekṣya codyānam atīva ramyam
gaṇeśvarair nandimukhaiś ca sārdhamuvāca devaṃ praṇipatya devī
śrīdevyuvāca
udyānaṃ darśitaṃ deva prabhayā parayā yutam
kṣetrasya ca guṇānsarvānpunarme vaktumarhasi
asya kṣetrasya māhātmyamavimuktasya sarvathā
vaktumarhasi deveśa devadeva vṛṣadhvaja
sūta uvāca
devyāstadvacanaṃ śrutvā devadevo varaprabhuḥ
āghrāya vadanāmbhojaṃ tadāha girijāṃ hasan
śrībhagavānuvāca
idaṃ guhyatamaṃ kṣetraṃ sadā vārāṇasī mama
sarveṣāmeva jantūnāṃ heturmokṣasya sarvadā
asminsiddhāḥ sadā devi madīyaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ
nānāliṅgadharā nityaṃ mama lokābhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ
abhyasyanti paraṃ yogaṃ yuktātmāno jitendriyāḥ
nānāvṛkṣasamākīrṇe nānāvihagaśobhite
kamalotpalapuṣpāḍhyaiḥ sarobhiḥ samalaṃkṛte
apsarogaṇagandharvaiḥ sadā saṃsevite śubhe
rocate me sadā vāso yena kāryeṇa tacchṛṇu
manmanā mama bhaktaś ca mayi nityārpitakriyaḥ
yathā mokṣamavāpnoti anyatra na tathā kvacit
kāmaṃ hyatra mṛto devi janturmokṣāya kalpate
etanmama puraṃ divyaṃ guhyādguhyatamaṃ mahat
brahmādayo vijānanti ye ca siddhā mumukṣavaḥ
ataḥ paramidaṃ kṣetraṃ parā ceyaṃ gatirmama
vimuktaṃ na mayā yasmānmokṣyate vā kadācana
mama kṣetramidaṃ tasmād avimuktamiti smṛtam
naimiṣe ca kurukṣetre gaṅgādvāre ca puṣkare
snānātsaṃsevanādvāpi na mokṣaḥ prāpyate yataḥ
iha samprāpyate yena tata etadviśiṣyate
prayāge vā bhavenmokṣa iha vā matparigrahāt
prayāgādapi tīrthāgryād avimuktamidaṃ śubham
dharmasyopaniṣat satyaṃ mokṣasyopaniṣac chamaḥ
kṣetratīrthopaniṣadaṃ na vidurbudhasattamāḥ
kāmaṃ bhuñjan svapan krīḍan kurvan hi vividhāḥ kriyāḥ
avimukte tyajetprāṇān janturmokṣāya kalpate
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām
na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā
tasmātsaṃsevanīyaṃ hi avimuktaṃ hi muktaye
jaigīṣavyaḥ parāṃ siddhiṃ gato yatra mahātapāḥ
asya kṣetrasya māhātmyādbhaktyā ca mama bhāvitaḥ
jaigīṣavyaguhā śreṣṭhā yogināṃ sthānamiṣyate
dhyāyantastatra māṃ nityaṃ yogāgnirdīpyate bhṛśam
kaivalyaṃ paramaṃ yāti devānāmapi durlabham
avyaktaliṅgairmunibhiḥ sarvasiddhāntavedibhiḥ
iha samprāpyate mokṣo durlabho 'nyatra karhicit
tebhyaścāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi yogaiśvaryamanuttamam
ātmanaścaiva sāyujyamīpsitaṃ sthānameva ca
kubero'tra mama kṣetre mayi sarvārpitakriyaḥ
kṣetrasaṃsevanādeva gaṇeśatvamavāpa ha
saṃvarto bhavitā yaś ca so'pi bhakto mamaiva tu
ihaivārādhya māṃ devi siddhiṃ yāsyatyanuttamām
parāśarasutau yogī ṛṣirvyāso mahātapāḥ
mama bhakto bhaviṣyaś ca vedasaṃsthāpravartakaḥ
raṃsyate so'pi padmākṣi kṣetre 'sminmunipuṅgavaḥ
brahmā devarṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ viṣṇurvāpi divākaraḥ
devarājastathā śakro ye'pi cānye divaukasaḥ
upāsate mahātmānaḥ sarve māmiha suvrate
anye'pi yogino divyāśchannarūpā mahātmanaḥ
ananyamanaso bhūtvā māmihopāsate sadā
viṣayāsaktacitto'pi tyaktadharmaratirnaraḥ
iha kṣetre mṛtaḥ so'pi saṃsāre na punarbhavet
ye punarnirmamā dhīrāḥ sattvasthā vijitendriyāḥ
vratinaś ca nirārambhāḥ sarve te mayi bhāvitāḥ
devadevaṃ samāsādya dhīmantaḥ saṃgavarjitāḥ
gatā iha paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate
janmāntarasahasreṣu yaṃ na yogī samāpnuyāt
tamihaiva paraṃ mokṣaṃ prasādānmama suvrate
goprekṣakam idaṃ kṣetraṃ brahmaṇā sthāpitaṃ purā
kailāsabhavanaṃ cātra paśya divyaṃ varānane
goprekṣakam athāgamya dṛṣṭvā māmatra mānavaḥ
na durgatimavāpnoti kalmaṣaiś ca vimucyate
kapilāhradam ityevaṃ tathā vai brahmaṇā kṛtam
gavāṃ stanyajatoyena tīrthaṃ puṇyatamaṃ mahat
atrāpi svayamevāhaṃ vṛṣadhvaja iti smṛtaḥ
sānnidhyaṃ kṛtavān devi sadāhaṃ dṛśyate tvayā
bhadratoyaṃ ca paśyeha brahmaṇā ca kṛtaṃ hradam
sarvairdevairahaṃ devi asmindeśe prasāditaḥ
gacchopaśamam īśeti upaśāntaḥ śivas tathā
atrāhaṃ brahmaṇānīya sthāpitaḥ parameṣṭhinā
brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgṛhya viṣṇunā sthāpitaḥ punaḥ
brahmaṇāpi tato viṣṇuḥ proktaḥ saṃvignacetasā
mayānītamidaṃ liṅgaṃ kasmāt sthāpitavān asi
tamuvāca punar viṣṇur brahmāṇaṃ kupitānanam
rudre deve mamātyantaṃ parā bhaktirmahattarā
mayaiva sthāpitaṃ liṅgaṃ tava nāmnā bhaviṣyati
hiraṇyagarbha ityevaṃ tato 'trāhaṃ samāsthitaḥ
dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ mama lokaṃ vrajennaraḥ
tataḥ punarapi brahmā mama liṅgamidaṃ śubham
sthāpayāmāsa vidhivadbhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ
svarlīneśvara ityevamatrāhaṃ svayamāgataḥ
prāṇān iha narastyaktvā na punarjāyate kvacit
ananyā sā gatistasya yogināṃ caiva yā smṛtā
asminnapi mayā deśe daityo daivatakaṇṭakaḥ
vyāghrarūpaṃ samāsthāya nihato darpito balī
vyāghreśvara iti khyāto nityamatrāhamāsthitaḥ
na punardurgatiṃ yāti dṛṣṭvainaṃ vyāghramīśvaram
utpalo vidalaścaiva yau daityau brahmaṇā purā
strīvadhyau darpitau dṛṣṭvā tvayaiva nihatau raṇe
sāvajñaṃ kandukenātra tasyedaṃ dehamāsthitam
ādāvatrāhamāgamya prasthito gaṇapaiḥ saha
jyeṣṭhasthānamidaṃ tasmādetanme puṇyadarśanam
devaiḥ samantād etāni liṅgāni sthāpitānyataḥ
dṛṣṭvāpi niyato martyo dehabhede gaṇo bhavet
pitrā te śailarājena purā himavatā svayam
mama priyahitaṃ sthānaṃ jñātvā liṅgaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
śaileśvaramiti khyātaṃ dṛśyatāmiha cādarāt
dṛṣṭvaitanmanujo devi na durgatimato vrajet
nadyeṣā varuṇā devi puṇyā pāpapramocanī
kṣetrametad alaṃkṛtya jāhnavyā saha saṃgatā
sthāpitaṃ brahmaṇā cāpi saṃgame liṅgamuttamam
saṃgameśvaram ityevaṃ khyātaṃ jagati dṛśyatām
saṃgame devanadyā hi yaḥ snātvā manujaḥ śuciḥ
arcayet saṃgameśvaraṃ tasya janmabhayaṃ kutaḥ
idaṃ manye mahākṣetraṃ nivāso yogināṃ param
kṣetramadhye ca yatrāhaṃ svayaṃ bhūtvāgramāsthitaḥ
madhyameśvaramityevaṃ khyātaḥ sarvasurāsuraiḥ
siddhānāṃ sthānametaddhi madīyavratadhāriṇām
yogināṃ mokṣalipsūnāṃ jñānayogaratātmanām
dṛṣṭvainaṃ madhyameśānaṃ janma prati na śocati
sthāpitaṃ liṅgametattu śukreṇa bhṛgusūnunā
nāmnā śukreśvaraṃ nāma sarvasiddhāmarārcitam
dṛṣṭvainaṃ niyataḥ sadyo mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ
mṛtaś ca na punarjantuḥ saṃsārī tu bhavennaraḥ
purā jambūkarūpeṇa asuro devakaṇṭakaḥ
brahmaṇo hi varaṃ labdhvā gomāyurbandhaśaṅkitaḥ
nihato himavatputri jambūkeśastato hyaham
adyāpi jagati khyātaṃ surāsuranamaskṛtam
dṛṣṭvainamapi deveśaṃ sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt
grahaiḥ śukrapurogaiś ca etāni sthāpitāni ha
paśya puṇyāni liṅgāni sarvakāmapradāni tu
evametāni puṇyāni mannivāsāni pārvati
kathitāni mama kṣetre guhyaṃ cānyadidaṃ śṛṇu
catuḥkrośaṃ caturdikṣu kṣetrametatprakīrtitam
yojanaṃ viddhi cārvaṅgi mṛtyukāle 'mṛtapradam
mahālayagiristhaṃ māṃ kedāre ca vyavasthitam
gaṇatvaṃ labhate dṛṣṭvā hyasminmokṣo hyavāpyate
gāṇapatyaṃ labhedyasmādyataḥ sā muktiruttamā
tato mahālayāt tasmāt kedārānmadhyamādapi
smṛtaṃ puṇyatamaṃ kṣetramavimuktaṃ varānane
kedāraṃ madhyamaṃ kṣetraṃ sthānaṃ caiva mahālayam
mama puṇyāni bhūrloke tebhyaḥ śreṣṭhatamaṃ tvidam
yataḥ sṛṣṭāstvime lokāstataḥ kṣetramidaṃ śubham
kadācinna mayā muktamavimuktaṃ tato 'bhavat
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ mama dṛṣṭveha mānavaḥ
sadyaḥ pāpavinirmuktaḥ paśupāśairvimucyate
śaileśaṃ saṃgameśaṃ ca svarlīnaṃ madhyameśvaram
hiraṇyagarbham īśānaṃ goprekṣaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam
upaśāntaṃ śivaṃ caiva jyeṣṭhasthānanivāsinam
śukreśvaraṃ ca vikhyātaṃ vyāghreśaṃ jambukeśvaram
dṛṣṭvā na jāyate martyaḥ saṃsāre duḥkhasāgare
sūta uvāca
evam uktvā mahādevo diśaḥ sarvā vyalokayat
vilokya saṃsthite paścāddevadeve maheśvare
akasmādabhavatsarvaḥ sa deśojjvalito yathā
tataḥ pāśupatāḥ siddhā bhasmābhyaṅgasitaprabhāḥ
māheśvarā mahātmānas tathā vai niyatavratāḥ
bahavaḥ śataśo 'bhyetya namaścakrurmaheśvaram
punarnirīkṣya yogeśaṃ dhyānayogaṃ ca kṛtsnaśaḥ
tasthurātmānamāsthāya līyamānā iveśvare
sthitānāṃ sa tadā teṣāṃ devadeva umāpatiḥ
sa bibhratparamāṃ mūrtiṃ babhūva puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ
kṛtsnaṃ jagadihaikasthaṃ kartum anta iva sthitaḥ
tasya tāṃ paramāṃ mūrtimāsthitasya jagatprabhoḥ
na śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ hṛṣṭaromā girīndrajā
tatastvadṛṣṭamākāraṃ buddhvā sā prakṛtisthitam
prakṛtermūrtimāsthāya yogena parameśvarī
taṃ śaśāka punardraṣṭuṃ harasya ca mahātmanaḥ
tataste layamādhāya yoginaḥ puruṣasya tu
viviśurhṛdayaṃ sarve dagdhasaṃsārabījinaḥ
pañcākṣarasya vai bījaṃ saṃsmarantaḥ suśobhanam
sarvapāpaharaṃ divyaṃ purā caiva prakāśitam
nīlalohitamūrtisthaṃ punaścakre vapuḥ śubham
taṃ dṛṣṭvā śailajā prāha hṛṣṭasarvatanūruhā
stuvatī caraṇau natvā ka ime bhagavanniti
tāmuvāca suraśreṣṭhastadā devīṃ girīndrajām
śrībhagavānuvāca
madīyaṃ vratamāśritya bhaktimadbhir dvijottamaiḥ
yairyairyogā ihābhyastās teṣām ekena janmanā
kṣetrasyāsya prabhāvena bhaktyā ca mama bhāmini
anugraho mayā hyevaṃ kriyate mūrtitaḥ svayam
tasmād etan mahat kṣetraṃ brahmādyaiḥ sevitaṃ tathā
śrutimadbhiś ca viprendraiḥ saṃsiddhaiś ca tapasvibhiḥ
pratimāsaṃ tathāṣṭamyāṃ pratimāsaṃ caturdaśīm
ubhayoḥ pakṣayordevi vārāṇasyāmupāsyate
śaśibhānūparāge ca kārtikyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
sarvaparvasu puṇyeṣu viṣuveṣvayaneṣu ca
pṛthivyāṃ sarvatīrthāni vārāṇasyāṃ tu jāhnavīm
uttarapravahāṃ puṇyāṃ mama mauliviniḥsṛtām
pituste girirājasya śubhāṃ himavataḥ sutām
puṇyasthānasthitāṃ puṇyāṃ puṇyadikpravahāṃ sadā
bhajante sarvato 'bhyetya ye tāñchṛṇu varānane
saṃnihatya kurukṣetraṃ sārdhaṃ tīrthaśatais tathā
puṣkaraṃ nimiṣaṃ caiva prayāgaṃ ca pṛthūdakam
drumakṣetraṃ kurukṣetraṃ naimiṣaṃ tīrthasaṃyutam
kṣetrāṇi sarvato devi devatā ṛṣayas tathā
saṃdhyā ca ṛtavaścaiva sarvā nadyaḥ sarāṃsi ca
samudrāḥ sapta caivātra devatīrthāni kṛtsnaśaḥ
bhāgīrathīṃ sameṣyanti sarvaparvasu suvrate
avimukteśvaraṃ dṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭvā caiva triviṣṭapam
kālabhairavamāsādya dhūtapāpāni sarvaśaḥ
bhavanti hi sureśāni sarvaparvasu parvasu
pṛthivyāṃ yāni puṇyāni mahāntyāyatanāni ca
praviśanti sadābhyetya puṇyaṃ parvasu parvasu
avimuktaṃ kṣetravaraṃ mahāpāpanibarhaṇam
kedāre caiva yalliṅgaṃ yacca liṅgaṃ mahālaye
madhyameśvarasaṃjñaṃ ca tathā pāśupateśvaram
śaṅkukarṇeśvaraṃ caiva gokarṇau ca tathā hyubhau
drumacaṇḍeśvaraṃ nāma bhadreśvaram anuttamam
sthāneśvaraṃ tathaikāgraṃ kāleśvaram ajeśvaram
bhairaveśvaram īśānaṃ tathauṃkārakasaṃjñitam
amareśaṃ mahākālaṃ jyotiṣaṃ bhasmagātrakam
yāni cānyāni puṇyāni sthānāni mama bhūtale
aṣṭaṣaṣṭisamākhyāni rūḍhānyanyāni kṛtsnaśaḥ
tāni sarvāṇyaśeṣāṇi vārāṇasyāṃ viśanti mām
sarvaparvasu puṇyeṣu guhyaṃ caitadudāhṛtam
teneha labhate janturmṛto divyāmṛtaṃ padam
snātasya caiva gaṅgāyāṃ dṛṣṭena ca mayā śubhe
sarvayajñaphalaistulyamiṣṭaiḥ śatasahasraśaḥ
sadya eva samāpnoti kiṃ tataḥ paramādbhutam
sarvāyatanamukhyāni divi bhūmau giriṣv api
parātparataraṃ devī budhyasveti mayoditam
aviśabdena pāpastu vedoktaḥ kathyate dvijaiḥ
tena muktaṃ mayā juṣṭamavimuktam ata ucyate
ityuktvā bhagavān rudraḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥ
sudṛṣṭaṃ kuru deveśi avimuktaṃ gṛhaṃ mama
ityuktvā bhagavān devas tayā sārdham umāpatiḥ
darśayāmāsa bhagavān śrīparvatamanuttamam
avimukteśvare nityam avasacca sadā tayā
sarvagatvācca sarvatvāt sarvātmā sadasanmayaḥ
śrīparvatamanuprāpyadevyā deveśvaro haraḥ
kṣetrāṇi darśayāmāsa sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ
kuṇḍīprabhaṃ ca paramaṃ divyaṃ vaiśravaṇeśvaram
āśāliṅgaṃ ca deveśaṃ divyaṃ yacca bileśvaram
rāmeśvaraṃ ca paramaṃ viṣṇunā yatpratiṣṭhitam
dakṣiṇadvārapārśve tu kuṇḍaleśvaramīśvaram
pūrvadvārasamīpasthaṃ tripurāntakamuttamam
vivṛddhaṃ giriṇā sārdhaṃ devadevanamaskṛtam
madhyameśvaramityuktaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam
amareśvaraṃ ca varadaṃ devaiḥ pūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
gocarmeśvaram īśānaṃ tathendreśvaram adbhutam
karmeśvaraṃ ca vipulaṃ kāryārthaṃ brahmaṇā kṛtam
śrīmatsiddhavaṭaṃ caiva sadāvāso mamāvyaye
ajena nirmitaṃ divyaṃ sākṣādajabilaṃ śubham
tatraiva pāduke divye madīye ca bileśvare
tatra śṛṅgāṭakākāraṃ śṛṅgāṭācalamadhyame
śṛṅgāṭakeśvaraṃ nāma śrīdevyā tu pratiṣṭhitam
mallikārjunakaṃ caiva mama vāsamidaṃ śubham
rajeśvaraṃ ca paryāye rajasā supratiṣṭhitam
gajeśvaraṃ ca vaiśākhaṃ kapoteśvaramavyayam
koṭīśvaraṃ mahātīrthaṃ rudrakoṭigaṇaiḥ purā
sevitaṃ devi paśyādya sarvasmādadhikaṃ śubham
dvidevakulasaṃjñaṃ ca brahmaṇā dakṣiṇe śubham
uttare sthāpitaṃ caiva viṣṇunā caiva śailajam
mahāpramāṇaliṅgaṃ ca mayā pūrvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
paścime parvate paśya brahmeśvaramaleśvaram
alaṃkṛtaṃ tvayā brahman purastān munibhiḥ saha
ityuktvā tadgṛhe tiṣṭhad alaṃgṛhamiti smṛtam
tatrāpi tīrthaṃ tīrthajñe vyomaliṅgaṃ ca paśya me
kadambeśvaram etaddhi skandenaiva pratiṣṭhitam
gomaṇḍaleśvaraṃ caiva nandādyaiḥ supratiṣṭhitam
devaiḥ sarvaistu śakrādyaiḥ sthāpitāni varānane
śrīmaddevahradaprānte sthānānīmāni paśya me
tathā hārapure devi tava hāre nipātite
tvayā hitāya jagatāṃ hārakuṇḍamidaṃ kṛtam
śivarudrapure caiva tatkāyopari suvrate
tatra pitrā suśailena sthāpitaṃ tvacaleśvaram
alaṃkṛtaṃ mayā brahma purastān munibhiḥ saha
caṇḍikeśvarakaṃ devi caṇḍikeśā tavātmajā
caṇḍikānirmitaṃ sthānam aṃbikātīrtham uttamam
rucikeśvarakaṃ caiva dhāraiṣā kapilā śubhā
eteṣu devi sthāneṣu tīrtheṣu vividheṣu ca
pūjayenmāṃ sadā bhaktyā mayā sārdhaṃ hi modate
śrīśaile saṃtyajed dehaṃ brāhmaṇo dagdhakilbiṣaḥ
mucyate nātra saṃdeho hyavimukte yathā śubham
mahāsnānaṃ ca yaḥ kuryādghṛtena vidhinaiva tu
sa yāti mama sāyujyaṃ sthāneṣveteṣu suvrate
snānaṃ palaśataṃ jñeyamabhyaṅgaṃ pañcaviṃśati
palānāṃ dve sahasre tu mahāsnānaṃ prakīrtitam
snāpya liṅgaṃ madīyaṃ tu gavyenaiva ghṛtena ca
viśodhya sarvadravyaistu vāribhir abhiṣiñcati
saṃmārjya śatayajñānāṃ snānena prayutaṃ tathā
pūjayā śatasāhasramanantaṃ gītavādinām
mahāsnāne prasaktaṃ tu snānamaṣṭaguṇaṃ smṛtam
jalena kevalenaiva gandhatoyena bhaktitaḥ
anulepanaṃ tu tat sarvaṃ pañcaviṃśatpalena vai
śamīpuṣpaṃ ca vidhinā bilvapatraṃ ca paṅkajam
anyānyapi ca puṣpāṇi bilvapatraṃ na saṃtyajet
caturdroṇair mahādevam aṣṭadroṇairathāpi vā
daśadroṇais tu naivedyam aṣṭadroṇairathāpi vā
śatadroṇasamaṃ puṇyam āḍhake'pi vidhīyate
vittahīnasya viprasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
bherīmṛdaṅgamurajatimirāpaṭahādibhiḥ
vāditrairvividhaiścānyairninādairvividhairapi
jāgaraṃ kārayedyastu prārthayecca yathākramam
sa bhṛtyaputradāraiś ca tathā saṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ
sārdhaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā prārthayelliṅgam uttamam
dravyahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ śraddhāhīnaṃ sureśvara
kṛtaṃ vā na kṛtaṃ vāpi kṣantumarhasi śaṅkara
ityuktvā vai japedrudraṃ tvaritaṃ śāntimeva ca
japitvaivaṃ mahābījaṃ tathā pañcākṣarasya vai
sa evaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu sarvayajñeṣu yatphalam
tatphalaṃ samavāpnoti vārāṇasyāṃ yathā mṛtaḥ
tathaiva mama sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
matpriyārthamidaṃ kāryaṃ madbhaktairvidhipūrvakam
ye na kurvanti te bhaktā na bhavanti na saṃśayaḥ
sūta uvāca
niśamya vacanaṃ devī gatvā vārāṇasīṃ purīm
avimukteśvaraṃ liṅgaṃ payasā ca ghṛtena ca
arcayāmāsa deveśaṃ rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam
avimukte ca tapasā mandarasya mahātmanaḥ
kalpayāmāsa vai kṣetraṃ mandare cārukandare
tatrāndhakaṃ mahādaityaṃ hiraṇyākṣasutaṃ prabhuḥ
anugṛhya gaṇatvaṃ ca prāpayāmāsa līlayā
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamādarāt
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi kṣetramāhātmyamuttamam
sarvakṣetreṣu yatpuṇyaṃ tatsarvaṃ sahasā labhet
śrāvayedvā dvijānsarvān kṛtaśaucān jitendriyān
sa eva sarvayajñasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vārāṇasīśrīśailamāhātmyakathanaṃ nāma dvinavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
andhako nāma daityendro mandare cārukandare
damitastu kathaṃ lebhe gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ yathāśrutam
sūta uvāca
andhakānugrahaṃ caiva mandare śoṣaṇaṃ tathā
varalābhamaśeṣaṃ ca pravadāmi samāsataḥ
hiraṇyākṣasya tanayo hiraṇyanayanopamaḥ
purāndhaka iti khyātastapasā labdhavikramaḥ
prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ sākṣādavadhyatvamavāpya ca
trailokyamakhilaṃ bhuktvā jitvā cendrapuraṃ purā
līlayā cāprayatnena trāsayāmāsa vāsavam
bādhitāstāḍitā baddhāḥ pātitāstena te surāḥ
viviśurmandaraṃ bhītā nārāyaṇapurogamāḥ
evaṃ saṃpīḍya vai devān andhako'pi mahāsuraḥ
yadṛcchayā giriṃ prāpto mandaraṃ cārukandaram
tataste samastāḥ surendrāḥ sasādhyāḥ sureśaṃ maheśaṃ puretyāhurevam
drutaṃ cālpavīryaprabhinnāṅgabhinnā vayaṃ daityarājasya śastrairnikṛttāḥ
itīdamakhilaṃ śrutvā daityāgamam anaupamam
gaṇeśvaraiś ca bhagavānandhakābhimukhaṃ yayau
tatrendrapadmodbhavaviṣṇumukhyāḥ sureśvarā vipravarāś ca sarve
jayeti vācā bhagavantam ūcuḥ kirīṭabaddhāñjalayaḥ samantāt
athāśeṣāsurāṃstasya koṭikoṭiśatais tataḥ
bhasmīkṛtya mahādevo nirbibhedāndhakaṃ tadā
śūlena śūlinā protaṃ dagdhakalmaṣakañcukam
dṛṣṭvāndhakaṃ nanādeśaṃ praṇamya sa pitāmahaḥ
tannādaśravaṇānnedurdevā devaṃ praṇamya tam
nanṛturmunayaḥ sarve mumudurgaṇapuṅgavāḥ
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi devāḥ śaṃbhostadopari
trailokyamakhilaṃ harṣānnananda ca nanāda ca
dagdho'gninā ca śūlena protaḥ preta ivāndhakaḥ
sāttvikaṃ bhāvamāsthāya cintayāmāsa cetasā
janmāntare'pi devena dagdho yasmācchivena vai
ārādhito mayā śaṃbhuḥ purā sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ
tasmādetanmayā labdhamanyathā nopapadyate
yaḥ smarenmanasā rudraṃ prāṇānte sakṛdeva vā
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ kiṃ punarbahuśaḥ smaran
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
śaraṇaṃ prāpya tiṣṭhanti tameva śaraṇaṃ vrajet
evaṃ saṃcintya tuṣṭātmā so 'ndhakaś cāndhakārdanam
sagaṇaṃ śivamīśānamastuvatpuṇyagauravāt
prārthitastena bhagavān paramārtiharo haraḥ
hiraṇyanetratanayaṃ śūlāgrasthaṃ sureśvaraḥ
provāca dānavaṃ prekṣya ghṛṇayā nīlalohitaḥ
tuṣṭo'smi vatsa bhadraṃ te kāmaṃ kiṃ karavāṇi te
varānvaraya daityendra varado'haṃ tavāndhaka
śrutvā vākyaṃ tadā śaṃbhor hiraṇyanayanātmajaḥ
harṣagadgadayā vācā provācedaṃ maheśvaram
bhagavandevadeveśa bhaktārtihara śaṅkara
tvayi bhaktiḥ prasīdeśa yadi deyo varaś ca me
śrutvā bhavo'pi vacanamandhakasya mahātmanaḥ
pradadau durlabhāṃ śraddhāṃ daityendrāya mahādyutiḥ
gāṇapatyaṃ ca daityāya pradadau cāvaropya tam
praṇemustaṃ surendrādyā gāṇapatye pratiṣṭhitam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge andhakagāṇapatyātmako nāma trinavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathamasya pitā daityo hiraṇyākṣaḥ sudāruṇaḥ
viṣṇunā sūdito viṣṇur vārāhatvaṃ kathaṃ gataḥ
tasya śṛṅgaṃ maheśasya bhūṣaṇatvaṃ kathaṃ gatam
etatsarvaṃ viśeṣeṇa sūta vaktumihārhasi
sūta uvāca
hiraṇyakaśiporbhrātā hiraṇyākṣa iti smṛtaḥ
purāndhakāsureśasya pitā kālāntakopamaḥ
devāñjitvātha daityendro baddhvā ca dharaṇīmimām
nītvā rasātalaṃ cakre vandīm indīvaraprabhām
tataḥ sabrahmakā devāḥ parimlānamukhaśriyaḥ
bādhitāstāḍitā baddhvā hiraṇyākṣeṇa tena vai
balinā daityamukhyena krūreṇa sudurātmanā
praṇamya śirasā viṣṇuṃ daityakoṭivimardanam
sarve vijñāpayāmāsurdharaṇībandhanaṃ hareḥ
śrutvaitadbhagavān viṣṇurdharaṇībandhanaṃ hariḥ
bhūtvā yajñavarāho 'sau yathā liṅgodbhave tathā
daityaiś ca sārdhaṃ daityendraṃ hiraṇyākṣaṃ mahābalam
daṃṣṭrāgrakoṭyā hatvainaṃ reje daityāntakṛtprabhuḥ
kalpādiṣu yathāpūrvaṃ praviśya ca rasātalam
ānīya vasudhāṃ devīmaṅkasthāmakarodbahiḥ
tatas tuṣṭāva deveśaṃ devadevaḥ pitāmahaḥ
śakrādyaiḥ sahito bhūtvā harṣagadgadayā girā
śāśvatāya varāhāya daṃṣṭriṇe daṇḍine namaḥ
nārāyaṇāya sarvāya brahmaṇe paramātmane
kartre dhartre dharāyāstu hartre devāriṇāṃ svayam
kartre netre surendrāṇāṃ śāstre ca sakalasya ca
tvamaṣṭamūrtistvamanantamūrtistvamādidevastvamanantaveditaḥ
tvayā kṛtaṃ sarvamidaṃ prasīda sureśa lokeśa varāha viṣṇo
tathaikadaṃṣṭrāgramukhāgrakoṭibhāgaikabhāgārdhatamena viṣṇo
hatāḥ kṣaṇāt kāmada daityamukhyāḥ svadaṃṣṭrakoṭyā saha putrabhṛtyaiḥ
tvayoddhṛtā deva dharā dhareśa dharādharākāra dhṛtāgradaṃṣṭre
dharādharaiḥ sarvajanaiḥ samudraiḥ surāsuraiḥ sevitacandravaktra
tvayaiva deveśa vibho kṛtaś ca jayaḥ surāṇāmasureśvarāṇām
aho pradattastu varaḥ prasīda vāgdevatā vārijasaṃbhavāya
tava romṇi sakalāmareśvarā nayanadvaye śaśiravī padadvaye
nihitā rasātalagatā vasuṃdharā tava pṛṣṭhataḥ sakalatārakādayaḥ
jagatāṃ hitāya bhavatā vasuṃdharā bhagavan rasātalapuṭaṃ gatā tadā
abaloddhṛtā ca bhagavaṃstavaiva sakalaṃ tvayaiva hi dhṛtaṃ jagadguro
iti vākpatirbahuvidhaistavārcanaiḥ praṇipatya viṣṇumamaraiḥ prajāpatiḥ
vividhānvarān harimukhāttu labdhavān harinābhivārijadehabhṛt svayam
atha tāmuddhṛtāṃ tena dharāṃ devā munīśvarāḥ
mūrdhnyāropya namaścakruś cakriṇaḥ saṃnidhau tadā
anenaiva varāheṇa coddhṛtāsi varaprade
kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakāryeṇa śatahastena viṣṇunā
dharaṇi tvaṃ mahābhoge bhūmistvaṃ dhenuravyaye
lokānāṃ dhāriṇī tvaṃ hi mṛttike hara pātakam
manasā karmaṇā vācā varade vārijekṣaṇe
tvayā hatena pāpena jīvāmastvatprasādataḥ
ityuktā sā tadā devī dharā devair athābravīt
varāhadaṃṣṭrābhinnāyāṃ dharāyāṃ mṛttikāṃ dvijāḥ
mantreṇānena yo bibhrat mūrdhni pāpātpramucyate
āyuṣmān balavān dhanyaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ
kramādbhuvi divaṃ prāpya karmānte modate suraiḥ
atha deve gate tyaktvā varāhe kṣīrasāgaram
vārāharūpamanaghaṃ cacāla ca dharā punaḥ
tasya daṃṣṭrābharākrāntā devadevasya dhīmataḥ
yadṛcchayā bhavaḥ paśyan jagāma jagadīśvaraḥ
daṃṣṭrāṃ jagrāha dṛṣṭvā tāṃ bhūṣaṇārthamathātmanaḥ
dadhāra ca mahādevaḥ kūrcānte vai mahorasi
devāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sendrā devadevasya vaibhavam
dharā pratiṣṭhitā hyevaṃ devadevena līlayā
bhūtānāṃ saṃplave cāpi viṣṇoścaiva kalevaram
brahmaṇaś ca tathānyeṣāṃ devānāmapi līlayā
vibhuraṅgavibhāgena bhūṣito na yadi prabhuḥ
kathaṃ vimuktirviprāṇāṃ tasmāddaṃṣṭrī maheśvaraḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge varāhaprādurbhāvo nāma caturnavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nṛsiṃhena hataḥ pūrvaṃ hiraṇyākṣāgrajaḥ śrutam
kathaṃ niṣūditastena hiraṇyakaśipurvada
sūta uvāca
hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putraḥ prahrāda iti viśrutaḥ
dharmajñaḥ satyasampannas tapasvī cābhavatsudhīḥ
janmaprabhṛti deveśaṃ pūjayāmāsa cāvyayam
sarvajñaṃ sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvadevabhavodbhavam
tamādipuruṣaṃ bhaktyā parabrahmasvarūpiṇam
brahmaṇo 'dhipatiṃ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārakāraṇam
so'pi viṣṇostathābhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā putraṃ samāhitam
namo nārāyaṇāyeti govindeti muhurmuhuḥ
stuvantaṃ prāha devāriḥ pradahanniva pāpadhīḥ
na māṃ jānāsi durbuddhe sarvadaityāmareśvaram
prahrāda vīra duṣputra dvijadevārtikāraṇam
ko viṣṇuḥ padmajo vāpi śakraś ca varuṇo'thavā
vāyuḥ somastatheśānaḥ pāvako mama yaḥ samaḥ
māmevārcaya bhaktyā ca svalpaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ sadā
prahrāda jīvite vāñchā tavaiṣā śṛṇu cāsti cet
śrutvāpi tasya vacanaṃ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ sudhīḥ
prahrādaḥ pūjayāmāsa namo nārāyaṇeti ca
namo nārāyaṇāyeti sarvadaityakumārakān
adhyāpayāmāsa ca tāṃ brahmavidyāṃ suśobhanām
durlaṅghyāṃ cātmano dṛṣṭvā śakrādibhir api svayam
putreṇa laṅghitāmājñāṃ hiraṇyaḥ prāha dānavān
etaṃ nānāvidhairvadhyaṃ duṣputraṃ hantumarhatha
evamuktāstadā tena daityena sudurātmanā
nijaghnurdevadevasya bhṛtyaṃ prahrādamavyayam
tatra tatpratikṛtaṃ tadā surairdaityarājatanayaṃ dvijottamāḥ
kṣīravārinidhiśāyinaḥ prabhorniṣphalaṃ tvatha babhūva tejasā
tadātha garvabhinnasya hiraṇyakaśipoḥ prabhuḥ
tatraivāvirabhūddhantuṃ nṛsiṃhākṛtimāsthitaḥ
jaghāna ca sutaṃ prekṣya pitaraṃ dānavādhamam
bibheda tatkṣaṇādeva karajair niśitaiḥ śataiḥ
tato nihatya taṃ daityaṃ sabāndhavamaghāpahaḥ
pīḍayāmāsa daityendraṃ yugāntāgnirivāparaḥ
nādaistasya nṛsiṃhasya ghorairvitrāsitaṃ jagat
ā brahmabhuvanād viprāḥ pracacāla ca suvratāḥ
dṛṣṭvā surāsuramahoragasiddhasādhyās tasmin kṣaṇe hariviriñcimukhā nṛsiṃham
dhairyaṃ balaṃ ca samavāpya yayurvisṛjya ā diṅmukhāntam asurakṣaṇatatparāś ca
tatastairgataiḥ saiṣa devo nṛsiṃhaḥ sahasrākṛtiḥ sarvapāt sarvabāhuḥ
sahasrekṣaṇaḥ somasūryāgninetrastadā saṃsthitaḥ sarvamāvṛtya māyī
taṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ suraśreṣṭhā lokā lokācale sthitāḥ
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sayamāḥ samarudgaṇāḥ
parātparataraṃ brahma tattvāt tattvatamaṃ bhavān
jyotiṣāṃ tu paraṃ jyotiḥ paramātmā jaganmayaḥ
sthūlaṃ sūkṣmaṃ susūkṣmaṃ ca śabdabrahmamayaḥ śubhaḥ
vāgatīto nirālaṃbo nirdvandvo nirupaplavaḥ
yajñabhugyajñamūrtistvaṃ yajñināṃ phaladaḥ prabhuḥ
bhavānmatsyākṛtiḥ kaurmamāsthāya jagati sthitaḥ
vārāhīṃ caiva tāṃ saiṃhīmāsthāyehavyavasthitaḥ
devānāṃ devarakṣārthaṃ nihatya ditijeśvaram
dvijaśāpacchalenaivam avatīrṇo'si līlayā
na dṛṣṭaṃ yattvadanyaṃ hi bhavān sarvaṃ carācaram
bhavānviṣṇurbhavān rudro bhavāneva pitāmahaḥ
bhavānādirbhavānanto bhavāneva vayaṃ vibho
bhavāneva jagatsarvaṃ pralāpena kimīśvara
māyayā bahudhā saṃsthamadvitīyamayaṃ prabho
stoṣyāmastvāṃ kathaṃ bhāsi devadeva mṛgādhipa
stuto'pi vividhaiḥ stutyairbhāvairnānāvidhaiḥ prabhuḥ
na jagāma dvijāḥ śāntiṃ mānayanyonimātmanaḥ
yo nṛsiṃhastavaṃ bhaktyā paṭhedvārthaṃ vicārayet
śrāvayedvā dvijānsarvān viṣṇuloke mahīyate
tadantare śivaṃ devāḥ sendrāḥ sabrahmakāḥ prabhum
samprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarvaṃ vijñāpya mṛgarūpiṇaḥ
tato brahmādayastūrṇaṃ saṃstūya parameśvaram
ātmatrāṇāya śaraṇaṃ jagmuḥ paramakāraṇam
mandarasthaṃ mahādevaṃ krīḍamānaṃ sahomayā
sevitaṃ gaṇagandharvaiḥ siddhairapsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ
devatābhiḥ saha brahmā bhītabhītaḥ sagadgadam
praṇamya daṇḍavadbhūmau tuṣṭāva parameśvaram
brahmovāca
namaste kālakālāya namaste rudra manyave
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te
ugro'si sarvabhūtānāṃ niyantāsi śivo'si naḥ
namaḥ śivāya śarvāya śaṅkarāyārttihāriṇe
mayaskarāya viśvāya viṣṇave brahmaṇe namaḥ
antakāya namastubhyamumāyāḥ pataye namaḥ
hiraṇyabāhave sākṣāddhiraṇyapataye namaḥ
śarvāya sarvarūpāya puruṣāya namonamaḥ
sadasadvyaktihīnāya mahataḥ kāraṇāya te
nityāya viśvarūpāya jāyamānāya te namaḥ
jātāya bahudhā loke prabhūtāya namonamaḥ
rudrāya nīlarudrāya kadrudrāya pracetase
kālāya kālarūpāya namaḥ kālāṅgahāriṇe
mīḍhuṣṭamāya devāya śitikaṇṭhāya te namaḥ
mahīyase namastubhyaṃ hantre devāriṇāṃ sadā
tārāya ca sutārāya tāraṇāya namonamaḥ
harikeśāya devāya śaṃbhave paramātmane
devānāṃ śaṃbhave tubhyaṃ bhūtānāṃ śaṃbhave namaḥ
śambhave haimavatyāś ca manyave rudrarūpiṇe
kapardine namastubhyaṃ kālakaṇṭhāya te namaḥ
hiraṇyāya maheśāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namonamaḥ
bhasmadigdhaśarīrāya daṇḍamuṇḍīśvarāya ca
namo hrasvāya dīrghāya vāmanāya namonamaḥ
nama ugratriśūlāya ugrāya ca namo namaḥ
bhīmāya bhīmarūpāya bhīmakarmaratāya te
agrevadhāya vai bhūtvā namo dūrevadhāya ca
dhanvine śūline tubhyaṃ gadine haline namaḥ
cakriṇe varmiṇe nityaṃ daityānāṃ karmabhedine
sadyāya sadyarūpāya sadyojātāya te namaḥ
vāmāya vāmarūpāya vāmanetrāya te namaḥ
aghorarūpāya vikaṭāya vikaṭaśarīrāya te namaḥ
puruṣarūpāya puruṣaikatatpuruṣāya vai namaḥ
puruṣārthapradānāya pataye parameṣṭhine
īśānāya namastubhyamīśvarāya namonamaḥ
brahmaṇe brahmarūpāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te
sarvaviṣṇurnṛsiṃhasya rūpamāsthāya viśvakṛt
hiraṇyakaśipuṃ hatvā karajairniśitaiḥ svayam
daityendrairbahubhiḥ sārdhaṃ hitārthaṃ jagatāṃ prabhuḥ
saiṃhīṃ samānayanyoniṃ bādhate nikhilaṃ jagat
yatkṛtyamatra deveśa tatkuruṣva bhavāniha
ugro'si sarvaduṣṭānāṃ niyantāsi śivo'si naḥ
kālakūṭādivapuṣā trāhi naḥ śaraṇāgatān
śukraṃ tu vṛttaṃ viśveśa krīḍā vai kevalaṃ vayam
tavonmeṣanimeṣābhyāmasmākaṃ pralayodayau
unmīlayet tvayi brahman vināśo'sti na te śiva
saṃtaptāsmo vayaṃ deva hariṇāmitatejasā
sarvalokahitāyainaṃ tattvaṃ saṃhartumicchasi
sūta uvāca
vijñāpitas tathā devaḥ prahasanprāha tān surān
abhayaṃ ca dadau teṣāṃ haniṣyāmīti taṃ prabhuḥ
so'pi śakraḥ suraiḥ sārdhaṃ praṇipatya yathāgatam
jagāma bhagavān brahmā tathānye ca surottamāḥ
athotthāya mahādevaḥ śārabhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ
yayau prānte nṛsiṃhasya garvitasya mṛgāśinaḥ
apahṛtya tadā prāṇān śarabhaḥ surapūjitaḥ
siṃhāttato naro bhūtvā jagāma ca yathākramam
evaṃ stutastadā devairjagāma sa yathākramam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi saṃstavaṃ śārvamuttamam
rudralokamanuprāpya rudreṇa saha modate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge nārasiṃhe pañcanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ devo mahādevo viśvasaṃhārakārakaḥ
śarabhākhyaṃ mahāghoraṃ vikṛtaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ
kiṃ kiṃ dhairyaṃ kṛtaṃ tena brūhi sarvam aśeṣataḥ
sūta uvāca
evamabhyarthito devairmatiṃ cakre kṛpālayaḥ
yattejastu nṛsiṃhākhyaṃ saṃhartuṃ parameśvaraḥ
tadarthaṃ smṛtavān rudro vīrabhadraṃ mahābalam
ātmano bhairavaṃ rūpaṃ mahāpralayakārakam
ājagāma purā sadyo gaṇānāmagrato hasan
sāṭṭahāsair gaṇavarair utpatadbhir itastataḥ
nṛsiṃharūpairatyugraiḥ koṭibhiḥ parivāritaḥ
tāvadbhir abhito vīrairnṛtyadbhiś ca mudānvitaiḥ
krīḍadbhiś ca mahādhīrairbrahmādyaiḥ kandukairiva
adṛṣṭapūrvairanyaiś ca veṣṭito vīravanditaḥ
kalpāntajvalanajvālo vilasallocanatrayaḥ
āttaśastro jaṭājūṭe jvaladbālendumaṇḍitaḥ
bālendudvitayākāratīkṣṇadaṃṣṭrāṅkuradvayaḥ
ākhaṇḍaladhanuḥkhaṇḍasaṃnibhabhrūlatāyutaḥ
mahāpracaṇḍahuṅkārabadhirīkṛtadiṅmukhaḥ
nīlameghāñjanākārabhīṣaṇaśmaśruradbhutaḥ
vādakhaṇḍam akhaṇḍābhyāṃ bhrāmayaṃstriśikhaṃ muhuḥ
vīrabhadro'pi bhagavān vīraśaktivijṛmbhitaḥ
svayaṃ vijñāpayāmāsa kimatra smṛtikāraṇam
ājñāpaya jagatsvāmin prasādaḥ kriyatāṃ mayi
śrībhagavānuvāca
akāle bhayamutpannaṃ devānāmapi bhairava
jvalitaḥ sa nṛsiṃhāgniḥ śamayainaṃ durāsadam
sāntvayan bodhayādau taṃ tena kiṃ nopaśāmyati
tato matparamaṃ bhāvaṃ bhairavaṃ saṃpradarśaya
sūkṣmaṃ sūkṣmeṇa saṃhṛtya sthūlaṃ sthūlena tejasā
vaktramānaya kṛttiṃ ca vīrabhadra mamājñayā
ityādiṣṭo gaṇādhyakṣaḥ praśāntavapurāsthitaḥ
jagāma raṃhasā tatra yatrāste narakesarī
tatastaṃ bodhayāmāsa vīrabhadro haro harim
uvāca vākyamīśānaḥ pitā putramivaurasam
śrīvīrabhadra uvāca
jagatsukhāya bhagavann avatīrṇo'si mādhava
sthityarthena ca yukto'si pareṇa parameṣṭhinā
jantucakraṃ bhagavatā rakṣitaṃ matsyarūpiṇā
pucchenaiva samābadhya bhramannekārṇave purā
bibharṣi kūrmarūpeṇa vārāheṇoddhṛtā mahī
anena harirūpeṇa hiraṇyakaśipurhataḥ
vāmanena balirbaddhastvayā vikramatā punaḥ
tvam eva sarvabhūtānāṃ prabhāvaḥ prabhur avyayaḥ
yadā yadā hi lokasya duḥkhaṃ kiṃcit prajāyate
tadā tadāvatīrṇastvaṃ kariṣyasi nirāmayam
nādhikastvatsamo'pyasti hare śivaparāyaṇa
tvayā dharmāś ca vedāś ca śubhe mārge pratiṣṭhitāḥ
yadartham avatāro'yaṃ nihataḥ so'pi keśava
atyantaghoraṃ bhagavannarasiṃha vapustava
upasaṃhara viśvātmaṃstvameva mama saṃnidhau
sūta uvāca
ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ śāntayā girā
tato'dhikaṃ mahāghoraṃ kopaṃ prajvālayaddhariḥ
śrīnṛsiṃha uvāca
āgato'si yatastatra gaccha tvaṃ mā hitaṃ vada
idānīṃ saṃhariṣyāmi jagadetaccarācaram
saṃhartur na hi saṃhāraḥ svato vā parato'pi vā
śāsitaṃ mama sarvatra śāstā ko'pi na vidyate
matprasādena sakalaṃ samaryādaṃ pravartate
ahaṃ hi sarvaśaktīnāṃ pravartakanivartakaḥ
yad yad vibhūtimat sattvaṃ śrīmadūrjitameva vā
tattadviddhi gaṇādhyakṣa mama tejovijṛmbhitam
devatāparamārthajñā mamaiva paramaṃ viduḥ
madaṃśāḥ śaktisampannā brahmaśakrādayaḥ surāḥ
mannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ purā brahmā caturmukhaḥ
tallalāṭasamutpanno bhagavānvṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
rajasādhiṣṭhitaḥ sraṣṭā rudrastāmasa ucyate
ahaṃ niyantā sarvasya matparaṃ nāsti daivatam
viśvādhikaḥ svatantraś ca kartā hartākhileśvaraḥ
idaṃ tu matparaṃ tejaḥ kaḥ punaḥ śrotumicchati
ato māṃ śaraṇaṃ prāpya gaccha tvaṃ vigatajvaraḥ
avehi paramaṃ bhāvamidaṃ bhūtamaheśvaraḥ
kālo'smyahaṃ kālavināśaheturlokān samāhartum ahaṃ pravṛttaḥ
mṛtyormṛtyuṃ viddhi māṃ vīrabhadra jīvantyete matprasādena devāḥ
sūta uvāca
sāhaṅkāramidaṃ śrutvā harer amitavikramaḥ
vihasyovāca sāvajñaṃ tato visphuritādharaḥ
śrīvīrabhadra uvāca
kiṃ na jānāsi viśveśaṃ saṃhartāraṃ pinākinam
asadvādo vivādaś ca vināśastvayi kevalaḥ
tavānyonyāvatārāṇi kāni śeṣāṇi sāṃpratam
kṛtāni yena kenāpi kathāśeṣo bhaviṣyati
doṣaṃ tvaṃ paśya etattvamavasthāmīdṛśīṃ gataḥ
tena saṃhāradakṣeṇa kṣaṇātsaṃkṣayameṣyasi
prakṛtistvaṃ pumān rudrastvayi vīryaṃ samāhitam
tvannābhipaṅkajājjātaḥ pañcavaktraḥ pitāmahaḥ
sṛṣṭyarthena jagatpūrvaṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam
lalāṭe cintayāmāsa tapasyugre vyavasthitaḥ
tallalāṭādabhūcchaṃbhoḥ sṛṣṭyarthaṃ tanna dūṣaṇam
aṃśo'haṃ devadevasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ
tvatsaṃhāre niyukto'smi vinayena balena ca
evaṃ rakṣo vidāryaiva tvaṃ śaktikalayā yutaḥ
ahaṅkārāvalepena garjasi tvamatandritaḥ
upakāro hyasādhūnāmapakārāya kevalam
yadi siṃha maheśānaṃ svapunarbhūta manyase
na tvaṃ sraṣṭā na saṃhartā na svatantro hi kutracit
kulālacakravacchaktyā prerito'si pinākinā
adyāpi tava nikṣiptaṃ kapālaṃ kūrmarūpiṇaḥ
harahāralatāmadhye mugdha kasmānna budhyase
vismṛtaṃ kiṃ tadaṃśena daṃṣṭrotpātanapīḍitaḥ
vārāhavigrahaste 'dya sākrośaṃ tārakāriṇā
dagdho'si yasya śūlāgre viṣvaksenacchalādbhavān
dakṣayajñe śiraśchinnaṃ mayā te yajñarūpiṇaḥ
adyāpi tava putrasya brahmaṇaḥ pañcamaṃ śiraḥ
chinnaṃ tamenābhisaṃdhaṃ tadaṃśaṃ tasya tadbalam
nirjitastvaṃ dadhīcena saṃgrāme samarudgaṇaḥ
kaṇḍūyamāne śirasi kathaṃ tadvismṛtaṃ tvayā
cakraṃ vikramato yasya cakrapāṇe tava priyam
kutaḥ prāptaṃ kṛtaṃ kena tvayā tadapi vismṛtam
te mayā sakalā lokā gṛhītāstvaṃ payonidhau
nidrāparavaśaḥ śeṣe sa kathaṃ sāttviko bhavān
tvadādistambaparyantaṃ rudraśaktivijṛmbhitam
śaktimānabhitastvaṃ ca hyanalastvaṃ ca mohitaḥ
tattejaso'pi māhātmyaṃ yuvāṃ draṣṭuṃ na hi kṣamau
sthūlā ye hi prapaśyanti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
dyāvāpṛthivyā indrāgniyamasya varuṇasya ca
dhvāntodare śaśāṅkasya janitvā parameśvaraḥ
kālo'si tvaṃ mahākālaḥ kālakālo maheśvaraḥ
atastvamugrakalayā mṛtyormṛtyurbhaviṣyasi
sthiradhanvā kṣayo vīro vīro viśvādhikaḥ prabhuḥ
upahastā jvaraṃ bhīmo mṛgapakṣihiraṇmayaḥ
śāstāśeṣasya jagato na tvaṃ naivacaturmukhaḥ
itthaṃ sarvaṃ samālokya saṃharātmānam ātmanā
no cedidānīṃ krodhasya mahābhairavarūpiṇaḥ
