vajrāśaniriva sthāṇostvevaṃ mṛtyuḥ patiṣyati
sūta uvāca
ityukto vīrabhadreṇa nṛsiṃhaḥ krodhavihvalaḥ
nanāda tanuvegena taṃ gṛhītuṃ pracakrame
atrāntare mahāghoraṃ vipakṣabhayakāraṇam
gaganavyāpi durdharṣaśaivatejaḥsamudbhavam
vīrabhadrasya tadrūpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva dṛśyate
na taddhiraṇmayaṃ saumyaṃ na sauraṃ nāgnisaṃbhavam
na taḍiccandrasadṛśamanaupamyaṃ maheśvaram
tadā tejāṃsi sarvāṇi tasmin līnāni śāṅkare
tato vyakto mahātejā vyakte saṃbhavatastataḥ
rudrasādhāraṇaṃ caiva cihnitaṃ vikṛtākṛti
tataḥ saṃhārarūpeṇa suvyaktaḥ parameśvaraḥ
paśyatāṃ sarvadevānāṃ jayaśabdādimaṅgalaiḥ
sahasrabāhur jaṭilaścandrārdhakṛtaśekharaḥ
sa mṛgārdhaśarīreṇa pakṣābhyāṃ cañcunā dvijāḥ
atitīkṣṇamahādaṃṣṭro vajratulyanakhāyudhaḥ
kaṇṭhe kālo mahābāhuś catuṣpād vahnisaṃbhavaḥ
yugāntodyatajīmūtabhīmagaṃbhīraniḥsvanaḥ
samaṃ kupitavṛttāgnivyāvṛttanayanatrayaḥ
spaṣṭadaṃṣṭro 'dharoṣṭhaś ca huṅkāreṇa yuto haraḥ
haristaddarśanādeva vinaṣṭabalavikramaḥ
bibhrad aurmyaṃ sahasrāṃśoradhaḥ khadyotavibhramam
atha vibhramya pakṣābhyāṃ nābhipāde 'bhyudārayan
pādāvābadhya pucchena bāhubhyāṃ bāhumaṇḍalam
bhindannurasi bāhubhyāṃ nijagrāha haro harim
tato jagāma gaganaṃ devaiḥ saha maharṣibhiḥ
sahasaiva bhayādviṣṇuṃ vihagaś ca yathoragam
utkṣipyotkṣipya saṃgṛhya nipātya ca nipātya ca
uḍḍīyoḍḍīya bhagavān pakṣāghātavimohitam
hariṃ harantaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ viśveśānaṃ tamīśvaram
anuyānti surāḥ sarve namovākyena tuṣṭuvuḥ
nīyamānaḥ paravaśo dīnavaktraḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ haristaṃ lalitākṣaraiḥ
śrīnṛsiṃha uvāca
namo rudrāya śarvāya mahāgrāsāya viṣṇave
nama ugrāya bhīmāya namaḥ krodhāya manyave
namo bhavāya śarvāya śaṅkarāya śivāya te
kālakālāya kālāya mahākālāya mṛtyave
vīrāya vīrabhadrāya kṣayadvīrāya śūline
mahādevāya mahate paśūnāṃ pataye namaḥ
ekāya nīlakaṇṭhāya śrīkaṇṭhāya pinākine
namo 'nantāya sūkṣmāya namaste mṛtyumanyave
parāya parameśāya parātparatarāya te
parātparāya viśvāya namaste viśvamūrttaye
namo viṣṇukalatrāya viṣṇukṣetrāya bhānave
kaivartāya kirātāya mahāvyādhāya śāśvate
bhairavāya śaraṇyāya mahābhairavarūpiṇe
namo nṛsiṃhasaṃhartre kāmakālapurāraye
mahāpāśaughasaṃhartre viṣṇumāyāntakāriṇe
tryaṃbakāya tryakṣarāya śipiviṣṭāya mīḍhuṣe
mṛtyuñjayāya śarvāya sarvajñāya makhāraye
makheśāya vareṇyāya namaste vahnirūpiṇe
mahāghrāṇāya jihvāya prāṇāpānapravartine
triguṇāya triśūlāya guṇātītāya yogine
saṃsārāya pravāhāya mahāyantrapravartine
namaścandrāgnisūryāya muktivaicitryahetave
varadāyāvatārāya sarvakāraṇahetave
kapāline karālāya pataye puṇyakīrttaye
amoghāyāgninetrāya lakulīśāya śaṃbhave
bhiṣaktamāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine yogarūpiṇe
meghavāhāya devāya pārvatīpataye namaḥ
avyaktāya viśokāya sthirāya sthiradhanvine
sthāṇave kṛttivāsāya namaḥ pañcārthahetave
varadāyaikapādāya namaścandrārdhamauline
namaste 'dhvararājāya vayasāṃ pataye namaḥ
yogīśvarāya nityāya satyāya parameṣṭhine
sarvātmane namastubhyaṃ namaḥ sarveśvarāya te
ekadvitricatuḥpañcakṛtvas te 'stu namonamaḥ
daśakṛtvastu sāhasrakṛtvaste ca namonamaḥ
namo 'parimitaṃ kṛtvānantakṛtvo namonamaḥ
namonamo namo bhūyaḥ punarbhūyo namonamaḥ
sūta uvāca
nāmnāmaṣṭaśatenaivaṃ stutvāmṛtamayena tu
punastu prārthayāmāsa nṛsiṃhaḥ śarabheśvaram
yadā yadā mamājñānamatyahaṅkāradūṣitam
tadā tadāpanetavyaṃ tvayaiva parameśvara
evaṃ vijñāpayanprītaḥ śaṅkaraṃ narakesarī
nanvaśakto bhavān viṣṇo jīvitāntaṃ parājitaḥ
tadvaktraśeṣamātrāntaṃ kṛtvā sarvasya vigraham
śuktiśityaṃ tadā maṅgaṃ vīrabhadraḥ kṣaṇāttataḥ
devā ūcuḥ
atha brahmādayaḥ sarve vīrabhadra tvayā dṛśā
jīvitāḥ smo vayaṃ devāḥ parjanyeneva pādapāḥ
yasya bhīṣā dahatyagnir udeti ca raviḥ svayam
vāto vāti ca so 'si tvaṃ mṛtyurdhāvati pañcamaḥ
yadavyaktaṃ paraṃ vyoma kalātītaṃ sadāśivam
bhagavaṃstvāmeva bhavaṃ vadanti brahmavādinaḥ
ke vayameva dhātukye vedane parameśvaraḥ
na viddhi paramaṃ dhāma rūpalāvaṇyavarṇane
upasargeṣu sarveṣu trāyasvāsmān gaṇādhipa
ekādaśātman bhagavānvartate rūpavān haraḥ
īdṛśān te 'vatārāṇi dṛṣṭvā śiva bahūṃstamaḥ
kadācit saṃdihen nāsmāṃs tvaccintāstamayā tathā
guñjāgirivarataṭāmitarūpāṇi sarvaśaḥ
abhyasaṃhara gamyaṃ te na nītavyaṃ parāparā
dve tanū tava rudrasya vedajñā brāhmaṇā viduḥ
ghorāpyanyā śivāpyanyā te pratyekamanekadhā
ihāsmānpāhi bhagavan nityāhatamahābalaḥ
bhavatā hi jagatsarvaṃ vyāptaṃ svenaiva tejasā
brahmaviṣṇvindracandrādi vayaṃ ca pramukhāḥ surāḥ
surāsurāḥ samprasūtās tvattaḥ sarve maheśvara
brahmā ca indro viṣṇuś ca yamādyā na surāsurān
tato nigṛhya ca hariṃ siṃha ity upacetasam
yato bibharṣi sakalaṃ vibhajya tanumaṣṭadhā
ato 'smān pāhi bhagavan surān dānair abhīpsitaiḥ
uvāca tān surāndevo maharṣīṃś ca purātanān
yathā jale jalaṃ kṣiptaṃ kṣīraṃ kṣīre ghṛtaṃ ghṛte
eka eva tadā viṣṇuḥ śivalīno na cānyathā
eṣa eva nṛsiṃhātmā sadarpaś ca mahābalaḥ
jagatsaṃhārakāreṇa pravṛtto narakesarī
yājanīyo namastasmai madbhaktisiddhikāṅkṣibhiḥ
etāvaduktvā bhagavānvīrabhadro mahābalaḥ
apaśyan sarvabhūtānāṃ tatraivāntaradhīyata
nṛsiṃhakṛttivasanastadāprabhṛti śaṅkaraḥ
vaktraṃ tanmuṇḍamālāyāṃ nāyakatvena kalpitam
tato devā nirātaṅkāḥ kīrtayantaḥ kathāmimām
vismayotphullanayanā jagmuḥ sarve yathāgatam
ya idaṃ paramākhyānaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiḥ samanvitam
paṭhitvā śṛṇute caiva sarvaduḥkhavināśanam
dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam ārogyaṃ puṣṭivardhanam
sarvavighnapraśamanaṃ sarvavyādhivināśanam
apamṛtyupraśamanaṃ mahāśāntikaraṃ śubham
aricakrapraśamanaṃ sarvādhipravināśanam
tato duḥsvapnaśamanaṃ sarvabhūtanivāraṇam
viṣagrahakṣayakaraṃ putrapautrādivardhanam
yogasiddhipradaṃ samyak śivajñānaprakāśakam
śeṣalokasya sopānaṃ vāñchitārthaikasādhanam
viṣṇumāyānirasanaṃ devatāparamārthadam
vāñchāsiddhipradaṃ caiva ṛddhiprajñādisādhanam
idaṃ tu śarabhākāraṃ paraṃ rūpaṃ pinākinaḥ
prakāśitavyaṃ bhakteṣu cireṣūdyamiteṣu ca
taireva paṭhitavyaṃ ca śrotavyaṃ ca śivātmabhiḥ
śivotsaveṣu sarveṣu caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca
paṭhetpratiṣṭhākāleṣu śivasannidhikāraṇam
coravyāghrāhisiṃhāntakṛto rājabhayeṣu ca
atrānyotpātabhūkampadavāgnipāṃsuvṛṣṭiṣu
ulkāpāte mahāvāte vinā vṛṣṭyātivṛṣṭiṣu
atastatra paṭhedvidvāñchivabhakto dṛḍhavrataḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi stavaṃ sarvamanuttamam
sa rudratvaṃ samāsādya rudrasyānucaro bhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śarabhaprādurbhāvo nāma ṣaṇṇavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
jalandharaṃ jaṭāmauliḥ purā jambhārivikramam
kathaṃ jaghāna bhagavān bhaganetraharo haraḥ
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa suvrata
sūta uvāca
jalandhara iti khyāto jalamaṇḍalasaṃbhavaḥ
āsīdantakasaṃkāśastapasā labdhavikramaḥ
tena devāḥ sagandharvāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
nirjitāḥ samare sarve brahmā ca bhagavānajaḥ
jitvaiva devasaṃghātaṃ brahmāṇaṃ vai jalandharaḥ
jagāma devadeveśaṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvaharaṃ gurum
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ divārātram aviśramam
jalandhareśayostena nirjito madhusūdanaḥ
jalandharo'pi taṃ jitvā devadevaṃ janārdanam
provācedaṃ diteḥ putrān nyāyadhīrjetumīśvaram
sarve jitā mayā yuddhe śaṅkaro hyajito raṇe
taṃ jitvā sarvamīśānaṃ gaṇapair nandinā kṣaṇāt
ahameva bhavatvaṃ ca brahmatvaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā
vāsavatvaṃ ca yuṣmākaṃ dāsye dānavapuṅgavāḥ
jalandharavacaḥ śrutvā sarve te dānavādhamāḥ
jagarjuruccaiḥ pāpiṣṭhā mṛtyudarśanatatparāḥ
daityairetaistathānyaiś ca rathanāgaturaṅgamaiḥ
saṃnaddhaiḥ saha saṃnahya śarvaṃ prati yayau balī
bhavo'pi dṛṣṭvā daityendraṃ merukūṭamiva sthitam
avadhyatvam api śrutvā tathānyair bhaganetrahā
brahmaṇo vacanaṃ rakṣan rakṣako jagatāṃ prabhuḥ
sāṃbaḥ sanandī sagaṇaḥ provāca prahasanniva
kiṃ kṛtyamasureśāna yuddhenānena sāṃpratam
madbāṇairbhinnasarvāṅgo martumabhyudyate mudā
jalandharo'pi tadvākyaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam
sureśvaramuvācedaṃ suretarabaleśvaraḥ
vākyenālaṃ mahābāho devadeva vṛṣadhvaja
candrāṃśusannibhaiḥ śastrairhara yoddhumihāgataḥ
niśamyāsya vacaḥ śūlī pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā
mahāṃbhasi cakārāśu rathāṅgaṃ raudramāyudham
kṛtvārṇavāṃbhasi sitaṃ bhagavān rathāṅgaṃ smṛtvā jagattrayamanena hatāḥ surāś ca
dakṣāndhakāntakapuratrayayajñahartā lokatrayāntakakaraḥ prahasaṃtadāha
pādena nirmitaṃ daitya jalandhara mahārṇave
balavān yadi coddhartuṃ tiṣṭha yoddhuṃ na cānyathā
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā krodhenādīptalocanaḥ
pradahanniva netrābhyāṃ prāhālokya jagattrayam
jalandhara uvāca
gadāmuddhṛtya hatvā ca nandinaṃ tvāṃ ca śaṅkara
hatvā lokānsuraiḥ sārdhaṃ ḍuṇḍubhān garuḍo yathā
hantuṃ carācaraṃ sarvaṃ samartho'haṃ savāsavam
ko maheśvara madbāṇairacchedyo bhuvanatraye
bālabhāve ca bhagavān tapasaiva vinirjitaḥ
brahmā balī yauvane vai munayaḥ surapuṅgavaiḥ
dagdhaṃ kṣaṇena sakalaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
tapasā kiṃ tvayā rudra nirjito bhagavānapi
indrāgniyamavitteśavāyuvārīśvarādayaḥ
na sehire yathā nāgā gandhaṃ pakṣipateriva
na labdhvā divi bhūmau ca bāhavo mama śaṅkara
samastānparvatānprāpya gharṣitāś ca gaṇeśvara
girīndro mandaraḥ śrīmānnīlo meruḥ suśobhanaḥ
gharṣito bāhudaṇḍena kaṇḍūnodārtham āpatat
gaṅgā niruddhā bāhubhyāṃ līlārthaṃ himavadgirau
nārīṇāṃ mama bhṛtyaiś ca vajro baddho divaukasām
vaḍavāyā mukhaṃ bhagnaṃ gṛhītvā vai kareṇa tu
tatkṣaṇādeva sakalaṃ caikārṇavamabhūdidam
airāvatādayo nāgāḥ kṣiptāḥ sindhujalopari
saratho bhagavānindraḥ kṣiptaś ca śatayojanam
garuḍo'pi mayā baddho nāgapāśena viṣṇunā
urvaśyādyā mayā nītā nāryaḥ kārāgṛhāntaram
kathaṃcillabdhavān śakraḥ śacīmekāṃ praṇamya mām
māṃ na jānāsi daityendraṃ jalandharamumāpate
sūta uvāca
evamukto mahādevaḥ prādahadvai rathaṃ tadā
tasya netrāgnibhāgaikakalārdhārdhena cākulam
daityānāmatulabalairhayaiś ca nāgair daityendrās tripuraripor nirīkṣaṇena
nāgād vaiśasam anusaṃvṛtaś ca nāgairdeveśaṃ vacanamuvāca cālpabuddhiḥ
kiṃ kāryaṃ mama yudhi devadaityasaṃghairhantuṃ yatsakalamidaṃ kṣaṇātsamarthaḥ
yattasmādbhayamihanāsti yoddhum īśa vāñchaiṣā vipulatarā na saṃśayo'tra
tasmāttvaṃ mama madanāridakṣaśatro yajñāre tripuraripo mamaiva vīraiḥ
bhūtendrairharivadanena devasaṃghairyoddhuṃ te balamiha cāsti ceddhi tiṣṭha
ityuktvātha mahādevaṃ mahādevārinandanaḥ
na cacāla na sasmāra nihatānbāndhavānyudhi
durmadenāvinītātmā dorbhyāmāsphoṭya dorbalāt
sudarśanākhyaṃ yaccakraṃ tena hantuṃ samudyataḥ
durdhareṇa rathāṅgena kṛcchreṇāpi dvijottamāḥ
sthāpayāmāsa vai skandhe dvidhābhūtaś ca tena vai
kuliśena yathā chinno dvidhā girivaro dvijāḥ
papāta daityo balavānañjanādririvāparaḥ
tasya raktena raudreṇa sampūrṇam abhavatkṣaṇāt
tadraktamakhilaṃ rudraniyogānmāṃsameva ca
mahārauravamāsādya raktakuṇḍamabhūdaho
jalandharaṃ hataṃ dṛṣṭvā devagandharvapārṣadāḥ
siṃhanādaṃ mahatkṛtvā sādhu deveti cābruvan
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi jalandharavimardanam
śrāvayedvā yathānyāyaṃ gāṇapatyamavāpnuyāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge jalandharavadho nāma saptanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ devena vai sūta devadevānmaheśvarāt
sudarśanākhyaṃ vai labdhaṃ vaktumarhasi viṣṇunā
sūta uvāca
devānām asurendrāṇām abhavacca sudāruṇaḥ
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ vināśakaraṇo mahān
te devāḥ śaktimuśalaiḥ sāyakairnataparvabhiḥ
prabhidyamānāḥ kuntaiś ca dudruvurbhayavihvalāḥ
parājitāstadā devā devadeveśvaraṃ harim
praṇemustaṃ sureśānaṃ śokasaṃvignamānasāḥ
tān samīkṣyātha bhagavān devadeveśvaro hariḥ
praṇipatya sthitāndevānidaṃ vacanamabravīt
vatsāḥ kimiti vai devāś cyutālaṅkāravikramāḥ
samāgatāḥ sasaṃtāpā vaktumarhatha suvratāḥ
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā tathābhūtāḥ surottamāḥ
praṇamyāhuryathāvṛttaṃ devadevāya viṣṇave
bhagavandevadeveśa viṣṇo jiṣṇo janārdana
dānavaiḥ pīḍitāḥ sarve vayaṃ śaraṇamāgatāḥ
tvameva devadeveśa gatirnaḥ puruṣottama
tvameva paramātmā hi tvaṃ pitā jagatāmapi
tvameva bhartā hartā ca bhoktā dātā janārdana
hantumarhasi tasmāttvaṃ dānavāndānavārdana
daityāś ca vaiṣṇavairbrāhmai raudrairyāmyaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ
kauberaiścaiva saumyaiś ca nairṛtyairvāruṇairdṛḍhaiḥ
vāyavyaiś ca tathāgneyair aiśānair vārṣikaiḥ śubhaiḥ
saurai raudrais tathā bhīmaiḥ kampanair jṛmbhaṇair dṛḍhaiḥ
avadhyā varalābhātte sarve vārijalocana
sūryamaṇḍalasambhūtaṃ tvadīyaṃ cakram udyatam
kuṇṭhitaṃ hi dadhīcena cyāvanena jagadguro
daṇḍaṃ śārṅgaṃ tavāstraṃ ca labdhaṃ daityaiḥ prasādataḥ
purā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ tripurāriṇā
rathāṅgaṃ suśitaṃ ghoraṃ tena tān hantum arhasi
tasmāttena nihantavyā nānyaiḥ śastraśatairapi
tato niśamya teṣāṃ vai vacanaṃ vārijekṣaṇaḥ
vācaspatimukhānāha sa hariścakrabhṛt svayam
śrīviṣṇur uvāca
bhobho devā mahādevaṃ sarvair devaiḥ sanātanaiḥ
samprāpya sāṃprataṃ sarvaṃ kariṣyāmi divaukasām
devā jalandharaṃ hantuṃ nirmitaṃ hi purāriṇā
labdhvā rathāṅgaṃ tenaiva nihatya ca mahāsurān
sarvāndhundhumukhāndaityānaṣṭaṣaṣṭiśatān surān
sabāndhavānkṣaṇādeva yuṣmān saṃtārayāmyaham
sūta uvāca
evam uktvā suraśreṣṭhān suraśreṣṭhamanusmaran
suśreṣṭhastadā śreṣṭhaṃ pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram
liṅgaṃ sthāpya yathānyāyaṃ himavacchikhare śubhe
meruparvatasaṃkāśaṃ nirmitaṃ viśvakarmaṇā
tvaritākhyena rudreṇa raudreṇa ca janārdanaḥ
snāpya sampūjya gandhādyairjvālākāraṃ manoramam
tuṣṭāva ca tadā rudraṃ sampūjyāgnau praṇamya ca
devaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa bhavādyena yathākramam
pūjayāmāsa ca śivaṃ praṇavādyaṃ namo'ntakam
devaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa bhavādyena maheśvaram
pratināma sa padmena pūjayāmāsa śaṅkaram
agnau ca nāmabhir devaṃ bhavādyaiḥ samidādibhiḥ
svāhāntairvidhivaddhutvā pratyekamayutaṃ prabhum
tuṣṭāva ca punaḥ śaṃbhuṃ bhavādyairbhavamīśvaram
śrīviṣṇuruvāca
bhavaḥ śivo haro rudraḥ puruṣaḥ padmalocanaḥ
arthitavyaḥ sadācāraḥ sarvaśaṃbhurmaheśvaraḥ
īśvaraḥ sthāṇurīśānaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt
varīyān varado vandyaḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ
gaṅgādharaḥ śūladharaḥ parārthaikaprayojanaḥ
sarvajñaḥ sarvadevādigiridhanvā jaṭādharaḥ
candrāpīḍaścandramaulirvidvānviśvāmareśvaraḥ
vedāntasārasaṃdohaḥ kapālī nīlalohitaḥ
dhyānādhāroparicchedyo gaurībhartā gaṇeśvaraḥ
aṣṭamūrtirviśvamūrtistrivargaḥ svargasādhanaḥ
jñānagamyo dṛḍhaprajño devadevastrilocanaḥ
vāmadevo mahādevaḥ pāṇḍuḥ paridṛḍho dṛḍhaḥ
viśvarūpo virūpākṣo vāgīśaḥ śucirantaraḥ
sarvapraṇayasaṃvādī vṛṣāṅko vṛṣavāhanaḥ
īśaḥ pinākī khaṭvāṅgī citraveṣaścirantanaḥ
tamoharo mahāyogī goptā brahmāṅgahṛjjaṭī
kālakālaḥ kṛttivāsāḥ subhagaḥ praṇavātmakaḥ
unmattaveṣaś cakṣuṣyo durvāsāḥ smaraśāsanaḥ
dṛḍhāyudhaḥ skandaguruḥ parameṣṭhī parāyaṇaḥ
anādimadhyanidhano giriśo giribāndhavaḥ
kuberabandhuḥ śrīkaṇṭho lokavarṇottamottamaḥ
sāmānyadevaḥ kodaṇḍī nīlakaṇṭhaḥ paraśvadhī
viśālākṣo mṛgavyādhaḥ sureśaḥ sūryatāpanaḥ
dharmakarmākṣamaḥ kṣetraṃ bhagavān bhaganetrabhit
ugraḥ paśupatis tārkṣyaḥ priyabhaktaḥ priyaṃvadaḥ
dātā dayākaro dakṣaḥ kapardī kāmaśāsanaḥ
śmaśānanilayaḥ sūkṣmaḥ śmaśānastho maheśvaraḥ
lokakartā bhūtapatirmahākartā mahauṣadhī
uttaro gopatirgoptā jñānagamyaḥ purātanaḥ
nītiḥ sunītiḥ śuddhātmā somaḥ somarataḥ sukhī
somapo 'mṛtapaḥ somo mahānītirmahāmatiḥ
ajātaśatrurālokaḥ saṃbhāvyo havyavāhanaḥ
lokakāro vedakāraḥ sūtrakāraḥ sanātanaḥ
maharṣiḥ kapilācāryo viśvadīptistrilocanaḥ
pinākapāṇir bhūdevaḥ svastidaḥ svastikṛtsadā
tridhāmā saubhagaḥ śarvaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvagocaraḥ
brahmadhṛg viśvasṛk svargaḥ karṇikāraḥ priyaḥ kaviḥ
śākho viśākho gośākhaḥ śivo naikaḥ kratuḥ samaḥ
gaṅgāplavodako bhāvaḥ sakalaḥ sthapatiḥ sthiraḥ
vijitātmā vidheyātmā bhūtavāhanasārathiḥ
sagaṇo gaṇakāryaś ca sukīrtiś chinnasaṃśayaḥ
kāmadevaḥ kāmapālo bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaḥ
bhasmapriyo bhasmaśāyī kāmī kāntaḥ kṛtāgamaḥ
samāyukto nivṛttātmā dharmayuktaḥ sadāśivaḥ
caturmukhaścaturbāhur durāvāso durāsadaḥ
durgamo durlabho durgaḥ sarvāyudhaviśāradaḥ
adhyātmayoganilayaḥ sutantustantuvardhanaḥ
śubhāṅgo lokasāraṅgo jagadīśo 'mṛtāśanaḥ
bhasmaśuddhikaro merurojasvī śuddhavigrahaḥ
hiraṇyaretās taraṇir marīcir mahimālayaḥ
mahāhrado mahāgarbhaḥ siddhavṛndāravanditaḥ
vyāghracarmadharo vyālī mahābhūto mahānidhiḥ
amṛtāṅgo 'mṛtavapuḥ pañcayajñaḥ prabhañjanaḥ
pañcaviṃśatitattvajñaḥ pārijātaḥ parāvaraḥ
sulabhaḥ suvrataḥ śūro vāṅmayaikanidhirnidhiḥ
varṇāśramagururvarṇī śatrujicchatrutāpanaḥ
āśramaḥ kṣapaṇaḥ kṣāmo jñānavānacalācalaḥ
pramāṇabhūto durjñeyaḥ suparṇo vāyuvāhanaḥ
dhanurdharo dhanurvedo guṇarāśirguṇākaraḥ
anantadṛṣṭirānando daṇḍo damayitā damaḥ
abhivādyo mahācāryo viśvakarmā viśāradaḥ
vītarāgo vinītātmā tapasvī bhūtabhāvanaḥ
unmattaveṣaḥ pracchanno jitakāmo jitapriyaḥ
kalyāṇaprakṛtiḥ kalpaḥ sarvalokaprajāpatiḥ
tapasvī tārako dhīmān pradhānaprabhur avyayaḥ
lokapālo 'ntarhitātmā kalpādiḥ kamalekṣaṇaḥ
vedaśāstrārthatattvajño niyamo niyamāśrayaḥ
candraḥ sūryaḥ śaniḥ keturvirāmo vidrumacchaviḥ
bhaktigamyaḥ paraṃ brahma mṛgabāṇārpaṇo 'naghaḥ
adrirājālayaḥ kāntaḥ paramātmā jagadguruḥ
sarvakarmācalastvaṣṭā maṅgalyo maṅgalāvṛtaḥ
mahātapā dīrghatapāḥ sthaviṣṭhaḥ sthaviro dhruvaḥ
ahaḥ saṃvatsaro vyāptiḥ pramāṇaṃ paramaṃ tapaḥ
saṃvatsarakaro mantraḥ pratyayaḥ sarvadarśanaḥ
ajaḥ sarveśvaraḥ snigdho mahāretā mahābalaḥ
yogī yogyo mahāretāḥ siddhaḥ sarvādir agnidaḥ
vasurvasumanāḥ satyaḥ sarvapāpaharo haraḥ
amṛtaḥ śāśvataḥ śānto bāṇahastaḥ pratāpavān
kamaṇḍaludharo dhanvī vedāṅgo vedavinmuniḥ
bhrājiṣṇur bhojanaṃ bhoktā lokanetā durādharaḥ
atīndriyo mahāmāyaḥ sarvāvāsaścatuṣpathaḥ
kālayogī mahānādo mahotsāho mahābalaḥ
mahābuddhir mahāvīryo bhūtacārī purandaraḥ
niśācaraḥ pretacārī mahāśaktir mahādyutiḥ
anirdeśyavapuḥ śrīmān sarvahāryamito gatiḥ
bahuśruto bahumayo niyatātmā bhavodbhavaḥ
ojastejo dyutikaro nartakaḥ sarvakāmakaḥ
nṛtyapriyo nṛtyanṛtyaḥ prakāśātmā pratāpanaḥ
buddhaspaṣṭākṣaro mantraḥ sanmānaḥ sārasaṃplavaḥ
yugādikṛd yugāvarto gaṃbhīro vṛṣavāhanaḥ
iṣṭo viśiṣṭaḥ śiṣṭeṣṭaḥ śarabhaḥ śarabho dhanuḥ
apāṃ nidhiradhiṣṭhānaṃ vijayo jayakālavit
pratiṣṭhitaḥ pramāṇajño hiraṇyakavaco hariḥ
virocanaḥ suragaṇo vidyeśo vibudhāśrayaḥ
bālarūpo balonmāthī vivarto gahano guruḥ
karaṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ kartā sarvabandhavimocanaḥ
vidvattamo vītabhayo viśvabhartā niśākaraḥ
vyavasāyo vyavasthānaḥ sthānado jagadādijaḥ
dundubho lalito viśvo bhavātmātmani saṃsthitaḥ
vīreśvaro vīrabhadro vīrahā vīrabhṛd virāṭ
vīracūḍāmaṇirvettā tīvranādo nadīdharaḥ
ājñādharastriśūlī ca śipiviṣṭaḥ śivālayaḥ
vālakhilyo mahācāpastigmāṃśur nidhir avyayaḥ
abhirāmaḥ suśaraṇaḥ subrahmaṇyaḥ sudhāpatiḥ
maghavānkauśiko gomān viśrāmaḥ sarvaśāsanaḥ
lalāṭākṣo viśvadehaḥ sāraḥ saṃsāracakrabhṛt
amoghadaṇḍī madhyastho hiraṇyo brahmavarcasī
paramārthaḥ paramayaḥ śambaro vyāghrako 'nalaḥ
rucir vararucir vandyo vācaspatiraharpatiḥ
ravirvirocanaḥ skandhaḥ śāstā vaivasvato janaḥ
yuktirunnatakīrtiś ca śāntarāgaḥ parājayaḥ
kailāsapatikāmāriḥ savitā ravilocanaḥ
vidvattamo vītabhayo viśvahartā nivāritaḥ
nityo niyatakalyāṇaḥ puṇyaśravaṇakīrtanaḥ
dūraśravā viśvasaho dhyeyo duḥsvapnanāśanaḥ
uttārako duṣkṛtihā durdharṣo duḥsaho 'bhayaḥ
anādirbhūrbhuvolakṣmīḥ kirīṭī tridaśādhipaḥ
viśvagoptā viśvabhartā sudhīro rucirāṅgadaḥ
janano janajanmādiḥ prītimānnītimānnayaḥ
viśiṣṭaḥ kāśyapo bhānurbhīmo bhīmaparākramaḥ
praṇavaḥ saptadhācāro mahākāyo mahādhanuḥ
janmādhipo mahādevaḥ sakalāgamapāragaḥ
tattvātattvavivekātmā vibhūṣṇur bhūtibhūṣaṇaḥ
ṛṣirbrāhmaṇavijjiṣṇurjanmamṛtyujarātigaḥ
yajño yajñapatiryajvā yajñānto 'moghavikramaḥ
mahendro durbharaḥ senī yajñāṅgo yajñavāhanaḥ
pañcabrahmasamutpattirviśveśo vimalodayaḥ
ātmayonir anādyantaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatsaptalokadhṛk
gāyatrīvallabhaḥ prāṃśurviśvāvāsaḥ prabhākaraḥ
śiśurgirirataḥ samrāṭsuṣeṇaḥ suraśatruhā
amogho 'riṣṭamathano mukundo vigatajvaraḥ
svayaṃjyotir anujyotir ātmajyotir acañcalaḥ
piṅgalaḥ kapilaśmaśruḥ śāstranetras trayītanuḥ
jñānaskandho mahājñānī nirutpattir upaplavaḥ
bhago vivasvānādityo yogācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ
udārakīrtir udyogī sadyogī sadasanmayaḥ
nakṣatramālī rākeśaḥ sādhiṣṭhānaḥ ṣaḍāśrayaḥ
pavitrapāṇiḥ pāpārirmaṇipūro manogatiḥ
hṛtpuṇḍarīkamāsīnaḥ śuklaḥ śānto vṛṣākapiḥ
viṣṇurgrahapatiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ samartho 'narthanāśanaḥ
adharmaśatrurakṣayyaḥ puruhūtaḥ puruṣṭutaḥ
brahmagarbho bṛhadgarbho dharmadhenurdhanāgamaḥ
jagaddhitaiṣī sugataḥ kumāraḥ kuśalāgamaḥ
hiraṇyavarṇo jyotiṣmān nānābhūtadharo dhvaniḥ
arogo niyamādhyakṣo viśvāmitro dvijottamaḥ
bṛhajjyotiḥ sudhāmā ca mahājyotiranuttamaḥ
mātāmaho mātariśvā nabhasvān nāgahāradhṛk
pulastyaḥ pulaho 'gastyo jātūkarṇyaḥ parāśaraḥ
nirāvaraṇadharmajño viriñco viṣṭaraśravāḥ
ātmabhūr aniruddho 'trijñānamūrtir mahāyaśāḥ
lokacūḍāmaṇirvīraḥ caṇḍasatyaparākramaḥ
vyālakalpo mahākalpo mahāvṛkṣaḥ kalādharaḥ
alaṃkariṣṇus tvacalo rociṣṇurvikramottamaḥ
āśuśabdapatirvegī plavanaḥ śikhisārathiḥ
asaṃsṛṣṭo 'tithiḥ śakraḥ pramāthī pāpanāśanaḥ
vasuśravāḥ kavyavāhaḥ pratapto viśvabhojanaḥ
jaryo jarādhiśamano lohitaś ca tanūnapāt
pṛṣadaśvo nabhoyoniḥ supratīkas tamisrahā
nidāghastapano meghaḥ pakṣaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ
mukhānilaḥ suniṣpannaḥ surabhiḥ śiśirātmakaḥ
vasaṃto mādhavo grīṣmo nabhasyo bījavāhanaḥ
aṅgirā munirātreyo vimalo viśvavāhanaḥ
pāvanaḥ purujicchakras trividyo naravāhanaḥ
mano buddhirahaṅkāraḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetrapālakaḥ
tejonidhir jñānanidhir vipāko vighnakārakaḥ
adharo 'nuttaro jñeyo jyeṣṭho niḥśreyasālayaḥ
śailo nagastanurdeho dānavārirarindamaḥ
cārudhīr janakaścāruviśalyo lokaśalyakṛt
caturvedaścaturbhāvaścaturaścaturapriyaḥ
āmnāyo'tha samāmnāyastīrthadevaśivālayaḥ
bahurūpo mahārūpaḥ sarvarūpaś carācaraḥ
nyāyanirvāhako nyāyo nyāyagamyo nirañjanaḥ
sahasramūrdhā devendraḥ sarvaśastraprabhañjanaḥ
muṇḍo virūpo vikṛto daṇḍī dānto guṇottamaḥ
piṅgalākṣo'tha haryakṣo nīlagrīvo nirāmayaḥ
sahasrabāhuḥ sarveśaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarvalokabhṛt
padmāsanaḥ paraṃ jyotiḥ parāvaraṃ paraṃ phalam
padmagarbho mahāgarbho viśvagarbho vicakṣaṇaḥ
parāvarajño bījeśaḥ sumukhaḥ sumahāsvanaḥ
devāsuragururdevo devāsuranamaskṛtaḥ
devāsuramahāmātro devāsuramahāśrayaḥ
devādidevo devarṣidevāsuravarapradaḥ
devāsureśvaro divyo devāsuramaheśvaraḥ
sarvadevamayo 'cintyo devatātmātmasaṃbhavaḥ
īḍyo 'nīśaḥ suravyāghro devasiṃho divākaraḥ
vibudhāgravaraśreṣṭhaḥ sarvadevottamottamaḥ
śivajñānarataḥ śrīmān śikhiśrīparvatapriyaḥ
jayastaṃbho viśiṣṭambho narasiṃhanipātanaḥ
brahmacārī lokacārī dharmacārī dhanādhipaḥ
nandī nandīśvaro nagno nagnavratadharaḥ śuciḥ
liṅgādhyakṣaḥ surādhyakṣo yugādhyakṣo yugāvahaḥ
svavaśaḥ savaśaḥ svargaḥ svaraḥ svaramayasvanaḥ
bījādhyakṣo bījakartā dhanakṛd dharmavardhanaḥ
daṃbho 'dambho mahādaṃbhaḥ sarvabhūtamaheśvaraḥ
śmaśānanilayastiṣyaḥ seturapratimākṛtiḥ
lokottarasphuṭālokastryaṃbako nāgabhūṣaṇaḥ
andhakārirmakhadveṣī viṣṇukandharapātanaḥ
vītadoṣo 'kṣayaguṇo dakṣāriḥ pūṣadantahṛt
dhūrjaṭiḥ khaṇḍaparaśuḥ sakalo niṣkalo 'naghaḥ
ādhāraḥ sakalādhāraḥ pāṇḍurābho mṛḍo naṭaḥ
pūrṇaḥ pūrayitā puṇyaḥ sukumāraḥ sulocanaḥ
sāmageyaḥ priyakaraḥ puṇyakīrtiranāmayaḥ
manojavastīrthakaro jaṭilo jīviteśvaraḥ
jīvitāntakaro nityo vasuretā vasupriyaḥ
sadgatiḥ satkṛtiḥ saktaḥ kālakaṇṭhaḥ kalādharaḥ
mānī mānyo mahākālaḥ sadbhūtiḥ satparāyaṇaḥ
candrasaṃjīvanaḥ śāstā lokagūḍho 'marādhipaḥ
lokabandhurlokanāthaḥ kṛtajñaḥ kṛtibhūṣaṇaḥ
anapāyyakṣaraḥ kāntaḥ sarvaśāstrabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
tejomayo dyutidharo lokamāyo 'graṇīr aṇuḥ
śucismitaḥ prasannātmā durjayo duratikramaḥ
jyotirmayo nirākāro jagannātho jaleśvaraḥ
tumbavīṇī mahākāyo viśokaḥ śokanāśanaḥ
trilokātmā trilokeśaḥ śuddhaḥ śuddhī rathākṣajaḥ
avyaktalakṣaṇo vyakto vyaktāvyakto viśāṃpatiḥ
varaśīlo varatulo māno mānadhano mayaḥ
brahmā viṣṇuḥ prajāpālo haṃso haṃsagatiryamaḥ
vedhā dhātā vidhātā ca attā hartā caturmukhaḥ
kailāsaśikharāvāsī sarvāvāsī satāṃ gatiḥ
hiraṇyagarbho hariṇaḥ puruṣaḥ pūrvajaḥ pitā
bhūtālayo bhūtapatirbhūtido bhuvaneśvaraḥ
saṃyogī yogavidbrahma brahmaṇyo brāhmaṇapriyaḥ
devapriyo devanātho devajño devacintakaḥ
viṣamākṣaḥ kalādhyakṣo vṛṣāṅko vṛṣavardhanaḥ
nirmado nirahaṅkāro nirmoho nirupadravaḥ
darpahā darpito dṛptaḥ sarvartuparivartakaḥ
saptajihvaḥ sahasrārciḥ snigdhaḥ prakṛtidakṣiṇaḥ
bhūtabhavyabhavannāthaḥ prabhavo bhrāntināśanaḥ
artho'nartho mahākośaḥ parakāryaikapaṇḍitaḥ
niṣkaṇṭakaḥ kṛtānando nirvyājo vyājamardanaḥ
sattvavān sāttvikaḥ satyakīrtistambhakṛtāgamaḥ
akaṃpito guṇagrāhī naikātmā naikakarmakṛt
suprītaḥ sumukhaḥ sūkṣmaḥ sukaro dakṣiṇo 'nalaḥ
skandhaḥ skandhadharo dhuryaḥ prakaṭaḥ prītivardhanaḥ
aparājitaḥ sarvasaho vidagdhaḥ sarvavāhanaḥ
adhṛtaḥ svadhṛtaḥ sādhyaḥ pūrvamūrtiryaśodharaḥ
varāhaśṛṅgadhṛg vāyur balavān ekanāyakaḥ
śrutiprakāśaḥ śrutimān ekabandhur anekadhṛk
śrīvallabhaśivārambhaḥ śāntabhadraḥ samañjasaḥ
bhūśayo bhūtikṛdbhūtirbhūṣaṇo bhūtavāhanaḥ
akāyo bhaktakāyasthaḥ kālajñānī kalāvapuḥ
satyavratamahātyāgī niṣṭhāśāntiparāyaṇaḥ
parārthavṛttir varado viviktaḥ śrutisāgaraḥ
anirviṇṇo guṇagrāhī kalaṅkāṅkaḥ kalaṅkahā
svabhāvarudro madhyasthaḥ śatrughno madhyanāśakaḥ
śikhaṇḍī kavacī śūlī caṇḍī muṇḍī ca kuṇḍalī
mekhalī kavacī khaḍgī māyī saṃsārasārathiḥ
amṛtyuḥ sarvadṛk siṃhas tejorāśir mahāmaṇiḥ
asaṃkhyeyo 'prameyātmā vīryavān kāryakovidaḥ
vedyo vedārthavidgoptā sarvācāro munīśvaraḥ
anuttamo durādharṣo madhuraḥ priyadarśanaḥ
sureśaḥ śaraṇaṃ sarvaḥ śabdabrahma satāṃ gatiḥ
kālabhakṣaḥ kalaṅkāriḥ kaṅkaṇīkṛtavāsukiḥ
maheṣvāso mahībhartā niṣkalaṅko viśṛṅkhalaḥ
dyumaṇis taraṇir dhanyaḥ siddhidaḥ siddhisādhanaḥ
nivṛttaḥ saṃvṛtaḥ śilpo vyūḍhorasko mahābhujaḥ
ekajyotir nirātaṅko naro nārāyaṇapriyaḥ
nirlepo niṣprapañcātmā nirvyagro vyagranāśanaḥ
stavyastavapriyaḥ stotā vyāsamūrtir anākulaḥ
niravadyapadopāyo vidyārāśiravikramaḥ
praśāntabuddhirakṣudraḥ kṣudrahā nityasundaraḥ
dhairyāgryadhuryo dhātrīśaḥ śākalyaḥ śarvarīpatiḥ
paramārthagurur dṛṣṭir gurur āśritavatsalaḥ
raso rasajñaḥ sarvajñaḥ sarvasattvāvalaṃbanaḥ
sūta uvāca
evaṃ nāmnāṃ sahasreṇa tuṣṭāva vṛṣabhadhvajam
snāpayāmāsa ca vibhuḥ pūjayāmāsa paṅkajaiḥ
parīkṣārthaṃ hareḥ pūjākamaleṣu maheśvaraḥ
gopayāmāsa kamalaṃ tadaikaṃ bhuvaneśvaraḥ
hṛtapuṣpo haristatra kimidaṃ tvabhyacintayat
jñātvā svanetramuddhṛtya sarvasattvāvalambanam
pūjayāmāsa bhāvena nāmnā tena jagadgurum
tatastatra vibhurdṛṣṭvā tathābhūtaṃ haro harim
tasmādavatatārāśu maṇḍalātpāvakasya ca
koṭibhāskarasaṃkāśaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitam
jvālāmālāvṛtaṃ divyaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ bhayaṅkaram
śūlaṭaṅkagadācakrakuntapāśadharaṃ haram
varādabhayahastaṃ ca dvīpicarmottarīyakam
itthaṃbhūtaṃ tadā dṛṣṭvā bhavaṃ bhasmavibhūṣitam
hṛṣṭo namaścakārāśu devadevaṃ janārdanaḥ
dudruvustaṃ parikramya sendrā devāstrilocanam
cacāla brahmabhuvanaṃ cakampe ca vasuṃdharā
dadāha tejastacchaṃbhoḥ prāntaṃ vai śatayojanam
adhastāccordhvataścaiva hāhetyakṛta bhūtale
tadā prāha mahādevaḥ prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ
samprekṣya praṇayādviṣṇuṃ kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ sthitam
jñātaṃ mayedamadhunā devakāryaṃ janārdana
sudarśanākhyaṃ cakraṃ ca dadāmi tava śobhanam
yadrūpaṃ bhavatā dṛṣṭaṃ sarvalokabhayaṃkaram
hitāya tava yatnena tava bhāvāya suvrata
śāntaṃ raṇājire viṣṇo devānāṃ duḥkhasādhanam
śāntasya cāstraṃ śāntaḥ syācchāntenāstreṇa kiṃ phalam
śāntasya samare cāstraṃ śāntireva tapasvinām
yoddhuḥ śāntyā balacchedaḥ parasya balavṛddhidaḥ
devairaśāntairyadrūpaṃ madīyaṃ bhāvayāvyayam
kimāyudhena kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana
kṣamā yudhi na kāryaṃ vai yoddhuṃ devārisūdana
anāgate vyatīte ca daurbalye svajanotkare
akālike tvadharme ca anarthe vārisūdana
evamuktvā dadau cakraṃ sūryāyutasamaprabham
netraṃ ca netā jagatāṃ prabhurvai padmasannibham
tadāprabhṛti taṃ prāhuḥ padmākṣamiti suvratam
dattvainaṃ nayanaṃ cakraṃ viṣṇave nīlalohitaḥ
pasparśa ca karābhyāṃ vai suśubhābhyāmuvāca ha
varado 'haṃ varaśreṣṭha varānvaraya cepsitān
bhaktyā vaśīkṛto nūnaṃ tvayāhaṃ puruṣottama
ityukto devadevena devadevaṃ praṇamya tam
tvayi bhaktirmahādeva prasīda varamuttamam
nānyamicchāmi bhaktānāmārtayo nāsti yatprabho
tacchrutvā vacanaṃ tasya dayāvān sutarāṃ bhavaḥ
pasparśa ca dadau tasmai śraddhāṃ śītāṃśubhūṣaṇaḥ
prāha caivaṃ mahādevaḥ paramātmānamacyutam
mayi bhaktaś ca vandyaś ca pūjyaścaiva surāsuraiḥ
bhaviṣyasi na saṃdeho matprasādātsurottama
yadā satī dakṣaputrī vinindyaiva sulocanā
mātaraṃ pitaraṃ dakṣaṃ bhaviṣyati sureśvarī
divyā haimavatī viṣṇo tadā tvamapi suvrata
bhaginīṃ tava kalyāṇīṃ devīṃ haimavatīmumām
niyogād brahmaṇaḥ sādhvīṃ pradāsyasi mamaiva tām
matsaṃbandhī ca lokānāṃ madhye pūjyo bhaviṣyasi
māṃ divyena ca bhāvena tadāprabhṛti śaṅkaram
drakṣyase ca prasannena mitrabhūtamivātmanā
ityuktvāntardadhe rudro bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
janārdano'pi bhagavān devānāmapi saṃnidhau
ayācata mahādevaṃ brahmāṇaṃ munibhiḥ samam
mayā proktaṃ stavaṃ divyaṃ padmayone suśobhanam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
pratināmni hiraṇyasya tat tasya phalam āpnuyāt
aśvamedhasahasreṇa phalaṃ bhavati tasya vai
ghṛtādyaiḥ snāpayedrudraṃ sthālyā vai kalaśaiḥ śubhaiḥ
nāmnāṃ sahasreṇānena śraddhayā śivamīśvaram
so'pi yajñasahasrasya phalaṃ labdhvāsureśvaraiḥ
pūjyo bhavati rudrasya prītirbhavati tasya vai
tathāstviti tathā prāha padmayonerjanārdanam
jagmatuḥ praṇipatyainaṃ devadevaṃ jagadgurum
tasmānnāmnāṃ sahasreṇa pūjayed anagho dvijāḥ
japennāmnāṃ sahasraṃ ca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge sahasranāmabhiḥ pūjanād viṣṇucakralābho nāmāṣṭanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
saṃbhavaḥ sūcito devyāstvayā sūta mahāmate
savistaraṃ vadasvādya satītve ca yathātatham
menājatvaṃ mahādevyā dakṣayajñavimardanam
viṣṇunā ca kathaṃ dattā devadevāya śaṃbhave
kalyāṇaṃ vā kathaṃ tasya vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
teṣāṃ tadvacanaṃ śrutvā sūtaḥ paurāṇikottamaḥ
saṃbhavaṃ ca mahādevyāḥ prāha teṣāṃ mahātmanām
sūta uvāca
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ daṇḍine tat suvistaram
yuṣmābhir vai kumārāya tena vyāsāya dhīmate
tasmādahamupaśrutya pravadāmi suvistaram
vacanādvo mahābhāgāḥ praṇamyomāṃ tathā bhavam
sā bhagākhyā jagaddhātrī liṅgamūrtestrivedikā
liṅgastu bhagavāndvābhyāṃ jagatsṛṣṭirdvijottamāḥ
liṅgamūrtiḥ śivo jyotistamasaścopari sthitaḥ
liṅgavedisamāyogādardhanārīśvarobhavat
brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe devamagre putraṃ caturmukham
prāhiṇoti sma tasyaiva jñānaṃ jñānamayo haraḥ
viśvādhiko 'sau bhagavānardhanārīśvaro vibhuḥ
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ taṃ devo jāyamānamapaśyata
so'pi rudraṃ mahādevaṃ brahmāpaśyata śaṅkaram
taṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃsthitaṃ devamardhanārīśvaraṃ prabhum
tuṣṭāva vāgbhir iṣṭābhir varadaṃ vārijodbhavaḥ
vibhajasveti viśveśaṃ viśvātmānamajo vibhuḥ
sasarja devīṃ vāmāṅgātpatnīṃ caivātmanaḥ samām
śraddhā hyasya śubhā patnī tataḥ puṃsaḥ purātanī
saivājñayā vibhordevī dakṣaputrī babhūva ha
satīsaṃjñā tadā sā vai rudramevāśritā patim
dakṣaṃ vinindya kālena devī mainā hyabhūtpunaḥ
nāradasyaiva dakṣo'pi śāpādevaṃ vinindya ca
avajñādurmado dakṣo devadevamumāpatim
anādṛtya kṛtiṃ jñātvā satī dakṣeṇa tatkṣaṇāt
bhasmīkṛtvātmano dehaṃ yogamārgeṇa sā punaḥ
babhūva pārvatī devī tapasā ca gireḥ prabhoḥ
jñātvaitadbhagavān bhargo dadāha ruṣitaḥ prabhuḥ
dakṣasya vipulaṃ yajñaṃ cyāvaner vacanādapi
cyavanasya suto dhīmān dadhīca iti viśrutaḥ
vijitya viṣṇuṃ samare prasādāt tryaṃbakasya ca
viṣṇunā lokapālāṃś ca śaśāpa ca munīśvaraḥ
rudrasya krodhajenaiva vahninā haviṣā surāḥ
vināśo vai kṣaṇādeva māyayā śaṅkarasya vai
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devīsaṃbhavo nāma navanavatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vijitya viṣṇunā sārdhaṃ bhagavānparameśvaraḥ
sarvāndadhīcavacanātkathaṃ bheje maheśvaraḥ
sūta uvāca
dakṣayajñe suvipule devān viṣṇupurogamān
dadāha bhagavān rudraḥ sarvān munigaṇān api
bhadro nāma gaṇastena preṣitaḥ parameṣṭhinā
viprayogena devyā vai duḥsahenaiva suvratāḥ
so'sṛjad vīrabhadraś ca gaṇeśānromajāñchubhān
gaṇeśvaraiḥ samāruhya rathaṃ bhadraḥ pratāpavān
gantuṃ cakre matiṃ yasya sārathirbhagavānajaḥ
gaṇeśvarāś ca te sarve vividhāyudhapāṇayaḥ
vimānairviśvato bhadraistamanvayuratho surāḥ
himavacchikhare ramye hemaśṛṅge suśobhane
yajñavāṭas tathā tasya gaṅgādvārasamīpataḥ
taddeśe caiva vikhyātaṃ śubhaṃ kanakhalaṃ dvijāḥ
dagdhuṃ vai preṣitaścāsau bhagavān parameṣṭhinā
tadotpāto babhūvātha lokānāṃ bhayaśaṃsanaḥ
parvatāś ca vyaśīryanta pracakampe vasuṃdharā
marutaś cāpy aghūrṇanta cukṣubhe makarālayaḥ
agnayo naiva dīpyanti na ca dīpyati bhāskaraḥ
grahāś ca na prakāśyante na devā na ca dānavāḥ
tataḥ kṣaṇāt praviśyaiva yajñavāṭaṃ mahātmanaḥ
romajaiḥ sahito bhadraḥ kālāgnirivacāparaḥ
uvāca bhadro bhagavān dakṣaṃ cāmitatejasam
saṃparkādeva dakṣādya munīndevān pinākinā
dagdhuṃ saṃpreṣitaś cāhaṃ bhavantaṃ samunīśvaraiḥ
ityuktvā yajñaśālāṃ tāṃ dadāha gaṇapuṅgavaḥ
gaṇeśvarāś ca saṃkruddhā yūpānutpāṭya cikṣipuḥ
prastotrā saha hotrā ca dagdhaṃ caiva gaṇeśvaraiḥ
gṛhītvā gaṇapāḥ sarvān gaṅgāsrotasi cikṣipuḥ
vīrabhadro mahātejāḥ śakrasyodyacchataḥ karam
vyaṣṭambhayad adīnātmā tathānyeṣāṃ divaukasām
bhagasya netre cotpāṭya karajāgreṇa līlayā
nihatya muṣṭinā dantān pūṣṇaścaivaṃ nyapātayat
tathā candramasaṃ devaṃ pādāṅguṣṭhena līlayā
gharṣayāmāsa bhagavān vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān
cicheda ca śirastasya śakrasya bhagavānprabhoḥ
vahnerhastadvayaṃ chittvā jihvāmutpāṭya līlayā
jaghāna mūrdhni pādena vīrabhadro mahābalaḥ
yamasya daṇḍaṃ bhagavān pracicheda svayaṃ prabhuḥ
jaghāna devamīśānaṃ triśūlena mahābalam
trayastriṃśatsurānevaṃ vinihatyāprayatnataḥ
trayaś ca triśataṃ teṣāṃ trisāhasraṃ ca līlayā
trayaṃ caiva surendrāṇāṃ jaghāna ca munīśvarān
anyāṃś ca devān devo'sau sarvānyuddhāya saṃsthitān
jaghāna bhagavān rudraḥ khaḍgamuṣṭyādisāyakaiḥ
atha viṣṇurmahātejāś cakram udyamya mūrchitaḥ
yuyodha bhagavāṃstena rudreṇa saha mādhavaḥ
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam
viṣṇoryogabalāttasya divyadehāḥ sudāruṇāḥ
śaṅkhacakragadāhastā asaṃkhyātāś ca jajñire
tānsarvānapi devo'sau nārāyaṇasamaprabhān
nihatya gadayā viṣṇuṃ tāḍayāmāsa mūrdhani
tataścorasi taṃ devaṃ līlayaiva raṇājire
papāta ca tadā bhūmau visaṃjñaḥ puruṣottamaḥ
punarutthāya taṃ hantuṃ cakramudyamya sa prabhuḥ
krodharaktekṣaṇaḥ śrīmān atiṣṭhat puruṣarṣabhaḥ
tasya cakraṃ ca yadraudraṃ kālādityasamaprabham
vyaṣṭambhayad adīnātmā karasthaṃ na cacāla saḥ
atiṣṭhat stambhitastena śṛṅgavāniva niścalaḥ
tribhiś ca dharṣitaṃ śārṅgaṃ tridhābhūtaṃ prabhostadā
śārṅgakoṭiprasaṅgād vai cicheda ca śiraḥ prabhoḥ
chinnaṃ ca nipapātāsu śirastasya rasātale
vāyunā preritaṃ caiva prāṇajena pinākinā
praviveśa tadā caiva tadīyāhavanīyakam
tat pratidhvastakalaśaṃ bhagnayūpaṃ satoraṇam
pradīpitamahāśālaṃ dṛṣṭvā yajño'pi dudruve
taṃ tadā mṛgarūpeṇa dhāvantaṃ gaganaṃ prati
vīrabhadraḥ samādhāya viśiraskamathākarot
tataḥ prajāpatiṃ dharmaṃ kaśyapaṃ ca jagadgurum
ariṣṭaneminaṃ vīro bahuputraṃ munīśvaram
munim aṅgirasaṃ caiva kṛṣṇāśvaṃ ca mahābalaḥ
jaghāna mūrdhni pādena dakṣaṃ caiva yaśasvinam
cicheda ca śirastasya dadāhāgnau dvijottamāḥ
sarasvatyāś ca nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca
nikṛtya karajāgreṇa vīrabhadraḥ pratāpavān
tasthau śriyā vṛto madhye pretasthāne yathā bhavaḥ
etasminneva kāle tu bhagavānpadmasaṃbhavaḥ
bhadramāha mahātejāḥ prārthayanpraṇataḥ prabhuḥ
alaṃ krodhena vai bhadra naṣṭāścaiva divaukasaḥ
prasīda kṣamyatāṃ sarvaṃ romajaiḥ saha suvrata
so'pi bhadraḥ prabhāveṇa brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
śamaṃ jagāma śanakaiḥ śāntastasthau tadājñayā
devo 'pi tatra bhagavān antarikṣe vṛṣadhvajaḥ
sagaṇaḥ sarvadaḥ śarvaḥ sarvalokamaheśvaraḥ
prārthitaścaiva devena brahmaṇā bhagavān bhavaḥ
hatānāṃ ca tadā teṣāṃ pradadau pūrvavattanum
indrasya ca śirastasya viṣṇoścaiva mahātmanaḥ
dakṣasya ca munīndrasya tathānyeṣāṃ maheśvaraḥ
vāgīśyāścaiva nāsāgraṃ devamātustathaiva ca
naṣṭānāṃ jīvitaṃ caiva varāṇi vividhāni ca
dakṣasya dhvastavaktrasya śirasā bhagavānprabhuḥ
kalpayāmāsa vai vaktraṃ līlayā ca mahān bhavaḥ
dakṣo'pi labdhasaṃjñaś ca samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ
tuṣṭāva devadeveśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ vṛṣabhadhvajam
stutastena mahātejāḥ pradāya vividhānvarān
gāṇapatyaṃ dadau tasmai dakṣāyākliṣṭakarmaṇe
devāś ca sarve deveśaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ parameśvaram
nārāyaṇaś ca bhagavān tuṣṭāva ca kṛtāñjaliḥ
brahmā ca munayaḥ sarve pṛthakpṛthagajodbhavam
tuṣṭuvur devadeveśaṃ nīlakaṇṭhaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
tān devān anugṛhyaiva bhavo 'pyantaradhīyata
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivakṛddakṣayajñavidhvaṃsano nāma śatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ himavataḥ putrī babhūvāṃbā satī śubhā
kathaṃ vā devadeveśamavāpa patimīśvaram
sūta uvāca
sā menātanum āśritya svecchayaiva varāṅganā
tadā haimavatī jajñe tapasā ca dvijottamāḥ
jātakarmādikāḥ sarvāścakāra ca girīśvaraḥ
dvādaśe ca tadā varṣe pūrṇe haimavatī śubhā
tapastepe tayā sārdhamanujā ca śubhānanā
anyā ca devī hyanujā sarvaloke namaskṛtā
ṛṣayaś ca tadā sarve sarvalokamaheśvarīm
tuṣṭuvus tapasā devīṃ samāvṛtya samantataḥ
jyeṣṭhā hyaparṇā hyanujā caikaparṇā śubhānanā
tṛtīyā ca varārohā tathā caivaikapāṭalā
tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvaraḥ
vaśīkṛto mahādevaḥ sarvabhūtapatirbhavaḥ
etasminneva kāle tu tārako nāma dānavaḥ
tārātmajo mahātejā babhūva ditinandanaḥ
tasya putrāstrayaścāpi tārakākṣo mahāsuraḥ
vidyunmālī ca bhagavān kamalākṣaś ca vīryavān
pitāmahas tathā caiṣāṃ tāro nāma mahābalaḥ
tapasā labdhavīryaś ca prasādādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhoḥ
so'pi tāro mahātejāstrailokyaṃ sacarācaram
vijitya samare pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca jitavān asau
tayoḥ samabhavadyuddhaṃ sughoraṃ romaharṣaṇam
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu divārātram aviśramam
sarathaṃ viṣṇumādāya cikṣepa śatayojanam
tāreṇa vijitaḥ saṃkhye dudrāva garuḍadhvajaḥ
tāro varāñchataguṇaṃ labdhvā śataguṇaṃ balam
pitāmahājjagatsarvamavāpa ditinandanaḥ
devendrapramukhāñjitvā devāndeveśvareśvaraḥ
vārayāmāsa tair devān sarvalokeṣu māyayā
devatāś ca sahendreṇa tārakādbhayapīḍitāḥ
na śāntiṃ lebhire śūrāḥ śaraṇaṃ vā bhayārditāḥ
tadāmarapatiḥ śrīmān saṃnipatyāmaraprabhuḥ
uvācāṅgirasaṃ devo devānāmapi saṃnidhau
bhagavaṃstārako nāma tārajo dānavottamaḥ
tena saṃnihatā yuddhe vatsā gopatinā yathā
bhayāttasmānmahābhāga bṛhadyuddhe bṛhaspate
aniketā bhramantyete śakuntā iva pañjare
asmākaṃ yāny amoghāni āyudhāny aṅgiro vara
tāni moghāni jāyante prabhāvādamaradviṣaḥ
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi dviguṇāni bṛhaspate
viṣṇunā yodhito yuddhe tenāpi na ca sūditaḥ
yastenānirjito yuddhe viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā
kathamasmadvidhastasya sthāsyate samare 'grataḥ
evam uktas tu śakreṇa jīvaḥ sārdhaṃ surādhipaiḥ
sahasrākṣeṇa ca vibhuṃ samprāpyāha kuśadhvajam
so'pi tasya mukhācchrutvā praṇayātpraṇatārtihā
devairaśeṣaiḥ sendraistu jīvamāha pitāmahaḥ
jāne vo'rtiṃ surendrāṇāṃ tathāpi śṛṇu sāṃpratam
vinindya dakṣaṃ yā devī satī rudrāṅgasaṃbhavā
umā haimavatī jajñe sarvalokanamaskṛtā
tasyāścaiveha rūpeṇa yūyaṃ devāḥ surottamāḥ
vibhoryatadhvamākraṣṭuṃ rudrasyāsya mano mahat
tayoryogena sambhūtaḥ skandaḥ śaktidharaḥ prabhuḥ
ṣaḍāsyo dvādaśabhujaḥ senānīḥ pāvakiḥ prabhuḥ
svāheyaḥ kārtikeyaś ca gāṅgeyaḥ śaradhāmajaḥ
devaḥ śākho viśākhaś ca naigameśaś ca vīryavān
senāpatiḥ kumārākhyaḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ
līlayaiva mahāsenaḥ prabalaṃ tārakāsuram
bālo'pi vinihatyaiko devān saṃtārayiṣyati
evam uktas tadā tena brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā
bṛhaspatis tathā sendrair devair devaṃ praṇamya tam
meroḥ śikharamāsādya smaraṃ sasmāra suvrataḥ
smaraṇāddevadevasya smaro'pi saha bhāryayā
ratyā samaṃ samāgamya namaskṛtya kṛtāñjaliḥ
saśakramāha taṃ jīvaṃ jagajjīvo dvijottamāḥ
smṛto yadbhavatā jīva samprāpto'haṃ tavāntikam
brūhi yanme vidhātavyaṃ tamāha surapūjitaḥ
tam āha bhagavāñchakraḥ saṃbhāvya makaradhvajam
śaṅkareṇāṃbikāmadya saṃyojaya yathāsukham
tayā sa ramate yena bhagavān vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
tena mārgeṇa mārgasva patnyā ratyānayā saha
so'pi tuṣṭo mahādevaḥ pradāsyati śubhāṃ gatim
viprayuktastayā pūrvaṃ labdhvā tāṃ girijāmumām
evamukto namaskṛtya devadevaṃ śacīpatim
devadevāśramaṃ gantuṃ matiṃ cakre tayā saha
gatvā tadāśraye śaṃbhoḥ saha ratyā mahābalaḥ
vasaṃtena sahāyena devaṃ yoktumanā bhavat
tataḥ samprekṣya madanaṃ hasan devas triyaṃbakaḥ
nayanena tṛtīyena sāvajñaṃ tam avaikṣata
tato'sya netrajo vahnirmadanaṃ pārśvataḥ sthitam
adahattatkṣaṇādeva lalāpa karuṇaṃ ratiḥ
ratyāḥ pralāpamākarṇya devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
kṛpayā parayā prāha kāmapatnīṃ nirīkṣya ca
amūrto'pi dhruvaṃ bhadre kāryaṃ sarvaṃ patistava
ratikāle dhruve bhadre kariṣyati na saṃśayaḥ
yadā viṣṇuś ca bhavitā vāsudevo mahāyaśāḥ
śāpādbhṛgormahātejāḥ sarvalokahitāya vai
tadā tasya suto yaś ca sa patiste bhaviṣyati
sā praṇamya tadā rudraṃ kāmapatnī śucismitā
jagāma madanaṃ labdhvā vasaṃtena samanvitā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge madanadāho nāmaikādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
tapasā ca mahādevyāḥ pārvatyā vṛṣabhadhvaja
prītiś ca bhagavāñcharvo vacanādbrahmaṇastadā
hitāya cāśramāṇāṃ ca krīḍārthaṃ bhagavānbhavaḥ
tadā haimavatīṃ devīmupayeme yathāvidhi
jagāma sa svayaṃ brahmā marīcyādyairmaharṣibhiḥ
tapovanaṃ mahādevyāḥ pārvatyāḥ padmasaṃbhavaḥ
pradakṣiṇīkṛtya ca tāṃ devīṃ sa jagato'raṇīm
kim arthaṃ tapasā lokānsaṃtāpayasi śailaje
tvayā sṛṣṭaṃ jagatsarvaṃ mātastvaṃ mā vināśaya
tvaṃ hi saṃdhārayellokān imān sarvān svatejasā
sarvadeveśvaraḥ śrīmānsarvalokapatirbhavaḥ
yasya vai devadevasya vayaṃ kiṅkaravādinaḥ
sa evaṃ parameśānaḥ svayaṃ ca varayiṣyati
varade yena sṛṣṭāsi na vinā yastvayāṃbike
vartate nātra saṃdehastava bharttā bhaviṣyati
ityuktvā tāṃ namaskṛtya muhuḥ samprekṣya pārvatīm
gate pitāmahe devo bhagavān parameśvaraḥ
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartuṃ dvijarūpeṇa cāśramam
sā ca dṛṣṭvā mahādevaṃ dvijarūpeṇa saṃsthitam
pratibhādyaiḥ prabhuṃ jñātvā nanāma vṛṣabhadhvajam
sampūjya varadaṃ devaṃ brāhmaṇacchadmanāgatam
tuṣṭāva parameśānaṃ pārvatī parameśvaram
anugṛhya tadā devīmuvāca prahasanniva
kuladharmāśrayaṃ rakṣan bhūdharasya mahātmanaḥ
krīḍārthaṃ ca satāṃ madhye sarvadevapatirbhavaḥ
svayaṃvare mahādevī tava divyasuśobhane
āsthāya rūpaṃ yatsaumyaṃ sameṣye'haṃ saha tvayā
ityuktvā tāṃ samālokya devo divyena cakṣuṣā
jagāmeṣṭaṃ tadā divyaṃ svapuraṃ prayayau ca sā
dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭastadā devīṃ menayā tuhinācalaḥ
āliṅgyāghrāya sampūjya putrīṃ sākṣāttapasvinīm
duhiturdevadevena na jānannabhimantritam
svayaṃvaraṃ tadā devyāḥ sarvalokeṣvaghoṣayat
atha brahmā ca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ sākṣājjanārdanaḥ
śakraś ca bhagavān vahnirbhāskaro bhaga eva ca
tvaṣṭāryamā vivasvāṃś ca yamo varuṇa eva ca
vāyuḥ somastatheśāno rudrāś ca munayas tathā
aśvinau dvādaśādityā gandharvā garuḍas tathā
yakṣāḥ siddhāstathā sādhyā daityāḥ kiṃpuruṣoragāḥ
samudrāś ca nadā vedā mantrāḥ stotrādayaḥ kṣaṇāḥ
nāgāś ca parvatāḥ sarve yajñāḥ sūryādayo grahāḥ
trayastriṃśacca devānāṃ trayaś ca triśataṃ tathā
trayaś ca trisahasraṃ ca tathānye bahavaḥ surā
jagmur girīndraputryāstu svayaṃvaramanuttamam
atha śailasutā devī haimamāruhya śobhanam
vimānaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtam
apsarobhiḥ pranṛttābhiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaiḥ
gandharvasiddhairvividhaiḥ kinnaraiś ca suśobhanaiḥ
bandibhiḥ stūyamānā ca sthitā śailasutā tadā
sitātapatraṃ ratnāṃśumiśritaṃ cāvahattathā
mālinī giriputryāstu saṃdhyā pūrṇendumaṇḍalam
cāmarāsaktahastābhir divyastrībhiś ca saṃvṛtā
mālāṃ gṛhya jayā tasthau suradrumasamudbhavām
vijayā vyajanaṃ gṛhya sthitā devyāḥ samīpagā
mālāṃ pragṛhya devyāṃ tu sthitāyāṃ devasaṃsadi
śiśurbhūtvā mahādevaḥ krīḍārthaṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
utsaṅgatalasaṃsupto babhūva bhagavānbhavaḥ
atha dṛṣṭvā śiśuṃ devāstasyā utsaṃgavarttinam
ko'yam atreti saṃmantrya cukṣubhuś ca samāgatāḥ
vajramāhārayattasya bāhum udyamya vṛtrahā
sa bāhurudyamastasya tathaiva samupasthitaḥ
stambhitaḥ śiśurūpeṇa devadevena līlayā
vajraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhuṃ cālayituṃ tathā
vahniḥ śaktiṃ tathā kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka tathā sthitaḥ
yamo'pi daṇḍaṃ khaḍgaṃ ca nirṛtirmunipuṅgavāḥ
varuṇo nāgapāśaṃ ca dhvajayaṣṭiṃ samīraṇaḥ
somo gadāṃ dhaneśaś ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍabhṛtāṃ varaḥ
īśānaś ca tathā śūlaṃ tīvramudyamya saṃsthitaḥ
rudrāś ca śūlamādityā muśalaṃ vasavas tathā
mudgaraṃ stambhitāḥ sarve devenāśu divaukasaḥ
stambhitā devadevena tathānye ca divaukasaḥ
śiraḥ prakampayan viṣṇuś cakram udyamya saṃsthitaḥ
tasyāpi śiraso bālaḥ sthiratvaṃ pracakāra ha
cakraṃ kṣeptuṃ na śaśāka bāhūṃścālayituṃ na ca
pūṣā dantān daśan dantair bālamaikṣata mohitaḥ
tasyāpi daśanāḥ petur dṛṣṭamātrasya śaṃbhunā
balaṃ tejaś ca yogaṃ ca tathaivāstambhayad vibhuḥ
atha teṣu sthiteṣveva manyumatsu sureṣvapi
brahmā paramasaṃvigno dhyānamāsthāya śaṅkaram
bubudhe devamīśānam umotsaṃge tamāsthitam
sa buddhvā devamīśānaṃ śīghram utthāya vismitaḥ
vavande caraṇau śaṃbhorastuvacca pitāmahaḥ
buddhistvaṃ sarvalokānām ahaṅkāras tvam īśvaraḥ
bhūtānāmindriyāṇāṃ ca tvameveśa pravarttakaḥ
tavāhaṃ dakṣiṇāddhastātsṛṣṭaḥ pūrvaṃ purātanaḥ
vāmahastān mahābāho devo nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
iyaṃ ca prakṛtirdevī sadā te sṛṣṭikāraṇa
patnīrūpaṃ samāsthāya jagatkāraṇamāgatā
namastubhyaṃ mahādeva mahādevyai namonamaḥ
prasādāttava deveśa niyogācca mayā prajāḥ
devādyāstu imāḥ sṛṣṭā mūḍhāstvadyogamohitāḥ
kuru prasādameteṣāṃ yathāpūrvaṃ bhavantvime
sūta uvāca
vijñāpyaivaṃ tadā brahmā devadevaṃ maheśvaram
saṃstambhitāṃstadā tena bhagavān āha padmajaḥ
mūḍhāstha devatāḥ sarvā naiva budhyata śaṅkaram
devadevam ihāyāntaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam
gacchadhvaṃ śaraṇaṃ śīghraṃ devāḥ śakrapurogamāḥ
sanārāyaṇakāḥ sarve munibhiḥ śaṅkaraṃ prabhum
sārdhaṃ mayaiva deveśaṃ paramātmānamīśvaram
anayā haimavatyā ca prakṛtyā saha sattamam
tatra te stambhitāstena tathaiva surasattamāḥ
praṇemur manasā sarve sanārāyaṇakāḥ prabhum
atha teṣāṃ prasanno bhūddevadevastriyaṃbakaḥ
yathāpūrvaṃ cakārāśu vacanādbrahmaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
tata evaṃ prasanne tu sarvadevanivāraṇam
vapuścakāra deveśo divyaṃ paramamadbhutam
tejasā tasya devāste sendracandradivākarāḥ
sabrahmakāḥ sasādhyāś ca sanārāyaṇakās tathā
sayamāś ca sarudrāś ca cakṣuraprārthayan vibhum
tebhyaś ca paramaṃ cakṣuḥ sarvadṛṣṭau ca śaktimat
dadāvaṃbāpatiḥ śarvo bhavānyāś ca calasya ca
labdhvā cakṣustadā devā indraviṣṇupurogamāḥ
sabrahmakaḥ saśakrāś ca tamapaśyanmaheśvaram
brahmādyā nemire tūrṇaṃ bhavānī ca girīśvaraḥ
munayaś ca mahādevaṃ gaṇeśāḥ śivasaṃmatāḥ
sasarjuḥ puṣpavṛṣṭiṃ ca khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
devadundubhayo nedustuṣṭuvurmunayaḥ prabhum
jagurgandharvamukhyāś ca nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ
mumuhurgaṇapāḥ sarve mumodāṃbā ca pārvatī
tasya devī tadā hṛṣṭā samakṣaṃ tridivaukasām
pādayoḥ sthāpayāmāsa mālāṃ divyāṃ sugandhinīm
sādhu sādhviti samprocya tayā tatraiva cārcitam
saha devyā namaścakruḥ śirobhir bhūtalāśritaiḥ
sarve sabrahmakā devāḥ sayakṣoragarākṣasāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge umāsvayaṃvaro nāma dvyadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
atha brahmā mahādevamabhivandya kṛtāñjaliḥ
udvāhaḥ kriyatāṃ deva ityuvāca maheśvaram
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
yatheṣṭamiti lokeśaṃ prāha bhūtapatiḥ prabhuḥ
udvāhārthaṃ maheśasya tatkṣaṇādeva suvratāḥ
brahmaṇā kalpitaṃ divyaṃ puraṃ ratnamayaṃ śubham
athāditirditiḥ sākṣāddanuḥ kadruḥ sukālikā
pulomā surasā caiva siṃhikā vinatā tathā
siddhirmāyā kriyā durgā devī sākṣātsudhā svadhā
sāvitrī vedamātā ca rajanī dakṣiṇā dyutiḥ
svāhā svāhāmatir buddhir ṛddhir vṛddhiḥ sarasvatī
rākā kuhūḥ sinīvālī devī anumatī tathā
dharaṇī dhāraṇī celā śacī nārāyaṇī tathā
etāścānyāś ca devānāṃ mātaraḥ patnayas tathā
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti jagmuḥ sarvā mudānvitāḥ
uragā garuḍā yakṣā gandharvāḥ kinnarā gaṇāḥ
sāgarā girayo meghā māsāḥ saṃvatsarās tathā
vedā mantrās tathā yajñāḥ stomā dharmāś ca sarvaśaḥ
huṅkāraḥ praṇavaścaiva pratihārāḥ sahasraśaḥ
koṭirapsaraso divyāstāsāṃ ca paricārikāḥ
yāś ca sarveṣu dvīpeṣu devalokeṣu nimnagāḥ
tāś ca strīvigrahāḥ sarvāḥ saṃjagmurhṛṣṭamānasāḥ
gaṇapāś ca mahābhāgāḥ sarvalokanamaskṛtāḥ
udvāhaḥ śaṅkarasyeti tatrājagmurmudānvitāḥ
abhyayuḥ śaṅkhavarṇāś ca gaṇakoṭyo gaṇeśvarāḥ
daśabhiḥ kekarākṣaś ca vidyuto'ṣṭābhir eva ca
catuḥṣaṣṭyā viśākhāś ca navabhiḥ pārayātrikaḥ
ṣaḍbhiḥ sarvāntakaḥ śrīmān tathaiva vikṛtānanaḥ
jvālākeśo dvādaśabhiḥ koṭibhir gaṇapuṅgavaḥ
saptabhiḥ samadaḥ śrīmān dundubho'ṣṭābhir eva ca
pañcabhiś ca kapālīśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saṃdārakaḥ śubhaḥ
koṭikoṭibhir eveha gaṇḍakaḥ kuṃbhakas tathā
viṣṭambho 'ṣṭābhir eveha gaṇapaḥ sarvasattamaḥ
pippalaś ca sahasreṇa saṃnādaś ca tathā dvijāḥ
āveṣṭanas tathāṣṭābhiḥ saptabhiścandratāpanaḥ
mahākeśaḥ sahasreṇa koṭīnāṃ gaṇapo vṛtaḥ
kuṇḍī dvādaśabhir vīras tathā parvatakaḥ śubhaḥ
kālaś ca kālakaścaiva mahākālaḥ śatena vai
āgnikaḥ śatakoṭyā vai koṭyāgnimukha eva ca
ādityamūrdhā koṭyā ca tathā caiva dhanāvahaḥ
saṃnāmaś ca śatenaiva kumudaḥ koṭibhis tathā
amoghaḥ kokilaścaiva koṭikoṭyā sumantrakaḥ
kākapāṭo 'paraḥ ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā saṃtānakaḥ prabhuḥ
mahābalaś ca navabhir madhupiṅgaś ca piṅgalaḥ
nīlo navatyā deveśaḥ pūrṇabhadrastathaiva ca
koṭīnāṃ caiva saptatyā caturvaktro mahābalaḥ
koṭikoṭisahasrāṇāṃ śatair viṃśatibhir vṛtāḥ
tatrājagmus tathā devāste sarve śaṅkaraṃ bhavam
bhūtakoṭisahasreṇa pramathaḥ koṭibhistribhiḥ
vīrabhadraścatuḥṣaṣṭyā romajāścaiva koṭibhiḥ
karaṇaścaiva viṃśatyā navatyā kevalaḥ śubhaḥ
pañcākṣaḥ śatamanyuś ca meghamanyus tathaiva ca
kāṣṭhakūṭaś catuḥṣaṣṭyā sukeśo vṛṣabhas tathā
virūpākṣaś ca bhagavān catuḥṣaṣṭyā sanātanaḥ
tāluketuḥ ṣaḍāsyaś ca pañcāsyaś ca sanātanaḥ
saṃvartakas tathā caitro lakulīśaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ
lokāntakaś ca dīptāsyas tathā daityāntakaḥ prabhuḥ
mṛtyuhṛt kālahā kālo mṛtyuñjayakaras tathā
viṣādo viṣadaścaiva vidyutaḥ kāntakaḥ prabhuḥ
devo bhṛṅgī riṭiḥ śrīmān devadevapriyas tathā
aśanir bhāsakaś caiva catuḥṣaṣṭyā sahasrapāt
ete cānye ca gaṇapā asaṃkhyātā mahābalāḥ
sarve sahasrahastāś ca jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇaḥ
candrarekhāvataṃsāś ca nīlakaṇṭhās trilocanāḥ
hārakuṇḍalakeyūramukuṭādyair alaṃkṛtāḥ
brahmendraviṣṇusaṃkāśā aṇimādiguṇairvṛtāḥ
sūryakoṭipratīkāśāstatrājagmurgaṇeśvarāḥ
pātālacāriṇaścaiva sarvalokanivāsinaḥ
tuṃbarurnārado hāhā hūhūścaiva tu sāmagāḥ
ratnānyādāya vādyāṃś ca tatrājagmustadā puram
ṛṣayaḥ kṛtsnaśastatra devagītāstapodhanāḥ
puṇyān vaivāhikān mantrān japur hṛṣṭamānasāḥ
tata evaṃ pravṛtte tu sarvataś ca samāgame
girijāṃ tām alaṃkṛtya svayameva śucismitām
puraṃ praveśayāmāsa svayam ādāya keśavaḥ
sadasyāha ca deveśaṃ nārāyaṇamajo harim
bhavānagre samutpanno bhavānyā saha daivataiḥ
vāmāṅgādasya rudrasya dakṣiṇāṅgādahaṃ prabho
manmūrtistuhinādrīśo yajñārthaṃ sṛṣṭa eva hi
eṣā haimavatī jajñe māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ
śrautasmārtapravṛttyartham udvāhārtham ihāgataḥ
ato'sau jagatāṃ dhātrī dhātā tava mamāpi ca
asya devasya rudrasya mūrtibhir vihitaṃ jagat
kṣmābagnikhendusūryātmapavanātmā yato bhavaḥ
tathāpi tasmai dātavyā vacanācca girermama
eṣā hy ajā śuklakṛṣṇā lohitā prakṛtirbhavān
śreyo'pi śailarājena saṃbandho 'yaṃ tavāpi ca
tava pādme samudbhūtaḥ kalpe nābhyaṃbujādaham
madaṃśasyāsya śailasya mamāpi ca gururbhavān
sūta uvāca
bāḍham ityajam āhāsau devadevo janārdanaḥ
devāś ca munayaḥ sarve devadevaś ca śaṅkaraḥ
tataścotthāya vidvānsaḥ padmanābhaḥ praṇamya tām
pādau prakṣālya devasya karābhyāṃ kamalekṣaṇaḥ
abhyukṣad ātmano mūrdhni brahmaṇaś ca gires tathā
tvadīyaiṣā vivāhārthaṃ menajā hyanujā mama
ityuktvā sodakaṃ dattvā devīṃ deveśvarāya tām
svātmānamapi devāya sodakaṃ pradadau hariḥ
atha sarve muniśreṣṭhāḥ sarvavedārthapāragāḥ
ūcurdātā gṛhītā ca phalaṃ dravyaṃ vicārataḥ
eṣa devo haro nūnaṃ māyayā hi tato jagat
ityuktvā taṃ praṇemuś ca prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ
sasṛjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
devadundubhayo nedurnanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ
vedāś ca mūrtimantaste praṇemustaṃ maheśvaram
brahmaṇā munibhiḥ sārdhaṃ devadevamumāpatim
devo'pi devīmālokya salajjāṃ himaśailajām
na tṛpyatyanavadyāṅgī sā ca devaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
varado 'smīti taṃ prāha hariṃ so'pyāha śaṅkaram
tvayi bhaktiḥ prasīdeti brahmākhyāṃ ca dadau tu saḥ
tatastu punarevāha brahmā vijñāpayanprabhum
havirjuhomi vahnau tu upādhyāyapade sthitaḥ
dadāsi mama yadyājñāṃ kartavyo hyakṛto vidhiḥ
tamāha śaṅkaro devaṃ devadevo jagatpatiḥ
yadyadiṣṭaṃ suraśreṣṭha tatkuruṣva yathepsitam
kartāsmi vacanaṃ sarvaṃ devadeva pitāmaha
tataḥ praṇamya hṛṣṭātmā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
hastaṃ devasya devyāś ca yuyoja paramaṃ prabhuḥ
jvalanaś ca svayaṃ tatra kṛtāñjalirupasthitaḥ
śrautairetairmahāmantrairmūrtimadbhir upasthitaiḥ
yathoktavidhinā hutvā lājānapi yathākramam
ānītānviṣṇunā viprān sampūjya vividhairvaraiḥ
triś ca taṃ jvalanaṃ devaṃ kārayitvā pradakṣiṇam
muktvā hastasamāyogaṃ sahitaiḥ sarvadaivataiḥ
suraiś ca mānavaiḥ sarvaiḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā
nanāma bhagavānbrahmā devadevamumāpatim
tataḥ pādyaṃ tayor dattvā śaṃbhorācamanaṃ tathā
madhuparkaṃ tathā gāṃ ca praṇamya ca punaḥ śivam
atiṣṭhadbhagavānbrahmā devairindrapurogamaiḥ
bhṛgvādyamunayaḥ sarve cākṣataistilataṇḍulaiḥ
sūryādayaḥ samabhyarcya tuṣṭuvurvṛṣabhadhvajam
śivaḥ samāpya devoktaṃ vahnimāropya cātmani
tayā samāgato rudraḥ sarvalokahitāya vai
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi bhavodvāhaṃ śucismitaḥ
śrāvayedvā dvijāñchuddhānvedavedāṅgapāragān
sa labdhvā gāṇapatyaṃ ca bhavena saha modate
yatrāyaṃ kīrtyate vipraistāvadāste tadā bhavaḥ
tasmāt sampūjya vidhivat kīrtayennānyathā dvijāḥ
udvāhe ca dvijendrāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ dvijottamāḥ
kīrtanīyamidaṃ sarvaṃ bhavodvāhamanuttamam
kṛtodvāhastadā devyā haimavatyā vṛṣadhvajaḥ
sagaṇo nandinā sārdhaṃ sarvadevagaṇairvṛtaḥ
purīṃ vārāṇasīṃ divyāmājagāma mahādyutiḥ
avimukte sukhāsīnaṃ praṇamya vṛṣabhadhvajam
apṛcchatkṣetramāhātmyaṃ bhavānī harṣitānanā
athāhārdhendutilakaḥ kṣetramāhātmyamuttamam
avimuktasya māhātmyaṃ vistarācchakyate nahi
vaktuṃ mayā sureśāni ṛṣisaṃghābhipūjitam
kiṃ mayā varṇyate devī hyavimuktaphalodayaḥ
pāpināṃ yatra muktiḥ syānmṛtānām ekajanmanā
anyatra tu kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vārāṇasyāṃ vyapohati
vārāṇasyāṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ paiśācyanarakāvaham
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi piśācatvaṃ varaṃ nṛṇām
na tu śakrasahasratvaṃ svarge kāśīpurīṃ vinā
yatra triviṣṭapo devo yatra viśveśvaro vibhuḥ
oṃkāreśaḥ kṛttivāsā mṛtānāṃ na punarbhavaḥ
uktvā kṣetrasya māhātmyaṃ saṃkṣepācchaśiśekharaḥ
darśayāmāsa codyānaṃ parityajya gaṇeśvarān
tatraiva bhagavān jāto gajavaktro vināyakaḥ
daityānāṃ vighnarūpārtham avighnāya divaukasām
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamuttamam
yathāśrutaṃ mayā sarvaṃ prasādādvaḥ suśobhanam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge pārvatīvivāhavarṇanaṃ nāma tryadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ vināyako jāto gajavaktro gaṇeśvaraḥ
kathaṃ prabhāvastasyaivaṃ sūta vaktumihārhasi
sūta uvāca
etasminnantare devāḥ sendropendrāḥ sametya te
dharmavighnaṃ tadā kartuṃ daityānāmabhavandvijāḥ
asurā yātudhānāś ca rākṣasāḥ krūrakarmiṇaḥ
tāmasāś ca tathā cānye rājasāś ca tathā bhuvi
avighnaṃ yajñadānādyaiḥ samabhyarcya maheśvaram
brahmāṇaṃ ca hariṃ viprā labdhepsitavarā yataḥ
tato 'smākaṃ suraśreṣṭhāḥ sadā vijayasaṃbhavaḥ
teṣāṃ tatastu vighnārthamavighnāya divaukasām
putrārthaṃ caiva nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ karmasiddhaye
vighneśaṃ śaṅkaraṃ sraṣṭuṃ gaṇapaṃ stotumarhatha
ityuktvānyonyamanaghaṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ śivamīśvaram
namaḥ sarvātmane tubhyaṃ sarvajñāya pinākine
anaghāya viriñcāya devyāḥ kāryārthadāyine
akāyāyārthakāyāya hareḥ kāyāpahāriṇe
kāyāntasthāmṛtādhāramaṇḍalāvasthitāya te
kṛtādibhedakālāya kālavegāya te namaḥ
kālāgnirudrarūpāya dharmādyaṣṭapadāya ca
kālīviśuddhadehāya kālikākāraṇāya te
kālakaṇṭhāya mukhyāya vāhanāya varāya te
aṃbikāpataye tubhyaṃ hiraṇyapataye namaḥ
hiraṇyaretase caiva namaḥ śarvāya śūline
kapāladaṇḍapāśāsicarmāṅkuśadharāya ca
pataye haimavatyāś ca hemaśuklāya te namaḥ
pītaśuklāya rakṣārthaṃ surāṇāṃ kṛṣṇavartmane
pañcamāya mahāpañcayajñināṃ phaladāya ca
pañcāsyaphaṇihārāya pañcākṣaramayāya te
pañcadhā pañcakaivalyadevairarcitamūrtaye
pañcākṣaradṛśe tubhyaṃ parātparatarāya te
ṣoḍaśasvaravajrāṅgavaktrāyākṣayarūpiṇe
kādipañcakahastāya cādihastāya te namaḥ
ṭādipādāya rudrāya tādipādāya te namaḥ
pādimeṇḍhrāya yadyaṅgadhātusaptakadhāriṇe
śāntātmarūpiṇe sākṣāt kṣadantakrodhine namaḥ
lavarephahalāṅgāya niraṅgāya ca te namaḥ
sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ hṛdi niḥsvanakāriṇe
bhruvor ante sadā sadbhir dṛṣṭāyātyantabhānave
bhānusomāgninetrāya paramātmasvarūpiṇe
guṇatrayoparisthāya tīrthapādāya te namaḥ
tīrthatattvāya sārāya tasmādapi parāya te
ṛgyajuḥsāmavedāya oṃkārāya namo namaḥ
oṅkāre trividhaṃ rūpamāsthāyoparivāsine
pītāya kṛṣṇavarṇāya raktāyātyantatejase
sthānapañcakasaṃsthāya pañcadhāṇḍabahiḥ kramāt
brahmaṇe viṣṇave tubhyaṃ kumārāya namonamaḥ
aṃbāyāḥ parameśāya sarvoparicarāya te
mūlasūkṣmasvarūpāya sthūlasūkṣmāya te namaḥ
sarvasaṃkalpaśūnyāya sarvasmādrakṣitāya te
ādimadhyāntaśūnyāya citsaṃsthāya namonamaḥ
yamāgnivāyurudrāṃbusomaśakraniśācaraiḥ
diṅmukhe diṅmukhe nityaṃ sagaṇaiḥ pūjitāya te
sarveṣu sarvadā sarvamārge sampūjitāya te
rudrāya rudranīlāya kadrudrāya pracetase
maheśvarāya dhīrāya namaḥ sākṣācchivāya te
atha śṛṇu bhagavan stavacchalena kathitamajendramukhaiḥ surāsureśaiḥ
makhamadanayamāgnidakṣayajñakṣapaṇavicitraviceṣṭitaṃ kṣamasva
sūta uvāca
yaḥ paṭhettu stavaṃ bhaktyā śakrāgnipramukhaiḥ suraiḥ
kīrtitaṃ śrāvayedvidvān sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge devastutirnāma caturadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
yadā sthitāḥ sureśvarāḥ praṇamya caivamīśvaram
tadāṃbikāpatir bhavaḥ pinākadhṛṅ maheśvaraḥ
dadau nirīkṣaṇaṃ kṣaṇādbhavaḥ sa tānsurottamān
praṇemurādarāddharaṃ surā mudārdralocanāḥ
bhavaḥ sudhāmṛtopamairnirīkṣaṇairnirīkṣaṇāt
tadāha bhadramastu vaḥ sureśvarān maheśvaraḥ
varārthamīśa vīkṣyate surā gṛhaṃ gatāstvime
praṇamya cāha vākpatiḥ patiṃ nirīkṣya nirbhayaḥ
suretarādibhiḥ sadā hyavighnamarthito bhavān
samastakarmasiddhaye surāpakārakāribhiḥ
tataḥ prasīdatād bhavān suvighnakarmakāraṇam
surāpakārakāriṇāmihaiṣa eva no varaḥ
tatastadā niśamya vai pinākadhṛk sureśvaraḥ
gaṇeśvaraṃ sureśvaraṃ vapurdadhāra saḥ śivaḥ
gaṇeśvarāś ca tuṣṭuvuḥ sureśvarā maheśvaram
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ bhavārttihāriṇaṃ śubham
ibhānanāśritaṃ varaṃ triśūlapāśadhāriṇam
samastalokasaṃbhavaṃ gajānanaṃ tadāṃbikā
daduḥ puṣpavarṣaṃ hi siddhā munīndrās tathā khecarā devasaṃghāstadānīm
tadā tuṣṭuvuścaikadantaṃ sureśāḥ praṇemurgaṇeśaṃ maheśaṃ vitandrāḥ
tadā tayorvinirgataḥ subhairavaḥ sa mūrtimān
sthito nanarta bālakaḥ samastamaṅgalālayaḥ
vicitravastrabhūṣaṇair alaṃkṛto gajānanaḥ
maheśvarasya putrako 'bhivandya tātam ambikām
jātamātraṃ sutaṃ dṛṣṭvā cakāra bhagavānbhavaḥ
gajānanāya kṛtyāṃstu sarvānsarveśvaraḥ svayam
ādāya ca karābhyāṃ ca susukhābhyāṃ bhavaḥ svayam
āliṅgyāghrāya mūrdhānaṃ mahādevo jagadguruḥ
tavāvatāro daityānāṃ vināśāya mamātmaja
devānāmupakārārthaṃ dvijānāṃ brahmavādinām
yajñaś ca dakṣiṇāhīnaḥ kṛto yena mahītale
tasya dharmasya vighnaṃ ca kuru svargapathe sthitaḥ
adhyāpanaṃ cādhyayanaṃ vyākhyānaṃ karma eva ca
yo 'nyāyataḥ karotyasmin tasya prāṇānsadā hara
varṇāccyutānāṃ nārīṇāṃ narāṇāṃ narapuṅgava
svadharmarahitānāṃ ca prāṇānapahara prabho
yāḥ striyastvāṃ sadā kālaṃ puruṣāś ca vināyaka
yajanti tāsāṃ teṣāṃ ca tvatsāmyaṃ dātumarhasi
tvaṃ bhaktān sarvayatnena rakṣa bālagaṇeśvara
yauvanasthāṃś ca vṛddhāṃś ca ihāmutra ca pūjitaḥ
jagattraye 'tra sarvatra tvaṃ hi vighnagaṇeśvaraḥ
saṃpūjyo vandanīyaś ca bhaviṣyasi na saṃśayaḥ
māṃ ca nārāyaṇaṃ vāpi brahmāṇam api putraka
yajanti yajñairvā viprairagre pūjyo bhaviṣyasi
tvām anabhyarcya kalyāṇaṃ śrautaṃ smārtaṃ ca laukikam
kurute tasya kalyāṇam akalyāṇaṃ bhaviṣyati
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiḥ śūdraiścaiva gajānana
sampūjya sarvasiddhyarthaṃ bhakṣyabhojyādibhiḥ śubhaiḥ
tvāṃ gandhapuṣpadhūpādyair anabhyarcya jagattraye
devairapi tathānyaiś ca labdhavyaṃ nāsti kutracit
abhyarcayanti ye lokā mānavāstu vināyakam
te cārcanīyāḥ śakrādyair bhaviṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ
ajaṃ hariṃ ca māṃ vāpi śakramanyānsurānapi
vighnair bādhayasi tvāṃ cennārcayanti phalārthinaḥ
sasarja ca tadā vighnagaṇaṃ gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ
gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ namaskṛtvāpyatiṣṭhattasya cāgrataḥ
tadā prabhṛti loke 'sminpūjayanti gaṇeśvaram
daityānāṃ dharmavighnaṃ ca cakārāsau gaṇeśvaraḥ
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ skandāgrajasamudbhavam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā sukhībhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge vināyakotpattirnāma pañcādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nṛtyārambhaḥ kathaṃ śaṃbhoḥ kimarthaṃ vā yathātatham
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ śrutaḥ skandāgrajodbhavaḥ
sūta uvāca
dāruko 'surasambhūtas tapasā labdhavikramaḥ
sūdayāmāsa kālāgniriva devāndvijottamān
dārukeṇa tadā devāstāḍitāḥ pīḍitā bhṛśam
brahmāṇaṃ ca tatheśānaṃ kumāraṃ viṣṇumeva ca
yamamindramanuprāpya strīvadhya iti cāsuraḥ
strīrūpadhāribhiḥ stutyairbrahmādyairyudhi saṃsthitaiḥ
bādhitāstena te sarve brahmāṇaṃ prāpya vai dvijāḥ
vijñāpya tasmai tatsarvaṃ tena sārdhamumāpatim
samprāpya tuṣṭuvuḥ sarve pitāmahapurogamāḥ
brahmā prāpya ca deveśaṃ praṇamya bahudhā nataḥ
dāruṇo bhagavāndāruḥ pūrvaṃ tena vinirjitāḥ
nihatya dārukaṃ daityaṃ strīvadhyaṃ trātumarhasi
vijñaptiṃ brahmaṇaḥ śrutvā bhagavān bhaganetrahā
devīmuvāca deveśo girijāṃ prahasanniva
bhavatīṃ prārthayāmyadya hitāya jagatāṃ śubhe
vadhārthaṃ dārukasyāsya strīvadhyasya varānane
atha sā tasya vacanaṃ niśamya jagato'raṇiḥ
viveśa dehe devasya deveśī janmatatparā
ekenāṃśena deveśaṃ praviṣṭā devasattamam
na viveda tadā brahmā devāścendrapurogamāḥ
girijāṃ pūrvavacchaṃbhordṛṣṭvā pārśvasthitāṃ śubhām
māyayā mohitastasyāḥ sarvajño'pi caturmukhaḥ
sā praviṣṭā tanuṃ tasya devadevasya pārvatī
kaṇṭhasthena viṣeṇāsya tanuṃ cakre tadātmanaḥ
tāṃ ca jñātvā tathābhūtāṃ tṛtīyenekṣaṇena vai
sasarja kālīṃ kāmāriḥ kālakaṇṭhīṃ kapardinīm
jātā yadā kālimakālakaṇṭhī jātā tadānīṃ vipulā jayaśrīḥ
devetarāṇāmajayastvasiddhyā tuṣṭirbhavānyāḥ parameśvarasya
jātāṃ tadānīṃ surasiddhasaṃghā dṛṣṭvā bhayād dudruvur agnikalpām
kālīṃ garālaṃkṛtakālakaṇṭhīm upendrapadmodbhavaśakramukhyāḥ
tathaiva jātaṃ nayanaṃ lalāṭe sitāṃśulekhā ca śirasyudagrā
kaṇṭhe karālaṃ niśitaṃ triśūlaṃ kare karālaṃ ca vibhūṣaṇāni
sārdhaṃ divyāṃbarā devyāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
siddhendrasiddhāś ca tathā piśācā jajñire punaḥ
ājñayā dārukaṃ tasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ parameśvarī
dānavaṃ sūdayāmāsa sūdayantaṃ surādhipān
saṃraṃbhātiprasaṃgād vai tasyāḥ sarvamidaṃ jagat
krodhāgninā ca viprendrāḥ saṃbabhūva tadāturam
bhavo'pi bālarūpeṇa śmaśāne pretasaṃkule
ruroda māyayā tasyāḥ krodhāgniṃ pātum īśvaraḥ
taṃ dṛṣṭvā bālamīśānaṃ māyayā tasya mohitā
utthāpyāghrāya vakṣojaṃ stanaṃ sā pradadau dvijāḥ
stanajena tadā sārdhaṃ kopamasyāḥ papau punaḥ
krodhenānena vai bālaḥ kṣetrāṇāṃ rakṣako 'bhavat
mūrtayo 'ṣṭau ca tasyāpi kṣetrapālasya dhīmataḥ
evaṃ vai tena bālena kṛtā sā krodhamūrchitā
kṛtamasyāḥ prasādārthaṃ devadevena tāṇḍavam
saṃdhyāyāṃ sarvabhūtendraiḥ pretaiḥ prītena śūlinā
pītvā nṛtyāmṛtaṃ śaṃbhor ākaṇṭhaṃ parameśvarī
nanarta sā ca yoginyaḥ pretasthāne yathāsukham
tatra sabrahmakā devāḥ sendropendrāḥ samantataḥ
praṇemustuṣṭuvuḥ kālīṃ punardevīṃ ca pārvatīm
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ tāṇḍavaṃ śūlinaḥ prabhoḥ
yogānandena ca vibhostāṇḍavaṃ ceti cāpare
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge śivatāṇḍavakathanaṃ nāma ṣaḍadhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
puropamanyunā sūta gāṇapatyaṃ maheśvarāt
kṣīrārṇavaḥ kathaṃ labdho vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
sūta uvāca
evaṃ kālīm upālabhya gate deve triyaṃbake
upamanyuḥ samabhyarcya tapasā labdhavānphalam
upamanyuriti khyāto muniś ca dvijasattamāḥ
kumāra iva tejasvī krīḍamāno yadṛcchayā
kadācit kṣīram alpaṃ ca pītavān mātulāśrame
īrṣyayā mātulasuto hy apibat kṣīram uttamam
pītvā sthitaṃ yathākāmaṃ dṛṣṭvā provāca mātaram
mātarmātarmahābhāge mama dehi tapasvini
gavyaṃ kṣīram atisvādu nālpamuṣṇaṃ namāmyaham
sūta uvāca
upalālitaivaṃ putreṇa putram āliṅgya sādaram
duḥkhitā vilalāpārtā smṛtvā nairdhanyamātmanaḥ
smṛtvā smṛtvā punaḥ kṣīramupamanyurapi dvijāḥ
dehi dehīti tāmāha rodamāno mahādyutiḥ
uñchavṛttyārjitān bījān svayaṃ piṣṭvā ca sā tadā
bījapiṣṭaṃ tadāloḍya toyena kalabhāṣiṇī
aihyehi mama putreti sāmapūrvaṃ tataḥ sutam
āliṅgyādāya duḥkhārtā pradadau kṛtrimaṃ payaḥ
pītvā ca kṛtrimaṃ kṣīraṃ mātrā dattaṃ dvijottamāḥ
naitatkṣīramiti prāha mātaraṃ cātivihvalaḥ
duḥkhitā sā tadā prāha samprekṣyāghrāya mūrdhani
saṃmārjya netre putrasya karābhyāṃ kamalāyate
taṭinī ratnapūrṇāste svargapātālagocarāḥ
bhāgyahīnā na paśyanti bhaktihīnāś ca ye śive
rājyaṃ svargaṃ ca mokṣaṃ ca bhojanaṃ kṣīrasaṃbhavam
na labhante priyāṇyeṣāṃ no tuṣyati sadā bhavaḥ
bhavaprasādajaṃ sarvaṃ nānyadevaprasādajam
anyadeveṣu niratā duḥkhārtā vibhramanti ca
kṣīraṃ tatra kuto 'smākaṃ mahādevo na pūjitaḥ
pūrvajanmani yaddattaṃ śivamudyamya vai suta
tadeva labhyaṃ nānyattu viṣṇumudyamya vā prabhum
niśamya vacanaṃ māturupamanyurmahādyutiḥ
bālo'pi mātaraṃ prāha praṇipatya tapasvinīm
tyaja śokaṃ mahābhāge mahādevo'sti cetkvacit
cirādvā hyacirādvāpi kṣīrodaṃ sādhayāmyaham
sūta uvāca
tāṃ praṇamyaivamuktvā sa tapaḥ kartuṃ pracakrame
tamāha mātā suśubhaṃ kurviti sutarāṃ sutam
anujñātastayā tatra tapastepe sudustaram
himavatparvataṃ prāpya vāyubhakṣaḥ samāhitaḥ
tapasā tasya viprasya vidhūpitamabhūjjagat
praṇamyāhustu tatsarve haraye devasattamāḥ
śrutvā teṣāṃ tadā vākyaṃ bhagavānpuruṣottamaḥ
kimidaṃ tviti saṃcintya jñātvā tatkāraṇaṃ ca saḥ
jagāma mandaraṃ tūrṇaṃ maheśvaradidṛkṣayā
dṛṣṭvā devaṃ praṇamyaivaṃ provācedaṃ kṛtāñjaliḥ
bhagavan brāhmaṇaḥ kaścidupamanyuritiśrutaḥ
kṣīrārthamadahatsarvaṃ tapasā taṃ nivāraya
etasminnantare devaḥ pinākī parameśvaraḥ
śakrarūpaṃ samāsthāya gantuṃ cakre matiṃ tadā
atha jagāma munestu tapovanaṃ gajavareṇa sitena sadāśivaḥ
saha surāsurasiddhamahoragair amararājatanuṃ svayamāsthitaḥ
sahaiva cāruhya tadā dvipaṃ taṃ pragṛhya vālavyajanaṃ vivasvān
vāmena śacyā sahitaṃ surendraṃ kareṇa cānyena sitātapatram
rarāja bhagavān somaḥ śakrarūpī sadāśivaḥ
sitātapatreṇa yathā candrabiṃbena mandaraḥ
āsthāyaivaṃ hi śakrasya svarūpaṃ parameśvaraḥ
jagāmānugrahaṃ kartum upamanyos tadāśramam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā parameśānaṃ śakrarūpadharaṃ śivam
praṇamya śirasā prāha munirmunivarāḥ svayam
pāvitaścāśramaścāyaṃ mama deveśvaraḥ svayam
prāptaḥ śakro jagannātho bhagavānbhānunā prabhuḥ
evamuktvā sthitaṃ vīkṣya kṛtāñjalipuṭaṃ dvijam
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā śakrarūpadharo haraḥ
tuṣṭo'smi te varaṃ brūhi tapasānena suvrata
dadāmi cepsitān sarvān dhaumyāgraja mahāmate
evamuktastadā tena śakreṇa munisattamaḥ
varayāmi śive bhaktimityuvāca kṛtāñjaliḥ
tato niśamya vacanaṃ muneḥ kupitavatprabhuḥ
prāha savyagramīśānaḥ śakrarūpadharaḥ svayam
māṃ na jānāsi devarṣe devarājānamīśvaram
trailokyādhipatiṃ śakraṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam
madbhakto bhava viprarṣe māmevārcaya sarvadā
dadāmi sarvaṃ bhadraṃ te tyaja rudraṃ ca nirguṇam
tataḥ śakrasya vacanaṃ śrutvā śrotravidāraṇam
upamanyuridaṃ prāha japan pañcākṣaraṃ śubham
manye śakrasya rūpeṇa nūnam atrāgataḥ svayam
kartuṃ daityādhamaḥ kaścid dharmavighnaṃ ca nānyathā
tvayaiva kathitaṃ sarvaṃ bhavanindāratena vai
prasaṃgāddevadevasya nirguṇatvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
bahunātra kimuktena mayādyānumitaṃ mahat
bhavāntarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ śrutā nindā bhavasya tu
śrutvā nindāṃ bhavasyātha tatkṣaṇādeva saṃtyajet
svadehaṃ taṃ nihatyāśu śivalokaṃ sa gacchati
yo vācotpāṭayejjihvāṃ śivanindāratasya tu
triḥ saptakulamuddhṛtya śivalokaṃ sa gacchati
āstāṃ tāvanmamecchāyāḥ kṣīraṃ prati surādhamam
nihatya tvāṃ śivāstreṇa tyajāmyetatkalevaram
purā mātrā tu kathitaṃ tathyameva na saṃśayaḥ
pūrvajanmani cāsmābhir apūjita iti prabhuḥ
evamuktvā tu taṃ devamupamanyurabhītavat
śakraṃ cakre matiṃ hantum atharvāstreṇa mantravit
bhasmādhārānmahātejā bhasmamuṣṭiṃ pragṛhya ca
atharvāstraṃ tatastasmai sasarja ca nanāda ca
dagdhuṃ svadeham āgneyīṃ dhyātvā vai dhāraṇāṃ tadā
atiṣṭhacca mahātejāḥ śuṣkendhanamivāvyayaḥ
evaṃ vyavasite vipre bhagavānbhaganetrahā
vārayāmāsa saumyena dhāraṇāṃ tasya yoginaḥ
atharvāstraṃ tadā tasya saṃhṛtaṃ candrakeṇa tu
kālāgnisadṛśaṃ cedaṃ niyogānnandinas tathā
svarūpameva bhagavānāsthāya parameśvaraḥ
darśayāmāsa viprāya bālendukṛtaśekharam
kṣīradhārāsahasraṃ ca kṣīrodārṇavameva ca
dadhyāderarṇavaṃ caiva ghṛtodārṇavameva ca
phalārṇavaṃ ca bālasya bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaṃ tathā
apūpagirayaścaiva tathātiṣṭhan samantataḥ
upamanyumuvāca sasmito bhagavānbandhujanaiḥ samāvṛtam
girijām avalokya sasmitāṃ saghṛṇaṃ prekṣyatu taṃ tadā ghṛṇī
bhuṅkṣva bhogānyathākāmaṃ bāndhavaiḥ paśya vatsa me
upamanyo mahābhāga tavāṃbaiṣā hi pārvatī
mayā putrīkṛto'syadya dattaḥ kṣīrodadhis tathā
madhunaścārṇavaścaiva dadhnaścārṇava eva ca
ājyodanārṇavaścaiva phalalehyārṇavas tathā
apūpagirayaścaiva bhakṣyabhojyārṇavaḥ punaḥ
pitā tava mahādevaḥ pitā vai jagatāṃ mune
mātā tava mahābhāgā jaganmātā na saṃśayaḥ
amaratvaṃ mayā dattaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ ca śāśvatam
varānvaraya dāsyāmi nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
evamuktvā mahādevaḥ karābhyāmupagṛhya tam
āghrāya mūrdhani vibhurdadau devyāstadā bhavaḥ
devī tanayamālokya dadau tasmai girīndrajā
yogaiśvaryaṃ tadā tuṣṭā brahmavidyāṃ dvijottamāḥ
so'pi labdhvā varaṃ tasyāḥ kumāratvaṃ ca sarvadā
tuṣṭāva ca mahādevaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā
varayāmāsa ca tadā vareṇyaṃ virajekṣaṇam
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā praṇipatya punaḥ punaḥ
prasīda devadeveśa tvayi cāvyabhicāriṇī
śraddhā caiva mahādeva sānnidhyaṃ caiva sarvadā
evamuktastadā tena prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ
dattvepsitaṃ hi viprāya tatraivāntaradhīyata
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge upamanyucaritaṃ nāma saptādhikaśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
dṛṣṭo 'sau vāsudevena kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
dhaumyāgrajastato labdhaṃ divyaṃ pāśupataṃ vratam
kathaṃ labdhaṃ tadā jñānaṃ tasmātkṛṣṇena dhīmatā
vaktumarhasi tāṃ sūta kathāṃ pātakanāśinīm
sūta uvāca
svecchayā hyavatīrṇo'pi vāsudevaḥ sanātanaḥ
nindayanneva mānuṣyaṃ dehaśuddhiṃ cakāra saḥ
putrārthaṃ bhagavāṃstatra tapastaptuṃ jagāma ca
āśramaṃ copamanyorvai dṛṣṭavāṃstatra taṃ munim
namaścakāra taṃ dṛṣṭvā dhaumyāgrajamaho dvijāḥ
bahumānena vai kṛṣṇastriḥ kṛtvā vai pradakṣiṇam
tasyāvalokanādeva muneḥ kṛṣṇasya dhīmataḥ
naṣṭameva malaṃ sarvaṃ kāyajaṃ karmmajaṃ tathā
bhasmanoddhūlanaṃ kṛtvā upamanyurmahādyutiḥ
tamagniriti viprendrā vāyurityādibhiḥ kramāt
divyaṃ pāśupataṃ jñānaṃ pradadau prītamānasaḥ
muneḥ prasādānmānyo 'sau kṛṣṇaḥ pāśupate dvijāḥ
tapasā tvekavarṣānte dṛṣṭvā devaṃ maheśvaram
sāṃbaṃ sagaṇamavyagraṃ labdhavānputramātmanaḥ
tadāprabhṛti taṃ kṛṣṇaṃ munayaḥ saṃśitavratāḥ
divyāḥ pāśupatāḥ sarve tasthuḥ saṃvṛtya sarvadā
anyaṃ ca kathayiṣyāmi muktyarthaṃ prāṇināṃ sadā
sauvarṇīṃ mekhalāṃ kṛtvā ādhāraṃ daṇḍadhāraṇam
sauvarṇaṃ piṇḍikaṃ cāpi vyajanaṃ daṇḍameva ca
naraiḥ striyātha vā kāryaṃ maṣībhājanalekhanīm
kṣurāḥ kartarikā cāpi atha pātramathāpi vā
pāśupatāya dātavyaṃ bhasmoddhūlitavigrahaiḥ
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃ vātha nivedayet
ātmavittānusāreṇa yoginaṃ pūjayedbudhaḥ
te sarve pāpanirmuktāḥ samastakulasaṃyutāḥ
yānti rudrapadaṃ divyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
tasmādanena dānena gṛhastho mucyate bhavāt
yogināṃ saṃpradānena śivaḥ kṣipraṃ prasīdati
rājyaṃ putraṃ dhanaṃ bhavyamaśvaṃ yānamathāpi vā
sarvasvaṃ vāpi dātavyaṃ yadīcchenmokṣamuttamam
adhruveṇa śarīreṇa dhruvaṃ sādhyaṃ prayatnataḥ
bhavyaṃ pāśupataṃ nityaṃ saṃsārārṇavatārakam
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ saṃkṣepānna ca saṃśayaḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe pūrvabhāge 'ṣṭottaraśatatamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kṛṣṇas tuṣyati keneha sarvadeveśvareśvaraḥ
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ sūta sarvārthavidbhavān
sūta uvāca
purā pṛṣṭo mahātejā mārkaṇḍeyo mahāmuniḥ
aṃbarīṣeṇa viprendrās tad vadāmi yathātatham
aṃbarīṣa uvāca
mune samastadharmāṇāṃ pāragas tvaṃ mahāmate
mārkaṇḍeya purāṇo 'si purāṇārthaviśāradaḥ
nārāyaṇānāṃ divyānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ śreṣṭhamuttamam
tatkiṃ brūhi mahāprājña bhaktānāmiha suvrata
sūta uvāca
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā samutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ
smaran nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ kṛṣṇam acyutam avyayam
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu bhūpa yathānyāyaṃ puṇyaṃ nārāyaṇātmakam
smaraṇaṃ pūjanaṃ caiva praṇāmo bhaktipūrvakam
pratyekam aśvamedhasya yajñasya samam ucyate
ya ekaḥ puruṣaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ paramātmā janārdanaḥ
yasmādbrahmā tataḥ sarvaṃ samāśrityaiva mucyate
dharmamekaṃ pravakṣyāmi yaddṛṣṭaṃ viditaṃ mayā
purā tretāyuge kaścit kauśiko nāma vai dvijaḥ
vāsudevaparo nityaṃ sāmagānarataḥ sadā
bhojanāsanaśayyāsu sadā tadgatamānasaḥ
udāracaritaṃ viṣṇor gāyamānaḥ punaḥ punaḥ
viṣṇoḥ sthalaṃ samāsādya hareḥ kṣetramanuttamam
agāyata hariṃ tatra tālavarṇalayānvitam
mūrcchanāsvarayogena śrutibhedena bheditam
bhaktiyogaṃ samāpanno bhikṣāmātraṃ hi tatra vai
tatraivaṃ gāyamānaṃ ca dṛṣṭvā kaściddvijastadā
padmākhya iti vikhyātastasmai cānnaṃ dadau tadā
sakuṭumbo mahātejā hyuṣṇamannaṃ hi tatra vai
kauśiko hi tadā hṛṣṭo gāyannāste hariṃ prabhum
śṛṇvannāste sa padmākhyaḥ kāle kāle vinirgataḥ
kālayogena samprāptāḥ śiṣyā vai kauśikasya ca
sapta rājanyavaiśyānāṃ viprāṇāṃ kulasaṃbhavāḥ
jñānavidyādhikāḥ śuddhā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ
teṣām api tathānnādyaṃ padmākṣaḥ pradadau svayam
śiṣyaiśca sahito nityaṃ kauśiko hṛṣṭamānasaḥ
viṣṇusthale hariṃ tatra āste gāyanyathāvidhi
tatraiva mālavo nāma vaiśyo viṣṇuparāyaṇaḥ
dīpamālāṃ harernityaṃ karoti prītimānasaḥ
mālavī nāma bhāryā ca tasya nityaṃ pativratā
gomayena samālipya hareḥ kṣetraṃ samantataḥ
bhartrā sahāste suprītā śṛṇvatī gānamuttamam
kuśasthalātsamāpannā brāhmaṇāḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ
pañcāśadvai samāpannā harer gānārtham uttamāḥ
sādhayanto hi kāryāṇi kauśikasya mahātmanaḥ
jñānavidyārthatattvajñāḥ śṛṇvanto hyavasaṃstu te
khyātamāsīttadā tasya gānaṃ vai kauśikasya tat
śrutvā rājā samabhyetya kaliṅgo vākyamabravīt
kauśikādya gaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ gāyasveha ca māṃ punaḥ
śṛṇudhvaṃ ca tathā yūyaṃ kuśasthalajanā api
tacchrutvā kauśikaḥ prāha rājānaṃ sāntvayā girā
na jihvā me mahārājan vāṇī ca mama sarvadā
harer anyam apindraṃ vā stauti naiva ca vakṣyati
evamukte tu tacchiṣyo vāsiṣṭho gautamo hariḥ
sārasvatastathā citraścitramālyastathā śiśuḥ
ūcuste pārthivaṃ tadvadyathā prāha ca kauśikaḥ
śravakāste tathā procuḥ pārthivaṃ viṣṇutatparāḥ
śrotrāṇīmāni śṛṇvanti hareranyaṃ na pārthiva
gānakīrtiṃ vayaṃ tasya śṛṇumo 'nyāṃ na ca stutim
tacchrutvā pārthivo ruṣṭo gāyatāmiti cābravīt
svabhṛtyānbrāhmaṇā hyete kīrtiṃ śṛṇvanti me yathā
na śṛṇvanti kathaṃ tasmāt gāyamāne samantataḥ
evam uktāstadā bhṛtyā jaguḥ pārthivamuttamam
niruddhamārgā viprāste gāne vṛtte tu duḥkhitāḥ
kāṣṭhaśaṅkubhir anyonyaṃ śrotrāṇi vidadhurdvijāḥ
kauśikādyāśca tāṃ jñātvā manovṛttiṃ nṛpasya vai
prasahyāsmāṃstu gāyeta svagāne 'sau nṛpaḥ sthitaḥ
iti viprāḥ suniyatā jihvāgraṃ cichiduḥ karaiḥ
tato rājā susaṃkruddhaḥ svadeśāttānnyavāsayat
ādāya sarvaṃ vittaṃ ca tataste jagmuruttarām
diśamāsādya kālena kāladharmeṇa yojitāḥ
tānāgatānyamo dṛṣṭvā kiṃ kartavyamiti sma ha
coṣṭitaṃ tatkṣaṇe rājan brahmā prāha surādhipān
kauśikādīn dvijānadya vāsayadhvaṃ yathāsukham
gānayogena ye nityaṃ pūjayanti janārdanam
tānānayata bhadraṃ vo yadi devatvamicchatha
ityuktā lokapālaste kauśiketi punaḥ punaḥ
mālaveti tathā kecit padmākṣeti tathāpare
krośamānāḥ samabhyetya tānādāya vihāyasā
brahmalokaṃ gatāḥ śīghraṃ muhūrtenaiva te surāḥ
kauśikādīṃstato dṛṣṭvā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ
pratyudgamya yathānyāyaṃ svāgatenābhyapūjayat
tataḥ kolāhalamabhūdatigauravamulbaṇam
brahmaṇā caritaṃ dṛṣṭvā devānāṃ nṛpasattama
hiraṇyagarbho bhagavāṃstānnivārya surottamān
kauśikādīnsamādāya munīn devaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
viṣṇulokaṃ yayau śīghraṃ vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ
tatra nārāyaṇo devaḥ śvetadvīpanivāsibhiḥ
jñānayogeśvaraiḥ siddhairviṣṇubhaktaiḥ samāhitaiḥ
nārāyaṇasamair divyaiś caturbāhudharaiḥ śubhaiḥ
viṣṇucihnasamāpannairdīpyamānairakalmaṣaiḥ
aṣṭāśītisahasraiśca sevyamāno mahājanaiḥ
asmābhirnāradādyaiśca sanakādyairakalmaṣaiḥ
bhūtairnānāvidhaiścaiva divyastrībhiḥ samantataḥ
sevyamāno 'tha madhye vai sahasradvārasaṃvṛte
sahasrayojanāyāme divye maṇimaye śubhe
vimāne vimale citre bhadrapīṭhāsane hariḥ
lokakārye prasaktānāṃ dattadṛṣṭiśca mādhavaḥ
tasminkāle 'tha bhagavān kauśikādyaiśca saṃvṛtaḥ
āgamya praṇipatyāgre tuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam
tato kilokya bhagavān harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
kauśiketyāha saṃprītyā tānsarvāṃśca yathākramam
jayaghoṣo mahān āsīnmahāścarye samāgate
brahmāṇamāha viśvātmā śṛṇu brahman mayoditam
kauśikasya ime viprāḥ sādhyasādhanatatparāḥ
hitāya sampravṛttā vai kuśasthalanivāsinaḥ
matkīrtiśravaṇe yuktā jñānatattvārthakovidāḥ
ananyadevatābhaktāḥ sādhyā devā bhavantvime
divyarūpadharaḥ śrīmān śṛṇvangānamihādhipaḥ
āsva nityaṃ yathākāmaṃ yāvallokā bhavanti vai
padmākṣamāha bhagavān dhanado bhavamādhavaḥ
dhanānāmīśvaro bhūtvā yathākālaṃ hi māṃ punaḥ
mālavaṃ mālavīṃ caivaṃ prāha dāmodaro hariḥ
mama loke yathākālaṃ bhāryayā saha mālava
divyarūpadharaḥ śrīmān śṛṇvangānamihādhipaḥ
āsva nityaṃ yathākāmaṃ yāvallokā bhavanti vai
padmākṣamāha bhagavān dhanado bhavamādhavaḥ
dhanānāmīśvaro bhūtvā yathākālaṃ hi māṃ punaḥ
āgamya dṛṣṭvā māṃ nityaṃ kuru rājyaṃ yathāsukham
evamuktvā harirviṣṇurbrahmāṇamidamabravīt
kauśikasyāsya gānena yoganidrā ca me gatā
viṣṇusthale ca māṃ stauti śiṣyaireṣa samantataḥ
rājñā nirastaḥ krūreṇa kaliṅgena mahīyasā
sa jihvāchedanaṃ kṛtvā hareranyaṃ kathañcana
na stoṣyāmīti niyataḥ prāpto 'sau mama lokatām
ete ca viprā niyatā mama bhaktā yaśasvinaḥ
śrotracchidramathāhatya śaṅkubhirvai parasparam
śroṣyāmo naiva cānyadvai hareḥ kīrtimitisma ha
ete viprāśca devatvaṃ mama sānnidhyameva ca
mālavo bhāryayā sārdhaṃ matkṣetraṃ parimṛjya vai
dīpamālādibhirnityamabhyarcya satataṃ hi mām
gānaṃ śṛṇoti niyato matkīrticaritānvitam
tenāsau prāptavāṃllokaṃ mama brahmā sanātanam
padmākṣo 'sau dadau bhojyaṃ kauśikasya mahātmanaḥ
dhaneśatvam avāpto 'sau mama sānnidhyameva ca
evamuktvā haristatra samāje lokapūjitaḥ
tasmin kṣaṇe samāpannā madhurākṣarapeśalaiḥ
vipañcīguṇatattvajñair vādyavidyāviśāradaiḥ
mandaṃ mandasmitā devī vicitrābharaṇānvitā
gāyamānā samāyātā lakṣmīrviṣṇuparigrahā
vṛtā sahasrakoṭībhiraṅganābhiḥ samantataḥ
tato gaṇādhipā dṛṣṭvā bhuśuṇḍīparighāyudhāḥ
brahmādīṃstarjayantaste munīndevānsamantataḥ
utsārayantaḥ saṃhṛṣṭā dhiṣṭhitāḥ parvatopamāḥ
sarve vayaṃ hi niryātāḥ sārdhaṃ vai brahmaṇā suraiḥ
tasmin kṣaṇe samāhūtastuṃbarurmunisattamaḥ
praviveśa samīpaṃ vai devyā devasya caiva hi
tatrāsīno yathāyogaṃ nānāmūrcchāsamanvitam
jagau kalapadaṃ hṛṣṭo vipañcīṃ cābhyavādayat
nānāratnasamāyuktair divyair ābharaṇottamaiḥ
divyamālyaistathā śubhraiḥ pūjito munisattamaḥ
nirgatas tuṃbarur hṛṣṭo 'nye ca ṛṣayaḥ surāḥ
dṛṣṭvā sampūjitaṃ yāntaṃ yathāyogamarindama
nārado 'tha munirdṛṣṭvā tuṃbaroḥ satkriyāṃ hareḥ
śokāviṣṭena manasā saṃtaptahṛdayekṣaṇaḥ
cintām āpedivāṃstatra śokamūrcchākulātmakaḥ
kenāhaṃ hi haretyāsye yogaṃ devīsamīpataḥ
aho tuṃbaruṇā prāptaṃ dhiṅ māṃ mūḍhaṃ vicetasam
yo 'haṃ hareḥ saṃnikāśaṃ bhūtairniryātitaḥ katham
jīvanyāsyāmi kutrāhamaho tuṃbaruṇā kṛtam
iti saṃcintayan viprastapa āsthitavānmuniḥ
divyaṃ varṣasahasraṃ tu nirucchvāsasamanvitaḥ
dhyāyanviṣṇumathādhyāste tuṃbaroḥ satkriyāṃ smaran
rodamāno muhurvidvān dhiṅ māmiti ca cintayan
tatra yatkṛtavānviṣṇustacchṛṇuṣva narādhipa
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kauśikavṛttakathanaṃ nāma prathamo 'dhyāyaḥ
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
tato nārāyaṇo devastasmai sarvaṃ pradāya vai
kālayogena viśvātmā samaṃ cakre 'tha tumbaroḥ
nāradaṃ muniśārdūlamevaṃ vṛttamabhūtpurā
nārāyaṇasya gītānāṃ gānaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ punaḥ punaḥ
gānenārādhito viṣṇuḥ satkīrtijñānavarcasī
dadāti tuṣṭiṃ sthānaṃ ca yathāsau kauśikasya vai
padmākṣaprabhṛtīnāṃ ca saṃsiddhiṃ pradadau hariḥ
tasmāttvayā mahārāja viṣṇukṣetre viśeṣataḥ
arcanaṃ gānanṛtyādyaṃ vādyotsavasamanvitam
kartavyaṃ viṣṇubhaktairhi puruṣairaniśaṃ nṛpa
śrotavyaṃ ca sadā nityaṃ śrotavyo'sau haristathā
viṣṇukṣetre tu yo vidvān kārayedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ
gānanṛtyādikaṃ caiva viṣṇvākhyānāṃ kathāṃ tathā
jātismṛtiṃ ca medhāṃ ca tathaivoparame smṛtim
prāpnoti viṣṇusāyujyaṃ satyametannṛpādhipa
etatte kathitaṃ rājan yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
kiṃ vadāmi ca te bhūyo vada dharmabhṛtāṃ vara
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge viṣṇumāhātmyaṃ nāma dvitīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
ambarīṣa uvāca
mārkaṇḍeya mahāprājña kena yogena labdhavān
gānavidyāṃ mahābhāga nārado bhagavānmuniḥ
tuṃbarośca samānatvaṃ kasminkāla upeyivān
etadācakṣva me sarvaṃ sarvajño'si mahāmate
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śruto mayāyamartho vai nāradāddevadarśanāt
svayam āha mahātejā nārado 'sau mahāmatiḥ
saṃtapyamāno bhagavān divyaṃvarṣasahasrakam
nirucchvāsena saṃyuktastuṃbarorgauravaṃ smaran
tatāpa ca mahāghoraṃ taporāśistapaḥ param
athāntarikṣe śuśrāva nārado 'sau mahāmuniḥ
vāṇīṃ divyāṃ mahāghoṣām adbhutām aśarīriṇīm
kimarthaṃ muniśārdūla tapastapasi duścaram
ulūkaṃ paśya gatvā tvaṃ yadi gāne ratā matiḥ
mānasottaraśaile tu gānabandhuriti smṛtaḥ
gaccha śīghraṃ ca paśyainaṃ gānavittvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
ityukto vismayāviṣṭo nārado vāgvidāṃ varaḥ
mānasottaraśaile tu gānabandhuṃ jagāma vai
gandharvāḥ kinnarā yakṣāstathā cāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
samāsīnāstu parito gānabandhuṃ tatastataḥ
gānavidyāṃ samāpannaḥ śikṣitāstena pakṣiṇā
snigdhakaṇṭhasvarās tatra samāsīnā mudānvitāḥ
tato nāradamālokya gānabandhuruvāca ha
praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ svāgatenābhyapūjayat
kimarthaṃ bhagavānatra cāgato 'si mahāmate
kiṃ kāryaṃ hi mayā brahman brūhi kiṃ karavāṇi te
nārada uvāca
ulūkendra mahāprājña śṛṇu sarvaṃ yathātatham
mama vṛttaṃ pravakṣyāmi purā bhūtaṃ mahādbhutam
atīte hi yuge vidvannārāyaṇasamīpagam
māṃ vinirdhūya saṃhṛṣṭaḥ samāhūya ca tuṃbarum
lakṣmīsamanvito viṣṇuraśṛṇodgānamuttamam
brahmādayaḥ surāḥ sarve nirastāḥ sthānato 'cyutāḥ
kauśikādyāḥ samāsīnā gānayogena vai harim
evamārādhya samprāptā gāṇapatyaṃ yathāsukham
tenāhamatiduḥkhārtastapastaptumihāgataḥ
yaddattaṃ yaddhutaṃ caiva yathā vā śrutameva ca
yadadhītaṃ mayā sarvaṃ kalāṃ nārhati ṣoḍaśīm
viṣṇormāhātmyayuktasya gānayogasya vai tataḥ
saṃcintyāhaṃ tapo ghoraṃ tadarthaṃ taptavān dvija
divyavarṣasahasraṃ vai tato hyaśṛṇavaṃ punaḥ
vāṇīm ākāśasambhūtāṃ tvāmuddiśya vihaṅgama
ulūkaṃ gaccha devarṣe gānabandhuṃ matiryadi
gāne cedvartate brahman tatra tvaṃ vetsyase cirāt
ityahaṃ preritastena tvatsamīpam ihāgataḥ
kiṃ kariṣyāmi śiṣyo'haṃ tava māṃ pālayāvyaya
gānabandhuruvāca
śṛṇu nārada yadvṛttaṃ purā mama mahāmate
atyāścaryasamāyuktaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham
bhuvaneśa iti khyāto rājābhūd dhārmikaḥ purā
aśvamedhasahasraiśca vājapeyāyutena ca
gavāṃ koṭyarbude caiva suvarṇasya tathaiva ca
vāsasāṃ rathahastināṃ kanyāśvānāṃ tathaiva ca
dattvā sa rājā viprebhyo medinīṃ pratipālayan
nivārayan svake rājye geyayogena keśavam
anyaṃ vā geyayogena gāyanyadi sa me bhavet
vadhyaḥ sarvātmanā tasmād vedair īḍyaḥ paraḥ pumān
gānayogena sarvatra striyo gāyantu nityaśaḥ
sūtamāgadhasaṃghāśca gītaṃ te kārayantu vai
ityājñāpya mahātejā rājyaṃ vai paryapālayat
tasya rājñaḥ purābhyāśe harimitra iti śrutaḥ
brāhmaṇo viṣṇubhaktaśca sarvadvandvavivarjitaḥ
nadīpulinamāsādya pratimāṃ ca hareḥ śubhām
abhyarcya ca yathānyāyaṃ ghṛtadadhyuttaraṃ bahu
miṣṭānnaṃ pāyasaṃ dattvā harerāvedya pūpakam
praṇipatya yathānyāyaṃ tatra vinyastamānasaḥ
agāyata hariṃ tatra tālavarṇalayānvitam
atīva snehasaṃyuktas tadgatenāntarātmanā
tato rājñaḥ samādeśāccārāstatra samāgatāḥ
tadarcanādi sakalaṃ nirdhūya ca samantataḥ
brāhmaṇaṃ taṃ gṛhītvā te rājñe samyaṅnyavedayan
tato rājā dvijaśreṣṭhaṃ paribhartsya sudurmatiḥ
rājyānniryātayāmāsa hṛtvā sarvaṃ dhanādikam
pratimāṃ ca hareścaiva mlecchā hṛtvā yayuḥ punaḥ
tataḥ kālena mahatā kāladharmamupeyivān
sa rājā sarvalokeṣu pūjyamānaḥ samantataḥ
kṣudhārtaśca tathā khinno yamamāha suduḥkhitaḥ
kṣuttṛṭ ca vartate deva svargatasyāpi me sadā
mayā pāpaṃ kṛtaṃ kiṃ vā kiṃ kariṣyāmi vai yama
yama uvāca
tvayā hi sumahatpāpaṃ kṛtamajñānamohataḥ
harimitraṃ prati tadā vāsudevaparāyaṇam
harimitre kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vāsudevārcanādiṣu
tena pāpena samprāptaḥ kṣudrogastvāṃ sadā nṛpa
dānayajñādikaṃ sarvaṃ pranaṣṭaṃ te narādhipa
gītavādyasamopetaṃ gāyamānaṃ mahāmatim
harimitraṃ samāhūya hṛtavānasi taddhanam
upahārādikaṃ sarvaṃ vāsudevasya sannidhau
tava bhṛtyaistadā luptaṃ pāpaṃ cakrustvadājñayā
hareḥ kīrtiṃ vinā cānyad brāhmaṇena nṛpottama
na geyayoge gātavyaṃ tasmātpāpaṃ kṛtaṃ tvayā
naṣṭaste sarvaloko'dya gaccha parvatakoṭaram
pūrvotsṛṣṭaṃ svadehaṃ taṃ khādannityaṃ nikṛtya vai
tasmin kāle tvimaṃ dehaṃ khādannityaṃ kṣudhānvitaḥ
