mahānirayasaṃsthastvaṃ yāvanmanvantaraṃ bhavet
manvantare tato 'tīte bhūmyāṃ tvaṃ ca bhaviṣyasi
tataḥ kālena samprāpya mānuṣyamavagacchasi
gānabandhuruvāca
evamuktvā yamo vidvāṃstatraivāntaradhīyata
harimitro vimānena stūyamāno gaṇādhipaiḥ
viṣṇulokaṃ gataḥ śrīmān saṃgṛhya gaṇabāndhavān
bhuvaneśo nṛpo hyasmin koṭare parvatasya vai
khādamānaḥ śavaṃ nityam āste kṣuttṛṭsamanvitaḥ
adrākṣaṃ taṃ nṛpaṃ tatra sarvametanmamoktavān
samālokyāhamājñāya harimitraṃ sameyivān
vimānenārkavarṇena gacchantamamarairvṛtam
indradyumnaprasādena prāptaṃ me hyāyuruttamam
tenāhaṃ harimitraṃ vai dṛṣṭavān asmi suvrata
tadaiśvaryaprabhāvena mano me samupāgatam
gānavidyāṃ prati tadā kinnaraiḥ samupāviśam
ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ gānayogena me mune
jihvā prasāditā spaṣṭā tato gānamaśikṣayam
tatastu dviguṇenaiva kālenābhūdiyaṃ mama
gānayogasamāyuktā gatā manvantarā daśa
gānācāryo 'bhavaṃ tatra gandharvādyāḥ samāgatāḥ
ete kinnarasaṃghā vai māmācāryamupāgatāḥ
tapasā naiva śakyā vai gānavidyā tapodhana
tasmācchrutena saṃyukto mattastvaṃ gānamāpnuhi
evamukto munistaṃ vai praṇipatya jagau tadā
tacchṛṇuṣva muniśreṣṭha vāsudevaṃ namasya tu
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
ulūkenaivamuktastu nārado munisattamaḥ
śikṣākrameṇa saṃyuktastatra gānam aśikṣayat
gānabandhustadāhedaṃ tyaktalajjo bhavādhunā
ulūka uvāca
strīsaṃgame tathā gīte dyūte vyākhyānasaṃgame
vyavahāre tathāhāre tvarthānāṃ ca samāgame
āye vyaye tathā nityaṃ tyaktalajjastu vai bhavet
na kuñcitena gūḍhena nityaṃ prāvaraṇādibhiḥ
hastavikṣepabhāvena vyāditāsyena caiva hi
niryātajihvāyogena na geyaṃ hi kathañcana
na gāyedūrdhvabāhuśca nordhvadṛṣṭiḥ kathañcana
svāṅgaṃ nirīkṣamāṇena paraṃ samprekṣatā tathā
saṃghaṭṭe ca tathotthāne kaṭisthānaṃ na śasyate
hāso roṣastathā kampas tathānyatra smṛtiḥ punaḥ
naitāni śastarūpāṇi gānayoge mahāmate
naikahastena śakyaṃ syāttālasaṃghaṭṭanaṃ mune
kṣudhārtena bhayārtena tṛṣṇārtena tathaiva ca
gānayogo na kartavyo nāndhakāre kathañcana
evamādīni cānyāni na kartavyāni gāyatā
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
evamuktaḥ sa bhagavāṃstenoktairvidhilakṣaṇaiḥ
aśikṣayattathā gītaṃ divyaṃ varṣasahasrakam
tataḥ samastasampanno gītaprastārakādiṣu
vipañcyādiṣu sampannaḥ sarvasvaravibhāgavit
ayutāni ca ṣaṭtriṃśatsahasrāṇi śatāni ca
svarāṇāṃ bhedayogena jñātavānmunisattamaḥ
tato gandharvasaṃghāśca kinnarāṇāṃ tathaiva ca
muninā saha saṃyuktāḥ prītiyuktā bhavanti te
gānabandhuṃ muniḥ prāha prāpya gānamanuttamam
tvāṃ samāsādya sampannas tvaṃ hi gītaviśāradaḥ
dhvāṅkṣaśatro mahāprājña kimācārya karomi te
gānabandhuruvāca
brahmaṇo divase brahman manavastu caturdaśa
tatas trailokyasamplāvo bhaviṣyati mahāmune
tāvanme tvāyuṣo bhāvastāvanme paramaṃ śubham
manasā dhyāyitaṃ me syāddakṣiṇā munisattama
nārada uvāca
atītakalpasaṃyoge garuḍastvaṃ bhaviṣyasi
svasti te 'stu mahāprājña gamiṣyāmi prasīda mām
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
evamuktvā jagāmātha nārado'pi janārdanam
śvetadvīpe hṛṣīkeśaṃ gāpayāmāsa gītakān
tatra śrutvā tu bhagavānnāradaṃ prāha mādhavaḥ
tuṃbarorna viśiṣṭo'si gītairadyāpi nārada
yadā viśiṣṭo bhavitā taṃ kālaṃ pravadāmyaham
gānabandhuṃ samāsādya gānārthajño bhavānasi
manorvaivasvatasyāham aṣṭaviṃśatime yuge
dvāparānte bhaviṣyāmi yaduvaṃśakulodbhavaḥ
devakyāṃ vasudevasya kṛṣṇo nāmnā mahāmate
tadānīṃ māṃ samāsādya smārayethā yathātatham
tatra tvāṃ gītasampannaṃ kariṣyāmi mahāvratam
tuṃbarośca samaṃ caiva tathātiśayasaṃyutam
tāvatkālaṃ yathāyogaṃ devagandharvayoniṣu
śikṣayasva yathānyāyam ityuktvāntaradhīyata
tato muniḥ praṇamyainaṃ tathātiśayasaṃyutam
devarṣirdevasaṃkāśaḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ
tapasāṃ nidhiratyantaṃ vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ
skandhe vipañcīmāsādya sarvalokāṃścacāra saḥ
vāruṇaṃ yāmyam āgneyam aindraṃ kauberameva ca
vāyavyaṃ ca tatheśānaṃ saṃsadaṃ prāpya dharmavit
gāyamāno hariṃ samyagvīṇāvādavicakṣaṇaḥ
gandharvāpsarasāṃ saṃghaiḥ pūjyamānas tatastataḥ
brahmalokaṃ samāsādya kasmiṃścitkālaparyaye
hāhāhūhūśca gandharvau gītavādyaviśāradau
brahmaṇo gāyakau divyau nityau gandharvasattamau
tatra tābhyāṃ samāsādya gāyamāno hariṃ prabhum
brahmaṇā ca mahātejāḥ pūjito munisattamaḥ
taṃ praṇamya mahātmānaṃ sarvalokapitāmaham
cacāra ca yathākāmaṃ sarvalokeṣu nāradaḥ
tataḥ kālena mahatā gṛhaṃ prāpya ca tumbaroḥ
vīṇāmādāya tatrastho hyagāyata mahāmuniḥ
svarakalpāstu tatrasthāḥ ṣaḍjādyāḥ sapta vai matāḥ
krīḍato bhagavāndṛṣṭvā nirgataśca susatvaram
śikṣayāmāsa bahuśastatra tatra mahāmatiḥ
śramayogena saṃyukto nārado'pi mahāmuniḥ
saptasvarāṅganāḥ paśyan gānavidyāviśāradaḥ
āsīdvīṇā samāyoge na tāstantryaḥ prapedire
tato raivatake kṛṣṇaṃ praṇipatya mahāmuniḥ
vijñāpayadaśeṣaṃ tu śvetadvīpe tu yat purā
nārāyaṇena kathitaṃ gānayogamanuttamam
tacchrutvā prāhasankṛṣṇaḥ prāha jāṃbavatīṃ mudā
etaṃ munivaraṃ bhadre śikṣayasva yathāvidhi
vīṇāgānasamāyoge tathetyuktvā ca sā harim
prahasantī yathāyogaṃ śikṣayāmāsa taṃ munim
tataḥ saṃvatsare pūrṇe punarāgamya mādhavam
praṇipatyāgratastasthau punarāha sa keśavaḥ
satyāṃ samīpamāgaccha śikṣayasva yathāvidhi
tathetyuktvā satyabhāmāṃ praṇipatyajagau muniḥ
tayā sa śikṣito vidvān pūrṇe saṃvatsare punaḥ
vāsudevaniyukto 'sau rukmiṇīsadanaṃ gataḥ
aṅganābhistatastābhirdāsībhirmunisattamaḥ
ukto 'sau gāyamāno'pi na svaraṃ vetsi vai mune
tataḥ śrameṇa mahatā vatsaratrayasaṃyutam
śikṣito'sau tadā devyā rukmiṇyāpi jagau muniḥ
tataḥ svarāṅganāḥ prāpya tantrīyogaṃ mahāmuneḥ
āhūya kṛṣṇo bhagavān svayameva mahāmunim
aśikṣayadameyātmā gānayogamanuttamam
tato 'tiśayamāpannas tumbaror munisattamaḥ
tato nanarta devarṣiḥ praṇipatya janārdanam
uvāca ca hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarvajñastvaṃ mahāmune
prahasya gānayogena gāyasva mama sannidhau
etatte prārthitaṃ prāptaṃ mama loke tathaiva ca
nityaṃ tumbaruṇā sārdhaṃ gāyasva ca yathātatham
evamukto munistatra yathāyogaṃ cacāra saḥ
yadā sampūjayan kṛṣṇo rudraṃ bhuvananāyakam
tadā jagau harestasya niyogācchaṅkarāya vai
rukmiṇyā saha satyā ca jāṃbavatyā mahāmuniḥ
kṛṣṇena ca nṛpaśreṣṭha śrutijātiviśāradaḥ
eṣa vo muniśārdūlāḥ prokto gītakramo muneḥ
brāhmaṇo vāsudevākhyāṃ gāyamāno bhṛśaṃ nṛpa
hareḥ sālokyamāpnoti rudragāno 'dhiko bhavet
anyathā narakaṃ gacched gāyamāno 'nyadeva hi
karmaṇā manasā vācā vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ
gāyan śṛṇvaṃstamāpnoti tasmādgeyaṃ paraṃ viduḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge vaiṣṇavagītakathanaṃ nāma tṛtīyo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
vaiṣṇavā iti ye proktā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ
kāni cihnāni teṣāṃ vai tanno brūhi mahāmate
teṣāṃ vā kiṃ karotyeṣa bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ
etanme sarvamācakṣva sūta sarvārthavittama
sūta uvāca
aṃbarīṣeṇa vai pṛṣṭo mārkaṇḍeyaḥ purā muniḥ
yuṣmābhir adya yat proktaṃ tadvadāmi yathātatham
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu rājanyathānyāyaṃ yanmāṃ tvaṃ paripṛcchasi
yatrāste viṣṇubhaktastu tatra nārāyaṇaḥ sthitaḥ
viṣṇureva hi sarvatra yeṣāṃ vai devatā smṛtā
kīrtyamāne harau nityaṃ romāñco yasya vartate
kaṃpaḥ svedas tathākṣeṣu dṛśyante jalabindavaḥ
viṣṇubhaktisamāyuktān śrautasmārtapravartakān
prīto bhavati yo dṛṣṭvā vaiṣṇavo 'sau prakīrtitaḥ
nānyadācchādayedvastraṃ vaiṣṇavo jagato raṇe
viṣṇubhaktam athāyāntaṃ yo dṛṣṭvā saṃmukhasthitaḥ
praṇāmādi karotyevaṃ vāsudeve yathā tathā
sa vai bhakta iti jñeyaḥ sa jayī syājjagattraye
rūkṣākṣarāṇi śṛṇvanvai tathā bhāgavateritaḥ
praṇāmapūrvaṃ kṣāntyā vai yo vadedvaiṣṇavo hi saḥ
gandhapuṣpādi kiṃ sarvaṃ śirasā yo hi dhārayet
hareḥ sarvamitītyevaṃ matvāsau vaiṣṇavaḥ smṛtaḥ
viṣṇukṣetre śubhānyeva karoti snehasaṃyutaḥ
pratimāṃ ca harernityaṃ pūjayetprayatātmavān
viṣṇubhaktaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ karmaṇā manasā girā
nārāyaṇaparo nityaṃ mahābhāgavato hi saḥ
bhojanārādhanaṃ sarvaṃ yathāśaktyā karoti yaḥ
viṣṇubhaktasya ca sadā yathānyāyaṃ hi kathyate
nārāyaṇaparo vidvān yasyānnaṃ prītamānasaḥ
aśnāti taddharerāsyaṃ gatamannaṃ na saṃśayaḥ
svārcanādapi viśvātmā prīto bhavati mādhavaḥ
mahābhāgavate tacca dṛṣṭvāsau bhaktavatsalaḥ
vāsudevaparaṃ dṛṣṭvā vaiṣṇavaṃ dagdhakilbiṣam
devāpi bhītāstaṃ yānti praṇipatya yathāgatam
śrūyatāṃ hi purāvṛttaṃ viṣṇubhaktasya vaibhavam
dṛṣṭvā yamo 'pi vai bhaktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ dagdhakilbiṣam
utthāya prāñjalirbhūtvā nanāma bhṛgunandanam
tasmāt sampūjayed bhaktyā vaiṣṇavān viṣṇuvannaraḥ
sa yāti viṣṇusāmīpyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
anyabhaktasahasrebhyo viṣṇubhakto viśiṣyate
viṣṇubhaktasahasrebhyo rudrabhakto viśiṣyate
rudrabhaktātparataro nāsti loke na saṃśayaḥ
tasmāttu vaiṣṇavaṃ cāpi rudrabhaktamathāpi vā
pūjayetsarvayatnena dharmakāmārthamuktaye
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge viṣṇubhaktakathanaṃ nāma caturtho 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
aikṣvākur aṃbarīṣo vai vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ
pālayāmāsa pṛthivīṃ viṣṇorājñāpuraḥsaraḥ
śrutametanmahābuddhe tatsarvaṃ vaktumarhasi
nityaṃ tasya hareścakraṃ śatrurogabhayādikam
hantīti śrūyate loke dhārmikasya mahātmanaḥ
aṃbarīṣasya caritaṃ tatsarvaṃ brūhi sattama
māhātmyamanubhāvaṃ ca bhaktiyogamanuttamam
yathāvacchrotumicchāmaḥ sūta vaktuṃ tvamarhasi
sūta uvāca
śrūyatāṃ muniśārdūlāścaritaṃ tasya dhīmataḥ
aṃbarīṣasya māhātmyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ param
triśaṅkordayitā bhāryā sarvalakṣaṇaśobhitā
aṃbarīṣasya jananī nityaṃ śaucasamanvitā
yoganidrāsamārūḍhaṃ śeṣaparyaṅkaśāyinam
nārāyaṇaṃ mahātmānaṃ brahmāṇḍakamalodbhavam
tamasā kālarudrākhyaṃ rajasā kanakāṇḍajam
sattvena sarvagaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam
arcayāmāsa satataṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ
mālyadānādikaṃ sarvaṃ svayamevamacīkarat
gandhādipeṣaṇaṃ caiva dhūpadravyādikaṃ tathā
bhūmerālepanādīni haviṣāṃ pacanaṃ tathā
tatkautukasamāviṣṭā svayameva cakāra sā
śubhā padmāvatī nityaṃ vācā nārāyaṇeti vai
anantetyeva sā nityaṃ bhāṣamāṇā pativratā
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tatpareṇāntarātmanā
arcayāmāsa govindaṃ gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ śuciḥ
viṣṇubhaktānmahābhāgān sarvapāpavivarjitān
dānamānārcanairnityaṃ dhanaratnairatoṣayat
tataḥ kadācitsā devī dvādaśīṃ samupoṣya vai
hareragre mahābhāgā suṣvāpa patinā saha
tatra nārāyaṇo devastāmāha puruṣottamaḥ
kim icchasi varaṃ bhadre mattas tvam brūhi bhāmini
sā dṛṣṭvā tu varaṃ vavre putro me vaiṣṇavo bhavet
sārvabhaumo mahātejāḥ svakarmanirataḥ śuciḥ
tathetyuktvā dadau tasyai phalam ekaṃ janārdanaḥ
sā prabuddhā phalaṃ dṛṣṭvā bhartre sarvaṃ nyavedayat
bhakṣayāmāsa saṃhṛṣṭā phalaṃ tadgatamānasā
tataḥ kālena sā devī putraṃ kulavivardhanam
asūta sā sadācāraṃ vāsudevaparāyaṇam
śubhalakṣaṇasampannaṃ cakrāṅkitatanūruham
jātaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitā putraṃ kriyāḥ sarvāścakāra vai
aṃbarīṣa iti khyāto loke samabhavatprabhuḥ
pitaryuparate śrīmānabhiṣikto mahāmuniḥ
mantriṣvādhāya rājyaṃ ca tapa ugraṃ cakāra saḥ
saṃvatsarasahasraṃ vai japannārāyaṇaṃ prabhum
hṛtpuṇḍarīkamadhyasthaṃ sūryamaṇḍalamadhyataḥ
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadhārayantaṃ caturbhujam
śuddhajāṃbūnadanibhaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ pītāṃbaradharaṃ prabhum
śrīvatsavakṣasaṃ devaṃ puruṣaṃ puruṣottamam
tato garuḍamāruhya sarvadevairabhiṣṭutaḥ
ājagāma sa viśvātmā sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ
airāvatamivācintyaṃ kṛtvā vai garuḍaṃ hariḥ
svayaṃ śakra ivāsīnastamāha nṛpasattamam
indro 'hamasmi bhadraṃ te kiṃ dadāmi varaṃ ca te
sarvalokeśvaro 'haṃ tvāṃ rakṣituṃ samupāgataḥ
aṃbarīṣa uvāca
nāhaṃ tvam abhisaṃdhāya tapa āsthitavāniha
tvayā dattaṃ ca neṣyāmi gaccha śakra yathāsukham
mama nārāyaṇo nāthastaṃ namāmi jagatpatim
gacchendra mā kṛthāstvatra mama buddhivilopanam
tataḥ prahasya bhagavān svarūpam akaroddhariḥ
śārṅgacakragadāpāṇiḥ khaḍgahasto janārdanaḥ
garuḍopari sarvātmā nīlācala ivāparaḥ
devagandharvasaṃghaiśca stūyamānaḥ samantataḥ
praṇamya sa ca saṃtuṣṭastuṣṭāva garuḍadhvajam
prasīda lokanātheśa mama nātha janārdana
kṛṣṇa viṣṇo jagannātha sarvalokanamaskṛta
tvamādistvamanādistvamanantaḥ pūruṣaḥ prabhuḥ
aprameyo vibhurviṣṇurgovindaḥ kamalekṣaṇaḥ
maheśvarāṅgajo madhye puṣkaraḥ khagamaḥ khagaḥ
kavyavāhaḥ kapālī tvaṃ havyavāhaḥ prabhañjanaḥ
ādidevaḥ kriyānandaḥ paramātmātmani sthitaḥ
tvāṃ prapanno'smi govinda jaya devakinandana
jaya deva jagannātha pāhi māṃ puṣkarekṣaṇa
nānyā gatistvadanyā me tvameva śaraṇaṃ mama
sūta uvāca
tamāha bhagavānviṣṇuḥ kiṃ te hṛdi cikīrṣitam
tatsarvaṃ te pradāsyāmi bhakto'si mama suvrata
bhaktipriyo 'haṃ satataṃ tasmāddātumihāgataḥ
aṃbarīṣa uvāca
lokanātha parānanda nityaṃ me vartate matiḥ
vāsudevaparo nityaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ
yathā tvaṃ devadevasya bhavasya paramātmanaḥ
tathā bhavāmyahaṃ viṣṇo tava deva janārdana
pālayiṣyāmi pṛthivīṃ kṛtvā vai vaiṣṇavaṃ jagat
yajñahomārcanaiścaiva tarpayāmi surottamān
vaiṣṇavānpālayiṣyāmi nihaniṣyāmi śātravān
lokatāpabhaye bhīta iti me dhīyate matiḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
evamastu yathecchaṃ vai cakrametatsudarśanam
purā rudraprasādena labdhaṃ vai durlabhaṃ mayā
ṛṣiśāpādikaṃ duḥkhaṃ śatrurogādikaṃ tathā
nihaniṣyati te nityamityuktvāntaradhīyata
sūta uvāca
tataḥ praṇamya mudito rājā nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum
praviśya nagarīṃ ramyāmayodhyāṃ paryapālayat
brāhmaṇādīṃśca varṇāṃśca svasvakarmaṇy ayojayat
nārāyaṇaparo nityaṃ viṣṇubhaktānakalmaṣān
pālayāmāsa hṛṣṭātmā viśeṣeṇa janādhipaḥ
aśvamedhaśatairiṣṭvā vājapeyaśatena ca
pālayāmāsa pṛthivīṃ sāgarāvaraṇāmimām
gṛhe gṛhe haristasthau vedaghoṣo gṛhe gṛhe
nāmaghoṣo hareścaiva yajñaghoṣastathaiva ca
abhavannṛpaśārdūle tasmin rājyaṃ praśāsati
nāsasyā nātṛṇā bhūmirna durbhikṣādibhiryutā
rāgahīnāḥ prajā nityaṃ sarvopadravavarjitāḥ
aṃbarīṣo mahātejāḥ pālayāmāsa medinīm
tasyaivaṃvartamānasya kanyā kamalalocanā
śrīmatī nāma vikhyātā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutā
pradānasamayaṃ prāptā devamāyeva śobhanā
tasminkāle muniḥ śrīmānnārado 'bhyāgataścavai
aṃbarīṣasya rājño vai parvataśca mahāmatiḥ
tāvubhāvāgatau dṛṣṭvā praṇipatya yathāvidhi
aṃbarīṣo mahātejāḥ pūjayāmāsa tāv ṛṣī
kanyāṃ tāṃ ramamāṇāṃ vai meghamadhye śatahradām
prāha tāṃ prekṣya bhagavān nāradaḥ sasmitas tadā
keyaṃ rājanmahābhāgā kanyā surasutopamā
brūhi dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭha sarvalakṣaṇaśobhitā
rājovāca
duhiteyaṃ mama vibho śrīmatī nāma nāmataḥ
pradānasamayaṃ prāptā varamanveṣate śubhā
ityukto muniśārdūlastāmaicchannārado dvijāḥ
parvato'pi munistāṃ vai cakame munisattamāḥ
anujñāpya ca rājānaṃ nārado vākyamabravīt
rahasyāhūya dharmātmā mama dehi sutāmimām
parvato hi tathā prāha rājānaṃ rahasi prabhuḥ
tāvubhau saha dharmātmā praṇipatya bhayārditaḥ
ubhau bhavantau kanyāṃ me prārthayānau kathaṃ tvaham
kariṣyāmi mahāprājña śṛṇu nārada me vacaḥ
tvaṃ ca parvata me vākyaṃ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi yatprabho
kanyeyaṃ yuvayorekaṃ varayiṣyati cecchubhā
tasmai kanyāṃ prayacchāmi nānyathā śaktirasti me
tathetyuktvā tato bhūyaḥ śvo yāsyāva iti sma ha
ityuktvā muniśārdūlau jagmatuḥ prītimānasau
vāsudevaparau nityamubhau jñānavidāṃvarau
viṣṇulokaṃ tato gatvā nārado munisattamaḥ
praṇipatya hṛṣīkeśaṃ vākyametaduvāca ha
śrotavyamasti bhagavannātha nārāyaṇa prabho
rahasi tvāṃ pravakṣyāmi namaste bhuvaneśvara
tataḥ prahasya govindaḥ sarvānutsārya taṃ munim
brūhītyāha ca viśvātmā munirāha ca keśavam
tvadīyo nṛpatiḥ śrīmānaṃbarīṣo mahīpatiḥ
tasya kanyā viśālākṣī śrīmatī nāma nāmataḥ
pariṇetumanās tatra gato 'smi vacanaṃ śṛṇu
parvato 'yaṃ muniḥ śrīmāṃstava bhṛtyastaponidhiḥ
tāmaicchat so'pi bhagavannāvāmāha janādhipaḥ
aṃbarīṣo mahātejāḥ kanyeyaṃ yuvayorvaram
lāvaṇyayuktaṃ vṛṇuyādyadi tasmai dadāmyaham
ityāhāvāṃ nṛpastatra tathetyuktvāhamāgataḥ
āgamiṣyāmi te rājan śvaḥ prabhāte gṛhaṃ tviti
āgato'haṃ jagannātha kartumarhasi me priyam
vānarānanavadbhāti parvatasya mukhaṃ yathā
tathā kuru jagannātha mama cedicchasi priyam
tathetyuktvā sa govindaḥ prahasya madhusūdanaḥ
tvayoktaṃ ca kariṣyāmi gaccha saumya yathāgatam
evamuktvā munirhṛṣṭaḥ praṇipatya janārdanam
manyamānaḥ kṛtātmānaṃ tathāyodhyāṃ jagāma saḥ
gate munivare tasminparvato 'pi mahāmuniḥ
praṇamya mādhavaṃ hṛṣṭo rahasyenamuvāca ha
vṛttaṃ tasya nivedyāgre nāradasya jagatpate
golāṅgūlamukhaṃ yadvanmukhaṃ bhāti tathā kuru
tacchrutvā bhagavānviṣṇustvayoktaṃ ca karomi vai
gaccha śīghramayodhyāṃ vai māvedīr nāradasya vai
tvayā me saṃvidaṃ tatra tathetyuktvā jagāma saḥ
tato rājā samājñāya prāptau munivarau tadā
māṅgalyairvividhaiḥ sarvāmayodhyāṃ dhvajamālinīm
maṇḍayāmāsa puṣpaiśca lājaiścaiva samantataḥ
aṃbusiktagṛhadvārāṃ siktāpaṇamahāpathām
divyagandharasopetāṃ dhūpitāṃ divyadhūpakaiḥ
kṛtvā ca nagarīṃ rājā maṇḍayāmāsa tāṃ sabhām
divyairgandhaistathā dhūpai ratnaiśca vividhaistathā
alaṃkṛtāṃ maṇistaṃbhairnānāmālyopaśobhitām
parārdhyāstaraṇopetair divyair bhadrāsanair vṛtām
kṛtvā nṛpendrastāṃ kanyāṃ hyādāya praviveśa ha
sarvābharaṇasampannāṃ śrīrivāyatalocanām
karasaṃmitamadhyāṅgīṃ pañcasnigdhāṃ śubhānanām
strībhiḥ parivṛtāṃ divyāṃ śrīmatīṃ saṃśritāṃ tadā
sabhā ca sā bhūpateḥ samṛddhā maṇipravekottamaratnacitrā
nyastāsanā mālyavatī subaddhā tāmāyayuste nararājavargāḥ
athāparo brahmavarātmajo hi traividyavidyo bhagavānmahātmā
saparvato brahmavidāṃ variṣṭho mahāmunirnārada ājagāma
tāvāgatau samīkṣyātha rājā saṃbhrāntamānasaḥ
divyamāsanam ādāya pūjayāmāsa tāvubhau
ubhau devarṣisiddhau tau ubhau jñānavidāṃ varau
samāsīnau mahātmānau kanyārthaṃ munisattamau
tāvubhau praṇipatyāgre kanyāṃ tāṃ śrīmatīṃ śubhām
sutāṃ kamalapatrākṣīṃ prāha rājā yaśasvinīm
anayoryaṃ varaṃ bhadre manasā tvam ihecchasi
tasmai mālām imāṃ dehi praṇipatya yathāvidhi
evamuktā tu sā kanyā strībhiḥ parivṛtā tadā
mālāṃ hiraṇmayīṃ divyāmādāya śubhalocanā
yatrāsīnau mahātmānau tatrāgamya sthitā tadā
vīkṣamāṇā muniśreṣṭhau nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā
śākhāmṛgānanaṃ dṛṣṭvā nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā
golāṅgulamukhaṃ kanyā kiṃcit trāsasamanvitā
saṃbhrāntamānasā tatra pravātakadalī yathā
tasthau tām āha rājāsau vatse kiṃ tvaṃ kariṣyasi
anayor ekam uddiśya dehi mālāmimāṃ śubhe
sā prāha pitaraṃ trastā imau tau naravānarau
muniśreṣṭhaṃ na paśyāmi nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā
anayor madhyatas tvekam ūnaṣoḍaśavārṣikam
sarvābharaṇasampannam atasīpuṣpasaṃnibham
dīrghabāhuṃ viśālākṣaṃ tuṅgīrasthalam uttamam
rekhāṅkitakaṭigrīvaṃ raktāntāyatalocanam
namracāpānukaraṇapaṭubhrūyugaśobhitam
vibhaktatrivalīvyaktaṃ nābhivyaktaśubhodaram
hiraṇyāṃbarasaṃvītaṃ tuṅgaratnanakhaṃ śubham
padmākārakaraṃ tvenaṃ padmāsyaṃ padmalocanam
sunāsaṃ padmahṛdayaṃ padmanābhaṃ śriyā vṛtam
dantapaṅktibhiratyarthaṃ kundakuḍmalasannibhaiḥ
hasantaṃ māṃ samālokya dakṣiṇaṃ ca prasārya vai
pāṇiṃ sthitamamuṃ tatra paśyāmi śubhamūrdhajam
saṃbhrāntamānasāṃ tatra vepatīṃ kadalīmiva
sthitāṃ tāmāha rājāsau vatse kiṃ tvaṃ kariṣyasi
evamukte muniḥ prāha nāradaḥ saṃśayaṃ gataḥ
kiyanto bāhavastasya kanye brūhi yathātatham
bāhudvayaṃ ca paśyāmītyāha kanyā śucismitā
prāha tāṃ parvatastatra tasya vakṣaḥsthale śubhe
kiṃ paśyasi ca me brūhi kare kiṃ vāsya paśyasi
kanyā tamāha mālāṃ vai pañcarūpāmanuttamām
vakṣaḥsthale 'sya paśyāmi kare kārmukasāyakān
evamuktau muniśreṣṭhau parasparamanuttamau
manasā cintayantau tau māyeyaṃ kasyacid bhavet
māyāvī taskaro nūnaṃ svayameva janārdanaḥ
āgato na yathā kuryātkatham asmanmukhaṃ tvidam
golāṅgūlatvamityevaṃ cintayāmāsa nāradaḥ
parvato'pi yathānyāyaṃ vānaratvaṃ kathaṃ mama
prāptamityeva manasā cintāmāpedivāṃstathā
tato rājā praṇamyāsau nāradaṃ parvataṃ tathā
bhavadbhyāṃ kimidaṃ tatra kṛtaṃ buddhivimohajam
svasthau bhavantau tiṣṭhetāṃ yathā kanyārtham udyatau
evamuktau muniśreṣṭhau nṛpamūcaturulbaṇau
tvameva mohaṃ kuruṣe nāvāmiha kathañcana
āvayorekameṣā te varayatveva māciram
tataḥ sā kanyakā bhūyaḥ praṇipatyeṣṭadevatām
māyāmādāya tiṣṭhantaṃ tayormadhye samāhitam
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktam atasīpuṣpasannibham
dīrghabāhuṃ supuṣṭāṅgaṃ karṇāntāyatalocanam
pūrvavatpuruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā mālāṃ tasmai dadau hi sā
anantaraṃ hi sā kanyā na dṛṣṭā manujaiḥ punaḥ
tato nādaḥ samabhavat kimetaditi vismitau
tāmādāya gato viṣṇuḥ svasthānaṃ puruṣottamaḥ
purā tadarthamaniśaṃ tapastaptvā varāṅganā
śrīmatī sā samutpannā sā gatā ca tathā harim
tāvubhau muniśārdūlau dhikkṛtāvatiduḥkhitau
vāsudevaṃ prati tadā jagmaturbhavanaṃ hareḥ
tāvāgatau samīkṣyāha śrīmatīṃ bhagavānhariḥ
muniśreṣṭhau samāyātau gūha svātmānamatra vai
tathetyuktvā ca sā devī prahasantī cakāra ha
nāradaḥ praṇipatyāgre prāha dāmodaraṃ harim
priyaṃ hi kṛtavānadya mama tvaṃ parvatasya hi
tvameva nūnaṃ govinda kanyāṃ tāṃ hṛtavān asi
vimohyāvāṃ svayaṃ buddhyā pratārya surasattama
ityuktaḥ puruṣo viṣṇuḥ pidhāya śrotramacyutaḥ
pāṇibhyāṃ prāha bhagavān bhavadbhyāṃ kimudīritam
kāmavānapi bhāvo'yaṃ munivṛttiraho kila
evamukto muniḥ prāha vāsudevaṃ sa nāradaḥ
karṇamūle mama kathaṃ golāṅgūlamukhaṃ tviti
karṇamūle tamāhedaṃ vānaratvaṃ kṛtaṃ mayā
parvatasya mayā vidvan golāṅgūlamukhaṃ tava
mayā tava kṛtaṃ tatra priyārthaṃ nānyathā tviti
parvato 'pi tathā prāha tasyāpyevaṃ jagāda saḥ
śṛṇvatorubhayostatra prāha dāmodaro vacaḥ
priyaṃ bhavadbhyāṃ kṛtavān satyenātmānamālabhe
nāradaḥ prāha dharmātmā āvayormadhyataḥ sthitaḥ
dhanuṣmān puruṣaḥ ko 'tra tāṃ hṛtvā gatavānkila
tac chrutvā vāsudevo 'sau prāha tau munisattamau
māyāvino mahātmāno bahavaḥ santi sattamāḥ
tatra sā śrīmatī nūnam adṛṣṭvā munisattamau
cakrapāṇirahaṃ nityaṃ caturbāhuriti sthitaḥ
tāṃ tathā nāhamaicchaṃ vai bhavadbhyāṃ viditaṃ hi tat
ityuktau praṇipatyainamūcatuḥ prītimānasau
ko 'tra doṣastava vibho nārāyaṇa jagatpate
daurātmyaṃ tannṛpasyaiva māyāṃ hi kṛtavānasau
ityuktvā jagmatustasmānmunīnāradaparvatau
aṃbarīṣaṃ samāsādya śāpenainamayojayat
nāradaḥ parvataścaiva yasmādāvāmihāgatau
āhūya paścādanyasmai kanyāṃ tvaṃ dattavānasi
māyāyogena tasmāttvāṃ tamo hyabhibhaviṣyati
tena cātmānamatyarthaṃ yathāvattvaṃ ca vetsyasi
evaṃ śāpe pradatte tu tamorāśirathotthitaḥ
nṛpaṃ prati tataścakraṃ viṣṇoḥ prādurabhūt kṣaṇāt
cakravitrāsitaṃ ghoraṃ tāvubhau tamo 'bhyagāt
tataḥ saṃtrastasarvāṅgau dhāvamānau mahāmunī
pṛṣṭhataścakramālokya tamorāśiṃ durāsadam
kanyāsiddhiraho prāptā hyāvayoriti vegitau
lokālokāntamaniśaṃ dhāvamānau bhayārditau
trāhi trāhīti govindaṃ bhāṣamāṇau bhayārditau
viṣṇulokaṃ tato gatvā nārāyaṇa jagatpate
vāsudeva hṛṣīkeśa padmanābha janārdana
trāhyāvāṃ puṇḍarīkākṣa nātho 'si puruṣottama
tato nārāyaṇaścintya śrīmāñchrīvatsalāñchanaḥ
nivārya cakraṃ dhvāntaṃ ca bhaktānugrahakāmyayā
aṃbarīṣaśca madbhaktastathaitau munisattamau
anayorasya ca tathā hitaṃ kāryaṃ mayādhunā
āhūya tattamaḥ śrīmān girā prahlādayan hariḥ
provāca bhagavān viṣṇuḥ śṛṇutāṃ ma idaṃvacaḥ
ṛṣiśāpo na caivāsīdanyathā ca varo mama
datto nṛpāya rakṣārthaṃ nāsti tasyānyathā punaḥ
aṃbarīṣasya putrasya naptuḥ putro mahāyaśāḥ
śrīmān daśaratho nāma rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ
tasyāhamagrajaḥ putro rāmanāmā bhavāmyaham
tatra me dakṣiṇo bāhur bharato nāma vai bhavet
śatrughno nāma savyaśca śeṣo 'sau lakṣmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ
tatra māṃ samupāgaccha gacchedānīṃ nṛpaṃ vinā
muniśreṣṭhau ca hitvā tvamiti smāha ca mādhavaḥ
evam uktaṃ tamo nāśaṃ tatkṣaṇāc ca jagāma vai
nivāritaṃ hareścakraṃ yathāpūrvamatiṣṭhata
muniśreṣṭhau bhayānmuktau praṇipatya janārdanam
nirgatau śokasaṃtaptau ūcatustau parasparam
adyaprabhṛti dehāntamāvāṃ kanyāparigraham
na kariṣyāva ityuktvā pratijñāya ca tāvṛṣī
yogadhyānaparau śuddhau yathāpūrvaṃ vyavasthitau
aṃbarīṣaśca rājāsau paripālya ca medinīm
sabhṛtyajñātisampanno viṣṇulokaṃ jagāma vai
mānārthamaṃbarīṣasya tathaiva munisiṃhayoḥ
rāmo dāśarathir bhūtvā nātmavedīśvaro 'bhavat
munayaśca tathā sarve bhṛgvādyā munisattamāḥ
māyā na kāryā vidvadbhirityāhuḥ prekṣya taṃ harim
nāradaḥ parvataścaiva ciraṃ jñātvā viceṣṭitam
māyāṃ viṣṇorvinindyaiva rudrabhaktau babhūvatuḥ
etaddhi kathitaṃ sarvaṃ mayā yuṣmākamadya vai
aṃbarīṣasya māhātmyaṃ māyāvitvaṃ ca vai hareḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvāpi mānavaḥ
māyāṃ visṛjya puṇyātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati
idaṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ puṇyaṃ vedairudīritam
sāyaṃ prātaḥ paṭhennityaṃ viṣṇoḥ sāyujyamāpnuyāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge śrīmatyākhyānaṃ nāma pañcamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
māyāvitvaṃ śrutaṃ viṣṇordevadevasya dhīmataḥ
kathaṃ jyeṣṭhāsamutpattir devadevājjanārdanāt
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ lomaharṣaṇa tattvataḥ
sūta uvāca
anādinidhanaḥ śrīmāndhātā nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ
jagaddvaidhamidaṃ cakre mohanāya jagatpatiḥ
viṣṇurvai brāhmaṇānvedānvedadharmān sanātanān
śriyaṃ padmāṃ tathā śreṣṭhāṃ bhāgamekamakārayat
jyeṣṭhāmalakṣmīmaśubhāṃ vedabāhyān narādhamān
adharmaṃ ca mahātejā bhāgamekam akalpayat
alakṣmīmagrataḥ sṛṣṭvā paścātpadmāṃ janārdanaḥ
jyeṣṭhā tena samākhyātā alakṣmīrdvijasattamāḥ
amṛtodbhavavelāyāṃ viṣānantaramulbaṇāt
aśubhā sā tathotpannā jyeṣṭhā iti ca vai śrutam
tataḥ śrīśca samutpannā padmā viṣṇuparigrahaḥ
duḥsaho nāma viprarṣirupayeme 'śubhāṃ tadā
jyeṣṭhāṃ tāṃ paripūrṇo 'sau manasā vīkṣya dhiṣṭhitām
lokaṃ cacāra hṛṣṭātmā tayā saha munistadā
yasmin ghoṣo hareścaiva harasya ca mahātmanaḥ
vedaghoṣastathā viprā homadhūmastathaiva ca
bhasmāṅgino vā yatrāsaṃstatra tatra bhayārditā
pidhāya karṇau saṃyāti dhāvamānā itastataḥ
jyeṣṭhāmevaṃvidhāṃ dṛṣṭvā duḥsaho mohamāgataḥ
tayā saha vanaṃ gatvā cacāra sa mahāmuniḥ
tapo mahadvane ghore yāti kanyā pratigraham
na kariṣyāmi cetyuktvā pratijñāya ca tāmṛṣiḥ
yogajñānaparaḥ śuddho yatra yogīśvaro muniḥ
tatrāyāntaṃ mahātmānaṃ mārkaṇḍeyamapaśyata
praṇipatya mahātmānaṃ duḥsaho munimabravīt
bhāryeyaṃ bhagavanmahyaṃ na sthāsyati kathañcana
kiṃ karomīti viprarṣe hyanayā saha bhāryayā
praviśāmi tathā kutra kuto na praviśāmyaham
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
śṛṇu duḥsaha sarvatra akīrtiraśubhānvitā
alakṣmīratulā ceyaṃ jyeṣṭhā ityabhiśabditā
nārāyaṇaparā yatra vedamārgānusāriṇaḥ
rudrabhaktā mahātmāno bhasmoddhūlitavigrahāḥ
sthitā yatra janā nityaṃ mā viśethāḥ kathañcana
nārāyaṇa hṛṣīkeśa puṇḍarīkākṣa mādhava
acyutānanta govinda vāsudeva janārdana
rudra rudreti rudreti śivāya ca namo namaḥ
namaḥ śivatarāyeti śaṅkarāyeti sarvadā
mahādeva mahādeva mahādeveti kīrtayet
umāyāḥ pataye caiva hiraṇyapataye sadā
hiraṇyabāhave tubhyaṃ vṛṣāṅkāya namo namaḥ
nṛsiṃha vāmanācintya mādhaveti ca ye janāḥ
vakṣyanti satataṃ hṛṣṭā brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāstathā
vaiśyāḥ śūdrāśca ye nityaṃ teṣāṃ dhanagṛhādiṣu
ārāme caiva goṣṭheṣu na viśethāḥ kathañcana
jvālāmālākarālaṃ ca sahasrādityasannibham
cakraṃ viṣṇoratīvograṃ teṣāṃ hanti sadāśubham
svāhākāro vaṣaṭkāro gṛhe yasmin hi vartate
taddhitvā cānyamāgaccha sāmaghoṣe 'tha yatra vā
vedābhyāsaratā nityaṃ nityakarmaparāyaṇāḥ
vāsudevārcanaratā dūratastānvisarjayet
agnihotraṃ gṛhe yeṣāṃ liṅgārcā vā gṛheṣu ca
vāsudevatanurvāpi caṇḍikā yatra tiṣṭhati
dūrato vraja tān hitvā sarvapāpavivarjitān
nityanaimittikairyajñairyajanti ca maheśvaram
tān hitvā vraja cānyatra duḥsaha tvaṃ sahānayā
śrotriyā brāhmaṇā gāvo guravo 'tithayaḥ sadā
rudrabhaktāśca pūjyante yairnityaṃ tānvivarjayet
duḥsaha uvāca
yasminpraveśo yogyo me tadbrūhi munisattama
tvadvākyādbhayanirmukto viśāmyeṣāṃ gṛhe sadā
mārkaṇḍeya uvāca
na śrotriyā dvijā gāvo guravo 'tithayaḥ sadā
yatra bhartā ca bhāryā ca parasparavirodhinau
sabhāryastvaṃ gṛhaṃ tasya viśethā bhayavarjitaḥ
devadevo mahādevo rudrastribhuvaneśvaraḥ
vinindyo yatra bhagavān viśasva bhayavarjitaḥ
vāsudevaratirnāsti yatra nāsti sadāśivaḥ
japahomādikaṃ nāsti bhasma nāsti gṛhe nṛṇām
parvaṇyabhyarcanaṃ nāsti caturdaśyāṃ viśeṣataḥ
kṛṣṇāṣṭamyāṃ ca rudrasya saṃdhyāyāṃ bhasmavarjitāḥ
caturdaśyāṃ mahādevaṃ na yajanti ca yatra vai
viṣṇor nāmavihīnā ye saṃgatāśca durātmabhiḥ
namaḥ kṛṣṇāya śarvāya śivāya parameṣṭhine
brāhmaṇāśca narā mūḍhā na vadanti durātmakāḥ
tatraiva satataṃ vatsa sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
vedaghoṣo na yatrāsti gurupūjādayo na ca
pitṛkarmavihīnāstu sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
rātrau rātrau gṛhe yasmin kalaho vartate mithaḥ
anayā sārdhamaniśaṃ viśa tvaṃ bhayavarjitaḥ
liṅgārcanaṃ yasya nāsti yasya nāsti japādikam
rudrabhaktirvinindā ca tatraiva viśa nirbhayaḥ
atithiḥ śrotriyo vāpi gurur vā vaiṣṇavo'pi vā
na santi yadgṛhe gāvaḥ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
bālānāṃ prekṣamāṇānāṃ yatrādattvā tvabhakṣayan
bhakṣyāṇi tatra saṃhṛṣṭaḥ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
anabhyarcya mahādevaṃ vāsudevamathāpi vā
ahutvā vidhivadyatra tatra nityaṃ samāviśa
pāpakarmaratā mūḍhā dayāhīnāḥ parasparam
gṛhe yasmin samāsante deśe vā tatra saṃviśa
prākārāgāravidhvaṃsā na caiveḍyā kuṭumbinī
tadgṛhaṃ tu samāsādya vasa nityaṃ hi hṛṣṭadhīḥ
yatra kaṇṭakino vṛkṣā yatra niṣpāvavallarī
brahmavṛkṣaśca yatrāsti sabhāryas tvaṃ samāviśa
agastyārkādayo vāpi bandhujīvo gṛheṣu vai
karavīro viśeṣeṇa nandyāvartamathāpi vā
mallikā vā gṛhe yeṣāṃ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
kanyā ca yatra vai vallī drohī vā ca jaṭī gṛhe
bahulā kadalī yatra sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
tālaṃ tamālaṃ bhallātaṃ tittiḍīkhaṇḍameva ca
kadambaḥ khadiraṃ vāpi sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
nyagrodhaṃ vā gṛhe yeṣāmaśvatthaṃ cūtameva vā
uduṃbaraṃ vā panasaṃ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
yasya kākagṛhaṃ niṃbe ārāme vā gṛhe'pi vā
daṇḍinī muṇḍinī vāpi sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
ekā dāsī gṛhe yatra trigavaṃ pañcamāhiṣam
ṣaḍaśvaṃ saptamātaṅgaṃ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
yasya kālī gṛhe devī pretarūpā ca ḍākinī
kṣetrapāle'thavā yatra sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
bhikṣubiṃbaṃ ca vai yasya gṛhe kṣapaṇakaṃ tathā
bauddhaṃ vā biṃbamāsādya tatra pūrṇaṃ samāviśa
śayanāsanakāleṣu bhojanāṭanavṛttiṣu
yeṣāṃ vadati no vāṇī nāmāni ca hareḥ sadā
tadgṛhaṃ te samākhyātaṃ sabhāryasya niveśitum
pāṣaṇḍācāraniratāḥ śrautasmārtabahiṣkṛtāḥ
viṣṇubhaktivinirmuktā mahādevavinindakāḥ
nāstikāśca śaṭhā yatra sabhāryas tvaṃ samāviśa
sarvasmādadhikatvaṃ ye na vadanti pinākinaḥ
sādhāraṇaṃ smarantyenaṃ sabhāryastvaṃ samāviśa
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śakraḥ sarvasureśvaraḥ
rudraprasādajāśceti na vadanti durātmakāḥ
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ śakraśca sama eva ca
vadanti mūḍhāḥ khadyotaṃ bhānuṃ vā mūḍhacetasaḥ
teṣāṃ gṛhe tathā kṣetra āvāse vā sadānayā
viśa bhuṅkṣva gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ api pūrṇamananyadhīḥ
ye 'śnanti kevalaṃ mūḍhāḥ pakvamannaṃ vicetasaḥ
snānamaṅgalahīnāś ca teṣāṃ tvaṃ gṛham āviśa
yā nārī śaucavibhraṣṭā dehasaṃskāravarjitā
sarvabhakṣaratā nityaṃ tasyāḥ sthāne samāviśa
malināsyāḥ svayaṃ martyā malināṃbaradhāriṇaḥ
maladantā gṛhasthāśca gṛhe teṣāṃ samāviśa
pādaśaucavinirmuktāḥ saṃdhyākāle ca śāyinaḥ
saṃdhyāyām aśnute ye vai gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa
atyāśanaratā martyā atipānaratā narāḥ
dyūtavādakriyāmūḍhāḥ gṛhe teṣāṃ samāviśa
brahmasvahāriṇo ye cāyogyāṃścaiva yajanti vā
śūdrānnabhojino vāpi gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa
madyapānaratāḥ pāpā māṃsabhakṣaṇatatparāḥ
paradāraratā martyā gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa
parvaṇyanarcābhiratā maithune vā divā ratāḥ
saṃdhyāyāṃ maithunaṃ yeṣāṃ gṛhe teṣāṃ samāviśa
pṛṣṭhato maithunaṃ yeṣāṃ śvānavanmṛgavacca vā
jale vā maithunaṃ kuryāt sabhāryas tvaṃ samāviśa
rajasvalāṃ striyaṃ gaccheccāṇḍālīṃ vā narādhamaḥ
kanyāṃ vā gogṛhe vāpi gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa
bahunā kiṃ pralāpena nityakarmabahiṣkṛtāḥ
rudrabhaktivihīnā ye gṛhaṃ teṣāṃ samāviśa
śṛṅgairdivyauṣadhaiḥ kṣudraiḥ śepha ālipya gacchati
bhagadrāvaṃ karotyasmāt sabhāryas tvaṃ samāviśa
sūta uvāca
ityuktvā sa muniḥ śrīmān nirmārjya nayane tadā
brahmarṣirbrahmasaṃkāśas tatraivāntarddhim ātanot
duḥsahaśca tathoktāni sthānāni ca samīyivān
viśeṣāddevadevasya viṣṇor nindāratātmanām
sabhāryo muniśārdūlaḥ saiṣā jyeṣṭhā iti smṛtā
duḥsahastāmuvācedaṃ taḍāgāśramamantare
āsva tvamatra cāhaṃ vai pravekṣyāmi rasātalam
āvayoḥ sthānamālokya nivāsārthaṃ tataḥ punaḥ
āgamiṣyāmi te pārśvamityuktā tamuvāca sā
kim aśnāmi mahābhāga ko me dāsyati vai balim
ityuktastāṃ muniḥ prāha yāḥ striyastvāṃ yajanti vai
balibhiḥ puṣpadhūpaiśca na tāsāṃ ca gṛhaṃ viśa
ityuktvā tvāviśattatra pātālaṃ bilayogataḥ
adyāpi ca vinirmagno muniḥ sa jalasaṃstare
grāmaparvatabāhyeṣu nityamāste 'śubhā punaḥ
prasaṅgād devadeveśo viṣṇustribhuvaneśvaraḥ
lakṣmyā dṛṣṭastayā lakṣmīḥ sā tamāha janārdanam
bhartā gato mahābāho bilaṃ tyaktvā sa māṃ prabho
anāthāhaṃ jagannātha vṛttiṃ dehi namo'stu te
sūta uvāca
ityukto bhagavānviṣṇuḥ prahasyāha janārdanaḥ
jyeṣṭhāmalakṣmīṃ deveśo mādhavo madhusūdanaḥ
śrīviṣṇuruvāca
ye rudramanaghaṃ śarvaṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam
aṃbāṃ haimavatīṃ vāpi janitrīṃ jagatāmapi
madbhaktānnindayantyatra teṣāṃ vittaṃ tavaiva hi
ye'pi caiva mahādevaṃ vinindyaiva yajanti mām
mūḍhā hyabhāgyā madbhaktā api teṣāṃ dhanaṃ tava
yasyājñayā hyahaṃ brahmā prasādādvartate sadā
ye yajanti vinindyaiva mama vidveṣakārakāḥ
madbhaktā naiva te bhaktā iva vartanti durmadāḥ
teṣāṃ gṛhaṃ dhanaṃ kṣetramiṣṭāpūrtaṃ tavaiva hi
sūta uvāca
ityuktvā tāṃ parityajya lakṣmyālakṣmīṃ janārdanaḥ
jajāpa bhagavān rudram alakṣmīkṣayasiddhaye
tasmātpradeyastasyai ca balirnityaṃmunīśvarāḥ
viṣṇubhaktairna saṃdehaḥ sarvayatnena sarvadā
aṅganābhiḥ sadā pūjyā balibhirvividhairdvijāḥ
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
alakṣmīvṛttamanagho lakṣmīvāllabhate gatim
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge alakṣmīvṛttaṃ nāma ṣaṣṭho 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kiṃ japānmucyate jantuḥ sarvalokabhayādibhiḥ
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ prāpnoti paramāṃ gatim
alakṣmīṃ vātha saṃtyajya gamiṣyati japena vai
lakṣmīvāso bhavenmartyaḥ sūta vaktumihārhasi
sūta uvāca
purā pitāmahenoktaṃ vasiṣṭhāya mahātmane
vakṣye saṃkṣepataḥ sarvaṃ sarvalokahitāya vai
śṛṇvantu vacanaṃ sarve praṇipatya janārdanam
devadevamajaṃ viṣṇuṃ kṛṣṇamacyutamavyayam
sarvapāpaharaṃ śuddhaṃ mokṣadaṃ brahmavādinam
manasā karmaṇā vācā yo vidvānpuṇyakarmakṛt
nārāyaṇaṃ japennityaṃ praṇamya puruṣottamam
svapannārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ gacchannārāyaṇaṃ tathā
bhuñjannārāyaṇaṃ viprāstiṣṭhañjāgratsanātanam
unmiṣannimiṣanvāpi namo nārāyaṇeti vai
bhojyaṃ peyaṃ ca lehyaṃ ca namo nārāyaṇeti ca
abhimantrya spṛśanbhuṅkte sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ prāpnoti ca satāṃ gatim
alakṣmīśca mayā proktā patnī yā duḥsahasya ca
nārāyaṇapadaṃ śrutvā gacchatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
yā lakṣmīrdevadevasya hareḥ kṛṣṇasya vallabhā
gṛhe kṣetre tathāvāse tanau vasati suvratāḥ
āloḍya sarvaśāstrāṇi vicārya ca punaḥ punaḥ
idam ekaṃ suniṣpannaṃ dhyeyo nārāyaṇaḥ sadā
kiṃ tasya bahubhirmantraiḥ kiṃ tasya bahubhirvrataiḥ
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
tasmātsarveṣu kāleṣu namo nārāyaṇeti ca
japetsa yāti viprendrā viṣṇulokaṃ sabāndhavaḥ
anyacca devadevasya śṛṇvantu munisattamāḥ
mantro mayā purābhyastaḥ sarvavedārthasādhakaḥ
dvādaśākṣarasaṃyukto dvādaśātmā purātanaḥ
tasyaiveha ca māhātmyaṃ saṃkṣepātpravadāmi vaḥ
kaściddvijo mahāprājñastapastaptvā kathañcana
putramekaṃ tathotpādya saṃskāraiśca yathākramam
yojayitvā yathākālaṃ kṛtopanayanaṃ punaḥ
adhyāpayāmāsa tadā sa ca novāca kiṃcana
na jihvā spandate tasya duḥkhito 'bhūddvijottamaḥ
vāsudeveti niyatam aitareyo vadatyasau
pitā tasya tathā cānyāṃ pariṇīya yathāvidhi
putrānutpādayāmāsa tathaiva vidhipūrvakam
vedānadhītya sampannā babhūvuḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
aitareyasya sā mātā duḥkhitā śokamūrchitā
uvāca putrāḥ sampannā vedavedāṅgapāragāḥ
brāhmaṇaiḥ pūjyamānā vai modayanti ca mātaram
mama tvaṃ bhāgyahīnāyāḥ putro jāto nirākṛtiḥ
mamātra nidhanaṃ śreyo na kathañcana jīvitam
ityuktaḥ sa ca nirgamya yajñavāṭaṃ jagāma vai
tasminyāte dvijānāṃ tu na mantrāḥ pratipedire
aitareye sthite tatra brāhmaṇā mohitāstadā
tato vāṇī samudbhūtā vāsudeveti kīrtanāt
aitareyasya te viprāḥ praṇipatya yathātatham
pūjāṃcakrus tato yajñaṃ svayameva samāgatam
tataḥ samāpya taṃ yajñamaitareyo dhanādibhiḥ
sarvavedān sadasyāha sa ṣaḍaṅgān samāhitaḥ
tuṣṭuvuśca tathā viprā brahmādyāśca tathā dvijāḥ
sasarjuḥ puṣpavarṣāṇi khecarāḥ siddhacāraṇāḥ
evaṃ samāpya vai yajñamaitareyo dvijottamāḥ
mātaraṃ pūjayitvā tu viṣṇoḥ sthānaṃ jagāma ha
etadvai kathitaṃ sarvaṃ dvādaśākṣaravaibhavam
paṭhatāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ nityaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam
japedyaḥ puruṣo nityaṃ dvādaśākṣaramavyayam
sa yāti divyamatulaṃ viṣṇostatparamaṃ padam
api pāpasamācāro dvādaśākṣaratatparaḥ
prāpnoti paramaṃ sthānaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
kiṃ punarye svadharmasthā vāsudevaparāyaṇāḥ
divyaṃ sthānaṃ mahātmānaḥ prāpnuvantīti suvratāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvādaśākṣarapraśaṃsā nāma saptamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
aṣṭākṣaro dvijaśreṣṭhā namo nārāyaṇeti ca
dvādaśākṣaramantraśca paramaḥ paramātmanaḥ
mantraḥ ṣaḍakṣaro viprāḥ sarvavedārthasaṃcayaḥ
yaścauṃ namaḥ śivāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ
tathā śivatarāyeti divyaḥ pañcākṣaraḥ śubhaḥ
mayaskarāya cetyevaṃ namaste śaṅkarāya ca
saptākṣaro 'yaṃ rudrasya pradhānapuruṣasya vai
brahmā ca bhagavānviṣṇuḥ sarve devāḥ savāsavāḥ
mantrairetairdvijaśreṣṭhā munayaśca yajanti tam
śaṅkaraṃ devadeveśaṃ mayaskaramajodbhavam
śivaṃ ca śaṅkaraṃ rudraṃ devadevamumāpatim
prāhurnamaḥ śivāyeti namaste śaṅkarāya ca
mayaskarāya rudrāya tathā śivatarāya ca
japtvā mucyeta vai vipro brahmahatyādibhiḥ kṣaṇāt
purā kaściddvijaḥ śakto dhundhumūka iti śrutaḥ
āsīttṛtīye tretāyāmāvartte ca manoḥ prabhoḥ
meghavāhanakalpe vai brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ
megho bhūtvā mahādevaṃ kṛttivāsasamīśvaram
bahumānena vai rudraṃ devadevo janārdanaḥ
khinno 'tibhārādrudrasya niḥśvāsocchvāsavarjitaḥ
vijñāpya śitikaṇṭhāya tapaścakre 'mbujekṣaṇaḥ
tapasā paramaiśvaryaṃ balaṃ caiva tathādbhutam
labdhavānparameśānācchaṅkarātparamātmanaḥ
tasmātkalpastadā cāsīnmeghavāhanasaṃjñayā
tasminkalpe muneḥ śāpād dhundhumūkasamudbhavaḥ
dhundhumūkātmajastena durātmā ca babhūva saḥ
dhundhumūkaḥ purāsakto bhāryayā saha mohitaḥ
tasyāṃ vai sthāpito garbhaḥ kāmāsaktena cetasā
amāvāsyāmahanyeva muhūrte rudradaivate
antarvatnī tadā bhāryā muktā tena yathāsukham
asūta sā ca tanayaṃ viśalyākhyā prayatnataḥ
rudre muhūrte mandena vīkṣite munisattamāḥ
mātuḥ pitustathāriṣṭaṃ sa saṃjātastathātmanaḥ
ṛṣī tamūcaturviprā dhundhumūkaṃ mithastadā
mitrāvaruṇanāmānau duṣputra iti sattamau
vasiṣṭhaḥ prāha nīco 'pi prabhāvādvai bṛhaspateḥ
putrastavāsau durbuddhirapi mucyati kilbiṣāt
duḥkhito dhundhumūko 'sau dṛṣṭvā putram avasthitam
jātakarmādikaṃ kṛtvā vidhivatsvayameva ca
adhyāpayāmāsa ca taṃ vidhinaiva dvijottamāḥ
tenādhītaṃ yathānyāyaṃ dhaundhumūkena suvratāḥ
kṛtodvāhastadā gatvā guruśuśrūṣaṇe rataḥ
anenaiva muniśreṣṭhā dhaundhumūkena durmadāt
bhuktvānyāṃ vṛṣalīṃ dṛṣṭvā svabhāryāvad divāniśam
ekaśayyāsanagato dhaundhumūko dvijādhamaḥ
tathā cacāra durbuddhistyaktvā dharmagatiṃ parām
mādhvī pītā tayā sārdhaṃ tena rāgavivṛddhaye
kenāpi kāraṇenaiva tām uddiśya dvijottamāḥ
nihatā sā ca pāpena vṛṣalī gatamaṅgalā
tatastasyāstadā tasya bhrātṛbhirnihataḥ pitā
mātā ca tasya durbuddher dhaundhumūkasya śobhanā
bhāryā ca tasya durbuddheḥ śyālāste cāpi suvratāḥ
rājñā kṣaṇādaho naṣṭaṃ kulaṃ tasyāśca tasya ca
gatvāsau dhaundhumūkaśca yena kenāpi līlayā
dṛṣṭvā tu taṃ muniśreṣṭhaṃ rudrajāpyaparāyaṇam
labdhvā pāśupataṃ tadvai purā devānmaheśvarāt
labdhvā pañcākṣaraṃ caiva ṣaḍakṣaramanuttamam
punaḥ pañcākṣaraṃ caiva japtvā lakṣaṃ pṛthak pṛthak
vrataṃ kṛtvā ca vidhinā divyaṃ dvādaśamāsikam
kāladharmaṃ gataḥ kalpe pūjitaśca yamena vai
uddhṛtā ca tathā mātā pitā śyālāśca suvratāḥ
patnī ca subhagā jātā susmitā ca pativratā
tābhir vimānam āruhya devaiḥ sendrair abhiṣṭutaḥ
gāṇapatyam anuprāpya rudrasya dayito 'bhavat
tasmād aṣṭākṣarānmantrāt tathā vai dvādaśākṣarāt
bhavetkoṭiguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
tasmājjapeddhiyo nityaṃ prāguktena vidhānataḥ
śaktibījasamāyuktaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ kathāsarvasvamuttamam
yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādvāpi śrāvayedvā dvijottamān
sa yāti brahmalokaṃ tu rudrajāpyamanuttamam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge aṣṭamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
devaiḥ purā kṛtaṃ divyaṃ vrataṃ pāśupataṃ śubham
brahmaṇā ca svayaṃ sūta kṛṣṇenākliṣṭakarmaṇā
patitena ca vipreṇa dhaundhumūkena vai tathā
kṛtvā japtvā gatiḥ prāptā kathaṃ pāśupataṃ vratam
kathaṃ paśupatirdevaḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ paraṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
sūta uvāca
purā śāpādvinirmukto brahmaputro mahāyaśāḥ
rudrasya devadevasya marudeśādihāgataḥ
tyaktvā prasādādrudrasya uṣṭradehamajājñayā
śilādaputramāsādya namaskṛtya vidhānataḥ
merupṛṣṭhe munivaraḥ śrutvā dharmamanuttamam
māheśvaraṃ muniśreṣṭhā hyapṛcchacca punaḥ punaḥ
nandinaṃ praṇipatyainaṃ kathaṃ paśupatiḥ prabhuḥ
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ tatsarvaṃ ca tadāha saḥ
tatsarvaṃ śrutavān vyāsaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ
tasmād aham upaśrutya yuṣmākaṃ pravadāmi vai
sarve śṛṇvantu vacanaṃ namaskṛtvā maheśvaram
sanatkumāra uvāca
kathaṃ paśupatirdevaḥ paśavaḥ ke prakīrtitāḥ
kaiḥ pāśaiste nibadhyante vimucyante ca te katham
śailādir uvāca
sanatkumāra vakṣyāmi sarvam etad yathātatham
rudrabhaktasya śāntasya tava kalyāṇacetasaḥ
brahmādyāḥ sthāvarāntāśca devadevasya dhīmataḥ
paśavaḥ parikīrtyante saṃsāravaśavartinaḥ
teṣāṃ patitvādbhagavān rudraḥ paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ
anādinidhano dhātā bhagavānviṣṇuravyayaḥ
māyāpāśena badhnāti paśuvatparameśvaraḥ
sa eva mocakasteṣāṃ jñānayogena sevitaḥ
avidyāpāśabaddhānāṃ nānyo mocaka iṣyate
tamṛte paramātmānaṃ śaṅkaraṃ parameśvaram
caturviṃśatitattvāni pāśā hi parameṣṭhinaḥ
taiḥ pāśairmocayatyekaḥ śivo jīvairupāsitaḥ
nibadhnāti paśūnekaścaturviṃśatipāśakaiḥ
sa eva bhagavānrudro mocayatyapi sevitaḥ
daśendriyamayaiḥ pāśairantaḥ karaṇasaṃbhavaiḥ
bhūtatanmātrapāśaiśca paśūnmocayati prabhuḥ
indriyārthamayaiḥ pāśair baddhvā viṣayinaḥ prabhuḥ
āśu bhaktā bhavantyevaṃ parameśvarasevayā
bhaja ityeṣa dhātur vai sevāyāṃ parikīrtitaḥ
tasmātsevā budhaiḥ proktā bhaktiśabdena bhūyasī
brahmādistambaparyantaṃ paśūnbaddhvā maheśvaraḥ
tribhirguṇamayaiḥ pāśaiḥ kāryaṃ kārayati svayam
dṛḍhena bhaktiyogena paśubhiḥ samupāsitaḥ
mocayatyeva tānsadyaḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ
bhajanaṃ bhaktirityuktā vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ
sarvakāryeṇa hetutvāt pāśacchedapaṭīyasī
satyaḥ sarvaga ityādi śivasya guṇacintanā
rūpopādānacintā ca mānasaṃ bhajanaṃ viduḥ
vācikaṃ bhajanaṃ dhīrāḥ praṇavādijapaṃ viduḥ
kāyikaṃ bhajanaṃ sadbhiḥ prāṇāyāmādi kathyate
dharmādharmamayaiḥ pāśairbandhanaṃ dehināmidam
mocakaḥ śiva evaiko bhagavānparameśvaraḥ
caturviṃśatitattvāni māyākarmaguṇā iti
kīrtyante viṣayāśceti pāśā jīvanibandhanāt
tairbaddhāḥ śivabhaktyaiva mucyante sarvadehinaḥ
pañcakleśamayaiḥ pāśaiḥ paśūnbadhnāti śaṅkaraḥ
sa eva mocakas teṣāṃ bhaktyā samyagupāsitaḥ
avidyāmasmitāṃ rāgaṃ dveṣaṃ ca dvipadāṃ varāḥ
vadantyabhiniveśaṃ ca kleśānpāśatvamāgatān
tamo moho mahāmohas tāmisra iti paṇḍitāḥ
andhatāmisra ityāhuravidyāṃ pañcadhā sthitām
tāñjīvān muniśārdūlāḥ sarvāṃścaivāpyavidyayā
śivo mocayati śrīmānnānyaḥ kaścidvimocakaḥ
avidyāṃ tama ityāhurasmitāṃ moha ityapi
mahāmoha iti prājñā rāgaṃ yogaparāyaṇāḥ
dveṣaṃ tāmisra ityāhurandhatāmisra ityapi
tathaivābhiniveśaṃ ca mithyājñānaṃ vivekinaḥ
tamaso 'ṣṭavidhā bhedā mohaścāṣṭavidhaḥ smṛtaḥ
mahāmohaprabhedāśca budhairdaśa vicintitāḥ
aṣṭādaśavidhaṃ cāhustāmisraṃ ca vicakṣaṇāḥ
andhatāmisrabhedāśca tathāṣṭādaśadhā smṛtāḥ
avidyayāsya saṃbandho nātīto nāstyanāgataḥ
bhavedrāgeṇa devasya śaṃbhoraṅganivāsinaḥ
kāleṣu triṣu saṃbandhastasya dveṣeṇa no bhavet
māyātītasya devasya sthāṇoḥ paśupatervibhoḥ
tathaivābhiniveśena saṃbandho na kadācana
śaṅkarasya śaraṇyasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ
kuśalākuśalaistasya saṃbandho naiva karmabhiḥ
bhavetkālatraye śaṃbhoravidyāmativartinaḥ
vipākaiḥ karmaṇāṃ vāpi na bhavedeva saṃgamaḥ
kāleṣu triṣu sarvasya śivasya śivadāyinaḥ
sukhaduḥkhair asaṃspṛśyaḥ kālatritayavartibhiḥ
sa tair vinaśvaraiḥ śaṃbhur bodhānandātmakaḥ paraḥ
āśayairaparāmṛṣṭaḥ kālatritayagocaraiḥ
dhiyāṃ patiḥ svabhūr eṣa mahādevo maheśvaraḥ
aspṛśyaḥ karmasaṃskāraiḥ kālatritayavartibhiḥ
tathaiva bhogasaṃskārairbhagavānantakāntakaḥ
puṃviśeṣaparo devo bhagavānparameśvaraḥ
cetanācetanāyuktaprapañcād akhilāt paraḥ
loke sātiśayatvena jñānaiśvaryaṃ vilokyate
śivenātiśayatvena śivaṃ prāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ
pratisargaṃ prasūtānāṃ brahmaṇāṃ śāstravistaram
upadeṣṭā sa evādau kālāvacchedavartinām
kālāvacchedayuktānāṃ gurūṇāmapyasau guruḥ
sarveṣāmeva sarveśaḥ kālāvacchedavarjitaḥ
anādireṣa saṃbandho vijñānotkarṣayoḥ paraḥ
sthitayorīdṛśaḥ sarvaḥ pariśuddhaḥ svabhāvataḥ
ātmaprayojanābhāve parānugraha eva hi
prayojanaṃ samastānāṃ kāryāṇāṃ parameśvaraḥ
praṇavo vācakastasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ
śivarudrādiśabdānāṃ praṇavo'pi paraḥ smṛtaḥ
śaṃbhoḥ praṇavavācyasya bhāvanā tajjapādapi
yā siddhiḥ svaparā prāpyā bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
jñānatattvaṃ prayatnena yogaḥ pāśupataḥ paraḥ
uktastu devadevena sarveṣām anukaṃpayā
sa hovācaiva yājñavalkyo yadakṣaraṃ gārgyayoginaḥ
abhivadanti sthūlamanantaṃ mahāścaryam adīrgham alohitam amastakam āsāyam ata evopurānasamasaṃgam agandham arasam acakṣuṣkam aśrotram avāṅmano 'tejaskam apramāṇam anusukham anāmagotram amaram ajaram anāmayam amṛtam oṃśabdam amṛtam asaṃvṛtam apūrvam anaparam anantam abāhyaṃ tad aśnāti kiṃcana na tad aśnāti kiṃcana
etatkālavyaye jñātvā paraṃ pāśupataṃ prabhum
yoge pāśupate cāsmin yasyārthaḥ kila uttame
kṛtvauṃkāraṃ pradīpaṃ mṛgaya gṛhapatiṃ sūkṣmam ādyantarasthaṃ saṃyamya dvāravāsaṃ pavanapaṭutaraṃ nāyakaṃ cendriyāṇām
vāgjālaiḥ kasya hetor vibhaṭasi tu bhayaṃ dṛśyate naiva kiṃcid dehasthaṃ paśya śaṃbhuṃ bhramasi kimu pare śāstrajāle 'ndhakāre
evaṃ samyagbudhairjñātvā munīnāmatha coktaṃ śivena
asamarasaṃ pañcadhā kṛtvā bhavaṃ cātmani yojayet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge navamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
bhūya eva mamācakṣva mahimānamumāpateḥ
bhavabhakta mahāprājña bhagavannandikeśvara
śailādiruvāca
sanatkumāra saṃkṣepāttava vakṣyāmyaśeṣataḥ
mahimānaṃ maheśasya bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
nāsya prakṛtibandho 'bhūdbuddhibandho na kaścana
na cāhaṅkārabandhaśca manobandhaśca no 'bhavat
cittabandho na tasyābhūcchrotrabandho na cābhavat
na tvacāṃ cakṣuṣāṃ vāpi bandho jajñe kadācana
jihvābandho na tasyābhūdghrāṇabandho na kaścana
pādabandhaḥ pāṇibandho vāgbandhaścaiva suvrata
upasthendriyabandhaśca bhūtatanmātrabandhanam
nityaśuddhasvabhāvena nityabuddho nisargataḥ
nityamukta iti prokto munibhistattvavedibhiḥ
anādimadhyaniṣṭhasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
buddhiṃ sūte niyogena prakṛtiḥ puruṣasya ca
ahaṅkāraṃ prasūte 'syā buddhistasya niyogataḥ
antaryāmīti deheṣu prasiddhasya svayaṃbhuvaḥ
indriyāṇi daśaikaṃ ca tanmātrāṇi ca śāsanāt
ahaṅkāro 'ti saṃsūte śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
tanmātrāṇi niyogena tasya saṃsuvate prabhoḥ
mahābhūtānyaśeṣeṇa mahādevasya dhīmataḥ
brahmādīnāṃ tṛṇāntaṃ hi dehināṃ dehasaṃgatim
mahābhūtānyaśeṣāṇi janayanti śivājñayā
adhyavasyati sarvārthānbuddhistasyājñayā vibhoḥ
antaryāmīti deheṣu prasiddhasya svayaṃbhuvaḥ
svabhāvasiddhamaiśvaryaṃ svabhāvādeva bhūtayaḥ
tasyājñayā samastārthānahaṅkāro 'timanyate
cittaṃ cetayate cāpi manaḥ saṃkalpayatyapi
śrotraṃ śṛṇoti tacchaktyā śabdasparśādikaṃ ca yat
śambhor ājñābalenaiva bhavasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
vacanaṃ kurute vākyaṃ nādānādi kadācana
śarīrāṇāmaśeṣāṇāṃ tasya devasya śāsanāt
karoti pāṇirādānaṃ na gatyādi kadācana
sarveṣāmeva jantūnāṃ niyamādeva vedhasaḥ
vihāraṃ kurute pādo notsargādi kadācana
samastadehivṛndānāṃ śivasyaiva niyogataḥ
utsargaṃ kurute pāyurna vadeta kadācana
jantorjātasya sarvasya parameśvaraśāsanāt
ānandaṃ kurute śaśvadupasthaṃ vacanādvibhoḥ
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāmīśvarasyaiva śāsanāt
avakāśamaśeṣāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ samprayacchati
ākāśaṃ sarvadā tasya paramasyaiva śāsanāt
nirdeśena śivasyaiva bhedaiḥ prāṇādibhirnijaiḥ
bibharti sarvabhūtānāṃ śarīrāṇi prabhañjanaḥ
nirdeśāddevadevasya saptaskandhagato marut
lokayātrāṃ vahatyeva bhedaiḥ svairāvahādibhiḥ
nāgādyaiḥ pañcabhirbhedaiḥ śarīreṣu pravartate
apadeśena devasya paramasya samīraṇaḥ
havyaṃ vahati devānāṃ kavyaṃ kavyāśināmapi
pākaṃ ca kurute vahniḥ śaṅkarasyaiva śāsanāt
bhuktamāhārajātaṃ yat pacate dehināṃ tathā
udarasthaḥ sadā vahnirviśveśvaraniyogataḥ
saṃjīvayantyaśeṣāṇi bhūtānyāpastadājñayā
avilaṅghyā hi sarveṣāmājñā tasya garīyasī
carācarāṇi bhūtāni bibhartyeva tadājñayā
ājñayā tasya devasya devadevaḥ purandaraḥ
jīvatāṃ vyādhibhiḥ pīḍāṃ mṛtānāṃ yātanāśataiḥ
viśvambharaḥ sadākālaṃ lokaiḥ sarvairalaṅghyayā
devān pātyasurān hanti trailokyamakhilaṃ sthitaḥ
adhārmikāṇāṃ vai nāśaṃ karoti śivaśāsanāt
varuṇaḥ salilairlokān saṃbhāvayati śāsanāt
majjayatyājñayā tasya pāśairbadhnāti cāsurān
puṇyānurūpaṃ sarveṣāṃ prāṇināṃ samprayacchati
vittaṃ vitteśvarastasya śāsanāt parameṣṭhinaḥ
udayāstamaye kurvankurute kālamājñayā
ādityastasya nityasya satyasya paramātmanaḥ
puṣpāṇyauṣadhijātāni prahlādayati ca prajāḥ
amṛtāṃśuḥ kalādhāraḥ kālakālasya śāsanāt
ādityā vasavo rudrā aśvinau marutastathā
anyāśca devatāḥ sarvāstacchāsanavinirmitāḥ
gandharvā devasaṃghāś ca siddhāḥ sādhyāśca cāraṇāḥ
yakṣarakṣaḥpiśācāśca sthitāḥ śāstreṣu vedhasaḥ
grahanakṣatratārāśca yajñā vedāstapāṃsi ca
ṛṣīṇāṃ ca gaṇāḥ sarve śāsanaṃ tasya dhiṣṭhitāḥ
kavyāśināṃ gaṇāḥ sapta samudrā girisiṃdhavaḥ
śāsane tasya vartante kānanāni sarāṃsi ca
kalāḥ kāṣṭhā nimeṣāścamuhūrtā divasāḥ kṣapāḥ
ṛtvabdapakṣamāsāśca niyogāttasya dhiṣṭhitāḥ
yugamanvantarāṇyasya śaṃbhostiṣṭhanti śāsanāt
parāścaiva parārdhāśca kālabhedāstathāpare
devānāṃ jātayaścāṣṭau tiraścāṃ pañca jātayaḥ
manuṣyāśca pravartante devadevasya dhīmataḥ
jātāni bhūtavṛndāni caturdaśasu yoniṣu
sarvalokaniṣaṇṇāni tiṣṭhantyasyaiva śāsanāt
caturdaśasu lokeṣu sthitā jātāḥ prajāḥ prabhoḥ
sarveśvarasya tasyaiva niyogavaśavartinaḥ
pātālāni samastāni bhuvanānyasya śāsanāt
brahmāṇḍāni ca śeṣāṇi tathā sāvaraṇāni ca
vartamānāni sarvāṇi brahmāṇḍāni tadājñayā
vartante sarvabhūtādyaiḥ sametāni samantataḥ
atītānyapyasaṃkhyāni brahmāṇḍāni tadājñayā
pravṛttāni padārthaughaiḥ sahitāni samantataḥ
brahmāṇḍāni bhaviṣyanti saha vastubhir ātmakaiḥ
kariṣyanti śivasyājñāṃ sarvairāvaraṇaiḥ saha
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge daśamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
vibhūtīḥ śivayormahyam ācakṣva tvaṃ gaṇādhipa
parāparavidāṃ śreṣṭha parameśvarabhāvita
nandikeśvara uvāca
hanta te kathayiṣyāmi vibhūtīḥ śivayoraham
sanatkumāra yogīndra brahmaṇastanayottama
paramātmā śivaḥ proktaḥ śivā sā ca prakīrtitā
śivameveśvaraṃ prāhurmāyāṃ gaurīṃ vidurbudhāḥ
puruṣaṃ śaṅkaraṃ prāhurgaurīṃ ca prakṛtiṃ dvijāḥ
arthaḥ śaṃbhuḥ śivā vāṇī divaso 'jaḥ śivā niśā
saptatanturmahādevo rudrāṇī dakṣiṇā smṛtā
ākāśaṃ śaṅkaro devaḥ pṛthivī śaṅkarapriyā
samudro bhagavān rudro velā śailendrakanyakā
vṛkṣaḥ śūlāyudho devaḥ śūlapāṇipriyā latā
brahmā haro'pi sāvitrī śaṅkarārdhaśarīriṇī
viṣṇurmaheśvaro lakṣmīrbhavānī parameśvarī
vajrapāṇirmahādevaḥ śacī śailendrakanyakā
jātavedāḥ svayaṃ rudraḥ svāhā śarvārdhakāyinī
yamastriyaṃbako devas tatpriyā girikanyakā
varuṇo bhagavān rudro gaurī sarvārthadāyinī
bālenduśekharo vāyuḥ śivā śivamanoramā
candrārdhamaulir yakṣendraḥ svayamṛddhiḥ śivā smṛtā
candrārdhaśekharaścandro rohiṇī rudravallabhā
saptasaptiḥ śivaḥ kāntā umā devī suvarcalā
ṣaṇmukhas tripuradhvaṃsī devasenā harapriyā
umā prasūtir vai jñeyā dakṣo devo maheśvaraḥ
puruṣākhyo manuḥ śaṃbhuḥ śatarūpā śivapriyā
vidurbhavānīmākūtiṃ ruciṃ ca parameśvaram
bhṛgurbhagākṣihā devaḥ khyātis trinayanapriyā
marīcirbhagavānrudraḥ saṃbhūtirvallabhā vibhoḥ
vidurbhavānīṃ rucirāṃ kaviṃ ca parameśvaram
gaṅgādharo 'ṅgirā jñeyaḥ smṛtiḥ sākṣādumā smṛtā
pulastyaḥ śaśabhṛnmauliḥ prītiḥ kāntā pinākinaḥ
pulahastripuradhvaṃsī dayā kālaripupriyā
kraturdakṣakratudhvaṃsī saṃnatir dayitā vibhoḥ
trinetro 'trirumā sākṣādanasūyā smṛtā budhaiḥ
ūrjāmāhurumāṃ vṛddhāṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca maheśvaram
śaṅkaraḥ puruṣāḥ sarve striyaḥ sarvā maheśvarī
pulliṅgaśabdavācyā ye te ca rudrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
strīliṅgaśabdavācyā yāḥ sarvā gauryā vibhūtayaḥ
sarve strīpuruṣāḥ proktāstayoreva vibhūtayaḥ
padārthaśaktayo yā yās tā gaurīti vidurbudhāḥ
sā sā viśveśvarī devī sa ca sarvo maheśvaraḥ
śaktimantaḥ padārthā ye sa sa sarvo maheśvaraḥ
aṣṭau prakṛtayo devyā mūrtayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
tathā vikṛtayastasyā dehabaddhavibhūtayaḥ
visphuliṅgā yathā tāvadagnau ca bahudhā smṛtāḥ
jīvāḥ sarve tathā śarvo dvandvasattvamupāgataḥ
gaurīrūpāṇi sarvāṇi śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām
śarīriṇastathā sarve śaṅkarāṃśā vyavasthitāḥ
śrāvyaṃ sarvamumārūpaṃ śrotā devo maheśvaraḥ
viṣayitvaṃ vibhurdhatte viṣayātmakatāmumā
sraṣṭavyaṃ vastujātaṃ tu dhatte śaṅkaravallabhā
sraṣṭā sa eva viśvātmā bālacandrārdhaśekharaḥ
dṛśyavastu prajārūpaṃ bibharti bhuvaneśvarī
draṣṭā viśveśvaro devaḥ śaśikhaṇḍaśikhāmaṇiḥ
rasajātam umārūpaṃ ghreyajātaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ
devo rasayitā śaṃbhurghrātā ca bhuvaneśvaraḥ
mantavyavastutāṃ dhatte mahādevī maheśvarī
mantā sa eva viśvātmā mahādevo maheśvaraḥ
boddhavyaṃ vastu rūpaṃ ca bibharti bhavavallabhā
devaḥ sa eva bhagavān boddhā bālenduśekharaḥ
pīṭhākṛtirumā devī liṅgarūpaśca śaṅkaraḥ
pratiṣṭhāpya prayatnena pūjayanti surāsurāḥ
ye ye padārthā liṅgāṅkās te te śarvavibhūtayaḥ
arthā bhagāṅkitā ye ye te te gauryā vibhūtayaḥ
svargapātālalokāntabrahmāṇḍāvaraṇāṣṭakam
jñeyaṃ sarvamumārūpaṃ jñātā devo maheśvaraḥ
bibharti kṣetratāṃ devī tripurāntakavallabhā
kṣetrajñatvam atho dhatte bhagavānandhakāntakaḥ
śivaliṅgaṃ samutsṛjya yajante cānyadevatāḥ
sa nṛpaḥ saha deśena rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet
śivabhakto na yo rājā bhakto 'nyeṣu sureṣu yaḥ
svapatiṃ yuvatis tyaktvā yathā jāreṣu rājate
brahmādayaḥ surāḥ sarve rājānaśca maharddhikāḥ
mānavā munayaścaiva sarve liṅgaṃ yajanti ca
viṣṇunā rāvaṇaṃ hatvā sasainyaṃ brahmaṇaḥ sutam
sthāpitaṃ vidhivadbhaktyā liṅgaṃ tīre nadīpateḥ
kṛtvā pāpasahasrāṇi hatvā vipraśataṃ tathā
bhāvātsamāśrito rudraṃ mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
sarve liṅgamayā lokāḥ sarve liṅge pratiṣṭhitāḥ
tasmādabhyarcayelliṅgaṃ yadīcchecchāśvataṃ padam
sarvākārau sthitāvetau naraiḥ śreyo 'rthibhiḥ śivau
pūjanīyau namaskāryau cintanīyau ca sarvadā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
mūrtayo 'ṣṭau mamācakṣva śaṅkarasya mahātmanaḥ
viśvarūpasya devasya gaṇeśvara mahāmate
nandikeśvara uvāca
hanta te kathayiṣyāmi mahimānamumāpateḥ
viśvarūpasya devasya sarojabhavasaṃbhava
bhūr āpo 'gnir marud vyoma bhāskaro dīkṣitaḥ śaśī
bhavasya mūrtayaḥ proktāḥ śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
khātmenduvahnisūryāṃbhodharāpavana ityapi
tasyāṣṭa mūrtayaḥ proktā devadevasya dhīmataḥ
agnihotre'rpite tena sūryātmani mahātmani
tadvibhūtistathā sarve devāstṛpyanti sarvadāḥ
vṛkṣasya mūlasekena yathā śākhopaśākhikāḥ
tathā tasyārcayā devās tathā syus tadvibhūtayaḥ
tasya dvādaśadhā bhinnaṃ rūpaṃ sūryātmakaṃ prabhoḥ
sarvadevātmakaṃ yājyaṃ yajanti munipuṅgavāḥ
amṛtākhyā kalā tasya sarvasyādityarūpiṇaḥ
bhūtasaṃjīvanī ceṣṭā loke 'smin pīyate sadā
candrākhyakiraṇāstasya dhūrjaṭerbhāskarātmanaḥ
oṣadhīnāṃ vivṛddhyarthaṃ himavṛṣṭiṃ vitanvate
śuklākhyā raśmayastasya śaṃbhormārtaṇḍarūpiṇaḥ
dharmaṃ vitanvate loke sasyapākādikāraṇam
divākarātmanastasya harikeśāhvayaḥ karaḥ
nakṣatrapoṣakaścaiva prasiddhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
viśvakarmāhvayastasya kiraṇo budhapoṣakaḥ
sarveśvarasya devasya saptasaptisvarūpiṇaḥ
viśvavyaca iti khyātaḥ kiraṇastasya śūlinaḥ
śukrapoṣakabhāvena pratītaḥ sūryarūpiṇaḥ
saṃyadvasur iti khyāto yasya raśmistriśūlinaḥ
lohitāṅgaṃ prapuṣṇāti sahasrakiraṇātmanaḥ
arvāvasur iti khyāto raśmistasya pinākinaḥ
bṛhaspatiṃ prapuṣṇāti sarvadā tapanātmanaḥ
svarāḍiti samākhyātaḥ śivasyāṃśuḥ śanaiścaram
haridaśvātmanastasya prapuṣṇāti divāniśam
sūryātmakasya devasya viśvayonerumāpateḥ
suṣumṇākhyaḥ sadā raśmiḥ puṣṇāti śiśiradyutim
saumyānāṃ vasujātānāṃ prakṛtitvamupāgatā
tasya somāhvayā mūrtiḥ śaṅkarasya jagadguroḥ
tasya somātmakaṃ rūpaṃ śukratvena vyavasthitam
śarīrabhājāṃ sarveṣāṃ devasyāntakaśāsinaḥ
śarīriṇāmaśeṣāṇāṃ manasyeva vyavasthitam
vapuḥ somātmakaṃ śaṃbhostasya sarvajagadguroḥ
śaṃbhoḥ ṣoḍaśadhā bhinnā sthitāmṛtakalātmanaḥ
sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu somākhyā mūrtiruttamā
devānpitṝṃś ca puṣṇāti sudhayāmṛtayā sadā
mūrtiḥ somāhvayā tasya devadevasya śāsituḥ
puṣṇātyoṣadhijātāni dehināmātmaśuddhaye
somāhvayā tanustasya bhavānīmiti nirdiśet
yajñānāṃ patibhāvena jīvānāṃ tapasāmapi
prasiddharūpametadvai somātmakam umāpateḥ
jalānāmoṣadhīnāṃ ca patibhāvena viśrutam
somātmakaṃ vapustasya śaṃbhorbhagavataḥ prabhoḥ
devo hiraṇmayo mṛṣṭaḥ parasparavivekinaḥ
karaṇānāmaśeṣāṇāṃ devatānāṃ nirākṛtiḥ
jīvatvena sthite tasmiñchive somātmake prabhau
madhurā vilayaṃ yāti sarvalokaikarakṣiṇī
yajamānāhvayā mūrtiḥ śaivī havyairaharniśam
puṣṇāti devatāḥ sarvāḥ kavyaiḥ pitṛgaṇānapi
yajamānāhvayā yā sā tanuścāhutijā tayā
vṛṣṭyā bhāvayati spaṣṭaṃ sarvameva parāparam
antaḥsthaṃ ca bahiḥsthaṃ ca brahmāṇḍānāṃ sthitaṃ jalam
bhūtānāṃ ca śarīrasthaṃ śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī
nadīnāmamṛtaṃ sākṣānnadānāmapi sarvadā
samudrāṇāṃ ca sarvatra vyāpī sarvamumāpatiḥ
saṃjīvinī samastānāṃ bhūtānāmeva pāvinī
aṃbikā prāṇasaṃsthā yā mūrtir ambumayī parā
antaḥsthaś ca bahiḥsthaś ca brahmāṇḍānāṃ vibhāvasuḥ
yajñānāṃ ca śarīrasthaḥ śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī
śarīrasthā ca bhūtānāṃ śreyasī mūrtiraiśvarī
mūrtiḥ pāvakasaṃsthā yā śaṃbhoratyantapūjitā
bhedā ekonapañcāśad vedavidbhir udāhṛtāḥ
havyaṃ vahati devānāṃ śaṃbhoryajñātmakaṃ vapuḥ
kavyaṃ pitṛgaṇānāṃ ca hūyamānaṃ dvijātibhiḥ
sarvadevamayaṃ śaṃbhoḥ śreṣṭham agnyātmakaṃ vapuḥ
vadanti vedaśāstrajñā yajanti ca yathāvidhi
antaḥstho jagadaṇḍānāṃ bahiḥsthaśca samīraṇaḥ
śarīrasthaśca bhūtānāṃ śaivī mūrtiḥ paṭīyasī
prāṇādyā nāgakūrmādyā āvahādyāśca vāyavaḥ
īśānamūrterekasya bhedāḥ sarve prakīrtitāḥ
antaḥsthaṃ jagadaṇḍānāṃ bahiḥsthaṃ ca viyadvibhoḥ
śarīrasthaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ śaṃbhor mūrtir garīyasī
śaṃbhor viśvambharā mūrtiḥ sarvabrahmādhidevatā
carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ dhāraṇe matā
carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ śarīrāṇi vidurbudhāḥ
pañcakeneśamūrtīnāṃ samārabdhāni sarvathā
pañcabhūtāni candrārkāvātmeti munipuṅgavāḥ
mūrtayo 'ṣṭau śivasyāhurdevadevasya dhīmataḥ
ātmā tasyāṣṭamī mūrtiryajamānāhvayā parā
carācaraśarīreṣu sarveṣveva sthitā tadā
dīkṣitaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ prāhurātmānaṃ ca munīśvarāḥ
yajamānāhvayā mūrtiḥ śivasya śivadāyinaḥ
mūrtayo 'ṣṭau śivasyaitā vandanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ
śreyo'rthibhir narair nityaṃ śreyasāmekahetavaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
bhūyo 'pi vada me nandin mahimānamumāpateḥ
aṣṭamūrtermaheśasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
nandikeśvara uvāca
vakṣyāmi te maheśasya mahimānamumāpateḥ
aṣṭamūrterjagadvyāpya sthitasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ dhātā viśvambharātmakaḥ
śarva ityucyate devaḥ sarvaśāstrārthapāragaiḥ
viśvambharātmanastasya śarvasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
vikeśī kathyate patnī tanayo 'ṅgārakaḥ smṛtaḥ
bhava ityucyate devo bhagavān vedavādibhiḥ
saṃjīvanasya lokānāṃ bhavasya paramātmanaḥ
umā saṃkīrtitā devī sutaḥ śukraśca sūribhiḥ
saptalokāṇḍakavyāpī sarvalokaikarakṣitā
vahnyātmā bhagavāndevaḥ smṛtaḥ paśupatirbudhaiḥ
svāhā patnyātmanastasya proktā paśupateḥ priyā
ṣaṇmukho bhagavān devo budhaiḥ putra udāhṛtaḥ
samastabhuvanavyāpī bhartā sarvaśarīriṇām
pavanātmā budhairdeva īśāna iti kīrtyate
īśānasya jagatkarturdevasya pavanātmanaḥ
śivā devī budhair uktā putraścāsya manojavaḥ
carācarāṇāṃ bhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ sarvakāmadaḥ
vyomātmā bhagavāndevo bhīma ityucyate budhaiḥ
mahāmahimno devasya bhīmasya gaganātmanaḥ
diśo daśa smṛtā devyaḥ sutaḥ sargaśca sūribhiḥ
sūryātmā bhagavāndevaḥ sarveṣāṃ ca vibhūtidaḥ
rudra ityucyate devairbhagavān bhuktimuktidaḥ
sūryātmakasya rudrasya bhaktānāṃ bhaktidāyinaḥ
suvarcalā smṛtā devī sutaścāsya śanaiścaraḥ
samastasaumyavastūnāṃ prakṛtitvena viśrutaḥ
somātmako budhairdevo mahādeva iti smṛtaḥ
somātmakasya devasya mahādevasya sūribhiḥ
dayitā rohiṇī proktā budhaścaiva śarīrajaḥ
havyakavyasthitiṃ kurvan havyakavyāśināṃ tadā
yajamānātmako devo mahādevo budhaiḥ prabhuḥ
ugra ityucyate sadbhirīśānaśceti cāparaiḥ
ugrāhvayasya devasya yajamānātmanaḥ prabhoḥ
dīkṣā patnī budhairuktā saṃtānākhyaḥ sutastathā
śarīriṇāṃ śarīreṣu kaṭhinaṃ koṅkaṇādivat
pārthivaṃ tadvapurjñeyaṃ śarvatattvaṃ bubhutsubhiḥ
dehe dehe tu deveśo dehabhājāṃ yadavyayam
vastudravyātmakaṃ tasya bhavasya paramātmanaḥ
jñeyaṃ ca tattvavidbhirvai sarvavedārthapāragaiḥ
āgneyaḥ pariṇāmo yo vigraheṣu śarīriṇām
mūrtiḥ paśupatirjñeyā sā tattvaṃ vettumicchubhiḥ
vāyavyaḥ pariṇāmo yaḥ śarīreṣu śarīriṇām
budhair īśeti sā tasya tanurjñeyā na saṃśayaḥ
suṣiraṃ yaccharīrasthamaśeṣāṇāṃ śarīriṇām
bhīmasya sā tanurjñeyā tattvavijñānakāṅkṣibhiḥ
cakṣurādigataṃ tejo yaccharīrasthamaṅginām
rudrasyāpi tanurjñeyā paramārthaṃ bubhutsubhiḥ
sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu manaścandrātmakaṃ hi yat
mahādevasya sā mūrtirboddhavyā tattvacintakaiḥ
ātmā yo yajamānākhyaḥ sarvabhūtaśarīragaḥ
mūrtirugrasya sā jñeyā paramātmabubhutsubhiḥ
jātānāṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ caturdaśasu yoniṣu
aṣṭamūrterananyatvaṃ vadanti paramarṣayaḥ
saptamūrtimayānyāhur īśasyāṅgāni dehinām
ātmā tasyāṣṭamī mūrtiḥ sarvabhūtaśarīragā
aṣṭamūrtimamuṃ devaṃ sarvalokātmakaṃ vibhum
bhajasva sarvabhāvena śreyaḥ prāptuṃ yadīcchasi
prāṇino yasya kasyāpi kriyate yadyanugrahaḥ
aṣṭamūrtermaheśasya kṛtamārādhanaṃ bhavet
nigrahaścet kṛto loke dehino yasya kasyacit
aṣṭamūrtermaheśasya sa eva vihito bhavet
yadyavajñā kṛtā loke yasya kasyacid aṅginaḥ
aṣṭamūrtermaheśasya vihitā sā bhavedvibhoḥ
abhayaṃ yat pradattaṃ syādaṅgino yasya kasyacit
ārādhanaṃ kṛtaṃ tasmādaṣṭamūrterna saṃśayaḥ
sarvopakārakaraṇaṃ pradānamabhayasya ca
ārādhanaṃ tu devasya aṣṭamūrterna saṃśayaḥ
sarvopakārakaraṇaṃ sarvānugraha eva ca
tadarcanaṃ paraṃ prāhuraṣṭamūrtermunīśvarāḥ
anugrahaṇamanyeṣāṃ vidhātavyaṃ tvayāṅginām
sarvābhayapradānaṃ ca śivārādhanamicchatā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge trayodaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
pañca brahmāṇi me nandinnācakṣva gaṇasattama
śreyaḥkaraṇabhūtāni pavitrāṇi śarīriṇām
nandikeśvara uvāca
śivasyaiva svarūpāṇi pañca brahmāhvayāni te
kathayāmi yathātattvaṃ padmayoneḥ sutottama
sarvalokaikasaṃhartā sarvalokaikarakṣitā
sarvalokaikanirmātā pañcabrahmātmakaḥ śivaḥ
sarveṣāmeva lokānāṃ yadupādānakāraṇam
nimittakāraṇaṃ cāhuḥ sa śivaḥ pañcadhā smṛtaḥ
mūrtayaḥ pañca vikhyātāḥ pañca brahmāhvayāḥ parāḥ
sarvalokaśaraṇyasya śivasya paramātmanaḥ
kṣetrajñaḥ prathamā mūrtiḥ śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
bhoktā prakṛtivargasya bhogyasyeśānasaṃjñitaḥ
sthāṇostatpuruṣākhyā ca dvitīyā mūrtirucyate
prakṛtiḥ sā hi vijñeyā paramātmaguhātmikā
aghorākhyā tṛtīyā ca śaṃbhormūrtirgarīyasī
buddheḥ sā mūrtirityuktā dharmādyaṣṭāṅgasaṃyutā
caturthī vāmadevākhyā mūrtiḥ śaṃbhor garīyasī
ahaṅkārātmakatvena vyāpya sarvaṃ vyavasthitā
sadyojātāhvayā śaṃbhoḥ pañcamī mūrtirucyate
manastattvātmakatvena sthitā sarvaśarīriṣu
īśānaḥ paramo devaḥ parameṣṭhī sanātanaḥ
śrotrendriyātmakatvena sarvabhūteṣvavasthitaḥ
sthitastatpuruṣo devaḥ śarīreṣu śarīriṇām
tvagindriyātmakatvena tattvavidbhirudāhṛtaḥ
aghoro'pi mahādevaścakṣurātmatayā budhaiḥ
kīrtitaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ śarīreṣu vyavasthitaḥ
jihvendriyātmakatvena vāmadevo'pi viśrutaḥ
aṅgabhājām aśeṣāṇām aṅgeṣu paridhiṣṭhitaḥ
ghrāṇendriyātmakatvena sadyojātaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ
prāṇabhājāṃ samastānāṃ vigraheṣu vyavasthitaḥ
sarveṣveva śarīreṣu prāṇabhājāṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
vāgindriyātmakatvena budhairīśāna ucyate
pāṇīndriyātmakatvena sthitastatpuruṣo budhaiḥ
ucyate vigraheṣveva sarvavigrahadhāriṇām
sarvavigrahiṇāṃ dehe hyaghoro'pi vyavasthitaḥ
pādendriyātmakatvena kīrtitas tattvavedibhiḥ
pāyvindriyātmakatvena vāmadevo vyavasthitaḥ
sarvabhūtanikāyānāṃ kāyeṣu munibhiḥ smṛtaḥ
upasthātmatayā devaḥ sadyojātaḥ sthitaḥ prabhuḥ
iṣyate vedaśāstrajñairdeheṣu prāṇadhāriṇām
īśānaṃ prāṇināṃ devaṃ śabdatanmātrarūpiṇam
ākāśajanakaṃ prāhurmunivṛndārakaprajāḥ
prāhustatpuruṣaṃ devaṃ sparśatanmātrakātmakam
samīrajanakaṃ prāhurbhagavantaṃ munīśvarāḥ
rūpatanmātrakaṃ devamaghoramapi ghorakam
prāhurvedavido mukhyā janakaṃ jātavedasaḥ
rasatanmātrarūpatvāt prathitaṃ tattvavedinaḥ
vāmadevam apāṃ prāhurjanakatvena saṃsthitam
sadyojātaṃ mahādevaṃ gandhatanmātrarūpiṇam
bhūmyātmānaṃ praśaṃsanti sarvatattvārthavedinaḥ
ākāśātmānam īśānam ādidevaṃ munīśvarāḥ
parameṇa mahattvena sambhūtaṃ prāhuradbhutam
prabhuṃ tatpuruṣaṃ devaṃ pavanaṃ pavanātmakam
samastalokavyāpitvāt prathitaṃ sūrayo viduḥ
athārcitatayā khyātamaghoraṃ dahanātmakam
kathayanti mahātmānaṃ vedavākyārthavedinaḥ
toyātmakaṃ mahādevaṃ vāmadevaṃ manoramam
jagatsaṃjīvanatvena kathitaṃ munayo viduḥ
viśvaṃbharātmakaṃ devaṃ sadyojātaṃ jagadgurum
carācaraikabhartāraṃ paraṃ kavivarā viduḥ
pañcabrahmātmakaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam
śivānandaṃ tadityāhur munayas tattvadarśinaḥ
pañcaviṃśatitattvātmā prapañce yaḥ pradṛśyate
pañcabrahmātmakatvena sa śivo nānyatāṃ gataḥ
pañcaviṃśatitattvātmā pañcabrahmātmakaḥ śivaḥ
śreyo'rthibhir ato nityaṃ cintanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcabrahmakathanaṃ nāma caturdaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
bhūyo 'pi śivamāhātmyaṃ samācakṣva mahāmate
sarvajño hyasi bhūtānām adhinātha mahāguṇa
śailādiruvāca
śivamāhātmyamekāgraḥ śṛṇu vakṣyāmi te mune
bahubhirbahudhā śabdaiḥ kīrtitaṃ munisattamaiḥ
sadasadrūpamityāhuḥ sadasatpatirityapi
taṃ śivaṃ munayaḥ kecitpravadanti ca sūrayaḥ
bhūtabhāvavikāreṇa dvitīyena sa ucyate
vyaktaṃ tena vihīnatvād avyaktam asadityapi
ubhe te śivarūpe hi śivādanyaṃ na vidyate
tayoḥ patitvācca śivaḥ sadasatpatirucyate
kṣarākṣarātmakaṃ prāhuḥ kṣarākṣaraparaṃ tathā
śivaṃ maheśvaraṃ kecinmunayastattvacintakāḥ
uktamakṣaramavyaktaṃ vyaktaṃ kṣaramudāhṛtam
rūpe te śaṅkarasyaiva tasmānna para ucyate
tayoḥ paraḥ śivaḥ śāntaḥ kṣarākṣaraparo budhaiḥ
ucyate paramārthena mahādevo maheśvaraḥ
samastavyaktarūpaṃ tu tataḥ smṛtvā sa mucyate
samaṣṭivyaṣṭirūpaṃ tu samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam
vadanti kecidācāryāḥ śivaṃ paramakāraṇam
samaṣṭiṃ viduravyaktaṃ vyaṣṭiṃ vyaktaṃ munīśvarāḥ
rūpe te gadite śaṃbhor nāstyanyad vastusaṃbhavam
tayoḥ kāraṇabhāvena śivo hi parameśvaraḥ
ucyate yogaśāstrajñaiḥ samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam
kṣetrakṣetrajñarūpī ca śivaḥ kaiścidudāhṛtaḥ
paramātmā paraṃ jyotirbhagavānparameśvaraḥ
caturviṃśatitattvāni samaṣṭivyaṣṭikāraṇam
prāhuḥ kṣetrajñaśabdena bhoktāraṃ puruṣaṃ tathā
kṣetrakṣetravidāvete rūpe tasya svayaṃbhuvaḥ
na kiṃcicca śivādanyaditi prāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ
aparabrahmarūpaṃ taṃ parabrahmātmakaṃ śivam
kecidāhurmahādevam anādinidhanaṃ prabhum
bhūtendriyāntaḥ karaṇapradhānaviṣayātmakam
aparaṃ brahma nirdiṣṭaṃ paraṃ brahma cidātmakam
brahmaṇī te maheśasya śivasyāsya svayaṃbhuvaḥ
śaṅkarasya parasyaiva śivādanyanna vidyate
vidyāvidyāsvarūpī ca śaṅkaraḥ kaiściducyate
dhātā vidhātā lokānāmādidevo maheśvaraḥ
vidyeti ca tamevāhuravidyeti munīśvarāḥ
prapañcajātamakhilaṃ te svarūpe svayaṃbhuvaḥ
bhrāntirvidyā paraṃ ceti śivarūpamanuttamam
avāpurmunayo yogātkecidāgamavedinaḥ
artheṣu bahurūpeṣu vijñānaṃ bhrāntirucyate
ātmākāreṇa saṃvittirbudhairvidyeti kīrtyate
vikalparahitaṃ tattvaṃ paramityabhidhīyate
tṛtīyarūpamīśasya nānyat kiṃcana sarvataḥ
vyaktāvyaktajñarūpīti śivaḥ kaiścinnigadyate
vidhātā sarvalokānāṃ dhātā ca parameśvaraḥ
trayoviṃśatitattvāni vyaktaśabdena sūrayaḥ
vadantyavyaktaśabdena prakṛtiḥ ca parāṃ tathā
kathayanti jñaśabdena puruṣaṃ guṇabhoginam
tattrayaṃ śāṅkaraṃ rūpaṃ nānyat kiṃcid aśāṅkaram
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
punareva mahābuddhe śrotumicchāmi tattvataḥ
bahubhirbahudhā śabdaiḥ śabditāni munīśvaraiḥ
śailādiruvāca
punaḥ punaḥ pravakṣyāmi śivarūpāṇi te mune
bahubhirbahudhā śabdaiḥ śabditāni munīśvaraiḥ
kṣetrajñaḥ prakṛtirvyaktaṃ kālātmeti munīśvaraiḥ
ucyate kaiścidācāryairāgamārṇavapāragaiḥ
kṣetrajñaṃ puruṣaṃ prāhuḥ pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ budhāḥ
vikārajātaṃ niḥśeṣaṃ prakṛtervyaktamityapi
pradhānavyaktayoḥ kālaḥ pariṇāmaikakāraṇam
taccatuṣṭayamīśasya rūpāṇāṃ hi catuṣṭayam
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ puruṣaṃ pradhānaṃ vyaktarūpiṇam
kathayanti śivaṃ kecidācāryāḥ parameśvaram
hiraṇyagarbhaḥ kartāsya bhoktā viśvasya pūruṣaḥ
vikārajātaṃ vyaktākhyaṃ pradhānaṃ kāraṇaṃ param
teṣāṃ catuṣṭayaṃ buddheḥ śivarūpacatuṣṭayam
procyate śaṅkarādanyadasti vastu na kiṃcana
piṇḍajātisvarūpī tu kathyate kaiścid īśvaraḥ
carācaraśarīrāṇi piṇḍākhyāny akhilāny api
sāmānyāni samastāni mahāsāmānyameva ca
kathyante jātiśabdena tāni rūpāṇi dhīmataḥ
virāṭ hiraṇyagarbhātmā kaiścidīśo nigadyate
hiraṇyagarbho lokānāṃ heturlokātmako virāṭ
sūtrāvyākṛtarūpaṃ taṃ śivaṃ śaṃsanti kecana
avyākṛtaṃ pradhānaṃ hi tadrūpaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
lokā yenaiva tiṣṭhanti sūtre maṇigaṇā iva
tatsūtramiti vijñeyaṃ rūpamadbhutavikramam
antaryāmī paraḥ kaiścitkaiścidīśaḥ prakīrtyate
svayaṃjyotiḥ svayaṃvedyaḥ śivaḥ śaṃbhurmaheśvaraḥ
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāmantaryāmī śivaḥ smṛtaḥ
sarveṣāmeva bhūtānāṃ paratvātpara ucyate
paramātmā śivaḥ śaṃbhuḥ śaṅkaraḥ parameśvaraḥ
prājñataijasaviśvākhyaṃ tasya rūpatrayaṃ viduḥ
suṣuptisvapnajāgrantamavasthātrayameva tat
virāṭ hiraṇyagarbhākhyam avyākṛtapadāhvayam
turīyasya śivasyāsya avasthātrayagāminaḥ
hiraṇyagarbhaḥ puruṣaḥ kāla ity eva kīrtitāḥ
tisro 'vasthā jagatsṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārahetavaḥ
bhavaviṣṇuviriñcākhyamavasthātrayamīśituḥ
ārādhya bhaktyā muktiṃ ca prāpnuvanti śarīriṇaḥ
kartā kriyā ca kāryaṃ ca karaṇaṃ ceti sūribhiḥ
śaṃbhoścatvāri rūpāṇi kīrtyante parameṣṭhinaḥ
pramātā ca pramāṇaṃ ca prameyaṃ pramitistathā
catvāryetāni rūpāṇi śivasyaiva na saṃśayaḥ
īśvarāvyākṛtaprāṇavirāḍbhūtendriyātmakam
śivasyaiva vikāro 'yaṃ samudrasyeva vīcayaḥ
īśvaraṃ jagatāmāhurnimittaṃ kāraṇaṃ tathā
avyākṛtaṃ pradhānaṃ hi taduktaṃ vedavādibhiḥ
hiraṇyagarbhaḥ prāṇākhyo virāṭ lokātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ
mahābhūtāni bhūtāni kāryāṇi indriyāṇi ca
śivasyaitāni rūpāṇi śaṃsanti munisattamāḥ
paramātmā śivādanyo nāstīti kavayo viduḥ
śivajātāni tattvāni pañcaviṃśanmanīṣibhiḥ
uktāni na tadanyāni salilādūrmivṛndavat
pañcaviṃśatpadārthebhyaḥ śivatattvaṃ paraṃ viduḥ
tāni tasmādananyāni suvarṇakaṭakādivat
sadāśiveśvarādyāni tattvāni śivatattvataḥ
jātāni na tadanyāni mṛddravyaṃ kuṃbhabhedavat
māyā vidyā kriyā śaktirjñānaśaktiḥ kriyāmayī
jātāḥ śivānna saṃdehaḥ kiraṇā iva sūryataḥ
sarvātmakaṃ śivaṃ devaṃ sarvāśrayavidhāyinam
bhajasva sarvabhāvena śreyaścetprāptumicchasi
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ṣoḍaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
bhūyo devagaṇaśreṣṭha śivamāhātmyamuttamam
śṛṇvato nāsti me tṛptis tvadvākyāmṛtapānataḥ
kathaṃ śarīrī bhagavān kasmādrudraḥ pratāpavān
sarvātmā ca kathaṃ śambhuḥ kathaṃ pāśupataṃ vratam
kathaṃ vā devamukhyaiśca śruto dṛṣṭaśca śaṅkaraḥ
śailādiruvāca
avyaktādabhavatsthāṇuḥ śivaḥ paramakāraṇam
sa sarvakāraṇopeta ṛṣir viśvādhikaḥ prabhuḥ
devānāṃ prathamaṃ devaṃ jāyamānaṃ mukhāmbujāt
dadarśa cāgre brahmāṇaṃ cājñayā tamavaikṣata
dṛṣṭo rudreṇa deveśaḥ sasarja sakalaṃ ca saḥ
varṇāśramavyavasthāśca sthāpayāmāsa vai virāṭ
somaṃ sasarja yajñārthaṃ somādidamajāyata
caruśca vahniryajñaśca vajrapāṇiḥ śacīpatiḥ
viṣṇurnārāyaṇaḥ śrīmān sarvaṃ somamayaṃ jagat
rudrādhyāyena te devā rudraṃ tuṣṭuvurīśvaram
prasannavadanastasthau devānāṃ madhyataḥ prabhuḥ
apahṛtya ca vijñānameṣāmeva maheśvaraḥ
devā hyapṛcchaṃstaṃ devaṃ ko bhavāniti śaṅkaram
abravīdbhagavānrudro hyahamekaḥ purātanaḥ
āsaṃ prathama evāhaṃ vartāmi ca surottamāḥ
bhaviṣyāmi ca loke 'sminmatto nānyaḥ kutaścana
vyatiriktaṃ na matto 'sti nānyat kiṃcit surottamāḥ
nityo 'nityo 'hamanagho brahmāhaṃ brahmaṇaspatiḥ
diśaśca vidiśaścāhaṃ prakṛtiśca pumānaham
triṣṭubjagatyanuṣṭup ca chando'haṃ tanmayaḥ śivaḥ
satyo'haṃ sarvagaḥ śāntastretāgnirgauravaṃ guruḥ
gaurahaṃ gahvaraścāhaṃ nityaṃ gahanagocaraḥ
jyeṣṭho'haṃ sarvatattvānāṃ variṣṭho'ham apāṃ patiḥ
āpo'haṃ bhagavānīśas tejo'haṃ vedirapyaham
ṛgvedo'haṃ yajurvedaḥ sāmavedo'ham ātmabhūḥ
atharvaṇo'haṃ mantro'haṃ tathā cāṅgirasāṃ varaḥ
itihāsapurāṇāni kalpo'haṃ kalpanāpyaham
akṣaraṃ ca kṣaraṃ cāhaṃ kṣāntiḥ śāntirahaṃ kṣamā
guhyo'haṃ sarvavedeṣu vareṇyo'ham ajo'pyaham
puṣkaraṃ ca pavitraṃ ca madhyaṃ cāhaṃ tataḥ param
bahiścāhaṃ tathā cāntaḥ purastādahamavyayaḥ
jyotiścāhaṃ tamaścāhaṃ brahmā viṣṇurmaheśvaraḥ
buddhiścāhamahaṅkārastanmātrāṇīndriyāṇi ca
evaṃ sarvaṃ ca māmeva yo veda surasattamāḥ
sa eva sarvavitsarvaṃ sarvātmā parameśvaraḥ
gāṃ gobhirbrāhmaṇān sarvān brāhmaṇyena havīṃṣi ca
āyuṣāyustathā satyaṃ satyena surasattamāḥ
dharmaṃ dharmeṇa sarvāṃśca tarpayāmi svatejasā
ityādau bhagavānuktvā tatraivāntaradhīyata
nāpaśyanta tato devaṃ rudraṃ paramakāraṇam
te devāḥ paramātmānaṃ rudraṃ dhyāyanti śaṅkaram
sanārāyaṇakā devāḥ sendrāśca munayastathā
tathordhvabāhavo devā rudraṃ stunvanti śaṃkaram
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge saptadaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
devā ūcuḥ
ya eṣa bhagavān rudro brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
skandaścāpi tathā cendro bhuvanāni caturdaśa
aśvinau grahatārāśca nakṣatrāṇi ca khaṃ diśaḥ
bhūtāni ca tathā sūryaḥ somaścāṣṭau grahāstathā
prāṇaḥ kālo yamo mṛtyuramṛtaḥ parameśvaraḥ
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca vartamānaṃ maheśvaraḥ
viśvaṃ kṛtsnaṃ jagatsarvaṃ satyaṃ tasmai namonamaḥ
tvamādau ca tathā bhūto bhūrbhuvaḥ svastathaiva ca
ante tvaṃ viśvarūpo 'si śīrṣaṃ tu jagataḥ sadā
brahmaikastvaṃ dvitridhārthamadhaśca tvaṃ sureśvaraḥ
śāntiśca tvaṃ tathā puṣṭistuṣṭiścāpyahutaṃ hutam
viśvaṃ caiva tathāviśvaṃ dattaṃ vādattam īśvaram
kṛtaṃ cāpyakṛtaṃ devaṃ paramapyaparaṃ dhruvam
parāyaṇaṃ satāṃ caiva hyasatāmapi śaṅkaram
apāma somam amṛtā abhūmāganma jyotiravidāma devān
kiṃ nūnam asmān kṛṇavad arātiḥ kimu dhūrtiramṛtaṃ martyasya
etajjagaddhitaṃ divyamakṣaraṃ sūkṣmamavyayam
prājāpatyaṃ pavitraṃ ca saumyamagrāhyamavyayam
agrāhyeṇāpi vā grāhyaṃ vāyavyena samīraṇaḥ
saumyena saumyaṃ grasati tejasā svena līlayā
tasmai namo 'pasaṃhartre mahāgrāsāya śūline
hṛdisthā devatāḥ sarvā hṛdi prāṇe pratiṣṭhitāḥ
hṛdi tvamasi yo nityaṃ tisro mātrāḥ parastu saḥ
śiraścottarataścaiva pādau dakṣiṇatastathā
yo vai cottarataḥ sākṣātsa oṅkāraḥ sanātanaḥ
oṅkāro yaḥ sa eveha praṇavo vyāpya tiṣṭhati
anantastārasūkṣmaṃ ca śuklaṃ vaidyutameva ca
paraṃ brahmā sa īśāna eko rudraḥ sa eva ca
bhavānmaheśvaraḥ sākṣānmahādevo na saṃśayaḥ
ūrdhvamunnāmayatyeva sa oṅkāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
prāṇānavati yastasmāt praṇavaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
sarvaṃ vyāpnoti yastasmātsarvavyāpī sanātanaḥ
brahmā hariśca bhagavānādyantaṃ nopalabdhavān
tathānye ca tato 'nanto rudraḥ paramakāraṇam
yastārayati saṃsārāttāra ityabhidhīyate
sūkṣmo bhūtvā śarīrāṇi sarvadā hyadhitiṣṭhati
tasmātsūkṣmaḥ samākhyāto bhagavannīlalohitaḥ
nīlaśca lohitaścaiva pradhānapuruṣānvayāt
skandate 'sya yataḥ śukraṃ tathā śukram apaiti ca
vidyotayati yastasmādvaidyutaḥ parigīyate
bṛhattvād bṛṃhaṇatvācca bṛhate ca parāpare
tasmādbṛṃhati yasmāddhi paraṃ brahmeti kīrtitam
advitīyo 'tha bhagavāṃsturīyaḥ parameśvaraḥ
īśānamasya jagataḥ svardṛśāṃ cakṣur īśvaram
īśānamindrasūrayaḥ sarveṣāmapi sarvadā
īśānaḥ sarvavidyānāṃ yattadīśāna ucyate
yadīkṣate ca bhagavānnirīkṣyamiti cājñayā
ātmajñānaṃ mahādevo yogaṃ gamayati svayam
bhagavāṃścocyate devo devadevo maheśvaraḥ
sarvāṃllokānkrameṇaiva yo gṛhṇati maheśvaraḥ
visṛjatyeṣa deveśo vāsayatyapi līlayā
eṣo hi devaḥ pradiśo 'nusarvāḥ pūrvo hi jātaḥ sa u garbhe antaḥ
sa eva jātaḥ sa janiṣyamāṇaḥ pratyaṅmukhastiṣṭhati sarvatomukhaḥ
upāsitavyaṃ yatnena tadetatsadbhiravyayam
yato vāco nivartante hyaprāpya manasā saha
tadagrahaṇameveha yadvāgvadati yatnataḥ
aparaṃ ca paraṃ veti parāyaṇamiti svayam
vadanti vācaḥ sarvajñaṃ śaṅkaraṃ nīlalohitam
eṣa sarvo namastasmai puruṣaḥ piṅgalaḥ śivaḥ
sa eṣa sa mahārudro viśvaṃ bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyati
bhuvanaṃ bahudhā jātaṃ jāyamānamitastataḥ
hiraṇyabāhurbhagavān hiraṇyapatirīśvaraḥ
aṃbikāpatirīśāno hemaretā vṛṣadhvajaḥ
umāpatirvirūpākṣo viśvasṛgviśvavāhanaḥ
brahmāṇaṃ vidadhe yo 'sau putramagre sanātanam
prahiṇoti sma tasyaiva jñānamātmaprakāśakam
tamekaṃ puruṣaṃ rudraṃ puruhutaṃ puruṣṭutam
vālāgramātraṃ hṛdayasya madhye viśvaṃ devaṃ vahnirūpaṃ vareṇyam
tamātmasthaṃ ye 'nupaśyanti dhīrāsteṣāṃ śāntiḥ śāśvatī netareṣām
mahato yo mahīyāṃśca hyaṇorapyaṇuravyayaḥ
guhāyāṃ nihitaścātmā jantorasya maheśvaraḥ
veśmabhūto 'sya viśvasya kamalastho hṛdi svayam
gahvaraṃ gahanaṃ tatsthaṃ tasyāntaścordhvataḥ sthitaḥ
tatrāpi dahraṃ gaganam oṅkāraṃ parameśvaram
vālāgramātraṃ tanmadhye ṛtaṃ paramakāraṇam
satyaṃ brahma mahādevaṃ puruṣaṃ kṛṣṇapiṅgalam
ūrdhvaretasam īśānaṃ virūpākṣamajodbhavam
adhitiṣṭhati yoniṃ yo yoniṃ vācaika īśvaraḥ
dehaṃ pañcavidhaṃ yena tamīśānaṃ purātanam
prāṇeṣvantarmanaso liṅgamāhuryasminkrodho yā ca tṛṣṇā kṣamā ca
tṛṣṇāṃ chittvā hetujālasya mūlaṃ buddhyā cintyaṃ sthāpayitvā ca rudre
ekaṃ tamāhurvai rudraṃ śāśvataṃ parameśvaram
parātparataraṃ vāpi parātparataraṃ dhruvam
brahmaṇo janakaṃ viṣṇorvahnervāyoḥ sadāśivam
dhyātvāgninā ca śodhyāṅgaṃ viśodhya ca pṛthakpṛthak
pañcabhūtāni saṃyamya mātrāvidhiguṇakramāt
mātrāḥ pañca catasraśca trimātrā dvistataḥ param
ekamātramamātraṃ hi dvādaśānte vyavasthitam
sthitvā sthāpyāmṛto bhūtvā vrataṃ pāśupataṃ caret
etadvrataṃ pāśupataṃ cariṣyāmi samāsataḥ
agnimādhāya vidhivad ṛgyajuḥsāmasaṃbhavaiḥ
upoṣitaḥ śuciḥ snātaḥ śuklāṃbaradharaḥ svayam
śuklayajñopavīti ca śuklamālyānulepanaḥ
juhuyād virajo vidvān virajāśca bhaviṣyati
vāyavaḥ pañca śudhyatāṃ vāṅmanaścaraṇādayaḥ
śrotraṃ jihvā tataḥ prāṇastato buddhistathaiva ca
śiraḥ pāṇistathā pārśvaṃ pṛṣṭhodaramanantaram
jaṅghe śiśnam upasthaṃ ca pāyurmeḍhraṃ tathaiva ca
tvacā māṃsaṃ ca rudhiraṃ medo 'sthīni tathaiva ca
śabdaḥ sparśaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca raso gandhastathaiva ca
bhūtāni caiva śudhyantāṃ dehe medādayastathā
annaṃ prāṇe mano jñānaṃ śudhyantāṃ vai śivecchayā
hutvājyena samidbhiśca caruṇā ca yathākramam
upasaṃhṛtya rudrāgniṃ gṛhītvā bhasma yatnataḥ
agnirityādinā dhīmān vimṛjyāṅgāni saṃspṛśet
etatpāśupataṃ divyaṃ vrataṃ pāśavimocanam
brāhmaṇānāṃ hitaṃ proktaṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ tathaiva ca
vaiśyānāmapi yogyānāṃ yatīnāṃ tu viśeṣataḥ
vānaprasthāśramasthānāṃ gṛhasthānāṃ satāmapi
vimuktirvidhinānena dṛṣṭvā vai brahmacāriṇām
agnirityādinā bhasma gṛhītvā hyagnihotrajam
so 'pi pāśupato vipro vimṛjyāṅgāni saṃspṛśet
bhasmācchanno dvijo vidvān mahāpātakasaṃbhavaiḥ
pāpair vimucyate sadyo mucyate ca na saṃśayaḥ
vīryam agneryato bhasma vīryavānbhasmasaṃyutaḥ
bhasmasnānarato vipro bhasmaśāyī jitendriyaḥ
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ śivasāyujyamāpnuyāt
tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhūtyaṅgaṃ pūjayed budhaḥ
rerekāro na kartavyas tuṃtuṃkārastathaiva ca
na tatkṣamati deveśo brahmā vā yadi keśavaḥ
mama putro bhasmadhārī gaṇeśaśca varānane
teṣāṃ viruddhaṃ yattyājyaṃ sa yāti narakārṇavam
gṛhastho brahmahīno'pi tripuṇḍraṃ yo na kārayet
pūjā karma kriyā tasya dānaṃ snānaṃ tathaiva ca
niṣphalaṃ jāyate sarvaṃ yathā bhasmani vai hutam
tasmācca sarvakāryeṣu tripuṇḍraṃ dhārayedbudhaḥ
ityuktvā bhagavānbrahmā stutvā devaiḥ samaṃ prabhuḥ
bhasmācchannaiḥ svayaṃ channo virarāma viśāṃpate
atha teṣāṃ prasādārthaṃ paśūnāṃ patirīśvaraḥ
sagaṇaścāṃbayā sārdhaṃ sānnidhyamakarotprabhuḥ
atha saṃnihitaṃ rudraṃ tuṣṭuvuḥ surapuṅgavam
rudrādhyāyena sarveśaṃ devadevam umāpatim
devo'pi devānālokya ghṛṇayā vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ
tuṣṭo'smītyāha devebhyo varaṃ dātuṃ surārihā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge 'ṣṭādaśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
taṃ prabhuṃ prītamanasaṃ praṇipatya vṛṣadhvajam
apṛcchanmunayo devāḥ prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ
devā ūcuḥ
bhagavān kena mārgeṇa pūjanīyo dvijātibhiḥ
kutra vā kena rūpeṇa vaktumarhasi śaṅkara
kasyādhikāraḥ pūjāyāṃ brāhmaṇasya kathaṃ prabho
kṣatriyāṇāṃ kathaṃ deva vaiśyānāṃ vṛṣabhadhvaja
strīśūdrāṇāṃ kathaṃ vāpi kuṇḍagolādināṃ tu vā
hitāya jagatāṃ sarvamasmākaṃ vaktumarhasi
sūta uvāca
teṣāṃ bhāvaṃ samālokya munīnāṃ nīlalohitaḥ
prāha gaṃbhīrayā vācā maṇḍalasthaḥ sadāśivaḥ
maṇḍale cāgrataḥ paśyandevadevaṃ sahomayā
devāśca munayaḥ sarve vidyutkoṭisamaprabham
aṣṭabāhuṃ caturvaktraṃ dvādaśākṣaṃ mahābhujam
ardhanārīśvaraṃ devaṃ jaṭāmukuṭadhāriṇam
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ raktamālyānulepanam
raktāṃbaradharaṃ sṛṣṭisthitisaṃhārakārakam
tasya pūrvamukhaṃ pītaṃ prasannaṃ puruṣātmakam
aghoraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ vaktraṃ nīlāñjanacayopamam
daṃṣṭrākarālamatyugraṃ jvālāmālāsamāvṛtam
raktaśmaśruṃ jaṭāyuktaṃ cottare vidrumaprabham
prasannaṃ vāmadevākhyaṃ varadaṃ viśvarūpiṇam
paścimaṃ vadanaṃ tasya gokṣīradhavalaṃ śubham
muktāphalamayairhārairbhūṣitaṃ tilakojjvalam
sadyojātamukhaṃ divyaṃ bhāskarasya smarāriṇaḥ
ādityam agrataḥ paśyanpūrvavaccaturānanam
bhāskaraṃ purato devaṃ caturvaktraṃ ca pūrvavat
bhānuṃ dakṣiṇato devaṃ caturvaktraṃ ca pūrvavat
ravimuttarato 'paśyanpūrvavaccaturānanam
vistārāṃ maṇḍale pūrve uttarāṃ dakṣiṇe sthitām
bodhanīṃ paścime bhāge maṇḍalasya prajāpateḥ
adhyāyanīṃ ca kauberyāmekavaktrāṃ caturbhujām
sarvābharaṇasampannāḥ śaktayaḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe bhāge viṣṇuṃ vāme janārdanam
ṛgyajuḥsāmamārgeṇa mūrtitrayamayaṃ śivam
īśānaṃ varadaṃ devamīśānaṃ parameśvaram
brahmāsanasthaṃ varadaṃ dharmajñānāsanopari
vairāgyaiśvaryasaṃyukte prabhūte vimale tathā
sāraṃ sarveśvaraṃ devamārādhyaṃ paramaṃ sukham
sitapaṅkajamadhyasthaṃ dīptādyair abhisaṃvṛtam
dīptāṃ dīpaśikhākārāṃ sūkṣmāṃ vidyutprabhāṃ śubhām
jayām agniśikhākārāṃ prabhāṃ kanakasaprabhām
vibhūtiṃ vidrumaprakhyāṃ vimalāṃ padmasannibhām
amoghāṃ karṇikākārāṃ vidyutaṃ viśvavarṇinīm
caturvaktrāṃ caturvarṇāṃ devīṃ vai sarvatomukhīm
somamaṅgārakaṃ devaṃ budhaṃ buddhimatāṃ varam
bṛhaspatiṃ bṛhadbuddhiṃ bhārgavaṃ tejasāṃ nidhim
mandaṃ mandagatiṃ caiva samantāttasya te sadā
sūryaṃ śivo jagannāthaḥ somaḥ sākṣādumā svayam
pañcabhūtāni śeṣāṇi tanmayaṃ ca carācaram
dṛṣṭvaiva munayaḥ sarve devadevamumāpatim
kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ sarve munayo devatāstathā
astuvan vāgbhir iṣṭābhir varadaṃ nīlalohitam
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
namaḥ śivāya rudrāya kadrudrāya pracetase
mīḍhuṣṭamāya śarvāya śipiviṣṭāya raṃhase
prabhūte vimale sāre hyādhāre parame sukhe
navaśaktyāvṛtaṃ devaṃ padmasthaṃ bhāskaraṃ prabhum
ādityaṃ bhāskaraṃ bhānuṃ raviṃ devaṃ divākaram
umāṃ prabhāṃ tathā prajñāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sāvitrikāmapi
vistārām uttarāṃ devīṃ bodhanīṃ praṇamāmyaham
āpyāyanīṃ ca varadāṃ brahmāṇaṃ keśavaṃ haram
somādivṛndaṃ ca yathākrameṇa sampūjya mantrairvihitakrameṇa
smarāmi devaṃ ravimaṇḍalasthaṃ sadāśivaṃ śaṅkaramādidevam
indrādidevāṃśca tatheśvarāṃśca nārāyaṇaṃ padmajamādidevam
prāgādyadhordhvaṃ ca yathākrameṇa vajrādipadmaṃ ca tathā smarāmi
siṃdūravarṇāya samaṇḍalāya suvarṇavajrābharaṇāya tubhyam
padmābhanetrāya sapaṅkajāya brahmendranārāyaṇakāraṇāya
rathaṃ ca saptāśvamanūruvīraṃ gaṇaṃ tathā saptavidhaṃ krameṇa
ṛtupravāheṇa ca vālakhilyān smarāmi mandehagaṇakṣayaṃ ca
hutvā tilādyair vividhais tathāgnau punaḥ samāpyaiva tathaiva sarvam
udvāsya hṛtpaṅkajamadhyasaṃsthaṃ smarāmi biṃbaṃ tava devadeva
smarāmi biṃbāni yathākrameṇa raktāni padmāmalalocanāni
padmaṃ ca savye varadaṃ ca vāme kare tathā bhūṣitabhūṣaṇāni
daṃṣṭrākarālaṃ tava divyavaktraṃ vidyutprabhaṃ daityabhayaṅkaraṃ ca
smarāmi rakṣābhirataṃ dvijānāṃ mandeharakṣogaṇabhartsanaṃ ca
somaṃ sitaṃ bhūmijam agnivarṇaṃ cāmīkarābhaṃ budhamindusūnum
bṛhaspatiṃ kāñcanasaṃnikāśaṃ śukraṃ sitaṃ kṛṣṇataraṃ ca mandam
smarāmi savyamabhayaṃ vāmamūrugataṃ varam
sarveṣāṃ mandaparyantaṃ mahādevaṃ ca bhāskaram
pūrṇenduvarṇena ca puṣpagandhaprasthena toyena śubhena pūrṇam
pātraṃ dṛḍhaṃ tāmramayaṃ prakalpya dāsye tavārghyaṃ bhagavanprasīda
namaḥ śivāya devāya īśvarāya kapardine
rudrāya viṣṇave tubhyaṃ brahmaṇe sūryamūrtaye
sūta uvāca
yaḥ śivaṃ maṇḍale devaṃ sampūjyaivaṃ samāhitaḥ
prātarmadhyāhnasāyāhne paṭhetstavamanuttamam
itthaṃ śivena sāyujyaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekonaviṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
ato rudro mahādevo maṇḍalasthaḥ pitāmahaḥ
pūjyo vai brāhmaṇānāṃ ca kṣatriyāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ
vaiśyānāṃ naiva śūdrāṇāṃ śuśrūṣāṃ pūjakasya ca
strīṇāṃ naivādhikāro 'sti pūjādiṣu na saṃśayaḥ
strīśūdrāṇāṃ dvijendraiśca pūjayā tatphalaṃ bhavet
nṛpāṇāmupakārārthaṃ brāhmaṇādyairviśeṣataḥ
evaṃ sampūjayeyur vai brāhmaṇādyāḥ sadāśivam
ityuktvā bhagavān rudrastatraivāntaradhātsvayam
te devā munayaḥ sarve śivamuddiśya śaṅkaram
praṇemuśca mahātmāno rudradhyānena vihvalāḥ
jagmur yathāgataṃ devā munayaśca tapodhanāḥ
tasmād abhyarcayennityamādityaṃ śivarūpiṇam
dharmakāmārthamuktyarthaṃ manasā karmaṇā girā
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
romaharṣaṇa sarvajña sarvaśāstrabhṛtāṃ vara
vyāsaśiṣya mahābhāga vāhneyaṃ vada sāṃpratam
śivena devadevena bhaktānāṃ hitakāmyayā
vedāt ṣaḍaṅgāduddhṛtya sāṃkhyayogācca sarvataḥ
tapaśca vipulaṃ taptvā devadānavaduścaram
