arthadeśādisaṃyuktaṃ gūḍhamajñānaninditam
varṇāśramakṛtairdharmairviparītaṃ kvacitsamam
śivena kathitaṃ śāstraṃ dharmakāmārthamuktaye
śatakoṭipramāṇena tatra pūjā kathaṃ vibhoḥ
snānayogādayo vāpi śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ
sūta uvāca
purā sanatkumāreṇa merupṛṣṭhe suśobhane
pṛṣṭo nandīśvaro devaḥ śailādiḥ śivasaṃmataḥ
pṛṣṭo'yaṃ praṇipatyaivaṃ munimukhyaiśca sarvataḥ
tasmai sanatkumārāya nandinā kulanandinā
kathitaṃ yacchivajñānaṃ śṛṇvantu munipuṅgavāḥ
śaivaṃ saṃkṣipya vedoktaṃ śivena paribhāṣitam
stutinindādirahitaṃ sadyaḥ pratyayakārakam
guruprasādajaṃ divyamanāyāsena muktidam
sanatkumāra uvāca
bhagavansarva bhūteśa nandīśvara maheśvara
kathaṃ pūjādayaḥ śaṃbhordharmakāmārthamuktaye
vaktumarhasi śailāde vinayenāgatāya me
sūta uvāca
samprekṣya bhagavānnandī niśamya vacanaṃ punaḥ
kālavelādhikārādyam avadad vadatāṃ varaḥ
śailādir uvāca
gurutaḥ śāstrataścaivamadhikāraṃ bravīmyaham
gauravādeva saṃjñaiṣā śivācāryasya nānyathā
svayamācarate yastu ācāre sthāpayatyapi
ācinoti ca śāstrārthān ācāryastena cocyate
tasmādvedārthatattvajñamācāryaṃ bhasmaśāyinam
gurumanveṣayedbhaktaḥ subhagaṃ priyadarśanam
pratipannaṃ janānandaṃ śrutismṛtipathānugam
vidyayābhayadātāraṃ laulyacāpalyavarjitam
ācārapālakaṃ dhīraṃ samayeṣu kṛtāspadam
taṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvabhāvena pūjayecchivavadgurum
ātmanā ca dhanenaiva śraddhāvittānusārataḥ
tāvadārādhayecchiṣyaḥ prasanno 'sau yathā bhavet
suprasanne mahābhāge sadyaḥ pāśakṣayo bhavet
gururmānyo guruḥ pūjyo gurureva sadāśivaḥ
saṃvatsaratrayaṃ vātha śiṣyānviprānparīkṣayet
prāṇadravyapradānena ādeśaiśca itastataḥ
uttamaścādhame yojyo nīca uttamavastuṣu
ākṛṣṭāstāḍitā vāpi ye viṣādaṃ na yānti vai
te yogyāḥ śivadharmiṣṭhāḥ śivadharmaparāyaṇāḥ
saṃyatā dharmasampannāḥ śrutismṛtipathānugāḥ
sarvadvandvasahā dhīrā nityamudyuktacetasaḥ
paropakāraniratā guruśuśrūṣaṇe ratāḥ
ārjavā mārdavāḥ svasthā anukūlāḥ priyaṃvadāḥ
amānino buddhimantastyaktaspardhā gataspṛhāḥ
śaucācāraguṇopetā dambhamātsaryavarjitāḥ
yogyā evaṃ dvijāḥ sarve śivabhaktiparāyaṇāḥ
evaṃvṛttasamopetā vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhiḥ
śodhyā evaṃvidhāścaiva tattvānāṃ ca viśuddhaye
śuddho vinayasampanno mithyākaṭukavarjitaḥ
gurvājñāpālakaścaiva śiṣyo 'nugrahamarhati
guruśca śāstravit prājñas tapasvī janavatsalaḥ
lokācārarato hyevaṃ tattvavinmokṣadaḥ smṛtaḥ
sarvalakṣaṇasampannaḥ sarvaśāstraviśāradaḥ
sarvopāyavidhānajñastattvahīnasya niṣphalam
svasaṃvedya pare tattve niścayo yasya nātmani
ātmano 'nugraho nāsti parasyānugrahaḥ katham
prabuddhastu dvijo yastu sa śuddhaḥ sādhayatyapi
tattvahīne kuto bodhaḥ kuto hyātmaparigrahaḥ
parigrahavinirmuktāste sarve paśava uditāḥ
paśubhiḥ preritā ye tu sarve te paśavaḥ smṛtāḥ
tasmāt tattvavido ye tu te muktā mocayanty api
saṃvittijananaṃ tattvaṃ parānandasamudbhavam
tattvaṃ tu viditaṃ yena sa evānandadarśakaḥ
na punarnāmamātreṇa saṃvittirahitastu yaḥ
anyo 'nyaṃ tārayennaiva kiṃ śilā tārayecchilām
yeṣāṃ tannāmamātreṇa muktirvai nāmamātrikā
yogināṃ darśanādvāpi sparśanādbhāṣaṇādapi
sadyaḥ saṃjāyate cājñā pāśopakṣayakāriṇī
athavā yogamārgeṇa śiṣyadehaṃ praviśya ca
bodhayed eva yogena sarvatattvāni śodhya ca
ṣaḍardhaśuddhir vihitā jñānayogena yoginām
śiṣyaṃ parīkṣya dharmajñaṃ dhārmikaṃ vedapāragam
brāhmaṇaṃ kṣatriyaṃ vaiśyaṃ bahudoṣavivarjitam
jñānena jñeyamālokya karṇāt karṇāgatena tu
dīpāddīpo yathā cānyaḥ saṃcared vidhivad guruḥ
bhauvanaṃ ca padaṃ caiva varṇākhyaṃ mātramuttamam
kālādhvaraṃ mahābhāga tattvākhyaṃ sarvasaṃmatam
bhidyate yasya sāmarthyād ājñāmātreṇa sarvataḥ
tasya siddhiśca muktiśca gurukāruṇyasaṃbhavā
pṛthivyādīni bhūtāni āviśanti ca bhauvane
śabdaḥ sparśastathā rūpaṃ raso gandhaśca bhāvataḥ
padaṃ varṇākhyakaṃ vipra buddhīndriyavikalpanam
karmendriyāṇi mātraṃ hi mano buddhirataḥ param
ahaṅkāramathāvyaktaṃ kālādhvaramiti smṛtam
puruṣādiviriñcyantamunmanatvaṃ parātparam
tatheśatvamiti proktaṃ sarvatattvārthabodhakam
ayogī naiva jānāti tattvaśuddhiṃ śivātmikām
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge viṃśo'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
parīkṣya bhūmiṃ vidhivadgandhavarṇarasādibhiḥ
alaṃkṛtya vitānādyairīśvarāvāhanakṣamām
ekahastapramāṇena maṇḍalaṃ parikalpayet
ālikhetkamalaṃ madhye pañcaratnasamanvitam
cūrṇairaṣṭadalaṃ vṛttaṃ sitaṃ vā raktameva ca
parivāreṇa saṃyuktaṃ bahuśobhāsamanvitam
āvāhya karṇikāyāṃ tu śivaṃ paramakāraṇam
arcayetsarvayatnena yathāvibhavavistaram
daleṣu siddhayaḥ proktāḥ karṇikāyāṃ mahāmune
vairāgyajñānanālaṃ ca dharmakandaṃ manoramam
vāmā jyeṣṭhā ca raudrī ca kālī vikaraṇī tathā
balavikaraṇī caiva balapramathinī kramāt
sarvabhūtasya damanī kesareṣu ca śaktayaḥ
manonmanī mahāmāyā karṇikāyāṃ śivāsane
vāmadevādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ dvandvanyāyena vinyaset
manonmanaṃ mahādevaṃ manonmanyātha madhyataḥ
sūryasomāgnisaṃbandhātpraṇavākhyaṃ śivātmakam
puruṣaṃ vinyasedvaktraṃ pūrve patre raviprabham
aghoraṃ dakṣiṇe pattre nīlāñjanacayopamam
uttare vāmadevākhyaṃ japākusumasannibham
sadyaṃ paścimapatre tu gokṣīradhavalaṃ nyaset
īśānaṃ karṇikāyāṃ tu śuddhasphaṭikasannibham
candramaṇḍalasaṃkāśaṃ hṛdayāyeti mantrataḥ
vāhneye rudradigbhāge śirase dhūmravarcase
śikhāyai ca namaśceti raktābhe nairṛte dale
kavacāyāñjanābhāya iti vāyudale nyaset
astrāyāgniśikhābhāya iti dikṣu pravinyaset
netrebhyaśceti caiśānyāṃ piṅgalebhyaḥ pravinyaset
śivaṃ sadāśivaṃ devaṃ maheśvaramataḥ param
rudraṃ viṣṇuṃ viriñciṃ ca sṛṣṭinyāyena bhāvayet
śivāya rudrarūpāya śāntyatītāya śaṃbhave
śāntāya śāntadaityāya namaścandramase tathā
vedyāya vidyādhārāya vahnaye vahnivarcase
kālāyai ca pratiṣṭhāyai tārakāyāntakāya ca
nivṛttyai dhanadevāya dhārāyai dhāraṇāya ca
mantrairetairmahābhūtavigrahaṃ ca sadāśivam
īśānamukuṭaṃ devaṃ puruṣāsyaṃ purātanam
aghorahṛdayaṃ hṛṣṭaṃ vāmaguhyaṃ maheśvaram
sadyamūrtiṃ smareddevaṃ sadasadvyaktikāraṇam
pañcavaktraṃ daśabhujamaṣṭatriṃśatkalāmayam
sadyamaṣṭaprakāreṇa prabhidya ca kalāmayam
vāmaṃ trayodaśavidhair vibhidya vitataṃ prabhum
aghoramaṣṭadhā kṛtvā kalārūpeṇa saṃsthitam
puruṣaṃ ca caturdhā vai vibhajya ca kalāmayam
īśānaṃ pañcadhā kṛtvā pañcamūrtyā vyavasthitam
haṃsa haṃseti mantreṇa śivabhaktyā samanvitam
oṅkāramātram oṅkāram akāraṃ samarūpiṇam
ā ī ū e tathā aṃbānukrameṇātmarūpiṇam
pradhānasahitaṃ devaṃ pralayotpattivarjitam
aṇoraṇīyāṃsamajaṃ mahato 'pi mahattamam
ūrdhvaretasam īśānaṃ virūpākṣamumāpatim
sahasraśirasaṃ devaṃ sahasrākṣaṃ sanātanam
sahasrahastacaraṇaṃ nādāntaṃ nādavigraham
khadyotasadṛśākāraṃ candrarekhākṛtiṃ prabhum
dvādaśānte bhruvormadhye tālumadhye gale kramāt
hṛddeśe 'vasthitaṃ devaṃ svānandamamṛtaṃ śivam
vidyudvalayasaṃkāśaṃ vidyutkoṭisamaprabham
śyāmaṃ raktaṃ kalākāraṃ śaktitrayakṛtāsanam
sadāśivaṃ smareddevaṃ tattvatrayasamanvitam
vidyāmūrtimayaṃ devaṃ pūjayecca yathākramāt
lokapālāṃstathāstreṇa pūrvādyānpūjayet pṛthak
caruṃ ca vidhināsādya śivāya vinivedayet
ardhaṃ śivāya dattvaiva śeṣārdhena tu homayet
aghoreṇātha śiṣyāya dāpayedbhoktumuttamam
upaspṛśya śucirbhūtvā puruṣaṃ vidhinā yajet
pañcagavyaṃ tataḥ prāśya īśānenābhimantritam
vāmadevena bhasmāṅgī bhasmanoddhūlayet kramāt
karṇayośca japeddevīṃ gāyatrīṃ rudradevatām
sasūtraṃ sapidhānaṃ ca vastrayugmena veṣṭitam
tatpūrvaṃ hemaratnaughairvāsitaṃ vai hiraṇmayam
kalaśānvinyasetpañca pañcabhirbrāhmaṇaistataḥ
homaṃ ca caruṇā kuryādyathāvibhavavistaram
śiṣyaṃ ca vāsayedbhaktaṃ dakṣiṇe maṇḍalasya tu
darbhaśayyāsamārūḍhaṃ śivadhyānaparāyaṇam
aghoreṇa yathānyāyamaṣṭottaraśataṃ punaḥ
ghṛtena hutvā duḥsvapnaṃ prabhāte śodhayenmalam
evaṃ copoṣitaṃ śiṣyaṃ snātaṃ bhūṣitavigraham
navavastrottarīyaṃ ca soṣṇīṣaṃ kṛtamaṅgalam
dukūlādyena vastreṇa netraṃ baddhvā praveśayet
suvarṇapuṣpasaṃmiśraṃ yathāvibhavavistaram
īśānena ca mantreṇa kuryātpuṣpāñjaliṃ prabhoḥ
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā rudrādhyāyena vā punaḥ
kevalaṃ praṇavenātha śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
dhyātvā tu devadeveśamīśāne saṃkṣipetsvayam
yasminmantre patetpuṣpaṃ tanmantrastasya sidhyati
śivāṃbhasā tu saṃspṛśya aghoreṇa ca bhasmanā
śiṣyamūrdhani vinyasya gandhādyaiḥ śiṣyamarcayet
vāruṇaṃ paramaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dvāraṃ vai sarvavarṇinām
kṣattriyāṇāṃ viśeṣeṇa dvāraṃ vai paścimaṃ smṛtam
netrāvaraṇamunmucya maṇḍalaṃ darśayettataḥ
kuśāsane tu saṃsthāpya dakṣiṇāmūrtimāsthitaḥ
tattvaśuddhiṃ tataḥ kuryātpañcatattvaprakārataḥ
nivṛttyā rudraparyantamaṇḍamaṇḍodbhavātmaja
pratiṣṭhayā tadūrdhvaṃ ca yāvadavyaktagocaram
viśveśvarāntaṃ vai vidyā kalāmātreṇa suvrata
tadūrdhvamārgaṃ saṃśodhya śivabhaktyā śivaṃ nayet
samarcanāya tattvasya tasya bhogeśvarasya vai
tattvatrayaprabhedena caturbhiruta vā tathā
homayed aṅgamantreṇa śāntyatītaṃ sadāśivam
sadyādibhistu śāntyantaṃ caturbhiḥ kalayā pṛthak
śāntyatītaṃ muniśreṣṭha īśānenāthavā punaḥ
pratyekamaṣṭottaraśataṃ diśā homaṃ tu kārayet
īśānyāṃ pañcamenātha pradhānaṃ parigīyate
samidājyacarūṃl lājān sarṣapāṃś ca yavāṃs tilān
dravyāṇi sapta hotavyaṃ svāhāntaṃ praṇavādikam
teṣāṃ pūrṇāhutirvipra īśānena vidhīyate
sahaṃsena yathānyāyaṃ praṇavādyena suvrata
aghoreṇa ca mantreṇa prāyaścittaṃ vidhīyate
jayādisviṣṭaparyantam agnikāryaṃ krameṇa tu
guṇasaṃkhyāprakāreṇa pradhānena ca yojayet
bhūtāni brahmabhirvāpi maunī bījādibhistathā
atha pradhānamātreṇa prāṇāpānau niyamya ca
ṣaṣṭhena bhedayedātmapraṇavāntaṃ kulākulam
anyo 'nyamupasaṃhṛtya brahmāṇaṃ keśavaṃ haram
rudre rudraṃ tamīśāne śive devaṃ maheśvaram
tasmāt sṛṣṭiprakāreṇa bhāvayedbhavanāśanam
sthāpyātmānam amuṃ jīvaṃ tāḍanaṃ dvāradarśanam
dīpanaṃ grahaṇaṃ caiva bandhanaṃ pūjayā saha
amṛtīkaraṇaṃ caiva kārayedvidhipūrvakam
ṣaṣṭhāntaṃ sadyasaṃyuktaṃ tṛtīyena samanvitam
phaḍantaṃ saṃhṛtiḥ proktā pañcabhūtaprakārataḥ
sadyādyaṣaṣṭhasahitaṃ śikhāntaṃ saphaḍantakam
tāḍanaṃ kathitaṃ dvāraṃ tattvānāmapi yoginaḥ
pradhānaṃ saṃpuṭīkṛtya tṛtīyena ca dīpanam
ādyena saṃpuṭīkṛtya pradhānaṃ grahaṇaṃ smṛtam
pradhānaṃ prathamenaiva saṃpuṭīkṛtya pūrvavat
bandhanaṃ paripūrṇena plāvanaṃ cāmṛtena ca
śāntyatītā tataḥ śāntirvidyā nāma kalāmalā
pratiṣṭhā ca nivṛttiśca kalāsaṃkramaṇaṃ smṛtā
tattvavarṇakalāyuktaṃ bhuvanena yathākramam
mantraiḥ pādaiḥ stavaṃ kuryādviśodhya ca yathāvidhi
ādyena yonibījena kalpayitvā ca pūrvavat
pūjāsamprokṣaṇaṃ viddhi tāḍanaṃ haraṇaṃ tathā
saṃhatasya ca saṃyogaṃ vikṣepaṃ ca yathākramam
arcanā ca tathā garbhadhāraṇaṃ jananaṃ punaḥ
adhikāro bhavedbhānorlayaścaiva viśeṣataḥ
uttamādyaṃ tathāntyena yonibījena suvrata
uddhāre prokṣaṇe caiva tāḍane ca mahāmune
aghoreṇa phaḍantena saṃsṛtiśca na saṃśayaḥ
pratitattvaṃ kramo hyeṣa yogamārgeṇa suvrata
muṣṭinā caiva yāvacca tāvatkālaṃ nayetkramāt
viṣuveṇa tu yogena nivṛttyādi śivāntikam
ekatra samatāṃ yāti nānyathā tu pṛthakpṛthak
nāsāgre dvādaśāntena pṛṣṭhena saha yoginām
kṣantavyamiti viprendra devadevasya śāsanam
hemarājatatāmrādyairvidhinā kalpitena ca
sakūrcena savastreṇa tantunā veṣṭitena ca
tīrthāṃbupūritenaiva ratnagarbheṇa suvrata
saṃhitāmantritenaiva rudrādhyāyastutena ca
secayecca tataḥ śiṣyaṃ śivabhaktaṃ ca dhārmikam
so 'pi śiṣyaḥ śivasyāgre guror agre ca sādaram
vahneśca dīkṣāṃ kurvīta dīkṣitaśca tathācaret
varaṃ prāṇaparityāgaśchedanaṃ śiraso 'pi vā
na tvanabhyarcya bhuñjīyādbhagavantaṃ sadāśivam
evaṃ dīkṣā prakartavyā pūjā caiva yathākramam
trikālam ekakālaṃ vā pūjayetparameśvaram
agnihotraṃ ca vedāśca yajñāśca bahudakṣiṇāḥ
śivaliṅgārcanasyaite kalāṃśenāpi no samāḥ
sadā yajati yajñena sadā dānaṃ prayacchati
sadā ca vāyubhakṣaśca sakṛdyo 'bhyarcayecchivam
ekakālaṃ dvikālaṃ vā trikālaṃ nityameva vā
ye'rcayanti mahādevaṃ te rudrā nātra saṃśayaḥ
nārudrastu spṛśed rudraṃ nārudro rudramarcayet
nārudraḥ kīrtayed rudraṃ nārudro rudramāpnuyāt
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ prokto hyadhikārividhikramaḥ
śivārcanārthaṃ dharmārthakāmamokṣaphalapradaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dīkṣāvidhir nāmaikaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
snānayāgādikarmāṇi kṛtvā vai bhāskarasya ca
śivasnānaṃ tataḥ kuryādbhasmasnānaṃ śivārcanam
ṣaṣṭhena mṛdamādāya bhaktyā bhūmau nyasenmṛdam
dvitīyena tathābhyukṣya tṛtīyena ca śodhayet
caturthenaiva vibhajenmalamekena śodhayet
snātvā ṣaṣṭhena taccheṣāṃ mṛdaṃ hastagatāṃ punaḥ
tridhā vibhajya sarvaṃ ca caturbhirmadhyamaṃ punaḥ
ṣaṣṭhena saptavārāṇi vāmaṃ mūlena cālabhet
daśavāraṃ ca ṣaṣṭhena diśāṃ bandhaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
vāmena tīrthaṃ savyena śarīramanulipya ca
snātvā sarvaiḥsmaran bhānumabhiṣekaṃ samācaret
śṛṅgeṇa parṇapuṭakaiḥ pālāśena dalena vā
saurair ebhiśca vividhaiḥ sarvasiddhikaraiḥ śubhaiḥ
saurāṇi ca pravakṣyāmi bāṣkalādyāni suvrata
aṅgāni sarvadeveṣu sārabhūtāni sarvataḥ
oṃ bhūḥ oṃ bhuvaḥ oṃsvaḥ oṃ mahaḥ oṃ janaḥ oṃ tapaḥ oṃsatyam oṃ ṛtam oṃ brahmā
navākṣaramayaṃ mantraṃ bāṣkalaṃ parikīrtitam
na kṣarantīti lokāni ṛtamakṣaramucyate
satyam akṣaram ityuktaṃ praṇavādinamo'ntakam
oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ suvaḥ tatsaviturvareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi
oṃ namaḥ sūryāya khakholkāya namaḥ
mūlamantramidaṃ proktaṃ bhāskarasya mahātmanaḥ
navākṣareṇa dīptāsyaṃ mūlamantreṇa bhāskaram
pūjayed aṅgamantrāṇi kathayāmi yathākramam
vedādibhiḥ prabhūtādyaṃ praṇavena ca madhyamam
oṃ bhūḥ brahma hṛdayāya oṃ bhuvaḥ viṣṇuśirase oṃsvaḥ rudraśikhāyai oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ jvālāmālinīśikhāyai oṃ mahaḥ maheśvarāya kavacāya oṃ janaḥ śivāya netrebhyaḥ oṃ tapaḥ tāpakāya astrāya phaṭ mantrāṇi kathitānyevaṃ saurāṇi vividhāni ca
etaiḥ śṛṅgādibhiḥ pātraiḥ svātmānam abhiṣecayet
tāmrakuṃbhena vā vipraḥ kṣatriyo vaiśya eva ca
sakuśena sapuṣpeṇa mantraiḥ sarvaiḥ samāhitaḥ
raktavastraparīdhānaḥ svācāmedvidhipūrvakam
sūryaśceti divā rātrau cāgniśceti dvijottamaḥ
āpaḥ punantu madhyāhne mantrācamanamucyate
ṣaṣṭhena śuddhiṃ kṛtvaiva japedādyamanuttamam
vauṣaḍantaṃ tathā mūlaṃ navākṣaram anuttamam
karaśākhāṃ tathāṅguṣṭhamadhyamānāmikāṃ nyaset
tale ca tarjanyaṅguṣṭhaṃ muṣṭibhāgāni vinyaset
navākṣaramayaṃ dehaṃ kṛtvāṅgairapi pāvitam
sūryo 'hamiti saṃcintya mantrairetairyathākramam
vāmahastagatair adbhir gandhasiddhārthakānvitaiḥ
kuśapuñjena cābhyukṣya mūlāgrairaṣṭadhā sthitaiḥ
āpo hi ṣṭhādibhiścaiva śeṣamāghrāya vai jalam
vāmanāsāpuṭenaiva dehe saṃbhāvayecchivam
arghyamādāya dehasthaṃ savyanāsāpuṭena ca
kṛṣṇavarṇena bāhyasthaṃ bhāvayecca śilāgatam
tarpayetsarvadevebhya ṛṣibhyaśca viśeṣataḥ
bhūtebhyaśca pitṛbhyaśca vidhinārghyaṃ ca dāpayet
vyāpinīṃ ca parāṃ jyotsnāṃ saṃdhyāṃ samyag upāsayet
prātarmadhyāhnasāyāhne arghyaṃ caiva nivedayet
raktacandanatoyena hastamātreṇa maṇḍalam
suvṛttaṃ kalpayedbhūmau prārthayeta dvijottamāḥ
prāṅmukhas tāmrapātraṃ ca sagandhaṃ prasthapūritam
pūrayedgandhatoyena raktacandanakena ca
raktapuṣpaistilaiścaiva kuśākṣatasamanvitaiḥ
dūrvāpāmārgagavyena kevalena ghṛtena ca
āpūrya mūlamantreṇa navākṣaramayena ca
jānubhyāṃ dharaṇīṃ gatvā devadevaṃ namasya ca
kṛtvā śirasi tatpātram arghyamūlena dāpayet
aśvamedhāyutaṃ kṛtvā yatphalaṃ parikīrtitam
tatphalaṃ labhate dattvā saurārghyaṃ sarvasaṃmatam
dattvaivārghyaṃ yajedbhaktyā devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam
athavā bhāskaraṃ ceṣṭvā āgneyaṃ snānamācaret
pūrvavadvai śivasnānaṃ mantramātreṇa bheditam
dantadhāvanapūrvaṃ ca snānaṃ sauraṃ ca śāṅkaram
vighneśaṃ varuṇaṃ caiva guruṃ tīrthaṃ samarcayet
baddhvā padmāsanaṃ tīrthe tathā tīrthaṃ samarcayet
tīrthaṃ saṃgṛhya vidhinā pūjāsthānaṃ praviśya ca
mārgeṇārghyapavitreṇa tadākramya ca pādukam
pūrvavatkaravinyāsaṃ dehavinyāsamācaret
arghyasya sādanaṃ caiva samāsātparikīrtitam
baddhvā padmāsanaṃ yogī prāṇāyāmaṃ samabhyaset
raktapuṣpāṇi saṃgṛhya kamalādyāni bhāvayet
ātmano dakṣiṇe sthāpya jalabhāṇḍaṃ ca vāmataḥ
tāmrapātrāṇi saurāṇi sarvakāmārthasiddhaye
arghyapātraṃ samādāya prakṣālya ca yathāvidhi
pūrvoktenāṃbunā sārdhaṃ jalabhāṇḍe tathaiva ca
astrodakena caivārghyamarghyadravyasamanvitam
saṃhitāmantritaṃ kṛtvā sampūjya prathamena ca
turīyeṇāvaguṇṭhyaiva sthāpayed ātmanopari
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca gandhapuṣpasamanvitam
aṃbhasā śodhite pātre sthāpayet pūrvavat pṛthak
saṃhitāṃ caiva vinyasya kavacenāvaguṇṭhya ca
arghyāmbunā samabhyukṣya dravyāṇi ca viśeṣataḥ
ādityaṃ ca japed devaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam
ādityo vai teja ūrjo balaṃ yaśo vivardhati
ityādinā namaskṛtya kalpayedāsanaṃ prabhoḥ
prabhūtaṃ vimalaṃ sāram ārādhyaṃ paramaṃ sukham
āgneyyādiṣu koṇeṣu madhyamāntaṃ hṛdā nyaset
aṅgaṃ pravinyaseccaiva bījamaṅkurameva ca
nālaṃ suṣirasaṃyuktaṃ sūtrakaṇṭakasaṃyutam
dalaṃ dalāgraṃ suśvetaṃ hemābhaṃ raktameva ca
karṇikākesaropetaṃ dīptādyaiḥ śaktibhirvṛtam
dīptā sūkṣmā jayā bhadrā vibhūtir vimalā kramāt
aghorā vikṛtā caiva dīptādyāścāṣṭaśaktayaḥ
bhāskarābhimukhāḥ sarvāḥ kṛtāñjalipuṭāḥ śubhāḥ
athavā padmahastā vā sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ
madhyato varadāṃ devīṃ sthāpayetsarvatomukhīm
āvāhayettato devīṃ bhāskaraṃ parameśvaram
navākṣareṇa mantreṇa bāṣkaloktena bhāskaram
āvāhane ca sānnidhyamanenaiva vidhīyate
mudrā ca padmamudrākhyā bhāskarasya mahātmanaḥ
mūlenārghyaṃ tato dadyātpādyamācamanaṃ pṛthak
punararghyapradānena bāṣkalena yathāvidhi
raktapadmāni puṣpāṇi raktacandanameva ca
dīpadhūpādinaivedyaṃ mukhavāsādir eva ca
tāṃbūlavartidīpādyaṃ bāṣkalena vidhīyate
āgneyyāṃ ca tathaiśānyāṃ nairṛtyāṃ vāyugocare
pūrvasyāṃ paścime caiva ṣaṭprakāraṃ vidhīyate
netrāntaṃ vidhinābhyarcya praṇavādinamo'ntakam
karṇikāyāṃ pravinyasya rūpakadhyānamācaret
sarve vidyutprabhāḥ śāntā raudramastraṃ prakīrtitam
daṃṣṭrākarālavadanaṃ hyaṣṭamūrti bhayaṅkaram
varadaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ padmavibhūṣitam
sarvābharaṇasampannā raktasraganulepanāḥ
raktāṃbaradharāḥ sarvā mūrtayastasya saṃsthitāḥ
samaṇḍalo mahādevaḥ siṃdūrāruṇavigrahaḥ
padmahasto 'mṛtāsyaśca dvihastanayanaḥ prabhuḥ
raktābharaṇasaṃyukto raktasraganulepanaḥ
itthaṃrūpadharaṃ dhyāyedbhāskaraṃ bhuvaneśvaram
padmabāhye śubhaṃ cātra maṇḍaleṣu samantataḥ
somamaṅgārakaṃ caiva budhaṃ buddhimatāṃvaram
bṛhaspatiṃ mahābuddhiṃ rudraputraṃ ca bhārgavam
śanaiścaraṃ tathā rāhuṃ ketuṃ dhūmraṃ prakīrtitam
sarve dvinetrā dvibhujā rāhuścordhvaśarīradhṛk
vivṛttāsyo 'ñjaliṃ kṛtvā bhrukuṭīkuṭilekṣaṇaḥ
śanaiścaraśca daṃṣṭrāsyo varadābhayahastadhṛk
svaiḥ svair bhāvaiḥ svanāmnā ca praṇavādinamo'ntakam
pūjanīyāḥ prayatnena dharmakāmārthasiddhaye
saptasaptagaṇāṃścaiva bahirdevasya pūjayet
ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ pannagāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ
grāmaṇyo yātudhānāśca tathā yakṣāśca mukhyataḥ
saptāśvān pūjayedagre saptacchandomayān vibhoḥ
vālakhilyagaṇaṃ caiva nirmālyagrahaṇaṃ vibhoḥ
pūjayedāsanaṃ mūrter devatāmapi pūjayet
arghyaṃ ca dāpayetteṣāṃ pṛthageva vidhānataḥ
āvāhane ca pūjānte teṣāmudvāsane tathā
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
bāṣkalaṃ ca japedagre daśāṃśena ca yojayet
kuṇḍaṃ ca paścime kuryādvartulaṃ caiva mekhalam
caturaṅgulamānena cotsedhādvistarādapi
ekahastapramāṇena nitye naimittike tathā
kṛtvāśvatthadalākāraṃ nābhiṃ kuṇḍe daśāṅgulam
tadardhena purastāttu gajoṣṭhasadṛśaṃ smṛtam
galamekāṅgulaṃ caiva śeṣaṃ dviguṇavistaram
tatpramāṇena kuṇḍasya tyaktvā kurvīta mekhalām
yatnena sādhayitvaiva paścāddhomaṃ ca kārayet
ṣaṣṭhenollekhanaṃ kuryāt prokṣayedvāriṇā punaḥ
āsanaṃ kalpayenmadhye prathamena samāhitaḥ
prabhāvatīṃ tataḥ śaktimādyenaiva tu vinyaset
bāṣkalenaiva sampūjya gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
bāṣkalenaiva mantreṇa kriyāṃ prati yajetpṛthak
mūlamantreṇa vidhinā paścātpūrṇāhutirbhavet
kramādevaṃ vidhānena sūryāgnirjanito bhavet
pūrvoktena vidhānena prāguktaṃ kamalaṃ nyaset
mukhopari samabhyarcya pūrvavadbhāskaraṃ prabhum
daśaivāhutayo deyā bāṣkalena mahāmune
aṅgānāṃ ca tathaikaikaṃ saṃhitābhiḥ pṛthak punaḥ
jayādisviṣṭaparyantam idhmaprakṣepameva ca
sāmānyaṃ sarvamārgeṣu pāraṃparyakrameṇa ca
nivedya devadevāya bhāskarāyāmitātmane
pūjāhomādikaṃ sarvaṃ dattvārghyaṃ ca pradakṣiṇam
aṅgaiḥ sampūjya saṃkṣipya hṛdyudvāsya namasya ca
śivapūjāṃ tataḥ kuryāddharmakāmārthasiddhaye
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ yajanaṃ bhāskarasya ca
yaḥ sakṛdvā yajeddevaṃ devadevaṃ jagadgurum
bhāskaraṃ paramātmānaṃ sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sarvapāpavivarjitaḥ
sarvaiśvaryasamopetas tejasāpratimaśca saḥ
putrapautrādimitraiśca bāndhavaiś ca samantataḥ
bhuktvaiva vipulān bhogānihaiva dhanadhānyavān
yānavāhanasampanno bhūṣaṇairvividhairapi
kālaṃ gato'pi sūryeṇa modate kālamakṣayam
punastasmādihāgatya rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ
vedavedāṅgasampanno brāhmaṇo vātra jāyate
punaḥ prāgvāsanāyogāddhārmiko vedapāragaḥ
sūryameva samabhyarcya sūryasāyujyamāpnuyāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvāviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
atha te sampravakṣyāmi śivārcanamanuttamam
trisaṃdhyam arcayed īśam agnikāryaṃ ca śaktitaḥ
śivasnānaṃ purā kṛtvā tattvaśuddhiṃ ca pūrvavat
puṣpahastaḥ praviśyātha pūjāsthānaṃ samāhitaḥ
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā dāhanāplāvanāni ca
gandhādivāsitakaro mahāmudrāṃ pravinyaset
vijñānena tanuṃ kṛtvā brahmāgnerapi yatnataḥ
avyaktabuddhyahaṅkāratanmātrāsaṃbhavāṃ tanum
śivāmṛtena saṃpūtaṃ śivasya ca yathātatham
adhoniṣṭyā vitastyāṃ tu nābhyāmupari tiṣṭhati
hṛdayaṃ tadvijānīyādviśvasyāyatanaṃ mahat
hṛtpadmakarṇikāyāṃ tu devaṃ sākṣātsadāśivam
pañcavaktraṃ daśabhujaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam
prativaktraṃ trinetraṃ ca śaśāṅkakṛtaśekharam
baddhapadmāsanāsīnaṃ śuddhasphaṭikasannibham
ūrdhvaṃ vaktraṃ sitaṃ dhyāyetpūrvaṃ kuṅkumasannibham
nīlābhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ vaktramatiraktaṃ tathottaram
gokṣīradhavalaṃ divyaṃ paścimaṃ parameṣṭhinaḥ
śūlaṃ paraśukhaḍgaṃ ca vajraṃ śaktiṃ ca dakṣiṇe
vāme pāśāṅkuśaṃ ghaṇṭāṃ nāgaṃ nārācamuttamam
varadābhayahastaṃ vā śeṣaṃ pūrvavadeva tu
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ citrāṃbaradharaṃ śivam
brahmāṅgavigrahaṃ devaṃ sarvadevottamottamam
pūjayetsarvabhāvena brahmāṅgairbrahmaṇaḥ patim
uktāni pañca brahmāṇi śivāṅgāni śṛṇuṣva me
śaktibhūtāni ca tathā hṛdayādīni suvrata
oṃ īśānaḥ sarvavidyānāṃ hṛdayāya śaktibījāya namaḥ
oṃ īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāmamṛtāya śirase namaḥ
oṃ brahmādhipataye kālāgnirūpāya śikhāyai namaḥ
oṃ brahmaṇo'dhipataye kālacaṇḍamārutāya kavacāya namaḥ
oṃ brahmaṇe bṛṃhaṇāya jñānamūrtaye netrāya namaḥ
oṃ śivāya sadāśivāya pāśupatāstrāya apratihatāya phaṭphaṭ
oṃ sadyojātāya bhavenānibhave bhavasya māṃ bhavodbhavāya śivamūrtaye namaḥ
oṃ haṃsaśikhāya vidyādehāya ātmasvarūpāya parāparāya śivāya śivatamāya namaḥ
kathitāni śivāṅgāni mūrtividyā ca tasya vai
brahmāṅgamūrti vidyāṅgasahitāṃ śivaśāsane
saurāṇi ca pravakṣyāmi bāṣkalādyāni suvrata
aṅgāni sarvavedeṣu sārabhūtāni suvrata
oṃbhūḥ oṃbhuvaḥ oṃ svaḥ oṃmahaḥ oṃ janaḥ oṃ tapaḥ oṃsatyam oṃṛtam oṃ brahmā navākṣaramayaṃ mantraṃ bāṣkalaṃ parikīrtitam
na kṣaratīti loke 'smiṃstato hyakṣaramucyate
satyam akṣaram ity uktaṃ praṇavādinamo'ntakam
oṃ bhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ tatsaviturvareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi
dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt
namaḥ sūryāya khakholkāya namaḥ
mūlamantramiti proktaṃ bhāskarasya mahātmanaḥ
navākṣareṇa dīptādyamūlamantreṇa bhāskaram
pūjayedaṅgamantrāṇi kathayāmi samāsataḥ
vedādibhiḥ prabhūtādyaṃ praṇavena tu madhyamam
oṃbhūḥ brahmaṇe hṛdayāya namaḥ
oṃbhuvaḥ viṣṇave śirase namaḥ
oṃsvaḥ rudrāya śikhāyai namaḥ oṃbhūrbhuvaḥ svaḥ jvālāmālinyai devāya namaḥ oṃmahaḥ maheśvarāya kavacāya namaḥ
oṃ janaḥ śivāya netrebhyo namaḥ
oṃ tapas tāpanāya astrāya namaḥ
evaṃ prasaṃgādeveha saurāṇi kathitāni ha
śaivāni ca samāsena nyāsayogena suvrata
itthaṃ mantramayaṃ devaṃ pūjayeddhṛdayāṃbuje
nābhau homaṃ tu kartavyaṃ janayitvā yathākramam
manasā sarvakāryāṇi śivāgnau devamīśvaram
pañcabrahmāṅgasambhūtaṃ śivamūrtiṃ sadāśivam
raktapadmāsanāsīnaṃ śakalīkṛtya yatnataḥ
mūlena mūrtimantreṇa brahmāṅgādyaistu suvrata
samidājyāhutīrhutvā manasā candramaṇḍalāt
candrasthānātsamutpannāṃ pūrṇadhārāmanusmaret
pūrṇāhutividhānena jñānināṃ śivaśāsane
śivaṃ vaktragataṃ dhyāyettejomātraṃ ca śāṅkaram
lalāṭe devadeveśaṃ bhrūmadhye vā smaretpunaḥ
yacca hṛtkamale sarvaṃ samāpya vidhivistaram
śuddhadīpaśikhākāraṃ bhāvayedbhavanāśanam
liṅge ca pūjayeddevaṃ sthaṇḍile vā sadāśivam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge trayoviṃśatitamo'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
vyākhyāṃ pūjāvidhānasya pravadāmi samāsataḥ
śivaśāstroktamārgeṇa śivena kathitaṃ purā
athobhau candanacarcitau hastau vauṣaḍantenādyañjaliṃ kṛtvā mūrtividyāśivādīni japtvā aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhikānta īśānādyaṃ kaniṣṭhikādimadhyamāntaṃ hṛdayāditṛtīyāntaṃ turīyamaṅguṣṭhenānāmikayā pañcamaṃ taladvayena ṣaṣṭhaṃ tarjanyaṅguṣṭhābhyāṃ nārācāstraprayogeṇa punarapi mūlaṃ japtvā turīyenāvaguṇṭhya śivahastam ityucyate
śivārcanā tena hastena kāryā
tattvagatamātmānaṃ vyavasthāpya tattvaśuddhiṃ pūrvavat
kṣmāmbho'gnivāyuvyomāntaṃ pañcacatuḥśuddhakoṭyante dhārāsahitena vyavasthāpya tacchuddhiṃ pūrvaṃ kuryāt
tattvaśuddhiḥ ṣaṣṭhena sadyena tṛtīyena phaḍantāddharāśuddhiḥ
ṣaṣṭhasahitena sadyena tṛtīyena phaḍantena vāritattvaśuddhiḥ
vāhneyatṛtīyena phaḍantenāgniśuddhiḥ
vāyavyacaturthena ṣaṣṭhasahitena phaḍantena vāyuśuddhiḥ
ṣaṣṭhena sasadyena tṛtīyena phaḍantenākāśaśuddhiḥ
upasaṃhṛtyaivaṃ sadyaṣaṣṭhena tṛtīyena mūlena phaḍantena tāḍanaṃ tṛtīyena saṃpuṭīkṛtya grahaṇaṃ mūlameva yonibījena saṃpuṭīkṛtvā bandhanaṃ bandhaḥ
evaṃ kṣāntātītādinivṛttiparyantaṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā praṇavena tattvatrayakam anudhyāya ātmānaṃ dīpaśikhākāraṃ puryaṣṭakasahitaṃ trayātītaṃ śaktikṣobheṇāmṛtadhārāṃ suṣumṇāyāṃ dhyātvā
śāntyatītādinivṛttiparyantānāṃ cāntarnādabindvakārokāramakārāntaṃ śivaṃ sadāśivaṃ rudraviṣṇubrahmāntaṃ sṛṣṭikrameṇāmṛtīkaraṇaṃ brahmanyāsaṃ kṛtvā pañcavaktreṣu pañcadaśanayanaṃ vinyasya mūlena pādādikeśāntaṃ mahāmudrāmapi baddhvā śivo'hamiti dhyātvā śaktyādīni vinyasya hṛdi śaktyā bījāṅkurānantarāt sasuṣirasūtrakaṇṭakapatrakesaradharmajñānavairāgyaiśvaryasūryasomāgnivāmājyeṣṭhāraudrīkālīkalavikaraṇībalavikaraṇībalapramathanīsarvabhūtadamanīḥ kesareṣu karṇikāyāṃ manonmanīmapi dhyātvā
āsanaṃ parikalpyaivaṃ sarvopacārasahitaṃ bahiryogopacāreṇāntaḥkaraṇaṃ kṛtvā nābhau vahnikuṇḍe pūrvavadāsanaṃ parikalpya sadāśivaṃ dhyātvā binduto 'mṛtadhārāṃ śivamaṇḍale nipatitāṃ dhyātvā lalāṭe maheśvaraṃ dīpaśikhākāraṃ dhyātvā ātmaśuddhiritthaṃ prāṇāpānau saṃyamya suṣumṇayā vāyuṃ vyavasthāpya ṣaṣṭhena tālumudrāṃ kṛtvā digbandhaṃ kṛtvā ṣaṣṭhena sthānaśuddhir vastrādipūtāntararghyapātrādiṣu praṇavena tattvatrayaṃ vinyasya tadupari binduṃ dhyātvā vipūrya dravyāṇi ca vidhāya amṛtaplāvanaṃ kṛtvā pādyapātrādiṣu teṣāmarghyavadāsanaṃ parikalpya saṃhitayābhimantryādyenābhyarcya dvitīyenāmṛtīkṛtvā tṛtīyena viśodhya caturthenāvaguṇṭhya pañcamenāvalokya ṣaṣṭhena rakṣāṃvidhāya caturthena kuśapuñjenārghyāṃbhasābhyukṣya ātmānamapi dravyāṇi punar arghyāṃbhasābhyukṣya sapuṣpeṇa sarvadravyāṇi pṛthakpṛthak śodhayet
sadyena gandhaṃ vāmena vastram
aghoreṇa ābharaṇaṃ puruṣeṇa naivedyam
īśānena puṣpāṇi athābhimantrayet
śivagāyatryā śeṣaṃ prokṣayet
pañcāmṛtapañcagavyādīni brahmāṅgamūlādyair abhimantrayet
pṛthakpṛthaṅmūlenārghyaṃ dhūpaṃ dattvācamanīyaṃ ca teṣāmapi dhenumudrāṃ ca darśayitvā kavacenāvaguṇṭhyāstreṇa rakṣāṃ ca vidhāya dravyaśuddhiṃ kuryāt
arghyodakamagre hṛdā gandham ādāyāstreṇa viśodhya pūjāprabhṛtikaraṇaṃ rakṣāntaṃ kṛtvaivaṃ dravyaśuddhiṃ pūjāsamarpaṇāntaṃ maunamāsthāya puṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā sarvamantrāṇi praṇavādinamo'ntājjapitvā puṣpāñjaliṃ tyajenmantraśuddhirittham
agre sāmānyārghyapātraṃ payasāpūrya gandhapuṣpādinā saṃhitayābhimantrya dhenumudrāṃ dattvā kavacenāvaguṇṭhyāstreṇa rakṣayet
pūjāṃ paryuṣitāṃ gāyatryā samabhyarcya sāmānyārghyaṃ dattvā gandhapuṣpadhūpācamanīyaṃ svadhāntaṃ namo'ntaṃ vā dattvā brahmabhiḥ pṛthakpṛthakpuṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā phaḍantāstreṇa nirmālyaṃ vyapohya īśānyāṃ caṇḍam abhyarcyāsanamūrticaṇḍaṃ sāmānyāstreṇa liṅgapīṭhaṃ śivaṃ pāśupatāstreṇa viśodhya mūrdhni puṣpaṃ nidhāya pūjayelliṅgaśuddhiḥ
āsanaṃ kūrmaśilāyāṃ bījāṅkuraṃ tadupari brahmaśilāyām anantanālasuṣire sūtrapatrakaṇṭakakarṇikākesaradharmajñānavairāgyaiśvaryasūryasomāgnikesaraśaktiṃ manonmanīṃ karṇikāyāṃ manonmanenānantāsanāyeti samāsenāsanaṃ parikalpya tadupari nivṛttyādikalāmayaṃ ṣaḍvidhasahitaṃ karmakalāṅgadehaṃ sadāśivaṃ bhāvayet
ubhābhyāṃ sapuṣpābhyāṃ hastābhyāmaṅguṣṭhena puṣpamāpīḍya āvāhanamudrayā śanaiḥśanaiḥ hṛdayādimastakāntam āropya hṛdā saha mūlaṃ plutam uccārya sadyena bindusthānādabhyadhikaṃ dīpaśikhākāraṃ sarvatomukhahastaṃ vyāpyavyāpakam āvāhya sthāpayet
pūrvahṛdā śivaśaktisamavāyena paramīkaraṇam amṛtīkaraṇaṃ hṛdayādimūlena sadyenāvāhanaṃ hṛdā mūlopari aghoreṇa saṃnirodhaṃ hṛdā mūlopari puruṣeṇa sānnidhyaṃ hṛdā mūlena īśānena pūjayediti upadeśaḥ
pañcamantrasahitena yathāpūrvamātmano dehanirmāṇaṃ tathā devasyāpi vahneścaivamupadeśaḥ
rūpakadhyānaṃ kṛtvā mūlena namaskārāntamāpādya svadhāntamācamanīyaṃ sarvaṃ namaskārāntaṃ vā svāhākārāntamarghyaṃ mūlena puṣpāñjaliṃ vauṣaḍantena sarvaṃ namaskārāntaṃ hṛdā vā īśānena vā rudragāyatryā oṃnamaḥ śivāyeti mūlamantreṇa vā pūjayet
puṣpāñjaliṃ dattvā punar dhūpācamanīyaṃ ṣaṣṭhena puṣpāvasaraṇaṃ visarjanaṃ mantrodakena mūlena saṃsnāpya sarvadravyābhiṣekamīśānena pratidravyamaṣṭapuṣpaṃ dattvaivamarghyaṃ ca gandhapuṣpadhūpācamanīyaṃ phaḍantāstreṇa pūjāpasaraṇaṃ śuddhodakena mūlena saṃsnāpya piṣṭāmalakādibhiḥ
uṣṇodakena haridrādyena liṅgamūrtiṃ pīṭhasahitāṃ viśodhya gandhodakahiraṇyodakamantrodakena rudrādhyāyaṃ paṭhamānaḥ nīlarudratvaritarudrapañcabrahmādibhiḥ namaḥ śivāyeti snāpayet
mūrdhni puṣpaṃ nidhāyaivaṃ na śūnyaṃ liṅgamastakaṃ kuryādatra ślokaḥ
yasya rāṣṭre tu liṅgasya mastakaṃ śūnyalakṣaṇam
tasyālakṣmīr mahārogo durbhikṣaṃ vāhanakṣayaḥ
tasmātpariharedrājā dharmakāmārthamuktaye
śūnye liṅge svayaṃ rājā rāṣṭraṃ caiva praṇaśyati
evaṃ susnāpyārghyaṃ ca dattvā saṃmṛjya vastreṇa gandhapuṣpavastrālaṅkārādīṃśca mūlena dadyāt
dhūpācamanīyadīpanaivedyādīṃśca mūlena pradhānenopari pūjanaṃ pavitrīkaraṇamityuktam
ārārtidīpādīṃścaiva dhenumudrāmudritāni kavacenāvaguṇṭhitāni ṣaṣṭhena rakṣitāni liṅge ca liṅgasyādhaḥ sādhāraṇaṃ ca darśayet
mūlena namaskāraṃ vijñāpyāvāhanasthāpanasaṃnirodhasānnidhyapādyācamanīyārghyagandhapuṣpadhūpanaivedyācamanīyahastodvartanamukhavāsādyupacārayuktaṃ brahmāṅgabhogamārgeṇa pūjayet
sakaladhyānaṃ niṣkalasmāraṇaṃ parāvaradhyānaṃ mūlamantrajapaḥ
daśāṃśaṃ brahmāṅgajapasamarpaṇam ātmanivedanastutinamaskārādayaśca gurupūjā ca pūrvato dakṣiṇe vināyakasya
ādau cānte ca saṃpūjyo vighneśo jagadīśvaraḥ
daivataiśca dvijaiścaiva sarvakarmārthasiddhaye
yaḥ śivaṃ pūjayedevaṃ liṅge vā sthaṇḍile'pi vā
sa yāti śivasāyujyaṃ varṣamātreṇa karmaṇā
liṅgārcakaśca ṣaṇmāsānnātra kāryā vicāraṇā
sapta pradakṣiṇāḥ kṛtvā daṇḍavat praṇamed budhaḥ
pradakṣiṇakramapādena aśvamedhaphalaṃ śatam
tasmāt sampūjayennityaṃ sarvakarmārthasiddhaye
bhogārthī bhogamāpnoti rājyārthī rājyamāpnuyāt
putrārthī tanayaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ rogī rogātpramucyate
yānyāṃścintayate kāmāṃs tānprāpnoti mānavaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge caturviṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
śivāgnikāryaṃ vakṣyāmi śivena paribhāṣitam
janayitvāgrataḥ prācīṃ śubhe deśe susaṃskṛte
pūrvāgramuttarāgraṃ ca kuryātsūtratrayaṃśubham
caturastrīkṛte kṣetre kuryātkuṇḍāni yatnataḥ
nityahomāgnikuṇḍaṃ ca trimekhalasamāyutam
catustridvyaṅgulāyāmā mekhalā hastamātrataḥ
hastamātraṃ bhavetkuṇḍaṃ yoniḥ prādeśamātrataḥ
aśvatthapatravad yoniṃ mekhalopari kalpayet
kuṇḍamadhye tu nābhiḥ syādaṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam
prādeśamātraṃ vidhinā kārayedbrahmaṇaḥ suta
ṣaṣṭhenollekhanaṃ proktaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ varmaṇā smṛtam
netreṇālokya vai kuṇḍaṃ ṣaḍrekhāḥ kārayedbudhaḥ
prāgāyatena viprendra brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarāḥ
uttarāgrāḥ śivā rekhāḥ prokṣayedvarmaṇā punaḥ
śamīpippalasambhūtām araṇīṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulām
mathitvā vahnibījena śaktinyāsaṃ hṛdaiva tu
prakṣipedvidhinā vahnimanvādhāya yathāvidhi
tūṣṇīṃ prādeśamātraistu yājñikaiḥ śakalaiḥ śubhaiḥ
parisammohanaṃ kuryājjalenāṣṭasu dikṣu vai
paristīrya vidhānena prāgādyevamanukramāt
uttarāgraṃ purastāddhi prāgagraṃ dakṣiṇe punaḥ
paścime cottarāgraṃ tu saumye pūrvāgrameva tu
aindre caindrāgramāvāhya yāmya evaṃ vidhīyate
saumyasyopari cāndrāgnaṃ vāruṇāgnam adhastataḥ
dvandvarūpeṇa pātrāṇi barhiḥṣv āsādya suvrata
adhomukhāni sarvāṇi dravyāṇi ca tathottare
tasyopari nyaseddarbhāñchivaṃ dakṣiṇato nyaset
pūjayenmūlamantreṇa paścāddhomaṃ samācaret
prokṣaṇīpātramādāya pūrayedaṃbunā punaḥ
prādeśamātrau tu kuśau sthāpayedudakopari
plāvayecca kuśāgraṃ tu vasoḥ sūryasya raśmibhiḥ
vikīrya sarvapātrāṇi susaṃprokṣya vidhānataḥ
praṇītāpātramādāya pūrayedaṃbunā punaḥ
anyodakakuśāgraistu samyagācchādya suvrata
hastābhyāṃ nāsikaṃ pātramaiśānyāṃ diśi vinyaset
ājyādhiśrayaṇaṃ kuryātpaścimottarataḥ śubham
bhasmamiśrāṃstathāṅgārān grāhayecchakalena vai
paścimottarato nītvā tatra cājyaṃ pratāpayet
kuśānagnau tu prajvālya paryagniṃ tribhirācaret
tānsarvāṃstatra niḥkṣipya cāgre cājyaṃ nidhāpayet
aṅguṣṭhamātrau tu kuśau prakṣālya vidhinaiva tu
paryagniṃ ca tataḥ kuryāttaireva navabhiḥ punaḥ
paryagniṃ ca punaḥ kuryāt tadājyamavaropayet
athāpakarṣayet pātraṃ krameṇottarapaścime
saṃyujya cāgniṃ kāṣṭhena prakṣālyāropya paścime
ājyasyotpavanaṃ kuryātpavitrābhyāṃ sahaiva tu
pṛthagādāya hastābhyāṃ pravāheṇa yathākramam
aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ tu ubhābhyāṃ mūlavidyayā
abhyukṣya dāpayedagnau pavitre ghṛtapaṅkite
sauvarṇaṃ sruksruvaṃ kuryād ratnimātreṇa suvrata
rājataṃ vā yathānyāyaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
athavā yājñikairvṛkṣaiḥ kartavyau sruksruvāvubhau
aratnimātramāyāmaṃ tatpotre tu bilaṃ bhavet
ṣaḍaṅgulaparīṇāhaṃ daṇḍamūlaṃ mahāmune
tadardhaṃ kaṇṭhanālaṃ syātpuṣkaraṃ mūlavadbhavet
govālasadṛśaṃ daṇḍaṃ sruvāgraṃ nāsikāsamam
puṭadvayasamāyuktaṃ muktādyena prapūritam
ṣaṭtriṃśadaṅgulāyāmamaṣṭāṅgulasavistaram
utsedhastu tadardhaṃ syātsūtreṇa samitaṃ tataḥ
saptāṅgulaṃ bhavedāsyaṃ vistarāyāmataḥ punaḥ
tribhāgaikaṃ bhavedagraṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ parityajet
kaṇṭhaṃ ca dvyaṅgulāyāmaṃ vistāraṃ caturaṅgulam
vedir aṣṭāṅgulāyāmā vistārastatpramāṇataḥ
tasya madhye bilaṃ kuryāccaturaṅgulamānataḥ
bilaṃ suvartitaṃ kuryādaṣṭapatraṃ sukarṇikam
parito bilabāhye tu paṭṭikārdhāṅgulena tu
tadbāhye ca vinidraṃ tu padmapatravicitritam
yavadvayapramāṇena tadbāhye paṭṭikā bhavet
vedikāmadhyato randhraṃ kaniṣṭhāṅgulamānataḥ
khātaṃ yāvanmukhāntaḥ syādbilamānaṃ tu nimnagam
daṇḍaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ nālaṃ daṇḍāgre daṇḍikātrayam
ardhāṅgulavivṛddhyā tu kartavyaṃ caturaṅgulam
trayodaśāṅgulāyāmaṃ daṇḍamūle ghaṭaṃ bhavet
dvyaṅgulastu bhavetkuṃbho nābhiṃ vidyāddaśāṅgulam
vedimadhye tathā kṛtvā pādaṃ kuryācca dvyaṅgulam
padmapṛṣṭhasamākāraṃ pādaṃ vai karṇikākṛtim
gajoṣṭhasadṛśākāraṃ tasya pṛṣṭhākṛtirbhavet
abhicārādikāryeṣu kuryātkṛṣṇāyasena tu
pañcaviṃśatkuśenaiva sruksruvau mārjayet punaḥ
agramagreṇa saṃśodhya madhyaṃ madhyena suvrata
mūlaṃ mūlena vidhinā agnau tāpya hṛdā punaḥ
ājyasthālī praṇītā ca prokṣaṇī tisra eva ca
sauvarṇī rājatī vāpi tāmrī vā mṛnmayī tu vā
anyathā naiva kartavyaṃ śāntike pauṣṭike śubhe
āyasī tvabhicāre tu śāntike mṛnmayī tu vā
ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ suvistīrṇaṃ pātrāṇāṃ mukhamucyate
prokṣaṇī dvyaṅgulotsedhā praṇītā dvyaṅgulādhikā
ājyasthālī tatastasyā utsedho dvyaṅgulādhikaḥ
yaiḥ samidbhirhutaṃ proktaṃ taireva paridhirbhavet
madhyāṅgulaparīṇāhā avakrā nirvraṇāḥ samāḥ
dvātriṃśadaṅgulāyāmāstisraḥ paridhayaḥ smṛtāḥ
dvātriṃśadaṅgulāyāmaistriṃśaddarbhaiḥ paristaret
caturaṅgulamadhye tu grathitaṃ tu pradakṣiṇam
abhicārādikāryeṣu śivāgnyādhānavarjitam
akomalāḥ sthirā vipra saṃgrāhyāstvābhicārike
samagrāḥ susamāḥ sthūlāḥ kaniṣṭhāṅgulasaṃmitāḥ
avakrā nirvraṇāḥ snigdhā dvādaśāṅgulasaṃmitāḥ
samidhasthaṃ pramāṇaṃ hi sarvakāryeṣu suvrata
gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ tataḥ śreṣṭha kāpilaṃ tu tato 'dhikam
āhutīnāṃ pramāṇaṃ tu sruvaṃ pūrṇaṃ yathā bhavet
annamakṣapramāṇaṃ syācchuktimātreṇa vai tilaḥ
yavānāṃ ca tadardhaṃ syātphalānāṃ svapramāṇataḥ
kṣīrasya madhuno dadhnaḥ pramāṇaṃ ghṛtavadbhavet
catuḥsruvapramāṇena sruvā pūrṇāhutirbhavet
tadardhaṃ sviṣṭakṛt proktaṃ śeṣaṃ sarvamathāpi vā
śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ caiva śivāgnau juhuyātsadā
laukikāgnau mahābhāga mohanoccāṭanādayaḥ
śivāgniṃ janayitvā tu sarvakarmaṇi suvrata
sapta jihvāḥ prakalpyaiva sarvakāryāṇi kārayet
athavā sarvakāryāṇi jihvāmātreṇa sidhyati
śivāgniriti viprendrā jihvāmātreṇa sādhakaḥ
oṃ bahurūpāyai madhyajihvāyai anekavarṇāyai dakṣiṇottaramadhyagāyai śāntipauṣṭikamokṣādiphalapradāyai svāhā
oṃ hiraṇyāyai cāmīkarābhāyai īśānajihvāyai jñānapradāyai svāhā
oṃ kanakāyai kanakanibhāyai ramyāyai aindrajihvāyai svāhā
oṃ raktāyai raktavarṇāyai āgneyajihvāyai anekavarṇāyai vidveṣaṇamohanāyai svāhā
oṃ kṛṣṇāyai nairṛtajihvāyai māraṇāyai svāhā
oṃ suprabhāyai paścimajihvāyai muktāphalāyai śāntikāyai pauṣṭikāyai svāhā
oṃ abhivyaktāyai vāyavyajihvāyai śatrūccāṭanāyai svāhā
oṃ vahnaye tejasvine svāhā
etāvad vahnisaṃskāram athavā vahnikarmasu
naimittike ca vidhinā śivāgniṃ kārayetpunaḥ
nirīkṣaṇaṃ prokṣaṇaṃ tāḍanaṃ ca ṣaṣṭhena phaḍantena abhyukṣaṇaṃ caturthena khananotkiraṇaṃ ṣaṣṭhena pūraṇaṃ samīkaraṇamādyena secanaṃ vauṣaḍantena kuṭṭanaṃ ṣaṣṭhena saṃmārjanopalepane turīyeṇa kuṇḍaparikalpanaṃ nivṛttyā tribhireva kuṇḍaparidhānaṃ caturthena kuṇḍārcanamādyena rekhācatuṣṭayasaṃpādanaṃ ṣaṣṭhena phaḍantena vajrīkaraṇaṃ catuṣpadāpādanamādyena evaṃ kuṇḍasaṃskāramaṣṭādaśavidham
kuṇḍasaṃskārānantaramakṣapāṭanaṃ ṣaṣṭhena viṣṭaranyāsamādyena vajrāsane vāgīśvaryāvāhanam
oṃ hrīṃ vāgīśvarīṃ śyāmavarṇāṃ viśālākṣīṃ yauvanonmattavigrahām
ṛtumatīṃ vāgīśvaraśaktimāvāhayāmi
vāgīśvarīṃ pūjayāmi
oṃ īṃ vāgīśvarāya namaḥ
āvāhanasthāpanasannidhānasaṃnirodhapūjāntaṃ vāgīśvarīṃ saṃbhāvya garbhādhānavahnisaṃskāram
ekavaktraṃ caturbhujaṃ śuddhasphaṭikābhaṃ varadābhayahastaṃ paraśumṛgadharaṃ jaṭāmukuṭamaṇḍitaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitamāvāhayāmi
oṃ īṃ vāgīśvarāya namaḥ
āvāhanasthāpanasannidhānasannirodhapūjāntaṃ vāgīśvarīṃ saṃbhāvya garbhādhānavahnisaṃskāram
araṇījanitaṃ kāntodbhavaṃ vā agnihotrajaṃ vā tāmrapātre śarāve vā ānīya nirīkṣaṇatāḍanābhyukṣaṇaprakṣālanam ādyena kravyādā śivaparityāgo 'pi prathamena vahnes traikāraṇaṃ jaṭharabhrūmadhyād āvāhyāgniṃ vaikāraṇamūrtāvāgneyena uddīpanamādyena puruṣeṇa saṃhitayā dhāraṇā dhenumudrāṃ turīyeṇāvaguṇṭhya jānubhyāmavaniṃ gatvā śarāvotthāpanaṃ kuṇḍopari nidhāya pradakṣiṇamāvartya turīyeṇātmasammukhāṃ vāgīśvarīṃ garbhanāḍyāṃ garbhādhānāntarīyeṇa kamalapradānamādyena vauṣaḍantena kuśārghyaṃ dattvā indhanapradānamādyena prajvālanaṃ garbhādhānaṃ ca sadyenādyena pūjanaṃ vāmena pūjanaṃ dvitīyena sīmantonnayanam aghoreṇa tṛtīyena pūjanam
avayavavyāptir vaktrodghāṭanaṃ vaktraniṣkṛtiriti tṛtīyena garbhajātakarmapuruṣeṇa pūjanaṃ turīyeṇa ṣaṣṭhena prokṣaṇaṃ sūtakaśuddhaye cāgnisūnurakṣākuśāstreṇa vaktreṇāgnau mūlam īśāgraṃ nairṛtimūlaṃ vāyavyāgraṃ vāyavyamūlamīśāgramiti kuśāstaraṇam iti pūrvoktam idhmam agramūlaghṛtāktaṃ lālāpanodāya ṣaṣṭhena juhuyāt
pañcapūrvātikrameṇa paridhiviṣṭaranyāso 'pi ādyena viṣṭaropari hiraṇyagarbhaharanārāyaṇānapi pūjayet
indrādilokapālāṃśca pūjayet
vajrāvartaparyantānapi pūjayet
vāgīśvaravāgīśvarīpūjādyenam udvāsya hutaṃ visarjayet
sraksruvasaṃskāramatho nirīkṣaṇaprokṣaṇatāḍanābhyukṣaṇādīni pūrvavat sraksruvaṃ ca hastadvaye gṛhītvā saṃsthāpanamādyena tāḍanamapi sruksruvopari darbhānulekhanamūlamadhyamāgreṇa tritvena srukśaktiṃ sruvamapi śaṃbhuṃ dakṣiṇapārśve kuśopari śaktaye namaḥ śaṃbhave namaḥ
tato hyantisūtreṇa sruksruvau turīyeṇa veṣṭayedarcayecca
dhenumudrāṃ darśayitvā turīyeṇāvaguṇṭhya ṣaṣṭhena rakṣāṃ vidhāya sruksruvasaṃskāraḥ pūrvamevoktaḥ
punarājyasaṃskāraḥ pūrvam evoktaḥ nirīkṣaṇaprokṣaṇatāḍanābhyukṣaṇādīni pūrvavat
ājyapratāpanamaiśānyāṃ vā ṣaṣṭhena vedyupari vinyasya ghṛtapātraṃ vitastimātraṃ kuśapavitraṃ vāmahastāṅguṣṭhānāmikāgraṃ gṛhītvā dakṣiṇāṅguṣṭhānāmikāmūlaṃ gṛhītvāgnijvālotpavanaṃ svāhāntena turīyeṇa punaḥ ṣaḍ darbhān gṛhītvā pūrvavatsvātmasaṃplavanaṃ svāhāntenādyena kuśadvayapavitrabandhanaṃ cādyena ghṛte nyasediti pavitrīkaraṇam
darbhadvayaṃ pragṛhyāgniprajvālanaṃ ghṛtaṃ tridhā vartayet
saṃprokṣyāgnau nidhāpayediti nīrājanam
punardarbhān gṛhītvā kīṭakādi nirīkṣyārghyeṇa saṃprokṣya darbhānagnau nidhāya ityavadyotanam
darbhadvayaṃ gṛhītvāgnijvālayā ghṛtaṃ nirīkṣayet
darbheṇa gṛhītvā tenāgradvayena śuklapakṣadvayenādyeneti kṛṣṇapakṣasampātanaṃ ghṛtaṃ tribhāgena vibhajya sruveṇaikabhāgenājyenāgnaye svāhā dvitīyenājyena somāya svāhā ājyena oṃ agnīṣomābhyāṃ svāhā ājyenāgnaye sviṣṭakṛte svāhā
punaḥ kuśena gṛhītvā saṃhitābhimantreṇa namo'ntenābhimantrayet
abhimantrya dhenumudrāpradarśanakavacāvaguṇṭhanāstreṇa rakṣām
atha saṃskṛte nidhāpayet ājyasaṃskāraḥ
ājyena srugvadanena cakrābhidhāraṇaṃ śaktibījādīśānamūrtaye svāhā
pūrvavat puruṣavaktrāya svāhā aghorahṛdayāya svāhā vāmadevāya guhyāya svāhā sadyojātamūrtaye svāhā
iti vaktrodghāṭanam
īśānamūrtaye tatpuruṣavaktrāya svāhā tatpuruṣavaktrāya aghorahṛdayāya svāhā aghorahṛdayāya vāmaguhyāya sadyojātamūrtaye svāhā iti vaktrasaṃdhānam
īśānamūrtaye tatpuruṣāya vaktrāya aghorahṛdayāya vāmadevāya guhyāya sadyojātāya svāhā iti vaktrasaṃdhānam
īśānamūrtaye tatpuruṣāya vaktrāya aghorahṛdayāya vāmadevāya guhyāya sadyojātamūrtaye svāhā iti vaktraikyakaraṇam
śivāgniṃ janayitvaivaṃ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
kevalaṃ jihvayā vāpi śāntikādyāni sarvadā
garbhādhānādikāryeṣu vahneḥ pratyekamavyaya
daśa āhutayo deyā yonibījena pañcadhā
śivāgnau kalpayeddivyaṃ pūrvavatparamāsanam
āvāhanaṃ tathā nyāsaṃ yathā deve tathārcanam
mūlamantraṃ sakṛjjaptvā devadevaṃ praṇamya ca
prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā sagarbhaṃ sarvasaṃmatam
pariṣecanapūrvaṃ ca tadidhmam abhighārya ca
juhuyādagnimadhye tu jvalite 'tha mahāmune
āghārāvapi cādhāya cājyenaiva tu ṣaṇmukhe
ājyabhāgau tu juhuyādvidhinaiva ghṛtena ca
cakṣuṣī cājyabhāgau tu cāgnaye ca tathottare
ātmano dakṣiṇe caiva somāyeti dvijottama
pratyaṅmukhasya devasya śivāgnerbrahmaṇaḥ suta
akṣi vai dakṣiṇaṃ caiva cottaraṃ cottaraṃ tathā
dakṣiṇaṃ tu mahābhāga bhavatyeva na saṃśayaḥ
ājyenāhutayastatra mūlenaiva daśaiva tu
caruṇā ca yathāvaddhi samidbhiśca tathā smṛtam
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato dadyānmūlamantreṇa suvrata
sarvāvaraṇadevānāṃ pañcapañcaiva pūrvavat
īśānādikrameṇaiva śaktibījakrameṇa ca
prāyaścittam aghoreṇa sveṣṭāntaṃ pūrvavatsmṛtam
triprakāraṃ mayā proktamagnikāryaṃ suśobhanam
yathāvasaram evaṃ hi kuryānnityaṃ mahāmune
jīvitānte labhetsvargaṃ labhate agnidīpanam
narakaṃ caiva nāpnoti yasya kasyāpi karmaṇaḥ
ahiṃsakaṃ careddhomaṃ sādhako muktikāṅkṣakaḥ
hṛdisthaṃ cintayedagniṃ dhyānayajñena homayet
dehasthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ śivaṃ sarvajagatpatim
taṃ jñātvā homayedbhaktyā prāṇāyāmena nityaśaḥ
bāhyahomapradātā tu pāṣāṇe darduro bhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcaviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
śailādiruvāca
athavā devamīśānaṃ liṅge sampūjayecchivam
brāhmaṇaḥ śivabhaktaśca śivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ
agnirityādinā bhasma gṛhītvā hyagnihotrajam
uddhūlayeddhi sarvāṅgamāpādatalamastakam
ācāmedbrahmatīrthena brahmasūtrī hyudaṅmukhaḥ
athauṃ namaḥ śivāyeti tanuṃ kṛtvātmanaḥ punaḥ
devaṃ ca tena mantreṇa pūjayetpraṇavena ca
sarvasmādadhikā pūjā aghoreśasya śūlinaḥ
sāmānyaṃ yajanaṃ sarvamagnikāryaṃ ca suvrata
mantrabhedaḥ prabhostasya aghoradhyānameva ca
mantraḥ
aghorebhyo 'tha ghorebhyo ghoraghoratarebhyaḥ śarvebhyaḥ sarvaśarvebhyo namaste astu rudrarūpebhyaḥ
aghorebhyaḥ praśāntahṛdayāya namaḥ
atha ghorebhyaḥ sarvātmabrahmaśirase svāhā
ghoraghoratarebhyaḥ jvālāmālinī śikhāyai vaṣaṭ
sarvebhyaḥ sarvaśarvebhyaḥ piṅgalakavacāya hum
namaste astu rudrarūpebhyaḥ netratrayāya vaṣaṭ
sahasrākṣāya durbhedāya pāśupatāstrāya huṃ phaṭ
snātvācāmya tanuṃ kṛtvā samabhyukṣyāghamarṣaṇam
tarpaṇaṃ vidhinā cārghyaṃ bhānave bhānupūjanam
samaṃ cāghorapūjāyāṃ mantramātreṇa bheditam
mārgaśuddhistathā dvāri pūjāṃ vāstvadhipasya ca
kṛtvā karaṃ viśodhyāgre sa śubhāsanamāsthitaḥ
nāsāgrakamale sthāpya dagdhākṣaḥ kṣubhikāgninā
vāyunā prerya tadbhasma viśodhya ca śubhāṃbhasā
śaktyāmṛtamaye brahmakalāṃ tatra prakalpayet
aghoraṃ pañcadhā kṛtvā pañcāṅgasahitaṃ punaḥ
itthaṃ jñānakriyāmevaṃ vinyasya ca vidhānataḥ
nyāsas trinetrasahito hṛdi dhyātvā varāsane
nābhau vahnigataṃ smṛtvā bhrūmadhye dīpavatprabhum
śāntyā bījāṅkurānantadharmādyairapi saṃyute
somasūryāgnisampanne mūrtitrayasamanvite
vāmādibhiśca sahite manonmanyāpyadhiṣṭhite
śivāsanetmamūrtistham akṣayākārarūpiṇam
aṣṭatriṃśatkalādehaṃ tritattvasahitaṃ śivam
aṣṭādaśabhujaṃ devaṃ gajacarmottarīyakam
siṃhājināṃbaradharamaghoraṃ parameśvaram
dvātriṃśākṣararūpeṇa dvātriṃśacchaktibhirvṛtam
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtam
kapālamālābharaṇaṃ sarvavṛścikabhūṣaṇam
pūrṇenduvadanaṃ saumyaṃ candrakoṭisamaprabham
candrarekhādharaṃ śaktyā sahitaṃ nīlarūpiṇam
haste khaḍgaṃ kheṭakaṃ pāśam eke ratnaiścitraṃ cāṅkuśaṃ nāgakakṣām
śarāsanaṃ pāśupataṃ tathāstraṃ daṇḍaṃ ca khaṭvāṅgamathāpare ca
tantrīṃ ca ghaṇṭāṃ vipulaṃ ca śūlaṃ tathāpare ḍāmarukaṃ ca divyam
vajraṃ gadāṃ ṭaṅkamekaṃ ca dīptaṃ samudgaraṃ hastamathāsya śaṃbhoḥ
varadābhayahastaṃ ca vareṇyaṃ parameśvaram
bhāvayetpūjayeccāpi vahnau homaṃ ca kārayet
homaśca pūrvavatsarvo mantrabhedaśca kīrtitaḥ
aṣṭapuṣpādi gandhādi pūjāstutinivedanam
antarbaliṃ ca kuṇḍasya vāhneyena vidhānataḥ
maṇḍalaṃ vidhinā kṛtvā mantrairetairyathākramam
rudrebhyo mātṛgaṇebhyo yakṣebhyo 'surebhyo grahebhyo rākṣasebhyo nāgebhyo nakṣatrebhyo viśvagaṇebhyaḥ kṣetrapālebhyaḥ atha vāyuvaruṇadigbhāge kṣetrapālabaliṃ kṣipet
arghyaṃ gandhaṃ ca puṣpaṃ ca dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ ca suvratāḥ
naivedyaṃ mukhavāsādi nivedyaṃ vai yathāvidhi
vijñāpyaivaṃ visṛjyātha aṣṭapuṣpaiśca pūjanam
sarvasāmānyametaddhi pūjāyāṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktamaghorārcādi suvrata
aghorārcāvidhānaṃ ca liṅge vā sthaṇḍile 'pi vā
sthaṇḍilātkoṭiguṇitaṃ liṅgārcanamanuttamam
liṅgārcanarato vipro mahāpātakasaṃbhavaiḥ
pāpairapi na lipyeta padmapatramivāṃbhasā
liṅgasya darśanaṃ puṇyaṃ darśanātsparśanaṃ varam
arcanādadhikaṃ nāsti brahmaputra na saṃśayaḥ
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktamaghorārcanamuttamam
varṣakoṭiśatenāpi vistareṇa na śakyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ṣaḍviṃśatitamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
prabhāvo nandinaścaiva liṅgapūjāphalaṃ śrutam
śrutibhiḥ saṃmitaṃ sarvaṃ romaharṣaṇa suvrata
jayābhiṣeka īśena kathito manave purā
hitāya meruśikhare kṣatriyāṇāṃ triśūlinā
tatkathaṃ ṣoḍaśavidhaṃ mahādānaṃ ca śobhanam
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ sūta buddhimatāṃvara
sūta uvāca
jīvacchrāddhaṃ purā kṛtvā manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prabhuḥ
merumāsādya deveśam astāvīnnīlalohitam
tapasā ca vinītāya prahṛṣṭaḥ pradadau bhavaḥ
divyaṃ darśanamīśānas tenāpaśyat tam avyayam
natvā sampūjya vidhinā kṛtāñjalipuṭaḥ sthitaḥ
harṣagadgadayā vācā provāca ca nanāma ca
devadeva jagannātha namaste bhuvaneśvara
jīvacchrāddhaṃ mahādeva prasādena vinirmitam
pūjitaś ca tato devo dṛṣṭaś caiva mayādhunā
śakrāya kathitaṃ pūrvaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam
jayābhiṣekaṃ deveśa vaktumarhasi me prabho
sūta uvāca
tasmai devo mahādevo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
jayābhiṣekamakhilamavadatparameśvaraḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
jayābhiṣekaṃ vakṣyāmi nṛpāṇāṃ hitakāmyayā
apamṛtyujayārthaṃ ca sarvaśatrujayāya ca
yuddhakāle tu samprāpte kṛtvaivamabhiṣecanam
svapatiṃ cābhiṣicyaiva gacchedyoddhuṃ raṇājire
vidhinā maṇḍapaṃ kṛtvā prapāṃ vā kūṭameva vā
navadhā sthāpayed vahniṃ brāhmaṇo vedapāragaḥ
tataḥ sarvābhiṣekārthaṃ sūtrapātaṃ ca kārayet
prāgādyaṃ varṇasūtraṃ ca dakṣiṇādyaṃ tathā punaḥ
sahasrāṇāṃ dvayaṃ tatra śatānāṃ ca catuṣṭayam
śeṣameva śubhaṃ koṣṭhaṃ teṣu koṣṭhaṃ tu saṃharet
bāhye vīthyāṃ padaṃ caikaṃ samantādupasaṃharet
aṅgasūtrāṇi saṃgṛhya vidhinā pṛthageva tu
prāgādyaṃ varṇasūtraṃ ca dakṣiṇādyaṃ tathā punaḥ
prāgādyaṃ dakṣiṇādyaṃ ca ṣaṭtriṃśat saṃharet kramāt
prāgādyāḥ paṅktayaḥ sapta dakṣiṇādyāstathā punaḥ
tasmādekonapañcāśatpaṅktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
nava paṅktīrharenmadhye gandhagomayavāriṇā
kamalaṃ cālikhettatra hastamātreṇa śobhanam
aṣṭapatraṃ sitaṃ vṛttaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam
aṣṭāṅgulapramāṇena karṇikā hemasannibhā
caturaṅgulamānena kesarasthānamucyate
dharmo jñānaṃ ca vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ ca yathākramam
āgneyādiṣu koṇeṣu sthāpayetpraṇavena tu
avyaktādīni vai dikṣu gātrākāreṇa vai nyaset
avyaktaṃ niyataḥ kālaḥ kālī ceti catuṣṭayam
sitaraktahiraṇyābhakṛṣṇā dharmādayaḥ kramāt
haṃsākāreṇa vai gātraṃ hemābhāsena suvratāḥ
ādhāraśaktimadhye tu kamalaṃ sṛṣṭikāraṇam
bindumātraṃ kalāmadhye nādākāramataḥ param
nādopari śivaṃ dhyāyed oṃkārākhyaṃ jagadgurum
manonmanīṃ ca padmābhaṃ mahādevaṃ ca bhāvayet
vāmādayaḥ krameṇaiva prāgādyāḥ kesareṣu vai
vāmā jyeṣṭhā tathā raudrī kālī vikaraṇī tathā
balā pramathinī devī damanī ca yathākramam
vāmadevādibhiḥ sārdhaṃ praṇavenaiva vinyaset
namo 'stu vāmadevāya namo jyeṣṭhāya śūline
rudrāya kālarūpāya kalāvikaraṇāya ca
balāya ca tathā sarvabhūtasya damanāya ca
manonmanāya devāya manonmanyai namonamaḥ
mantrairetairyathānyāyaṃ pūjayetparimaṇḍalam
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu
tṛtīyāvaraṇe caiva caturviṃśad anukramāt
piśācavīthir vai madhye nābhivīthiḥ samantataḥ
mantrairetairyathānyāyaṃ piśācānāṃ prakīrtitāḥ
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ tu padamaṣṭārasaṃyutam
teṣu teṣu pṛthaktvena padeṣu kamalaṃ kramāt
kalpayecchālinīvāragodhūmaiśca yavādibhiḥ
taṇḍulaiśca tilairvātha gaurasarṣapasaṃyutaiḥ
athavā kalpayedetairyathākālaṃ vidhānataḥ
aṣṭapatraṃ likhetteṣu karṇikākesarānvitam
śālīnāmāḍhakaṃ proktaṃ kamalānāṃ pṛthak pṛthak
taṇḍulānāṃ tadardhaṃ syāttadardhaṃ ca yavādayaḥ
droṇaṃ pradhānakuṃbhasya tadardhaṃ taṇḍulāḥ smṛtāḥ
tilānāmāḍhakaṃ madhye yavānāṃ ca tadardhakam
athāṃbhasā samabhyukṣya kamalaṃ praṇavena tu
teṣu sarveṣu vidhinā praṇavaṃ vinyasetkramāt
evaṃ samāpya cābhyukṣya padasāhasramuttamam
kalaśānāṃ sahasrāṇi haimāni ca śubhāni ca
uktalakṣaṇayuktāni kārayedrājatāni vā
tāmrajāni yathānyāyaṃ praṇavenārghyavāriṇā
dvādaśāṅgulavistāramudare samudāhṛtam
vartitaṃ tu tadardhena nābhistasya vidhīyate
kaṇṭhaṃ tu dvyaṅgulotsedhaṃ vistāraṃ caturaṅgulam
oṣṭhaṃ ca dvyaṅgulotsedhaṃ nirgamaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ smṛtam
tattadvai dviguṇaṃ divyaṃ śivakuṃbhe prakīrtitam
yavamātrāntaraṃ samyak tantunā veṣṭayeddhi vai
avaguṇṭhya tathābhyukṣya kuśopari yathāvidhi
pūrvavatpraṇavenaiva pūrayedgandhavāriṇā
sthāpayecchivakuṃbhāḍhyaṃ vardhanīṃ ca vidhānataḥ
madhyapadmasya madhye tu sakūrcaṃ sākṣataṃ kramāt
āveṣṭya vastrayugmena pracchādya kamalena tu
haimena citraratnena sahasrakalaśaṃ pṛthak
śivakuṃbhe śivaṃ sthāpya gāyatryā praṇaveṇa ca
vidmahe puruṣāyaiva mahādevāya dhīmahi
tanno rudraḥ pracodayāt
mantreṇānena rudrasya sānnidhyaṃ sarvadā smṛtam
vardhanyāṃ devīgāyatryā devīṃ saṃsthāpya pūjayet
gaṇāṃbikāyai vidmahe mahātapāyai dhīmahi
tanno gaurī pracodayāt
prathamāvaraṇe caiva vāmādyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaivātra pūrvādyānteṣu suvrata
aindravyūhasya madhye tu subhadrāṃ sthāpya pūjayet
bhadrāmāgneyacakre tu yāmye tu kanakāṇḍajām
aṃbikāṃ nairṛte vyūhe madhyakuṃbhe tu pūjayet
śrīdevīṃ vāruṇe bhāge vāgīśāṃ vāyugocare
gomukhīṃ saumyabhāge tu madhyakuṃbhe tu pūjayet
rudravyūhasya madhye tu bhadrakarṇāṃ samarcayet
aindrāgnividiśor madhye pūjayed aṇimāṃ śubhām
yāmyapāvakayormadhye laghimāṃ kamale nyaset
rākṣasāntakayor madhye mahimāṃ madhyato yajet
varuṇāsurayormadhye prāptiṃ vai madhyato yajet
varuṇānilayormadhye prākāmyaṃ kamale nyaset
vitteśānilayormadhye īśitvaṃ sthāpya pūjayet
vitteśeśānayormadhye vaśitvaṃ sthāpya pūjayet
aindreśeśānayor madhye yajet kāmāvasāyakam
dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ tṛtīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
śaktayastu caturviṃśatpradānakalaśeṣu ca
pūjayedvyūhamadhye tu pūrvavadvidhipūrvakam
dīkṣāṃ dīkṣāyikāṃ caiva caṇḍāṃ caṇḍāṃśunāyikām
sumatiṃ sumatyāyīṃ ca gopāṃ gopāyikāṃ tathā
atha nandaṃ ca nandāyīṃ pitāmahamataḥ param
pitāmahāyīṃ pūrvādyaṃ vidhinā sthāpya pūjayet
evaṃ sampūjya vidhinā tṛtīyāvaraṇaṃ śubham
saubhadraṃ vyūhamāsādya prathamāvaraṇe kramāt
prāgādyaṃ vidhinā sthāpya śaktyaṣṭakamanukramāt
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva prāgādyaṃ śṛṇu śaktayaḥ
ṣoḍaśaiva tu abhyarcya padmamudrāṃ tu darśayet
bindukā bindugarbhā ca nādinī nādagarbhajā
śaktikā śaktigarbhā ca parā caiva parāparā
prathamāvaraṇe 'ṣṭau ca śaktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
caṇḍā caṇḍamukhī caiva caṇḍavegā manojavā
caṇḍākṣī caṇḍanirghoṣā bhṛkuṭī caṇḍanāyikā
manotsedhā manodhyakṣā mānasī mānanāyikā
manoharī manohlādī manaḥprītirmaheśvarī
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
saubhadraḥ kathito vyūho bhadraṃ vyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
aindrī hautāśanī yāmyā nairṛtī vāruṇī tathā
vāyavyā caiva kauberī aiśānī cāṣṭaśaktayaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
hariṇī ca suvarṇā ca kāñcanī hāṭakī tathā
rukmiṇī satyabhāmā ca subhagā jambunāyikā
vāgbhavā vākpathā vāṇī bhīmā citrarathā sudhīḥ
vedamātā hiraṇyākṣī dvitīyāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
bhadrākhyaḥ kathito vyūhaḥ kanakākhyaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
vajraṃ śaktiṃ ca daṇḍaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ pāśaṃ dhvajaṃ tathā
gadāṃ triśūlaṃ kramaśaḥ prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
yuddhā prabuddhā caṇḍā ca muṇḍā caiva kapālinī
mṛtyuhantrī virūpākṣī kapardā kamalāsanā
daṃṣṭriṇī raṅgiṇī caiva lambākṣī kaṅkabhūṣaṇī
sambhāvā bhāvinī caiva ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
kathitaḥ prathamavyūho hyambikākhyaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
khecarī cātmanā sā ca bhavānī vahnirūpiṇī
vahninī vahninābhā ca mahimāmṛtalālasā
prathamāvaraṇe cāṣṭau śaktayaḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
kṣamā ca śikharā devī ṛturatnā śilā tathā
chāyā bhūtapatī dhanyā indramātā ca vaiṣṇavī
tṛṣṇā rāgavatī mohā kāmakopā mahotkaṭā
indrā ca badhirā devī ṣoḍaśaitāḥ prakīrtitāḥ
kathitaścāṃbikāvyūhaḥ śrīvyūhaṃ śṛṇu suvrata
sparśā sparśavatī gandhā prāṇāpānā samānikā
udānā vyānanāmā ca prathamāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
tamohatā prabhāmoghā tejinī dahanī tathā
bhīmāsyā jālinī coṣā śoṣiṇī rudranāyikā
vīrabhadrā gaṇādhyakṣā candrahāsā ca gahvarā
gaṇamātāmbikā caiva śaktayaḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
dvitīyāvaraṇe proktāḥ ṣoḍaśaiva yathākramāt
śrīvyūhaḥ kathito bhadraṃ vāgīśaṃ śṛṇu suvrata
dhārā vāridharā caiva vahnikī nāśakī tathā
martyātītā mahāmāyā vajriṇī kāmadhenukā
prathamāvaraṇe 'pyevaṃ śaktayo 'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ
payoṣṇī vāruṇī śāntā jayantī ca varapradā
plāvinī jalamātā ca payomātā mahāmbikā
raktā karālī caṇḍākṣī mahocchuṣmā payasvinī
māyā vidyeśvarī kālī kālikā ca yathākramam
ṣoḍaśaiva samākhyātāḥ śaktayaḥ sarvasaṃmatāḥ
vyūho vāgīśvaraḥ prokto gomukho vyūha ucyate
śaṅkhinī hālinī caiva laṅkāvarṇā ca kalkinī
yakṣiṇī mālinī caiva vamanī ca rasātmanī
prathamāvaraṇe caiva śaktayo 'ṣṭau prakīrtitāḥ
caṇḍā ghaṇṭā mahānādā sumukhī durmukhī balā
revatī prathamā ghorā sainyā līnā mahābalā
jayā ca vijayā caiva aparā cāparājitā
dvitīyāvaraṇe caiva śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu
kathito gomukhīvyūho bhadrakarṇīṃ śṛṇuṣva me
mahājayā virūpākṣī śuklābhā kāśamātṛkā
saṃhārī jātahārī ca daṃṣṭrālī śuṣkarevatī
prathamāvaraṇe cāṣṭau śaktayaḥ parikīrtitāḥ
pipīlikā puṇyahārī aśanī sarvahāriṇī
bhadrahā viśvahārī ca himā yogeśvarī tathā
chidrā bhānumatī chidrā saiṃhikī surabhī samā
sarvabhavyā ca vegākhyā śaktayaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu
mahāvyūhāṣṭakaṃ proktam upavyūhāṣṭakaṃ śṛṇu
aṇimāvyūham āveṣṭya prathamāvaraṇe kramāt
aindrā tu citrabhānuśca vāruṇī daṇḍireva ca
prāṇarūpī tathā haṃsaḥ svātmaśaktiḥ pitāmahaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
keśavo bhagavān rudraścandramā bhāskarastathā
mahātmā ca tathā hyātmā hyantarātmā maheśvaraḥ
paramātmā hyaṇurjīvaḥ piṅgalaḥ puruṣaḥ paśuḥ
bhoktā bhūtapatirbhīmo dvitīyāvaraṇe smṛtāḥ
kathitaś cāṇimāvyūho laghimākhyaṃ vadāmi te
śrīkaṇṭho'ntaśca sūkṣmaśca trimūrtiḥ śaśakastathā
amareśaḥ sthitīśaśca dārataśca tathāṣṭamaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
sthāṇurharaśca daṇḍeśo bhauktīśaḥ surapuṅgavaḥ
sadyojāto 'nugraheśaḥ krūrasenaḥ sureśvaraḥ
krodhīśaśca tathā caṇḍaḥ pracaṇḍaḥ śiva eva ca
ekarudrastathā kūrmaścaikanetraścaturmukhaḥ
dvitīyāvaraṇe rudrāḥ ṣoḍaśaiva prakīrtitāḥ
kathito laghimāvyūho mahimāṃ śṛṇu suvrata
ajeśaḥ kṣemarudraśca somo 'ṃśo lāṅgalī tathā
daṇḍāruś cārdhanārī ca ekāntaścānta eva ca
pālī bhujaṅganāmā ca pinākī khaḍgir eva ca
kāma īśastathā śveto bhṛguḥ ṣoḍaśa vai smṛtāḥ
kathito mahimāvyūhaḥ prāptivyūhaṃ śṛṇuṣva me
saṃvarto lakulīśaśca vāḍavo hastir eva ca
caṇḍayakṣo gaṇapatirmahātmā bhṛgujo 'ṣṭamaḥ
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
trivikramo mahājihva ṛkṣaḥ śrībhadra eva ca
mahādevo dadhīcaśca kumāraśca parāvaraḥ
mahādaṃṣṭraḥ karālaśca sūcakaśca suvardhanaḥ
mahādhvāṅkṣo mahānando daṇḍī gopālakastathā
prāptivyūhaḥ samākhyātaḥ prākāmyaṃ śṛṇu suvrata
puṣpadanto mahānāgo vipulānandakārakaḥ
śuklo viśālaḥ kamalo bilvaścāruṇa eva ca
prathamāvaraṇaṃ proktaṃ dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
ratipriyaḥ sureśānaścitrāṅgaśca sudurjayaḥ
vināyakaḥ kṣetrapālo mahāmohaśca jaṅgalaḥ
vatsaputro mahāputro grāmadeśādhipastathā
sarvāvasthādhipo devo meghanādaḥ pracaṇḍakaḥ
kāladūtaśca kathito dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ smṛtam
prākāmyaḥ kathito vyūha aiśvaryaṃ kathayāmi te
maṅgalā carcikā caiva yogeśā haradāyikā
bhāsurā suramātā ca sundarī mātṛkāṣṭamī
prathamāvaraṇe proktā dvitīyāvaraṇaṃ śṛṇu
gaṇādhipaśca mantrajño varadevaḥ ṣaḍānanaḥ
vidagdhaśca vicitraśca amogho mogha eva ca
aśvīrudraśca someśaś cottamodumbarastathā
sūta uvāca
snātvā devaṃ namaskṛtya devadevamumāpatim
divyena cakṣuṣā rudraṃ nīlalohitamīśvaram
dṛṣṭvā tuṣṭāva varadaṃ rudrādhyāyena śaṅkaram
devo 'pi tuṣṭyā nirvāṇaṃ rājyānte karmaṇaiva tu
tavāstīti sakṛccoktvā tatraivāntaradhīyata
svāyaṃbhuvo manurdevaṃ namaskṛtya vṛṣadhvajam
āruroha mahāmeruṃ mahāvṛṣamiveśvaraḥ
tatra devaṃ hiraṇyābhaṃ yogaiśvaryasamanvitam
sanatkumāraṃ varadamapaśyadbrahmaṇaḥ sutam
namaścakāra varadaṃ brahmaṇyaṃ brahmarūpiṇam
kṛtāñjalipuṭo bhūtvā tuṣṭāva ca mahādyutiḥ
so 'pi dṛṣṭvā manuṃ devo hṛṣṭaromābhavanmuniḥ
sanatkumāraḥ prāhedaṃ ghṛṇayā ca ghṛṇānidhe
sanatkumāra uvāca
dṛṣṭvā sarveśvarācchāntācchaṅkarānnīlalohitāt
labdhvābhiṣekaṃ samprāpto vivakṣurvada yadyapi
tasya tadvacanaṃ śrutvā praṇipatya kṛtāñjaliḥ
vijñāpayāmāsa kathaṃ karmaṇā nirvṛtirvibho
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ karmaṇā kevalena ca
jñānena nirvṛtiḥ siddhā vibho miśreṇa vā kvacit
atha tasya vacaḥ śrutvā śrutisāravidāṃ nidhiḥ
sanatkumāro bhagavānkarmaṇā nirvṛtiḥ kramāt
miśreṇa ca kramādeva kṣaṇājjñānena vai mune
purā mānena coṣṭratvam agamaṃ nandinaḥ prabhoḥ
śāpātpunaḥ prasādāddhi śivamabhyarcya śaṅkaram
prasādānnandinastasya karmaṇaiva suto hyaham
śrutvottamāṃ gatiṃ divyāmavasthāṃ prāptavānaham
śivārcanaprakāreṇa śivadharmeṇa nānyathā
rājñāṃ ṣoḍaśadānāni nandinā kathitāni ca
dharmakāmārthamuktyarthaṃ karmaṇaiva mahātmanā
tulādirohaṇādyāni śṛṇu tāni yathātatham
grahaṇādiṣu kāleṣu śubhadeśeṣu śobhanam
viṃśaddhastapramāṇena maṇḍapaṃ kūṭameva ca
yathāṣṭādaśahastena kalāhastena vā punaḥ
kṛtvā vediṃ tathā madhye navahastapramāṇataḥ
aṣṭahastena vā kāryā saptahastena vā punaḥ
dvihastā sārdhahastā vā vedikā cātiśobhanā
dvādaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktā sādhuramyā bhramantikā
parito nava kuṇḍāni caturasrāṇi kārayet
aindrikeśānayor madhye pradhānaṃ brahmaṇaḥ suta
athavā caturasraṃ ca yonyākāramataḥ param
strīṇāṃ kuṇḍāni viprendrā yonyākārāṇi kārayet
ardhacandraṃ trikoṇaṃ ca vartulaṃ kuṇḍameva ca
ṣaḍasraṃ sarvato vāpi trikoṇaṃ padmasannibham
aṣṭāsraṃ sarvamāne tu sthaṇḍilaṃ kevalaṃ tu vā
caturdvārasamopetaṃ catustoraṇabhūṣitam
diggajāṣṭakasaṃyuktaṃ darbhamālāsamāvṛtam
aṣṭamaṅgalasaṃyuktaṃ vitānopariśobhitam
tulāstaṃbhadrumāścātra bilvādīni viśeṣataḥ
bilvāśvatthapalāśādyāḥ kevalaṃ khādiraṃ tu vā
yena staṃbhaḥ kṛtaḥ pūrvaṃ tena sarvaṃ tu kārayet
athavā miśramārgeṇa veṇunā vā prakalpayet
aṣṭahastapramāṇaṃ tu hastadvayasamāyutam
tulāstaṃbhasya viṣkaṃbho 'nāhatas triguṇo mataḥ
dvyaṅgulena vihīnaṃ tu suvṛttaṃ nirvraṇaṃ tathā
ubhayorantaraṃ caiva ṣaḍḍhastaṃ nṛpate smṛtam
dvayoś caturhastakṛtam antaraṃ staṃbhayorapi
ṣaḍḍhastam antaraṃ jñeyaṃ staṃbhayorupari sthitam
vitastimātraṃ vistāro viṣkaṃbhastāvaduttaram
staṃbhayostu pramāṇena uttaradvārasaṃmitam
ṣaṭtriṃśanmātrasaṃyuktaṃ vyāyāmaṃ tu tulātmakam
viṣkaṃbhamaṣṭamātraṃ tu yavapañcakasaṃyutam
ṣaṭtriṃśanmātranābhaṃ syānnirmāṇādvartulaṃ śubham
agre mūle ca madhye ca hemapaṭṭena bandhayet
paṭṭamadhye prakartavyam avalambanakatrayam
tāmreṇa ca prakartavyam avalambanakatrayam
āreṇa vā prakartavyamāyasaṃ naiva kārayet
madhye cordhvamukhaṃ kāryam avalaṃbaḥ suśobhanaḥ
raśmibhistoraṇāgre vā bandhayecca vidhānataḥ
jihvāmekāṃ tulāmadhye toraṇaṃ tu vidhīyate
uttarasya ca madhye ca śaṅkuṃ dṛḍhamanuttamam
vitānenopari chādya dṛḍhaṃ samyakprayojayet
śaṅkoḥ suṣirasampannaṃ valayaṃ kārayenmune
tulāmadhye vitānena tulayā lambake tathā
valayena prayoktavyaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ vāvalaṃbanam
sudṛḍhaṃ ca tulāmadhye navamāṅgulamānataḥ
paṭṭasyaiva tu vistāraṃ pañcamātrapramāṇataḥ
aparau sudṛḍhau piṇḍau śubhadravyeṇa kārayet
śikyādhastātprakartavyau pañcaprādeśavistarau
sahasreṇa tu kartavyau palānāṃ dhārakāvubhau
śatāṣṭakena vā kuryātpalaiḥ ṣaṭśatameva vā
catustālaṃ ca kartavyo vistāro madhyamastathā
sārdhatritālavistāraḥ kalaśasya vidhīyate
badhnīyātpañcapātraṃ tu trimātraṃ ṣaṭkamucyate
caturdvārasamopetaṃ dvāramaṅgulamātrakam
kuṇḍalaiśca samopetaiḥ śuklaśuddhasamanvitaiḥ
kuṇḍale kuṇḍale kāryaṃ śṛṅkhalāparimaṇḍalam
śṛṅkhalādhāravalayam avalaṃbena yojayet
prādeśaṃ vā caturmātraṃ bhūmes tyaktvāvalambayet
ghaṭau puruṣamātrau tu kartavyau śobhanāvubhau
tau vālukābhiḥ sampūrya śivaṃ tatra viniṣkṣipet
dvihastamātramavaṭe sthāpanīyau prayatnataḥ
niḥśeṣaṃ pūrayed vidvān vālukābhiḥ samantataḥ
yena niścalatāṃ gacchettena mārgeṇa kārayet
śrūyatāṃ paramaṃ guhyaṃ vedikoparimaṇḍalam
aṣṭamāṅgulasaṃyuktaṃ maṅgalāṅkuraśobhitam
phalapuṣpasamākīrṇaṃ dhūpadīpasamanvitam
vedimadhye prakartavyaṃ darpaṇodarasannibham
ālikhenmaṇḍalaṃ pūrvaṃ caturdvārasamanvitam
śobhopaśobhāsampannaṃ karṇikākesarānvitam
varṇajātisamopetaṃ pañcavarṇaṃ tu kārayet
vajraṃ prāgantare bhāge āgneyyāṃ śaktimujjvalām
ālikheddakṣiṇe daṇḍaṃ nairṛtyāṃ khaḍgam ālikhet
pāśaś ca vāruṇe lekhyo dhvajaṃ vai vāyugocare
kauberyāṃ tu gadā lekhyā aiśānyāṃ śūlamālikhet
śūlasya vāmadeśena cakraṃ padmaṃ tu dakṣiṇe
evaṃ likhitvā paścācca homakarma samācaret
pradhānahomaṃ gāyatryā svāhā śakrāya vahnaye
yamāya rākṣaseśāya varuṇāya ca vāyave
kuberāyeśvarāyātha viṣṇave brahmaṇe punaḥ
svāhāntaṃ praṇavenaiva hotavyaṃ vidhipūrvakam
svaśākhāgnimukhenaiva jayādipratisaṃyutam
sviṣṭāntaṃ sarvakāryāṇi kārayedvidhivattadā
sarvahomāgrahome ca samit pālāśam ucyate
ekaviṃśatisaṃkhyātaṃ mantreṇānena homayet
ayanta idhma ātmā jātavedas tenedhyasva vardhasva ceddhavardhaya cāsmān prajayā paśubhir brahmavarcasenānnādyena sa medhaya svāhā
bhūḥ svāhā bhuvaḥ svāhā svaḥ svāhā bhūrbhuvaḥ svastathaiva ca
samiddhomaśca caruṇā ghṛtasya ca yathākramam
śuklānnapāyasaṃ caiva mudgānnaṃ caravaḥ smṛtāḥ
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
agna āyūṃṣi pavasa āsuvor jamiṣaṃ ca naḥ
āre bādhasva chunām
agnirṛṣiḥ pavamānaḥ pāñcajanyaḥ purohitaḥ
tam īmahe mahāgayam
agne pavasva svapā asme varcaḥ suvīryam
dadhadrayiṃ mayi poṣam
prajāpate na tvadetānyanyo viśvā jātāni paritā babhūva
yatkāmāste juhumastanno astu vayaṃ syāma patayo rayīṇām
gāyatryā ca pradhānasya samiddhomastathaiva ca
caruṇā ca tathājyasya śakrādīnāṃ ca homayet
vajrādīnāṃ ca hotavyaṃ sahasrārdhaṃ tataḥ kramāt
brahmayajñeti mantreṇa brahmaṇe viṣṇave punaḥ
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt
ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ kathito homamārgaḥ suśobhanaḥ
dūrvayā kṣīrayuktena pañcaviṃśatpṛthakpṛthak
tryaṃbakaṃ yajāmahe sugandhiṃ puṣṭivardhanam
urvārukam iva bandhanān mṛtyor mukṣīya māmṛtāt
dūrvāhomaḥ praśasto 'yaṃ vāstuhomaśca sarvathā
prāyaścittamaghoreṇa sarpiṣā ca śataṃśatam
brahmāṇaṃ dakṣiṇe vāme viṣṇuṃ viśvaguruṃ śivam
madhye devyā samaṃ jñeyamindrādigaṇasaṃvṛtam
ādityaṃ bhāskaraṃ bhānuṃ raviṃ devaṃ divākaram
uṣāṃ prabhāṃ tathā prajñāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sāvitrimeva ca
pañcaprakāravidhinā khakholkāya mahātmane
viṣṭarāṃ subhagāṃ caiva vardhanīṃ ca pradakṣiṇām
āpyāyanīṃ ca sampūjya devīṃ padmāsane ravim
prabhūtaṃ vātha kartavyaṃ vimalaṃ dakṣiṇe tathā
sāraṃ paścimabhāge ca ārādhyaṃ cottare yajet
madhye sukhaṃ vijānīyātkesareṣu yathākramam
dīptāṃ sūkṣmāṃ jayāṃ bhadrāṃ vibhūtiṃ vimalāṃ kramāt
amoghāṃ vidyutāṃ caiva madhyataḥ sarvatomukhīm
somamaṅgārakaṃ caiva budhaṃ gurumanukramāt
bhārgavaṃ ca tathā mandaṃ rāhuṃ ketuṃ tathaiva ca
pūjayeddhomayedevaṃ dāpayecca viśeṣataḥ
yogino bhojayettatra śivatattvaikapāragān
divyādhyayanasampannān kṛtvaivaṃ vidhivistaram
home pravartamāne ca pūrvadiksthānamadhyame
ārohayedvidhānena rudrādhyāyena vai nṛpam
dhārayettatra bhūpālaṃ ghaṭikaikāṃ vidhānataḥ
yajamāno japenmantraṃ rudragāyatrisaṃjñakam
ghaṭikārdhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā tatraivāsanam ārabhet
ālokya vāruṇaṃ dhīmānkūrcahastaḥ samāhitaḥ
nṛpaśca bhūṣaṇairyuktaḥ khaḍgakheṭakadhārakaḥ
svastirityādibhiścādāvante caiva viśeṣataḥ
puṇyāhaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ kāryaṃ vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ
jayamaṅgalaśabdādibrahmaghoṣaiḥ suśobhanaiḥ
nṛtyavādyādibhirgītaiḥ sarvaśobhāsamanvitaiḥ
svamevaṃ candradigbhāge suvarṇaṃ tatra vikṣipet
tulādhārau samau vṛttau tulābhāraḥ sadā bhavet
śataniṣkādhikaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tadardhaṃ madhyamaṃ smṛtam
tasyārdhaṃ ca kaniṣṭhaṃ syāttrividhaṃ tatra kalpitam
vastrayugmamathoṣṇīṣaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ kaṇṭhaśobhanam
aṅgulībhūṣaṇaṃ caiva maṇibandhasya bhūṣaṇam
etāni caiva sarvāṇi prārambhe dharmakarmaṇi
pāśupatavratāyātha bhasmāṅgāya pradāpayet
pūrvoktabhūṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ soṣṇīṣaṃ vastrasaṃyutam
dadyād etat prayoktṛbhya ācchādanapaṭaṃ budhaḥ
dakṣiṇāṃ ca śataṃ sārdhaṃ tadardhaṃ vā pradāpayet
yogināṃ caiva sarveṣāṃ pṛthaṅniṣkaṃ pradāpayet
yāgopakaraṇaṃ divyamācāryāya pradāpayet
itareṣāṃ yatīnāṃ tu pṛthaṅniṣkaṃ pradāpayet
tulārohasuvarṇaṃ ca śivāya vinivedayet
prāsādaṃ maṇḍapaṃ caiva prākāraṃ bhūṣaṇaṃ tathā
suvarṇapuṣpaṃ paṭahaṃ khaḍgaṃ vai kośameva ca
kṛtvā dattvā śivāyātha kiṃciccheṣaṃ ca buddhimān
ācāryebhyaḥ pradātavyaṃ bhasmāṅgebhyo viśeṣataḥ
bandīkṛtān visarjyātha kārāgṛhanivāsinaḥ
sahasrakalaśaistatra secayetparameśvaram
ghṛtena kevalenāpi devadevamumāpatim
payasā vātha dadhnā vā sarvadravyairathāpi vā
brahmakūrcena vā devaṃ pañcagavyena vā punaḥ
gāyatryā caiva gomūtraṃ gomayaṃ praṇavena vā
āpyāyasveti vai kṣīraṃ dadhikrāvṇoti vai dadhi
tejosītyājyam īśānamantreṇaivābhiṣecayet
devasya tveti deveśaṃ kuśāṃbukalaśena vai
rudrādhyāyena vā sarvaṃ snāpayetparameśvaram
sahasrakalaśaṃ śaṃbhornāmnāṃ caiva sahasrakaiḥ
viṣṇunā kathitairvāpi taṇḍinā kathitaistu vā
dakṣeṇa munimukhyena kīrtitairathavā punaḥ
mahāpūjā prakartavyā mahādevasya bhaktitaḥ
śivārcakāya dātavyā dakṣiṇā svaguroḥ sadā
dehārṇavaṃ ca sarveṣāṃ dakṣiṇā ca yathākramam
dīnāndhakṛpaṇānāṃ ca bālavṛddhakṛśāturān
bhojayecca vidhānena dakṣiṇāmapi dāpayet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tulāpuruṣadānavidhāvaṣṭāviṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
tulā te kathitā hyeṣā ādyā sāmānyarūpiṇī
hiraṇyagarbhaṃ vakṣyāmi dvitīyaṃ sarvasiddhidam
adhaḥ pātraṃ sahasreṇa hiraṇyena vidhīyate
ūrdhvapātraṃ tadardhena mukhaṃ saṃveśamātrakam
haimamevaṃ śubhaṃ kuryāt sarvālaṃkārasaṃyutam
adhaḥ pātre smareddevīṃ guṇatrayasamanvitām
caturviṃśatikāṃ devīṃ brahmaviṣṇvagnirūpiṇīm
ūrdhvapātre guṇātītaṃ ṣaḍviṃśakam umāpatim
ātmānaṃ puruṣaṃ dhyāyet pañcaviṃśakam agrajam
pūrvoktasthānamadhye 'tha vedikopari maṇḍale
śālimadhye kṣipennītvā navavastraiśca veṣṭayet
māṣakalkena cālipya pañcadravyeṇa pūjayet
īśānādyairyathānyāyaṃ pañcabhiḥ paripūjayet
pūrvavacchivapūjā ca homaścaiva yathākramam
devīṃ gāyatrikāṃ japtvā praviśet prāṅmukhaḥ svayam
vidhinaiva tu sampādya garbhādhānādikāṃ kriyām
kṛtvā ṣoḍaśamārgeṇa vidhinā brāhmaṇottamaḥ
dūrvāṅkuraistu kartavyā secanā dakṣiṇe puṭe
auduṃbaraphalaiḥ sārdham ekaviṃśatkuśodakam
īśānyāṃ tāvadevātra kuryātsīmantakarmaṇi
udvahetkanyakāṃ kṛtvā triṃśanniṣkeṇa śobhanām
alaṃkṛtya tathā hutvā śivāya vinivedayet
annaprāśanake vidvān bhojayetpāyasādibhiḥ
evaṃ viśvajitāntā vai garbhādhānādikāḥ kriyāḥ
śaktibījena kartavyā brāhmaṇairvedapāragaiḥ
śeṣaṃ sarvaṃ ca vidhivattulāhemavadācaret
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekonatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
adhunā sampravakṣyāmi tilaparvatamuttamam
pūrvoktasthānakāle tu kṛtvā sampūjya yatnataḥ
susame bhūtale ramye vedinā ca vivarjite
daśatālapramāṇena daṇḍaṃ saṃsthāpya vai mune
adbhiḥ saṃprokṣya paścāddhi tilāṃstvasminvinikṣipet
pañcagavyena taṃ deśaṃ prokṣayedbrāhmaṇottamaḥ
maṇḍalaṃ kalpayedvidvānpūrvavatsusamantataḥ
navavastraiśca saṃsthāpya ramyapuṣpairvikīrya ca
tasminsaṃcayanaṃ kāryaṃ tilabhārairviśeṣataḥ
daṇḍaprādeśamutsedhamuttamaṃ parikīrtitam
caturaṅgulahīnaṃ tu madhyamaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ
daṇḍatulyaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ syāddaṇḍahīnaṃ na kārayet
veṣṭayitvā navairvastraiḥ paritaḥ pūjayetkramāt
sadyādīni pravinyasya pūjayedvidhipūrvakam
aṣṭadikṣu ca kartavyāḥ pūrvoktā mūrtayaḥ kramāt
triniṣkena suvarṇena pratyekaṃ kārayetkramāt
dakṣiṇā vidhinā kāryā tulābhāravadeva tu
homaśca pūrvavat prokto yathāvanmunisattamāḥ
arcayeddevadeveśaṃ lokapālasamāvṛtam
tilaparvatamadhyasthaṃ tilaparvatarūpiṇam
śivārcanā ca kartavyā sahasrakalaśādibhiḥ
darśayettilamadhyasthaṃ devadevamumāpatim
pūjayitvā vidhānena krameṇa ca visarjayet
śrotriyāya daridrāya dāpayettilaparvatam
evaṃ tilanagaḥ proktaḥ sarvasmādadhikaḥ paraḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tilaparvatadānaṃ nāma triṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
athānyaṃ parvataṃ sūkṣmamalpadravyaṃ mahāphalam
dravyamātropasaṃyukte kāle madhyaṃ vidhīyate
gomayāliptabhūmau tu hyaṃbarāṇi prakīrya ca
tanmadhye nikṣipeddhīmāṃstilabhāratrayaṃ śubham
padmamaṣṭadalaṃ kuryātkarṇikākesarānvitam
daśaniṣkeṇa tatkāryaṃ tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
tilamadhye nyasetpadmaṃ padmamadhye maheśvaram
ārādhya vidhivaddevaṃ vāmādīni prapūjayet
śaktirūpaṃ suvarṇena triniṣkeṇa tu kārayet
nyāsaṃ tu paritaḥ kuryādvighneśānparibhāgataḥ
pūrvoktahemamānena vighneśānapi kārayet
tān abhyarcya vidhānena gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
japahomārcanādānābhiṣekādyaṃ ca pūrvavat
suvarṇamedinīdānaṃ pravakṣyāmi samāsataḥ
pūrvoktadeśakāle tu kārayenmunibhiḥ saha
lakṣaṇena yathāpūrvaṃ kuṇḍe vā maṇḍale 'thavā
medinīṃ kārayeddivyāṃ sahasreṇāpi vā punaḥ
ekahastā prakartavyā caturasrā suśobhanā
saptadvīpasamudrādyaiḥ parvatairabhisaṃvṛtā
sarvatīrthasamopetā madhye merusamanvitā
athavā madhyato dvīpaṃ navakhaṇḍaṃ prakalpayet
pūrvavannikhilaṃ kṛtvā maṇḍale vedimadhyataḥ
saptabhāgaikabhāgena sahasrādvidhipūrvakam
śivabhakte pradātavyā dakṣiṇā pūrvacoditā
sahasrakalaśādyaiśca śaṅkaraṃ pūjayecchivam
suvarṇamedinīproktaṃ liṅge 'smin dānam uttamam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge suvarṇamedinīdānaṃ nāma dvātriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
athānyat sampravakṣyāmi kalpapādapamuttamam
śataniṣkeṇa kṛtvaivaṃ sarvaśākhāsamanvitam
śākhānāṃ vividhaṃ kṛtvā muktādāmādyalambanam
divyairmārakataiścaiva cāṅkurāgraṃ pravinyaset
pravālaṃ kārayedvidvānpravālena drumasya tu
phalāni padmarāgaiśca parito 'sya suśobhayet
mūlaṃ ca nīlaratnena vajreṇa skandhamuttamam
vaiḍūryeṇa drumāgraṃ ca puṣparāgeṇa mastakam
gomedakena vai kandaṃ sūryakāntena suvrata
candrakāntena vā vedīṃ drumasya sphaṭikena vā
vitastimātramāyāmaṃ vṛkṣasya parikīrtitam
śākhāṣṭakasya mānaṃ ca vistāraṃ cordhvatastathā
tanmūle sthāpayelliṅgaṃ lokapālaiḥ samāvṛtam
pūrvoktavedimadhye tu maṇḍale sthāpya pādapam
pūjayed devam īśānaṃ lokapālāṃśca yatnataḥ
pūrvavajjapahomādyaṃ tulābhāravadācaret
nivedayeddrumaṃ śaṃbhoryogināṃ vātha vā nṛpa
bhasmāṅgibhyo 'thavā rājā sārvabhaumo bhaviṣyati
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kalpapādapadānavidhir nāma trayastriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
gaṇeśeśaṃ pravakṣyāmi dānaṃ pūrvoktamaṇḍape
sampūjya devadeveśaṃ lokapālasamāvṛtam
viśveśvarānyathāśāstraṃ sarvābharaṇasaṃyutān
daśaniṣkeṇa vai kṛtvā sampūjya ca vidhānataḥ
aṣṭadikṣvaṣṭakuṇḍeṣu pūrvavaddhomamācaret
pañcāvaraṇamārgeṇa pāraṃparyakrameṇa ca
saptaviprānsamabhyarcya kanyāmekāṃ tathottare
dāpayetsarvamantrāṇi svaiḥsvairmantrairanukramāt
dattvaivaṃ sarvapāpebhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge gaṇeśeśadānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma catustriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
atha te sampravakṣyāmi hemadhenuvidhikramam
sarvapāpapraśamanaṃ grahadurbhikṣanāśanam
upasargapraśamanaṃ sarvavyādhinivāraṇam
niṣkāṇāṃ ca sahasreṇa suvarṇena tu kārayet
tadardhenāpi vā samyak tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
śatena vā prakartavyā sarvarūpaguṇānvitā
gorūpaṃ sukhuraṃ divyaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam
khurāgre vinyasedvajraṃ śṛṅge vai padmarāgakam
bhruvormadhye nyaseddivyaṃ mauktikaṃ munisattamāḥ
vaiḍūryeṇa stanāḥ kāryā lāṅgūlaṃ nīlataḥ śubham
dantasthāne prakartavyaḥ puṣparāgaḥ suśobhanaḥ
paśuvatkārayitvā tu vatsaṃ kuryātsuśobhanam
suvarṇadaśaniṣkeṇa sarvaratnasuśobhitam
pūrvoktavedikāmadhye maṇḍalaṃ parikalpya tu
tanmadhye surabhiṃ sthāpya savatsāṃ sarvatattvavit
savatsāṃ surabhiṃ tatra vastrayugmena veṣṭayet
sampūjayed gāṃ gāyatryā savatsāṃ surabhiṃ punaḥ
athaikāgnividhānena homaṃ kuryādyathāvidhi
samidājyavidhānena pūrvavaccheṣamācaret
śivapūjā prakartavyā liṅgaṃ snāpya ghṛtādibhiḥ
gāmālabhya ca gāyatryā śivāyā dāpayecchubhām
dakṣiṇā ca prakartavyā triṃśanniṣkā mahāmate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hemadhenudānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma pañcatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
lakṣmīdānaṃ pravakṣyāmi mahadaiśvaryavardhanam
pūrvoktamaṇḍape kāryaṃ vedikoparimaṇḍale
śrīdevīmatulāṃ kṛtvā hiraṇyena yathāvidhi
sahasreṇa tadardhena tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
aṣṭottaraśatenāpi sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutām
maṇḍale vinyasellakṣmīṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutām
tasyāstu dakṣiṇe bhāge sthaṇḍile viṣṇumarcayet
arcayitvā vidhānena śrīsūktena sureśvarīm
arcayedviṣṇugāyatryā viṣṇuṃ viśvaguruṃ harim
ārādhya vidhinā devīṃ pūrvavaddhomam ācaret
samiddhutvā vidhānena ājyāhutimathācaret
pṛthagaṣṭottaraśataṃ homayed brāhmaṇottamaiḥ
āhūya yajamānaṃ tu tasyāḥ pūrvadiśi sthale
tasmai tāṃ darśayeddevīṃ daṇḍavat praṇamet kṣitau
praṇamya viṣṇuṃ tatrasthaṃ śivaṃ pūrvavadarcayet
tasyā viṃśatibhāgaṃ tu dakṣiṇā parikīrtitā
tadardhāṃśaṃ tu dātavyamitareṣāṃ yathārhataḥ
tatastu homayecchaṃbhuṃ bhakto yogī viśeṣataḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge lakṣmīdānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma ṣaṭtriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
athātaḥ sampravakṣyāmi tiladhenuvidhikramam
pūrvoktamaṇḍape kuryācchivapūjāṃ tu paścime
tasyāgre madhyato bhūmau padmamālikhya śobhanam
vastrairācchāditaṃ padmaṃ tanmadhye vinyasecchubham
tilapuṣpaṃ tu kṛtvātha hemapadmaṃ vinikṣipet
triṃśanniṣkena kartavyaṃ tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
pañcaniṣkeṇa kartavyaṃ tadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
tamārādhya vidhānena gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
padmasyottaradigbhāge viprān ekādaśa nyaset
tānabhyarcya vidhānena gandhapuṣpādibhiḥ kramāt
ācchādanottarāsaṃgaṃ viprebhyo dāpayetkramāt
uṣṇīṣaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ kuṇḍale ca vibhūṣite
hemāṅgulīyakaṃ dattvā brāhmaṇebhyo vidhānataḥ
ekaṃ daśa ca vastrāṇi teṣāmagre prakīrya ca
teṣu vastreṣu niḥkṣipya tilādyāni pṛthakpṛthak
kāṃsyapātraṃ śatapalaṃ vibhidyaikādaśāṃśakam
ikṣudaṇḍaṃ ca dātavyaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ
gośṛṅge tu hiraṇyena dviniṣkeṇa tu kārayet
rajatena tu kartavyāḥ khurā niṣkadvayena tu
evaṃ pṛthakpṛthag dattvā tattileṣu vinikṣipet
rudraikādaśamantraistu rudrebhyo dāpayettadā
padmasya pūrvadigbhāge viprāndvādaśa pūjitān
etenaiva tu mārgeṇa teṣu śraddhāsamanvitaḥ
dvādaśādityamantraiśca dāpayedevameva ca
pūrvavaddakṣiṇe bhāge viprānṣoḍaśa saṃsthitān
mūrtiṃ vighneśamantraiśca dāpayetpūrvavatpunaḥ
yajamānena kartavyaṃ sarvametadyathākramam
kevalaṃ rudradānaṃ vā ādityebhyo 'thavā punaḥ
mūrtyādīnāṃ ca vā deyaṃ yathāvibhavavistaram
padmaṃ vinyasya rājāsau śeṣaṃ vā kārayennṛpaḥ
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā pañcaniṣkeṇa bhūṣaṇam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tiladhenudānavidhinirūpaṇaṃ nāma saptatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
gosahasrapradānaṃ ca vadāmi śṛṇu suvrata
gavāṃ sahasramādāya savatsaṃ saguṇaṃ śubham
tās tv abhyarcya yathāśāstram aṣṭau samyakprayatnataḥ
tāsāṃ śṛṅgāṇi hemnātha pratiniṣkeṇa bandhayet
khurāṃśca rajatenaiva bandhayet kaṇṭhadeśataḥ
pratiniṣkeṇa kartavyaṃ karṇe vajraṃ ca śobhanam
śivāya dadyādviprebhyo dakṣiṇāṃ ca pṛthakpṛthak
daśaniṣkaṃ tadardhaṃ vā tasyārdhārdham athāpi vā
yathāvibhavavistāraṃ niṣkamātramathāpi vā
vastrayugmaṃ ca dātavyaṃ pṛthagvipreṣu śobhanam
gāvaścārādhya yatnena dātavyāḥ sumanoramāḥ
evaṃ dattvā vidhānena śivamabhyarcya śaṃkaram
japedagre yathānyāyaṃ gavāṃ stavamanuttamam
gāvo mamāgrato nityaṃ gāvo naḥ pṛṣṭhatastathā
hṛdaye me sadā gāvo gavāṃ madhye vasāmy aham
iti kṛtvā dvijāgryebhyo dattvā gatvā pradakṣiṇam
tadromavarṣasaṃkhyāni svargaloke mahīyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge gosahasrapradānaṃ nāmāṣṭatriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
hiraṇyāśvapradānaṃ ca vadāmi vijayāvaham
aśvamedhātpunaḥ śreṣṭhaṃ vadāmi śṛṇu suvrata
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa aṣṭottaraśatena vā
kṛtvāśvaṃ lakṣaṇairyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam
pañcakalyāṇasampannaṃ divyākāraṃ tu kārayet
sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvāṅgaiśca samanvitam
sarvāyudhasamopetamindravāhanamuttamam
tanmadhyadeśe saṃsthāpya turaṅgaṃ svaguṇānvitam
uccaiḥśravasakaṃ matvā bhaktyā caiva samarcayet
tasya pūrvadiśābhāge brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam
surendrabuddhyā sampūjya pañcaniṣkaṃ pradāpayet
sa cāśvaḥ śivabhaktāya dātavyo vidhinaiva tu
suvarṇāśvaṃ pradattvā tu ācāryamapi pūjayet
yathāvibhavavistāraṃ pañcaniṣkam athāpi vā
dīnāndhakṛpaṇānāthabālavṛddhakṛśāturān
toṣayedannadānena brāhmaṇāṃśca viśeṣataḥ
etadyaḥ kurute bhaktyā dānamaśvasya mānavaḥ

iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge hiraṇyāśvadānaṃ nāmaikonacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
kanyādānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvadānottamottamam
kanyāṃ lakṣaṇasampannāṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitām
mātāpitrostu saṃvādaṃ kṛtvā dattvā dhanaṃ mahat
ātmīkṛtyātha saṃsnāpya vastraṃ dattvā śubhaṃ navam
bhūṣaṇairbhūṣayitvātha gandhamālyairathārcayet
nimittāni samīkṣyātha gotranakṣatrakādikān
ubhayościttamālokya ubhau sampūjya yatnataḥ
dātavyā śrotriyāyaiva brāhmaṇāya tapasvine
sākṣādadhītavedāya vidhinā brahmacāriṇe
dāsadāsīdhanāḍhyaṃ ca bhūṣaṇāni viśeṣataḥ
kṣetrāṇi ca dhanaṃ dhānyaṃ vāsāṃsi ca pradāpayet
yāvanti dehe romāṇi kanyāyāḥ saṃtatau punaḥ
tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi rudraloke mahīyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge kanyādānavidhir nāma catvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
hiraṇyavṛṣadānaṃ ca kathayāmi samāsataḥ
vṛṣarūpaṃ hiraṇyena sahasreṇātha kārayet
tadardhārdhena vā dhīmāṃstadardhārdhena vā punaḥ
aṣṭottaraśatenāpi vṛṣabhaṃ dharmarūpiṇam
lalāṭe kārayetpuṇḍramardhacandrakalākṛtim
sphaṭikena tu kartavyaṃ khuraṃ tu rajatena vai
grīvāṃ tu padmarāgeṇa kakudgomedakena ca
grīvāyāṃ ghaṇṭāvalayaṃ ratnacitraṃ tu kārayet
vṛṣāṅkaṃ kārayettatra kiṅkiṇīvalayāvṛtam
pūrvoktadeśakāle tu vedikoparimaṇḍale
vṛṣendraṃ sthāpayettatra paścimāmukham agrataḥ
īśvaraṃ pūjayedbhaktyā vṛṣārūḍhaṃ vṛṣadhvajam
vṛṣendraṃ pūjya gāyatryā namaskṛtya samāhitaḥ
tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāya vidmahe dharmapādāya dhīmahi
tanno vṛṣaḥ pracodayāt
mantreṇānena sampūjya vṛṣaṃ dharmavivṛddhaye
homayecca ghṛtānnādyair yathāvibhavavistaram
vṛṣabhaḥ pūjya dātavyo brāhmaṇebhyaḥ śivāya vā
dakṣiṇā caiva dātavyā yathāvittānusārataḥ
etadyaḥ kurute bhaktyā vṛṣadānamanuttamam
śivasyānucaro bhūtvā tenaiva saha modate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge suvarṇavṛṣadānaṃ nāmaikacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
gajadānaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
dvijāya vā śivāyātha dātavyaḥ pūjya pūrvavat
gajaṃ sulakṣaṇopetaṃ haimaṃ vā rājataṃ tu vā
sahasraniṣkamātreṇa tadardhenāpi kārayet
tadardhārdhena vā kuryātsarvalakṣaṇabhūṣitam
pūrvoktadeśakāle ca devāya vinivedayet
aṣṭamyāṃ vā pradātavyaṃ śivāya parameṣṭhine
brāhmaṇāya daridrāya śrotriyāyāhitāgnaye
śivamuddiśya dātavyaṃ śivaṃ sampūjya pūrvavat
etadyaḥ kurute dānaṃ śivabhaktisamāhitam
sthitvā svarge ciraṃ kālaṃ rājā gajapatirbhavet
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvicatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
lokapālāṣṭakaṃ divyaṃ sākṣātparamadurlabham
sarvasaṃpatkaraṃ guhyaṃ paracakravināśanam
svadeśarakṣaṇaṃ divyaṃ gajavājivivardhanam
putravṛddhikaraṃ puṇyaṃ gobrāhmaṇahitāvaham
pūrvoktadeśakāle tu vedikoparimaṇḍale
madhye śivaṃ samabhyarcya yathānyāyaṃ yathākramam
digvidikṣu prakartavyaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ vālukāmayam
aṣṭau viprānsamabhyarcya vedavedāṅgapāragān
jitendriyān kulodbhūtān sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutān
śivābhimukham āsīnān āhateṣvaṃbareṣu ca
vastrair ābharaṇair divyair lokapālakamantrakaiḥ
gandhapuṣpaiḥ sudhūpaiśca brāhmaṇānarcayetkramāt
pūrvato homayedagnau lokapālakamantrakaiḥ
samidghṛtābhyāṃ hotavyamagnikāryaṃ krameṇa vā
evaṃ hutvā vidhānena ācāryaḥ śivavatsalaḥ
yajamānaṃ samāhūya sarvābharaṇabhūṣitān
tena tānpūjayitvātha dvijebhyo dāpayeddhanam
pṛthakpṛthaktanmantraiśca daśaniṣkaṃ ca bhūṣaṇam
daśaniṣkeṇa kartavyamāsanaṃ kevalaṃ pṛthak
snapanaṃ tatra kartavyaṃ śivasya vidhipūrvakam
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā yathāvibhavavistaram
evaṃ yaḥ kurute dānaṃ lokeśānāṃ tu bhaktitaḥ
lokeśānāṃ ciraṃ sthitvā sārvabhaumo bhavedbudhaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tricatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sanatkumāra uvāca
athānyat sampravakṣyāmi sarvadānottamottamam
pūrvoktadeśakāle ca maṇḍape ca vidhānataḥ
praṇayātkuṇḍamadhye ca sthaṇḍile śivasannidhau
pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ samāsādya padmayonimataḥ param
mantrābhyāṃ vidhinoktābhyāṃ praṇavādisamantrakam
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt
brahmabrāhmaṇavṛddhāya brahmaṇe viśvavedhase
śivāya haraye svāhā svadhā vauṣaḍ vaṣaṭ tathā
pūjayitvā vidhānena paścāddhomaṃ samācaret
sarvadravyaṃ hi hotavyaṃ dvābhyāṃ kuṇḍavidhānataḥ
ṛtvijau dvau prakartavyau guruṇā vedapāragau
tānuddiśya yathānyāyaṃ viprebhyo dāpayeddhanam
śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tebhyaḥ pṛthakpṛthaganuttamam
vastrābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam
gurureko hi vai śrīmān brahmā viṣṇurmaheśvaraḥ
teṣāṃ pṛthakpṛthagdeyaṃ bhojayedbrāhmaṇānapi
śivārcanā ca kartavyā snapanādi yathākramam
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge catuścatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
evaṃ ṣoḍaśa dānāni kathitāni śubhāni ca
jīvacchrāddhakramo 'smākaṃ vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
sūta uvāca
jīvacchrāddhavidhiṃ vakṣye samāsātsarvasaṃmatam
manave devadevena kathitaṃ brahmaṇā purā
vasiṣṭhāya ca śiṣṭāya bhṛgave bhārgavāya ca
śṛṇvantu sarvabhāvena sarvasiddhikaraṃ param
śrāddhamārgakramaṃ sākṣācchrāddhārhāṇāmapi kramam
viśeṣamapi vakṣyāmi jīvacchrāddhasya suvratāḥ
parvate vā nadītīre vane vāyatane 'pi vā
jīvacchrāddhaṃ prakartavyaṃ mṛtakāle prayatnataḥ
jīvacchrāddhe kṛte jīvo jīvanneva vimucyate
karma kurvannakurvanvā jñānī vājñānavānapi
śrotriyo 'śrotriyo vāpi brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo 'pi vā
vaiśyo vā nātra saṃdeho yogamārgagato yathā
parīkṣya bhūmiṃ vidhivadgandhavarṇarasādibhiḥ
śalyamuddhṛtya yatnena sthaṇḍilaṃ saikataṃ bhuvi
madhyato hastamātreṇa kuṇḍaṃ caivāyataṃ śubham
sthaṇḍilaṃ vā prakartavyamiṣumātraṃ punaḥ punaḥ
upalipya vidhānena cālipyāgniṃ vidhāya ca
anvādhāya yathāśāstraṃ parigṛhya ca sarvataḥ
paristīrya svaśākhoktaṃ pāraṃparyakramāgatam
samāpyāgnimukhaṃ sarvaṃ mantrairetairyathākramam
sampūjya sthaṇḍile vahnau homayetsamidādibhiḥ
ādau kṛtvā samiddhomaṃ caruṇā ca pṛthakpṛthak
ghṛtena ca pṛthak pātre śodhitena pṛthakpṛthak
juhuyādātmanoddhṛtya tattvabhūtāni sarvataḥ

oṃ janaḥ prakṛtaye svāhā

oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvāya bhūḥ svāhā

oṃ śarva dharāṃ me gopāya ghrāṇe gandhaṃ śarvapatnyai bhūḥ svāhā
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavāya devāya bhuvo namaḥ
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavāya devāya bhuvaḥ svāhā
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavasya devasya patnyai bhuvo namaḥ
oṃ bhava jalaṃ me gopāya jihvāyāṃ rasaṃ bhavasya patnyai bhuvaḥ svāhā

rudrāgniṃ me gopāya netre rūpaṃ rudrasya devasya patnyai svaḥ svāhā
ugra vāyuṃ me gopāya tvaci sparśaṃ ugrāya devāya maharnamaḥ
