oṃ ugra vāyuṃ me gopāya tvaci sparśamugrasya devasya patnyai devāya janaḥ svāhā

mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ dharme mahādevāya ṛtaṃ svāhā

mahādeva satyaṃ me gopāya śraddhāṃ mahādevasya patnyai ṛtaṃ svāhā

oṃ śivāya namaḥ

oṃ svaḥ svāhā
bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ svāhā
evaṃ krameṇa juhuyācchrāddhoktaṃ ca yathākramam
saptame 'hani yogīndrāñchrāddhārhān api bhojayet
śarvādīnāṃ ca viprāṇāṃ vastrābharaṇakambalān
vāhanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ kāṃsyatāmrādibhājanam
haimaṃ ca rājataṃ dhenuṃ tilān kṣetraṃ ca vaibhavam
dāsīdāsagaṇaścaiva dātavyo dakṣiṇāmapi
piṇḍaṃ ca pūrvavaddadyātpṛthagaṣṭaprakārataḥ
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayecca sadakṣiṇam
ekaṃ vā yoganirataṃ bhasmaniṣṭhaṃ jitendriyam
tryahaṃ caiva tu rudrasya mahācarunivedanam
viśeṣa evaṃ kathito 'śeṣaśrāddhacoditaḥ
mṛte kuryānna kuryādvā jīvanmukto yataḥ svayam
nityanaimittikādīni kuryād vā saṃtyajet tu vā
bāndhave 'pi mṛte tasya śaucāśaucaṃ na vidyate
sūtakaṃ ca na saṃdehaḥ snānamātreṇa śudhyati
paścājjāte kumāre ca sve kṣetre cātmano yadi
tasya sarvaṃ prakartavyaṃ putro 'pi brahmavid bhavet
kanyakā yadi saṃjātā paścāttasya mahātmanaḥ
ekaparṇā iva jñeyā aparṇā iva suvratāḥ
bhavatyeva na saṃdehastasyāścānvayajā api
mucyante nātra saṃdehaḥ pitaro narakādapi
mucyante karmaṇānena mātṛtaḥ pitṛtastathā
kālaṃ gate dvije bhūmau khaneccāpi dahettu vā
putrakṛtyamaśeṣaṃ ca kṛtvā doṣo na vidyate
karmaṇā cottareṇaiva gatirasya na vidyate
brahmaṇā kathitaṃ sarvaṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanām
punaḥ sanatkumārāya kathitaṃ tena dhīmatā
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāyaiva kathitaṃ brahmasūnunā
prasādāttasya devasya vedavyāsasya dhīmataḥ
jñātaṃ mayā kṛtaṃ caiva niyogādeva tasya tu
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ rahasyaṃ brahmasiddhidam
muniputrāya dātavyaṃ na cābhaktāya suvratāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge jīvacchrāddhavidhir nāma pañcacatvāriṃśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
jīvacchrāddhavidhiḥ proktastvayā sūta mahāmate
mūrkhāṇām api mokṣārthamasmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa
rudrādityavasūnāṃ ca śakrādīnāṃ ca suvrata
pratiṣṭhā kīdṛśī śaṃbhor liṅgamūrteśca śobhanā
viṣṇoḥ śakrasya devasya brahmaṇaśca mahātmanaḥ
agner yasya nirṛter varuṇasya mahādyuteḥ
vāyoḥ somasya yakṣasya kuberasyāmitātmanaḥ
īśānasya dharāyāśca śrīpratiṣṭhātha vā katham
durgāśivāpratiṣṭhā ca haimavatyāśca śobhanā
skandasya gaṇarājasya nandinaśca viśeṣataḥ
tathānyeṣāṃ ca devānāṃ gaṇānāmapi vā punaḥ
pratiṣṭhālakṣaṇaṃ sarvaṃ vistārād vaktumarhasi
bhavānsarvārthatattvajño rudrabhaktaśca suvrata
kṛṣṇadvaipāyanasyāsi sākṣāttvamaparā tanuḥ
sumanturjaiminiścaiva pailaśca paramarṣayaḥ
gurubhaktiṃ tathā kartuṃ samartho romaharṣaṇaḥ
iti vyāsasya vipulā gāthā bhāgīrathītaṭe
ekaḥ samo vā bhinno vā śiṣyastasya mahādyuteḥ
vaiśaṃpāyanatulyo 'si vyāsaśiṣyeṣu bhūtale
tasmādasmākamakhilaṃ vaktumarhasi sāṃpratam
evamuktvā sthiteṣveva teṣu sarveṣu tatra ca
babhūva vismayo 'tīva munīnāṃ tasya cāgrataḥ
athāntarikṣe vipulā sākṣāddevī sarasvatī
alaṃ munīnāṃ praśno 'yamiti vācā babhūva ha
sarvaṃ liṅgamayaṃ lokaṃ sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya sthāpayetpūjayecca tat
liṅgasthāpanasanmārganihitasvāyatāsinā
āśu brahmāṇḍamudbhidya nirgacchedaviśaṅkayā
upendrāmbhojagarbhendrayamāmbudhanadeśvarāḥ
tathānye ca śivaṃ sthāpya liṅgamūrtiṃ maheśvaram
sveṣu sveṣu ca pakṣeṣu pradhānāste yathā dvijāḥ
brahmā haraśca bhagavānviṣṇurdevī ramā dharā
lakṣmīrdhṛtiḥ smṛtiḥ prajñā dharā durgā śacī tathā
rudrāśca vasavaḥ skando viśākhaḥ śākha eva ca
naigameśaśca bhagavāṃllokapālā grahāstathā
sarve nandipurogāśca gaṇā gaṇapatiḥ prabhuḥ
pitaro munayaḥ sarve kuberādyāśca suprabhāḥ
ādityā vasavaḥ sāṃkhyā aśvinau ca bhiṣagvarau
viśvedevāśca sādhyāśca paśavaḥ pakṣiṇo mṛgāḥ
brahmādisthāvarāntaṃ ca sarvaṃ liṅge pratiṣṭhitam
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya sthāpayelliṅgamavyayam
yatnena sthāpitaṃ sarvaṃ pūjitaṃ pūjayedyadi
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ṣaṭcatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
iti niśamya kṛtāñjalayas tadā divi mahāmunayaḥ kṛtaniścayāḥ
śivataraṃ śivamīśvaramavyayaṃ manasi liṅgamayaṃ praṇipatya te
sakaladevapatirbhagavānajo hariraśeṣapatirguruṇā svayam
munivarāśca gaṇāśca surāsurā naravarāḥ śivaliṅgamayāḥ punaḥ
śrutvaivaṃ munayaḥ sarve ṣaṭkulīyāḥ samāhitāḥ
saṃtyajya sarvaṃ devasya pratiṣṭhāṃ kartumudyatāḥ
apṛcchansūtamanaghaṃ harṣagadgadayā girā
liṅgapratiṣṭhāṃ vipulāṃ sarve te śaṃsitavratāḥ
sūta uvāca
pratiṣṭhāṃ liṅgamūrtervo yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
pravakṣyāmi samāsena dharmakāmārthamuktaye
kṛtvaiva liṅgaṃ vidhinā bhuvi liṅgeṣu yatnataḥ
liṅgamekatamaṃ śailaṃ brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakam
hemaratnamayaṃ vāpi rājataṃ tāmrajaṃ tu vā
savedikaṃ sasūtraṃ ca samyagvistṛtamastakam
viśodhya sthāpayedbhaktyā savedikamanuttamam
liṅgavedī umā devī liṅgaṃ sākṣānmaheśvaraḥ
tayoḥ sampūjanād eva devī devaśca pūjitau
pratiṣṭhayā ca deveśo devyā sārdhaṃ pratiṣṭhitaḥ
tasmātsavedikaṃ liṅgaṃ sthāpayetsthāpakottamaḥ
mūle brahmā vasati bhagavānmadhyabhāge ca viṣṇuḥ sarveśānaḥ paśupatirajo rudramūrtirvareṇyaḥ
tasmālliṅgaṃ gurutarataraṃ pūjayetsthāpayedvā yasmātpūjyo gaṇapatirasau devamukhyaiḥ samastaiḥ
gandhaiḥ sragdhūpadīpaiḥ snapanahutabalistotramantropahārairnityaṃ ye 'bhyarcayanti tridaśavaratanuṃ liṅgamūrtiṃ maheśam
garbhādhānādināśakṣayabhayarahitā devagandharvamukhyaiḥ siddhairvandyāśca pūjyā gaṇavaranamitāste bhavantyaprameyāḥ
tasmādbhaktyopacāreṇa sthāpayetparameśvaram
pūjayecca viśeṣeṇa liṅgaṃ sarvārthasiddhaye
samarcya sthāpayelliṅgaṃ tīrthamadhye śivāsane
kūrcavastrādibhirliṅgamācchādya kalaśaiḥ punaḥ
lokapālādidaivatyaiḥ sakūrcaiḥ sākṣataiḥ śubhaiḥ
utkūrcaiḥ svastikādyaiśca citratantukaveṣṭitaiḥ
vajrādikāyudhopetaiḥ savastraiḥ sapidhānakaiḥ
lakṣayetparito liṅgamīśānena pratiṣṭhitam
dhūpadīpasamopetaṃ vitānavitatāṃbaram
lokapāladhvajaiścaiva gajādimahiṣādibhiḥ
citritaiḥ pūjitaiścaiva darbhamālā ca śobhanā
sarvalakṣaṇasampūrṇā tayā bāhye ca veṣṭayet
tato 'dhivāsayet toye dhūpadīpasamanvite
pañcāhaṃ vā tryahaṃ vātha ekarātram athāpi vā
vedādhyayanasampanno nṛtyagītādimaṅgalaiḥ
kiṅkiṇīravakopetaṃ tālavīṇāravairapi
īkṣayetkālamavyagro yajamānaḥ samāhitaḥ
utthāpya svastikaṃ dhyāyenmaṇḍape lakṣaṇānvite
saṃskṛte vedisaṃyukte navakuṇḍena saṃvṛte
pūrvoktavidhinā yukte sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyute
aṣṭamaṇḍalasaṃyukte digdhvajāṣṭakasaṃyute
pūrvoktalakṣaṇopetaiḥ kuṇḍaiḥ prāgāditaḥ kramāt
pradhānaṃ kuṇḍamīśānyāṃ caturasraṃ vidhīyate
athavā pañcakuṇḍaikaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ caikameva ca
yajñopakaraṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ śivārcāyāṃ hi bhūṣaṇaiḥ
vedimadhye mahāśayyāṃ pañcatūlīprakalpitām
kalpayetkāñcanopetāṃ sitavastrāvaguṇṭhitām
prakalpyaivaṃ śivaṃ caiva sthāpayetparameśvaram
prākśiraskaṃ nyaselliṅgamīśānena yathāvidhi
ratnanyāse kṛte pūrvaṃ kevalaṃ kalaśaṃ nyaset
liṅgamācchādya vastrābhyāṃ kūrcena ca samantataḥ
ratnanyāse prasakte 'tha vāmādyā nava śaktayaḥ
navaratnaṃ hiraṇyādyaiḥ pañcagavyena saṃyutaiḥ
sarvadhānyasamopetaṃ śilāyāmapi vinyaset
sthāpayedbrahmaliṅgaṃ hi śivagāyatrisaṃyutam
kevalaṃ praṇavenāpi sthāpayecchivamavyayam
brahmajajñānamantreṇa brahmabhāgaṃ prabhostathā
viṣṇugāyatriyā bhāgaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tvatha vinyaset
sūtre tattvatrayopete praṇavena pravinyaset
sarvaṃ namaḥ śivāyeti namo haṃsaḥ śivāya ca
rudrādhyāyena vā sarvaṃ parimṛjya ca vinyaset
sthāpayedbrahmabhiścaiva kalaśānvai samantataḥ
vedimadhye nyasetsarvān pūrvoktavidhisaṃyutān
madhyakuṃbhe śivaṃ devīṃ dakṣiṇe parameśvarīm
skandaṃ tayośca madhye tu skandakuṃbhe sucitrite
brahmāṇaṃ skandakuṃbhe vā īśakumbhe hariṃ tathā
athavā śivakuṃbhe ca brahmāṅgāni ca vinyaset
śivo maheśvaraścaiva rudro viṣṇuḥ pitāmahaḥ
brahmāṇyevaṃ samāsena hṛdayādīni cāṃbikā
vedimadhye nyaset sarvān pūrvoktavidhisaṃyutān
vardhanyāṃ sthāpayeddevīṃ gandhatoyena pūrya ca
hiraṇyaṃ rajataṃ ratnaṃ śivakuṃbhe pravinyaset
vardhanyām api yatnena gāyatryaṅgaiśca suvratāḥ
vidyeśvarāṃ diśāṃ kuṃbhe brahmakūrcena pūrite
ananteśādidevāṃśca praṇavādinamo'ntakam
navavastraṃ pratighaṭamaṣṭakuṃbheṣu dāpayet
vidyeśvarāṇāṃ kuṃbheṣu hemaratnādi vinyaset
vaktrakrameṇa hotavyaṃ gāyatryaṅgakrameṇa ca
jayādisviṣṭaparyantaṃ sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret
secayecchivakuṃbhena vardhanyā vaiṣṇavena ca
paitāmahena kuṃbhena brahmabhāgaṃ viśeṣataḥ
vidyeśvarāṇāṃ kuṃbhaiśca secayetparameśvaram
vinyasetsarvamantrāṇi pūrvavatsusamāhitaḥ
pūjayetsnapanaṃ kṛtvā sahasrādiṣu saṃbhavaiḥ
dakṣiṇā ca pradātavyā sahasrapaṇamuttamam
itareṣāṃ tadardhaṃ syāttadardhaṃ vā vidhīyate
vastrāṇi ca pradhānasya kṣetrabhūṣaṇagodhanam
utsavaśca prakartavyo homayāgabaliḥ kramāt
navāhaṃ vāpi saptāham ekāhaṃ ca tryahaṃ tathā
homaśca pūrvavatprokto nityamabhyarcya śaṅkaram
devānāṃ bhāskarādīnāṃ homaṃ pūrvavadeva tu
abhyantare tathā bāhye vahnau nityaṃ samarcayet
ya evaṃ sthāpayelliṅgaṃ sa eva parameśvaraḥ
tena devagaṇā rudrā ṛṣayo 'psarasastathā
sthāpitāḥ pūjitāścaiva trailokyaṃ sacarācaram
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge liṅgasthāpanaṃ nāma saptacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
sarveṣāmapi devānāṃ pratiṣṭhāmapi vistarāt
svair mantrair yāgakuṇḍāni vinyasyaikaikameva ca
sthāpayedutsavaṃ kṛtvā pūjayecca vidhānataḥ
bhānoḥ pañcāgninā kāryaṃ dvādaśāgnikrameṇa vā
sarvakuṇḍāni vṛttāni padmākārāṇi suvratāḥ
aṃbāyā yonikuṇḍaṃ syādvardhanyekā vidhīyate
śaktīnāṃ sarvakāryeṣu yonikuṇḍaṃ vidhīyate
gāyatrīṃ kalpayecchaṃbhoḥ sarveṣāmapi yatnataḥ
sarve rudrāṃśajā yasmātsaṃkṣepeṇa vadāmi vaḥ
gāyatrībhedāḥ
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi
tannaḥ śivaḥ pracodayāt
gaṇāṃbikāyai vidmahe karmasiddhyai ca dhīmahi
tanno gaurī pracodayāt
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe mahādevāya dhīmahi
tanno rudraḥ pracodayāt
tatpuruṣāya vidmahe vakratuṇḍāya dhīmahi
tanno dantiḥ pracodayāt
mahāsenāya vidmahe vāgviśuddhāya dhīmahi
tannaḥ skandaḥ pracodayāt
tīkṣṇaśṛṅgāya vidmahe vedapādāya dhīmahi
tanno vṛṣaḥ pracodayāt
harivaktrāya vidmahe rudravaktrāya dhīmahi
tanno nandī pracodayāt
nārāyaṇāya vidmahe vāsudevāya dhīmahi
tanno viṣṇuḥ pracodayāt
mahāṃbikāyai vidmahe karmasiddhyai ca dhīmahi
tanno lakṣmīḥ pracodayāt
samuddhṛtāyai vidmahe viṣṇunaikena dhīmahi
tanno dharā pracodayāt
vainateyāya vidmahe suvarṇapakṣāya dhīmahi
tanno garuḍaḥ pracodayāt
padmodbhavāya vidmahe vedavaktrāya dhīmahi
tannaḥ sraṣṭā pracodayāt
śivāsyajāyai vidmahe devarūpāyai dhīmahi
tanno vācā pracodayāt
devarājāya vidmahe vajrahastāya dhīmahi
tannaḥ śakraḥ pracodayāt
rudranetrāya vidmahe śaktihastāya dhīmahi
tanno vahniḥ pracodayāt
vaivasvatāya vidmahe daṇḍahastāya dhīmahi
tanno yamaḥ pracodayāt
niśācarāya vidmahe khaḍgahastāya dhīmahi
tanno nirṛtiḥ pracodayāt
śuddhahastāya vidmahe pāśahastāya dhīmahi
tanno varuṇaḥ pracodayāt
sarpaprāṇāya vidmahe yaṣṭihastāya dhīmahi
tanno vāyuḥ pracodayāt
yakṣeśvarāya vidmahe gadāhastāya dhīmahi
tanno yakṣaḥ pracodayāt
sarveśvarāya vidmahe śūlahastāya dhīmahi
tanno rudraḥ pracodayāt
kātyāyanyai vidmahe kanyākumāryai dhīmahi
tanno durgā pracodayāt
evaṃ prabhidya gāyatrīṃ tattaddevānurūpataḥ
pūjayet sthāpayetteṣāmāsanaṃ praṇavaṃ smṛtam
athavā viṣṇumatulaṃ sūktena puruṣeṇa vā
viṣṇuṃ caiva mahāviṣṇuṃ sadāviṣṇumanukramāt
sthāpayeddevagāyatryā parikalpya vidhānataḥ
vāsudevaḥ pradhānastu tataḥ saṃkarṣaṇaḥ svayam
pradyumno hyaniruddhaśca mūrtibhedāstu vai prabhoḥ
bahūni vividhānīha tasya śāpodbhavāni ca
sarvāvarteṣu rūpāṇi jagatāṃ ca hitāya vai
matsyaḥ kūrmo 'tha vārāho nārasiṃho 'tha vāmanaḥ
rāmo rāmaśca kṛṣṇaśca bauddhaḥ kalkī tathaiva ca
tathānyāni na devasya hareḥ śāpodbhavāni ca
teṣāmapi ca gāyatrīṃ kṛtvā sthāpya ca pūjayet
guhyāni devadevasya harernārāyaṇasya ca
vijñānāni ca yantrāṇi mantropaniṣadāni ca
pañca brahmāṅgajānīha pañcabhūtamayāni ca
namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ paramaśobhanaḥ
harer aṣṭākṣarāṇīha praṇavena samāsataḥ
oṃ namo vāsudevāya namaḥ saṃkarṣaṇāya ca
pradyumnāya pradhānāya aniruddhāya vai namaḥ
ekamekena mantreṇa sthāpayetparameśvaram
bimbāni yāni devasya śivasya parameṣṭhinaḥ
pratiṣṭhā caiva pūjā ca liṅgavanmunisattamāḥ
ratnavinyāsasahitaṃ kautukāni harerapi
acale kārayetsarvaṃ cale'pyevaṃ vidhānataḥ
tannetronmīlanaṃ kuryānnetramantreṇa suvratāḥ
kṣetrapradakṣiṇaṃ caiva ārāmasya purasya ca
jalādhivāsanaṃ caiva pūrvavatparikīrtitam
kuṇḍamaṇḍapanirmāṇaṃ śayanaṃ ca vidhīyate
hutvā navāgnibhāgena navakuṇḍe yathāvidhi
athavā pañcakuṇḍeṣu pradhāne kevale 'thavā
pratiṣṭhā kathitā divyā pāraṃparyakramāgatā
śilodbhavānāṃ biṃbānāṃ citrābhāsasya vā punaḥ
jalādhivāsanaṃ proktaṃ vṛṣendrasya prakīrtitam
prāsādasya pratiṣṭhāyāṃ pratiṣṭhā parikīrtitā
prāsādāṅgasya sarvasya yathāṅgānāṃ tanoriva
vṛṣāgnimātṛvighneśakumārānapi yatnataḥ
śreṣṭhāṃ durgāṃ tathā caṇḍīṃ gāyatryā vai yathāvidhi
prāgādyaṃ sthāpayecchaṃbhoraṣṭāvaraṇamuttamam
lokapālagaṇeśādyānapi śaṃbhoḥ pravinyaset
umā caṇḍī ca nandī ca mahākālo mahāmuniḥ
vighneśvaro mahābhṛṅgī skandaḥ saumyāditaḥ kramāt
indrādīnsveṣu sthāneṣu brahmāṇaṃ ca janārdanam
sthāpayeccaiva yatnena kṣetreśaṃ veśagocare
siṃhāsane hyanantādīn vidyeśāmapi ca kramāt
sthāpayetpraṇavenaiva guhyāṅgādīni paṅkaje
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ calasthāpanam uttamam
sarveṣāmapi devānāṃ devīnāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge 'ṣṭacatvāriṃśo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
aghoreśasya māhātmyaṃ bhavatā kathitaṃ purā
pūjāṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ devasya bhagavanvaktumarhasi
sūta uvāca
aghoreṇāṅgayuktena vidhivacca viśeṣataḥ
pratiṣṭhāliṅgavidhinā nānyathā munipuṅgavāḥ
tathāgnipūjāṃ vai kuryādyathā pūjā tathaiva ca
sahasraṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā
tilair homaḥ prakartavyo dadhimadhvājyasaṃyutaiḥ
ghṛtasaktumadhūnāṃ ca sarvaduḥkhapramārjanam
vyādhīnāṃ nāśanaṃ caiva tilahomastu bhūtidaḥ
sahasreṇa mahābhūtiḥ śatena vyādhināśanam
sarvaduḥkhavinirmukto japena ca na saṃśayaḥ
aṣṭottaraśatenaiva trikāle ca yathāvidhi
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa ṣaṇmāsājjāyate dhruvam
siddhayo naiva saṃdeho rājyamaṇḍalinām api
sahasreṇa jvaro yāti kṣīreṇa ca juhoti yam
trikālaṃ māsamekaṃ tu sahasraṃ juhuyātpayaḥ
māsena sidhyate tasya mahāsaubhāgyamuttamam
sidhyate cābdahomena kṣaudrājyadadhisaṃyutam
yavakṣīrājyahomena jātitaṇḍulakena vā
prīyeta bhagavānīśo hyaghoraḥ parameśvaraḥ
dadhnā puṣṭirnṛpāṇāṃ ca kṣīrahomena śāntikam
ṣaṇmāsaṃ tu ghṛtaṃ hutvā sarvavyādhivināśanam
rājayakṣmā tilair homānnaśyate vatsareṇa tu
yavahomena cāyuṣyaṃ ghṛtena ca jayastadā
sarvakuṣṭhakṣayārthaṃ ca madhunāktaiśca taṇḍulaiḥ
juhuyādayutaṃ nityaṃ ṣaṇmāsānniyataḥ sadā
ājyaṃ kṣīraṃ madhuścaiva madhuratrayamucyate
samastaṃ tuṣyate tasya nāśayedvai bhagandaram
kevalaṃ ghṛtahomena sarvarogakṣayaḥ smṛtaḥ
sarvavyādhiharaṃ dhyānaṃ sthāpanaṃ vidhinārcanam
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ proktamaghorasya mahātmanaḥ
pratiṣṭhā yajanaṃ sarvaṃ nandinā kathitaṃ purā
brahmaputrāya śiṣyāya tena vyāsāya suvratāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekonapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nigrahaḥ kathitastena śivavaktreṇa śūlinā
kṛtāparādhināṃ taṃ tu vaktumarhasi suvrata
tvayā na viditaṃ nāsti laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ tathā
śrautaṃ smārtaṃ mahābhāga romaharṣaṇa suvrata
sūta uvāca
purā bhṛgusutenokto hiraṇyākṣāya suvratāḥ
nigraho 'ghoraśiṣyeṇa śukreṇākṣayatejasā
tasya prasādād daityendro hiraṇyākṣaḥ pratāpavān
trailokyamakhilaṃ jitvā sadevāsuramānuṣam
utpādya putraṃ gaṇapaṃ cāndhakaṃ cāruvikramam
rarāja loke devena varāheṇa niṣūditaḥ
strībādhāṃ bālabādhāṃ ca gavāmapi viśeṣataḥ
kurvato nāsti vijayo mārgeṇānena bhūtale
tena daityena sā devī dharā nītā rasātalam
tenāghoreṇa devena niṣphalo nigrahaḥ kṛtaḥ
saṃvatsarasahasrānte varāheṇa ca sūditaḥ
tasmādaghorasiddhyarthaṃ brāhmaṇānnaiva bādhayet
strīṇāmapi viśeṣeṇa gavāmapi na kārayet
guhyād guhyatamaṃ gopyam atiguhyaṃ vadāmi vaḥ
ātatāyinamuddiśya kartavyaṃ nṛpasattamaiḥ
brāhmaṇebhyo na kartavyaṃ svarāṣṭreśasya vā punaḥ
atīvadurjaye prāpte bale sarve niṣūdite
adharmayuddhe samprāpte kuryādvidhimanuttamam
aghṛṇenaiva kartavyo hyaghṛṇenaiva kārayet
kṛtamātre na saṃdeho nigrahaḥ samprajāyate
lakṣamātraṃ pumāñjaptvā aghoraṃ ghorarūpiṇam
daśāṃśaṃ vidhinā hutvā tilena dvijasattamāḥ
sampūjya lakṣapuṣpeṇa sitena vidhipūrvakam
bāṇaliṅge 'thavā vahnau dakṣiṇāmūrtimāśritaḥ
siddhamantro 'nyathā nāsti draṣṭā siddhyādayaḥ punaḥ
siddhamantraḥ svayaṃ kuryātpretasthāne viśeṣataḥ
mātṛsthāne 'pi vā vidvānvedavedāṅgapāragaḥ
kevalaṃ mantrasiddho vā brāhmaṇaḥ śivabhāvitaḥ
kuryādvidhimimaṃ dhīmān ātmano 'rthaṃ nṛpasya vā
śūlāṣṭakaṃ nyased vidvān pūrvādīśānakāntakam
triśikhaṃ ca triśūlaṃ ca caturviṃśacchikhāgrataḥ
aghoravigrahaṃ kṛtvā saṃkalīkṛtavigrahaḥ
sarvanāśakaraṃ dhyātvā sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
kālāgnikoṭisaṃkāśaṃ svadehamapi bhāvayet
śūlaṃ kapālaṃ pāśaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ caiva śarāsanam
bāṇaṃ ḍamarukaṃ khaḍgamaṣṭāyudhamanukramāt
aṣṭahastaśca varado nīlakaṇṭho digaṃbaraḥ
pañcatattvasamārūḍho hyardhacandradharaḥ prabhuḥ
daṃṣṭrākarālavadano raudradṛṣṭirbhayaṅkaraḥ
huṃphaṭkāramahāśabdaśabditākhiladiṅmukhaḥ
trinetraṃ nāgapāśena subaddhamukuṭaṃ svayam
sarvābharaṇasampannaṃ pretabhasmāvaguṇṭhitam
bhūtaiḥ pretaiḥ piśācaiśca ḍākinībhiśca rākṣasaiḥ
saṃvṛtaṃ gajacarmeṇa ca sarpabhūṣaṇabhūṣitam
vṛścikābharaṇaṃ devaṃ nīlanīradanisvanam
nīlāñjanādrisaṃkāśaṃ siṃhacarmottarīyakam
dhyāyedevamaghoreśaṃ ghoraghorataraṃ śivam
ṣaṭtriṃśaduktamātrābhiḥ prāṇāyāmena suvratāḥ
mahāmudrāsamāyuktaḥ sarvakarmāṇi kārayet
siddhamantraś citāgnau vā pretasthāne yathāvidhi
sthāpayenmadhyadeśe tu aindre yāmye ca vāruṇe
kauberyāṃ vidhivat kṛtvā homakuṇḍāni śāstrataḥ
ācāryo madhyakuṇḍe tu sādhakāśca diśāsu vai
paristīrya vilomena pūrvavacchūlasaṃbhṛtaḥ
kālāgnipīṭhamadhyasthaḥ svayaṃ śiṣyaiśca tādṛśaiḥ
dhyātvā ghoramaghoreśaṃ dvātriṃśākṣarasaṃyutam
vibhītakena vai kṛtvā dvādaśāṅgulamānataḥ
pīṭhe nyasya nṛpendrasya śatrumaṅgārakeṇa tu
kuṇḍasyādhaḥ khanecchatruṃ brāhmaṇaḥ krodhamūrchitaḥ
adhomukhordhvapādaṃ tu sarvakuṇḍeṣu yatnataḥ
śmaśānāṅgāramānīya tuṣeṇa saha dāhayet
tatrāgniṃ sthāpayettūṣṇīṃ brahmacaryaparāyaṇaḥ
māyūrāstreṇa nābhyāṃ tu jvalanaṃ dīpayettataḥ
kañcukaṃ tuṣasaṃyuktaiḥ kārpāsāsthisamanvitaiḥ
raktavastrasamaṃ miśrairhemadravyairviśeṣataḥ
hastayantrodbhavaistailaiḥ saha homaṃ tu kārayet
aṣṭottarasahasraṃ tu homayedanupūrvaśaḥ
kṛṣṇapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ samārabhya yathākramam
aṣṭamyantaṃ tathāṅgāramaṇḍalasthānavarjitaḥ
evaṃ kṛte nṛpendrasya śatravaḥ kulajaiḥ saha
sarvaduḥkhasamopetāḥ prayānti yamasādanam
mantreṇānena cādāya nṛkapāle nakhaṃ tathā
keśaṃ nṛṇāṃ tathāṅgāraṃ tuṣaṃ kañcukameva ca
cīracchaṭāṃ rājadhūlīṃ gṛhasaṃmārjanasya vā
viṣasarpasya dantāni vṛṣadantāni yāni tu
gavāṃ caiva krameṇaiva vyāghradantanakhāni ca
tathā kṛṣṇamṛgāṇāṃ ca biḍālasya ca pūrvavat
nakulasya ca dantāni varāhasya viśeṣataḥ
daṃṣṭrāṇi sādhayitvā tu mantreṇānena suvratāḥ
japedaṣṭottaraśataṃ mantraṃ cāghoramuttamam
tatkapālaṃ nakhaṃ kṣetre gṛhe vā nagare 'pi vā
pretasthāne 'pi vā rāṣṭre mṛtavastreṇa veṣṭayet
śatror aṣṭamarāśau vā pariviṣṭe divākare
some vā pariviṣṭe tu mantreṇānena suvratāḥ
sthānanāśo bhavettasya śatrornāśaśca jāyate
śatruṃ rājñaḥ samālikhya gamane samavasthite
bhūtale darpaṇaprakhye vitānopari śobhite
catustoraṇasaṃyukte darbhamālāsamāvṛte
vedādhyayanasampanne rāṣṭre vṛddhiprakāśake
dakṣiṇena tu pādena mūrdhni saṃtāḍayetsvayam
evaṃ kṛte nṛpendrasya śatrunāśo bhaviṣyati
svarāṣṭrapatim uddiśya yaḥ kuryādābhicārikam
sa ātmānaṃ nihatyaiva svakulaṃ nāśayet kudhīḥ
tasmāt svarāṣṭragoptāraṃ nṛpatiṃ pālayetsadā
mantrauṣadhikriyādyaiśca sarvayatnena sarvadā
etadrahasyaṃ kathitaṃ na deyaṃ yasya kasyacit
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
nigraho ghorarūpo 'yaṃ kathito 'smākamuttamam
vajravāhanikāṃ vidyāṃ vaktumarhasi sattama
sūta uvāca
vajravāhanikā nāma sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī
anayā secayedvajraṃ nṛpāṇāṃ sādhayettathā
vajraṃ kṛtvā vidhānena tadvajramabhiṣicya ca
anayā vidyayā tasmin vinyaset kāñcanena ca
tataścākṣaralakṣaṃ ca japedvidvānsamāhitaḥ
vajrīdaśāṃśaṃ juhuyādvajrakuṇḍe ghṛtādibhiḥ
tadvajraṃ gopayennityaṃ dāpayennṛpatestataḥ
tena vajreṇa vai gacchañchatrūñjīyādraṇājire
purā pitāmahenaiva labdhā vidyā prayatnataḥ
devī śakropakārārthaṃ sākṣādvajreśvarī tathā
purā tvaṣṭā prajānātho hataputraḥ sureśvarāt
vidyayā harataḥ somamindravaireṇa suvratāḥ
tasminyajñe yathāprāptaṃ vidhinopakṛtaṃ haviḥ
tadaicchata mahābāhur viśvarūpavimardanaḥ
matputramavadhīḥ śakra na dāsye tava śobhanam
bhāgaṃ bhāgārhatā naiva viśvarūpo hatastvayā
ityuktvā cāśramaṃ sarvaṃ mohayāmāsa māyayā
tato māyāṃ vinirbhidya viśvarūpavimardanaḥ
prasahya somamapibatsagaṇaiśca śacīpatiḥ
tatastaccheṣamādāya krodhāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ
indrasya śatror vardhasva svāhetyagnau juhāva ha
tataḥ kālāgnisaṃkāśo vartanādvṛtrasaṃjñitaḥ
prādurāsīt sureśārir dudrāva ca vṛṣāntakaḥ
tataḥ kirīṭī bhagavānparityajya divaṃ kṣaṇāt
sahasranetraḥ sagaṇo dudrāva bhayavihvalaḥ
tadā tamāha sa vibhur hṛṣṭo brahmā ca viśvasṛṭ
tyaktvā vajraṃ tametena jahītyarim ariṃdamaḥ
so 'pi saṃnahya devendro devaiḥ sārdhaṃ mahābhujaḥ
nihatya cāprayatnena gatavānvigatajvaraḥ
tasmādvajreśvarīvidyā sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī
mandehā rākṣasā nityaṃ vijitā vidyayaiva tu
tāṃ vidyāṃ sampravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapramocanīm
oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ tatsaviturvareṇyaṃ bhargo devasya dhīmahi
dhiyo yo naḥ pracodayāt
oṃ phaṭ jahi huṃ phaṭ chinddhi bhinddhi jahi hana hana svāhā
vidyā vajreśvarītyeṣā sarvaśatrubhayaṅkarī
anayā saṃhṛtiḥ śaṃbhor vidyayā munipuṅgavāḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge ekapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
śrutā vajreśvarī vidyā brāhmī śakropakāriṇī
anayā sarvakāryāṇi nṛpāṇāmiti naḥ śrutam
viniyogaṃ vadasvāsyā vidyāyā romaharṣaṇa
sūta uvāca
vaśyamākarṣaṇaṃ caiva vidveṣaṇamataḥ param
uccāṭanaṃ stambhanaṃ ca mohanaṃ tāḍanaṃ tathā
utsādanaṃ tathā chedaṃ māraṇaṃ pratibandhanam
senāstaṃbhanakādīni sāvitryā sarvamācaret
āgaccha varade devi bhūmyāṃ parvatamūrdhani
brāhmaṇebhyo hyanujñātā gaccha devi yathāsukham
udvāsyānena mantreṇa gantavyaṃ nānyathā dvijāḥ
pratikāryaṃ tathā bāhyaṃ kṛtvā vaśyādikāṃ kriyām
udvāsya vahnimādhāya punaranyaṃ yathāvidhi
devīmāvāhya ca punar japet sampūjayet punaḥ
homaṃ ca vidhinā vahnau punareva samācaret
sarvakāryāṇi vidhinā sādhayedvidyayā punaḥ
jātīpuṣpaiśca vaśyārthī juhuyādayutatrayam
ghṛtena karavīreṇa kuryādākarṣaṇaṃ dvijāḥ
vidveṣaṇaṃ viśeṣeṇa kuryāllāṅgalakasya ca
tailenoccāṭanaṃ proktaṃ staṃbhanaṃ madhunā smṛtam
tilena mohanaṃ proktaṃ tāḍanaṃ rudhireṇa ca
kharasya ca gajasyātha uṣṭrasya ca yathākramam
staṃbhanaṃ sarṣapeṇāpi pāṭanaṃ ca kuśena ca
māraṇoccāṭane caiva rohībījena suvratāḥ
bandhanaṃ tvahipattreṇa senāstaṃbhamataḥ param
kunaṭyā niyataṃ vidyātpūjayetparameśvarīm
ghṛtena sarvasiddhiḥ syātpayasā vā viśudhyate
tilena roganāśaśca kamalena dhanaṃ bhavet
kāntirmadhūkapuṣpeṇa sāvitryā hyayutatrayam
jayādiprabhṛtīnsarvān sviṣṭāntaṃ pūrvavatsmṛtam
evaṃ saṃkṣepataḥ prokto viniyogo 'tivistṛtaḥ
japedvā kevalāṃ vidyāṃ sampūjya ca vidhānataḥ
sarvasiddhimavāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge dvipañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
mṛtyuñjayavidhiṃ sūta brahmakṣatraviśāmapi
vaktumarhasi cāsmākaṃ sarvajño 'si mahāmate
sūta uvāca
mṛtyuñjayavidhiṃ vakṣye bahunā kiṃ dvijottamāḥ
rudrādhyāyena vidhinā ghṛtena niyutaṃ kramāt
saghṛtena tilenaiva kamalena prayatnataḥ
dūrvayā ghṛtagokṣīramiśrayā madhunā tathā
caruṇā saghṛtenaiva kevalaṃ payasāpi vā
juhuyāt kālamṛtyorvā pratīkāraḥ prakīrtitaḥ
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge tripañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
sūta uvāca
triyaṃbakeṇa mantreṇa devadevaṃ triyaṃbakam
pūjayedbāṇaliṅge vā svayambhūte 'pi vā punaḥ
āyurvedavidairvāpi yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
aṣṭottarasahasreṇa puṇḍarīkeṇa śaṅkaram
kamalena sahasreṇa tathā nīlotpalena vā
sampūjya pāyasaṃ dattvā saghṛtaṃ caudanaṃ punaḥ
mudgānnaṃ madhunā yuktaṃ bhakṣyāṇi surabhīṇi ca
agnau homaśca vipulo yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ
pūrvoktairapi puṣpaiśca caruṇā ca viśeṣataḥ
japedvai niyutaṃ samyak samāpya ca yathākramam
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayedvai sadakṣiṇam
gavāṃ sahasraṃ dattvā tu hiraṇyamapi dāpayet
etadvaḥ kathitaṃ sarvaṃ sarahasyaṃ samāsataḥ
śivena devadevena śarveṇātyugraśūlinā
kathitaṃ meruśikhare skandāyāmitatejase
skandena devadevena brahmaputrāya dhīmate
sākṣātsanatkumāreṇa sarvalokahitaiṣiṇā
pārāśaryāya kathitaṃ pāraṃparyakramāgatam
śuke gate paraṃ dhāma dṛṣṭvā rudraṃ triyaṃbakam
gataśoko mahābhāgo vyāsaḥ para ṛṣiḥ prabhuḥ
skandasya saṃbhavaṃ śrutvā sthitāya ca mahātmane
triyaṃbakasya māhātmyaṃ mantrasya ca viśeṣataḥ
kathitaṃ bahudhā tasmai kṛṣṇadvaipāyanāya vai
tat sarvaṃ kathayiṣyāmi prasādādeva tasya vai
devaṃ sampūjya vidhinā japenmantraṃ triyaṃbakam
mucyate sarpapāpaiśca saptajanmakṛtairapi
saṃgrāme tatsarvaṃ labdhvā saubhāgyamatulaṃ bhavet
lakṣahomena rājyārthī rājyaṃ labdhvā sukhī bhavet
putrārthī putramāpnoti niyutena na saṃśayaḥ
dhanārthī prayutenaiva japedeva na saṃśayaḥ
dhanadhānyādibhiḥ sarvaiḥ sampūrṇaḥ sarvamaṅgalaiḥ
krīḍate putrapautraiśca mṛtaḥ svarge prajāyate
nānena sadṛśo mantro loke vede ca suvratāḥ
tasmāttriyaṃbakaṃ devaṃ tena nityaṃ prapūjayet
agniṣṭomasya yajñasya phalamaṣṭaguṇaṃ bhavet
trayāṇāmapi lokānāṃ guṇānāmapi yaḥ prabhuḥ
vedānāmapi devānāṃ brahmakṣatraviśāmapi
akārokāramakārāṇāṃ mātrāṇāmapi vācakaḥ
tathā somasya sūryasya vahneragnitrayasya ca
aṃbā umā mahādevo hyambakastu triyaṃbakaḥ
supuṣpitasya vṛkṣasya yathā gandhaḥ suśobhanaḥ
vāti dūrāt tathā tasya gandhaḥ śaṃbhormahātmanaḥ
tasmātsugandho bhagavān gandhārayati śaṅkaraḥ
gāndhāraśca mahādevo devānāmapi līlayā
sugandhastasya loke 'smin vāyur vāti nabhastale
tasmātsugandhistaṃ devaṃ sugandhi puṣṭivardhanam
yasya retaḥ purā śaṃbhorhareryonau pratiṣṭhitam
tasya vīryādabhūdaṇḍaṃ hiraṇmayam ajodbhavam
candrādityau sanakṣatrau bhūrbhuvaḥ svarmahastapaḥ
satyalokamatikramya puṣṭirvīryasya tasya vai
pañcabhūtānyahaṅkāro buddhiḥ prakṛtireva ca
puṣṭirbījasya tasyaiva tasmādvai puṣṭivardhanaḥ
taṃ puṣṭivardhanaṃ devaṃ ghṛtena payasā tathā
madhunā yavagodhūmamāṣabilvaphalena ca
kumudārkaśamīpatragaurasarṣapaśālibhiḥ
hutvā liṅge yathānyāyaṃ bhaktyā devaṃ yajāmahe
ṛtenānena māṃ pāśādbandhanātkarmayogataḥ
mṛtyośca bandhanāccaiva mukṣīya bhava tejasā
urvārukāṇāṃ pakvānāṃ yathā kālādabhūtpunaḥ
tathaiva kālaḥ samprāpto manunā tena yatnataḥ
evaṃ mantravidhiṃ jñātvā śivaliṅgaṃ samarcayet
tasya pāśakṣayo 'tīva yogino mṛtyunigrahaḥ
triyaṃbakasamo nāsti devo vā ghṛṇayānvitaḥ
prasādaśīlaḥ prītaśca tathā mantro 'pi suvratāḥ
tasmātsarvaṃ parityajya triyaṃbakamumāpatim
triyaṃbakeṇa mantreṇa pūjayetsusamāhitaḥ
sarvāvasthāṃ gato vāpi mukto 'yaṃ sarvapātakaiḥ
śivadhyānānna saṃdeho yathā rudrastathā svayam
hatvā bhittvā ca bhūtāni bhuktvā cānyāyato 'pi vā
śivamekaṃ sakṛtsmṛtvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge catuṣpañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
kathaṃ triyaṃbako devo devadevo vṛṣadhvajaḥ
dhyeyaḥ sarvārthasiddhyarthaṃ yogamārgeṇa suvrata
pūrvamevāpi nikhilaṃ śrutaṃ śrutisamaṃ punaḥ
vistareṇa ca tatsarvaṃ saṃkṣepādvaktumarhasi
sūta uvāca
evaṃ paitāmahenaiva nandī dinakaraprabhaḥ
merupṛṣṭhe purā pṛṣṭo munisaṃghaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ
so 'pi tasmai kumārāya brahmaputrāya suvratāḥ
mithaḥ provāca bhagavānpraṇatāya samāhitaḥ
nandikeśvara uvāca
evaṃ purā mahādevo bhagavānnīlalohitaḥ
giriputryāṃbayā devyā bhagavatyaikaśayyayā
pṛṣṭaḥ kailāsaśikhare hṛṣṭapuṣṭatanūruhaḥ
śrīdevyuvāca
yogaḥ katividhaḥ proktastatkathaṃ caiva kīdṛśam
jñānaṃ ca mokṣadaṃ divyaṃ mucyante yena jantavaḥ
śrībhagavānuvāca
prathamo mantrayogaśca sparśayogo dvitīyakaḥ
bhāvayogastṛtīyaḥ syād abhāvaśca caturthakaḥ
sarvottamo mahāyogaḥ pañcamaḥ parikīrtitaḥ
dhyānayukto japābhyāso mantrayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
nāḍīśuddhyadhiko yastu recakādikramānvitaḥ
samastavyastayogena jayo vāyoḥ prakīrtitaḥ
balasthirakriyāyukto dhāraṇādyaiśca śobhanaiḥ
dhāraṇātrayasaṃdīpto bhedatrayaviśodhakaḥ
kuṃbhakāvasthito 'bhyāsaḥ sparśayogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
mantrasparśavinirmukto mahādevaṃ samāśritaḥ
bahirantarvibhāgasthasphuratsaṃharaṇātmakaḥ
bhāvayogaḥ samākhyātāścittaśuddhipradāyakaḥ
vilīnāvayavaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam
śūnyaṃ sarvaṃ nirābhāsaṃ svarūpaṃ yatra cintyate
abhāvayogaḥ samproktaś cittanirvāṇakārakaḥ
nīrūpaḥ kevalaḥ śuddhaḥ svacchandaṃ ca suśobhanaḥ
anirdeśyaḥ sadālokaḥ svayaṃvedyaḥ samaṃ tataḥ
svabhāvo bhāsate yatra mahāyogaḥ prakīrtitaḥ
nityoditaḥ svayaṃjyotiḥ sarvacittasamutthitaḥ
nirmalaḥ kevalo hyātmā mahāyoga iti smṛtaḥ
aṇimādipradāḥ sarve sarve jñānasya dāyakāḥ
uttarottaravaiśiṣṭyameṣu yogeṣvanukramāt
ahaṃ saṃgavinirmukto mahākāśopamaḥ paraḥ
sarvāvaraṇanirmukto hyacintyaḥ svarasena tu
jñeyametatsamākhyātamagrāhyamapi daivataiḥ
pravilīno mahānsamyak svayaṃvedyaḥ svasākṣikaḥ
cakāstyānandavapuṣā tena jñeyam idaṃ matam
parīkṣitāya śiṣyāya brāhmaṇāyāhitāgnaye
dhārmikāyākṛtaghnāya dātavyaṃ kramapūrvakam
gurudaivatabhaktāya anyathā naiva dāpayet
nindito vyādhito 'lpāyus tathā caiva prajāyate
dāturapyevamanaghe tasmājjñātvaiva dāpayet
sarvasaṃgavinirmukto madbhakto matparāyaṇaḥ
sādhako jñānasaṃyuktaḥ śrautasmārtaviśāradaḥ
gurubhaktaśca puṇyātmā yogyo yogarataḥ sadā
eva devi samākhyāto yogamārgaḥ sanātanaḥ
sarvavedāgamāṃbhojamakarandaḥ sumadhyame
pītvā yogāmṛtaṃ yogī mucyate brahmavittamaḥ
evaṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ yogaiśvaryamanuttamam
atyāśramamidaṃ jñeyaṃ muktaye kena labhyate
tasmādiṣṭaiḥ samācāraiḥ śivārcanarataiḥ priye
ityuktvā bhagavāndevīmanujñāpya vṛṣadhvajaḥ
śaṅkukarṇaṃ samāsādya yuyojātmānamātmani
śailādiruvāca
tasmāttvamapi yogīndra yogābhyāsarato bhava
svayaṃbhuvaḥ parā mūrtirnūnaṃ brahmamayī varā
tasmātsarvaprayatnena mokṣārthī puruṣottamaḥ
bhasmasnāyī bhavennityaṃ yoge pāśupate rataḥ
dhyeyā yathākrameṇaiva vaiṣṇavī ca tataḥ parā
māheśvarī parā paścātsaiva dhyeyā yathākramam
yogeśvarasya yā niṣṭhā saiṣā saṃhṛtya varṇitā
sūta uvāca
evaṃ śilādaputreṇa nandinā kulanandinā
yogaḥ pāśupataḥ prokto bhasmaniṣṭhena dhīmatā
sanatkumāro bhagavānvyāsāyāmitatejase
tasmādahamapi śrutvā niyogāt sattriṇāmapi
kṛtakṛtyo 'smi viprebhyo namo yajñebhya eva ca
namaḥ śivāya śāntāya vyāsāya munaye namaḥ
granthaikādaśasāhasraṃ purāṇaṃ laiṅgamuttamam
aṣṭottaraśatādhyāyam ādimāṃśam ataḥ param
ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadadhyāyaṃ dharmakāmārthamokṣadam
atha te munayaḥ sarve naimiṣeyāḥ samāhitāḥ
praṇemurdevamīśānaṃ prītikaṇṭakitatvacaḥ
śākhāṃ paurāṇikīmevaṃ kṛtvaikādaśikāṃ prabhuḥ
brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavānidaṃ vacanamabravīt
laiṅgam ādyantam akhilaṃ yaḥ paṭhecchṛṇuyādapi
dvijebhyaḥ śrāvayedvāpi sa yāti paramāṃ gatim
tapasā caiva yajñena dānenādhyayanena ca
yā gatistasya vipulā śāstravidyā ca vaidikī
karmaṇā cāpi miśreṇa kevalaṃ vidyayāpi vā
nivṛttiścāsya viprasya bhavedbhaktiśca śāśvatī
mayi nārāyaṇe deve śraddhā cāstu mahātmanaḥ
vaṃśasya cākṣayā vidyā cāpramādaśca sarvataḥ
ityājñā brahmaṇastasmāttasya sarvaṃ mahātmanaḥ
ṛṣayaḥ procuḥ
ṛṣeḥ sūtasya cāsmākam eteṣām api cāsya ca
nāradasya ca yā siddhistīrthayātrāratasya ca
prītiśca vipulā yasmād asmākaṃ romaharṣaṇa
sā sadāstu virūpākṣaprasādāttu samantataḥ
evamukteṣu vipreṣu nārado bhagavānapi
karābhyāṃ suśubhāgrābhyāṃ sūtaṃ pasparśivāṃstvaci
svastyastu sūta bhadraṃ te mahādeve vṛṣadhvaje
śraddhā tavāstu cāsmākaṃ namastasmai śivāya ca
iti śrīliṅgamahāpurāṇe uttarabhāge pañcapañcāśattamo 'dhyāyaḥ
